B_4_C_1_0
BEGIN_
स ताम् पुष्करिणीम् गत्वा पद्म उत्पल झषाकुलाम् |रामः सौमित्रि सहितो विललाप अकुलेन्द्रियः || ४-१-१_END
BEGIN_
Rama, on arriving at that Lake of Lotuses called Pampa along with Lakshmana, which is full with lotuses, 
costuses, and fishes, lamented as his emotions are disturbed, on seeing the beauty of the Lake comparable 
with Seetha's face. [4-1-1]_END

B_4_C_1_1
BEGIN_
तत्र दृष्ट्वैवा ताम् हर्षात् इन्द्रियाणि चकम्पिरे |स कामवशम् आपन्नः सौमित्रिम् इदम् अब्रवीत् || 
४-१-२_END
BEGIN_
There, on seeing that Lake of Lotuses, thrilled are his senses with gladness, and he engrossed and overcame 
by passion spoke this way to Lakshmana. [4-1-2]_END

B_4_C_1_2
BEGIN_
सौमित्रे शोभते पम्पा वैदूर्य विमल उदका |फुल्ल पद्म उत्पलवती शोभिता विविधैः द्रुमैः || ४-१-३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh! Soumitri, magnificent is Pampa Lake with its cat's-eye-gem like waters, and she with her fully 
bloomed lotuses and costuses is beaming forth, along with many trees around her. [3-1-3]_END

B_4_C_1_3
BEGIN_
सौमित्रे पश्य पम्पायाः काननम् शुभ दर्शनम् |यत्र राजन्ति शैला वा द्रुमाः स शिखरा इव || ४-१-४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh! Soumitri, see the forest of Pampa, the auspicious one in its appearance... where the mountains 
or trees lustre with their mountainous peaks... [4-1-4]_END

B_4_C_1_4
BEGIN_
माम् तु शोकाभि सन्तप्तम् आधयः पीडयन्ति वै ||भरतस्य च दुःखेन वैदेह्या हरणेन च || ४-१-५_END
BEGIN_
"But I, who am well seethed by the anguish of Bharata, and even by the abduction of Seetha, am indeed 
distressed by my sensibilities and their distresses... [4-1-5]_END

B_4_C_1_5
BEGIN_
शोकार्तस्य अपि मे पम्पा शोभते चित्र कानना |व्यवकीर्णा बहु विधैः पुष्पैः शीतोदका शिवा || ४-१-६_END
BEGIN_
"This auspicious Pampa is pleasant to me with its delightful forests overspread with many diverse flowers, 
cool waters, though I am disquieted... [4-1-6]_END

B_4_C_1_6
BEGIN_
नलिनैः अपि संछन्ना हि अत्यर्थ शुभ दर्शना |सर्प व्याल अनुचरिता मृग द्विज समाकुला || ४-१-७_END
BEGIN_
"Even enwreathed with lotuses this is remarkably sacred in its aspect... rambling snakes and elephants 
and restless are the deer and birds flocks, as well... [4-1-7]_END

B_4_C_1_7
BEGIN_
अधिकम् प्रविभाति एतत् नील पीतम् तु शाद्वलम् |द्रुमाणाम् विविधैः पुष्पैः परिस्तोमैः इव अर्पितम् || 
४-१-८_END
BEGIN_
"All this is shining very much with bluish, yellowish grassland with a variety of trees... and with 
flowers covering it like flowery bed-sheet with variegated colours... [4-1-8]_END

B_4_C_2_0
BEGIN_
तौ तु दृष्ट्वा महात्मानौ भ्रातरौ राम लक्ष्मणौ |वर आयुध धरौ वीरौ सुग्रीवः श्ङ्कितोऽभवत् || ४-२-१_END
BEGIN_
On seeing them the wielders of best weapons and audacious ones, two brothers and great souls, namely 
Rama and Lakshmana, Sugreeva became ambiguous. [4-2-1]_END

B_4_C_1_8
BEGIN_
पुष्प भार समृद्धानि शिखराणि समन्ततः |लताभिः पुष्पित अग्राभिः उपगूढानि सर्वतः || ४-१-९_END
BEGIN_
"Everywhere the treetops are fully flowered and the onus of those flowers is on the rise, though they 
are wholly embraced by climbers and their apices. [4-1-9]_END

B_4_C_2_1
BEGIN_
उद्विग्न हृदयः सर्वा दिशः समवलोकयन् |न व्यतिष्ठत कस्मिन् चित् देशे वानर पुङ्गवः || ४-२-२_END
BEGIN_
Distressed at heart that foremost monkey gazed blankly in all directions and he did not remain at any 
one place. [4-2-2]_END

B_4_C_1_9
BEGIN_
सुख अनिलोऽयम् सौमित्रे कालः प्रचुर मन्मथः |गन्धवान् सुरभिर् मासो जात पुष्प फल द्रुमः || ४-१-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Pleasing is this breeze, oh! Soumitri, and Manmadha, the Love God, prevails at this time, and prideful 
is this month with its fragrance, flowers, fruits and trees... all anew... [4-1-10]_END

B_4_C_2_2
BEGIN_
नैव चक्रे मनः स्थातुम् वीक्षमाणो महाबलौ |कपेः परम भीतस्य चित्तम् व्यवससाद ह || ४-२-३_END
BEGIN_
On seeing those two great mighty ones that monkey has not even made-up his mind steadfast as he is very 
much frightened, and his heart is really sunken. [4- 2- 3]_END

B_4_C_2_3
BEGIN_
चिन्तयित्वा स धर्मात्मा विमृश्य गुरु लाघवम् |सुग्रीवः परम उद्विग्नः सर्वैः तैः वानरैः सह || ४-२-४_END
BEGIN_
He that righteous Sugreeva considering his own strength and weakness is much agitated, and along with 
all the other monkeys too are frightened. [4-2-4]_END

B_4_C_1_10
BEGIN_
पश्य रूपाणि सौमित्रे वनानाम् पुष्प शालिनाम् |सृजताम् पुष्प वर्षाणि वर्षम् तोयमुचाम् इव || ४-१-११_END
BEGIN_
"See this figuration of these forests enriched with these flowers, Soumitri! Outpouring is the flower 
rain, like the rain from rain-clouds... [4-1-11]_END

B_4_C_2_4
BEGIN_
ततः स सचिवेभ्यः तु सुग्रीवः प्लवगाधिपः |शशंस परम उद्विग्नः पश्यन् तौ राम लक्ष्मणौ || ४-२-५_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Rama and Lakshmana then that chief of monkeys Sugreeva with much dreadfulness said this to 
his ministers. [4- 2- 5]_END

B_4_C_1_11
BEGIN_
प्रस्तरेषु च रम्येषु विविधाः कानन द्रुमाः |वायु वेग प्रचलिताः पुष्पैः अवकिरन्ति गाम् || ४-१-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Also on those appeasing terraces of mountains there are many forest trees... speed of winds are swinging 
them to shower flowers onto ground... [4-1-12]_END

B_4_C_1_12
BEGIN_
पतितैः पतमानैः च पादपस्थैः च मारुतः |कुसुमैः पश्य सौमित्रे क्रीडतीव समन्ततः || ४-१-१३_END
BEGIN_
"These are the flowers already fallen, about to fall, or still on the trees, but everywhere the air 
is playing with these flowers, see that Lakshmana... [4-1-13]_END

B_4_C_2_5
BEGIN_
एतौ वनम् इदम् दुर्गम् वालि प्रणिहितौ ध्रुवम् |छद्मना चीर वसनौ प्रचरन्तौ इह आगतौ || ४-२-६_END
BEGIN_
"Here they come wearing jute cloths and move about in this impassable forest deceitfully, definitely 
Vali must have dispatched them... [4-2-6]_END

B_4_C_2_6
BEGIN_
ततः सुग्रीव सचिवा दृष्ट्वा परम धन्विनौ |जग्मुः गिरि तटात् तस्माद् अन्यत् शिखरम् उत्तमम् || ४-२-७_END
BEGIN_
Then on seeing the great archers Rama and Lakshmana the ministers of Sugreeva have gone from that mountain 
terrace to another high-peaked mountain. [4- 2- 7]_END

B_4_C_1_13
BEGIN_
विक्षिपन् विविधाः शाखा नगानाम् कुसुमोत्कटाः |मारुतः चलित स्थानैः षट्पदैः अनुगीयते || ४-१-१४_END
BEGIN_
"The honeybees are displaced when the wind rapidly moved numerous branches of trees with full of flowers, 
and though displaced those bees are singing as though in accompaniment to the singing breeze... [4-1-14]_END

B_4_C_3_0
BEGIN_
वचो विज्ञाय हनुमान् सुग्रीवस्य महात्मनः |पर्वतात् ऋष्यमूकात् तु पुप्लुवे यत्र राघवौ || ४-३-१_END
BEGIN_
Mindful of the words of noble-souled Sugreeva, Hanuma took his flight from Mt. Rishyamuka to where Raghavaa-s 
are. [4-3-1]_END

B_4_C_1_14
BEGIN_
मत्त कोकिल सन्नादैः नर्तयन् इव पादपान् |शैल कन्दर निष्क्रान्तः प्रगीत इव च अनिलः || ४-१-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Breeze coming out from those mountain caves along with the high callings of lusty black cuckoos are 
making the trees to dance, and the air itself is as though singing as an accompaniment to that dancing... 
[4-1-15]_END

B_4_C_2_7
BEGIN_
ते क्षिप्रम् अभिगम्य अथ यूथपा यूथपर्षभम् |हरयो वानर श्रेष्ठम् परिवार्य उपतस्थिरे || ४-२-८_END
BEGIN_
Then the group-leaders of monkeys quickly arrived as they fled, at that lofty monkey group-leader Sugreeva, 
the chieftain of monkeys, gathering around him there they stood at his nearby. [4-2-8]_END

B_4_C_3_1
BEGIN_
कपि रूपम् परित्यज्य हनुमान् मारुतात्मजः |भिक्षु रूपम् ततो भेजे शठबुद्धितया कपिः || ४-३-२_END
BEGIN_
Casting off his monkey's semblance Air-god's son Hanuma attained the persona of an ascetic, for that 
monkey is incredulous in mind about Raghava-s. [4-3-2]_END

B_4_C_1_15
BEGIN_
तेन विक्षिपता अत्यर्थम् पवनेन समन्ततः |अमी संसक्त शाखाग्रा ग्रथिता इव पादपाः || ४-१-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Entwined are the spires of trees when muchly moved by the air, thus the trees themselves seem to be 
entwined one with the other... [4-1-16]_END

B_4_C_2_8
BEGIN_
एवम् एक आयन गताः प्लवमाना गिरेः गिरिम् |प्रकंपयन्तो वेगेन गिरीणाम् शिखराणि च || ४-२-९_END
BEGIN_
Thus they reached to one course of return, after hopping from one mountain to the other, shuddering 
mountains and even thir peaks by their trample in hastiness. [4-2-9]_END

B_4_C_3_2
BEGIN_
ततः च हनुमान् वाचा श्लक्ष्णया सुमनोज्ञया |विनीतवत् उपागम्य राघवौ प्रणिपत्य च || ४-३-३अबभाषे 
च तौ वीरौ यथावत् प्रशशंस च |_END
BEGIN_
Then on nearing Raghava-s that Hanuma voicing softly and well pleasingly like an obedient one, that 
best monkey befittingly hailed, greeted and praised those two valiant ones. [4-3-3, 4a]_END

B_4_C_1_16
BEGIN_
स एव सुख संस्पर्शो वाति चन्दन शीतलः |गन्धम् अभ्यवहन् पुण्यम् श्रम अपनयो अनिलः || ४-१-१७_END
BEGIN_
"He, this breeze is thus a happy one for touch, carrying a coolant and the fragrance like that of the 
sandalwood, and this breezing is a merited one and a fatigue remover... [4-1-17]_END

B_4_C_2_9
BEGIN_
ततः शाखा मृगाः सर्वे प्लवमाना महाबलाः |बभंजुः च नगान् तत्र पुष्पितान् दुर्गम् आश्रितान् || ४-२-१०_END
BEGIN_
Then all of the tree-branch animals, who are great in their strength, have wrecked down the well-flowered 
trees that are clumped in that forest on that mountain by their swinging. [4- 2- 10]_END

B_4_C_3_3
BEGIN_
संपूज्य विधिवद् वीरौ हनुमान् वानरोत्तमः || ४-३-४उवाच कामतो वाक्यम् मृदु सत्य पराक्रमौ |_END
BEGIN_
The best Vanara Hanuma spoke soft-wordily, as desired by Sugreeva, to those candidly resolute ones, 
on making reverent obeisance to both of them. [4-3-4b, 5a]_END

B_4_C_1_17
BEGIN_
अमी पवन विक्षिप्ता विनन्दन्ती इव पादपाः |षट्पदैः अनुकूजद्भिः वनेषु मधु गन्धिषु || ४-१-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Air is vacillating these trees in this honey scented forest... and the trees appear to be enjoying 
their fluttering dance and seem to be swinging their treetops to appreciate the singing of honeybees 
that are humming in accompaniment to this dance... [4-1-18]_END

B_4_C_2_10
BEGIN_
आप्लवन्तो हरिवराः सर्वतः तम् महागिरिम् |मृग मार्जार शार्दूलान् त्रासयन्तो ययुः तदा || ४-२-११_END
BEGIN_
While those best monkeys hopped everywhere they have frightened deer, wildcats and tigers on that great 
mountain. [4-2-11]_END

B_4_C_3_4
BEGIN_
राजर्षि देव प्रतिमौ तापसौ संशित व्रतौ || ४-३-५देशम् कथम् इमम् प्राप्तौ भवन्तौ वर वर्णिनौ |त्रासयन्तौ 
मृग गणान् अन्याम् च वन चारिणः || ४-३-६_END
BEGIN_
"You two look like kingly saints, or deities by your build, ascetics with blest vows, but with ideal 
complexions... how come you arrived at this countryside scaring the herds of animals and other inhabitants 
of this forest... [4-3-5b, 6]_END

B_4_C_1_18
BEGIN_
गिरि प्रस्थेषु रम्येषु पुष्पवद्भिः मनोरमैः |संसक्त शिखरा शैला विराजन्ति महाद्रुमैः || ४-१-१९_END
BEGIN_
"On mountain-planes that are beautiful with fully flowered and pleasant tress that entwine the mountain 
peaks with their high treetops, and thus these mountains indeed liven up with these great trees...[4-1-19]_END

B_4_C_2_11
BEGIN_
ततः सुग्रीव सचिवाः पर्वतेन्द्रे समाहिताः |संगम्य कपि मुख्येन सर्वे प्रांजलयः स्थिताः || ४-२-१२_END
BEGIN_
Then the ministers of Sugreeva, assembled on that best mountain and gathered around the chief of monkeys 
Sugreeva, and all stood with their adjoined palms. [4-2-12]_END

B_4_C_3_5
BEGIN_
पम्पा तीर रुहान् वृक्षान् वीक्षमाणौ समंततः |इमाम् नदीम् शुभ जलाम् शोभयन्तौ तरस्विनौ || ४-३-७
धैर्यवन्तौ सुवर्णाभौ कौ युवाम् चीर वाससौ |निःश्वसन्तौ वर भुजौ पीडयन्तौ इमाः प्रजाः || ४-३-८_END
BEGIN_
"You mighty ones you are watching the trees grown on the banks of Pampa from all over, and owing to 
your presence on these banks you make this river Pampa with its propitious waters to shine forth... 
but you with your golden hue appear as courageous ones, yet you sigh over repeatedly, you wear jute-cloths, 
yet you look mighty shouldered... who are you that distress all the beings in this forest... [4-3-7, 
8]_END

B_4_C_1_19
BEGIN_
पुष्प संछन्न शिखरा मारुतः उत्क्षेप चंचला |अमी मधुकरोत्तंसाः प्रगीत इव पादपाः || ४-१-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Air is moving the treetops fully covered with flowers to swinging and the coronet like honeybees have 
to swing around those treetops, thus these trees themselves appear to be dancing to be dancing and singing... 
[4-1-20]_END

B_4_C_2_12
BEGIN_
ततः तु भय संत्रस्तम् वालि किल्बिष शन्कितम् |उवाच हनुमान् वाक्यम् सुग्रीवम् वाक्य कोविदः || ४-२-१३_END
BEGIN_
Then Hanuma, the ablest sentence-maker, said this sentence to Sugreeva who is dismayed with fear doubting 
Vali's mischief. [4-2-13]_END

B_4_C_3_6
BEGIN_
सिंह विप्रेक्षितौ वीरौ महाबल पराक्रमौ |शक्र चाप निभे चापे गृहीत्वा शत्रु नाशनौ || ४-३-९श्रीमन्तौ 
रूप संपन्नौ वृषभ श्रेष्ठ विक्रमौ |हस्ति हस्त उपम भुजौ द्युतिमन्तौ नरर्षभौ || ४-३- १०_END
BEGIN_
"Dauntless, bold and brave are you with sharp glances of lions, wielding bows like that of Indra's bow 
you are the real enemy destroyers... glorious, splendid, and even impetuous you appear like Sacred Bulls... 
elephant's trunks are your arms... and you foremost among men are self-resplendent... [4-3-9, 10]_END

B_4_C_1_20
BEGIN_
सुपुष्पितांस्तु पश्य एतान् कर्णिकारान् समन्ततः |हाटक प्रति संच्छन्नान् नरान् पीतांबरान् इव || ४-१-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Fully flowered are these Karnikaara plants all over with golden colour flowers at top and yellow coloured 
stems, and they look like men wearing golden ornaments on their upper body, while their loin cloth is 
yellow... [4-1-21]_END

B_4_C_2_13
BEGIN_
संभ्रमः त्यजताम् एष सर्वैः वालि कृते महान् |मलयोऽयम् गिरिवरो भयम् न इह अस्ति वालिनः || ४-२-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Perplexity be warded off... all of you discarded that great fear from Vali or his cruelty... there 
is no scare from Vali here on this best mountain, for it is Mt. Malaya... [4-2-14]_END

B_4_C_3_7
BEGIN_
प्रभया पर्वत इन्द्रः असौ युवयोः अवभासितः |राज्य अर्हौ अमर प्रख्यौ कथम् देशम् इह आगतौ || ४-३-११_END
BEGIN_
"This lord-like mountain is effulgent with your effulgence, you two look as kingdom-worthy, or worthy 
divinities, but how you have reached this countryside now... [4-3-11]_END

B_4_C_1_21
BEGIN_
अयम् वसन्तः सौमित्रे नाना विहग नादितः |सीतया विप्रहीणस्य शोक सन्दीपनो मम || ४-१-२२_END
BEGIN_
"This spring with the soundings of many birds, oh! Soumitri, is enkindling grief in me, for Seetha is 
disunited...[4-1-22]_END

B_4_C_2_14
BEGIN_
यस्मात् उद्विग्न चेताः त्वम् विद्रुतो हरिपुंगव |तम् क्रूर दर्शनम् क्रूरम् न इह पश्यामि वालिनम् || 
४-२-१५_END
BEGIN_
"By whom you are bewildered at heart and running away, oh, the best monkey Sugreeva, I do not see that 
cruel-looking, cruel Vali here... [4- 2-15]_END

B_4_C_3_8
BEGIN_
पद्म पत्र ईक्षणौ वीरौ जटा मण्डल धारिणौ |अन्योन्य सदृशौ वीरौ देव लोकात् इह आगतौ || ४-३-१२यदृच्छयेव 
संप्राप्तौ चन्द्र सूर्यौ वसुंधराम् |विशाल वक्षसौ वीरौ मानुषौ देव रूपिणौ || ४-३-१३सिंह स्कन्धौ 
महा उत्साहौ समदौ इव गोवृषौ |_END
BEGIN_
"Eyes of yours are like fine lotus petals, are you superhuman... nay, you wear tufts and braids, are 
you some undaunted human ascetics... nay, you look clonal, are you from some world of gods... nay, you 
are on earth, does this earth have a chance to receive Sun and Moon on her by her fortune... nay, are 
you some broad-chested deities in human form... lion-shouldered, very vehement and vigorous like Sacred 
Bulls... who you might be... [4-3-12, 13, 14a]_END

B_4_C_1_22
BEGIN_
माम् हि शोक समाक्रान्तम् संतापयति मन्मथः |हृष्टम् प्रवदमानश्च समाह्वयति कोकिलः || ४-१-२३_END
BEGIN_
"I, who am already pervaded by grief, am now well sweltered by the Love God, and this cuckoo that has 
happy calls is rather calling me down... [4-1-23]_END

B_4_C_2_15
BEGIN_
यस्मात् तव भयम् सौम्य पूर्वजात् पाप कर्मणः |स न इह वाली दुष्टात्मा न ते पश्यामि अहम् भयम् || ४-२-१६_END
BEGIN_
"From whom your fear is spurted, oh, gentle Sugreeva, that elder brother of yours, who is an evildoer 
and the one with harmful intent... that Vali is not here. Therefore I perceive no fear from him...[4-2-16]_END

B_4_C_3_9
BEGIN_
आयताः च सुवृत्ताः च बाहवः परिघोपमाः || ४-३-१४सर्व भूषण भूषार्हाः किम् अर्थम् न विभूषिताः |_END
BEGIN_
"Also lengthy are your hands, and spherical are your shoulders similar to clubs... they are worthy for 
decoration with every kind of ornament, for what reason they are undecorated... [4-3-14b, 15a]_END

B_4_C_1_23
BEGIN_
एष दाअत्यूहको हृष्टो रम्ये माम् वन निर्झरे |प्रणदन् मन्मथाविष्टम् शोचयिष्यति लक्ष्मण || ४-१-२४_END
BEGIN_
"This gallinule bird happily calling in the forest brooks is making me awesome with its calls, as the 
Love-god has already made me awestricken... [4-1-24]_END

B_4_C_2_16
BEGIN_
अहो शाखा मृगत्वम् ते व्यक्तम् एव प्लवंगम |लघु चित्ततया आत्मानम् न स्थापयसि यो मतौ || ४-२-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Aha! You made a monkey of yourself, oh, monkey, and you feel small, thus you are not able to stay firm 
in your mind by that fickleness, and your monkeyshines is clear by it... [4-2-17]_END

B_4_C_3_10
BEGIN_
उभौ योग्यौ अहम् मन्ये रक्षितुम् पृथिवीम् इमाम् || ४-३-१५स सागर वनाम् कृत्स्नाम् विन्ध्य मेरु विभूषिताम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"I deem that each of you are the choicest one to protect the earth adorned with Mt Meru and Vindhya 
range, and with all her oceans and forests... [4-3-15b, 16a]_END

B_4_C_1_24
BEGIN_
श्रुत्वा एतस्य पुरा शब्दम् आश्रमस्था मम प्रिया |माम् आहूय प्रमुदिता परमम् प्रत्यनन्दत || ४-१-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Earlier when we were in hermitage, on hearing this bird's call, dear Seetha used to call me to listen, 
and she herself was highly cheerful at this bird's calls... [4-1-25]_END

B_4_C_2_17
BEGIN_
बुद्धि विज्ञान संपन्न इङ्गितैः सर्वम् आचर |न हि अबुद्धिम् गतो राजा सर्व भूतानि शास्ति हि || ४-२-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Keep your intellect and wisdom firm, and express all your intents rightly in your body language in 
all your undertakings... certainly, a king getting into unintelligence cannot command all his subjects..." 
So said Hanuma to Sugreeva. [4-2-18]_END

B_4_C_4_0
BEGIN_
ततः प्रहृष्टो हनुमान् कृत्यवान् इति तत् वचः |
श्रुत्वा मधुर भावम् च सुग्रीवम् मनसा गतः || ४-४-१_END
BEGIN_
Then that Hanuma, who has good deeds for his credit, on hearing the words of
Lakshmana, and even knowing that they are finely meaningful, he rejoicingly recalled in his mind
that Sugreeva's effort is going to fructify. [4-4-1]_END

B_4_C_3_11
BEGIN_
इमे च धनुषी चित्रे श्लक्ष्णे चित्र अनुलेपने || ४-३-१६प्रकाशेते यथा इन्द्रस्य वज्रे हेम विभूषिते 
|_END
BEGIN_
"And these awesome bows are polished with odd things are smooth, and they are brightening like the gilded 
Thunderbolt of Indra. [4-3-16]_END

B_4_C_1_25
BEGIN_
एवम् विचित्राः पतगा नाना राव विराविणः |वृक्ष गुल्म लताः पश्य संपतन्ति समन्ततः|| ४-१-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Very many amusing birds of that kind are flitting all over on trees, bushes, and creepers emitting 
very many sounds... see them, Lakshmana... [4-1-26]_END

B_4_C_2_18
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवः तु शुभम् वाक्यम् श्रुत्वा सर्वम् हनूमतः |ततः शुभतरम् वाक्यम् हनूमन्तम् उवाच ह || ४-२-१९_END
BEGIN_
Sugreeva thus hearing entirely to all the propitious words of Hanuma spoke to Hanuma this opportune 
sentence, positively. [4-2-19]_END

B_4_C_4_1
BEGIN_
भाव्यो राज्यागमः तस्य सुग्रीवस्य महात्मनः |
यत् अयम् कृत्यवान् प्राप्तः कृत्यम् च एतत् उपागतम् || ४-४-२_END
BEGIN_
"Conceivable is the retrieval of the kingdom by that great souled Sugreeva...and for
which deed, this purposive Rama has come, and that deed desired by Rama is also achievable by
Sugreeva, and thus all this has came by..." thus thought Hanuma. [4-4-2]_END

B_4_C_3_12
BEGIN_
संपूर्णाः च शितैः बाणैः तूणाः च शुभ दर्शनाः || ४-३-१७जीवित अन्तकरैः घोरैः ज्वलद्भिः इव पन्नगैः |_END
BEGIN_
"Full with hazardous, life terminating, fiery snake like sharp arrows are these quivers, admirable in 
their appearance... [4-3-17b, 18a]_END

B_4_C_1_26
BEGIN_
विमिश्रा विहगाः पुंभिः आत्म व्यूह अभिनन्दिताः |भृङ्गराज प्रमुदिताः सौमित्रे मधुर स्वराः || ४-१-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Well mingled are these female birds with their male ones, for which they are well admired by their 
own flock, oh! Soumitri, and such birds are calling gladsomely together with the pleasing humming of 
king-bees... [4-1-27]_END

B_4_C_2_19
BEGIN_
दीर्घ बाहू विशालाक्षौ शर चाप असि धारिणौ |कस्य न स्यात् भयम् दृष्ट्वा हि एतौ सुर सुत उपमौ || ४-२-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Lengthy are their arms, broad are their eyes and they are the wielders of arrows, bows and swords... 
and on seeing them, to whom there will be no scare? These two are like the sons of some divinity..." 
Sugreeva thus spoke to Hanuma. [4-2-20]_END

B_4_C_4_2
BEGIN_
ततः परम संहृष्टः हनुमान् प्लवगोत्तमः |
प्रति उवाच ततो वाक्यम् रामम् वाक्य विशारदः || ४-४-३_END
BEGIN_
Then Hanuma, the ablest flyer is thus very gladdened...and in turn then spoke to
that very learned one, namely Rama. [4- 4-3]_END

B_4_C_3_13
BEGIN_
महा प्रमाणौ विपुलौ तप्त हाटक भूषणौ || ४-३-१८खड्गौ एतौ विराजेते निर्मुक्त भुजगौ इव |_END
BEGIN_
"Dazzling are these amply wide, broad and gilded swords like the snakes just released from their moults... 
[4-3-18b, 19a]_END

B_4_C_1_27
BEGIN_
अस्याः कूले प्रमुदिताः सन्घशः शकुनास्त्विह |दात्यूहरति विक्रन्दैः पुंस्कोकिल रुतैः अपि | ४-१-२८
स्वनन्ति पादपाः च इमे माम् अनङ्ग प्रदीपकाः |_END
BEGIN_
"At the shore of this Lake Pampa rejoicing are these birds in groups, and these trees loaded with the 
mating sounds of gallinule birds, and even loaded the callings of the male black cuckoos, are while 
inciting me they are inspiring love in me... [4-1-28, 29a]_END

B_4_C_2_20
BEGIN_
वालि प्रणिहितौ एव शन्के अहम् पुरुषोत्तमौ |राजानो बहु मित्राः च विश्वासो न अत्र हि क्षमः || ४-२-२१_END
BEGIN_
"I presume these two... those best of men are abetted by Vali to assault me... for, the kings like Vali 
do have many friends and trusting them absolutely is an unpardonable mistake... [4-2-21]_END

B_4_C_4_3
BEGIN_
किम् अर्थम् त्वम् वनम् घोरम् पम्पा कानन मण्डितम् |
आगतः सानुजो दुर्गम् नाना व्याल मृग आयुतम् || ४-४-४_END
BEGIN_
"What for you have come into these perilous forests hemming in Pampa Lake along with
your brother, for these are impenetrable forests abounding with many a serpent and animal?" Thus
Hanuma asked Rama. [4-4-4]_END

B_4_C_3_14
BEGIN_
एवम् माम् परिभाषन्तम् कस्माद् वै न अभि भाषतः || ४-३-१९सुग्रीवो नाम धर्मात्मा कश्चित् वानर पुंगवः 
|वीरो विनिकृतो भ्रात्रा जगत् भ्रमति दुःखितः || ४-३-२०_END
BEGIN_
"When I have been talking to you this way, what for you don't speak up... one named Sugreeva, somebody 
virtuous and worthily one among monkeys is expelled by his brother Vali, and he is roaming all over 
the world sorrowfully... [4-3-19b, 20]_END

B_4_C_1_28
BEGIN_
अशोक स्तबक अङ्गारः षट्पद स्वन निस्वनः || ४-१-२९माम् हि पल्लव ताम्रार्चिः वसन्ताग्निः प्रधक्ष्यति 
|_END
BEGIN_
"The fire called spring season will burn me down with its fiery paraphernalia like the clusters of red 
flowers of hellebore that are akin to fireballs, the humming of honeybees that is alike the rustle of 
campfires, and the coppery red colour of tender leaves just sprouted that is identical to burning fire... 
[4-1-29b, 30a]_END

B_4_C_2_21
BEGIN_
अरयः च मनुष्येण विज्ञेयाः छद्म चारिणः |विश्वस्तानाम् अविश्वस्ताः छिद्रेषु प्रहरन्ति अपि || ४-२-२२_END
BEGIN_
"By men the enemies are to be assessed... for, they move in disguise and distrustful enemies will trounce 
the complacently self-assured ones that relax in their own self-confidence on any possible occasion... 
[4-2-22]_END

B_4_C_4_4
BEGIN_
तस्य तद् वचनम् श्रुत्वा लक्ष्मणो राम चोदितः |
आचचक्षे महात्मानम् रामम् दशरथात्मजम् || ४-४-५_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of Hanuma, Lakshmana motivated by Rama, narrated about the
great soul Rama, the son of Dasharatha. [4-4-5]_END

B_4_C_3_15
BEGIN_
प्राप्तः अहम् प्रेषितः तेन सुग्रीवेण महात्मना |राज्ञा वानर मुख्यानाम् हनुमान् नाम वानरः || ४-३-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Delegated by that great soul and the king of important monkeys Sugreeva, I have come here and by name 
I am Hanuma, another Vanara... [4-3-21]_END

B_4_C_1_29
BEGIN_
न हि ताम् सूक्ष्मपक्ष्माक्षीम् सुकेशीम् मृदु भाषिणीम् || ४-१-३०अपश्यतो मे सौउमित्रे जीवितेऽस्ति 
प्रयोजनम् |_END
BEGIN_
"And if she with slender eyelids on her eyes, decent hairdo, and a soft spoken one, Oh! Soumitri, if 
she is unseen by me will there be any purposefulness of my life? [4-1-30b, 31a]_END

B_4_C_2_22
BEGIN_
कृत्येषु वाली मेधावी राजानो बहु दर्शनः |भवन्ति पर हन्तारः ते ज्ञेयाः प्राकृतैः नरैः || ४-२-२३_END
BEGIN_
"In exploits Vali is an ingenious one... and the kings will be observing many aspects of their enemies 
to eliminate them... and they the kings are to be known even by ordinary people... [4- 2- 23]_END

B_4_C_4_5
BEGIN_
राजा दशरथो नाम द्युतिमान् धर्म वत्सलः |
चातुर् वर्ण्यम् स्व धर्मेण नित्यम् एव अभिपालयन् || ४-४-६_END
BEGIN_
"The king named Dasharatha, a resplendent one and the patron of virtue was ruling
the four-caste system with its, and by his own rectitude, for he is also bound within that
four-caste system... [4-4-6]_END

B_4_C_3_16
BEGIN_
युवाभ्याम् स हि धर्मात्मा सुग्रीवः सख्यम् इच्छति |तस्य माम् सचिवम् वित्तम् वानरम् पवनात्मजम् || 
४-३-२२भिक्षु रूप प्रति च्छन्नम् सुग्रीव प्रिय कारणात् |ऋश्यमूकात् इह प्राप्तम् कामगम् कामचारिणम् 
|| ४-३-२३_END
BEGIN_
"He that righteous Sugreeva is desiring friendship with you two, and know me as a monkey and his minister, 
the son of Air-god... I had to come here from Mt. Rishyamuka in an ascetic's form only to appease that 
Sugreeva, and I can wend my way by my will, and wear any guise as I wish..." Hanuma said so to those 
brothers. [4-3-22, 23]_END

B_4_C_1_30
BEGIN_
अयम् हि रुचिरः तस्याः कालो रुचिर काननः || ४-१-३१कोकिलाकुल सीमान्तः दयिताया मम अनघः |_END
BEGIN_
"My dear Seetha has an enchantment for these enchanting woodlands bustling with koels up to their horizons, 
and Lakshmana, similarly enchanting is this vernal season to her... [4-1-31b, 32a]_END

B_4_C_2_23
BEGIN_
तौ त्वया प्राकृतेन एव गत्वा ज्ञेयौ प्लवंगम |इङ्गितानाम् प्रकारैः च रूपव्या भाषणेन च || ४-२-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Begone to them oh, monkey Hanuma, in a commoner's form, for your monkey-hood is distinguishable by 
Vali's agents, and know the intentions of those two by their conduct, by their semblance, and by their 
conversation, as well...[4-2-24]_END

B_4_C_4_6
BEGIN_
न द्वेष्टा विद्यते तस्य स तु द्वेष्टि न कंचन |
स तु सर्वेषु भूतेषु पितामह इव अपरः || ४-४-७_END
BEGIN_

B_4_C_5_0
BEGIN_
ऋश्यमूकात् तु हनुमान् गत्वा तम् मलयम् गिरिम् |आचचक्षे तदा वीरौ कपि राजाय राघवौ || ४-५-१_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma on going from Mt. Rishyamuka to Mt. Malaya, has reported to the king of monkeys Sugreeva, about

B_4_C_1_31
BEGIN_
मन्मध आयास संभूतो वसन्त गुण वर्धितः || ४-१-३२अयम् माम् धक्ष्यति क्षिप्रम् शोकाग्निः न चिरादिव |_END
BEGIN_
"This fire of grief born out of the throes of love, and furthered by the attributes of spring season 
will swiftly burn me down in no time... [4-1-32]_END

B_4_C_3_17
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा तु हनुमाम् तौ वीरौ राम लक्ष्मणौ |वाक्यज्ञो वाक्य कुशलः पुनः न उवाच किंचन || ४-३-२४_END
BEGIN_
Saying thus to those valorous Rama and Lakshmana, Hanumaan, the sententious wordsmith, spoke nothing 
further. [4-3-24]_END

B_4_C_2_24
BEGIN_
लक्षयस्व तयोः भावम् प्रहृष्ट मनसौ यदि |विश्वासयन् प्रशंसाभिः इङ्गितैः च पुनः पुनः || ४-२-२५मम 
एव अभिमुखम् स्थित्वा पृच्छ त्वम् हरि पुंगव |प्रयोजनम् प्रवेशस्य वनस्य अस्य धनुर् धरौ || ४-२-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Aim at their concepts and if they are pleasant-hearted, duly create confidence in them by conducting 
yourself, and also commending them again and again... oh, best of monkeys, Hanuma, set their face towards 
me alone in a compassionate manner, and you inquire about the reason of their entering this forest alone... 
of those bows wielders... [4-2-25, 26]_END

B_4_C_4_7
BEGIN_
अग्निष्टोमादिभिः यज्ञैः इष्टवान् आप्त दक्षिणैः |
तस्य अयम् पूर्वजः पुत्रो रामो नाम जनैः श्रुतः || ४-४-८_END
BEGIN_
"And he, King Dasharatha who performed rituals agniSToma and the like Vedic rituals
wherein he donated liberally, and this one is his eldest son, and he is renowned among people by
the name of Rama... [4-4-8]_END

B_4_C_5_1

Rama arrived along with his brother Lakshmana... [4-5-2]_END

B_4_C_1_32
BEGIN_
अपश्यत ताम् वनिताम् पश्यतो रुचिर द्रुमान् || ४-१-३३मम अयम् आत्मप्रभवो भूयस्त्वम् उपयास्यति |_END
BEGIN_
"As the one unable to see that lady but able to see beautiful trees the Love-god in me gains intensity... 
[4-1-33b, 34a]_END

B_4_C_3_18
BEGIN_
एतत् श्रुत्वा वचः तस्य रामो लक्ष्मणम् अब्रवीत् |प्रहृष्ट वदनः श्रीमान् भ्रातरम् पार्श्वतः स्थितम् 
|| ४-३-२५_END
BEGIN_
Hearing all those words said by Hanuma, that illustrious Rama is well pleased facially, spoke to his 
brother Lakshmana who is standing at his side. [4-3-25]_END

B_4_C_2_25
BEGIN_
शुद्ध आत्मानौ यदि एतौ जानीहि त्वम् प्लवंगम |व्याभाषितैः वा रूपैः वा विज्ञेया दुष्टता अनयोः || ४-२-२७_END
BEGIN_
"You shall know whether those two are clean at heart or otherwise, or about their evil-mindedness or 
otherwise by conversation..." Thus Sugreeva said to Hanuma. [4-2-27]_END

B_4_C_4_8
BEGIN_
शरण्यः सर्व भूतानाम् पितुः निर्देश पारगः |
ज्येष्टो दशरथस्य अयम् पुत्राणाम् गुणवत्तरः || ४-४-९
राज लक्षण संयुक्तः संयुक्तो राज्य सम्पदा ||
राजात् भ्रष्टो मया वस्तुम् वने सार्धम् इह आगतः || ४-४-१०_END
BEGIN_
"He is the protector of all beings and the follower of father's directives, he is
the eldest one among the sons of King Dasharatha... possessor of high virtues, qualities and royal
fortune befitting to a king... but he is deprived of his kingdom, and came hither to dwell in the
forests... nevertheless, followed by me...[4-4-9, 10]_END

B_4_C_5_2
BEGIN_
इक्ष्वाकूणाम् कुले जातो रामो दशरथात्मजः |धर्मे निगदितः च एव पितुर् निर्देश कारकः || ४-५-३_END
BEGIN_
"Rama is the son of king Dasharatha, one born in Ikshvaku dynasty, an adept one in virtue and thus an 
adherent of his father's orders... [4-5-3]_END

B_4_C_1_33
BEGIN_
अदृश्यमाना वैदेही शोकम् वर्धयती इह मे || ४-१-३४दृश्यमानो वसन्तः च स्वेद संसर्ग दूषकः |_END
BEGIN_
"Now, that invisible Seetha is intensifying my agony, and this visible spring season, the remover of 
the touch of sweat too, is doing the same... [4-1-34b, 35a]_END

B_4_C_3_19
BEGIN_
सचिवो अयम् कपीन्द्रस्य सुग्रीवस्य महात्मनः |तम् एव काङ्क्षमाणस्य मम अन्तिकम् इह आगतः || ४-३-२६_END
BEGIN_
"He is the minister of that noteworthy soul and king of monkeys, Sugreeva... whom alone I cherish, but 
he himself has drew nigh of me, on his own... [4-3-26]_END

B_4_C_2_26
BEGIN_
इति एवम् कपिराजेन संदिष्टो मारुतात्मजः |चकार गमने बुद्धिम् यत्र तौ राम लक्ष्मणौ || ४-२-२८_END
BEGIN_
Thus this way ordered by Sugreeva, the king of monkeys, Hanuma, the son of Air-god made up his mind 
to go there, where Rama and Lakshmana are. [4-2-28]_END

B_4_C_4_9
BEGIN_
भार्यया च महाभाग सीतया अनुगतो वशी |
दिन क्षये महातेजाः प्रभ एव दिवाकरः || ४-४-११_END
BEGIN_
"With his wife Seetha following him, oh, highly fortunate Hanuma, this
self-controlled and highly resplendent Rama came to forests like the Sun followed by his consort
Prabha, who vanishes when the day is abated..._END

B_4_C_5_3
BEGIN_
राजसूय अश्वमेधैः च वह्निः येन अभितर्पितः |दक्षिणाः च तथा उत्सृष्टा गावः शत सहस्रशः || ४-५-४तपसा 
सत्य वाक्येन वसुधा येन पालिता |स्त्री हेतोः तस्य पुत्रोऽयम् रामः अरणयम् समागतः || ४-५-५_END
BEGIN_
"By whom the ritual fire is well worshipped in Vedic rituals like rajasuuya, ashvametha, and thus cows 
in hundreds and thousands are donated in those rituals, by whom this earth is ruled devoutly and truthful 
to his word, such Dasharatha's son is this Rama, who has to come to forests owing to a woman... [4-5-4, 
5]_END

B_4_C_1_34
BEGIN_
माम् हि सा मृगशाबाक्षी चिन्ता शोक बलात्कृतम् || ४-१-३५संतापयति सौमित्रे कृइरः चैत्र वनानिलः |_END
BEGIN_
"Overwhelmed with the grief of worry about that deer eyed Seetha, such as I am, I am burnt down by this 
cruel vernal breeze of forests...[4-1-35b, 36a]_END

B_4_C_3_20
BEGIN_
तम् अभ्यभाष सौमित्रे सुग्रीव सचिवम् कपिम् |वाक्यज्ञम् मधुरैः वाक्यैः स्नेह युक्तम् अरिन्दम || ४-३-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Soumitri, with this minister of Sugreeva, the knower of sententiousness and a pleasant worded one, 
and one with friendliness you exchange pleasantries with that enemy destroyer Hanuma... [4-3-27]_END

B_4_C_2_27
BEGIN_
तथा इति संपूज्य वचः तु तस्यकपेः सुभीतस्य दुरासदस्य |महानुभावो हनुमान् ययौ तदास यत्र रामो 
अतिबली स लक्ष्मणः || ४-२-२९_END
BEGIN_
That marvellous monkey Hanuma agreeing for the words of that inaccessible and very much frightened Sugreeva, 
and on respectfully replying him saying that, 'I will do accordingly...' proceeded there where that 
highly mighty Rama is there along with Lakshmana. [4-2-29]_END

B_4_C_4_10
BEGIN_
अहम् अस्य अवरः भ्राता गुणैः दास्यम् उपागतः |
कृतज्ञस्य बहुज्ञस्य लक्ष्मणो नाम नामतः || ४-४०-१२_END
BEGIN_
"I am the one who obtained servitude by the justness of this faithful and
knowledgeable one, and his younger brother, by name I am named as Lakshmana... [4-4-12]_END

B_4_C_5_4
BEGIN_
तस्य अस्य वसतो अरण्ये नियतस्य महात्मनः |रावणेन हृता भार्या स त्वाम् शरणम् आगतः || ४-५-६_END
BEGIN_
"Ravana stole the wife of this principled one and great soul Rama when dwelling in forests, such as 
he is, he came seeking your refuge... [4-5-6]_END

B_4_C_1_35
BEGIN_
अमी मयूराः शोभन्ते प्रनृत्यन्तः ततः ततः || ४-१-३६स्त्वैः पक्षैः पवन उद्धूतैः गवाक्षैः स्फाटिकैः 
इव |_END
BEGIN_
"And these peacocks that dance here and there are shining forth with crystal like windows on their plumage, 
when up-shoved by the wind...[4-1-36b, 37a]_END

B_4_C_3_21
BEGIN_
न अन् ऋग्वेद विनीतस्य न अ\-\-यजुर्वेद धारिणः |न अ\-\-साम वेद विदुषः शक्यम् एवम् विभाषितुम् || ४-३-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Nay...the non-knower of Rig Veda, or the non-rememberer of Yajur Veda, or the non-scholar of Saama 
Veda... can possibly, or truly speak this way... [4-3-28]_END

B_4_C_4_11
BEGIN_
सुखार्हस्य महार्हस्य सर्वभूत हितात्मनः |
ऐश्वर्येण विहीनस्य वनवासे रतस्य च || ४-४-१३
रक्षस अपहृता भार्या रहिते काम रूपिणा |
तत् च न ज्ञायते रक्षः पत्नी येन अस्य वा हृता || ४-४-१४_END
BEGIN_
"He who aspires to keep up the well-being of all the beings, and he who is merited
for all comforts and respectability is now devoid of his prosperity and predisposed to forest
dwelling... such as he is, his wife is abducted by a guise changing demon in a lonely place, of
whom we know not... we know not which demon stole his wife... [4-4-13, 14]_END

B_4_C_6_0
BEGIN_
पुनरेव अब्रवीत् प्रीतः राघवम् रघुनन्दनम् |
अयम् आख्याति ते राम सेवकः मन्त्रि सत्तमः || ४-६-१
हनुमान् यन् निमित्तम् त्वम् निर्जनम् वनम् आगतः |
लक्ष्मणेन सह भ्रात्रा वसतः च वने तव ||४-६-२
रक्षसा अपहृता भार्या मैथिली जनक आत्मजा |
त्वया वियुक्ता रुदती लक्ष्मणेन च धीमता || ४-६-३_END
BEGIN_
Then Sugreeva who is gladdened again spoke to Rama of Raghu's dynasty, "My best
minister and this servant of yours Hanuma informed me of the reason for which you have come to
uninhabited forests along with your brother Lakshmana, and that while living in the forest, and
when you and this courageous Lakshmana are not her alongside a demon stole your wife Maithili, the
daughter of Janaka, wailing as she was. [4-6-3]_END

B_4_C_5_5
BEGIN_
भवता सख्य कामौ तौ भ्रातरौ राम लक्ष्मणौ |प्रगृह्य च अर्चयस्व एतौ पूजनीयतमौ उभौ || ४-५-७_END
BEGIN_
"These two brothers Rama and Lakshmana, are interested to make friendship with you... thus you receive 
these two and worship them, for they are most venerable ones..." Hanuma thus advised Sugreeva. [4-5-7]_END

B_4_C_1_36
BEGIN_
शिखिनीभिः परिवृतास्त एते मद मूर्छिताः || ४-१-३७मन्मथ अभिपरीतस्य मम मन्मथ वर्धनाः |_END
BEGIN_
"Those peacocks that are surorounded by their peahens and convulsed in love are intensifying longing 
in me, who am already muffled in love-longing... [4-1-37b, 38a]_END

B_4_C_3_22
BEGIN_
नूनम् व्यकरणम् कृत्स्नम् अनेन बहुधा श्रुतम् |बहु व्याहरता अनेन न किंचित् अप शब्दितम् || ४-३-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Definitely grammar is severally and comprehensively learnt by him... and though much is said by him 
not a single word has gone amiss of verbiage... [4-3-29]_END

B_4_C_4_12
BEGIN_
दनुः नाम दितेः पुत्रः शापात् राक्षसताम् गतः |
आख्यातः तेन सुग्रीवः समर्थो वानराधिपः || ४-४-१५
स ज्ञास्यति महावीर्यः तव भार्या अपहारिणम् |
एवम् उक्त्वा दनुः स्वर्गम् भ्राजमानो दिवम् गतः || ४-४-१६_END
BEGIN_
"One named Danu, son of Diti, who acquired demon-hood by curse had said that
Sugreeva, the chief of monkeys, is a capable one, and he even said, "that great valorous Sugreeva
can know about the abductor of your wife..." saying thus that Danu is released from the curse of
his demon-hood, moved skyward and went away to heavens while becoming self-luminous... [4-4-15,
16]_END

B_4_C_6_1
BEGIN_
अन्तरम् प्रेप्सुना तेन हत्वा गृध्रम् जटायुषम् |
भार्या वियोगजम् दुःखम् प्रापितः तेन रक्ष्सा || ४-६-४_END
BEGIN_
"And he also said about that arch demon's killing an eagle named Jatayu on waiting
for an opportunity, and his causing an agony in you by way of separating your wife. [4-6-4]_END

B_4_C_5_6
BEGIN_
श्रुत्वा हनुमतो वाक्यम् सुग्रीवो वानर अधिपः |दर्शनीयतमो भूत्वा प्रीत्या उवाच राघवम् || ४-५-८_END
BEGIN_
On hearing Hanuma's words Sugreeva, the chief of monkeys has become presentable and gladly spoke to 
Rama. [4-5-8]_END

B_4_C_1_37
BEGIN_

BEGIN_
"See Lakshmana, on that mountain terrace this peahen longing for love is dancing at the nearby of her 
husband, that peacock... [4-1-38b, 39a]_END

B_4_C_3_23
BEGIN_
न मुखे नेत्रयोः च अपि ललाटे च भ्रुवोः तथा |अन्येषु अपि च सर्वेषु दोषः संविदितः क्वचित् || ४-३-३०_END
BEGIN_

B_4_C_4_13
BEGIN_

BEGIN_
"All this is informed to you, as it is as you have asked..Myself and Rama, we now

B_4_C_6_2
BEGIN_
भर्या वियोगजम् दुःखम् न चिरात् त्वम् विमोक्ष्यसे |
अहम् ताम् आनयिष्यामि नष्टाम् वेदश्रुतीम् इव || ४-६-५_END
BEGIN_
"Before long you will get rid off your agony caused by the separation of wife, for I
will fetch her very soon, like the retrieval Vedic Scriptures. [4-6-5]_END

B_4_C_5_7
BEGIN_
भवान् धर्म विनीतः च सुतपाः सर्व वत्सलः |आख्याता वायुपुत्रेण तत्त्वतो मे भवद् गुणाः || ४-५-९_END
BEGIN_
"You are a trained one in treading righteous path, best by your scruples, and a kindlier one to all, 
so said Air-god's son Hanuma to me about your attributes, in subtlety... [4-5-9]_END

B_4_C_1_38

BEGIN_

B_4_C_6_3
BEGIN_

BEGIN_
"Oh! Enemy destroyer, Rama, I will fetch your wife to give her to you whether she is
in netherworlds or even in empyrean worlds. [4-6-6]_END

B_4_C_5_8
BEGIN_

a best achievement to me alone... [4-5-10]_END

B_4_C_1_39
BEGIN_

BEGIN_

B_4_C_3_25

BEGIN_

B_4_C_4_15
BEGIN_
सीता यस्य स्नुषा च आसीत् शरण्यो धर्मवत्सलः |

BEGIN_

daughter-in-law, such a shelterer's son Rama is now taking shelter under Sugreeva... [4-4-19]_END

B_4_C_6_4
BEGIN_
इदम् तथ्यम् मम वचः त्वम् अवेहि च राघव |
न शक्या सा जरयितुम् अपि सः इन्द्रैः सुर असुरैः || ४-६-७
तव भार्या महाबाहो भक्ष्यम् विष कृतम् यथा |_END
BEGIN_
"You may know that this word of mine is definite oh, Raghava. Your wife is as good
as an indigestible foodstuff made with poison, indigestive even to Indra, put together with all
gods and demons. [4-6-7, 8a]_END

B_4_C_5_9
BEGIN_
रोचते यदि मे सख्यम् बाहुः एष प्रसारितः |गृह्यताम् पाणिना पाणिः मर्यादा बध्यताम् ध्रुवा || ४-५-११_END
BEGIN_
"If you aspire my friendship here I extend my arm, take this hand of mine into yours, thus let the convention 
be stably made fast..." Thus Sugreeva proffered friendship to Rama. [4-5-11]_END

B_4_C_1_40
BEGIN_
मम त्वयम् विना वासः पुष्पमासे सुदुःसहः || ४-१-४१पश्य लक्ष्मण संरागः तिर्यक् योनिगतेषु अपि |यदेषा 
शिखिनी कामात् भर्तारम् अभिवर्तते || ४-१-४२_END
BEGIN_
"Living in this flowering month is unbearable for me... Lakshmana, see the fondness even in those originated 
in animals, thus that peahen in her passion is following her husband... [4-1-41b, 42]_END

B_4_C_3_26



B_4_C_4_16
BEGIN_
सर्व लोकस्य धर्मात्मा शरण्यः शरणम् पुरा |
गुरुर् मे राघवः सोऽयम् सुग्रीवम् शरणम् गतः || ४-४-२०_END
BEGIN_
"He who is a virtuous one and protector of all the world, and who is the only refuge
for all in earlier times... such a Raaghava, my mentor, is now seeking refuge with Sugreeva...
[4-4-20]_END

B_4_C_6_5
BEGIN_
त्यज शोकम् महाबाहो ताम् कान्ताम् आनयामि ते | ४-६-८
अनुमानात् तु जानामि मैथिली सा न संशयः |
ह्रियमाणा मया दृष्टा रक्षसा रौउद्र कर्मणा || ४-६-९
क्रोशन्ती राम रामेति लक्ष्मणेति च विस्वरम् |
स्फुरन्ती रावणस्य अन्के पन्नगेन्द्र वधूः यथा || ४-६-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Give-up your lamentation, oh, great-shouldered one, for I will bring back that lady
for you. And by inference I know her... undoubtedly I have seen Maithilee while that demon with
cruel deeds was abducting her... then she was crying piteously calling 'Rama, Rama...' and also
calling 'Lakshmana...' and she was writhing in the flanks of Ravana like the wife of serpent's
lord... [4-6-8b, 9, 10]_END

B_4_C_5_10
BEGIN_
एतत् तु वचनम् श्रुत्वा सुग्रीवस्य सुभाषितम् |संप्रहृष्ट मना हस्तम् पीडयामास पाणिना || ४-५-१२
हृष्टः सौहृदम् आलम्ब्य पर्यष्वजत पीडितम् |_END
BEGIN_
Rama is gladdened at heart on listening all those words well said by Sugreeva, and then clutched Sugreeva's 
hand in his, and ardently abiding by the vow of friendship he embraced Sugreeva, grippingly and happily. 
[4-5-12, 13a]_END

B_4_C_1_41
BEGIN_
माम् अपि एवम् विशालाक्षी जानकी जात संभ्रमा |मदनेन अभिवर्तेत यदि न अपहृता भवेत् || ४-१-४३_END
BEGIN_
"Had she, that broad eyed lady Seetha, not been abducted, she too would have followed me in this way 
with an ecstatic love... [4-1-43]_END

B_4_C_3_27

BEGIN_
"He has orderly refinement in speech that is remarkable and un-delaying, and he speaks propitious words 
that are heart-pleasing...[4-3-32]_END

B_4_C_4_17

"By whose beneficence all these people are always delighted, he that Rama is now

B_4_C_6_6
BEGIN_

BEGIN_
"Myself being the fifth one on the cliff of the mountain, on seeing me she dropped
the upper cloth of her sari along with auspicious jewellery. [4-6-11]_END

B_4_C_5_11
BEGIN_
ततो हनूमान् संत्यज्य भिक्षु रूपम् अरिन्दमः || ४-५-१३काष्ठयोः स्वेन रूपेण जनयामास पावकम् |दीप्यमानम् 
ततो वह्निम् पुष्पैः अभ्यर्च्य सत्कृतम् || ४-५-१४तयोर् मध्ये तु सुप्रीतो निदधौ सुसमाहितः |_END
BEGIN_
Then the destroyer of enemies Hanuma discarding the guise of ascetic assumed his original monkey form, 
and on producing fire with two sticks then made it to glow. decorated, worshipped with flowers, then 
gladly and devoutly placed that fire in between Rama and Sugreeva. [4-5-13b,14,15a]_END

B_4_C_1_42
BEGIN_
पश्य लक्ष्मण पुष्पाणि निष्फलानि भवन्ति मे |पुष्प भार समृद्धानाम् वनानाम् शिशिरात्यये || ४-१-४४_END
BEGIN_
"See Lakshmana, while these forests are abundantly weighty with flowers in wintry season these flowers 
are becoming futile to me... [4-1-44]_END

B_4_C_3_28



B_4_C_4_18
BEGIN_
येन सर्व गुणोपेताः पृथिव्याम् सर्व पार्थिवाः |
मानिताः सततम् राज्ञा सदा दशरथेन वै || ४-४-२२
तस्य अयम् पूर्वजः पुत्रः त्रिषु लोकेषु विश्रुतः |
सुग्रीवम् वानरेन्द्रम् तु रामः शरणम् आगतः || ४-४-२३_END
BEGIN_
"By which kingDasharatha, are all the kings with all possible good attributes are
always, and at all the times were esteemed to be safeguarded as defensible kings, such king's
eldest son Rama, renowned in all the three worlds for his own sheltering the needy, has now taken
shelter under monkeys lord Sugreeva... [4-4-22, 23]_END

B_4_C_6_7
BEGIN_
तानि अस्माभिः गृहीतानि निहितानि च राघव |
आनयिष्यामि अहम् तानि प्रत्यभिज्ञातुम् अर्हसि || ४-६-१२_END
BEGIN_

B_4_C_7_0
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु सुग्रीवः रामेण आर्तेन वानरः |
अब्रवीत् प्राञ्जलिः वाक्यम् सबाष्पम् बाष्प गद्गदः || ४-७-१_END
BEGIN_
Thus said by Rama in agony that monkey Sugreeva with his palms adjoined, and with
tears rolling in eyes and also voice trembling with tears said this to Rama. [4-7-1]_END

B_4_C_5_12
BEGIN_

B_4_C_1_43

BEGIN_
"His speech is generated in three places is enthralling... and whose heart is it that is disenchanted,

B_4_C_4_19
BEGIN_

BEGIN_
Thus Hanuman on speaking melodious words with politeness, also said to Raghava as,
"good, we may now approach Sugreeva...." [4-4-29]_END

BEGIN_

BEGIN_
The more he hugged those best decorative ornaments close to his heart, the more he
hissed like a wrathful serpent in a snake pit. [4-6-18]_END

B_4_C_3_35
BEGIN_
तत् तस्य वाक्यम् निपुणम् निशम्यप्रहृष्ट रूपः पवनात्मजः कपिः |मनः समाधाय जय उपपत्तौसख्यम् 
तदा कर्तुम् इयेष ताभ्याम् || ४-३-३९_END
BEGIN_
On observing that operative sentence of Lakshmana the monkey Hanuma is gladdened, as seen from his composure, 
and kept his mind at ease at the prospective victory, and then he wished to materialise the pact of 
friendship between Rama ad Sugreeva, at the earliest. [4-3-39]_END

B_4_C_4_30
BEGIN_

B_4_C_7_13
BEGIN_
हितम् वयस्य भावेन ब्रूमि न उपदिशामि ते |
वयस्यताम् पूजयन् मे न त्वम् शोचितुम् अर्हसि || ४-७-१४_END
BEGIN_
"I am telling a benefiting and friendly thought, but not instructing you, should you
regard my friendship then your saddening is inapt..." [Thus said Sugreeva to Rama.] [4-7-14]_END

B_4_C_6_20
BEGIN_
हरता मैथिलीम् येन माम् च रोषयता ध्रुवम् |
आत्मनो जीवित अन्ताय मृत्यु द्वारम् अपावृतम् || ४-६-२६_END
BEGIN_
"By whom Maithili is abducted and thus caused indignation in me, he has opened up
the doors of his death suicidally. [4-6-26]_END

B_4_C_8_6
BEGIN_
रजतम् वा सुवर्णम् वा शुभानि आभरणानि च |
अविभक्तानि साधूनाम् अवगच्छन्ति साधवः || ४-८-७_END
BEGIN_
"Gentle souls will be knowing that silver or gold, or even prosperous ornaments are
not to be apportioned among themselves as this is mine and that is yours. [4-8-7]_END

B_4_C_9_2
BEGIN_
राज्यम् प्रशासतः तस्य पितृ पैतामहम् महत् |
अहम् सर्वेषु कालेषु प्रणतः प्रेष्यवत् स्थितः || ४-९-३_END
BEGIN_
While he was ruling the great kingdom of my father and forefathers, I have always
bowed down to him like a servant and stood by him. [4-9-3]_END

B_4_C_5_25
BEGIN_
स तु तद् वचनम् श्रुत्वा राघवस्य आत्मनोहितम् |सुग्रीवः परम प्रीतः परमम् वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् ||४-५-२९_END
BEGIN_
On hearing Raghava's words that are appeasing for his self, Sugreeva is very completely satisfied and 
said this fine sentence. [4-5-29b, c]_END

B_4_C_1_56
BEGIN_
विक्षिप्ताम् पवनेन एताम् असौ तिलक मञ्जरीम् |षट्पदः सहसा अभ्येति मद उद्धूताम् इव प्रियाम् || ४-१-५८_END
BEGIN_
"That honeybee is quickly reaching these red flowers bouquets of Tilaka that are like his loved ones 
that are raising their faces with vigour�[4-1-58]_END

B_4_C_7_14
BEGIN_
मधुरम् सान्त्वितः तेन सुग्रीवेण स राघवः |
मुखम् अश्रु परि क्लिन्नम् वस्त्र अन्तेन प्रमार्जयत् || ४-७-१५_END
BEGIN_
Sweetly solaced thus by that Sugreeva Rama dabbed his face with the edge of cloth,
which is covered fully with tears. [4-7-15]_END

B_4_C_6_21
BEGIN_
मम दयित तमा हृता वनात् रजनिचरेण विमथ्य येन सा |
कथय मम रिपुम् तम् अद्य वै प्लवगपते यम सन्निधिम् नयामि || ४-६-२७_END
BEGIN_
" Oh, king of the fly-jumpers, tell me which demon forcibly stole her, my dearest
one than all, by molesting her in the forest, tell me about that enemy of mine, for sure I will
lead him to the fore of Death today itself... [4-6-27]_END

B_4_C_8_7
BEGIN_
आढ्यो वा अपि दरिद्रो वा दुःखितः सुखितोऽपि वा |
निर्दोषः च सदोषः च वयस्यः परमा गतिः || ४-८-८_END
BEGIN_
"May he be rich or poor, saddened or gladdened, flawless or flawed, a friend is the
ultimate recourse to any. [4-8-8]_END

B_4_C_5_26
BEGIN_
तव प्रसादेन नृसिंह वीरप्रियाम् च राज्यम् च समाप्नुयाम् अहम् |तथा कुरु त्वम् नर देव वैरिणम्
यथा न हिंस्यत् स पुनर् मम अग्रजम् || ४-५-३०_END
BEGIN_
"By your grace, oh, lion among men, let me regain my wife and kingdom too... oh, god of humans, as to 
how he does not suffer me again, thus you may please make happen... let not my elder brother turned 
as an enemy of mine suffer me again... [4-5-30]_END

B_4_C_9_3
BEGIN_
मायावी नाम तेजस्वी पूर्वजो दुन्दुभेः सुतः |
तेन तस्य महद् वैरम् वालिनः स्त्री कृतम् पुरा || ४-९-४_END
BEGIN_
There was a fierce demon named Maayaavi, the elder brother of Dundubhi and the son
of one demon named Maya. There was a great enmity between this Maayaavi and Vali owing to some
female. [4-9-4]_END

B_4_C_1_57
BEGIN_
कामिनाम् अयम् अत्यन्तम् अशोकः शोक वर्धनः |स्तबकैः पवन उत्क्षिप्तैः तर्जयन् इव माम् स्थितः || ४-१-५९_END
BEGIN_
"To the impassioned ones that Ashoka tree is very much enhancing grief, and with its bouquets of flowers 
hustled up by the wind it is sanding as though to daunt me... [4-1-59]_END

B_4_C_7_15
BEGIN_
प्रकृतिः स्थः तु काकुत्स्थः सुग्रीव वचनात् प्रभुः |
संपरिष्वज्य सुग्रीवम् इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् || ४-७-१६_END
BEGIN_
Lord Rama steadied himself in his own nature by the words of Sugreeva, and on
embracing him Rama said this sentence to him. [4-7-16]_END

B_4_C_8_8
BEGIN_
धन त्यागः सुख त्यागो देश त्यागोऽपि वा अनघः |
वयस्यार्थे प्रवर्तन्ते स्नेहम् दृष्ट्वा तथा विधम् || ४-८-९_END
BEGIN_
"On observing the course of friendship and knowing which is true friendship, the
true friends do not hesitate to extend wealth, pleasure or even their own country for the sake of
friendship." Sugreeva thus extolled Rama and his friendship. [4-8-9]_END

B_4_C_5_27
BEGIN_
सीत कपीन्द्र क्षणदा चराणाम्राजीव हेम ज्वलनोपमानानि |सुग्रीव राम प्रणय पसङ्गेवामानि नेत्राणि 
समम् स्फुरन्ति || ४-५-३१_END
BEGIN_
During the friendly conversation of Rama and Sugreeva, the left eyes of Seetha, Vali and Ravana that 
bear similitude with lotuses, golden orbs, and fireballs respectively have fluttered equally. [4-5-31]_END

B_4_C_9_4
BEGIN_
स तु सुप्ते जने रात्रौ किष्किन्धा द्वारम् आगतः |
नर्दति स्म सुसम्रब्धो वालिनम् च आह्वयत् रणे || ४-९-५_END
BEGIN_
He that Maayaavi arrived at the doors of Kishkindha in a night when the people are
sleeping, and blared very much inviting Vali for a fight. [4-9-5]_END

B_4_C_1_58
BEGIN_
अमी लक्ष्मण दृश्यन्ते चूताः कुसुम शालिनः |विभ्रम उत्सिक्त मनसः स अङ्गरागा नरा इव || ४-१-६०_END
BEGIN_
" Lakshmana, these mango trees bearing greenish yellow flower are appearing like men whose hearts are 
flirtatiously aroused, and who have creamed their bodies with greenish-yellow body cream� [4-1-60]_END

B_4_C_7_16
BEGIN_
कर्तव्यम् यत् वयस्येन स्निग्धेन च हितेन च |
अनुरूपम् च युक्तम् च कृतम् सुग्रीव तत् त्वया || ४-७-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Sugreeva, a friendly obligation that which is to be done, a benefiting, befitting
and a timely one too, is what you have performed with your friendly advise... [4-7-17]_END

B_4_C_8_9
BEGIN_
तत् तथा इति अब्रवीत् रामः सुग्रीवम् प्रिय दर्शनम् |
लक्ष्मणस्य अग्रतः लक्ष्म्या वासवस्य इव धीमतः || ४-८-१०_END
BEGIN_
"That is thus only," said Rama before Lakshmana, which Lakshmana is sagacious,
resplendent and who vies with Indra, about what is said by Sugreeva, which Sugreeva is by now
soft-natured in his looks, doffing off his jittery look. [4-8-10]_END

B_4_C_9_5
BEGIN_
प्रसुप्तः तु मम भ्राता नर्दितो भैरव स्वनम् |
श्रुत्वा न ममृषे वाली निष्पपात जवात् तदा || ४-९-६_END
BEGIN_
Then my brother who was also sleeping well, on hearing that bellowing in a
clamouring voice, did not tolerate and came out speedily. [4-9-6]_END

B_4_C_1_59
BEGIN_
सौमित्रे पश्य पम्पायाः चित्रासु वन राजिषु |किंनरा नरशार्दूल विचरन्ति ततः ततः || ४-१-६१_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, tigerly man Soumitri, see these Pampa's amazing forests ranges... and therein the nymphs are moving, 
hither and yon... [4-1-61]_END

B_4_C_7_17
BEGIN_
एष च प्रकृतिः स्थः अहम् अनुनीतः त्वया सखे |
दुर्लभो हि ईदृशो बन्धुः अस्मिन् काले विशेषतः || ४-७-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, friend, I steadied myself in my own nature when implored by you... it is
impossible to get this kind of friend, especially at these times... [4-7-18]_END

B_4_C_8_10
BEGIN_
ततो रामम् स्थितम् दृष्ट्वा लक्ष्मणम् च महाबलम् |
सुग्रीवः सर्वतः चक्षुः वने लोलम् अपातयत् || ४-८-११_END
BEGIN_
Then on seeing Rama standing there with greatly mighty Lakshmana, Sugreeva cast his
sight with his bolting eyes around that forest. [4-8-11]_END

B_4_C_9_6
BEGIN_
स तु वै निःसृतः क्रोधात् तम् हन्तुम् असुरोत्तमम् |
वार्यमाणः ततः स्त्रीभिः मया च प्रणत आत्मना || ४-९-७_END
BEGIN_
Though the females and myself bowed reverently to prevent Vali, he came out of
palace in all his anger to kill that great demon. [4-9-7]_END

B_4_C_1_60
BEGIN_
इमानि शुभ गन्धीनि पश्य लक्ष्मण सर्वशः |नलिनानि प्रकाशन्ते जले तरुण सूर्य वत् || ४-१-६२_END
BEGIN_
"See Lakshmana, these fragrant and propitious blue lotuses are everywhere in the waters, glistening 
like tender sun... [4-1-62]_END

B_4_C_7_18
BEGIN_
किम् तु यत्नः त्वया कार्यो मैथिल्याः परिमार्गणे |
राक्षसस्य च रौद्रस्य रावणस्य दुरात्मनः || ४-७-१९_END
BEGIN_
"But, trying to search for Maithili and that furious, evil-minded demon Ravana, is
your endeavour... [4-7-19]_END

B_4_C_9_7
BEGIN_
स तु निर्धूय सर्वान् नो निर्जगाम महाबलः |
ततः अहम् अपि सौहार्दान् निःसृतः वालिना सह || ४-९-८_END
BEGIN_
But Vali spurned all of us away and forged ahead, and then I also have started to go
along with Vali in all my predisposition. [4-9-8]_END

B_4_C_8_11
BEGIN_
स ददर्श ततः सालम् अविदूरे हरीश्वरः |
सुपुष्पम् ईषत् पत्र आढ्यम् भ्रमरैः उपशोभितम् || ४-८-१२_END
BEGIN_
He that lord of monkeys Sugreeva has then seen a well flowered sala tree not far off
from there, covered with some leaves and bedecked with honeybees. [4-8-12]_END

B_4_C_1_61
BEGIN_
एषा प्रसन्न सलिला पद्म नील उत्पलायुता |हंस कारण्डव आकीर्णा पम्पा सौगन्धिका युता || ४-१-६३_END
BEGIN_
"This Pampa Lake is shining forth with its tranquil waters, that contain lotuses, blue water-lily's, 
and red lotuses, along with swans and water-birds that permeate it � [4-1-63]_END

B_4_C_7_19
BEGIN_
मया च यद् अनुष्ठेयम् विस्रब्धेन तत् उच्यताम् |
वर्षासु इव च सुक्षेत्रे सर्वम् संपद्यते तव || ४-७-२०_END
BEGIN_
"What is to done by me that be said in all believability, and all your endeavour
will reap like the crops planted during rainy season in good lands... [4-7-20]_END

B_4_C_9_8
BEGIN_
स तु मे भ्रातरम् दृष्ट्वा माम् च दूरात् अवस्थितम् |
असुरो जात संत्रासः प्रदुद्राव तदा भृशम् || ४-९-९_END
BEGIN_
A great fear was induced in that demon on seeing my brother and me too coming from a
distance, and then he quickly ran away. [4-9-9]_END

B_4_C_8_12
BEGIN_
तस्य एकाम् पर्ण बहुलाम् शाखाम् भंक्त्वा सुशोभिताम् |
रामस्य आस्तीर्य सुग्रीवो निषसाद स राघवः || ४-८-१३_END
BEGIN_
And Sugreeva broke off one branch of that sala tree that is with many leaves and a
well charming one, and spreading it out for Rama, he sat on it with Raghava. [4-8-13]_END

B_4_C_1_62
BEGIN_
जले तरुण सूर्याभैः षट्पद आहत केसरैः |पन्कजैः शोभते पम्पा समन्तात् अभिसंवृता || ४-१-६४_END
BEGIN_
"Lotuses with the resplendence of tender sun enwrapping its waters, pollen grain pilfered by honeybees 
enwrapping those lotuses� with them this Pampa is beaming forth�_END

B_4_C_7_20
BEGIN_
मया च यदिदम् वाक्यम् अभिमानात् समीरितम् |
तत् त्वया हरिशार्दूल तत् त्वम् इति उपधार्यताम् || ४-७-२१_END
BEGIN_
"What that is spoken by me is in my self-confidence but not in any self-conceit, oh,
tigerly-monkey, deem them as doubtless facts... [4-7-21]_END

B_4_C_9_9
BEGIN_
तस्मिन् द्रवति संत्रस्ते हि आवाम् द्रुततरम् गतौ |
प्रकाशः अपि कृतः मार्गः चन्द्रेण उद्गच्छता तदा || ४-९-१०_END
BEGIN_
While he is running away in fear we quickly followed him on a path that is barely
lit by moonlight of the moon who is just coming up. [4-9-10]_END

B_4_C_8_13
BEGIN_
तौ आसीनौ ततः दृष्ट्वा हनूमान् अपि लक्ष्मणम् |
साल शाखाम् समुत्पाट्य विनीतम् उपवेशयत् || ४-८-१४_END
BEGIN_
On seeing those two sitting on a branch then Hanuma also broke a branch of sala tree
for the modest Lakshmana and seated Lakshmana on it. [4-8-14]_END

B_4_C_1_63
BEGIN_
चक्रवाक युता नित्यम् चित्र प्रस्थ वनान्तरा |मातंग मृग यूथैः च शोभते सलिल अर्थिभिः || ४-१-६५_END
BEGIN_
"This Pampa is always bedecked with the ruddy geese, amazing deep areas of the forest, and with water 
thirsty herds of elephants and deer, and with them it gleams forth... [4-1-65]_END

B_4_C_7_21
BEGIN_
अनृतम् न उक्त पूर्वम् मे न च वक्ष्ये कदाचन |
एतत् ते प्रतिजानामि सत्येन एव शपामि अहम् || ४-७-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Untruth is not uttered by me earlier nor will be at anytime from now, and all this
I am promising you taking oath on that truthfulness alone.. [4-7-22]_END

B_4_C_9_10
BEGIN_
स तृणैः आवृतम् दुर्गम् धरण्या विवरम् महत् |
प्रविवेश असुरः वेगात् आवाम् आसाद्य विष्ठितौ || ४-९-११_END
BEGIN_
That demon speedily entered an un-enterable cavity under the ground, covered with
grass, and we too having reached there speedily stood at the aperture of that cavity for a while.
[4-9-11]_END

B_4_C_8_14
BEGIN_
सुख उपविष्टम् रामम् तु प्रसन्नम् उदधिम् यथा |
साल पुष्पाव संकीर्णे तस्मिन् गिरिवर उत्तमे || ४-८-१५
ततः प्रहृष्टः सुग्रीवः श्लक्ष्णया शुभया गिरा |
उवाच प्रणयाद् रामम् हर्ष व्याकुलित अक्षरम् || ४-८-१६_END
BEGIN_
Then to him, who by now is comfortably sitting on a flowery mat laid by the bestrewn
flowers of sala trees on that best mountain like a quiet ocean, to such Rama who by his very
presence delights hearts, that gladsome Sugreeva said this in friendship with his gentle and
gracious words that fluttered with happiness while he spoke. [4-8-15, 16]_END

B_4_C_1_64
BEGIN_
पवन आहत वेगाभिः ऊर्मिभिः विमले अंभसि |पन्कजानि विराजन्ते ताड्यमानानि लक्ष्मण || ४-१-६६_END
BEGIN_
"In the tranquil water the speed of wind is throbbing ripples, and the ripples throb the lotuses, thus 
the throbbing and rippling lotuses appear beautiful� [4-1-66]_END

B_4_C_7_22
BEGIN_
ततः प्रहृष्टः सुग्रीवः वानरैः सचिवैः सह |
राघवस्य वचः श्रुत्वा प्रतिज्ञातम् विशेषतः || ४-७-२३_END
BEGIN_
Then on hearing the words of Rama Sugreeva along with his monkey ministers is
gladdened, especially of Rama promise. [4-7-23]_END

B_4_C_9_11
BEGIN_
तम् प्रविष्टम् रिपुम् दृष्ट्वा बिलम् रोष वशम् गतः |
माम् उवाच ततो वाली वचनम् क्षुभित इन्द्रियः || ४-९-१२_END
BEGIN_
Then Vali has gone into the enfoldment of fury on observing the entry of that demon
into the hole, whereby his senses felt outraged, and he said this sentence to me. [4-9-12]_END

B_4_C_8_15
BEGIN_
अहम् विनिकृतो भ्रात्रा चरामि एष भयार्दितः |
ऋष्यमूकम् गिरि वरम् हृत भार्यः सुदुःखितः || ४-८-१७_END
BEGIN_
"My brother calumniated me and stole my wife, with his fear and my anguish haunting
me I am moving about this best mountain Rishyamuka. [4-8-17]_END

B_4_C_1_65
BEGIN_
पद्म पत्र विशालाक्षीम् सततम् प्रिय पन्कजाम् |अपश्यतो मे वैदेहीम् जीवितम् न अभिरोचते || ४-१-६७_END
BEGIN_
"That one with lotus-petal-like broad eyes, who always holds the lotuses dear...without finding that 
Vaidehi... to me my life is uninteresting... [4-1-67]_END

B_4_C_7_23
BEGIN_
एवम् एकान्त संपृक्तौ ततः तौ नर वानरौ |
उभौ अन्योन्य सदृशम् सुख दुःखम् अभाष्ताम् || ४-७-२४_END
BEGIN_
Then those two, the man and the monkey, met in privacy and both discussed in a
mutually befitting manner about their pleasures and pains. [4-7-24]_END

B_4_C_8_16
BEGIN_
सोऽहम् त्रस्तः भये मग्नः वने संब्रान्त चेतनः |
वालिना निकृतः भ्रात्रा कृत वैरः च राघव || ४-८-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Affronted by my brother, oh, Raghava, I am made as his enemy, such as I am, I am
living on with a scared and dazed vitality far flung in fear. [4-8-18]_END

B_4_C_9_12
BEGIN_
इह तिष्ठ अद्य सुग्रीव बिल द्वारि समाहितः |
यावत् अत्र प्रविश्य अहम् निहन्मि समरे रिपुम् || ४-९-१३_END
BEGIN_
Then Vali said to me, "Now you stay here on the alert, Sugreeva, at the entrance of
this hole till I return on destroying the enemy in a fight on my entering this hole..."
[4-9-13]_END

B_4_C_1_66
BEGIN_
अहो कामस्य वामत्वम् यो गताम् अपि दुर्लभाम् |स्मारयिष्यति कल्याणीम् कल्याण तर वादिनीम् || ४-१-६८_END
BEGIN_
"Aha! Deplorable is the deviousness of Love-god, for he is causing reminisces about that graceful lady 
who articulates that gracefully, even if she is gone away and cannot be regained now... [4-1-68]_END

B_4_C_7_24
BEGIN_
महानुभावस्य वचो निशम्य
हरिर् नृपाणाम् अधिपस्य तस्य |
कृतम् स मेने हरिवीर मुख्यः
तदा च कार्यम् हृदयेन विद्वान् || ४-७-२५_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the word of that intellectual, highly capable one and the best king among
kings, namely Rama, he that Sugreeva, the chief among the monkey heroes, thought at heart that his
manoeuvre to surpass his dominant brother Vali is accomplished. [4-7-25]_END

B_4_C_8_17
BEGIN_
वालिनः मे भय आर्तस्य सर्वलोक अभयंकर |
मम अपि त्वम् अनाथस्य प्रसादम् कर्तुम् अर्हसि || ४-८-१९_END
BEGIN_
"I am agonized by the fear from Vali, oh, protector of all the worlds, you protect
me too for I am unprotected, and able are you to accord protection." Thus Sugreeva appealed to
Rama. [4-8-19]_END

B_4_C_9_13
BEGIN_
मया तु एतत् वचः श्रुत्वा याचितः स परंतपः |
शापयित्वा च माम् पद्भ्याम् प्रविवेश बिलम् ततः || ४-९-१४_END
BEGIN_
On hearing those words I requested him to allow me too to come in to the hole, but
he being the great tormentor of his enemies disallowed it, and he made me to swear on his feet and
entered that hole. [4-9-15]_END

B_4_C_10_0
BEGIN_
ततः क्रोध समाविष्टम् सम्रब्धम् तम् उपागतम् |
अहम् प्रसादयान् चक्रे भ्रातरम् हित काम्यया || ४-१०-१_END
BEGIN_
"Then desiring both of our well-being I have begged of my brother who is enveloped
in anger and behaving capriciously. [4-10-1]_END

B_4_C_1_67
BEGIN_
शक्यो धारयितुम् कामो भवेत् अभ्यागतो मया |यदि भूयो वसन्तो माम् न हन्यात् पुष्पित द्रुमः || ४-१-६९_END
BEGIN_
"If this spring with its flowered trees is not going to deaden me... the Love-god is a possible one 
to tolerate, though now he came upon me forcefully...[4-1-69]_END

B_4_C_8_18
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु तेजस्वी धर्मज्ञो धर्म वत्सलः |
प्रत्युवाच स काकुत्स्थः सुग्रीवम् प्रहसन् इव || ४-८-२०_END
BEGIN_
Thus said by Sugreeva, the resplendent and virtuous Rama, the patron of
righteousness replied Sugreeva as though laughing off the task. [4-8-20]_END

B_4_C_9_14
BEGIN_
तस्य प्रविष्टस्य बिलम् साग्रः संवत्सरः गतः |
स्थितस्य च बिल द्वारि सः कालः व्यत्यवर्तत || ४-९-१५_END
BEGIN_
Well over a year is over after his entering into that cleavage, and to me too who
stayed at the entrance of the cleavage that much time had passed away. [4-9-15]_END

B_4_C_10_1
BEGIN_
दिष्ट्या असि कुशली प्राप्तो निहतः च त्वया रिपुः |
अनाथस्य हि मे नाथः त्वम् एको अनाथ नन्दनः || ४-१०-२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, orphan's, delight Rama, I addressed him like this, "Luckily you have eliminated
the enemy and returned safely, and to an orphaned one like me you alone are the protector.
[4-10-2]_END

B_4_C_1_68
BEGIN_
यानि स्म रमणीयानि तया सह भवन्ति मे |तानि एव अरमणीयानि जायन्ते मे तया विना || ४-१-७०_END
BEGIN_
"All those places or objects that were delightful ones to me when she was with me, and they alone are 
now becoming anguishing ones to me...for she parted from me� [4-1-70]_END

B_4_C_8_19
BEGIN_
उपकार फलम् मित्रम् अपकारो अरि लक्षणम् |
अद्य एव तम् वधिष्यामि तव भार्या अपहारिणम् || ४-८-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Helping is the fruit of friendship while harming is enemy's trait, hence I wish to
kill him today only, that abductor of your wife..." Rama continued thus. [4-8-21]_END

B_4_C_9_15
BEGIN_
अहम् तु नष्टम् तम् ज्ञात्वा स्नेहात् आगत संभ्रमः |
भ्रातरम् न प्रपश्यामि पाप शङ्कि च मे मनः || ४-९-१६_END
BEGIN_
I thought I lost him for my brother is unseen, and in all fondness towards him my
mind started to doubt about some harm might have befallen on him. [4-9-16]_END

B_4_C_10_2
BEGIN_
इदम् बहु शलाकम् ते पूर्ण चन्द्रम् इव उदितम् |
छत्रम् स वाल व्यजनम् प्रतीच्छस्व मया धृतम् || ४-१०-३_END
BEGIN_
Let this regal umbrella unfolded like a full moon, with its many of its spikes, and
with accompanying fur-fans may please be accepted while I hold it for you. [4-10-3]_END

B_4_C_1_69
BEGIN_
पद्मकोश पलाशानि द्रष्टुम् दृष्टिः हि मन्यते |सीताया नेत्र कोशाभ्याम् सदृशान् इति लक्ष्मण || ४-१-७१_END
BEGIN_
"To gaze the petals of the lotus buds my sight is fascinated... and in them I perceive the pair of Seetha's 
bud-like eyes...Oh! Lakshmana...and they are alike thus... [4-1-71]_END

B_4_C_8_20
BEGIN_
इमे हि मे महाभाग पत्रिणः तिग्म तेजसः |
कार्तिकेय वन उद्भूताः शरा हेम विभूषिताः || ४-८-२२
कन्क पत्र परिच्छन्ना महेन्द्र अशनि सन्निभाः |
सुपर्वाणः सुतीक्ष्ण अग्रा सरोषा भुजगा इव || ४-८-२३_END
BEGIN_
"These are my arrows winged from pinion of the hern, oh, highly fortunate Sugreeva,
these that are decorated in gold sparkle sharply like the Thunderbolts of Indra, and they are
begotten from the reed forest of Kartikeya, ends tied with eagles feathers for fins, smooth are
their nodes, sharp are their tips that pierce sharply, and these will be like enraged snakes.
[4-8-22, 23]_END

B_4_C_10_3
BEGIN_
आर्तस्य अथ बिला द्वारि स्थितः संवत्सरम् नृप |
दृष्ट्वा च शोणितम् द्वारि बिलात् च अपि समुत्थितम् || ४-१०-४
शोक संविग्न हृदयो भृशम् व्याकुलित इन्द्रियः |
अपिधाय बिल द्वारम् शैल शृङ्गेण तत् तदा || ४-१०-५
तस्मात् देशात् अपाक्रम्य किष्किन्धाम् प्राविशम् पुनः |_END
BEGIN_
"Saddened I was after staying at the entrance of the cave for one year, oh, king,
and on seeing the blood that started to flow from out the cave in the entrance my heart is engulfed
in sadness and my senses perturbed very much, and then covering that cave's entrance with a
hilltop, and departing from that country, I re-entered Kishkindha. [4-10-4, 5, 6a]_END

B_4_C_9_16
BEGIN_
अथ दीर्घस्य कालस्य बिलात् तस्मात् विनिःसृतम् |
सः फेनम् रुधिरम् दृष्ट्वा ततो अहम् भृशदुःखितः || ४-९-१७_END
BEGIN_
After a long time blood with foam gushed out that hole, and on seeing it I was
deeply saddened. [4-9-17]_END

B_4_C_1_70
BEGIN_
पद्म केसर संसृष्टो वृक्षान्तर विनिःसृतः |निःश्वास इव सीताया वाति वायुः मनोहरः || ४-१-७२_END
BEGIN_
"This breeze� let out from within the thickets of forests, breezing touching the pollen of lotuses, 
is reminding Seetha's exhale, as such it is heart-stealing� [4-1-72]_END

B_4_C_8_21
BEGIN_
वालि सज्ञम् अमित्रम् ते भ्रातरम् कृत किल्बिषम् |
शरैः विनिहतम् पश्य विकीर्णम् इव पर्वतम् || ४-८-२४_END
BEGIN_
"You may see your malicious and intimidating brother, someone denotative by name
Vali, eradicated with these very arrows and splintered down like a mountain." Rama said so to
Sugreeva. [4-8-24]_END

B_4_C_10_4
BEGIN_
विषादात् इह माम् दृष्ट्वा पौरैः मंत्रिभिर् एव च || ४-१०-६
अभिषिक्तो न कामेन तन्मे क्षन्तुम् त्वम् अर्हसि |_END
BEGIN_
"On seeing me returning with grief, the citizens and ministers alike crowned me, but
that is not at my desire, therefore it is apt of you pardon me. [4-10-6b, 7a]_END

B_4_C_9_17
BEGIN_
नर्दताम् असुराणाम् च ध्वनिः मे श्रोत्रम् आगतः |
न रस्तस्य च संग्रामे क्रोशतो अपि स्वनो गुरोः || ४-९-१८_END
BEGIN_
Sounds of screaming demon came to my ear, but the screeches of my brother who is
involved in fight are unheard, in the least. [4-9-18]_END

B_4_C_1_71
BEGIN_
सौमित्रे पश्य पम्पाया दक्षिणे गिरि सानुषु |पुष्पितान् कर्णिकारस्य यष्टिम् परम शोभिताम् || ४-१-७३_END
BEGIN_
"Soumitri, see those flowered Karnikara trees with their tree-trunks on those southern hill-terraces 
of Pampa, they are highly splendorous... [4-1-73]_END

B_4_C_8_22
BEGIN_
राघवस्य वचः श्रुत्वा सुग्रीवो वाहिनी पतिः |
प्रहर्षम् अतुलम् लेभे साधु साध्विति च अब्रवीत् || ४-८-२५_END
BEGIN_
On hearing Raghava's words, the lord of monkey-force Sugreeva attained much
happiness and said, 'good, good...' [4-8-25]_END

B_4_C_10_5
BEGIN_
त्वम् एव राजा मानार्हः सदा च अहम् यथा पुरा || ४-१०-७
राजभावे नियोगः अयम् मम त्वत् विरहात् कृतः |
स अमात्य पौर नगरम् स्थितम् निहत कण्टकम् || ४-१०-८_END
BEGIN_
"As an estimable one you alone are the king, and I will be as I was, and
establishing me in kingship is owing to your unavailability, but the capital with citizens and
ministers is kept up without thorniness. [4-10-7b, 8]_END

B_4_C_9_18
BEGIN_
अहम् तु अवगतः बुद्ध्या चिह्नैः तैः भ्रातरम् हतम् |
पिधाय च बिल द्वारम् शिलया गिरि मात्रया || ४-९-१९
शोकार्तः च उदकम् कृत्वा किष्किन्धाम् आगतः सखे |
गूहमानस्य मे तत्त्वम् यत्नतः मंत्रिभिः श्रुतम् ||४-९-२०_END
BEGIN_
Oh, friend, Rama... I have surmised and concluded in mind by the indications that my
brother is finished, and covered the cavity's opening with a mountain similar boulder, and
performed water oblations to my deceased brother with saddening pain, and then returned to
Kishkindha. But the ministers have persuaded and heard from me the actual happening though I was
concealing it. [4-9-19, 20]_END

B_4_C_1_72
BEGIN_
अधिकम् शैल राजोऽयम् धातुभिः तु विभूषितः |विचित्रम् सृजते रेणुम् वायु वेग विघट्टितम् || ४-१-७४_END
BEGIN_
"That one, that kingly mountain which is ornamentally impregnated with ores and minerals is exhausting 
much mass of wondrous dust with the colour of its ores, that is drifted by the wind's speed... [4-1-74]_END

B_4_C_8_23
BEGIN_
राम शोक अभिभूतो अहम् शोक आर्तानाम् भवान् गतिः |
वयस्य इति कृत्वा हि त्वयि अहम् परिदेवये || ४-८-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Rama, I am confounded in sadness, and for those lamenting sadly you are the only
recourse, and because you have befriended me I am opening up my woes before you. [4-8-26]_END

B_4_C_10_6
BEGIN_
न्यास भूतम् इदम् राज्यम् तव निर्यातयामि अहम् |
मा च रोषम् कृथाः सौम्य मम शत्रु निषूदन|| ४-१०-९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, gentle one, I am now returning this custodial kingdom to you, oh, enemy
eliminator, you need not be hostile towards me. [4-10-9]_END

B_4_C_9_19
BEGIN_
ततः अहम् तैः समागम्य समेतैः अभिषेचितः |
राज्यम् प्रशासतः तस्य न्यायतो मम राघव || ४-९-२१
आजगाम रिपुम् हत्वा दानवम् स तु वानरः |_END
BEGIN_
Then duly summoned by all of those ministers I was crowned, and while I was ruling
the kingdom judiciously, oh, Raghava, that semi-human Vali returned on killing that demoniac enemy.
[4-9-21, 22a]_END

B_4_C_1_73
BEGIN_
गिरि प्रस्थास्तु सौमित्रे सर्वतः संप्रपुष्पितैः |निष्पत्रैः सर्वतो रम्यैः प्रदीप्ता इव किंशुकैः 
|| ४-१-७५_END
BEGIN_
"On the mountainsides, Soumitri, all over fully flowered are the exquisite Kimshuka trees, while their 
leaves are hidden under those reddish flowers, and with them that mountain is as though aglow... [4-1-75]_END

B_4_C_8_24
BEGIN_
त्वम् हि पाणि प्रदानेन वयस्यो मे अग्नि साक्षिकम् |
कृतः प्राणैः बहुमतः सत्येन च शपामि अहम् || ४-८-२७_END
BEGIN_
"By extending a helping hand and befriending me while sacred fire bore witness, you
have indeed become my dearest friend on par with my life, and hence I take promise on truth to
broach. [4-8-27]_END

B_4_C_10_7
BEGIN_
याचे त्वाम् शिरसा राजन् मया बद्धो अयम् अंजलिः |
बलात् अस्मिन् समागम्य मंत्रिभिः पुर वासिभिः || ४-१०-१०
राजभावे नियुक्तो अहम् शून्य देश जिगीषया |_END
BEGIN_
"I beg you with my bowed head and with my prayerful palm-fold, the ministers and the
city dwellers have collectively and forcibly nominated me to the kingship, only to keep the
kingless kingdom under control. [4-10-10, 11a]_END

B_4_C_9_20
BEGIN_
अभिषिक्तम् तु माम् दृष्ट्वा कोपात् संरक्त लोचनः || ४-९-२२
मदीयान् मंत्रिणः बद्ध्वा परुषम् वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_
But on seeing me crowned his eyes were reddened in anger, and he arrested all my
ministers as he spoke rudely. [4-9-22b, 23a]_END

B_4_C_1_74
BEGIN_
पम्पा तीर रुहाः च इमे संसक्ता मधु गन्धिनः |मालती मल्लिका पद्म करवीराः च पुष्पिताः || ४-१-७६_END
BEGIN_
"On the banks of Pampa these jasmines, water-lilies, red oleanders have grown up and they are now flowered 
that is wetted with the fragrance of nectar...[4-1-76]_END

B_4_C_8_25
BEGIN_
वयस्य इति कृत्वा च विस्रब्धः प्रवदामि अहम् |
दुःखम् अन्तर्गतम् तन् मे मनो हरति नित्यशः || ४-८-२८_END
BEGIN_
"By befriending you I am able to say clearly about my internal sorrow without any
hitches and hold-ups, which is always rending my heart..." So said Sugreeva to Rama. [4-8-28]_END

B_4_C_10_8
BEGIN_
स्निग्धम् एवम् ब्रुवाणम् माम् स विनिर्भर्त्स्य वानरः || ४-१०-११
धिक् त्वाम् इति च माम् उक्त्वा बहु तत् तत् उवाच ह |_END
BEGIN_
"While I was speaking that politely he threatened me and indeed used many expletives
starting from 'fie, fie, upon you.' and the like. [4-10-11b, 12a]_END

B_4_C_9_21
BEGIN_
निग्रहे च समर्थस्य तम् पापम् प्रति राघव || ४-९-२३
न प्रावर्तत मे बुद्धिः भ्रातृ गौरव यंत्रिता |_END
BEGIN_
And oh, Raghava, though I was capable enough to counter him, my reason was
controlled by my esteem to brotherhood, and I was indisposed to commit that sin of defying
brotherhood. [4-9-23b, 24a]_END

B_4_C_1_75
BEGIN_
केतक्यः सिन्धुवाराः च वासन्त्यः च सुपुष्पिताः |माधव्यो गन्धपूर्णाः च कुंदगुल्माः च सर्वशः || ४-१-७७_END
BEGIN_
"The Mogra bushes, Sinduka, Vaasanti are well flowered. Maadhavi, flowers are also fully fragrant, and 
everywhere there are bushes of Jasmine... [4-1-77]_END

B_4_C_8_26
BEGIN_
एतावत् उक्त्वा वचनम् बाष्प दूषित लोचनः |
बाष्प दूषितया वाचा न उच्चैः श्क्नोति भाषितुम् || ४-८-२९_END
BEGIN_
Sugreeva said this much sentence with tears abusing his eyes and his voice is unable
talk aloud since it is equally abused by tears. [4-8-29]_END

B_4_C_10_9
BEGIN_
प्रकृतीः च समानीय मंत्रिणः चैव सम्मतान् || ४-१०-१२
माम् आह सुहृदाम् मध्ये वाक्यम् परम गर्हितम् |_END
BEGIN_
"And summoning people and venerable ministers he hurled very abusive words at me
among friends. [4-10-12b, 13a]_END

B_4_C_9_22
BEGIN_
हत्वा शत्रुम् सः मे भ्राता प्रविवेश पुरम् तदा || ४-९-२४
मानयन् तम् महात्मानम् यथावत् च अभिअवादयम् |
उक्ताः च न आशिषः तेन संतुष्टेन अन्तरात्मना || ४-९-२५_END
BEGIN_
He that brother of mine entered the capital thus on destroying the enemy, and I
hailed him as usual while respecting that audacious soul, but his inner self is unsatisfied and I
remained unblest. [4-9-24b, 25]_END

B_4_C_1_76
BEGIN_
चिरिबिल्वा मधूकाः च वञ्जुला वकुलाः तथा |चम्पकाः तिलकाः च एव नागवृक्षाः च पुष्पिताः || ४-१-७८_END
BEGIN_
"Charming are the saplings of Bilva, and Madhooka, and plants like Vakula, Champaka, Tilaka, Naaga trees 
are well flowered.... [4-1-78]_END

B_4_C_8_27
BEGIN_
बाष्प वेगम् तु सहसा नदी वेगम् इव आगतम् |
धारयामास धैर्येण सुग्रीवः राम संनिधौ || ४-८-३०_END
BEGIN_
Sugreeva courageously controlled the sudden haste of tears that came up hastily and
suddenly like a river in the presence of Rama. [4-8-30]_END

B_4_C_10_10
BEGIN_
विदितम् वो मया रात्रौ मायावी स महाअसुरः || ४-१०-१३
माम् समाह्वयत क्रुद्धो युद्ध कांक्षी तदा पुरा |_END
BEGIN_
"You all are aware that earlier the gigantic and rancorous demon Maayaavi invited me
desiring a duel in that night. [4-10-13b, 14a]_END

B_4_C_9_23
BEGIN_
नत्वा पादौ अहम् तस्य मुकुटेन अस्पृशम् प्रभो |
अपि वाली मम क्रोधात् न प्रसादम् चकार सः || ४-९-२६_END
BEGIN_
Oh, lord Rama, though I bowed with the crown touching his feet, he that rancorous
Vali showed no quarter towards me." So said Sugreeva to Rama. [4-9-25]_END

B_4_C_11_0
BEGIN_
रामस्य वचनम् श्रुत्वा हर्ष पौरुष वर्धनम् |
सुग्रीवः पूजयाम् चक्रे राघवम् प्रशशंस च || ४-११-१_END
BEGIN_
Sugreeva started to adore and extol Raghava on hearing the words of Rama that are
inculcating happiness and pride. [4-11-1]_END

B_4_C_1_77
BEGIN_
पद्मकाः च एव शोभन्ते नील अशोकाः च पुष्पिताःलोध्राः च गिरि पृष्ठेषु सिंह केसर पिन्जराः || ४-१-७९_END
BEGIN_
"Padmaka plants are well flourishing, and like that Neela, Ashoka are also flowered... trees on the 
mountain terraces namely Lodhra trees are brownish like lion's mane... [4-1-79]_END

B_4_C_8_28
BEGIN_
स निगृह्य तु तम् बाष्पम् प्रमृज्य नयने शुभे |
विनिःश्वस्य च तेजस्वी राघवम् पुनरूचिवान् || ४-८-३१_END
BEGIN_
He that bright Sugreeva controlled those tears, and on wiping his fortunate eyes,
but sighing heavily he again started to speak this sentence to Raghava. [4-8-31]_END

B_4_C_10_11
BEGIN_
तस्य तद् भाषितम् श्रुत्वा निःसृतः अहम् नृपाअलयात् || ४-१०-१४
अनुयातः च माम् तूर्णम् अयम् भ्राता सुदारुणः |_END
BEGIN_
"On hearing his call for a duel I went out of the royal palace, and this very
hazardous brother of mine quickly followed me. [4-10-14b, 15a]_END

B_4_C_11_1
BEGIN_
असंशयम् प्रज्वलितैः तीक्ष्णैर् मर्म अतिगैः शरैः |
त्वम् दहेः कुपितो लोकान् युगान्त इव भास्करः || ४-११-२_END
BEGIN_
"It is doubtless that you will burn down everything when you are angry, like the
blazing sun at the end of era, with these arrows of yours that are highly blazing, incisive and
invaders on stealthy places." Thus Sugreeva started extolling Rama. [4-11-2]_END

B_4_C_1_78
BEGIN_
अन्कोलाः च कुरण्टाः च पूर्णकाः पारिभद्रकाः |चूताः पाटलयः च अपि कोविदाराः च पुष्पिताः || ४-१-८०_END
BEGIN_
"The trees of Alangium, Kurntaka, Poornaka, Devadaaru, and also the Mango trees, and like that Patala 
trees, and the trees of Mountain ebony are flowered...[4-1-80]_END

B_4_C_8_29
BEGIN_
पुरा अहम् वलिना राम राज्यात् स्वात् अवरोपितः |
परुषाणि च संश्राव्य निर्धूतो अस्मि बलीयसा || ४-८-३२_END
BEGIN_
"Earlier he that forceful Vali deposed me from my kingdom, oh Rama, and speaking
harsh words he even banished me. [4-8-32]_END

B_4_C_10_12
BEGIN_
स तु दृष्ट्वा एव माम् रात्रौ स द्वितीयम् महाबलः || ४-१०-१५
प्राद्रवत् भय संत्रस्तो वीक्ष्य आवाम् समुपागतौ |
अभिद्रुतः तु वेगेन विवेश स महाबिलम् || ४-१०-१६_END
BEGIN_
"And that formidable demon Maayaavi ran away as he was fraught with fear on seeing
me with a second one at my side, and he speedily entered a great cavity of earth on seeing us two
nearly reaching him. [4-10-15b, 16]_END

B_4_C_11_2
BEGIN_
वालिनः पौरुषम् यत् तद् यत् च वीर्यम् धृतिः च या |
तन् मम एक मनाः श्रुत्वा विधत्स्व यद् अनन्तरम् || ४-११-३_END
BEGIN_
"That which is impetuousness of Vali, that which is his bravery and courageousness
are there, they may be listened from me single-mindedly, and later you impose that which need be
imposed. [4-11-3]_END

B_4_C_1_79
BEGIN_
मुचुकुंद अर्जुनाः च एव दृश्यन्ते गिरिसानुषुकेतक उद्दालकाः च एव शिरीषाः शिंशुपा धवाः || १-४-८१_END
BEGIN_
"Muchukunda trees, also Arjuna trees are seen on mountain terraces...Date palm trees, Uddaalaka trees 
also... like that the Shiriisha tree, simshupa trees, and dhava trees... [4-1-81]_END

B_4_C_8_30
BEGIN_
हृता भार्या च मे तेन प्राणेभ्यो अपि गरीयसी |
सुहृदः च मदीया ये संयता बन्धनेषु ते || ४-८-३३_END
BEGIN_
"My wife who is loftier than my lives is stolen by him, and those that are my
sympathisers they are also captivated and imprisoned by him. [4-8-33]_END

B_4_C_10_13
BEGIN_
तम् प्रविष्टम् विदित्वा तु सुघोरम् सुमहद् बिलम् |
अयम् उक्तो अथ मे भ्राता मया तु क्रूर दर्शनः || ४-१०-१७_END
BEGIN_
"On knowing the demon's entry into that great precarious cavity, I said to this one,
this cruel looking brother of mine. [4-10-17]_END

B_4_C_11_3
BEGIN_
समुद्रात् पश्चिमात् पूर्वम् दक्षिणाद् अपि च उत्तरम् |
क्रामति अनुदिते सूर्ये वाली व्यपगत क्लमः || ४-११-४_END
BEGIN_
"Before the dawn of sun Vali unweariedly strides from western ocean to eastern, and
even from southern to northern for offering water oblations to the rising sun. [4-11-4]_END

B_4_C_1_80
BEGIN_
शाल्मल्यः किंशुकाः च एव रक्ताः कुरवकाः तथा |तिनिशा नक्तमालाः च चंदनाः स्यंदनाः तथा || १-४-८२_END
BEGIN_
"Silk cotton trees, palaasha trees also, like that are red mehandi trees, thus are Tinisha and Naktamaala 
trees, sandalwood trees, spandana trees are all thus well flowered... [4-1-82]_END

B_4_C_8_31
BEGIN_
यत्नवान् च स दुष्टात्मा मद् विनाशाय राघव |
बहुशः तत् प्रयुक्ताः च वानरा निहता मया || ४-८-३४_END
BEGIN_
"He that very evil minded one tried many times to annihilate me, and Raghava, I
killed those combatants monkeys that are deployed by Vali to kill me. [4-8-34]_END

B_4_C_10_14
BEGIN_
अहत्वा न अस्ति मे शक्तिः प्रति गन्तुम् इतः पुरीम् |
बिल द्वारि प्रतीक्ष त्वम् यावत् एनम् निहन्मि अहम् || ४-१०-१८_END
BEGIN_
"My power will not let me return from here to the capital without killing that
demon, hence you wait at this cavity's entrance, till I kill that demon and come out of the cavity.
[4-10-18]_END

B_4_C_11_4
BEGIN_
अग्राणि आरुह्य शैलानाम् शिखराणि महान्ति अपि |
ऊर्ध्वम् उत्पात्य तरसा प्रति गृह्णाति वीर्यवान् || ४-११-५_END
BEGIN_
"Ascending the heights of mountains and even rending their greatest peaks, that
mighty one volleys them upwards and in turn catches them, as though they are play balls.
[4-11-5]_END

B_4_C_1_81
BEGIN_
हिन्तालः तिलकाः च एव नाग वृक्षाः च पुष्पिताः |पुष्पितान् पुष्पित अग्राभिः लताभिः परिवेष्टितान् || 
४-१-८३_END
BEGIN_
"Flowered are the trees like hintaala, tilaka, and naaga trees, and they are enfolded by the flowered 
climber-plants at their apices... [4-1-83]_END

B_4_C_8_32
BEGIN_
शंकया एतया अहम् च दृष्ट्वा त्वाम् अपि राघव |
न उपसर्पामि अहम् भीतो भये सर्वे हि बिभ्यति || ४-८-३५_END
BEGIN_
"With the same doubt I did not even near you when I saw you... in fear everything
will be fearsome, isn't it... [4-8-35]_END

B_4_C_10_15
BEGIN_
स्थितोऽयम् इति मत्वा अहम् प्रविष्टः तु दुरासदम् |
तम् मे मार्गयतः तत्र गतः संवत्सरः तदा || ४-१०-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Believing that he stayed at the entrance of the cavity I entered that impenetrable
cavity, and then in searching for that demon there one year elapsed. [4-10-19]_END

B_4_C_11_5
BEGIN_
बहवः सारवन्तः च वनेषु विविधा द्रुमाः |
वालिना तरसा भग्ना बलम् प्रथयता आत्मनः || ४-११-६_END
BEGIN_
"As a show his strength Vali used to personally fell many sturdy trees of diverse
origin by his might. [4-11-6]_END

B_4_C_1_82
BEGIN_
द्रुमान् पश्य इह सौमित्रे पम्पाया रुचिरान् बहून् |वात विक्षिप्त विटपान् यथा आसन्नान् द्रुमान् इमान् 
|| ४-१-८४लताः समनुवर्तन्ते मत्ता इव वर स्त्रियः |_END
BEGIN_
"See the splendorous trees of Pampa here, oh! Soumitri...their branches bestirred by wind and bend onto 
other trees, as though these trees are nearby and within the reach of climber-plants... thus the climber-plants 
passionately bear upon those trees, like the doting of passionate women... [ [4-1-84, 85a]_END

B_4_C_8_33
BEGIN_
केवलम् हि सहाया मे हनुमत् प्रमुखास्त्विमे |
अतः अहम् धारयामि अद्य प्राणान् कृच्छ्र गतः अपि सन् || ४-८-३६_END
BEGIN_
"Though I am engulfed in tribulations I still bear my lives even today due to these
important monkeys like Hanuma and others, who are the only helping hands of mine. [4-8-36]_END

B_4_C_10_16
BEGIN_
स तु दृष्टो मया शत्रुः अनिर्वेदात् भयाअवहः |
निहतः च मया सद्यः सः सर्वैः सह बन्धुभिः || ४-१०-२०_END
BEGIN_
