"I have seen that terrified enemy of mine effortlessly, and I killed him immediately
along with all of his relatives. [4-10-20]_END

B_4_C_11_6
BEGIN_
महिषो दुन्दुभिर् नाम कैलास शिखर प्रभः |
बलम् नाग सहस्रस्य धारयामास वीर्यवान् || ४-११-७_END
BEGIN_
"One named Dundubhi was there in the form of a buffalo, whose size shone forth like
Mt. Kailash and who bears the strength of a thousand elephants." Thus Sugreeva started telling
Dundubhi's episode to Rama. [4-11-7]_END

B_4_C_1_83
BEGIN_
पादपात् पादपम् गच्छन् शैलात् शैलम् वनात् वनम् || ४-१-८५वाति न एक रस आस्वाद सम्मोदित इव अनिलः |_END
BEGIN_
"And the breeze is perhaps unhappy by savouring only one kind of nectarine aroma, hence it appears to 
be gliding from tree to tree, forest to forest, mountain to mountain... while going from tree to tree, 
mountain to mountain, forest to forest... [4-1-85b, 86a]_END

B_4_C_8_34
BEGIN_
एते हि कपयः स्निग्धा माम् रक्षन्ति समन्ततः |
सह गच्छन्ति गन्तव्ये नित्यम् तिष्ठन्ति च स्थिते || ४-८-३७_END
BEGIN_
"These are the friendly monkeys guarding me all over, while I go they go along with
me, and if I were to stay they too will stay. [4-8-37]_END

B_4_C_10_17
BEGIN_
तस्य आस्यात् तु प्रवृत्तेन रुधिरौघेण तद् बिलम् |
पूर्णम् आसीत् दुराक्रामम् स्वनतः तस्य भूतले || ४-१०-२१_END
BEGIN_
"That cavity has become impassable, since it is fully filled with the gushes of
blood emanating from the mouth of that demon who fell yelling onto ground. [4-10-21]_END

B_4_C_11_7
BEGIN_
स वीर्य उत्सेक दुष्टात्मा वर दानेन च मोहितः |
जगाम स महाकायः समुद्रम् सरिताम् पतिम् || ४-११-८_END
BEGIN_
"He that evil-minded and colossal bodied Dundubhi was bemused by the vanity of his
own vigour, and by the boon bestowed oo him, and once he went to the lord of rivers, namely the
Ocean. [4-11-8]_END

B_4_C_1_84
BEGIN_
केचित् पर्याप्त कुसुमाः पादपा मधु गन्धिनः || ४-१-८६केचित् मुकुल संवीताः श्याम वर्णा इव आबभुः |_END
BEGIN_
"Some trees are full with flowers whose nectar is fragrant, and some shine forth with dark colour as 
they are enveloped with buds... [4-1-86b, 87a]_END

B_4_C_8_35
BEGIN_
संक्षेपः ते एष मे राम किम् उक्त्वा विस्तरम् हि ते |
स मे ज्येष्ठो रिपुः भ्राता वाली विश्रुत पौरुषः || ३-८-३८_END
BEGIN_
"Rama, this is briefly my sad-story and why tell this very broadly to you as it
would be too tedious... my elder brother Vali is a renowned one for his intrepidity, and he that
Vali alone is my enemy. [4-8-38]_END

B_4_C_10_18
BEGIN_
सूदयित्वा तु तम् शत्रुम् विक्रान्तम् तम् अहम् सुखम् |
निष्क्रामम् न एव पश्यामि बिलस्य पिहितम् मुखम् || ४-१०-२२_END
BEGIN_
"On my killing that invading enemy easily, I could not see any exit from that cavity
as its mouth was closed. [4-10-22]_END

B_4_C_11_8
BEGIN_
ऊर्मिमंतम् अतिक्रम्य सागरम् रत्न संचयम् |
मम युद्धम् प्रयच्छ इति तम् उवाच महार्णवम् || ४-११-९_END
BEGIN_
"Deriding the garner of weaves and gems he said to that vastly ocean "give me a
fight" [4-11-9]_END

B_4_C_1_85
BEGIN_
इदम् मृष्टम् इदम् स्वादु प्रफुल्लम् इदम् इत्यपि || ४-१-८७राग युक्तो मधुकरः कुसुमेषु आवलीयते ||_END
BEGIN_
"And the honeybee on assessing each of the flower as 'this one is pure... this one is delicious... and 
this one is well bloomed...' is plunging into them... [4-1-87b, 88a]_END

B_4_C_8_36
BEGIN_
तद् विनाशे अपि मे दुःखम् प्रमृष्टम् स्यात् अनन्तरम् |
सुखम् मे जीवितम् चैव तद् विनाश निबन्धनम् || ३-८-३९_END
BEGIN_
"His end ends my distress and my later life and quietude are subjected to his
destruction. [4-8-39]_END

B_4_C_10_19
BEGIN_
विक्रोशमानस्य तु मे सुग्रीव इति पुनः पुनः |
यतः प्रतिवचो नास्ति ततः अहम् भृश दुःखितः || ४-१०-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Wherefore I did not get a reply though I repeatedly shouted, 'Sugreeva, oh,
Sugreeva.' thereby I was very saddened. [4-10-23]_END

B_4_C_11_9
BEGIN_
ततः समुद्रो धर्मात्मा समुत्थाय महाबलः |
अब्रवीद् वचनम् राजन् असुरम् काल चोदितम् || ४-११-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Then, oh, Rama, that virtue-minded and very powerful ocean rose up from his tabular
position to heights, and spoke these words to that demon Dundubhi who is driven to doom by his own
time. [4-11-10]_END

B_4_C_1_86
BEGIN_
निलीय पुनर् उत्पत्य सहसा अन्यत्र गच्छति |मधु लुब्धो मधुकरः पंपा तीर द्रुमेषु असौ || ४-१-८८_END
BEGIN_
"On plunging into the flowers that nectar-avaricious honeybee is again coming up, and quickly going 
elsewhere in the trees on the banks of Pampa... [4-1-8]_END

B_4_C_8_37
BEGIN_
एष मे राम शोकान्तः शोक आर्तेन निवेदितः |
दुःखितः सुखितः वा अपि सख्युः नित्यम् सखा गतिः || ३-८-४०_END
BEGIN_
"Grief stricken such as I am, I have submitted as to how my misery ends, whether one
is gladdened or saddened he has recourse only to his friend." So said Sugreeva to Rama.
[4-8-40]_END

B_4_C_10_20
BEGIN_
पाद प्रहारैः तु मया बहुभिः परिपातितम् |
ततः अहम् तेन निष्क्रम्य पथा पुरम् उपागतः || ४-१०-२४_END
BEGIN_
"With my foot I pounded and smashed that lidded hilltop, and from there I exited
that way and arrived here. [4-10-24]_END

B_4_C_11_10
BEGIN_
समर्थो न अस्मि ते दातुम् युद्धम् युद्ध विशारद |
श्रूयताम् त्वम् अभिधास्यामि यत् ते युद्धम् प्रदास्यति || ४-११-११_END
BEGIN_
"I am not capable to give you a fight, oh, war-expert, but I will name him who can
give you a fight, listen." So said ocean to the demon. [4-11-11]_END

B_4_C_1_87
BEGIN_
इयम् कुसुम सन्घातैः उपस्तीर्णा सुखा कृता |स्वयम् निपतितैः भूमिः शयन प्रस्तरैः इव || ४-१-८९_END
BEGIN_
"These clusters of flowers that have fallen on their own are spreading out like a bed of flowers laid 
on, with them the ground appears to endow comfort... [4-1-89]_END

B_4_C_8_38
BEGIN_
श्रुत्वा एतत् च वचः रामः सुग्रीवम् इदम् अब्रवीत् |
किम् निमित्तम् अभूत् वैरम् श्रोतुम् इच्छामि तत्त्वतः || ३-८-४१_END
BEGIN_
Hearing all that is spoken by Sugreeva, Rama asked, "What for chanced the enmity? I
am interested to listen, in its reality...[4-8-41]_END

B_4_C_11_11
BEGIN_
शैल राजो महारण्ये तपस्वि शरणम् परम् |
शंकर श्वशुरो नाम्ना हिमवान् इति विश्रुतः || ४-११-१२
महा प्रस्रवण उपेतो बहु कन्दर निर्झरः |
स समर्थः तव प्रीतिम् अतुलाम् कर्तुम् अर्हति || ४-११-१३_END
BEGIN_
"A sublime shelter for sages and the father-in-law of Shankara is there in great
forests, well-know by the name Himavan, the king of mountains, and he embodies great cascades,
cataracts, and caves, and he alone is capable to accord a matchless happiness to you in the form of
a fight." So said ocean to Dundubhi. [4-11-12, 13]_END

B_4_C_10_21
BEGIN_
तत्र अनेन अस्मि सम्रुद्धः राज्यम् मृगयत आत्मनः |
सुग्रीवेण नृशंसेन विस्मृत्य भ्रातृ सौहृदम् || ४-१०-२५_END
BEGIN_
"As such this cruel fantasist of kingdom trammelled me in there forgetting the
clannishness." So said Vali to all the courtiers. [4-10-25]_END

B_4_C_8_39
BEGIN_
सुखम् हि कारणम् श्रुत्वा वैरस्य तव वानर |
आनन्तर्यद् विधास्यामि संप्रधार्य बलाबलम् || ३-८-४२_END
BEGIN_
"On knowing the cause of your enmity, oh, monkey, and after a proper thought, and
deciding upon the strength and weakness of the cause of enmity, or of the enmity itself, I will do
the needful very easily. [4-8-42]_END

B_4_C_1_88
BEGIN_
विविधा विविधैः पुष्पैः तैः एव नगसानुषु |विस्तेएर्णाः पीत रक्ताभा सौमित्रे प्रस्तराः कृताः || १-४-९०_END
BEGIN_
"On mountain slopes varied flowers are spread out, with them the colour of diverse mountain slabs is 
rendered into yellow-red hue... [4-1-90]_END

B_4_C_10_22
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा तु माम् तत्र वस्त्रेण एकेन वानरः |
तदा निर्वासयामास वाली विगत साध्वसः || ४-१०-२६_END
BEGIN_
"On saying thus that monkey ruthlessly banished me, then and there in the court
itself, who am with a single clothing on my body. [4-10-26]_END

B_4_C_11_12
BEGIN_
तम् भीतम् इति विज्ञाय समुद्रम् असुरोत्तमः |
हिमवद् वनम् आगम्य शरः चापाद् इव च्युतः || ४-११-१४
ततः तस्य गिरेः श्वेता गजेन्द्र प्रतिमाः शिलाः |
चिक्षेप बहुधा भूमौ दुन्दुभिर् विननाद च || ४-११-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Fathoming that ocean to be scared of him that noted demon Dundubhi arrived at the
forests of Himavan like an arrow darted from bow, and that Dundubhi started to blare discordantly
and toss the rock-faces of that mountain that are like white elephants in their figuration,
severally. [4-11-14, 15]_END

B_4_C_8_40
BEGIN_
बलवान् हि मम अमर्षः श्रुत्वा त्वाम् अवमानितम् |
वर्धते हृदय उत्कम्पी प्रावृड् वेग इव अंभसः || ३-८-४३_END
BEGIN_
"On hearing that you are insulted my intense anger that can flutter my heartbeat is
intensifying like the intensifying speed of waters in rainy reason. [4-8-43]_END

B_4_C_1_89
BEGIN_
हिमान्ते पश्य सौमित्रे वृक्षाणाम् पुष्प संभवम् |पुष्प मासे हि तरवः संघर्षात् इव पुष्पिताः || ४-१-९१_END
BEGIN_
"Soumitri see the bloom of flowers in spring after winter, as if the trees have indeed bore the flowers 
in competition with one another... [4-1-91]_END

B_4_C_10_23
BEGIN_
तेन अहम् अपविद्धः च हृत दारः च राघव |
तत् भयात् च महीम् सर्वान् क्रान्तवान् स वन अर्णवाम् || ४-१०-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Thus he threw me away and even stole my wife, oh, Rama, and owing to his fear alone
I roamed all over the earth with its forests and oceans. [4-10-27]_END

B_4_C_11_13
BEGIN_
ततः श्वेत अम्बुद आकारः सौम्यः प्रीति कर आकृतिः |
हिमवान् अब्रवीद् वाक्यम् स्व एव शिखरे स्थितः || ४-११-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Then he who is like a silver cloud in his figuration, a gentle and delightful one
in his appearance, that Himavan spoke these words to the demon staying on his own cliff.
[4-11-16]_END

B_4_C_1_90
BEGIN_
आह्वयन्त इव अन्योन्यम् नगाः षट्पद नादिताः |कुसुमोत्तंस विटपाः शोभन्ते बहु लक्ष्मण || ४-१-९२_END
BEGIN_
"The drones of honeybees among the trees with flowered treetops appear to be the talk of trees, and 
the swinging branches of trees appear to be their invitational gestures to one another, thus those trees 
look highly attractive... [4-1-92]_END

B_4_C_8_41
BEGIN_
हृष्टः कथय विस्रब्धो यावत् आरोप्यते धनुः |
सृष्टः च हि मया बाणो निरस्तः च रिपुः तव || ३-८-४४_END
BEGIN_
"Be glad to say in belief, Sugreeva, before I take aim with my bow, and even before
I release the arrow, and even before silencing your enemy." Rama assured Sugreeva in this way.
[4-8-44]_END

B_4_C_10_24
BEGIN_
ऋश्यमूकम् गिरि वरम् भार्या हरण दुःखितः |
प्रविष्टो अस्मि दुराधर्षम् वालिनः कारणान्तरे || ४-१०-२८_END
BEGIN_
"I who am saddened by stealing my wife have entered this safest mountain Rishyamuka,
which is impenetrable for Vali by another reason. [4-10-28]_END

B_4_C_11_14
BEGIN_
क्लेष्टुम् अर्हसि माम् न त्वम् दुन्दुभे धर्म वत्सल |
रण कर्मसु अकुशलः तपस्वि शरणो हि अहम् || ४-११-१७_END
BEGIN_
"It is inapt of you to annoy me, oh, virtuous Dundubhi, I am just a shelterer of
sages, and an unskilled one in fights." So said Himavan to Dundubhi. [4-11-17]_END

B_4_C_1_91
BEGIN_
एष कारण्डवः पक्षी विगाह्या सलिलम् शुभम् |रमते कान्ताया सार्थम् कामम् उद्दीपयन् इव || ४-१-९३_END
BEGIN_
"Entering the blessed waters this bird, partridge, is rejoicing together with his female, kindling desire 
in me too... [4-1-93]_END

B_4_C_8_42
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु सुग्रीवः काकुत्स्थेन महात्मना |
प्रहर्षम् अतुलम् लेभे चतुर्भिः सह वानरैः|| ३-८-४५_END
BEGIN_
Thus said by the great souled Rama, Sugreeva is very much rejoiced along with four
of vanara-s available in his attendance. [4-8-45]_END

B_4_C_10_25
BEGIN_
एतत् ते सर्वम् आख्यातम् वैर अनुकथनम् महत् |
अनागसा मया प्राप्तम् व्यसनम् पश्य राघव || ४-१०-२९_END
BEGIN_
"All this notable account of enmity is reported to you, oh, Raghava, and you may
examine the dire straits befallen on me at no fault of mine. [4-10-29]_END

B_4_C_11_15
BEGIN_
तस्य तद् वचनम् श्रुत्वा गिरि राजस्य धीमतः |
उवाच दुन्दुभिर् वाक्यम् क्रोधात् संरक्त लोचनः || ४-११-१८_END
BEGIN_
"On hearing the words of that modest king of mountains Dundubhi's uyes are bloodshot
and he said this sentence. [4-11-18]_END

B_4_C_1_92
BEGIN_
मंदकिन्यास्तु यदिदम् रूपम् एतन् मनोररम् |स्थाने जगति विख्याता गुणाः तस्या मनोरमाः || ४-१-९४_END
BEGIN_
"This sort of heart pleasing nature is also available with River Ganga, and that alone reasonably signifies 
the popularity of River Pampa in the world... [4-1-94]_END

B_4_C_8_43
BEGIN_
ततः प्रहृ^इष्ट वदनः सुग्रीवः लक्ष्मणाग्रजे |
वैरस्य कारणम् तत्त्वम् आख्यातुम् उपचक्रमे || ३-८-४६_END
BEGIN_
Then with a pleased countenance Sugreeva started to tell Rama about the cause of the
enmity, it all it truthfulness. [4-8-46]_END

B_4_C_10_26
BEGIN_
वालिनः च भयात् तस्य सर्वलोक भयापह |
कर्तुम् अर्हसि मे वीर प्रसादम् तस्य निग्रहात् || ४-१०-३०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, the fear-remover of all the worlds, it is apt of you to bestow me
invulnerability from the fear of Vali, and oh, valiant one, as well as to rein him in." Sugreeva
requested Rama thus. [4-10-30]_END

B_4_C_1_93
BEGIN_
यदि दृश्येत सा साध्वी यदि च इह वसेम हि |स्पृहयेयम् न शक्राय न अयोध्यायै रघूत्तम || ४-१-९५_END
BEGIN_
"If that devot lady Seetha is found, and also if we were to stay here only, I neither think about Indra's 
throne in Heavens nor Ayodhya's throne, which is like Indra's throne on the earth... [4-1-95]_END

B_4_C_11_16
BEGIN_
यदि युद्धे असमर्थः त्वम् मद् भयाद् वा निरुद्यमः |
तम् आचक्ष्व प्रदद्यात् मे यो हि युद्धम् युयुत्सतः || ४-११-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Whether you are incapable to fight with me, or not venturing me as you are scared
of me is not my concern, but tell me who can really give me a very combative fight,. [4-11-19]_END

B_4_C_10_27
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः स तेजस्वी धर्मज्ञो धर्म संहितम् |
वचनम् वक्तुम् आरेभे सुग्रीवम् प्रहसन् इव || ४-१०-३१_END
BEGIN_
When he is requested thus by Sugreeva, that virtuous and resplendent Rama started to
tell Sugreeva, the words that abide by virtue, as though trivializing the task on hand.
[4-10-31]_END

B_4_C_11_17
BEGIN_
हिमवान् अब्रवीद् वाक्यम् श्रुत्वा वाक्य विशारदः |
अनुक्त पूर्वम् धर्मात्मा क्रोधात् तम् असुरोत्तमम् || ४-११-२०_END
BEGIN_
On hearing Dundubhi's arrogant words that honest Himavan being an expert in
sentence-making, had to say angry words to that fierce demon that were never uttered by him
earlier. [4-11-20]_END

B_4_C_1_94
BEGIN_
न हि एवम् रमणीयेषु शाद्वलेषु तया सह |रमतो मे भवेत् चिन्ता न स्पृहा अन्येषु वा भवेत् ||४-१-९६_END
BEGIN_
"Nay... if I were to take delight this way in these pleasant green meadows along with her, there will 
be no worry to me... nor interest in other things... [4-1-96]_END

B_4_C_10_28
BEGIN_
अमोघाः सूर्य संकाशा निशिता मे शरा इमे |
तस्मिन् वालिनि दुर्वृत्ते पतिष्यन्ति रुष अन्विताः || ४-१०-३२_END
BEGIN_
"Admirable and sun-like burners are these arrows of mine that are now mingled with
my wrath, and they are bound fall on that evil minded Vali. [4-10-32]_END

B_4_C_11_18
BEGIN_
वाली नाम महा प्राज्ञः शक्र पुत्र प्रतापवान् |
अध्यास्ते वानरः श्रीमान् किष्किन्धाम् अतुल प्रभाम् || ४-११-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, war-expert Dundubhi, Indra's son is there, a brave and glorious one by name
Vali, and he is now presiding over the matchlessly pompous city Kishkindha. [4-11-21]_END

B_4_C_1_95
BEGIN_
अमी हि विविधैः पुष्पैः तरवो रुचिर च्छदाः |कानने अस्मिन् विना कान्ताम् चित्तम् उत्पादयन्ति मे || 
४-१-९७_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed these beautifully leaved and variously flowered trees are maddening my heart as I am without 
that lady Seetha in this forest... [4-1-97]_END

B_4_C_10_29
BEGIN_
यावत् तम् न हि पश्येयम् तव भार्य अपहारिणम् |
तावत् स जीवेत् पापात्मा वाली चारित्र दूषकः || ४-१०-३३_END
BEGIN_
"He that stealer of your wife, that evil-minded abuser of history lives as long as I
descry. [4-10-33]_END

B_4_C_11_19
BEGIN_
स समर्थो महा प्राज्ञः तव युद्ध विशारदः |
द्वन्द्व युद्धम् स दातुम् ते नमुचिः इव वासवः || ४-११-२२_END
BEGIN_
"He is a highly intelligent one and a war-expert too, and he is the capable one to
give you a duel, like Indra to Namuchi. [4-11-22]_END

B_4_C_1_96
BEGIN_
पश्य शीत जलाम् च इमाम् सौमित्रे पुष्कर आयुताम् |चक्रवाक अनुचरिताम् कारण्डव निषेविताम् || ४-१-९८_END
BEGIN_
"See the cool water of this Pampa Lake, Soumitri, filled with blue lotuses, and with ruddy geese well 
moving in, and well venerated by the partridge birds...[4-1-98]_END

B_4_C_10_30
BEGIN_
आत्म अनुमानात् पश्यामि मग्नः त्वाम् शोक सागरे |
त्वाम् अहम् तारयिष्यामि बाढम् प्राप्स्यसि पुष्कलम् || ४-१०-३४_END
BEGIN_
"By my experience I see how you are deluged in a sea of sadness, but I will make you
to get over that sea, and you will definitely regain abundantly whatever you lost." Rama assured
Sugreeva thus. [4-10-34]_END

B_4_C_1_97
BEGIN_
प्लवैः क्रौञ्चैः च संपूर्णाम् महा मृग निषेविताम् |अधिकम् शोभते पम्पा विकूजद्भिः विहङ्गमैः || ४-१-९९_END
BEGIN_
"Well filled with waterfowls, curlew birds, and adored by great animals, this Pampa glistens much with 
pleasantly calling birds...[4-1-99]_END

B_4_C_11_20
BEGIN_
तम् शीघ्रम् अभिगच्छ त्वम् यदि युद्धम् इह इच्छसि |
स हि दुर्मर्षणो नित्यम् शूरः समर कर्मणि || ४-११-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Approach him promptly if you desire a fight now, and he is an intrepid one who will
always be in the manoeuvres of war, and indeed none can assail him." Thus said Himavan to that
demon Dundubhi. [4-11-23]_END

B_4_C_10_31
BEGIN_
तस्य तत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा हर्ष पौरुष वर्धनम् |
सुग्रीवः परम प्रीतः सु महत् वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् || ४-१०-३५_END
BEGIN_
Hearing that sentence of Rama, which is enhancing happiness and self-esteem,
Sugreeva is very gladdened and further said this great sentence. [4-10-35]_END

B_4_C_1_98
BEGIN_
दीपयन्ती इव मे कामम् विविधा मुदिता द्विजाः |श्यामाम् चन्द्र मुखीम् स्मृत्वा प्रियाम् पद्म निभ ईक्षणाम् 
|| ४-१-१००_END
BEGIN_
"Enkindling passion in me, are these umpteen gladdened birds, reminding me of my dear one who is in 
the mid of her youth, moonfaced, and with the radiance of lotuses in her eyes... [4-1-100]_END

B_4_C_11_21
BEGIN_
श्रुत्वा हिमवतो वाक्यम् कोप आविष्टः स दुन्दुभिः |
जगाम ताम् पुरीम् तस्य किष्किन्धाम् वालिनः तदा || ४-११-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Then on hearing Himavan's words he that Dundubhi is convulsed in anger and
proceeded to Vali's city Kishkindha.. [4-11-24]_END

B_4_C_1_99
BEGIN_
पश्य सानुषु चित्रेषु मृगीभिः सहितान् मृगान् |माम् पुनः मृग शबाक्षी वैदेह्या विरहीकृतम् |व्यधयन्तीव 
मे चित्तम् संचरन्तः ततः ततः || ४-१-१०१_END
BEGIN_
"See that female deer along with male deer moving there and there on those wonderful mountainsides... 
and at me, who am weaned away from such a fawn-eyed lady Seetha... and such as I am, my heart is further 
agonised on seeing these wide-eyed deer, and for not seeing her, the wide-eyed Seetha... [4-1-101]_END

B_4_C_11_22
BEGIN_
धारयन् माहिषम् रूपम् तीक्ष्ण शृङ्गो भयावहः |
प्रावृषि इव महा मेघः तोय पूर्णो नभस्तले || ४-११-२५
ततः तु द्वारम् आगम्य किष्किन्धाया महाबलः |
ननर्द कम्पयन् भूमिम् दुन्दुभिर् दुन्दुभिर् यथा || ४-११-२६_END
BEGIN_
"That great mighty demon Dundubhi wearing the look of a buffalo with sharp horns was
awe-inspiring, and like the arrival of a massive dark cloud in rainy season full with water on the
edge of firmament, he arrived at the gateway of Kishkindha and bellowed clamorously like a war-drum
as though to quake the earth. [4-11-25, 26]_END

B_4_C_1_100
BEGIN_
अस्मिन् सानुनि रम्ये हि मत्त द्विज गणाकुले |पश्य अयम् यदि ताम् कन्ताम् ततः स्वस्ति भवेत् मम || ४-१-१०२_END
BEGIN_
"If only I can see that lady on those spectacular terraces filled with impassioned bird groups with 
much ado, then there shall be peace for me... [4-1-102]_END

B_4_C_11_23
BEGIN_
समीपजान् द्रुमान् भंजन् वसुधाम् दारयन् खुरैः |
विषाणेन उल्लिखन् दर्पात् तद् द्वारम् द्विरदो यथा || ४-११-२७_END
BEGIN_
"He bellowed uprooting trees that are rooted nearby, scooping the earth with hooves,
and insolently goring the gateway with horns like a goring elephant. [4-11-27]_END

B_4_C_11_24
BEGIN_
अन्तःपुर गतो वाली श्रुत्वा शब्दम् अमर्षणः |
निष्पपात सह स्त्रीभिः ताराभिः इव चंद्रमाः || ४-११-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Vali who by then went into his palace chambers became intolerant to hear that noise
and fell out from there along with ladies, like the moon with stars. [4-11-28]_END

B_4_C_1_101
BEGIN_
जीवेयम् खलु सौमित्रे मया सह सुमध्यमा |सेवेत यदि वैदेही पम्पायाः पवनम् शुभम् || ४-१-१०३_END
BEGIN_
"I live along for sure, Soumitri, if that slender-waisted Vaidehi basks in this benignant breeze of 
Pampa along with me... [4-1-103]_END

B_4_C_11_25
BEGIN_
मितम् व्यक्त अक्षर पदम् तम् उवाच स दुन्दुभिम् |
हरीणाम् ईश्वरो वाली सर्वेषाम् वन चारिणाम् || ४-११-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Vali being the lord of monkeys, and of all the other forest-dwellers as well, spoke
a clearly worded brief sentence to Dundubhi. [4-11-29]_END

B_4_C_1_102
BEGIN_
पद्म सौगन्धिक वहम् शिवम् शोक विनाशनम् |धन्या लक्ष्मण सेवन्ते पम्पाया वन मरुतम् || ४-१-१०४_END
BEGIN_
""Lakshmana, the breeze from the greenswards of Pampa that carries the fragrance of lotuses including 
that of red lotuses is an auspicious one, an eliminator of melancholy, and those that adore such a breeze 
are fortunate ones... [4-1-104]_END

B_4_C_11_26
BEGIN_
किम् अर्थम् नगर द्वारम् इदम् रुद् ध्वा विनर्दसे |
दुन्दुभे विदितो मेऽसि रक्ष प्राणान् महाबल || ४-११-३०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Dundubhi, impeding the gateway of this city what for you are bellowing, I know
you, oh, might one, save your lives." Vali cautioned that demon that way. [4-11-30]_END

B_4_C_1_103
BEGIN_
श्यमा पद्म पलाशाक्षी प्रिया विरहिता मया |कथम् धरयति प्राणान् विवशा जनकात्मजा || ४-१-१०५_END
BEGIN_
"That youthful, lotus-petal eyed beloved of mine, that Janaka's daughter... how can that helpless lady 
bear her lives without me... [4-1-105]_END

B_4_C_11_27
BEGIN_
तस्य तद् वचनम् श्रुत्वा वानरेन्द्रस्य धीमतः |
उवाच दुन्दुभिर् वाक्यम् क्रोधात् संरक्त लोचनः || ४-११-३१_END
BEGIN_
"On hearing that sentence of Vali, the tactful lord of monkeys, Dundubhi said this
sentence with his eyes bloodshot in anger." Thus Sugreeva continued his narration to Rama.
[4-11-31]_END

B_4_C_1_104
BEGIN_
किम् नु वक्ष्यामि धर्मज्ञम् राजानम् सत्य वादिनम् |जनकम् पृष्ट सीतम् तम् कुशलम् जन संसदि || ४-१-१०६_END
BEGIN_
"What sort of well-being can I say to that virtuous and truth speaking King Janaka, if he enquires about 
Seetha's well-being among hosts of people? [4-1-106]_END

B_4_C_11_28
BEGIN_
न त्वम् स्त्री सन्निधौ वीर वचनम् वक्तुम् अर्हसि |
मम युद्धम् प्रयच्छ अद्य ततो ज्ञास्यामि ते बलम् || ४-११-३२_END
BEGIN_
"It is inapt of you to speak words in the vicinity of ladies, oh, valiant Vali, give
me a duel now and then I can appreciate your might." [4-11-32]_END

B_4_C_1_105
BEGIN_
या मम् अनुगता मन्दम् पित्रा प्रस्थापितुम् वनम् |सीता धर्मम् समास्थय क्व नु सा वर्तते प्रिया || ४-१-१०७_END
BEGIN_
"She who accompanied me, an unfortunate one whom his father sent to forests, taking up a virtuous course... 
now where will be she, that ladylove of mine, be abiding... [4-1-107]_END

B_4_C_12_0
BEGIN_
एतच् च वचनम् श्रुत्वा सुग्रीवस्य सुभाषितम् |
प्रत्ययार्थम् महातेजा रामो जग्राह कार्मुकम् || ४-१२-१_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the well-spoken words of Sugreeva that expressed doubt about Rama's
valour, that great resplendent Rama took-up bow to inculcate credence in Sugreeva. [4-12-1]_END

B_4_C_11_29
BEGIN_
अथवा धारयिष्यामि क्रोधम् अद्य निशाम् इमाम् |
गृह्यताम् उदयः स्वैरम् काम भोगेषु वानर || ४-११-३३_END
BEGIN_
"Otherwise I bear up my rage for this night, oh, monkey, you may unrestrainedly
delight yourself till morning in your voluptuous gratifications, for you are now surrounded by your
ladies." [4-11-33]_END

B_4_C_1_106
BEGIN_
तया विहीनः कृपणः कथम् लक्ष्मण धारये |य माम् अनुगता रज्यात् भ्रष्टम् विहत चेतसम् || ४-१-१०८_END
BEGIN_
"Whose kingdom is forfeited, and whose soul succumbed to the circumstance at the time of exile, but 
she accompanied suchlike me, and Lakshmana, without her how I can I live on in desolation... [4-1-108]_END

B_4_C_12_1
BEGIN_
स गृहीत्वा धनुर् घोरम् शरम् एकम् च मानदः |
सालम् उद्दिश्य चिक्षेप पूरयन् स रवैः दिशः || ४-१२-२_END
BEGIN_
Rama, the bestower of dignity to the sufferers, took up his dreadful bow, aimed at a
sala tree, and darted single arrow, by which all the directions reverberated with the twang of his
bowstring. [4-12-2]_END

B_4_C_11_30
BEGIN_
दीयताम् संप्रदानम् च परिष्वज्य च वानरान् |
सर्व शखा मृगेन्द्रत्वम् संसादय सुहृज्जनम् || ४-११-३४_END
BEGIN_
"Also embrace all the monkeys and bequeath endowments to them, and you may bid adieu
to all the good-hearted people of yours for you are the king of all the tree-branch animals, as you
may not see them later. [4-11-34]_END

B_4_C_1_107
BEGIN_
तत् चारु अञ्चित पद्माक्षम् सुगन्धि शुभम् अव्रणम् |अपश्यतो मुखम् तस्याः सीदति इव मतिः मम || ४-१-१०९_END
BEGIN_
"She who has a pretty and beaming face with lotus-like eyes, that is fragrant, auspicious and scarless, 
and not seeing such a face my mind is as though sinking... [4-1-109]_END

B_4_C_12_2
BEGIN_
स विसृष्टो बलवता बाणः स्वर्ण परिष्कृतः |
भित्त्वा सालान् गिरि प्रस्थम् सप्त भूमिम् विवेश ह || ४-१२-३_END
BEGIN_
The golden arrow released by the mighty Rama perforated all the seven sala trees,
and even the levelled areas of mountain, and then entered the earth. [4-12-3]_END

B_4_C_11_31
BEGIN_
सु दृष्टाम् कुरु किष्किन्धाम् कुरुष्व आत्म समम् पुरे |
क्रीडयस्व च समम् स्त्रीभिः अहम् ते दर्प शासनः || ४-११-३५_END
BEGIN_
"Let Kishkindha city be seen clearly by you as last sight, and keep someone
equalling you as in charge of city, and also rejoice with the females till sunrise as there is no
tomorrow to you. [4-11-35]_END

B_4_C_1_108
BEGIN_
स्मित हास्यान्तर युतम् गुणवत् मधुरम् हितम् |वैदेह्याः वाक्यम् अतुलम् कदा श्रोष्यामि लक्ष्मण || ४-१-११०_END
BEGIN_
" Lakshmana, when can I hear that conversation of Vaidehi that will have smiles and wits in between... 
wisdom wise pleasing, friendly and unique one in its own way... [4-1-110]_END

B_4_C_12_3
BEGIN_
सायकः तु मुहूर्तेन सालान् भित्त्वा महाजवः |
निष्पत्य च पुनः तूर्णम् तम् एव प्रविवेश ह || ४-१२-४_END
BEGIN_
Thus that arrow which briskly drilled all the sala trees, came up in a moment from
under the earth, and again swiftly re-entered the quiver of Rama. [4-12-4]_END

B_4_C_11_32
BEGIN_
यो हि मत्तम् प्रमत्तम् वा भग्नम् वा रहितम् कृशम् |
हन्यात् स भ्रूणहा लोके त्वद् विधम् मद मोहितम् || ४-११-३६_END
BEGIN_
"He who kills a drunken one, unvigilant one, defeated one, or one without weapons,
or an atrophied one, he get the sin of foeticide in the world, and your present state is suchlike."
Dundubhi incited Vali in this way. [4-11-36]_END

B_4_C_1_109
BEGIN_
प्राप्य दुःखम् वने श्यामा माम् मन्मध विकर्शितम् |नष्ट दुःखेव हृष्टेव साध्वी साधु अभ्यभाषत || ४-१-१११_END
BEGIN_
"That youthful and decent lady though succumbed to suffering in forests used to look as though got rid 
of her sufferings, and as though gladsome woman, and she used to speak to me, one smitten by her love, 
very fondly... [4-1-111]_END

B_4_C_12_4
BEGIN_
तान् दृष्ट्वा सप्त निर्भिन्नान् सालान् वानरपुंगवः |
रामस्य शर वेगेन विस्मयम् परमम् गतः || ४-१२-५_END
BEGIN_
On seeing them the seven sala trees that are profoundly fissured, that best monkey
Sugreeva went into a stunning astonishment at the rapidity of Rama's arrow. [4-12-5]_END

B_4_C_11_33
BEGIN_
स प्रहस्य अब्रवीत् मन्दम् क्रोधात् तम् असुरेश्वरम् |
विसृज्य ताः स्त्रियः सर्वाः तारा प्रभृतिकाः तदा || ४-११-३७_END
BEGIN_
"Then Vali laughed that demon off, discharged all the females namely Tara and
others, and then he spoke to that stupid lord of demons in anger. [4-11-37]_END

B_4_C_1_110
BEGIN_
किम् नु वक्ष्यामि अयोध्यायाम् कौसल्याम् हि नृपात्मज |क्व सा स्नुषा इति पृच्छन्तीम् कथम् च अति मनस्विनीम् 
|| ४-१-११२_END
BEGIN_
"What can I say in Ayodhya to that kind hearted lady and my mother Kausalya, oh, prince Lakshmana, when 
she asks �where is she, my daughter-in-law? And how is she? ' [4-1-112]_END

B_4_C_12_5
BEGIN_
स मूर्ध्ना न्यपतत् भूमौ प्रलंबीकृत भूषणः |
सुग्रीवः परम प्रीतो राघवाय कृतांजलिः || ४-१२-६_END
BEGIN_
Highly gladdened Sugreeva made palm-fold in that astonishment, kneeled while his
ornaments dangled, and prostrated before Raghava with his head touching the ground. [4-12-6]_END

B_4_C_11_34
BEGIN_
मत्तो अयम् इति मा मंस्था यदि अभीतो असि संयुगे |
मदो अयम् संप्रहारे अस्मिन् वीर पानम् समर्थ्यताम् || ४-११-३८_END
BEGIN_
"Don't surmise that I am drunk, and should you be unafraid of a fight, regard this
drunkenness of mine as the toast of a gallant fighter in this deadly fight." Vali said so to
Dundubhi. [4-11-38]_END

B_4_C_1_111
BEGIN_
गच्छ लक्ष्मण पश्य त्वम् भरतम् भ्रातृउ वत्सलम् |न हि अहम् जीवितुम् शक्तः ताम् ऋते जनकात्मजम् || ४-१-११३_END
BEGIN_
"Begone! Lakshmana.... you may see Bharata, that affectionate one for his brothers... I may not be able 
to live on leaving off Seetha... isn't so!" [So said Rama to Lakshmana] [4-1-113]_END

B_4_C_12_6
BEGIN_
इदम् च उवाच धर्मज्ञम् कर्मणा तेन हर्षितः |
रामम् सर्व अस्त्र विदुषाम् श्रेष्ठम् शूरम् अवस्थितम् || ४-१२-७_END
BEGIN_
Overjoyed with that deed Sugreeva said this to that virtue-knower, the one who is
proficient among all experts of missiles, namely the valorous Rama, who is just in his presence
him. [4-12-7]_END

B_4_C_13_0
BEGIN_
ऋश्यमूकात् स धर्मात्मा किष्किन्धाम् लक्ष्मण अग्रजः |जगाम सह सुग्रीवो वालि विक्रम पालिताम् || ४-१३-१
समुद्यम्य महत् चापम् रामः कांचन भूषितम् |शराम् च आदित्य संकाशान् गृहीत्वा रण साधकान् || ४-१३-२_END
BEGIN_
That righteous Rama readying his great bow decorated with gold, and on taking blazing sun similar arrows 
that are victory-oriented in wars, proceeded from Rishyamuka along with Sugreeva to the city ruled by 
the valour of Vali, namely Kishkindha. [4-13-1, 2]_END

B_4_C_11_35
BEGIN_
तम् एवम् उक्त्वा संक्रुद्धो मालाम् उत्क्षिप्य कांचनीम् |
पित्रा दत्ताम् महेन्द्रेण युद्धाय व्यवतिष्ठत || ४-११-३९_END
BEGIN_
"Saying that way to that Dundubhi that highly enraged Vali heaved up the golden
chest-pendant around his neck on to his chest, which was given by his father Mahendra, and stood
firm for fight. [4-11-39]_END

B_4_C_1_112
BEGIN_
इति रामम् महात्मानम् विलपन्तम् अनाथ वत् |उवाच लक्ष्मणो भ्राता वचनम् युक्तम् अव्ययम् || ४-१-११४_END
BEGIN_
To that great-souled Rama who is bewailing that way like a waif, his brother Lakshmana said these appropriate 
and infallible words. [4-1-114]_END

B_4_C_12_7
BEGIN_
स इन्द्रान् अपि सुरान् सर्वाम् त्वम् बाणैः पुरुषर्षभ |
समर्थः समरे हन्तुम् किम् पुनर् वालिनम् प्रभो || ४-१२-८_END
BEGIN_
"You with your arrows, oh, best one among men, are capable of eliminating all the
gods including Indra, oh, lord, then why to speak of Vali. [4-12-8]_END

B_4_C_13_1
BEGIN_
अग्रतः तु ययौ तस्य राघवस्य महात्मनः |सुग्रीवः संहत ग्रीवो लक्ष्मणः च महाबलः || ४-१३-३_END
BEGIN_
Stern-necked Sugreeva and the great mighty Lakshmana strode ahead of that great soul Rama. [4-13-3]_END

B_4_C_11_36
BEGIN_
विषाणयो गृहीत्वा तम् दुन्दुभिम् गिरि संनिभम् |
आविध्यत तथा वाली विनदन् कपि कुंजरः || ४-११-४०_END
BEGIN_
"Then that elephantine monkey Vali took that mountain-similar Dundubhi by horns, and
booming highly he whirled and bumped him onto ground. [4-11-40]_END

B_4_C_1_113
BEGIN_
संस्थम्भ राम भद्रम् ते मा शुचः पुरुषोत्तम |न ईदृइशानाम् मतिः मन्दा भवति अकलुषात्मनाम् || ४-१-११५_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, best one among men, please control yourself Rama, let safety betide you, do not lament, the intellect 
of your kind of unblemished souls does not become languorous... [4-1-115]_END

B_4_C_12_8
BEGIN_
येन सप्त महा साला गिरिर् भूमिः च दारिताः |
बाणेन एकेन काकुत्स्थ स्थाता ते को रण अग्रतः || ४-१२-९_END
BEGIN_
"By whom seven great sala trees, a mountain and also the earth is ripped off with
only one arrow, oh Kakutstha, who then can stand up to you in the vanguard of war. [4-12-9]_END

B_4_C_13_2
BEGIN_
पृष्ठतो हनुमान् वीरो नलो नीलः च वीर्यवान् |तारः चैव महातेजा हरि यूथप यूथपाः || ४-१३-४_END
BEGIN_
The brave Hanuma, dauntless Nala and Neela, and the captain of monkey's captains Tara of great energy 
followed them rearward. [4-13-4]_END

B_4_C_11_37
BEGIN_
वाली व्यापादयाम् चक्रे ननर्द च महास्वनम् |
श्रोत्राभ्याम् अथ रक्तम् तु तस्य सुस्राव पात्यतः || ४-११-४१_END
BEGIN_
"Vali while blaring highly with great sound repeatedly whirled him and thrown onto
ground, and while Dundubhi was hurled and thrown to ground, blood gushed out of his two ears.
[4-11-41]_END

B_4_C_12_9
BEGIN_
अद्य मे विगतः शोकः प्रीतिर् अद्य परा मम |
सुहृदम् त्वाम् समासाद्य महेन्द्र वरुणोपमम् || ४-१२-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Today on gaining a kind-hearted friend like you, who is similar to Indra and
Rain-god who accord favour on their own, my distress is gone and my joy is heightened.
[4-12-10]_END

B_4_C_1_114
BEGIN_
स्मृत्वा वियोगजम् दुःखम् त्यज स्नेहम् प्रिये जने |अति स्नेह परिष्वन्गात् वर्तिः अर्द्रा अपि दह्यते 
|| ४-१-११६_END
BEGIN_
"Recollect the sadness caused by departure of loved ones, and it may please be forsaken for some extent, 
with the embrace of too much of friendship of the water-drenched wick with oil, even that water-drenched 
wick burns in the lamp... [4-1-116]_END

B_4_C_13_3
BEGIN_
ते वीक्षमाणा वृक्षाम् च पुष्प भार अवलम्बिनः |प्रसन्न अंबुवहाः चैव सरितः सागरम् गमाः || ४-१३-५_END
BEGIN_
They moved on looking at the trees that are drooping with the weight of their flowers, and at he rivers 
that are carrying pleasant water while themselves are coursing towards ocean. [4-13-5]_END

B_4_C_11_38
BEGIN_
तयोः तु क्रोध संरम्भात् परस्पर जयैषिणोः |
युद्धम् समभवत् घोरम् दुन्दुभेर् वालिनः तथा || ४-११-४२_END
BEGIN_
"There occurred a gruesome fight among those two, Dundubhi and Vali, who by their
fury are impetuous and who aspired victory over the other. [4-11-42]_END

B_4_C_1_115

BEGIN_
"On remembering the fondness for dear ones, intellect of your kind of unblemished souls will not become 
languorous. Leave off the sadness caused by separation._END

B_4_C_12_10
BEGIN_
तम् अद्य एव प्रियार्थम् मे वैरिणम् भ्रातृ रूपिणम् |
वालिनम् जहि काकुत्स्थ मया बद्धो अयम् अंजलिः || ४-१२-११_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, today itself you eliminate that enemy of mine in a brother's semblance
for my happiness, for which I adjoin my palms in supplication." Thus Sugreeva requested Rama.
[4-12-11]_END

B_4_C_13_4
BEGIN_
कन्दराणि च शैलाम् च निर्दराणि गुहाः तथा |शिखराणि च मुख्यानि दरीः च प्रिय दर्शनाः || ४-१३-६_END
BEGIN_
They on seeing house-like caverns, crags, ravines and caves, and monumental peaks, cavities that are 
pleasant for sight have moved on. [4-13-6]_END

B_4_C_11_39
BEGIN_
अयुध्यत तदा वाली शक्र तुल्य पराक्रमः |
मुष्टिभिर् जानुभिः पद्भिः शिलाभिः पादपैः तथा || ४-११-४३_END
BEGIN_
"Then Vali who is similar to Indra in his fortitude fought with him with his fists,
knees and feet, and like that with boulders and trees. [4-11-43]_END

B_4_C_1_116
BEGIN_
यदि गच्छति पतालम् ततो अभ्यऽधिकम् एव वा |सर्वधा रावणः तात न भविष्यति राघव || ४-१-११७_END
BEGIN_
"If Ravana goes to the netherworlds, or still deeper worlds from there, oh my brother, still he will 
not live, Raghava... [4-1-117]_END

B_4_C_12_11
BEGIN_
ततो रामः परिष्वज्य सुग्रीवम् प्रिय दर्शनम् |
प्रत्युवाच महाप्राज्ञो लक्ष्मणानुगतम् वचः || ४-१२-१२_END
BEGIN_
That great percipient Rama embraced Sugreeva, which Sugreeva is pleasant in his look
for he gained confidence by now, and who is an alternate of Lakshmana to partake Rama's affection,
and then Rama said these words to such a Sugreeva in reply. [4-12-12]_END

B_4_C_13_5
BEGIN_
वैदूर्य विमलैः तोयैः पद्मैः च आकोश कुड्मलैः |शोभितान् सजलान् मार्गे तटाकान् च अवलोकयन् || ४-१३-७_END
BEGIN_
On their way they observed lakes that are glistening forth with gem-like waters without slime, and with 
lotus buds in budding stage. [4-13-7]_END

B_4_C_11_40
BEGIN_
परस्परम् घ्नतोः तत्र वानर असुरयोः तदा |
आसीत् हीनो असुरो युद्धे शक्र सूनुः व्यवर्धत || ४-११-४४_END
BEGIN_
"While each is assaulting the other in that fight between that monkey and demon,
that demon is impaired and Indra's son Vali toughened. [4-11-44]_END

B_4_C_1_117
BEGIN_
प्रवृत्तिः लभ्यताम् तावत् तस्य पापस्य रक्षसः |ततः हास्यति वा सीताम् निधनम् वा गमिष्यति || ४-१-११८_END
BEGIN_
"Let the emplacement of that sinning demon e obtained... and then he either cedes Seetha or enters into 
his own doom... [4-1-118]_END

B_4_C_12_12
BEGIN_
अस्माद् गच्छाम किष्किन्धाम् क्षिप्रम् गच्छ त्वम् अग्रतः |
गत्वा च आह्वय सुग्रीव वालिनम् भ्रातृ गन्धिनम् || ४-१२-१३_END
BEGIN_
""Let us quickly go from here to Kishkindha, oh, Sugreeva, you move in advance, and
on going there you invite that Vali, one redolent of your brotherhood." So said Rama to Sugreeva.
[4-12-13]_END

B_4_C_13_6
BEGIN_
कारण्डैस्सारसैर्हंसैर्वञ्जुलैर्जलकुक्कुटैः |चक्रवाकैस्थाचान्यैश्शकुनैर्प्रतिनादितान् || - यद्वा 
-कारण्डैः सारसैः हंसैः वंजुलैः जल कुक्कुटैः |चक्रवाकैः तथा च अन्यैः शकुनैः प्रतिनादितान् || 
४-१३-८_END
BEGIN_
Those lakes are reverberant with Karandava-s, Saarasa-s, Swans, Vanjula-s and other waterfowls, also 
like that with Chakravaaka-s and other birds. [4-13-8]_END

B_4_C_11_41
BEGIN_
तम् तु दुन्दुभिम् उद्यम्य धरण्याम् अभ्यपातयत् |
युद्धे प्राणहरे तस्मिन् निष्पिष्टो दुन्दुभिः तदा || ४-११-४५_END
BEGIN_
"In that life-taking fight when Dundubhi is lifted up and flung to ground, he is
completely pounded out. [4-11-45]_END

B_4_C_1_118
BEGIN_
यदि याति दितेः गर्भम् रावणः सह सीताया |तत्र अपि एनम् हनिष्यामि न चेत् दास्यति मैथिलीम् || ४-१-११९_END
BEGIN_
"Even if he enters the womb of Diti along with Seetha, and if he does not give away Seetha, even there 
I wish to slay him,...[4-1-119]_END

B_4_C_12_13
BEGIN_
सर्वे ते त्वरितम् गत्वा किष्किन्धाम् वालिनः पुरीम् |
वृक्षैः आत्मानम् आवृत्य हि अतिष्ठन् गहने वने || ४-१२-१४_END
BEGIN_
They all on quickly going to Kishkindha, the city of Vali, hedged themselves in the
thickets of forest trees and waited. [4-12-14]_END

B_4_C_13_7
BEGIN_
मृदुशष्पाङ्कुराअहारान्निर्भयान्वनगोचरान् |चरतांसर्वतोपश्यन्स्थलीषु हरिणान्स्थितान् || - यद्वा -
मृदु शष्प अंकुर आहारान् निर्भयान् वन गोचरान् |चरताम् सर्वतो अपश्यन् स्थलीषु हरिणान् स्थितान् || 
४-१३-९_END
BEGIN_
They have seen fearless deer feeding on soft grass blades everywhere, somewhere moving here and there 
in the forest, and else where standing. [4-13-9]_END

B_4_C_11_42
BEGIN_
स्रोत्रेभ्यो बहु रक्तम् तु तस्य सुस्राव पात्यतः |
पपात च महाबाहुः क्षितौ पंचत्वम् आगतः || ४-११-४६_END
BEGIN_
"While he is felled down much blood is flown out from the vent-holes of his body,
nine of them, ears, nose, eyes etc., and on his falling that mighty one Dundubhi attained the
fifth-state. [4-11-46]_END

B_4_C_14_0
BEGIN_
सर्वे ते त्वरितम् गत्वा किष्किन्धाम् वालिनः पालिताम् |
वृक्षैर् आत्मानम् आवृत्य व्यतिष्ठन् गहने वने || ४-१४-१_END
BEGIN_
They all on quickly going to Kishkindha, the city of Vali, hedged themselves in the
thickets of forest trees and waited. [4-14-1]_END

B_4_C_1_119
BEGIN_
स्वास्थ्यम् भद्रम् भजस्व आर्यः त्यजताम् कृपणा मतिः |अर्थो हि नष्ट कार्यार्थैः न अयत्ने न अधिगम्यते 
|| ४-१-१२०_END
BEGIN_
"May you rejuvenate and be secure, oh, revered one, cast-off your pathetic mood... result of purpose 
will be lost indeed, for the endeavourers without a try, thus nothing can be regained by them... [4-1-120]_END

B_4_C_12_14
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवो अपि व्यनदद् घोरम् वालिनो ह्वान कारणात् |
गाढम् परिहितो वेगान् नादैः भिन्दन् इव अंबरम् || ४-१२-१५_END
BEGIN_
Sugreeva firmly tightened his girdle-cloth for the duel and shouted boisterously for
the purpose of inviting Vali for a duel, and his rapidity in shouting appeared as though to crack
the sky. [4-12-15]_END

B_4_C_13_8
BEGIN_
तटाक वैरिणः च अपि शुक्ल दन्त विभूषितान् |घोरान् एकचरान् वन्यान् द्विरदान् कूल घातिनः || ४-१३-१०_END
BEGIN_
They have also seen the forest elephants that have white tusks for their ornaments and that are moving 
in herds, and which are the dangerous enemies of lakes as they destroy lakebeds. [4-13-10]_END

B_4_C_11_43
BEGIN_
तम् तोलयित्वा बाहुभ्याम् गत सत्त्वम् अचेतनम् |
चिक्षेप वेगवान् वाली वेगेन एकेन योजनम् || ४-११-४७_END
BEGIN_
"Then the hastiest Vali swayed that dead and inanimate demon with both of his hands
and hurled him a yojana distance in a single flick. [4-11-47]_END

B_4_C_14_1
BEGIN_
विसार्य सर्वतो दृष्टिम् कानने कानन प्रियः |
सुग्रीवो विपुल ग्रीवः क्रोधम् आहारयद् भृशम् || ४-१४-२_END
BEGIN_
That forest lover with tumultuous voice Sugreeva cast his eye everywhere and assumed
tremendous fury. [4-14-2]_END

B_4_C_1_120
BEGIN_
उत्साहो बलवान् आर्य नास्ति उत्साहात् परम् बलम् |सः उत्साहस्य हि लोकेषु न किंचित् अपि दुर्लभम् || 
४-१-१२१_END
BEGIN_
"Vehemence is might, oh, noble one, there is no superior might than vehemence and to him with vehemence 
there is no impossibility in the world,... even the slightest... [4-1-121]_END

B_4_C_12_15
BEGIN_
तम् श्रुत्वा निनदम् भ्रातुः क्रुद्धो वाली महाबलः |
निष्पपात सुसंरब्धो भास्करो अस्त तटात् इव || ४-१२-१६_END
BEGIN_
On hearing his brother's shouting that great mighty Vali is infuriated and
impetuously rushed out of his palace chambers, like the sun falling back onto sky from his dusking
brink. [4-12-16]_END

B_4_C_13_9
BEGIN_
मत्तन् गिरि तट उद्घुष्टान् पर्वतान् इव जंगमान् |वानरान् द्विरद प्रख्यान् मही रेणु समुक्षितान् || 
४-१३-११_END
BEGIN_
Also seen are the vigorous and elephantine monkeys that are like mobile mountains, begrimed with dust, 
and bellowing on mountain ridges. [4-13-11]_END

B_4_C_11_44
BEGIN_
तस्य वेग प्रविद्धस्य वक्त्रात् क्षतज बिन्दवः |
प्रपेतुः मारुत उत्क्षिप्ता मतंगस्य आश्रमम् प्रति || ४-११-४८_END
BEGIN_
"And while he is thrown that hastily blood drops oozed from his mouth, and flung by
air they fell in the hermitage of sage Matanga. [4-11-48]_END

B_4_C_14_2
BEGIN_
ततः तु निनदम् घोरम् कृत्वा युद्धाय च आह्वयत् |
परिवारैः परिवृतो नादैर् भिन्दन् इव अंबरम् || ४-१४-३
गर्जन् इव महामेघो वायु वेग पुरस्सरः |_END
BEGIN_
Then Sugreeva encompassed by his followers war-whooped ghastlily, like a great cloud
that emerged accelerated by gusty wind and that is thundering as though to rip the sky, inviting
Vali for fight. [4-14-3]_END

B_4_C_1_121
BEGIN_
उत्साहवन्तः पुरुषा न अवसीदन्ति कर्मसु |उत्साह मत्रम् आश्रित्य सीताम् प्रतिलप्स्याम् जनकीम् || ४-१-१२२_END
BEGIN_
"Vehement men do not regress in deeds, and taking hold of vehemence alone we regain Seetha...[4-1-122]_END

B_4_C_12_16
BEGIN_
ततः सुतुमुलम् युद्धम् वालि सुग्रीवयोः अभूत् |
गगने ग्रहयोः घोरम् बुध अंगारकयोः इव || ४-१२-१७_END
BEGIN_
Then a very tumultuous and awful fight occurred between Vali and Sugreeva, which is
like the awful fight between the planets Mercury and Mars in skies. [4-12-17]_END

B_4_C_13_10
BEGIN_
वने वन चराम् च अन्यान् खेचराम् च विहंगमान् |पश्यन्तः त्वरिता जग्मुः सुग्रीव वश वर्तिनः || ४-१३-१२_END
BEGIN_
On seeing other forest beings in that forest and birds moving aloft in sky, those followers of Sugreeva 
quickly moved on. [4-13-12]_END

B_4_C_14_3
BEGIN_
अथ बालार्क सदृशो दृप्त सिम्ह गतिः ततः || ४-१४-४
दृष्ट्वा रामम् क्रिया दक्षम् सुग्रीवो वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_
Then Sugreeva who is like the rising sun and whose stride is like that of a proud
lion saw the adroit Rama and then said this sentence. [4-14-4b, 5a]_END

B_4_C_11_45
BEGIN_
तान् दृष्ट्वा पतिताम् तत्र मुनिः शोणित विप्रुषः |
क्रुद्धः तस्य महाभाग चिन्तयामास कोन्वम् || ४-११-४९_END
BEGIN_
"On seeing the blood drops fallen there, oh Rama, that sage is enraged and thought,
'who is he indeed, who dropped the blood...' Thus Sugreeva narrated to Rama. [4-11-49]_END

B_4_C_1_122
BEGIN_
त्यज्य काम वृत्तत्वम् शोकम् सम् न्यस्य पृष्टतः |महात्मानम् कृतात्मानम् आत्मानम् न अवबुध्यसे || ४-१-१२३_END
BEGIN_
"You leave off this enclosure of ardency and pushback that compassion ... you are not able to know your 
great and controlled soul...with these thoughts of self-pity and fondness... [4-1-123]_END

B_4_C_12_17
BEGIN_
तलैः अशनि कल्पैः च वज्र कल्पैः च मुष्टिभिः |
जघ्नतुः समरे अन्योन्यम् भ्रातरौ क्रोध मूर्च्छितौ || ४-१२-१८_END
BEGIN_
Those two brothers who are convulsed in frenzy battered each other in that fight
with their thunderbolt-like palms, and lightning-like fists. [4-12-18]_END

B_4_C_13_11
BEGIN_
तेषाम् तु गच्छताम् तत्र त्वरितम् रघुनंदनः |द्रुम षण्ड वनम् दृष्ट्वा रामः सुग्रीवम् अब्रवीत् || ४-१३-१३_END
BEGIN_
While they are quickly going, Rama, the delight of Raghu's dynasty, saw there a clump of forest trees 
and he asked Sugreeva like this. [4-13-13]_END

B_4_C_11_46
BEGIN_
येन अहम् सहसा स्पृष्टः शोणितेन दुरात्मना |
कोऽयम् दुरात्मा दुर् बुद्धिः अकृतात्मा च बालिशः || ४-११-५०_END
BEGIN_
" 'By which evil-spirited one I am abruptly touched with blood? Who is that
evil-minded one? Who is that malevolent, disobedient and a reckless one?' Thus the sage Matanga
pondered. [4-11-50]_END

B_4_C_14_4
BEGIN_
हरि वागुरया व्याप्तम् तप्त कांचन तोरणाम् || ४-१४-५
प्राप्ताः स्म ध्वज यंत्र आढ्याम् किष्किन्धाम् वालिनः पुरीम् |_END
BEGIN_
" She whose arch-way is decorated in gold, who is spread out with snares of monkeys,
and who is impregnated with flags and machinery, we arrived at such city of Vali, Kishkindha.
[4-14-5b, 6a]_END

B_4_C_1_123
BEGIN_
एवम् संबोधितः तेन शोकोपहत चेतनः |त्य्ज्य शोकम् च मोहम् च रामो धैर्यम् उपागमत् || ४-१-१२४_END
BEGIN_
Thus addressed by Lakshmana, then Rama whose conscience is marred by emotions, got rid of pity and fondness, 
and acquired courage, to perform the deed demanded of his incarnation. [4-1-124]_END

B_4_C_12_18
BEGIN_
ततो रामो धनुष् पाणिः तौ उभौ समुदैक्षत |
अन्योन्य सदृशौ वीरौ उभौ देवौ इव अश्विनौ || ४-१२-१९_END
BEGIN_
Then Rama wielding bow in his hand watched those valiant ones that are alike in
their appearance, like the Ashwin twins among gods. [4-12-19]_END

B_4_C_13_12
BEGIN_
एष मेघ इव आकाशे वृक्ष षण्डः प्रकाशते |मेघ संघात विपुलः पर्यन्त कदली वृतः || ४-१३-१४_END
BEGIN_
"This cluster of trees surrounded with plantain trees is like an accumulation of thick clouds, and this 
is shining forth like a cloudscape in sky. [4-13-14]_END

B_4_C_14_5
BEGIN_
प्रतिज्ञा या कृता वीर त्वया वालि वधे पुरा || ४-१४-६
सफलाम् कुरु ताम् क्षिप्रम् लताम् काल इव आगतः |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh Brave one, you make happen the promise you earlier made regarding the
elimination of Vali on time, like the time of sprouting that enables a creeper-plant to bear a
sprout on time. [4-14-6b, 7a]_END

B_4_C_11_47
BEGIN_
इति उक्त्वा स विनिष्क्रम्य ददृशे मुनिसत्तम |
महिषम् पर्वत आकारम् गत असुम् पतितम् भुवि || ४-११-५१_END
BEGIN_
"Thinking thus and coming out of hermitage that celebrated sage has seen the
mountainous buffalo fallen on ground lifelessly. [4-11-51]_END

B_4_C_1_124
BEGIN_
सोऽभ्य अतिक्रामत् अव्यग्रः ताम् अचिन्त्य पराक्रमः |रामः पम्पाम् सु रुचिराम् रम्याम् पारिप्लव द्रुमान् 
|| ४-१-१२५_END
BEGIN_
He that inestimable valiant Rama strode forward those areas of charming Pampa Lake, with the charm of 
wind-flopped trees, getting rid of grief. [4-1-125]_END

B_4_C_12_19
BEGIN_
यत् न अवगच्छत् सुग्रीवम् वालिनम् वा अपि राघवः |
ततो न कृतवान् बुद्धिम् मोक्तुम् अन्तकरम् शरम् || ४-१२-२०_END
BEGIN_
For which reason Raghava could not differentiate between Sugreeva or Vali, for the
same reason did not make up his mind to release his arrow, otherwise it would have been a deadening
arrow, as confusion is the only reason for Rama. [4-12-20]_END

B_4_C_13_13
BEGIN_
किम् एतत् ज्ञातुम् इच्छामि सखे कौतूहलम् मम |कौतूहल अपनयनम् कर्तुम् इच्छामि अहम् त्वया || ४-१३-१५_END
BEGIN_
"What is this? I wish to know and oh, friend, I wish you to clear this inquisitiveness of mine. [4-13-15]_END

B_4_C_14_6
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु धर्मात्मा सुग्रीवेण स राघवः || ४-१४-७
तम् एव उवाच वचनम् सुग्रीवम् शत्रु सूदनः |_END
BEGIN_
When thus said by Sugreeva that enemy-destroyer and righteous Raghava said this word
Sugreeva. [4-14-7b, 8a]_END

B_4_C_11_48
BEGIN_
स तु विज्ञाय तपसा वानरेण कृतम् हि तत् |
उत्ससर्ज महा शापम् क्षेप्तारम् वानरम् प्रति || ४-११-५२_END
BEGIN_
"On knowing by his ascetic power that this deed is done by the monkey, he released a
great curse on him who tossed the cadaver of buffalo. [4-11-52]_END

B_4_C_1_125
BEGIN_
निरीक्षमाणः सहसा महात्मा सर्वम् वनम् निर्झर कन्दराम् च |उद्विग्न चेताः सह लक्ष्मणेन विचार्य दुःखोपहतः 
प्रतस्थे || ४-१-१२६_END
BEGIN_
That great one Rama on observing all over quickly, all round the forest with its brooks and caves, and 
reviewing with Lakshmana, though agonised at heart that anguished one travelled on. [4-1-126]_END

B_4_C_12_20
BEGIN_
एतस्मिन् अन्तरे भग्नः सुग्रीवः तेन वालिना |
अपश्यन् राघवम् नाथम् ऋश्यमूकम् प्रदुद्रुवे || ४-१२-२१_END
BEGIN_
Meanwhile Sugreeva is unable to spot out his benefactor Raghava as Vali whacked him
down, and thereby he immediately fled to Mt. Rishyamuka. [4-12-21]_END

B_4_C_13_14
BEGIN_
तस्य तद् वचनम् श्रुत्वा राघवस्य महात्मनः |गच्छन्न् एव आचचक्षे अथ सुग्रीवः तत् महद् वनम् || ४-१३-१६_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that sentence of that great soul Raghava, then Sugreeva described about the significance 
of that forest while proceeding on the way. [4-13-16]_END

B_4_C_11_49
BEGIN_
इह तेन अप्रवेष्टव्यम् प्रविष्टस्य वधो भवेत् |
वनम् मत् संश्रयम् येन दूषितम् रुधिर स्रवैः || ४-११-५३_END
BEGIN_
"Untreadable is this sheltering wood of mine to him who has stained it with squirts
of blood, and if he enters this place peradventure, fatality occurs on him. [4-11-53]_END

B_4_C_14_7
BEGIN_
कृत अभिज्ञान चिह्नः त्वम् अनया गज साह्वया || ४-१४-८
लक्ष्मणेन समुत्पाट्य एषा कण्ठे कृता तव |_END
BEGIN_
"By which creeper-garland that Lakshmana plucked out and garlanded you, by this
creeper-garland of gaja-flowers alone your identification is marked. [4-14-8b, 9a]_END

B_4_C_1_126
BEGIN_
तम् मत्त मातङ्ग विलास गामी गच्छन्तम् अव्यग्र मनाः महात्मा |स लक्ष्मणो राघवम् अप्रमत्तो ररक्ष धर्मेण 
बलेन च एव || ४-१-१२७_END
BEGIN_
While that great soul Rama is walking ahead, that great souled Lakshmana whose stride is also like that 
of an elephant, and whose deeds are agreeable to Rama, vigilantly protected Rama with an un-despaired 
mind and even by his virtue and strength. [4-1-127]_END

B_4_C_12_21
BEGIN_
क्लान्तो रुधिर सिक्त अंगो प्रहारैः जर्जरी कृतः |
वालिना अभिद्रुतः क्रोधात् प्रविवेश महावनम् || ४-१२-२२_END
BEGIN_
Sugreeva is debilitated and enervated by Vali's thwacking till his limbs soaked in
blood, and he entered the great forest of Rishyamuka as Vali chased him. [4-12-22]_END

B_4_C_13_15
BEGIN_
एतद् राघव विस्तीर्णम् आश्रमम् श्रम नाशनम् |उद्यान वन संपन्नम् स्वादु मूल फल उदकम् || ४-१३-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Raghava, this spacious hermitage with abundant gardens and dainty tubers, fruits and water is a weary 
remover." Thus Sugreeva started telling Rama. [4-13-17]_END

B_4_C_15_0
BEGIN_
अथ तस्य निनादम् तम् सुग्रीवस्य महात्मनः |
शुश्राव अन्तःपुर गतो वाली भ्रातुर् अमर्षणः || ४-१५-१_END
BEGIN_
Then the illiberal Vali has clearly heard that outcry of his plain-spoken brother
Sugreeva from his palace chambers. [4-15-1]_END

B_4_C_11_50
BEGIN_
क्षिपता पादपाः च इमे संभग्नाः च असुरीम् तनुम् |
समन्तात् आश्रमम् पूर्णम् योजनम् मामकम् यदि || ४-११-५४
आगमिष्यति दुर्बुद्धिः व्यक्तम् स न भविष्यति |_END
BEGIN_
"By his hurling the demon's body these trees are also completely destroyed, hence he
ought not set his foot in a distance of one full yojana around this hermitage, and if that
evil-minded one places his foot then he evidently does not exist. [4-11-54, 55a]_END

B_4_C_14_8
BEGIN_
सोभासे अपि अधिकम् वीर लतया कण्ठसक्तया || ४-१४-९
विपरीत इव आकाशे सूर्यो नक्षत्र मालया |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh brave-one, you are shining forth with this creeper-garland laced at your neck
like the night time sun with a garland of stars. [4-14-9b, 10a]_END

B_4_C_1_127
BEGIN_
तौ ऋष्यमूकस्य समीप चारी चरन् ददर्श अद्भुत दर्शनीयौ |शाखा मृगाणाम् अधिपः तरस्वी वितत्रसे नैव चिचेष्ट 
चेष्टाम् || ४-१-१२८_END
BEGIN_
He who is the chief of Vanara-s, who moves about Mt. Rishyamuka, while he is meandering thereabout he 
happened to see those two who are so amazing for a look, namely Rama and Lakshmana, by which he is so 
frightened that he is petrified. [4-1-128]_END

B_4_C_12_22
BEGIN_
तम् प्रविष्टम् वनम् दृष्ट्वा वाली शाप भयात् ततः |
मुक्तो हि असि त्वम् इति उक्त्वा स निवृत्तो महाबलः || ४-१२-२३_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Sugreeva's entry into the forest of Rishyamuka, Vali said to him "you are
let off for now..." and saying so he returned to Kishkindha from there in view of fear from curse
of Sage Matanga. [4-12-23]_END

B_4_C_13_16
BEGIN_
अत्र सप्तजना नाम मुनयः संशित व्रताः |सप्त एव आसन् अधः शीर्षा नियतम् जल शायिनः || ४-१३-१८_END
BEGIN_
"There were hermits named sapta jana, Seven Persons, who were dourly vowed 
with their heads pendulous downward and legs up, as in shiirSa aasana , 
the upside-down yogic body posture, and who always reclined in water. [4-13-18]_END

B_4_C_15_1
BEGIN_
श्रुत्वा तु तस्य निनदम् सर्वभूत प्रकंपनम् |
मदः च एकपदे नष्टः क्रोधः च आपादितो महान् || ४-१५-२_END
BEGIN_
On hearing Sugreeva's outcry that is shuddering all beings Vali's insolence is
diminished as high furore superimposed on it. [4-15-2]_END

B_4_C_11_51
BEGIN_
ये च अस्य सचिवाः केचित् संश्रिता मामकम् वनम् || ४-११-५५
न च तैः इह वस्तव्य श्रुत्वा यांतु यथा सुखम् |_END
BEGIN_
"And some of his friends that are dependent on my woods shall not live here and they
may depart on hearing my words and solace themselves with my words. [4-11-55b, 56a]_END

B_4_C_14_9
BEGIN_
अद्य वालि समुत्थम् ते भयम् वैरम् च वानर || ४-१४-१०
एकेन अहम् प्रमोक्ष्यामि बाण मोक्षेण संयुगे |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh Vanara, today itself I will set you free from the fear and enmity whipped up by
Vali by releasing a single arrow in fight. [4-14-10b, 11a]_END

B_4_C_1_128
BEGIN_
स तौ महात्मा गज मन्द गामि शखा मृगः तत्र चिरन् चरन्तौ |दृष्ट्वा विषादम् परमम् जगाम चिन्ता परीतो भय 
भार मग्नः || ४-१-१२९_END
BEGIN_
On seeing those two Rama and Lakshmana who are advancing his way, he that great soul who is a tree-branch 
animal, and he who strides like an elephant, derived profound agony that muffled him in worry, and he 
is engulfed under the weight of his fear. [4-1-129]_END

B_4_C_12_23
BEGIN_
राघवो अपि सह भ्रात्रा सह चैव हनूमता |
तदेव वनम् आगच्छत् सुग्रीवो यत्र वानरः || ४-१२-२४_END
BEGIN_
Raghava also came to that forest, along with his brother Lakshmana and along with
Hanuma, where that monkey Sugreeva fled. [4-12-24]_END

B_4_C_13_17
BEGIN_
सप्त रात्रे कृत आहारा वायुना अचल वासिनः |दिवम् वर्ष शतैः याताः सप्तभिः सकलेवराः || ४-१३-१९_END
BEGIN_
"They were making diet on air alone that too once in seven days, and living unwaveringly in that way 
they practised their asceticism for seven hundred years and went to heavens with their bodies. [4-13-19]_END

B_4_C_15_2
BEGIN_
ततो रोष परीत अंगो वाली स कनक प्रभः |
उपरक्त इव आदित्यः सद्यो निष्प्रभताम् गतः || ४-१५-३_END
BEGIN_
Then, embitterment overspreading on all his limbs Vali with golden-hue is
immediately rendered non-luminous like the eclipsed sun. [4-15-3]_END

B_4_C_11_52
BEGIN_
ते अपि वा यदि तिष्टन्ति शपिष्ये तान् अपि ध्रुवम् || ४-११-५६
वने अस्मिन् मामके नित्यम् पुत्रवत् परिरक्षते |
पत्र अंकुर विनाशाय फल मूल अभवाय च || ४-११-५७_END
BEGIN_
"This forest of mine is always protected like my own son, and if the monkeys of Vali
wish to stay behind in this forest alone for further destruction of leaves or sprouts, or even for
the non-existence of fruits and tubers of this forest, defiantly they too will be cursed.
[4-11-57]_END

B_4_C_14_10
BEGIN_
मम दर्शय सुग्रीव वैरिणम् भ्रातृ रूपिणम् || ४-१४-११
वाली विनिहतो यावद् वने पांसुषु चेष्टते |_END
BEGIN_
"You show me your enemy in a brother's mien, oh, monkey, by then he will be rolling
in the dust of this forest eliminated by me. [4-14-11b, 12a]_END

B_4_C_1_129
BEGIN_
तम् आश्रमम् पुण्य सुखम् शरण्यम् सदैव शाखा मृग सेवितान्तम् |त्रस्ताः च दृष्ट्वा हरयोः अभिजग्मुः महौजसौ 
राघव लक्ष्मणौ तौ || ४-१-१३०_END
BEGIN_
On seeing those magnificent two, Rama and Lakshmana, the monkeys are frightened and fled towards the 
pious hermitage of Sage Matanga, which has an inland that is always adored by monkeys for it is consolatory 
and sheltering them. [4-1-130]_END

B_4_C_12_24
BEGIN_
तम् समीक्ष्य आगतम् रामम् सुग्रीवः सह लक्ष्मणम् |
ह्रीमान् दीनम् उवाच इदम् वसुधाम् अवलोकयन् || ४-१२-२५_END
BEGIN_
Seeing the arrival of Rama with Lakshmana, Sugreeva ashamedly turned his eyes down
to earth and piteously spoke this without eyeing Rama [4-12-25]_END

B_4_C_15_3
BEGIN_
वाली दंष्ट्रा करालः तु क्रोधाद् दीप्त अग्नि लोचनः |
भाति उत्पतित पद्माभः समृणाल इव ह्रदः || ४-१५-४_END
BEGIN_
With asymmetrical teeth and with burning fireball like eyes Vali is reflective of a
lake whose red-lotuses are uprooted leaving stalks afloat. [4-15-4]_END

B_4_C_13_18
BEGIN_
तेषाम् एतत् प्रभावेण द्रुम प्राकार संवृतम् |आश्रमम् सुदुराधर्षम् अपि स इन्द्रैः सुर असुरैः || ४-१३-२०_END
BEGIN_
"This hermitage that has encircling trees for its compound wall has become highly unassailable even 
for Indra together with all gods and demons. [4-13-20]_END

B_4_C_11_53
BEGIN_
दिवसः च अद्य मर्यादा यम् द्रष्टा श्वः अस्मि वानरम् |
बहु वर्ष सहस्राणि स वै शैलः भविष्यति || ४-११-५८_END
BEGIN_
"And today is the day of limit and the monkey whom I will see tomorrow, he will be
petrified for many thousand years to come. [4-11-58]_END

B_4_C_14_11
BEGIN_
यदि दृष्टि पथम् प्राप्तो जीवन् स विनिवर्तते || ४-१४-१२
ततो दोषेण मा गच्छेत् सद्यो गर्हेच्च माम् भवान् |_END
BEGIN_
"If he returns to live even after my espying him then immediately you can find fault
with me, you can even deride me. [4-14-12b, 13a]_END

B_4_C_12_25
BEGIN_
आह्वयस्व इति माम् उक्त्वा दर्शयित्वा च विक्रमम् |
वैरिणा घातयित्वा च किम् इदानीम् त्वया कृतम् || ४-१२-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Showing your dexterity you encouraged me to invite Vali for fight, but you got me
battered by my enemy, what is this done by you." [4-12-26]_END

B_4_C_13_19
BEGIN_
पक्षिणो वर्जयन्ति एतत् तथा अन्ये वनचारिणः |विशन्ति मोहाद् ये अपि अत्र न निवर्तन्ते ते पुनः || ४-१३-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Birds and other forest moving animals forbear this hermitage and those that unknowingly enter in there 
they do not return. [4-13-21]_END

B_4_C_15_4
BEGIN_
शब्दम् दुर्मर्षणम् श्रुत्वा निष्पपात ततो हरिः |
वेगेन च पद न्यासैर् दारयन् इव मेदिनीम् || ४-१५-५_END
BEGIN_
That monkey Vali then on hearing that intolerable noise bolted out of palace
chambers thumping his feet as though to shatter the earth. [4-15-5]_END

B_4_C_11_54
BEGIN_
ततः ते वानराः श्रुत्वा गिरम् मुनि समीरिताम् |
निश्चक्रमुः वनात् तस्मात् तान् दृष्ट्वा वालिर् अब्रवीत् || ४-११-५९_END
BEGIN_
"Then those monkeys on hearing the clear wording of the sage started out from that
forest, and on their coming to Kishkindha, Vali saw them and spoke this way to them. [4-11-59]_END

B_4_C_14_12
BEGIN_
प्रत्यक्षम् सप्त ते साला मया बाणेन दारिताः || ४-१४-१३
ततो वेत्सि बलेन अद्य वालिनम् निहतम् मया |_END
BEGIN_
"Seven saala trees are rived with a single of arrow of mine in your presence,
thereby be sure that Vali will be dispatched now, by my might. [4-14-13b, 14a]_END

B_4_C_12_26
BEGIN_
ताम् एव वेलाम् वक्तव्यम् त्वया राघव तत्त्वतः |
वालिनम् न निहन्मि इति ततो न अहम् इतो व्रजे || ४-१२-२७_END
BEGIN_
"You should have truly made it known at that time only, oh, Raghava, that you will
not kill Vali, then I would not have come here, to Kishkindha. [4-12-27]_END

B_4_C_15_5
BEGIN_
तम् तु तारा परिष्वज्य स्नेहाद् दर्शित सौहृदा |
उवाच त्रस्त संभ्रांता हित उदर्कम् इदम् वचः || ४-१५-६_END
BEGIN_
His wife Tara stepped in and showing goodwill and amity hugged him, for she is in
fear and bewilderment, and said this word that is beneficial in its futurity if Vali heeds it.
[4-15-6]_END

B_4_C_13_20
BEGIN_
विभूषण रवाअः च अत्र श्रूयंते सकलाक्षराः |तूर्य गीत स्वनाअः च अपि गन्धो दिव्यः च राघव || ४-१३-२२_END
BEGIN_
"From there artistically worded lyrical and instrumental tunes, and even the sounds of ornaments are 
audible, and oh, Raghava, one can sense a divine fragrance too. [4-13-22]_END

B_4_C_16_0
BEGIN_
ताम् एवम् ब्रुवतीम् ताराम् ताराधिप निभ आननाम् |वाली निर्भर्त्सयामास वचनम् च इदम् अब्रवीत् || ४-१६-१_END
BEGIN_
While Tara with a face that shines like the lord of stars is speaking thus, Vali dauntingly spoke to 
her with these words. [4-16-1]_END

B_4_C_11_55
BEGIN_
किम् भवन्तः समस्ताः च मतंग वन वासिनः |
मत् समीपम् अनुप्राप्ता अपि स्वस्ति वनौकसाम् || ४-११-६०_END
BEGIN_
" 'Why all of you dwellers of Matanga forest arrived in my presence, even so, are
you the dwellers of that forest safe?' Thus Vali asked all. [4-11-60]_END

B_4_C_14_13
BEGIN_
अनृतम् न उक्त पूर्वम् मे चिरम् कृच्छ्रे अपि तिष्ठता || ४-१४-१४
धर्म लोभ परीतेन न च वक्ष्ये कथंचन |_END
BEGIN_
"Just bound by the anxiousness to implement righteousness untruth is unsaid by me
earlier though I am involved in distresses for a long time, and hereafter it will not be said in
anywise. [4-14-14b, 15a]_END

B_4_C_12_27
BEGIN_
तस्य च एवम् ब्रुवाणस्य सुग्रीवस्य महात्मनः |
करुणम् दीनया वाचा राघवः पुनर् अब्रवीत् || ४-१२-२८_END
BEGIN_
Rama replied that great-souled Sugreeva who is speaking woefully with pathetic words
in this way. [4-12-28]_END

B_4_C_15_6
BEGIN_
साधु क्रोधम् इमम् वीर नदी वेगम् इव आगतम् |
शयनाद् उत्थितः काल्यम् त्यज भुक्ताम् इव स्रजम् || ४-१५-७_END
BEGIN_
"Oh brave one, you better gently leave off this anger that is coming on like a
gushing river as is done with an enjoyed chaplet on getting up from bed in early hours.
[4-15-7]_END

B_4_C_13_21
BEGIN_
त्रेताग्नयो अपि दीप्यन्ते धूमो हि एष प्रदृश्यते |वेष्टयन् इव वृक्ष अग्रान् कपोत अंग अरुणो घनः || 
४-१३-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Even the triadic ritual-fires glow there, and their thick and ochry coloured smoke like that of a reddish-brown 
pigeon is apparent muffling the treetops. [4-13-23]_END

B_4_C_16_1
BEGIN_
गर्जतो अस्य च सुसंरब्धम् भ्रातुः शत्रोर् विशेषतः |मर्षयिष्यामि केन कारणेन वरानने || ४-१६-२_END
BEGIN_
"He is an younger brother and an adversary in particular, oh, pretty-faced Tara, can I by any reason 
tolerate him when he kept raving on frenetically, tell me. [4-16-2]_END

B_4_C_11_56
BEGIN_
ततः ते कारणम् सर्वम् तथा शापम् च वालिनः |
शशंसुर् वानराः सर्वे वलिने हेममालिने || ४-११-६१_END
BEGIN_
"Then all of those monkeys have reported to Vali, the one with a golden
chest-pendant, all the reasons for their exit, likewise the curse to Vali. [4-11-61]_END

B_4_C_14_14
BEGIN_
सफलाम् च करिष्यामि प्रतिज्ञाम् जहि संभ्रमम् || ४-१४-१५
प्रसूतम् कलमक्षेत्रे वर्षेण इव शतक्रतुः |_END
BEGIN_
"As Indra fructifies the sprouted paddy field I will make happen my promise, hence
leave off your perplexity." [4-14-15b, 16a]_END

B_4_C_12_28
BEGIN_
सुग्रीव श्रूयताम् तात क्रोधः च व्यपनीयताम् |
कारणम् येन बाणो अयम् स मया न विसर्जितः || ४-१२-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Sugreeva, by which reason I have not let-off an arrow such as that of mine, that
reason may be heard and let the anger be discarded. [4-12-29]_END

B_4_C_15_7
BEGIN_
काल्यम् एतेन संग्रामम् करिष्यसि च वानर |
वीर ते शत्रु बाहुल्यम् फल्गुता वा न विद्यते || ४-१५-८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, monkey, you can fight with him in early hours of tomorrow, oh, brave one,
evidently you neither have divers enemies nor your valour is trivialised."_END

B_4_C_13_22
BEGIN_
एते वृक्षाः प्रकाशन्ते धूम संसक्त मस्तकाः |मेघ जाल प्रतिच्छन्ना वैदूर्य गिरयो यथा || ४-१३-२४_END
BEGIN_
"When that smoke is mantling their tops these trees are beaming forth like mountains of gems overlaid 
with clusters of clouds. [4-13-24]_END

B_4_C_16_2
BEGIN_
अधर्षितानाम् शूराणाम् समरेषु अनिवर्तिनाम् |धर्षणाम् अर्षणम् भीरु मरणात् अतिरिच्यते || ४-१६-३_END
BEGIN_
"To those valiant ones who neither give ground nor get assailed in wars, oh, shyly, endurance of a overweening 
war-whoop is more than death. [4-16-3]_END

B_4_C_11_57
BEGIN_
एतत् श्रुत्वा तदा वाली वचनम् वनर ईरितम् |
स महर्षिम् समासाद्य याचते स्म कृत अंजलिः || ४-११-६२_END
BEGIN_
"Then on hearing all those words narrated by monkeys Vali approached that great sage
and begged of him on becoming humble with palm-fold. [4-11-62]_END

B_4_C_14_15
BEGIN_
तद् आह्वान निमित्तम् च वालिनो हेममालिनः || ४-१४-१६
सुग्रीव कुरु तम् शब्दम् निष्पतेद् येन वानरः |_END
BEGIN_
"Thereby to invite that Vali with golden pendant, oh, Sugreeva, you make such a
war-cry by which that monkey Vali comes out. [4-14-16b, 17a]_END

B_4_C_12_29
BEGIN_
अलंकारेण वेषेण प्रमाणेन गतेन च |
त्वम् च सुग्रीव वाली च सदृशौ स्थः परस्परम् || ४-१२-३०_END
BEGIN_
"By ornamentation, attire, physicality and movements, you and Vali look-alike.
[4-12-30]_END

B_4_C_15_8
BEGIN_
सहसा तव निष्क्रामो मम तावत् न रोचते |
श्रूयताम् अभिधास्यामि यन् निमित्तम् निवार्यते || ४-१५-९_END
BEGIN_
"Your quick exiting is disagreeable for me, and what for you are dissuaded that may
be listened as I tell. [4-15-9]_END

B_4_C_13_23
BEGIN_
कुरु प्रणामम् धर्मात्मन् तेषाम् उद्दिश्य राघवः |लक्ष्मणेन सह भ्रात्रा प्रयतः संयत अंजलिः || ४-१३-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Offer salutations determinedly and adjoining palms addressing the sages called Seven Persons, oh Raghava, 
along with brother Lakshmana [4-13-25]_END

B_4_C_16_3
BEGIN_
सोढुम् न च समर्थो अहम् युद्ध कामस्य संयुगे |सुग्रीवस्य च संरंभम् हीन ग्रीवस्य गर्जतम् || ४-१६-४_END
BEGIN_
"I am incapable of withstanding that dumbly Sugreeva's bawling commotion desiring a brawling duel. [4-16-4]_END

B_4_C_11_58
BEGIN_
महर्षिः तम् अनादृत्य प्रविवेश आश्रमम् प्रति |
शाप धारण भीतः तु वाली विह्वलताम् गतः || ४-११-६३_END
BEGIN_
"The sage inconsiderate of Vali's request withdrew into hermitage, and fearing to
bear the brunt of the curse Vali was distraught and withdrew from that place. [4-11-63]_END

B_4_C_14_16
BEGIN_
जितकाशी जयश्लाघी त्वया च अधर्षितः पुरात् || ४-१४-१७
निष्पतिष्यति असंगेन वाली स प्रियसम्युगः |_END
BEGIN_
"Vali is a willing fighter who shines forth by his victories and one who is given
ovation for his triumphs, and undefeated by you as yet, such as he is he may be incited with
war-whoop so that he comes out without any hindrance. [4-14-17b, 18a]_END

B_4_C_12_30
BEGIN_
स्वरेण वर्चसा च एव प्रेक्षितेन च वानर |
विक्रमेण च वाक्यैः च व्यक्तिम् वाम् न उपलक्षये || ४-१२-३१_END
BEGIN_
"By your voice, bodily glow also thus in your looking, also in bravery and in
speech, oh monkey, I could not mark any difference. [4-12-31]_END

B_4_C_15_9
BEGIN_
पूर्वम् आपतितः क्रोधात् स त्वाम् आह्वयते युधि |
निष्पत्य च निरस्तः ते हन्यमानो दिशो गतः || ४-१५-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Earlier Sugreeva came assaulting and inviting you for a combat, and you also have
gone out and rendered him as a nonentity, and being battered by you he fled in all directions.
[4-15-10]_END

B_4_C_13_24
BEGIN_
प्रणमन्ति हि ये तेषाम् ऋषीणाम् भावित आत्मनाम् |न तेषाम् अशुभम् किंचित् शरीरे राम दृश्यते || ४-१३-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Those that offer salutations to those sages with contemplated souls will evince no bodily trauma in 
the least." Thus said Sugreeva to Rama. [4-13-26]_END

B_4_C_16_4
BEGIN_
न च कार्यो विषादः ते राघवम् प्रति मत् कृते |धर्मज्ञः च कृतज्ञः च कथम् पापम् करिष्यति || ४-१६-५_END
BEGIN_
"Also, you need not bother about Raghava's doing some harm to me, as I wonder how a diligent man and 
knower of virtue can commit sin. [4-16-5]_END

B_4_C_11_59
BEGIN_
ततः शाप भयात् भीत ऋश्यमूकम् महागिरिम् |
प्रवेष्टुम् न इच्छति हरिः द्रष्टुम् वा अपि नरेश्वर || ४-११-६४_END
BEGIN_
"Then, dreaded by the fear of curse that monkey Vali does not aspire to enter the
great mountain Rishyamuka, oh, people's lord, Rama, or he does not even wish to look at it." Thus
Sugreeva continued his narration. [4-11-64]_END

B_4_C_14_17
BEGIN_
रिपूणाम् धर्षितम् श्रुत्वा मर्षयन्ति न संयुगे || ४-१४-१८
जानन्तः तु स्वकम् वीर्यम् स्त्री समक्षम् विशेषतः |_END
BEGIN_
"One who is assertive of his own valour will not tolerate to hear enemy's daring in
a brawl, that too in the presence of ladies." So said Rama to Sugreeva. [4-14-18b, 19a]_END

B_4_C_12_31
BEGIN_
ततो अहम् रूप सादृश्यात् मोहितो वानरोत्तम |
न उत्सृजामि महावेगम् शरम् शत्रु निबर्हणम् || ४-१२-३२_END
BEGIN_
"Thereby, oh, great monkey, I have not released this great speeded and enemy
annihilating arrow of mine as I was confused in the similarity of your personalities. [4-12-32]_END

B_4_C_15_10
BEGIN_
त्वया तस्य निरस्तस्य पीडितस्य विशेषतः |
इह एत्य पुनर् आह्वानम् शंकाम् जनयति इव मे || ४-१५-११_END
BEGIN_
"He who is undone earlier by you, particularly after torturing by you, his coming
here again and inviting you for a duel is causing a doubt in me. [4-15-11]_END

B_4_C_13_25
BEGIN_
ततो रामः सह भ्रात्रा लक्ष्मणेन कृतांजलिः |समुद्दिश्य महात्मानः तान् ऋषीन् अभ्यवादयत् || ४-१३-२७_END
BEGIN_
Then Rama along with brother Lakshmana adjoined palms, addressed himself to the great-souled sages known 
as Seven Persons, and offered salutations to them. [4-13-27]_END

B_4_C_16_5
BEGIN_
निवर्तस्व सह स्त्रीभिः कथम् भूयो अनुगच्छसि |सौहृदम् दर्शितम् तावत् मयि भक्तिः त्वया कृता || ४-१६-६_END
BEGIN_
"How do you follow me again, you return with all these females, truly you have expressed your friendliness 
owing to your devotion to me. [4-16-6]_END

B_4_C_11_60
BEGIN_
तस्य अप्रवेशम् ज्ञात्वा अहम् इदम् राम महावनम् |
विचरामि सह अमात्यो विषादेन विवर्जितः || ४-११-६५_END
BEGIN_
"Knowing the inaccessibility of this forest to him I got rid of my agony, Rama, and
I move here about in this great forest along with my ministers. [4-11-65]_END

B_4_C_14_18
BEGIN_
स तु राम वचः श्रुत्वा सुग्रीवो हेमपिंगलः || ४-१४-१९
ननर्द क्रूर नादेन विनिर्भिन्दन् इव अम्बरम् |_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of Rama he that Sugreeva with golden yellow complexion blared a
gruesome blare as though to completely rend the sky. [4-14-19b, 20a]_END

B_4_C_12_32
BEGIN_
जीवित अन्तकरम् घोरम् सादृश्यात् तु विशंकितः |
मूलघातो न नौ स्याद्धि द्वयोः इति कृतो मया || ४-१२-३३_END
BEGIN_
"I was ambiguous by your similarities, as such I have not released this ghastly and
life-taking arrow, otherwise the basic object of ours will be ruined, isn't it. [4-12-33]_END

B_4_C_15_11
BEGIN_
दर्पः च व्यवसायः च यादृशः तस्य नर्दतः |
निनादस्य च संरंभो न एतत् अल्पम् हि कारणम् || ४-१५-१२_END
BEGIN_
"The arrogance and endeavour of the shouter, and even the rampage of his furore, all
these will not have a trivial reason, isn't it. [4-15-12]_END

B_4_C_13_26
BEGIN_
अभिवाद्य च धर्मात्मा रामो भ्राता च लक्ष्मणः |सुग्रीवो वानराअः चैव जग्मुः संहृष्ट मानसाः | ४-१३-२८_END
BEGIN_
That righteous Rama along with brother Lakshmana, Sugreeva and other monkeys having worshipped those 
sages proceeded to Kishkindha well-pleased at heart. [4-13-28]_END

B_4_C_16_6
BEGIN_
प्रति योत्स्यामि अहम् गत्वा सुग्रीवम् जहि संभ्रमम् |दर्पम् च अस्य विनेष्यामि न च प्राणैर् वियोक्ष्यते 
|| ४-१६-७_END
BEGIN_
"You may do away with your perplexity as I will retaliate Sugreeva on my going there only to drive him 
and his arrogance out, but without letting his lives loose. [4-16-7]_END

B_4_C_11_61
BEGIN_
एषो अस्थिनिचयः तस्य दुन्दुभेः संप्रकाशते |
वीर्य उत्सेकात् निरस्तस्य गिरि कूट निभो महान् || ४-११-६६_END
BEGIN_
"This huge heap of bones that is shining forth like a mountaintop is that of
Dundubhi, which Vali once hurled by the vanity of his valour. [4-11-66]_END

B_4_C_14_19
BEGIN_
तत्र शब्देन वित्रस्ता गावो यान्ति हतप्रभाः || ४-१४-२०
राजदोष परामृष्टाः कुलस्त्रिय इव आकुलाः |_END
BEGIN_
By that sound of Sugreeva the splendour of cows is marred and they are running
helter-skelter like the well-born ladies who are mishandled by invaders due to the misrule of their
own king. [4-14-20b, 21a]_END

B_4_C_12_33
BEGIN_
त्वयि वीर विपन्ने हि अज्ञान् लाघवान् मया |
मौढ्यम् च मम बाल्यम् च ख्यापितम् स्यात् कपीस्वर || ४-१२-३४_END
BEGIN_
"When my unawareness and fallacy hazardously afflicts none but you in the form of my
own arrow, oh, brave lord of monkeys, then I will be establishing my own imbecility and naivety,
isn't it. [4-12-34]_END

B_4_C_15_12
BEGIN_
न असहायम् अहम् मन्ये सुग्रीवम् तम् इह आगतम् |
अवष्टब्ध सहायः च यम् आश्रित्य एष गर्जति || ४-१५-१३_END
BEGIN_
"I do not think that Sugreeva has come here unaccompanied, and on whom he is
dependant must be an unflinching support foregathered by Sugreeva. [4-15-13]_END

B_4_C_13_27
BEGIN_
ते गत्वा दूरम् अध्वानम् तस्मात् सप्त जन आश्रमात् |ददृशुः ताम् दुराधर्षाम् किष्किन्धाम् वालि पालिताम् 
|| ४-१३-२९_END
BEGIN_
Having gone a long way from that hermitage of Seven Persons they have seen that unassailable and Vali 
ruled city namely Kishkindha. [4-13-29]_END

B_4_C_16_7
BEGIN_
अहम् हि अजि स्थितस्य अस्य करिष्यामि यत् ईप्सितम् |वृक्षैः मुष्टि प्रहारैः च पीडितः प्रति यास्यति 
|| ४-१६-८_END
BEGIN_
"As he is firmed up for a combat, I will indeed have to effectuate what his desire is, by caning with 
trees and fistfights, by which roughed up he returns. [4-16-8]_END

B_4_C_11_62
BEGIN_
इमे च विपुलाः सालाः सप्त शाखा अवलंबिनः |
यत्र एकम् घटते वाली निष् पत्रयितुम् ओजसा || ४-११-६७_END
BEGIN_
"Also these are the seven enormous sala trees full with their branches, and Vali is
capable to make each of them leafless by his vigour, of course, one at a time. [4-11-67]_END

B_4_C_14_20
BEGIN_
द्रवन्ति च मृगाः शीघ्रम् भग्ना;इव रणे हयाः |
पतन्ति च खगा भूमौ क्षीण पुण्या इव ग्रहाः || ४-१४-२१_END
BEGIN_
And deer are hurriedly fleeing like war worsted horses, and the sky-flying birds are
falling to ground like planets or stars when their merit diminishes. [4-14-21b, c]_END

B_4_C_12_34
BEGIN_
दत्त अभय वधो नाम पातकम् महत् अद्भुतम् |
अहम् च लक्ष्मणः च एव सीत च वरवर्णिनी || ४-१२-३५
त्वत् अधीना वयम् सर्वे वने अस्मिन् शरणम् भवान् |_END
BEGIN_
"Eliminating one who is protected means a terrifying sin of highest order, even so,
myself and Lakshmana and also thus Seetha with her exquisite glow are all dependent on you, and you
are our shelterer in this forest. [4-12-35, 36a]_END

B_4_C_15_13
BEGIN_
प्रकृत्या निपुणः चैव बुद्धिमान् चैव वानरः |
न अपरीक्षित वीर्येण सुग्रीवः सख्यम् एष्यति || ४-१५-१४_END
BEGIN_
"By his nature Sugreeva is an expert and even so a clever one, and he does not enter
into friendship with anyone without examining his mettle. [4-15-14]_END

B_4_C_13_28
BEGIN_
ततस्तु रामानुज राम वानराःप्रगृह्य शस्त्राणि उदित उग्र तेजसा |पुरीम् सुरेश आत्मज वीर्य पालिताम्
वधाय शत्रोः पुनर् आगताः इह || ४-१३-३०_END
BEGIN_
Then Rama's bother Lakshmana, Rama, and other monkeys wielding their weapons and flaring with their 
upsurged fiery again came to eliminate that enemy Vali to the city that is ruled by the brawn of the 
same Vali, the son of Indra. [4-13-30]_END

B_4_C_16_8
BEGIN_
न मे गर्वितम् आयस्तम् सहिष्यति दुरात्मवान् |कृतम् तारे सहायत्वम् दर्शितम् सौहृदम् मयि || ४-१६-९_END
BEGIN_
"My nerve and pace of combat will be insufferable to that malign minded Sugreeva, oh, Tara, you have 
offered your helping suggestion and you have shown all your friendliness to me, it is enough. [4-16-9]_END

B_4_C_11_63
BEGIN_
एतत् अस्य असमम् वीर्यम् मया राम प्रकाशितम् |
कथम् तम् वालिनम् हन्तुम् समरे शक्ष्यसे नृप || ४-११-६८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, I am apprising all this to tell about the unequalled vitality of Vali,
and oh, king, then how is it possible for you to eliminate Vali in war." Thus Sugreeva enquired
with Rama. [4-11-68]_END

B_4_C_14_21
BEGIN_
ततः स जीमूत कृत प्रणादो
नादम् हि अमुंचत् त्वरया प्रतीतः |
सूर्यात्मजः शौर्य विवृद्ध तेजाः
सरित् पतिर्वा अनिल चंचल ऊर्मिः || ४-१४-२२_END
BEGIN_
Sugreeva, the son of Sun, who is well-known for cloud like thundering, and whose
vigour is now reinforced by his bravery, then promptly released an oceanic roar like an ocean with
splashing waves drifted by gales. [4-14-22]_END

B_4_C_12_35
BEGIN_
तस्मात् युध्यस्व भूयस्त्वम् मा शंकी च वानर || ४-१२-३६
एतन् मुहूर्ते तु मया पश्य वालिनम् आहवे |
निरस्तम् इषुणा एकेन वेष्टमानम् महीतले || ४-१२-३७_END
BEGIN_
"Therefore, oh, monkey, again you fight with him without doubting me, and I will
render him ineffective at this moment only with a single arrow of mine, and you can see Vali
squirming on the ground. [4-12-36, 37],_END

B_4_C_15_14
BEGIN_
पूर्वम् एव मया वीर श्रुतम् कथयतो वचः |
अंगदस्य कुमारस्य वक्ष्यामि अद्य हितम् वचः || ४-१५-१५_END
BEGIN_
"I am already briefed by our son Angada's information, and what I have heard I will
now relate that helpful word to you. [4-15-15]_END

B_4_C_16_9
BEGIN_
शापिता असि मम प्राणैः निवर्तस्व जनेन च |अलम् जित्वा निवर्तिष्ये तम् अहम् भ्रातरम् रणे || ४-१६-१०_END
BEGIN_
"I adjured you on my lives, return with your followers, and I shall return to you on easily defeating 
and returning that 'brother of mine." Said Vali to Tara. [4-16-10]_END

B_4_C_11_64
BEGIN_
तथा बृउवाणम् सुग्रीवम् प्रहसन् लक्ष्मणो अब्रवीत् |
कस्मिन् कर्मणि निर्वृत्ते श्रद्दध्या वालिनः वधम् || ४-११-६९_END
BEGIN_
When Sugreeva spoke that way Lakshmana a little smiled and asked him, "On performing
which act do you confide in the possibility of Vali's elimination?" [4-11-69]_END

B_4_C_12_36
BEGIN_
अभिज्ञानम् कुरुष्व त्वम् आत्मनो वानरेश्वर |
येन त्वाम् अभिजानीयाम् द्वन्द्व युद्धम् उपागतम् || ४-१२-३८_END
BEGIN_
"You have an identification for yourself, oh lord of monkeys, by which you can be
identified when you are engaged in duel. [4-12-38]_END

B_4_C_15_15
BEGIN_
अंगदः तु कुमरो अयम् वनांतम् उपनिर्गतः |
प्रवृत्तिः तेन कथिता चारैः असीत् निवेदिता || ४-१५-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Son Angada said this account when he returned from forests, and to him spies are
said to have reported this. [4-15-16]_END

B_4_C_16_10
BEGIN_
तम् तु तारा परिष्वज्य वालिनम् प्रिय वादिनी |चकार रुदती मन्दम् दक्षिणा सा प्रदक्षिणम् || ४-१६-११_END
BEGIN_
She that pleasant articulator and talented Tara then hugged and circumabulated Vali, suppressing her 
moaning, as an honour to the braver. [4-16-11]_END

B_4_C_11_65
BEGIN_
तम् उवाचथ सुग्रीवः सप्त सालन् इमान् पुरा |
एवम् एकैकशो वाली विव्याथ अथ स असकृत् || ४-११-७०_END
BEGIN_
Then Sugreeva said to Lakshmana, "earlier Vali used to agitate each of the trees,
one after the other, on many occasions." [4-11-70]_END

B_4_C_12_37
BEGIN_
गज पुष्पीम् इमाम् फुल्लाम् उत्पाट्य शुभ लक्षणाम् |
कुरु लक्ष्मण कण्ठे अस्य सुग्रीवस्य महात्मनः || ४-१२-३९_END
BEGIN_
"Lakshmana, pick up this gaja creeper that is beautiful in its appearance and let
this noble souled Sugreeva be garlanded with that." So said Rama to Lakshmana. [4-12-39]_END

B_4_C_15_16
BEGIN_
अयोध्य अधिपतेः पुत्रौ शूरौ समर दुर्जयौ |
इक्ष्वाकूणाम् कुले जातौ प्रथितौ राम लक्ष्मणौ || ४-१५-१७
सुग्रीव प्रिय कामार्थम् प्राप्तौ तत्र दुरासदौ |_END
BEGIN_
"Those that are born in Ikshvaku dynasty, sons of the king of Ayodhya, valiant and
unconquerable ones in war, called Rama and Lakshmana are there in this country. These two
unassailable ones have chanced there at Sugreeva's place to fulfil the longing desire of Sugreeva.
[4-15-17, 18a]_END

B_4_C_16_11
BEGIN_
ततः स्वस्त्ययनम् कृत्वा मंत्रवित् विजय एषिणी |अंतःपुरम् सह स्त्रीभिः प्रविष्टा शोक मोहिता || ४-१६-१२_END
BEGIN_
Then she who is a hymnodist that Tara has performed a hymnal bon voyage wishing triumph to Vali, and 
entered palace chambers along with other females, disoriented by her own sadness. [4-16-12]_END

B_4_C_11_66
BEGIN_
रामो निर्दारयेद् एषाम् बाणेन एकेन च द्रुमम् |
वालिनम् निहतम् मन्ये दृष्ट्वा रामस्य विक्रमम् || ४-११-७१_END
BEGIN_
"If Rama can rend one tree out of the seven with only one arrow, then on seeing
Rama's valour I can construe that Vali is utterly dead at his hand. [4-11-71]_END

B_4_C_12_38
BEGIN_
ततो गिरि तटे जाताम् उत्पाट्य कुसुमायुताम् |
लक्ष्मणो गज पुष्पीम् ताम् तस्य कण्ठे व्यसर्जयत् || ४-१२-४०_END
BEGIN_
Then Lakshmana plucked that gaja creeper with flowers growing at the foot of the
mountain, and slung it like a garland around the neck of that Sugreeva. [4-12-40] n_END

B_4_C_15_17
BEGIN_
स ते भ्रातुर् हि विख्यातः सहायो रण कर्मणि || ४-१५-१८
रामः पर बलमर्दी युगान्त अग्निः इव उत्थितः |_END
BEGIN_
"He is an acclaimed one for his warfare, and like the fire flaring up at the end of
era he shatters the strength of enemies, and he is Rama your brother's helpmate, they say so.
[4-15-18b, 19a]_END

B_4_C_16_12
BEGIN_
प्रविष्टायाम् तु तारायाम् सह स्त्रीभिः स्वम् आलयम् |नगर्या निर्ययौ क्रुद्धो महा सर्प इव श्वसन् || 
४-१६-१३_END
BEGIN_
On Tara entering her own palace chambers along with other females, Vali emerged out of the city hissing 
like an infuriated great snake. [4-16-13]_END

B_4_C_12_39
BEGIN_
स तथा शुशुभे श्रीमान् लतया कण्ठ सक्तया |
मालया इव बलाकानाम् ससंध्य इव तोयदः || ४-१२-४१_END
BEGIN_
He that prosperous Sugreeva with that flowery-creeper adorning his neck then shone
forth like a black rain cloud against a backdrop of rich ochry colour of sunset, and with a train
of herons adorning that cloud like a garland. [4-12-41]_END

B_4_C_11_67
BEGIN_
हतस्य महिषस्य अस्थि पादेन एकेन लक्ष्मण |
उद्यम्य प्रक्षिपेत् च अपि तरसा द्वे धनुः शते || ४-११-७२_END
BEGIN_
"Lakshmana, if he lifts and kicks the skeleton of this dead buffalo by the might of
his foot, and makes it fall at a distance of two hundred bow-lengths, I can confide." So said
Sugreeva to Lakshmana. [4-11-72]_END

B_4_C_15_18
BEGIN_
निवास वृक्षः साधूनाम् आपन्नानाम् परा गतिः | ४-१५-१९
आर्तानाम् संश्रयः चैव यशसः च एक भाजनम् |_END
BEGIN_
"And he is said to the habitable tree for the polite, the ultimate course for the
woebegone, a hospice for the agonised, and for grace Rama is the only abode. [4-15-19b, 20a]_END

B_4_C_16_13
BEGIN_
स निःश्वस्य महारोषो वाली परम वेगवान् |सर्वतः चारयन् दृष्टिम् शत्रु दर्शन कांक्षया || ४-१६-१४_END
BEGIN_
He that highly rancorous Vali suspired with high audacity and spread his sight everywhere intending 
to sight his enemy. [4-16-14]_END

B_4_C_12_40
BEGIN_
विभ्राजमानो वपुषा राम वाक्य समाहितः |
जगाम सह रामेण किष्किंधाम् पुनराप सः || ४-१२-४२_END
BEGIN_
He that Sugreeva whose physique became effulgent by that creeper-garland is again
emboldened by Rama's words, and he again advanced to Kishkindha with Rama, and reached it again.
[4-12-42]_END

B_4_C_11_68
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा तु सुग्रीवो रामम् रक्तान्त लोचनम् |
ध्यत्वा मुहूर्तम् काकुत्स्थम् पुनरेव वचो अब्रवीत् || ४-११-७३_END
BEGIN_
