Sugreeva paused for a while on saying thus to Rama, for Rama's eye-corners are
reddened with anger towards Vali, and then Sugreeva again spoke to Rama. [4-11-73]_END

B_4_C_15_19
BEGIN_
ज्ञान विज्ञान संपन्नो निदेशो निरतः पितुः || ४-१५-२०
धातूनाम् इव शैलेन्द्रो गुणानाम् आकरो महान् |_END
BEGIN_
"He is endowed with the knowledge of mundane and ultra-mundane things, he always
abides in the directives of his father, and as with Mt. Himalayas for all natural elements he is
the greatest mine of merits. [4-15-20b, 21a]_END

B_4_C_16_14
BEGIN_
स ददर्श ततः श्रीमान् सुग्रीवम् हेम पिङ्गलम् |सुसंवीतम् अवष्टब्धम् दीप्यमानम् इव अनलम् || ४-१६-१५_END
BEGIN_
Then that celebrated Vali saw Sugreeva who is in golden-ochre hue, whose girdle cloth is tightened for 
a fight, and who is with an air of self-confidence, blazing like fiery-fire. [4-16-15]_END

B_4_C_11_69
BEGIN_
शूरः च शूरमानी च प्रख्यात बल पौरुषः |
बलवान् वानरः वाली संयुगेषु अपराजितः || ४-११-७४_END
BEGIN_
"Vali is a mighty monkey, an intrepid one, who esteems his own intrepidity, and one
who is well renowned by his might and tenacity, and in combats he is an undefeated one.
[4-11-74]_END

B_4_C_15_20
BEGIN_
तत् क्षमो न विरोधः ते सह तेन महात्मना || ४-१५-२१
दुर्जयेन अप्रमेयेण रामेण रण कर्मसु |_END
BEGIN_
"By that reason, with that unconquerable on in conflicts, an imponderable one and a
great-soul Rama, your enmity is inapposite. [4-15-21b, 22a]_END

B_4_C_16_15
BEGIN_
तम् स दृष्ट्वा महाबाहुः सुग्रीवम् पर्यवस्थितम् |गाढम् परिदधे वासो वाली परम कोपिनः || ४-१६-१६_END
BEGIN_
That strong armed Vali who is highly provoked has also tightened his girdle cloth on seeing proximately 
available Sugreeva. [4-16-16]_END

B_4_C_15_21
BEGIN_
शूर वक्ष्यामि ते किंचिन् न च इच्छामि अभ्यसूयितुम् || ४-१५-२२
श्रूयताम् क्रियताम् चैव तव वक्ष्यामि यद् हितम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh dauntless one, I tell you this much that you shall not become overcritical of
him, and what I say is beneficial to you that may now be listened and even implemented. [4-15-22b,
23a]_END

B_4_C_11_70
BEGIN_
दृश्यन्ते च अस्य कर्माणि दुष्कराणि सुरैः अपि |
यानि संचिन्त्य भीतः अहम् ऋष्यमूकम् उपाश्रितः || ४-११-७५_END
BEGIN_
"His deeds that are impracticable even for gods are obvious, and scared for
recollecting them I took shelter of Mt. Rishyamuka. [4-11-75]_END

B_4_C_16_16
BEGIN_
स वाली गाढ संवीतो मुष्टिम् उद्यम्य वीर्यवान् |सुग्रीवम् एव अभिमुखो ययौ योद्धुम् कृत क्षणः || ४-१६-१७_END
BEGIN_
He that formidable Vali strongly tightening his girdle-cloth too, and proceeded towards Sugreeva in 
a well timed manner uplifting fists to fight him off. [4-16-17]_END

B_4_C_11_71
BEGIN_
तम् अजय्यम् अधृष्यम् च वानरेन्द्रम् अमर्षणम् |
विचिन्तयन् न मुंचामि ॠष्यमूकम् अमुम् तु अहम् || ४-११-७६_END
BEGIN_
"Concluding that the lord of monkeys Vali to be an unconquerable, unattackable,
unsympathetic one I am not leaving this Mt. Rishyamuka. [4-11-76]_END

B_4_C_15_22
BEGIN_
यौवराज्येन सुग्रीवम् तूर्णम् साधु अभिषेचय || ४-१५-२३
विग्रहम् मा कृथा वीर भ्रात्रा राजन् यवीयसा |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, king, let Sugreeva be decorously and quickly anointed as prince regent, and oh,
resolute one, let there be no hostility to your own younger brother. [4-15-23b, 24a]_END

B_4_C_16_17
BEGIN_
श्लिष्टम् मुष्टिम् समुद्यम्य संरब्धतरम् आगतः |सुग्रीवो अपि समुद्दिश्य वालिनम् हेम मालिनम् || ४-१६-१८_END
BEGIN_
Even Sugreeva has come at that imprudent Vali with golden pendant, on tightening his fists, lifting 
them up at the ready, and aiming them well at Vali. [4-16-18]_END

B_4_C_11_72
BEGIN_
उद्विग्नः शंकितः च अहम् विचरामि महावने |
अनुरक्तैः सह अमात्यैः हनुमत् प्रमुखैः वीरैः || ४-११-७७_END
BEGIN_
"I am moving about these forests along with earnest ministers like Hanuma and other
significant ones, only because I am disconcerted and sceptical of him. [4-11-77]_END

B_4_C_15_23
BEGIN_
अहम् हि ते क्षमम् मन्ये तेन रामेण सौहृदम् || ४-१५-२४
सुग्रीवेण च संप्रीतिम् वैरम् उत्सृज्य दूरतः |_END
BEGIN_
"Achieving unanimity with Sugreeva and solidarity with Rama by discarding enmity, in
effect is appropriate for you, thus I deem. [4-15-24b, 25a]_END

B_4_C_16_18
BEGIN_
तम् वाली क्रोध ताम्राक्षः सुग्रीवम् रण कोविदम् |आपतंतम् महा वेगम् इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् || ४-१६-१९_END
BEGIN_
Vali spoke this word to that Sugreeva who is swooping down on him, whose eyes are reddened in fury, 
and who is an expert and expeditious in fighting. [4-16-19]_END

B_4_C_11_73
BEGIN_
उपलब्धम् च मे श्लाघ्यम् सन् मित्रम् मित्र वत्सल |
त्वाम् अहम् पुरुषव्याघ्र हिमवन्तम् इव आश्रितः || ४-११-७८_END
BEGIN_
"I chanced upon a laudable and true friend in you, oh, Rama, the patron of friends,
hence I take shelter in you, oh, tigerly man, for you are the final resort for those seeking
salvation, like Mt. Himavan. [4-11-78]_END

B_4_C_15_24
BEGIN_
लालनीयो हि ते भ्राता यवीयान् एष वानरः || ४-१५-२५
तत्र वा सन्निहस्थो वा सर्वथा बन्धुः एव ते |_END
BEGIN_
"This Sugreeva is your younger brother and you should be keen about him, isn't it...
and whether he is here or there in Rishyamuka he is just your brother. [4-15-25b, 26a]_END

B_4_C_16_19
BEGIN_
एष मुष्टिर् महान् बद्धो गाढः सुनियत अंगुलिः |मया वेग विमुक्तः ते प्राणान् आदाय यास्यति || ४-१६-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Properly clenching fingers this great fist of mine is firmly clenched, and it will unclench only on 
taking your lives when I pitch this on you at full speed." So said Vali threateningly to Sugreeva. [4-16-20]_END

B_4_C_15_25
BEGIN_
नहि तेन समम् बन्धुम् भुवि पश्यामि किंचन || ४-१५-२६
दान मानादि सत्कर्रैः कुरुष्व प्रत्यनन्तरम् |
वैरम् एतत् सम् उत्स्रृज्य तव पार्श्वे स तिष्ठतु || ४-१५-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed, I do not see anyone on earth a coequal to him in kindred spirit, hence
leave off this enmity and honour him with bestowals and felicitations as an insider, and retain him
at your side. [4-15-26b, 27]_END

B_4_C_11_74
BEGIN_
किम् तु तस्य बलज्ञः अहम् दुर्भ्रातुः बलशालिनः |
अप्रत्यक्षम् तु मे वीर्यम् समरे तव राघव || ४-११-७९_END
BEGIN_
"I know the might of that mighty brother-the-malice of mine, and oh, Raghava, but
your valour in combat is imprecise to me." [4-11-79]_END

B_4_C_16_20
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु सुग्रीवः क्रुद्धो वालिनम् अब्रवीत् |तव च एष हरन् प्राणान् मुष्टिः पततु मूर्धनि || 
४-१६-२१_END
BEGIN_
Thus said, Sugreeva with high dudgeon said, "this fist of mine shall fall on your forehead plundering 
your lives." [4-16-21]_END

B_4_C_11_75
BEGIN_
न खलु अहम् त्वाम् तुलये न अवमन्ये न भीषये |
कर्मभिः तस्य भीमैः च कातर्यम् जनितम् मम || ४-११-८०_END
BEGIN_
"Definitely I am neither examining, nor demeaning, nor intimidating you, but his
macabre exploits caused cowardice in me. [4-11-80]_END

B_4_C_15_26
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवो विपुल ग्रीवो महाबन्धुः मतः तव |
भ्रातृ सौहृदम् आलंब्य न अन्या गति इह अस्ति ते || ४-१५-२८_END
BEGIN_
"That boisterously voiced Sugreeva is indisputably an excellent kinsman of yours,
and hence brace yourself with the fondness of brotherhood, as there is no other way out to you.
[4-15-28]_END

B_4_C_16_21
BEGIN_
ताडितः तेन तम् क्रुद्धः समभिक्रम्य वेगतः |अभवत् शोणित उद्गारी सापीड इव पर्वतः || ४-१६-२२_END
BEGIN_
Coming near instantaneously Vali hit him, whereby Sugreeva is enraged and became like a mountain streaming 
blood in its torrents. [4-16-22]_END

B_4_C_11_76
BEGIN_
कामम् राघव ते वाणी प्रमाणम् धैर्यम् आकृतिः |
सूचयन्ति परम् तेजो भस्म च्छन्नम् इव अनलम् || ४-११-८१_END
BEGIN_
"It is definite, oh, Raghava, your word, courage, and physique denote some sublime
radiance in you, as with ash covered fire." So said Sugreeva to Rama. [4-11-81]_END

B_4_C_16_22
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवेण तु निःशंकम् सालम् उत्पाट्य तेजसा |गात्रेषु अभिहतो वाली वज्रेण इव महा गिरिः || ४-१६-२३_END
BEGIN_
But Sugreeva unhesitatingly uprooted a saala tree with his force and thrashed the limbs of Vali as with 
the thunderbolt thrashing a great mountain. [4-16-23]_END

B_4_C_15_27
BEGIN_
यदि ते मत् प्रियम् कार्यम् यदि च अवैषि माम् हिताम् |
याच्यमानः प्रियत्वेन साधु वाक्यम् कुरुष्व मे || ४-१५-२९_END
BEGIN_
"If you look upon to do my favoured deed, and if you look upon me as an expedient
one, I beg of you in our loving attachment that my gentle word of advise be done. [4-15-29]_END

B_4_C_16_23
BEGIN_
स तु वृक्षेण निर्भग्नः साल ताडन विह्वलः |गुरु भार भर आक्रान्ता नौः ससार्था इव सागरे || ४-१६-२४_END
BEGIN_
But Vali when thwacked with saala tree had staggered and looked like a tossing ship in an ocean filled 
with heavy weight of merchandise and brimming with merchants, but on the brink of wrecking. [4-16-24]_END

B_4_C_11_77
BEGIN_
तस्य तद् वचनम् श्रुत्वा सुग्रीवस्य महत्मनः |
स्मित पूर्वम् अथः रामः प्रति उवाच हरिम् प्रति || ४-११-८२_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that word of great-souled Sugreeva, Rama smilingly replied that monkey in
his turn. [4-11-82]_END

B_4_C_15_28
BEGIN_
प्रसीद पथ्यम् श्रुणु जल्पितम् हि मे
न रोषम् एव अनुविधातुम् अर्हसि |
क्षमो हि ते कोशल राज सूनुना
न विग्रहः शक्र सम तेजसा || ४-१५-३०_END
BEGIN_
"Be graceful and it behove you to listen to my small but expedient talk, and
following up rancour alone is unbecoming of you, thereby your confrontation with the Prince of
Kosala will be unpardonable for his dynamism equals that of Indra." Thus Tara spoke to her husband
Vali. [4-15-30]_END

B_4_C_17_0
BEGIN_
ततः शरेण अभिहतो रामेण रण कर्कशः |पपात सहसा वाली निकृत्तैव पादपः || ४-१७-१_END
BEGIN_
When Rama's arrow hit him then Vali, the scourger in war, suddenly fell down like a hewed down tree. 
[4-17-1]_END

B_4_C_16_24
BEGIN_
तौ भीम बल विक्रान्तौ सुपर्ण सम वेगिनौ |प्रयुद्धौ घोर वपुषौ चन्द्र सूर्यौ इव अंबरे || ४-१६-२५
परस्परम् अमित्र घ्नौ च्छिद्र अन्वेषण तत्परौ |_END
BEGIN_
Those two, Vali and Sugreeva, with their sensational energy, triumphing zeal, frightful physiques, swiftness 
as good as the Divine Eagle Garuda, vigilance in exploring perilous body parts of one another, ravagement 
of their own enemies fought frighteningly, like the sun and moon in the sky, which is inconceivable. 
[4-16-25, 26a]_END

B_4_C_15_29
BEGIN_
तदा हि तारा हितम् एव वाक्यम्
तम् वालिनम् पथ्यम् इदम् बभाषे |
न रोचते तद् वचनम् हि तस्य
काल अभिपन्नस्य विनाश काले || ४-१५-३१_END
BEGIN_
Then, though Tara spoke beneficial and advisable words they are unimpressive to Vali
for he is impounded by fatality and driven by time to his doom. [4-15-31]_END

B_4_C_11_78
BEGIN_
यदि न प्रत्ययो अस्मासु विक्रमे तव वानर |
प्रत्ययम् समरे श्लाघ्यम् अहम् उत्पादयामि ते || ४-११-८३_END
BEGIN_
"If you are unable to confide in the intrepidity of ours, oh, monkey, I shall
ingrain commendable confidence in you with respect to our action." Thus Rama said to Sugreeva.
[4-11-83]_END

B_4_C_17_1
BEGIN_
स भूमौ न्यस्त सर्वांगः तप्त कांचन भूषणः |अपतत् देव राजस्य मुक्त रश्मिर् इव ध्वजः || ४-१७-२_END
BEGIN_
He who glittered with pure golden ornaments, that Vali fell down on earth while all of his limbs sank 
to dust, like the flag of Indra when released from its ropes. [4-17-2]_END

B_4_C_16_25
BEGIN_
ततो अवर्धत वाली तु बल वीर्य समन्वितः || ४-१६-२६सूर्य पुत्रो महावीर्यः सुग्रीवः परिहीयत |_END
BEGIN_
But Vali being the possessor of might and vigour progressed and though greatly mighty is son of sun, 
Sugreeva, regressed. [4-16-26b, 27a]_END

B_4_C_11_79
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा तु सुग्रीवम् सान्त्वयन् लक्ष्मणाग्रजः |
राघवो दुन्दुभेः कायम् पाद अंगुष्ठेन लीलया || ४-११-८४
तोलयित्वा महाबाहुः चिक्षेप दश योजनम् |
असुरस्य तनुम् शुष्कम् पादांगुष्टेन वीर्यवान् || ४-११-८५_END
BEGIN_
Saying so to Sugreeva in a comforting manner, he that dextrous, vigorous Rama, the
elder brother of Lakshmana sportively flipped the skeleton of Dundubhi with his big toe, and
flicked that withered body of the demon with his big toe itself to a ten yojana distance without
lifting his foot. [4-11-84, 85]_END

B_4_C_17_2
BEGIN_
अस्मिन् निपतिते भूमौ हरि ऋषाणाम् गणेश्वरे |नष्ट चन्द्रम् इव व्योम न व्यराजत मेदिनी || ४-१७-३_END
BEGIN_
On the fall of that lord of hosts of monkeys and bears onto earth, unilluminated is the earth like the 
welkin that has forsooth lost its moon. [4-17-3]_END

B_4_C_11_80
BEGIN_
क्षिप्तम् दृष्ट्वा ततः कायम् सुग्रीवः पुनर् अब्रवीत् |
लक्ष्मणस्य अग्रतो रामम् तपन्तम् इव भास्करम्
हरीणाम् अग्रतो वीरम् इदम् वचनम् अर्थवत् || ४-११-८६_END
BEGIN_
Then on seeing at the hurled body, and at valiant Rama who by now is like the
blazing sun, again Sugreeva said this meaningful word to Rama in the presence of Lakshmana and
other monkeys. [4-11-86]_END

B_4_C_16_26
BEGIN_
वालिना भग्न दर्पः तु सुग्रीवो मन्द विक्रमः || ४-१६-२७वालिनम् प्रति सामर्षो दर्शयामास राघवम् |_END
BEGIN_
Sugreeva became retardant in aggression when Vali routed his pride and then he exasperatedly started 
searching for Raghava to counteract Vali. [4-16-27]_END

B_4_C_17_3
BEGIN_
भूमौ निपतितस्य अपि तस्य देहम् महात्मनः |न श्रीर् जहाति न प्राणा न तेजो न पराक्रमः || ४-१७-४_END
BEGIN_
Though that great souled Vali fell onto earth, neither his brilliance, nor lives, nor resplendence, 
nor his bravery are unfettering from his body. [4-17-4]_END

B_4_C_16_27
BEGIN_
वृक्षैः स शाखैः शिखरैः वज्र कोटि निभैः नखैः || ४-१६-२८मुष्टिभिः जानुभिः पद्भिः बाहुभिः च पुनः पुनः 
|तयोः युद्द्धम् अभूत् घोरम् वृत्र वासवोः इव || ४-१६-२९_END
BEGIN_
Among those two there happened a deadly fight time and again using trees with branches, peaks of mountains, 
their own nails that are similar to the razor-sharp edges of thunderbolts, and with fists, knees, feet, 
and arms, like the fight that once chanced between demon Vritra and Indra. [4-16-28b, 29]_END

B_4_C_11_81
BEGIN_
आर्द्रः स मांसः प्रत्यग्रः क्षिप्तः कायः पुरा सखे |
परिश्रान्तेन मत्तेन भ्राता मे वालिना तदा|| ४-११-८७_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, friend, at that time when my tired and tipsy brother Vali tossed this body it
was unspoilt, wet with blood and full with flesh. [4-11-87]_END

B_4_C_17_4
BEGIN_
शक्र दत्ता वरा माला कान्चनी रत्न भूषिता |दधार हरि मुख्यस्य प्राणान् तेजः श्रियम् च सा || ४-१७-५_END
BEGIN_
That superb and gem-studded golden pendent given by Indra sustained that monkey chief's lives, resplendence 
and brilliance. [4-17-5]_END

B_4_C_11_82
BEGIN_
लघुः संप्रति निर्मांसः तृण भूतः च राघव |
क्षिप्ता एवम् प्रहर्षेण भवता रघुनंदन || ४-११-८८_END
BEGIN_
"Raghava, now this body is sleazy, without flesh, also rendered into a strawy
condition, and oh, Raghu's delight, you too flipped it because you are now energetic. [4-11-88]_END

B_4_C_17_5
BEGIN_
स तया मालया वीरो हैमया हरियूथपः |संध्यानुगत पर्यन्तः पयोधर इव अभवत् || ४-१७-६_END
BEGIN_
By still wearing that golden chest-pendant around his neck, that brave general of monkeys Vali appeared 
like a black-cloud smeared with the colour of golden sunset all around its edges. [4-17-6]_END

B_4_C_16_28
BEGIN_
तौ शोणितात्कौ युध्येताम् वानारौ वन् चारिणौ |मेघौ इव महा शब्दैः तर्जमानौ परस्परम् || ४-१६-३०_END
BEGIN_
Those forest moving vanara-s that are soaked in blood have gone on clashing, threatening each other, 
like two clouds clashing uproariously. [4-16-30]_END

B_4_C_11_83
BEGIN_
न अत्र शक्यम् बलम् ज्ञातुम् तव वा तस्य वा अधिकम् |
आर्द्रम् शुष्कम् इति हि एतत् सुमहद् राघव अन्तरम् || ४-११-८९_END
BEGIN_
"If it be said something is wet or dried up there chances a lot of difference, oh,
Raghava, thereby it may not be possible to assess whether you might is greater or his, as the
gravity of the case depends much on that wetness or dryness alone, isn't it." [4-11-89]_END

B_4_C_17_6
BEGIN_
तस्य माला च देहः च मर्मघाती च यः शरः |त्रिधा इव रचिता लक्ष्मीः पतितस्य अपि शोभते || ४-१७-७_END
BEGIN_
Even though Vali has fallen on ground his splendour is as though refulgent devising itself into three 
aspects, namely by his body, chest-pendant, and the arrow of Rama, which arrow is given to strike the 
crucial body parts alone, and which is still stuck in Vali's chest. [4-17-7]_END

B_4_C_16_29
BEGIN_
हीयमानम् अथ अपश्यत् सुग्रीवम् वानरेश्वरम् |प्रेक्षमाणम् दिशः च एव राघवः स मुहुर् मुहुर् || ४-१६-३१_END
BEGIN_
Raghava has then seen the lord of monkeys Sugreeva who is repeatedly eyeing all sides for help and who 
is even deteriorating in his enterprise. [4-16-31]_END

B_4_C_11_84
BEGIN_
स एव संशयः तात तव तस्य च यद् बलम् |
सालम् एकम् विनिर् भिद्या भवेत् व्यक्तिः बलाबले || ४-११-९०_END
BEGIN_
"That alone is the uncertainty in that matter, sire, whether your strength is
superior or his, and if a single sala tree is ripped in an outright manner the ability or otherwise
will be evident. [4-11-90]_END

B_4_C_17_7
BEGIN_
तत् अस्त्रम् तस्य वीरस्य स्वर्ग मार्ग प्रभावनम् |राम बाणासन क्षिप्तम् आवहत् परमाम् गतिम् || ४-१७-८_END
BEGIN_
That arrow which effectuates the pathway to heaven, now discharged from the bow of Rama has brought 
forth that redemption to brave Vali . [4-17-8]_END

B_4_C_16_30
BEGIN_
ततो रामो महातेजा आर्तम् दृष्ट्वा हरीश्वरम् |स शरम् वीक्षते वीरो वालिनो वध कांक्षया || ४-१६-३२_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the lord of monkeys Sugreeva in a forlornness, then the refulgent and fearless Rama scanned 
for an arrow aiming to eliminate Vali. [4-16-32]_END

B_4_C_18_0
BEGIN_
इति उक्तः प्रश्रितम् वाक्यम् धर्म अर्थ सहितम् हितम् |परुषम् वालिना रामो निहतेन विचेतसा || ४-१८-१_END
BEGIN_
Thus, Vali who is hit down by arrow and who is collapsing humbly spoke exacting words that contained 
probity, meaningfulness, and expedience, to Rama. [4-18-1]_END

B_4_C_11_85
BEGIN_
कृत्वा एतत् कार्मुकम् सज्यम् हस्ति हतम् इव अपरम् |
आकर्ण पूर्णम् आयम्य विसृजस्व महाशरम् || ४-११-९१_END
BEGIN_
"String the bowstring to this bow of yours, an alternate of elephant's trunk, and
stretch it out up to your ear, and release a great arrow. [4-11-91]_END

B_4_C_17_8
BEGIN_
तम् तथा पतितम् संख्ये गत अर्चिषम् इव अनलम् |ययातिम् इव पुण्यान्ते देव लोकात् परिच्युतम् || ४-१७-९
आदित्यम् इव कालेन युगान्ते भुवि पातितम् |महेन्द्रम् इव दुर्धर्षम् उपेन्द्रम् इव दुस्सहम् || ४-१७-१०
महेन्द्र पुत्रम् पतितम् वालिनम् हेम मालिनम् |व्यूढ उरस्कम् महाबाहुम् दीप्तास्यम् हरि लोचनम् || ४-१७-११
लक्ष्मण अनुचरो रामो ददर्श उपससर्प च |_END
BEGIN_
Then on seeing him who has fallen in war, the one with golden pendant, enormously chested, mightily 
armed, face golden, eye greenish, but who is like a fire extinct of its flame; who is like Indra in 
unassailability and like Upendra in indomitability; and who like Yayaati who has fallen from heaven, 
as well like the sun who falls onto earth from solar orbit when Time-ender flings him at the end of 
era; such as he is, on seeing that son of Indra, who forsooth has fallen, Rama neared him followed by 
Lakshmana. [4-17-9, 10, 11, 12a]_END

B_4_C_16_31
BEGIN_
ततो धनुषि संधाय शरम् आशी विष उपमम् |पूरयामास तत् चापम् काल चक्रम् इव अन्तकः || ४-१६-३३_END
BEGIN_
Then on tautening a venomous serpent like arrow in the bow, Rama started to draw out bowstring, whereby 
that bow attained a similitude with the Time-disc of the Terminator. [4-16-33]_END

B_4_C_18_1
BEGIN_
तम् निष्प्रभम् इव आदित्यम् मुक्त तोयम् इव अंबुदम् |उक्त वाक्यम् हरि श्रेष्ठम् उपशांतम् इव अनलम् 
|| ४-१८-२धर्म अर्थ गुण संपन्नम् हरि ईश्वरम् अनुत्तमम् |अधिक्षिप्तः तदा रामः पश्चात् वालिनम् 
अब्रवीत् || ४-१८-३_END
BEGIN_
Then to him who is rendered like a lusterless sun, fizzling out like a cloud that released its water, 
and who became like a quenched fire, to such a best monkey and an unexcelled lord of monkeys who has 
just now imputed Rama with words that are abounding with righteousness and meaningfulness, Rama spoke 
subsequently. [4-18-3, 4]_END

B_4_C_11_86
BEGIN_
इमम् हि सालम् प्रहितः त्वया शरो
न संशयो अत्र अस्ति विदारयिष्यति |
अलम् विमर्शेन मम प्रियम् ध्रुवम्
कुरुष्व राजन् प्रति शापितो मया || ४-११-९२_END
BEGIN_
"Darted by you your arrow will rip off this sala tree, oh, king, there is no doubt
in that matter, enough is this thinking of yours and you will definitely do me this favour, I pray
and swear upon me." [4-11-92]_END

B_4_C_17_9
BEGIN_
तम् तथा पतितम् वीरम् गत अर्चिष्मतम् इव अनलम् || ४-१७-१२बहुमान्य च तम् वीरम् वीक्षमाणम् शनैरिव |
उपयातौ महावीर्यौ भ्रातरौ राम लक्ष्मणौ || ४-१७-१३_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the brave Vali fallen like that, who by now is like fire with extinguished tongues of flames, 
and who is seeing droopily, those two valiant brothers, Rama and Lakshmana, neared him with due honour. 
[4-17-12b, 13]_END

B_4_C_16_32
BEGIN_
तस्य ज्यातल घोषेण त्रस्ताः पत्ररथेश्वराः |प्रदुद्रुवुर् मृगाः च एव युगांत इव मोहिताः || ४-१६-३४_END
BEGIN_
At the blast of bowstring the lordly birds and animals are panicked, like those that will be startled 
by the approach of ear ending, and they all fled. [4-16-34]_END

B_4_C_18_2
BEGIN_
धर्मम् अर्थम् च कामम् च समयम् च अपि लौकिकम् |अविज्ञाय कथम् बाल्यात् माम् इह अद्य विगर्हसे || ४-१८-४_END
BEGIN_
"Uncaring for probity, prosperity, pleasure deriving, and even for the social conventions, now how do 
you rebuke me childishly in this matter? [4-18-4]_END

B_4_C_11_87
BEGIN_
यथा हि तेजस्सु वरः सदा रविः
यथा हि शैलो हिमवान् महा अद्रिषु |
यथा चतुष्पात्सु च केसरी वरः
तथा नराणाम् असि विक्रमे वरः || ४-११-९३_END
BEGIN_
"As to how the sun is unsurpassed among all brilliances, as to how Himavan is
unmatched among all mountains, as to how the lion is unequalled among all quadrupeds, so you are
among all men for your unique valour." So said Sugreeva to Rama. [4-11-93]_END

B_4_C_17_10
BEGIN_
तम् दृष्ट्वा राघवम् वाली लक्ष्मणम् च महाबलम् |अब्रवीत् परुषम् वाक्यम् प्रश्रितम् धर्म संहितम् || 
४-१७-१४स भूमौ अल्पतेजोसुः निहतो नष्ट चेतनः |अर्थ सहितया वाचा गर्वितम् रण गर्वितम् || ४-१७-१५_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Rama and the great mighty Lakshmana as well, he who fell to ground flatly hurt by arrow, and 
whose energy and lives are trifling and vigour trivialised thereby, that Vali spoke these sarcastic 
words in his proper pride to Rama, who is taking pride in this conflict as a victor, which words at 
the same time have meaning, politeness, and self-righteousness. [4-17-14, 15]_END

B_4_C_16_33
BEGIN_
मुक्तस्तु वज्र निर्घोषः प्रदीप्त अशनि संनिभः |राघवेण महा बाणो वालि वक्षसि पातितः || ४-१६-३५_END
BEGIN_
The arrow released by Raghava that has the boom of thunderbolt's thunderclap and the flashes of a lightning 
fell on the chest of Vali. [4-16-35]_END

B_4_C_18_3
BEGIN_
अपृष्ट्वा बुद्धि संपन्नान् वृद्धान् आचार्य संमतान् |सौम्य वानर चापल्यात् त्वम् माम् वक्तुम् इह इच्छसि 
|| ४-१८-५_END
BEGIN_
"Unconsulted are the doyens of your race that are intellectually well off and agreeable to your mentors 
about rights and wrongs about your deeds, oh, gentle one, how do you wish to debate with me in this 
matter with your primate's caprice. [4-18-5]_END

B_4_C_17_11
BEGIN_
त्वम् नराधिपतेः पुत्रः प्रथितः प्रिय दर्शनः |पराङ्मुख वधम् कृत्वा को अत्र प्राप्तः त्वया गुणः |
यदहम् युद्ध सम्रब्धः त्वत् कृते निधनम् गतः || ४-१७-१६_END
BEGIN_
"You are a renowned prince with pleasing looks.. but, which kind of death I am getting now, that too 
when I was in the commotion of conflict with another, alas, that ignoble death is owing to you, and 
what merit is achieved by you in this undertaking of yours to kill someone who is facing away from you... 
[4-17-16]_END

B_4_C_16_34
BEGIN_
ततः तेन महातेजा वीर्य युक्तः कपीश्वरः |वेगेन अभिहतो वाली निपपात मही तले || ४-१६-३६_END
BEGIN_
Hit by the fleetness of that arrow then that highly magnificent and intrepid lord of monkeys Vali fell 
onto the plane of earth. [4-16-36]_END

B_4_C_18_4
BEGIN_
इक्ष्वाकूणाम् इयम् भूमिः स शैल वन कानना |मृग पक्षि मनुष्याणाम् निग्रह अनुग्रहेषु अपि || ४-१८-६_END
BEGIN_
"This earth with its mountains, woods, and forests, even along with the authority to condone or condemn 
the animals, birds, and humans on it belongs to Ikshvaku-s. [4-18-6]_END

B_4_C_17_12
BEGIN_
कुलीनः सत्त्व संपन्नः तेजस्वी चरितव्रतः |रामः करुणवेदी च प्रजानाम् च हितेरतः || ४-१७-१७सानुक्रोशो 
महोत्साहः समयज्ञो दृढव्रतः |इति एतत् सर्व भूतानि कथयन्ति यशो भुवि || ४-१७-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Rama is high-born, they say, gifted with mightiness, resplendent, pursuer of vows, mindful of mercy, 
delighter in people's welfare, sympathetic, greatly enthusiastic and assertively committed in doing 
good deeds, knower of time-and-action, all these living-beings on earth are thus relating your renown, 
aren't they. [4-17-17, 18]_END

B_4_C_16_35
BEGIN_
इन्द्र ध्वज इव उद्धूत पौर्ण मास्याम् महीतले |अश्वयुक् समये मासि गत सत्त्वो विचेतनः |बाष्प संरुद्ध 
कण्ठस्तु वाली च आर्त स्वरः शनैः || ४-१६-३७_END
BEGIN_
Like the flag that will be raised in honour of Indra during the month of ashvin on a full-moon day, 
but thrown onto earth along with its flagstaff after the festival, Vali with depleted energy and dissipated 
vitality slowly fell onto ground, and with tears blocking throat he moaned piteously. [4-16-37]_END

B_4_C_18_5
BEGIN_
ताम् पालयति धर्मात्मा भरतः सत्यवान् ऋजुः |धर्म काम अर्थ तत्त्वज्ञो निग्रह अनुग्रहे रतः || ४-१८-७_END
BEGIN_
"He who is virtue-souled, truth-abiding, plain-speaking, and the knower of the import of probity, pleasures, 
and prosperity, and the one who is concerned in controlling or condoning his subjects, that Bharata 
is the ruler of earth. [4-18-7]_END

B_4_C_17_13
BEGIN_
दमः शमः क्षमा धर्मो धृति सत्यम् पराक्रमः |पर्थिवानाम् गुणा राजन् दण्डः च अपकारिषु || १-१७-१९_END
BEGIN_
"To be able to control senses and will, forgiveness, conscientiousness, resoluteness, truthfulness, 
and adventurousness, oh, king, are the aptitudes of a king, and even punishing the wrongdoers, too. 
[4-17-19]_END

B_4_C_16_36
BEGIN_
नरोत्तमः काल युगांतकोपमम् शरोत्तमम् कांचन रूप्यभूषितम् |ससर्ज दीप्तम् तम् अमित्र मर्दनम् स धूममग्निम् 
मुखतो यथा हरः || ४-१६-३८_END
BEGIN_
That best one among men Rama released a blazing and enemy subjugating arrow which in simile is like 
an Epoch-ender at the end of era, and that best arrow decorated in gold and silver looked like the glance 
from the Third-Eye of Rudra, emitting fire with smoke. [4-16-38]_END

B_4_C_18_6
BEGIN_
नयः च विनयः च उभौ यस्मिन् सत्यम् च सुस्थितम् |विक्रमः च यथा दृष्टः स राजा देश कालवित् || ४-१८-८_END
BEGIN_
"In whom both scrupulousness and benignancy are there, truthfulness is firmed up, and valour as evinced 
by scriptures is evident, and he who is the knower of time and place is the king, namely Bharata. [4-18-8]_END

B_4_C_19_0
BEGIN_
स वानर महाराजः शयानः शर पीडितः |प्रत्युक्तो हेतुमद् वाक्यैः न उत्तरम् प्रत्यपद्यत || ४-१९-१_END
BEGIN_
That great vanara king Vali who is sprawling agonised by arrow, and to whom Rama gave a reply with well-reasoned 
words did not find any other reply to be given to Rama. [4-19-1]_END

B_4_C_17_14
BEGIN_
तान् गुणान् संप्रधार्य अहम् अग्र्यम् च अभिजनम् तव |तारया प्रतिषिद्धो अपि सुग्रीवेण समागतः || १-१७-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Concluding that those kingly characteristics will be obtainable in you, and even judging by the noble 
dynasty of yours, I have confronted Sugreeva though Tara dissuaded me. [4-17-20]_END

B_4_C_16_37
BEGIN_
अथ उक्षितः शोणित तोय विस्रवैःसुपुष्पित अशोक इव अचलोद्गतः |विचेतनो वासव सूनुर् आहवेप्रभ्रञ्शित 
इन्द्र ध्वजवत् क्षितिम् गतः || ४-१६-३९_END
BEGIN_
That Indra's son Vali, dampened with blood and sweat, then looked like just felled Ashoka tree which 
has stemmed up and so far standing high on a mountain with fully bloomed clusters of its blood-red flowers, 
and when his anima is undone he even looked like the flagstaff on which a flag is raised in honour of 
Indra, but which is altogether dislodged and abandoned on the ground. [4-16-39]_END

B_4_C_18_7
BEGIN_
तस्य धर्म कृत आदेशा वयम् अन्ये च पार्थिवः |चरामो वसुधाम् कृत्स्नाम् धर्म संतानम् इच्छवः || ४-१८-९_END
BEGIN_
"Holding his virtuous decree desiring to keep up the continuum of righteousness, we and some other kings 
are wayfaring this earth in its entirety. [4-18-9]_END

B_4_C_19_1
BEGIN_
अश्मभिः परिभिन्न अंगः पादपैर् आहतो भृशम् |राम बाणेन च आक्रान्तो जीवित अंते मुमोह सः || ४-१९-२_END
BEGIN_
He who is heavily thrashed with trees, whose limbs are variously cracked with boulders, and whom Rama's 
arrow finally vanquished, that Vali fainted at the time of his breathing his last. [4-19-2]_END

B_4_C_17_15
BEGIN_
न माम् अन्येन संरब्धम् प्रमत्तम् वेद्धुम् अर्हसि |इति मे बुद्धिर् उत्पन्ना बभूव अदर्शने तव || १-१७-२१_END
BEGIN_
"When you have not appeared before me when I confronted Sugreeva my concept was, 'it will be inapt of 
Rama to hurt me while I am combating with another combatant, besides, when I will be unvigilant in that 
fight...' [4-17-21]_END

B_4_C_18_8
BEGIN_
तस्मिन् नृपति शार्दूल भरते धर्म वत्सले |पालयति अखिलाम् पृथ्वीम् कः चरेत् धर्म विप्रियम् || ४-१८-१०_END
BEGIN_
"While that Bharata, the kingly-tiger and a patron of virtue, is ruling the earth in its entirety, who 
is there to conduct himself in an unacceptable way to morality on it? [4-18-10]_END

B_4_C_19_2
BEGIN_
तम् भार्या बाण मोक्षेण राम दत्तेन संयुगे |हतम् प्लवग शार्दूलम् तारा शुश्राव वालिनम् || ४-१९-३_END
BEGIN_
Tara, wife of Vali, heard that the tigerly monkey Vali perished in fight by the arrow released by Rama._END

B_4_C_17_16
BEGIN_
न त्वाम् विनिहत आत्मानम् धर्म ध्वजम् अधार्मिकम् |जाने पाप समाचारम् तृणैः कूपम् इव आवृतम् || १-१७-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Not known that your soul is put to death, not known that you are the unrighteous flag bearer of righteousness, 
to me not known that you are insidious like straw covered well. [4-17-22]_END

B_4_C_18_9
BEGIN_
ते वयम् मार्ग विभ्रष्टम् स्वधर्मे परमे स्थिताः |भरत आज्ञाम् पुरस्कृत्य निगृह्णीमो यथा विधि || ४-१८-११_END
BEGIN_
"Abiding in our own pre-eminent righteousness, and even abiding by the order of Bharata we punish him 
who deviated from the path of morality, according to custom. [4-18-11]_END

B_4_C_19_3
BEGIN_
सा सपुत्र अप्रियम् श्रुत्वा वधम् भर्तुः सुदारुणम् |निष्पपात भृशम् तस्मात् उद्विग्ना गिरि कंदरात् 
|| ४-१९-४_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the very gruesome killing of her husband that is unpleasant, she is highly anguished and 
rushed out of Kishkindha along with Angada. [4-19-4]_END

B_4_C_17_17
BEGIN_
सताम् वेष धरम् पापम् प्रच्छन्नम् इव पावकम् |न अहम् त्वाम् अभिजानामि धर्म छद्माभि संवृतम् || १-१७-२३_END
BEGIN_
"I have no knowledge that you are a sinner, one in the garb of a benign soul, and explicitly mantled 
under the garb of probity like ash covered fire. [4-17-23]_END

B_4_C_18_10
BEGIN_
त्वम् तु संक्लिष्ट धर्मः च कर्मणा च विगर्हितः |काम तंत्र प्रधानः च न स्थितो राज वर्त्मनि || ४-१८-१२_END
BEGIN_
"As for you, you brought virtue to a state of decadence, rendered yourself reprovable by your own decadent 
behaviour, for carnality alone has become your primary doctrine, and thus you have not abided by the 
conduct meetly to a king. [4-18-12]_END

B_4_C_19_4
BEGIN_
ये ते अंगद परीवारा वानरा हि महाबलाः |ते सकार्मुकम् आलोक्य रामम् त्रस्ताः प्रदुद्रुवुः || ४-१९-५_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Rama with bow those very mighty vanara-s that form the escort of Angada are scared to death, 
and they very quickly fled from there towards Kishkindha. [4-19-5]_END

B_4_C_17_18
BEGIN_
विषये वा पुरे वा ते यदा पापम् करोमि अहम् |न च त्वाम् अवजाने अहं कस्मात् त्वम् हंसि अकिल्बिषम् || 
१-१७-२४फल मूल अशनम् नित्यम् वानरम् वन गोचरम् |माम् इह अप्रतियुध्यन्तम् अन्येन च समागतम् || १-१७-२५_END
BEGIN_
"I am non-guilty as I have not committed any misdeed either in your country or in your city, nor I have 
taunted you; I am a vanara subsisting on fruits and tubers and always moving in forests alone; such 
as I am, what made you to torture me when I was not combating with you en face, furthermore, when I 
was involved with another? [4-17-24, 25]_END

B_4_C_18_11
BEGIN_
ज्येष्ठो भ्राता पिता चैव यः च विद्याम् प्रयच्छति |त्रयः ते पितरो ज्ञेया धर्मे च पथि वर्तिनः || ४-१८-१३_END
BEGIN_
"It is to be known by him who treads the way of righteousness that he has three fatherly personages, 
namely his own father, his elder brother, and the one who accords education to him. [4-18-13]_END

B_4_C_19_5
BEGIN_
सा ददर्श ततः त्रस्तान् हरीन् आपततो द्रुतम् |यूथाद् इव परिभ्रष्टान् मृगान् निहत यूथपान् || ४-१९-६_END
BEGIN_
Then on her way towards field of combat she saw the monkeys that are frightened and fleeing in disorder, 
like those animals that have wandered off from their herd when their master is killed. [4-19-6]_END

B_4_C_20_0
BEGIN_
राम चाप विसृष्टेन शरेण अंतकरेण तम् |
दृष्ट्वा विनिहतम् भूमौ तारा ताराधिप आनना || ४-२०-१
सा समासाद्य भर्तारम् पर्यष्वजत भामिनी |_END
BEGIN_
On seeing her husband felled to ground with a terminator like arrow released by
Rama, that resentful lady Tara whose face is lovely like the moon, reached and embraced him.
[4-20-1]_END

B_4_C_17_19
BEGIN_
त्वम् नराधिपतेः पुत्रः प्रतीतः प्रियदर्शनः |लिन्गम् अपि अस्ति ते राजन् दृश्यते धर्म सम्हितम् || 
१-१७-२६_END
BEGIN_
"You are renowned to be a prince with charming looks, oh, king, and indications agreeable to rectitude 
are also appearing on your body. [4-17-26]_END

B_4_C_18_12
BEGIN_
यवीयान् आत्मनः पुत्रः शिष्यः च अपि गुणोदितः |पुत्रवत् ते त्रयः चिंत्या धर्मः चैव अत्र कारणम् || 
४-१८-१४_END
BEGIN_
"An younger brother, a son, and a disciple with good characteristics, these three are to be deemed as 
one's own sons, for such matters take base on rectitude alone. [4-18-14]_END

B_4_C_19_6
BEGIN_
तान् उवाच समासाद्य दुःखितान् दुःखिता सती |राम वित्रासितान् सर्वान् अनुबद्धान् इव इषुभिः || ४-१९-७_END
BEGIN_
Nearing those monkeys that are already distressed at the fall of Vali, and that are highly frightened 
by Rama, and that are fleeing as though Rama's arrow is still tracking them down, Tara spoke to all 
of them, distressed as she is. [4-19-7]_END

B_4_C_20_1
BEGIN_
इषुणा अभिहतम् दृष्ट्वा वालिनम् कुंजरोपमम् || ४-२०-२
वानरम् पर्वत इन्द्र आभम् शोक संतप्त मानसा |
तारा तरुम् इव उन्मूलम् पर्यदेवयत् आतुरा || ४-२०-३_END
BEGIN_
Tara is agonised when she saw the elephantine and mountainous vanara, namely Vali,
reduced to no more than an uprooted tree, and she wailed fretfully with grief scorching heart.
[4-20-2b, 3]_END

B_4_C_17_20
BEGIN_
कः क्षत्रिय कुलेजातः श्रुतवान् नष्टसंशयः |धर्म लिंग प्रतिच्छन्नः क्रूरम् कर्म समाचरेत् || १-१७-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Will anybody born in Kshatriya's family, a learned one in Veda-s, thereby who is rid of ambiguities 
with respect to right and wrong, and who is cloaked in an air of probity, execute such a ruthless deed 
like this? [4-17-27]_END

B_4_C_18_13
BEGIN_
सूक्ष्मः परम दुर्ज्ञेयः सताम् धर्मः प्लवंगम |हृदिस्थः सर्व भूतानाम् आत्मा वेद शुभाशुभम् || ४-१८-१५_END
BEGIN_
"The probity practised by principled people is very subtle and highly imponderable, and the soul that 
abides in the hearts of all beings alone can differentiate between just and unjust. [4-18-15]_END

B_4_C_19_7
BEGIN_
वानरा राज सिंहस्य यस्य यूयम् पुरः सराः |तम् विहाय सुवित्रस्ताः कस्माद् द्रवत दुर्गताः || ४-१९-८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh! Vanara-s, what for you are running away in utter fright and desperation, leaving off your best 
king to whom all of you are ushers?" Thus Tara enquired with the monkeys. [4-19-8]_END

B_4_C_20_2
BEGIN_
रणे दारुण विक्रान्त प्रवीर प्लवताम् वर |
किम् इदीनाम् पुरो भागाम् अद्य त्वम् न अभिभाषसे || ४-२०-४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, stern one in fights, oh, victorious one, oh, best valiant, oh, best flier, I
have never blamed you either in your presence or in your absence, why do not you talk to me now?
[4-20-4]_END

B_4_C_17_21
BEGIN_
राम राघव कुले जातो धर्मवान् इति विश्रुतः |अभव्यो भव्य रूपेण किम् अर्थम् परिधावसे || १-१७-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Though born in Raghava's dynasty and renowned as a moralist you are actually amoral, and for what purpose 
you run around with this moral aspect? [4-17-28]_END

B_4_C_18_14
BEGIN_
चपलः चपलैः सार्धम् वानरैः अकृत आत्मभिः |जात्यंध इव जात्यन्धैः मंत्रयन् द्रक्ष्यसे नु किम् || ४-१८-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Like a blind by birth counselling with similarly blind, you being a vacillant, on your counselling 
only with frantic minded vacillant monkeys, what can you really fathom about right and wrong? [4-18-16]_END

B_4_C_19_8
BEGIN_
राज्य हेतोः स चेत् भ्राता भ्रात्रा कॄरेण पातितः |रामेण प्रसृतैः दूरात् मार्गणैः दूर पातिभिः || ४-१९-९_END
BEGIN_
"Whether or not a cruel brother made his brother to fall for the reason of kingdom with the arrows of 
Rama which can surge well from distance and fall on distant target? Aver it. [4-19-9]_END

B_4_C_20_3
BEGIN_
उत्तिष्ठ हरि शार्दूल भजस्व शयन उत्तमम् |
न एवम् विधाः शेरते हि भूमौ नृपति सत्तमाः || ४-२०-५_END
BEGIN_
"Arise, oh, tigerly monkey, you have to make use of a best bed as best kings will
not on repose on soil in this way, isn't it. [4-20-5]_END

B_4_C_17_22
BEGIN_
साम दानम् क्षमा धर्मः सत्यम् धृति पराक्रमौ |पार्थिवानाम् गुणा राजन् दण्डः च अपि अपकारिषु || १-१७-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Influencing, largesse, forbearance, probity, candour, and conquering are the attributes of the kings, 
oh, king, and even punishing the wrongdoers. [4-17-29]_END

B_4_C_18_15
BEGIN_
अहम् तु व्यक्तताम् अस्य वचनस्य ब्रवीमि ते |न हि माम् केवलम् रोषात् त्वम् विगर्हितुम् अर्हसि || ४-१८-१७_END
BEGIN_
"I will clarify about the words I have said, but I tell you that it is indeed inapt of you to disdain 
me just out of your outrage. [4-18-17]_END

B_4_C_19_9
BEGIN_
कपि पत्न्या वचः श्रुत्वा कपयः काम रूपिणः |प्राप्त कालम् अविश्लिष्टम् ऊचुर् वचनम् अंगनाम् || ४-१९-१०_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of monkey's wife those guise-changing monkeys spoke this sentence coherently to 
lady Tara, befitting to present time of chaos. [4-19-10]_END

B_4_C_20_4
BEGIN_
अतीव खलु ते कांता वसुधा वसुधाधिप |
गत असुर् अपि ताम् गात्रैः माम् विहाय निषेवसे || ४-२०-६_END
BEGIN_
"The earth seems to be a highly cherished darling of yours, oh, lord of the land, as
you still embrace her with your limbs leaving me off, even when your lives are drained.
[4-20-6]_END

B_4_C_17_23
BEGIN_
वयम् वनचरा राम मृगा मूल फल अशनाः |एषा प्रकृतिर् अस्माकम् पुरुषः त्वम् नरेश्वरः || १-१७-३०_END
BEGIN_
"We as animals live in forests while you are city dwellers, we live by eating fruits and tubers while 
you enjoy feasts and banquets, our nature is such to kill and get killed, thus you and me have no correlation. 
And you, even if you are a man and a prince for humans, you resorted to this animalistic way of killing 
me lying in the wait, thus your action is worse than that of an animal, if not subhuman or un-princely. 
[4-17-30]_END

B_4_C_18_16
BEGIN_
तत् एतत् कारणम् पश्य यत् अर्थम् त्वम् मया हतः |भ्रातुर् वर्तसि भार्यायाम् त्यक्त्वा धर्मम् सनातनम् 
|| ४-१८-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Realise this reason by which I have eliminated you... you misbehaved with your brother's wife, forsaking 
the perpetual tradition. [4-18-18]_END

B_4_C_19_10
BEGIN_
जीवपुत्रे निवर्तस्व पुत्रम् रक्षस्व च अन्दगम् |अंतको राम रूपेण हत्वा नयति वालिनम् || ४-१९-११_END
BEGIN_
"Return, oh, lady with a living son, and safeguard Angada, for the Terminator in the form of Rama is 
taking away Vali on killing. [4-19-11]_END

B_4_C_20_5
BEGIN_
व्यक्तम् अद्य त्वया वीर धर्मतः संप्रवर्तता |
किष्किंधा इव पुरी रम्या स्वर्ग मार्गे विनिर्मिता || ४-२०-७_END
BEGIN_
"It is evident that you, who conduct yourself righteously, must have built a
Kishkindha-like delightful city in the pathway to heaven by your leaving lovely Kishkindha.
[4-20-7]_END

B_4_C_17_24
BEGIN_
भूमिर् हिरण्यम् रूपम् च निग्रहे कारणानि च |तत्र कः ते वने लोभो मदीयेषु फलेषु वा || १-१७-३१_END
BEGIN_
"Territory, gold, and silver will be the causes while counteracting somebody, in that case, by what 
you are decoyed into these forests of mine or in the fruits of mine. [4-17-31]_END

B_4_C_18_17
BEGIN_
अस्य त्वम् धरमाणस्य सुग्रीवस्य महात्मनः |रुमायाम् वर्तसे कामात् स्नुषायाम् पाप कर्मकृत् || ४-१८-१९_END
BEGIN_
"While the great-souled Sugreeva is still alive, you with your habit of sinful acts have lustily misbehaved 
with Sugreeva's wife Ruma, who should be counted as your daughter-in-law. [4-18-19]_END

B_4_C_19_11
BEGIN_
क्षिप्तान् वृक्षान् समाविध्य विपुलाः च शिलाः तथा |वाली वज्र समैर् बाणैर् वज्रेण इव निपातितः || ४-१९-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Shattering trees and massive boulders that Vali hurled at him with thunderbolt like arrows Rama felled 
Vali as if by thunderbolt. [4-19-12]_END

B_4_C_20_6
BEGIN_
यानि अस्माभिः त्वया सार्धम् वनेषु मधु गंधिषु |
विहृतानि त्वया काले तेषाम् उपरमः कृतः || ४-२०-८_END
BEGIN_
"You bring an end to the pleasure trips you made along with us in the sweet smelling
forests from time to time by your departing. [4-20-8]_END

B_4_C_17_25
BEGIN_
नयः च विनयः च उभौ निग्रह अनुग्रहौ अपि |राज वृत्तिर् असंकीर्णा न नृपाः काम वृत्तयः || १-१७-३२_END
BEGIN_
"In the pairs of propriety and compliance, punishment and pardoning, no admixture is exercised in kingcraft, 
for the kings do not conduct themselves volitionally. [4-17-32]_END

B_4_C_18_18
BEGIN_
तद् व्यतीतस्य ते धर्मात् काम वृत्तस्य वानर |भ्रातृ भार्या अभिमर्शे अस्मिन् दण्डो अयम् प्रतिपादितः 
|| ४-१८-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Thereby, oh, vanara, this punishment is imposed on you, for your dissolute sinning in abusing your 
brother's wife, thereby for your transgression of tradition and virtue. [4-18-20]_END

B_4_C_19_12
BEGIN_
अभिभूतम् इदम् सर्वम् विद्रुतम् वानरम् बलम् |अस्मिन् प्लवग शार्दूले हते शक्र सम प्रभे || ४-१९-१३_END
BEGIN_
"When that tigerly fly-jumper Vali whose brilliance is similar to Indra is killed all this vanara force 
felt defenceless and fled. [4-19-13]_END

B_4_C_21_0
BEGIN_
ततो निपतिताम् ताराम् च्युताम् ताराम् इव अंबरात् |शनैः आश्वासयामास हनूमान् हरि यूथपः || ४-२१-१_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma, the leader of monkeys, then neared and slowly consoled Tara who has fallen to ground like a 
star from sky. [4-21-1]_END

B_4_C_20_7
BEGIN_
निरानंदा निराशा अहम् निमग्ना शोक सागरे |
त्वयि पंचत्वम् आपन्ने महायूथप यूथपे || ४-२०-९_END
BEGIN_
"When this fifth state betiding you, oh, great chief of chiefs of monkeys, I am
dejected, despaired and drowned in the sea of sadness. [4-20-9]_END

B_4_C_17_26
BEGIN_
त्वम् तु काम प्रधानः च कोपनः च अनवस्थितः |राज वृत्तेषु संकीर्णः शरासन परायणः || १-१७-३३_END
BEGIN_
"But, to you your self-interests are primary, and you are a wrathful, capricious, contriver of kingcraft, 
and an impetuous shooting-happy archer. [4-17-33]_END

B_4_C_18_19
BEGIN_
न हि लोक विरुद्धस्य लोक वृत्तात् अपेयुषः |दण्डात् अन्यत्र पश्यामि निग्रहम् हरि यूथप || ४-१८-२१_END
BEGIN_
"I foresee no other kind of control other than punishment to him who conducts himself contrary to the 
society and who is deviant of conventions. [4-18-21]_END

B_4_C_19_13
BEGIN_
रक्ष्यताम् नगरम् शूरैर् अंगदः च अभिषिच्यताम् |पदस्थम् वालिनः पुत्रम् भजिष्यन्ति प्लवंगमाः || ४-१९-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Let the city of Kishkindha be safeguarded and let Angada be anointed, and when Vali's son Angada is 
enthroned all the fly-jumpers will stand by him. [4-19-14]_END

B_4_C_21_1
BEGIN_
गुण दोष कृतम् जंतुः स्वकर्म फल हेतुकम् |अव्यग्रः तद् अवाप्नोति सर्वम् प्रेत्य शुभ अशुभम् || ४-२१-२_END
BEGIN_
"Living beings on doing the deeds of merit or demerit, or knowingly or unknowingly, will derive the 
resultant fruits of those deeds according to one's own destiny even after demise, and they shall bear 
them unrepentantly, may they be provident or improvident... [4-21-2]_END

B_4_C_20_8
BEGIN_
हृदयम् सुस्थिरम् मह्यम् दृष्ट्वा विनिहतम् भुवि |
यन् न शोक अभिसंतप्तम् स्फुटते अद्य सहस्रधा || ४-२०-१०_END
BEGIN_
"My heart is very sturdy - perhaps, even on seeing you slain and fallen to ground,
it is not splintering now into thousand splints, though it is tormented by sorrow. [4-20-10]_END

B_4_C_17_27
BEGIN_
न ते अस्ति अपचितिः धर्मे न अर्थे बुद्धिर् अवस्थिता |इन्द्रियैः काम वृत्तः सन् कृष्यसे मनुजेश्वर 
|| १-१७-३४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, king, you have no devotion to probity, nor your mind is firm about material gains, but as a free-willed 
one you are distracted by senses. [4-17-34]_END

B_4_C_18_20
BEGIN_
न च ते मर्षये पापम् क्ष्त्रियो अहम् कुलोद्गतः |औरसीम् भगिनीम् वा अपि भार्याम् वा अपि अनुजस्य यः 
|| ४-१८-२२प्रचरेत नरः कामात् तस्य दण्डो वधः स्मृतः |_END
BEGIN_
"As a Kshatriya emerged from a best dynasty I do not tolerate your wrongdoing, and the punishment to 
the one who lustfully indulges with his daughter, or with his sister, or with the wife of his younger 
brother is his elimination, as recalled from scriptures. [4-18-22, 23a]_END

B_4_C_19_14
BEGIN_
अथवा अरुचितम् स्थानम् इह ते रुचिरानने |आविशन्ति हि दुर्गाणि क्षिप्रम् अद्य एव वानराः || ४-१९-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Or, your staying here is not good, oh, one with a pleasant visage, for those monkeys of Sugreeva will 
promptly enter our strongholds on this day itself. [4-19-15]_END

B_4_C_21_2
BEGIN_
शोच्या शोचसि कम् शोच्यम् दीनम् दीना अनुकंपसे |कः च कस्य अनुशोच्यो अस्ति देहे अस्मिन् बुद्बुद उपमे 
|| ४-२१-३_END
BEGIN_
"Of which lamentable one you lament while you yourself are in a lamentable state? Of which pitiable 
one you take pity while you yourself are in a pitiable condition? Who is pitiable by whom in these bubbles 
like bodies? [4-21-3]_END

B_4_C_20_9
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवस्य त्वया भार्या हृता स च विवासितः |
यत् तत् तस्य त्वया व्युष्टिः प्राप्ता इयम् प्लवगाधिप || ४-२०-११_END
BEGIN_
"By which reason you have snatched away Sugreeva's wife, oh, chief of fliers, and
even expelled him from Kishkindha, that is the reason why you got this result. [4-20-11]_END

B_4_C_17_28
BEGIN_
हत्वा बाणेन काकुत्स्थ माम् इह अनपराधिनम् |किम् वक्ष्यसि सताम् मध्ये कर्म कृत्वा जुगुप्सितम् || १-१७-३५_END
BEGIN_
"How you are answerable to gentlemen, Rama, when you have done this detestable deed of killing an unoffending 
one like me with your arrow? [4-17-35]_END

B_4_C_18_21
BEGIN_
भरतः तु महीपालो वयम् तु आदेश वर्तिनः || ४-१८-२३त्वम् च धर्मात् अतिक्रान्तः कथम् शक्यम् उपेक्षितुम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
While Bharata is the lord of land and we are his proxies adhering to his orders, and while you too have 
overstepped the bounds of rightness, then how is it possible to be lenient? [4-18-23b, 24a]_END

B_4_C_19_15
BEGIN_
अभार्याः सह भार्याः च सन्ति अत्र वन चारिणः |लुब्धेभ्यो विप्रलब्धेयः तेभ्यो नः सुमहद् भयम् || ४-१९-१६_END
BEGIN_
"There are foresters in Kishkindha, some with wives and some without, some hankering after wives, some 
whom we have victimised, and from them we have very great danger." So said monkeys to Tara. [4-19-16]_END

B_4_C_21_3
BEGIN_
अंगदः तु कुमारो अयम् द्रष्टव्यो जीव पुत्रया |आयत्या च विधेयानि समर्थानि अस्य चिन्तय || ४-२१-४_END
BEGIN_
"You are the one with a living son, and you have to look after this young one Angada, and you have to 
think of the forthcoming activities for his well-being and for his performance of duty towards his father. 
[4-21-4]_END

B_4_C_20_10
BEGIN_
निःश्रेयस परा मोहात् त्वया च अहम् विगर्हिता |
या एषा अब्रुवम् हितम् वाक्यम् वानरेन्द्र हित एषिणी || ४-२०-१२_END
BEGIN_
"I am she who said a beneficial word to you with an interest in your well-being and
wishing your welfare, but oh, best monkey, you unmindfully brushed me off. [4-20-12]_END

B_4_C_17_29
BEGIN_
राजहा ब्रह्महा गोघ्नः चोरः प्राणिवधे रतः |नास्तिकः परिवेत्ता च सर्वे निरय गामिनः || १-१७-३६_END
BEGIN_
"A regicide, a Brahman-cide, a cow-slayer, a thief, an inveterate killer, an atheist, and an younger 
brother who marries before his elder, all of them will go to hell. [4-17-36]_END

B_4_C_18_22
BEGIN_
गुरु धर्म व्यतिक्रान्तम् प्राज्ञो धर्मेण पालयन् || ४-१८-२४भरतः काम युक्तानाम् निग्रहे पर्यवस्थितः 
|_END
BEGIN_
"While ruling righteously sensible Bharata punishes him who oversteps the momentous virtue, and he is 
poised to put down lustful ones. [4-18-24b, 25a]_END

B_4_C_19_16
BEGIN_
अल्पांतर गतानाम् तु श्रुत्वा वचनम् अंगना |आत्मनः प्रतिरूपम् सा बभाषे चारु हासिनी || ४-१९-१७_END
BEGIN_
On going a small distance ahead after listening those words, she whose smile will be winsome, that lady 
Tara said this befitting to her personality. [4-19-17]_END

B_4_C_21_4
BEGIN_
जानासि अनियताम् एवम् भूतानाम् आगतिम् गतिम् |तस्मात् शुभम् हि कर्तव्यम् पण्डितेन इह लौकिकम् || ४-२१-५_END
BEGIN_
"You are aware that the coming and going of beings, in their subtle forms of earth, water, fire, air 
and space into this mortal life and back is uncertain, thereby the prudent ones have to perform auspicious 
worldly deeds here in this world, say, the funeral of Vali. [4-21-5]_END

B_4_C_20_11
BEGIN_
रूप यौवन दृप्तानाम् दक्षिणानाम् च मानद |
नूनम् अप्सरसाम् आर्य चित्तानि प्रमथिष्यसि || ४-२०-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, endower of honour, apsara-s, the celestial dancers, will be proud of their
beauty, youthfulness, and expertise in romance, and oh, honourable one, you can stir up their
hearts towards you by your gallantry, definite is that. [4-20-13]_END

B_4_C_17_30
BEGIN_
सूचकः च कदर्यः च मित्र्घ्नो गुरुतल्पगः |लोकं पापात्मानम् एते गच्छन्ते न अत्र संशयः || १-१७-३७_END
BEGIN_
"A slander-monger, skinflint, friend-killer and one who makes love with his teacher's wife, they all 
go to the worlds of evil-souls, no doubt about it. [4-17-37]_END

B_4_C_18_23
BEGIN_
वयम् तु भरत आदेशम् विधिम् कृत्वा हरीश्वर |त्वत् विधान् भिन्न मर्यादान् निग्रहीतुम् व्यवस्थिताः || 
४-१८-२५_END
BEGIN_
"As for us, oh, monkey's lord, we effectuate our brother's orders and our duty, and we stand for curbing 
your kind of shatterers of ethics. [4-18-25b, c]_END

B_4_C_19_17
BEGIN_
पुत्रेण मम किम् कार्यम् किम् राज्येन किम् आत्मना |कपि सिम्हे महा भागे तस्मिन् भर्तरि नश्यति || ४-१९-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Of what avail is a son, or a kingdom, or I to myself when my husband that lion like monkey with great 
honour perished. [4-19-18]_END

B_4_C_21_5
BEGIN_
यस्मिन् हरि सहस्राणि शतानि नियुतानि च |वर्तयन्ति कृत आशानि सो अयम् दिष्टांतम् आगतः || ४-२१-६_END
BEGIN_
"In whom hundreds and thousands of monkeys are harboured and astir, for they have reposed their confidence 
in him alone, that Vali has arrived at his end. [4-21-6]_END

B_4_C_20_12
BEGIN_
कालो निःसंशयो नूनम् जीवित अंतकरः तव |
बलात् येन अवपन्नो असि सुग्रीवस्य अवशो वशम् || ४-२०-१४_END
BEGIN_
"The Time which is an undoubtable factor in respect of anybody has ended your life,
definite is that, and that Time alone perforce brought you, who are otherwise an uncontrollable
force, to the control of Sugreeva._END

B_4_C_17_31
BEGIN_
अधार्यम् चर्म मे सद्भी रोमाणि अस्थि च वर्जितम् |अभक्ष्याणि च मांसानि त्वत् विधैः धर्मचारिभिः || 
१-१७-३८_END
BEGIN_
"My skin is unwearable, holy people forbid my hair and bones, and uneatable is my meat for your kind 
of reputable people. [4-17-38]_END

B_4_C_18_24
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवेण च मे सख्यम् लक्ष्मणेन यथा तथा |दार राज्य निमित्तम् च निःश्रेयसकरः स मे || ४-१८-२६_END
BEGIN_
"My association with Sugreeva is as good as that with Lakshmana, nevertheless it betided with an understanding 
to regain Sugreeva's wife and kingdom, and he will give succour to me. [4-18-26]_END

B_4_C_19_18
BEGIN_
पाद मूलम् गमिष्यामि तस्य एव अहम् महात्मनः |यो असौ राम प्रयुक्तेन शरेण विनिपातितः || ४-१९-१९_END
BEGIN_
"I wish to consign myself at the base of foot of that great-soul, who is felled down by the arrow projected 
by Rama." So said Tara to fleeing monkeys. [4-19-19]_END

B_4_C_21_6
BEGIN_
यद् अयम् न्याय दृष्ट अर्थः साम दान क्षमा परः |गतो धर्म जिताम् भूमिम् न एनम् शोचितुम् अर्हसि || ४-२१-७_END
BEGIN_
"By which reason this Vali conducted himself judiciously, observing friendliness, courteousness and 
forgivingness, by that reason alone Vali is going to a domain in heavens which he righteously conquered 
for himself, and it is unapt of your sorrowing for him. [4-21-7]_END

B_4_C_20_13
BEGIN_
अस्थाने वालिनम् हत्वा युध्यमानम् परेण च |
न संतप्यति काकुत्स्थः कृत्वा सुगर्हितम् || ४-२०-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Rama's killing Vali when he is fighting with another is unbefitting in its method,
and he too is not at all worried for doing such a highly deplorable deed. [4-20-15]_END

B_4_C_17_32
BEGIN_
पंच पंच नखा भक्ष्या ब्रह्म क्षत्रेण राघव |शल्यकः श्वाविधो गोधा शशः कूर्मः च पंचमः || १-१७-३९_END
BEGIN_
"Raghava, five kinds of five-nailed animals, viz., a kind of wild rodent, a kind of wild-boar, a kind 
of lizard, a hare and fifthly the turtle are edible for Brahmans and Kshatriya-s. [4-17-39]_END

B_4_C_18_25
BEGIN_
प्रतिज्ञा च मया दत्ता तदा वानर संनिधौ |प्रतिज्ञा च कथम् शक्या मत् विधेन अनवेक्षितुम् || ४-१८-२७_END
BEGIN_
"I gave a promise to Sugreeva at the time of befriending him in the presence of vanara-s, and how is 
it possible for my kind to dishonour a given promise? [4-18-27]_END

B_4_C_19_19
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा प्रदुद्राव रुदती शोक मूर्च्छिता |शिरः च उरः च बाहुभ्याम् दुःखेन समभिघ्नती || ४-१९-२०_END
BEGIN_
Saying thus she started to wail and convulse in agony, and slapped her head and chest with both of her 
hands while she speedily rushed towards Vali. [4-19-20]_END

B_4_C_21_7
BEGIN_
सर्वे च हरि शार्दूलाः पुत्रः च अयम् तव अंगदः |हरि ऋक्ष पति राज्यम् च त्वत् सनाथम् अनिन्दिते || ४-२१-८_END
BEGIN_
"All the tigerly-monkeys, oh, impeccable Tara, including this son of yours Angada, and all the lords 
of monkeys and bears have their guardian angel in you. [4-21-8]_END

B_4_C_22_0
BEGIN_
वीक्षमाणः तु मंदासुः सर्वतो मंदम् उच्छ्वसन् |
आदौ एव तु सुग्रीवम् ददर्श अनुजम् अग्रतः || ४-२२-१_END
BEGIN_
With his life-force slowing down Vali respired slowly glancing everywhere, and he
firstly saw his brother Sugreeva afore him. [4-22-1]_END

B_4_C_20_14
BEGIN_
वैधव्यम् शोक संतापम् कृपणम् अकृपणा सती |
अदुह्ख उपचिता पूर्वम् वर्तयिष्यामि अनाथवत् || ४-२०-१६_END
BEGIN_
"So far I am not doleful or saddened, but now as a desolate seethed by sorrow I have
to undergo widowhood and dolefulness. [4-20-16]_END

B_4_C_17_33
BEGIN_
चर्म च अस्थि च मे राजन् न स्पृशन्ति मनीषिणः |अभक्ष्याणि च मांसानि सो अहम् पंच नखो हतः || १-१७-४०_END
BEGIN_
"Sensible people will not touch my skin and bones, oh, king, nor meats from my body are to be eaten, 
such as I am, a five-nailed animal, I am killed. [4-17-40]_END

B_4_C_19_20
BEGIN_
सा व्रजन्ती ददर्श अथ पतिम् निपतितम् भुवि |हन्तारम् दानव इन्द्राणाम् समरेषु अनिवर्तिनाम् || ४-१९-२१_END
BEGIN_
While she is still trudging then she saw her husband who is the destroyer of arch-demons like Maayaavi 
and Dundubhi, and who never retreated in combats, but now fallen down on ground. [4-19-21]_END

B_4_C_18_26
BEGIN_
तत् एभिः कारणैः सर्वैर् महद्भिः धर्म संहितैः |शासनम् तव यत् युक्तम् तत् भवान् अनुमन्यताम् || ४-१८-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Thereby you have to infer that a befitting punishment is given to you, owing to all these great reasons 
that abound with virtue and with supreme value. [4-18-28]_END

B_4_C_22_1
BEGIN_
तम् प्राप्त विजयम् वाली सुग्रीवम् प्लवग ईश्वरम् |
आभाष्य व्यक्तया वाचा सस्नेहम् इदम् अब्रवीत् || ४-२२-२_END
BEGIN_
Vali nodding at Sugreeva, who achieved triumph and became the lord of fly-jumpers,
amicably spoke this to him in an unambiguous tone. [4-22-2]_END

B_4_C_21_8
BEGIN_
तौ इमौ शोक संतप्तौ शनैः प्रेरय भामिनि |त्वया परिगृहीतो अयम् अंगदः शास्तु मेदिनीम् || ४-२१-९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, lady, inspirit these two, Sugreeva and Angada, that are searing in grief, and if you acquiesce 
then this Angada will rule over the earth. [4-21-9]_END

B_4_C_20_15
BEGIN_
लालितः च अंगदो वीरः सुकुमारः सुखोचितः |
वत्स्यते काम् अवस्थाम् मे पितृव्ये क्रोध मूर्च्छिते || ४-२०-१७_END
BEGIN_
"My Angada is raised fondly, a brave one with gracefulness and one who is accustomed
to comforts, but which will be the predicament he has to undergo when his paternal-uncle Sugreeva
gets into a fit of fury. [4-20-17]_END

B_4_C_17_34
BEGIN_
तारया वाक्यम् उक्तो अहम् सत्यम् सर्वज्ञया हितम् |तद् अतिक्रम्य मोहेन कालस्य वशम् आगतः || १-१७-४१_END
BEGIN_
"Though Tara appraised me with truthful and favourable words, I just disregarded her advise owing to 
my own delusion, and gone into the control of Time. [4-17-41]_END

B_4_C_19_21
BEGIN_
क्षेप्तारम् पर्वत इन्द्राणाम् वज्राणाम् इव वासवम् |महावात समाविष्टम् महामेघ औघ निःस्वनम् || ४-१९-२२_END
BEGIN_
She saw Vali who is a flinger of loftiest mountains as with Indra flinging his thunderbolt, who is a 
blaster as with great gusty winds, and who is a roarer as with a cluster of great black-clouds. [4-19-22]_END

B_4_C_18_27
BEGIN_
सर्वथा धर्म इति एव द्रष्टव्यः तव निग्रहः |वयस्यस्य उपकर्तव्यम् धर्मम् एव अनुपश्यता || ४-१८-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Anywise, you have to regard the punishment given to you is legitimate, and he whom rectitude guides 
has to render assistance to his friend, in any event. [4-18-29]_END

B_4_C_22_2
BEGIN_
सुग्रीव दोषेण न माम् गन्तुम् अर्हसि किल्बिषात् |
कृष्यमाणम् भविष्येण बुद्धि मोहेन माम् बलात् || ४-२२-३_END
BEGIN_
"Sugreeva, reckon me not by my iniquities, but reckon as one who is all the while
forcibly hauled into this futurity owing to my impropriety and obduracy. [4-22-3]_END

B_4_C_21_9
BEGIN_
संततिः च यथा दृष्टा कृत्यम् यत् च अपि सांप्रतम् |राज्ञः तत् क्रियताम् सर्वम् एष कालस्य निश्चयः || 
४-२१-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Whatever duty anticipated from a male descendent towards his father, and whatever activity that is 
to be done presently in respect of the dying king, let them be done, and that would be a timely decision. 
[4-21-10]_END

B_4_C_20_16
BEGIN_
कुरुष्व पितरम् पुत्र सुदृष्टम् धर्म वत्सलम् |
दुर्लभम् दर्शनम् तस्य तव वत्स भविष्यति || ४-२०-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, son Angada, clearly see your father, a patron of virtue, oh, boy, later it is
impossible to catch a glimpse of him." Thus Tara said to her son Angada. [4-20-18]_END

B_4_C_17_35
BEGIN_
त्वया नाथेन काकुत्स्थ न सनाथा वसुंधरा |प्रमदा शील संपूर्णा पति एव च विधर्मिणा || १-१७-४२_END
BEGIN_
"With you as her espouser the Earth is not with a correct spouse, as with any lady who is with full-fledged 
chastity, but with a husband who is without rectitude. [4-17-42]_END

B_4_C_19_22
BEGIN_
शक्रतुल्य पराक्रांतम् वृष्ट्वा इव उपरतम् घनम् |नर्दन्तम् नर्दताम् भीमम् शूरम् शूरेण पातितम् |
शार्दूलेन आमिषस्य अर्थे मृग राजम् इव आहतम् || ४-१९-२३_END
BEGIN_
He who equals Indra in the invasion of enemies, a violent thunderer at the opponent thunderers, a brave 
one felled by still brave one, and who is like a best animal killed by a tiger for the purpose of flesh, 
and quietened like black-cloud at the end of downpour, At him she saw. [4-19-23]_END

B_4_C_18_28
BEGIN_
शक्यम् त्वया अपि तत् कार्यम् धर्मम् एव अनुवर्तता |श्रूयते मनुना गीतौ श्लोकौ चारित्र वत्सलौ ||
गृहीतौ धर्म कुशलैः तथा तत् चरितम् मयाअ || ४-१८-३०_END
BEGIN_
"Had you pursued rightness you too would have done the same deed in imposing such a punishment, and 
we hear two verses that are given to the advocacy of good conventions, which the experts of rightness 
have also accepted, and which are said to be coined by Manu, and I too conducted myself only as detailed 
in those verses of law. [4-18-30]_END

B_4_C_22_3
BEGIN_
युगपद् विहितम् तात न मन्ये सुखम् अवयोः |
सौहार्दम् भ्रातृ युक्तम् हि तद् इदम् जातम् अन्यथा || ४-२२-४_END
BEGIN_
"I do not think that we two are fated to share blissfulness simultaneously, oh, boy,
therefore the amity seemly to brothers has cropped up otherwise. [4-22-4]_END

B_4_C_21_10
BEGIN_
संस्कार्यो हरि राजः तु अंगदः च अभिषिच्यताम् |सिंहासन गतम् पुत्रम् पश्यन्ती शान्तिम् एष्यसि || ४-२१-११_END
BEGIN_
"Cremation of the king of monkeys and anointment of Angada are the present time affairs, and seeing 
your son invested on the throne you can obtain peace." Thus spoke Hanuma to Tara. [4-21-11]_END

B_4_C_20_17
BEGIN_
समाश्वासय पुत्रम् त्वम् संदेशम् संदिशस्व मे |
मूर्ध्नि च एनम् समाघ्राय प्रवासम् प्रस्थितो हि असि || ४-२०-१९_END
BEGIN_
"You have started towards other world, isn't it, so reassure your son, kiss goodbye
on his forehead, and give me your parting messages." So said Tara to Vali. [4-20-19]_END

B_4_C_17_36
BEGIN_
शठो नैकृतिकः क्षुद्रो मिथ्या प्रश्रित मानसः |कथम् दशरथेन त्वम् जातः पापो महात्मना || १-१७-४३_END
BEGIN_
"How are you borne to that great-souled Dasharatha when you are artful, felonious, knavish, disposed 
to a false modesty subconsciously, and an evildoer? [4-17-43]_END

B_4_C_18_29
BEGIN_
राजभिः धृत दण्डाः च कृत्वा पापानि मानवाः |निर्मलाः स्वर्गम् आयान्ति सन्तः सुकृतिनो यथा || ४-१८-३१_END
BEGIN_
" 'When kings impose proper punishment on the humans who have sinned, they become sinless and enter 
heaven as with the pious souls with good deeds.' So says one verse of Manu. [4-18-31]_END

B_4_C_19_23
BEGIN_
अर्चितम् सर्व लोकस्य सपताकम् सवेदिकम् |नाग हेतोः सुपर्णेन चैत्यम् उन्मथितम् यथा || ४-१९-२४_END
BEGIN_
He who is like a sanctum that is hitherto worshipped by all people, that is decorated with flags and 
demarcated with podia, but just ravaged by an eagle for the sake of a snake which sneaked into that 
sanctum, and Tara saw such a Vali plumped on the ground. [4-19-24]_END

B_4_C_22_4
BEGIN_
प्रतिपद्य त्वम् अद्य एव राज्यम् एषाम् वन ओकसाम् |
माम् अपि अद्य एव गच्छंतम् विद्धि वैवस्वत क्षयम् || ४-२२-५_END
BEGIN_
"You realize that I am going to the abode of Time-god now itself, and hence propose
yourself as king of this forest-dweller's kingdom, now itself. [4-22-5]_END

B_4_C_21_11
BEGIN_
सा तस्य वचनम् श्रुत्वा भर्तृ व्यसन पीडिता |अब्रवीत् उत्तरम् तारा हनूमन्तम् अवस्थितम् || ४-२१-१२_END
BEGIN_
On hearing Hanuma's words she who is tormented by the plight of her husband, that Tara replied Hanuma 
who is standing nearby. [4-21-12]_END

B_4_C_20_18
BEGIN_
रामेण हि महत् कर्म कृतम् त्वाम् अभिनिघ्नता |
आनृण्यम् तु गतम् तस्य सुग्रीवस्य प्रतिश्रवे || ४-२०-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Really, Rama has not only done a great deed of hitting you down, but he also
achieved indebtedness towards Sugreeva, both in a single promise. [4-20-20]_END

B_4_C_17_37
BEGIN_
छिन्न चारित्र्य कक्ष्येण सताम् धर्म अतिवर्तिना |त्यक्त धर्म अंकुशेन अहम् निहतो राम हस्तिना || १-१७-४४_END
BEGIN_
"I am killed by an elephant called Rama that snapped off its girdle-cord called tradition, that infringed 
the conventions of righteous people, and that discarded the goad called virtue. [4-17-44]_END

B_4_C_18_30
BEGIN_
शसनात् वा अपि मोक्षात् वा स्तेनः पापात् प्रमुच्यते |राजा तु अशासन् पापस्य तद् आप्नोति किल्बिषम् 
|| ४-१८-३२_END
BEGIN_
" 'Either by punishment or by clemency a thief will be absolved from sin, but the king who does not 
impose proper punishment will derive the blot of that sin.' So says the other verse of Manu. [4-18-32]_END

B_4_C_19_24
BEGIN_
अवष्टभ्य अवतिष्ठंतम् ददर्श धनुर् ऊर्जितम् |रामम् रामानुजम् चैव भर्तुः चैव तथा अनुजम् || ४-१९-२५_END
BEGIN_
She saw Rama standing and abutting on his very powerful bow, and his younger brother Lakshmana, even 
at the younger brother of her husband, namely Sugreeva. [4-19-25]_END

B_4_C_22_5
BEGIN_
जीवितम् च हि राज्यम् च श्रियम् च विपुलाम् इमाम् |
प्रजहामि एष वै तूर्णम् अहम् च अगर्हितम् यशः || ४-२२-४-२२-६_END
BEGIN_
"Such as I am, I am indeed forgoing my life, kingdom, and this immense prosperity
and even the unenviable glory which adduces that 'Vali is unkillable,' right away. [4-22-6]_END

B_4_C_21_12
BEGIN_
अंगद प्रतिरूपाणाम् पुत्राणाम् एकतः शतम् |हतस्य अपि अस्य वीरस्य गात्र संश्लेषणम् वरम् || ४-२१-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Let there be a hundred selfsame Angada-s on one side, and this brave one the other, for me embracing 
him who is put to death is the best .... [4-21-13]_END

B_4_C_23_0
BEGIN_
ततः समुपजिघ्रंती कपि राजस्य तत् मुखम् |पतिम् लोकश्रुता तारा मृतम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् || ३-२३-१_END
BEGIN_
Then that renowned Tara closely whiffed that face of monkey's king Vali and spoke these words to her 
dead husband. [3-23-1]_END

B_4_C_20_19
BEGIN_
सकामो भव सुग्रीव रुमाम् त्वम् प्रतिपत्स्यसे |
भुंक्ष्व राज्यम् अनुद्विग्नः शस्तो भ्राता रिपुः तव || ४-२०-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Now, you are to your heart's content Sugreeva as you regain your wife Ruma, you may
even wallow in the kingdom unworriedly as your enemy-brother is silenced." So said Tara to
Sugreeva. [4-20-21]_END

B_4_C_17_38
BEGIN_
अशुभम् च अपि अयुक्तम् च सताम् च एव विगर्हितम् |वक्ष्यसे च ईदृशम् कृत्वा सद्भिः सह समागतः || १-१७-४५_END
BEGIN_
"On accomplishing this sort of unpropitious, unjustified killing, which is condemned by the righteous 
people, what can you say when you meet the godly men? [4-17-45]_END

B_4_C_18_31
BEGIN_
आर्येण मम मान्धात्रा व्यसनम् घोरम् ईप्सितम् |श्रमणेन कृते पापे यथा पापम् कृतम् त्वया || ४-१८-३३_END
BEGIN_
"When a renouncer has committed sin like that of the one committed by you, my venerable ancestor Maandhaata 
has given punishment which he desired. [4-18-33]_END

B_4_C_19_25
BEGIN_
तान् अतीत्य समासाद्य भर्तारम् निहतम् रणे |समीक्ष्य व्यथिता भूमौ संभ्रांता निपपात ह || ४-१९-२६_END
BEGIN_
Going past them she reached her husband who is routed in combat, and on observing him closely she indeed 
fell down on earth as she is distraught and dumbfounded. [4-19-26]_END

B_4_C_22_6
BEGIN_
अस्याम् त्वम् अहम् अवस्थायाम् वीर वक्ष्यामि यद् वचः |
यदि अपि असुकरम् राजन् कर्तुम् एव तद् अर्हसि || ४-२२-७_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, valiant Sugreeva, it will be apt of you to make happen the word I am going to
say even in such a situation in which now I am, and oh, king, even if that word of mine is
infeasible. [4-22-7]_END

B_4_C_21_13
BEGIN_
न च अहम् हरि राज्यस्य प्रभवामि अंगदस्य वा |पितृव्यः तस्य सुग्रीवः सर्व कार्येषुइ अनंतरः || ४-२१-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Who am I either for conducting the monkeys kingdom or to anoint Angada when Angada's paternal-uncle 
Sugreeva is close at hand? [4-21-14]_END

B_4_C_23_1
BEGIN_
शेषे त्वम् विषमे दुःखम् अकृत्वा वचनम् मम |उपल उपचिते वीर सुदुःखे वसुधा तले || ३-२३-२_END
BEGIN_
"Heedless of my word, oh, brave one, you are reposing miserably on a very rough and uneven ground spread 
with stones. [3-23-2]_END

B_4_C_20_20
BEGIN_
किम् माम् एवम् प्रलपतीम् प्रियाम् त्वम् न अभिभाषसे |
इमाः पश्य वरा बह्वयः भार्याः ते वानरेश्वर || ४-२०-२२_END
BEGIN_
""Oh, lord of monkeys, why do not you talk to me, the dear wife of yours, when I am
prattling at length, by the way, several of your comely wives are here, they are here, see them."
Thus Tara lamented. [4-20-22]_END

B_4_C_18_32
BEGIN_
अन्यैः अपि कृतम् पापम् प्रमत्तैः वसुधा अधिपैः |प्रायश्चित्तम् च कुर्वन्ति तेन तत् शाम्यते रजः || 
४-१८-३४_END
BEGIN_
"Such sin is acquired even by other kings who are unobservant in imposing proper punishment, and those 
kings had to make amends for it at appropriate time, by that propitiation they used to mitigate that 
filth of that sin. [4-18-34]_END

B_4_C_17_39
BEGIN_
उदासीनेषु यो अस्मासु विक्रमो अयम् प्रकाशितः |अपकारिषु ते राम न एवम् पश्यामि विक्रमम् || १-१७-४६_END
BEGIN_
"The valour that which is displayed on the unprejudiced few like us, oh, Rama, I do not see that sort 
of valour is shown by you in respect of your enemies. [4-17-46]_END

B_4_C_19_26
BEGIN_
सुप्ता इव पुनर् उत्थाय आर्य पुत्र इति वादिनी |रुरोद सा पतिम् दृष्ट्वा सम्वीतम् मृत्यु दामभिः || 
४-१९-२७_END
BEGIN_
On getting up as though reawakened from sleep she saw her husband bound fast by the strings of death, 
and then she wailingly addressed him as, "oh, nobleman's son..." [4-19-27]_END

B_4_C_22_7
BEGIN_
सुखार्हम् सुख संवृद्धम् बालम् एनम् अबालिशम् |
बाष्प पूर्ण मुखम् पश्य भूमौ पतितम् अंगदम् || ४-२२-८_END
BEGIN_
"Have a look at this Angada, who is privileged for all happiness, brought up in all
comforts, though a boy he is mannerly, and who with his tear-filled face fallen onto ground.
[4-22-8]_END

B_4_C_21_14
BEGIN_
न हि एषा बुद्धिः आस्थेया हनूमन् अंगदम् प्रति |पिता हि बंधुः पुत्रस्य न माता हरि सत्तम || ४-२१-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Hanuma, this thinking of yours that Angada is to be crowned is really untenable, oh, best monkey, father 
is the real defender of a son, but not the mother. [4-21-15]_END

B_4_C_20_21
BEGIN_
तस्या विलपितम् श्रुत्वा वानर्यः सर्वतः च ताः |
परिगृह्य अंगदम् दीना दुह्ख आर्ताः परिचुक्रुशुः || ४-२०-२३_END
BEGIN_
On listening Tara's lamentation the vanara females that are around became plaintive,
saddened pitiably and wept piteously embracing Angada. [4-20-23]_END

B_4_C_23_2
BEGIN_
मत्तः प्रियतरा नूनम् वानरेन्द्र मही तव |शेषे हि ताम् परिष्वज्य माम् च न प्रतिभाषसे || ३-२३-३_END
BEGIN_
"This earth must definitely be your beloved one, oh, best of monkeys, why because, you still embrace 
her while you recline on her, without replying me. [3-23-3]_END

B_4_C_18_33
BEGIN_
तत् अलम् परितापेन धर्मतः परिकल्पितः |वधो वानरशार्दूल न वयम् स्व वशे स्थिताः || ४-१८-३५_END
BEGIN_
"Thereby, enough with your annoyance, oh, tigerly vanara, as your elimination is devised righteously, 
and we too are not independent. [4-18-35]_END

B_4_C_17_40
BEGIN_
दृश्यमानः तु युध्येथा मया युधि नृपात्मज |अद्य वैवस्वतम् देवम् पश्येः त्वम् निहतो मया || १-१७-४७_END
BEGIN_
"Had you been in combat with me en face oh, prince, you would have been killed by me and by now you 
would have seen the death-god Yama. [4-17-47]_END

B_4_C_21_15
BEGIN_
न हि मम हरि राज संश्रयात्क्षमतरम् अस्ति परत्र च इह वा |अभिमुख हत वीर सेवितम्शयनम् इदम् मम 
सेवितुम् क्षमम् || ४-२१-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed there is nothing highly befitting to me, either in this world or in the other, than the auspices 
of the king of monkeys, and now to me the only befitting thing is to join in this brave one on this 
death bed, which he is adoring when put to death while he is facing away. [4-21-16]_END

B_4_C_19_27
BEGIN_
ताम् अवेक्ष्य तु सुग्रीवः क्रोशन्तीम् कुररीम् इव |विषादम् अगमत् कष्टम् दृष्ट्वा च अंगदम् आगतम् || 
४-१९-२८_END
BEGIN_
On observing her who is wailing like a female osprey, and even on looking at Angada who arrived there, 
a miserable remorse came upon Sugreeva. [4-19-28]_END

B_4_C_22_8
BEGIN_
मम प्राणैः प्रियतरम् पुत्रम् पुत्रम् इव औरसम् |
मया हीनम् अहीनार्थम् सर्वतः परिपालय || ४-२२-९_END
BEGIN_
"More dear than my own lives is my son, and when he is deprived of me you have to
foster him as if he is your own son, with no resources becoming sparse in every way. [4-22-9]_END

B_4_C_20_22
BEGIN_
किम् अंगदम् स अंगद वीर बाहो
विहाय यातो असि अद्य चिरम् प्रवासम् |
न युक्तम् एवम् गुण संनिकृष्टम्
विहाय पुत्रम् प्रिय पुत्रम् प्रिय चारु वेषम् || ४-२०-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, one with bracelets on your mighty arms, why you are going to an eternal abode
leaving your dear son Angada? Your going away leaving such a son, who possesses best aptitudes that
comes close to your abilities, and the one who always wears an exquisitely pleasant getup, is
unbefitting. [4-20-24]_END

B_4_C_23_3
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवस्य वशम् प्राप्तो विधिः एष भवत्य अहो |सुग्रीव एव विक्रांतो वीर साहसिक प्रिय || ३-२३-४_END
BEGIN_
"You have gone into the control of Sugreeva and Sugreeva alone triumphed, oh, brave one, oh, enthusiast 
in adventures, oho, is it fated to happen this way. [3-23-4]_END

B_4_C_18_34
BEGIN_
श्रुणु च अपि अपरम् भूयः कारणम् हरिपुंगव |तत् श्रुत्वा हि महत् वीर न मन्युम् कर्तुम् अर्हसि || ४-१८-३६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, brave and best one among monkeys, further listen to another cause, and on listening that important 
cause you will not be infuriated. [4-18-36]_END

B_4_C_17_41
BEGIN_
त्वया अदृश्येन तु रणे निहतो अहम् दुरासदः |प्रसुप्तः पन्नगेन इव नरः पाप वशम् गतः || १-१७-४८_END
BEGIN_
"An unassailable one, such as I am, I am killed by you while you remained invisible on the field of 
fight, as with a sinner bitten by a snake while he is asleep. [4-17-48]_END

B_4_C_22_9
BEGIN_
त्वम् अपि अस्य पिता दाता च परित्राता च सर्वतः |
भयेषु अभयदः चैव यथा अहम् प्लवगेश्वर || ४-२२-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, king of fly-jumpers, as with me you too are his father, patron, an overall
protector from all sides, and also thus an assurer in fear. [4-22-10]_END

B_4_C_20_23
BEGIN_
यदि अप्रियम् किंचिद् असंप्रधार्य
कृतम् मया स्यात् तव दीर्घ बाहो |
क्षमस्व मे तत् हरि वंश नाथ
व्रजामि मूर्ध्ना तव वीर पादौ || ४-२०-२५_END
BEGIN_
"If I have done any undesirable deed in an indiscriminate way, even in the least, I
may be pardoned for that, and here I bow down at your feet... oh, masterful one... oh, the lord of
monkeys lineage... oh, brave one... [Thus Tara wept for Vali.] [4-20-25]_END

B_4_C_23_4
BEGIN_
ऋक्ष वानर मुख्याः त्वाम् बलिनम् पर्युपासते |तेषाम् विलपितम् कृच्छ्रम् अंगदस्य च शोचतः || ३-२३-५
मम च इमा गिरः श्रुत्वा किम् त्वम् न प्रतिबुध्यसे |_END
BEGIN_
"These chiefs of bears and monkeys are adoring you in every respect as their most worshipful one, and 
on hearing their despairing wailing, and the lamentation of Angada, and even these utterance of mine 
in keen, why do not you comeback to senses. [3-23-5, 6a]_END

B_4_C_18_35
BEGIN_
न मे तत्र मनस्तापो न मन्युः हरिपुंगव |वागुराभिः च पाशैः च कूटैः च विविधैः नराः || ४-१८-३७प्रतिच्छन्नाः 
च दृश्याः च गृह्णन्ति सुबहून् मृगान् |_END
BEGIN_
"I have neither angst nor ire in this matter of my eliminating you, or, your reviling me, oh, best monkey, 
but listen to the other point I wish to make clear. People will be capturing several animals, either 
covertly or overtly, with snares, springes and even with numerous contrivances. [4-18-37, 38a]_END

B_4_C_17_42
BEGIN_
सुग्रीव प्रिय कामेन यद् अहम् निहतः त्वया |माम् एव यदि पूर्वम् त्वम् एतद् अर्थम् अचोदयः |मैथिलिम् 
अहम् एक आह्ना तव च आनीतवान् भवेः || १-१७-४९राक्षसम् च दुरात्मानाम् तव भार्य अपहारिणम् |कण्ठे 
बद्ध्वा प्रदद्याम् ते अनिहतम् रावणम् रणे || ३-१७-५०_END
BEGIN_
"For which purpose I am killed, intending to do good to Sugreeva is incidental to it, you should have 
assigned me for that purpose in the first instance itself, and I would have brought that evil-minded 
demon Ravana, the abductor of your wife in one day, that too without killing him in any fight, but by 
fastening him by neck, and I would have presented Maithili to you. [3-17-49, 50]_END

B_4_C_22_10
BEGIN_
एष तारात्मजः श्रीमान् त्वया तुल्य पराक्रमः |
रक्षसाम् च वधे तेषाम् अग्रतः ते भविष्यति || ४-२२-११_END
BEGIN_
"This admirable son of Tara is a coequal of yours in triumphs, and in eliminating
those demons he will be in your advance guard. [4-22-11]_END

B_4_C_20_24
BEGIN_
तथा तु तारा करुणम् रुदंती
भर्तुः समीपे सह वानरीभिः |
व्यवस्यत प्रायम् अनिन्द्य वर्णा
उपोपवेष्टुम् भुवि यत्र वाली || ४-२०-२६_END
BEGIN_
That Tara with her unblemished complexion is seated in the close proximity of her
husband along with other vanara females, and weeping pitiably in that way, she decided to
self-immolate, and thus she flounced down onto ground where Vali is slouching. [4-20-26]_END

B_4_C_23_5
BEGIN_
इदम् तत् वीर शयनम् तत्र शेषे हतो युधि || ३-२३-६शायिता निहता यत्र त्वया एव रिपवः पुरा |_END
BEGIN_
"Do you wish to repose on the very daybed on which you have laid your enemies to rest when you have 
once felled them in fights, or what? [3-23-6b, 7a]_END

B_4_C_18_36
BEGIN_
प्रधावितान् वा वित्रस्तान् विस्रब्धान् अतिविष्ठितान् || ४-१८-३८प्रमत्तान् अप्रमत्तान् वा नरा मांस 
अशिनो भृशम् |विध्यन्ति विमुखाम् च अपि न च दोषो अत्र विद्यते || ४-१८-३९_END
BEGIN_
"Meat eating people will undeniably kill animals, either they are speedily sprinting or standing steadily, 
fully dismayed or undismayed, vigilant or unvigilant, and even if they are facing away, in that there 
is no sacrilege. [4-18-38b, 39]_END

B_4_C_17_43
BEGIN_
न्यस्ताम् सागर तोये वा पाताले वा अपि मैथिलीम् |आनयेयम् तव आदेशात् श्वेताम् अश्वतरीम् इव || ४-१७-५१_END
BEGIN_
"I would have brought Maithili at your order even if she is lodged in oceanic waters or in nether worlds, 
as with the White Horse of Vedic lore. [4-17-51]_END

B_4_C_22_11
BEGIN_
अनुरूपाणि कर्माणि विक्रम्य बलवान् रणे |
करिष्यति एष तारेयः तरस्वी तरुणो अंगदः || ४-२२-१२_END
BEGIN_
"This mighty and sinewy son of Tara is youthful, and on overtaking in war this
Angada will undertake actions seemly for a son of mine. [4-22-12]_END

B_4_C_23_6
BEGIN_
विशुद्ध सत्त्व अभिजन प्रिययुद्ध मम प्रिय || ३-२३-७माम् अनाथाम् विहाय एकाम् गतः त्वम् असि मानद |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, successor of a clan with pristine calibre, oh, accorder of dignity, oh, devotee of fighting, oh, 
my dear, have you gone on leaving me without a protector and lonely? [3-23-7b, 8a]_END

B_4_C_18_37
BEGIN_
यान्ति राजर्षयः च अत्र मृगयाम् धर्म कोविदाः |तस्मात् त्वम् निहतो युद्धे मया बाणेन वानर |अयुध्यन् 
प्रतियुध्यन् वा यस्मात् शाखा मृगो हि असि || ४-१८-४०_END
BEGIN_
"In this world even the kingly sages well-versed in virtue will go on hunting, and hunting is no face 
to face game, as such, oh, vanara, therefore I felled you in combat with my arrow because you are a 
tree-branch animal, whether you are not combating with me or combating against me. [4-18-40]_END

B_4_C_22_12
BEGIN_
सुषेण दुहिता च इयम् अर्थ सूक्ष्म विनिश्चये |
औत्पातिके च विविधे सर्वतः परिनिष्ठिता || ४-२२-१३_END
BEGIN_
"In deciding meanings in all their subtleties and also in presages of diverse nature
this daughter of Sushena, Tara, is an insightful one in every way. [4-22-13]_END

B_4_C_17_44
BEGIN_
युक्तम् यत् प्रप्नुयात् राज्यम् सुग्रीवः स्वर् गते मयि |अयुक्तम् यद् अधर्मेण त्वया अहम् निहतो रणे 
|| ४-१७-५२_END
BEGIN_
"The fact of Sugreeva's getting the kingdom after my going to heaven is proper, but the fact of your 
killing me in war, unrighteously, is improper. [4-17-52]_END

B_4_C_23_7
BEGIN_
शूराय न प्रदातव्या कन्या खलु विपश्चिता || ३-२३-८शूर भार्याम् हताम् पश्य सद्यो माम् विधवाम् कृताम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Really considerate fathers shall never propose brides to adventurers, they say. Yes! See me the wife 
of an adventurer, in a trice rendered as a war-widow left in the lurch. [3-23-8b, 9a]_END

B_4_C_22_13
BEGIN_
यद् एष साधु इति ब्रूयात् कार्यम् तन् मुक्त संशयम् |
न हि तारा मतम् किंचित् अन्यथा परिवर्तते || ४-२२-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Whatever is said by her as proper that is doable indubitably, indeed nothing
contrary happens to her opinions, in the least. [4-22-14]_END

B_4_C_17_45
BEGIN_
कामम् एवम् विधम् लोकः कालेन विनियुज्यते |क्षमम् चेत् भवता प्राप्तम् उत्तरम् साधु चिंत्यताम् || ४-१७-५३_END
BEGIN_
"Admittedly the world is this way, and if possible a relevant reply may gently be thought ofabout your 
propriety in killing me..." So said Vali to Rama. [4-17-53]_END

B_4_C_18_38
BEGIN_
दुर्लभस्य च धर्मस्य जीवितस्य शुभस्य च |राजानो वानरश्रेष्ठ प्रदातारो न संशयः || ४-१८-४१_END
BEGIN_
"Kings are the bounteous benefactors of the unobtainable righteousness and propitious lifestyles, oh, 
best vanara, no doubt about it. [4-18-41]_END

B_4_C_23_8
BEGIN_
अवभग्नः च मे मानो भग्ना मे शाश्वती गतिः || ३-२३-९अगाधे च निमग्ना अस्मि विपुले शोक सागरे |_END
BEGIN_
"My honour is degenerated and my eternal happiness is disintegrated, and I am deluged in an abyssal 
boundless ocean called anguish. [3-23-9b, 10a]_END

B_4_C_22_14
BEGIN_
राघवस्य च ते कार्यम् कर्तव्यम् अविशंकया |
स्यात् अधर्मो हि अकरणे त्वाम् च हिंस्यात् अमानितः || ४-२२-१५_END
BEGIN_
"You have to accomplish Raghava's mission undoubtedly, and if it is unaccomplished
there will be infraction on your part because you befriended him before an altar of fire, and you
may even be punished for dishonouring him and your given word to him. [4-22-15]_END

B_4_C_17_46
BEGIN_
इति एवम् उक्त्वा परिशुष्क वक्त्रःशर अभिघातात् व्यथितो महात्मा |समीक्ष्य रामम् रवि संनिकाशम्
तूष्णीम् बभौ वानर राज सूनुः || ४-१७-५४_END
BEGIN_
That great-souled son of a vanara king Vali, whom the arrow impaled and agonised, on keenly seeing Rama 
whose resplendence equals the brightness of the sun, said that much and remained silent when his mouth 
has dried up. [4-17-54]_END

B_4_C_18_39
BEGIN_
तान् न हिंस्यात् न च आक्रोशेन् न आक्षिपेन् न अप्रियम् वदेत् |देवा मानुष रूपेण चरन्ति एते मही तले 
|| ४-१८-४२_END
BEGIN_
"They the kings are not to be harmed, also not to be reproved, not disparaged and nothing displeasing 
is spoken to them, as they are the divinities conducting themselves in human form on the plane of earth. 
[4-18-42]_END

B_4_C_23_9
BEGIN_
अश्म सारमयम् नूनम् इदम् मे हृदयम् दृढम् || ३-२३-१०भर्तारम् निहतम् दृष्ट्वा यत् न अद्य शतधा गतम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"And dense with metallic substance is this heart of mine in its solidity, since it is not splintering 
into hundredfold even on seeing my husband killed, it is definite. [3-23-10b, 11a]_END

B_4_C_24_0
BEGIN_
तम् आशु वेगेन दुरासदेन तु अभिप्लुताम् शोक महार्णवेन |पश्यन् तदा वालि अनुजः तरस्वी भ्रात्रुः वधेन 
अप्रतिमेन तेपे || ४-२४-१_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Tara who quickly deluged in a speedy and vast ocean of intolerable anguish, then that Vali's 
mighty brother Sugreeva regretted for the killing of his matchless brother. [4-24-1]_END

B_4_C_18_40
BEGIN_
त्वम् तु धर्मम् अविज्ञाय केवलम् रोषम् आस्थितः |विदूषयसि माम् धर्मे पितृ पैतामहे स्थितम् || ४-१८-४३_END
BEGIN_
"I am abiding by the ethicalness practised by my father and forefathers, but you revile me without the 
knowledge of rightness, just by clinging to your rancour." Thus said Rama to dying Vali. [4-18-43]_END

B_4_C_22_15
BEGIN_
इमाम् च मालाम् आधत्स्व दिव्याम् सुग्रीव कांचनीम् |
उदारा श्रीः स्थिता हि अस्याम् संप्रजह्यात् मृते मयि || ४-२२-१६_END
BEGIN_
"The bounteous goddess of triumph ensconced in this golden pendant will completely
leave it off on my death, avoiding the flaw of touching a corpse, isn't it... hence oh, Sugreeva,
you wear it." Thus Vali spoke to Sugreeva. [4-22-16]_END

B_4_C_23_10
BEGIN_
सुहृत् चैव हि भर्ता च प्रकृत्या च मम प्रियः || ३-२३-११प्रहारे च पराक्रान्तः शूरः पंचत्वम् आगतः |_END
BEGIN_
"By your nature you are my beloved, besides, you are a good-hearted one, more so, you are my husband, 
moreover, you are a valiant triumphing over your enemies in assaults, such as you are you have attained 
the fifth state, the death. [3-23-11b, 12a]_END

B_4_C_24_1
BEGIN_
स बाष्प पूर्णेन मुखेन् पश्यन् क्षणेन निर्विण्ण मना मनस्वी |जगाम रामस्य शनैः समीपम् भृत्यैः वृत्तः 
संपरिदूयमानः || ४-२४-२_END
BEGIN_
While that kind hearted Sugreeva observed Tara for a moment he is despaired at heart, tears filled his
