face, and lamenting very much he slowly paced to the near of Rama, surrounded by his attendants. [4-24-2]_END

B_4_C_22_16
BEGIN_
इति एवम् उक्तः सुग्रीवो वालिना भ्रातृ सौहृदात् |
हर्षम् त्यक्त्वा पुनर् दीनो ग्रह ग्रस्त इव उडु राट् || ४-२२-१७_END
BEGIN_
Thus, that way when Vali spoke to Sugreeva with brotherly kind-heartedness, Sugreeva
again waned away forgoing his spiritedness, like the lord of stars, namely the Moon, when eaten
away by the planet, namely Rahu, during lunar eclipse. [4-22-17]_END

B_4_C_18_41
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु रामेण वाली प्रव्यथितो भृशम् |न दोषम् राघवे दध्यौ धर्मे अधिगत निश्चयः || ४-१८-४४_END
BEGIN_
Vali is much distressed at heart of hearts when Rama has said categorically in that way, whereby, deriving 
certitude about rightness he found no incorrectness with Rama. [4-18-44]_END

B_4_C_23_11
BEGIN_
पति हीना तु या नारी कामम् भवतु पुत्रिणी || ३-२३-१२धन धान्य समृद्धा अपि विधवा इति उच्यते जनैः |_END
BEGIN_
"Perhaps a woman might have mothered many children, and perhaps affluent with riches and crops, still 
people will call her a widow, if she is without husband. [3-23-12b, 13a]_END

B_4_C_24_2
BEGIN_
स तम् समासाद्य गृहीत चापम् उदात्तम् आशी विष तुल्य बाणम् |यशश्विनम् लक्षण लक्षित अंगम् अवस्थितम् 
राघवम् इति उवाच || ४-२४-३_END
BEGIN_
On approaching him who is majestic, who is still handling his bow and snake-like arrow, a distinguished 
person with all of his limbs adorned with great attributes that an emperor should have by birth, to 
such a Raghava who is standing nearby, Sugreeva spoke this way. [4-24-3]_END

B_4_C_22_17
BEGIN_
तत् वालि वचनात् शान्तः कुर्वन् युक्तम् अतंद्रितः |
जग्राह सो अभ्यनुज्ञातो मालाम् ताम् चैव कांचनीम् || ४-२२-१८_END
BEGIN_
Quietened by Vali's words and conducting himself befittingly and attentively in the
given situation, Sugreeva has then taken that golden chain only when Vali authorised him.
[4-22-18]_END

B_4_C_18_42
BEGIN_
प्रत्युवाच ततो रामम् प्रांजलिर् वानरेश्वरः |यत् त्वम् आत्थ नरश्रेष्ठ तत् थथा एव न अत्र संशयः || 
४-१८-४५_END
BEGIN_
That lord of vanara-s then replied Rama with adjoined palms, "oh, best one among men, what all you have 
said is that way proper, undoubtedly. [4-18-45]_END

B_4_C_23_12
BEGIN_
स्व गात्र प्रभवे वीर शेषे रुधिर मण्डले || ३-२३-१३कृमि राग परिस्तोमे स्वकीये शयने यथा |_END
BEGIN_
"How do you repose now on a sheet of blood flowing from your own body, oh, brave one, as if you are 
reclining on your own bed spread with a bed sheet of red blood colour? [3-23-13b, 14a]_END

B_4_C_24_3
BEGIN_
यथा प्रतिज्ञातम् इदम् नरेन्द्र कृतम् त्वया दृउष्ट फलम् च कर्म |मम अद्य भोगेषु नरेन्द्र सूनो मनो 
निवृत्तम् हत जिवितेन || ४-२४-४_END
BEGIN_
"As promised, oh, best king, you have accomplished this deed with its eventual fruition of getting back 
the kingdom and my wife, but now, oh, prince, my heart is backsliding from extravagances of kingdom 
and kingship, as my life itself is rendered despicable, for I got my brother killed. [4-24-4]_END

B_4_C_22_18
BEGIN_
ताम् मालाम् कांचनीम् दत्त्वा वाली दृष्ट्वा आत्मजम् स्थितम् |
संसिद्धः प्रेत्य भावाय स्नेहात् अंगदम् अब्रवीत् || ४-२२-१९_END
BEGIN_
On giving away that golden pendant, and on seeing his son who is available nearby,
readying himself towards his end that is setting in, Vali affectionately spoke to Angada.
[4-22-19]_END

B_4_C_18_43
BEGIN_
प्रतिवक्तुम् प्रकृष्टे हि न अपकृष्टः तु शक्नुयात् |यत् अयुक्तम् मया पूर्वम् प्रमादात् वाक्यम् अप्रियम् 
|| ४-१८-४६तत्र अपि खलु माम् दोषम् कर्तुम् न अर्हसि राघव |_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed an ignoble cannot disprove a nobleman, Raghava, and with regards to the undesirable and improper 
words I have unwittingly spoken earlier, in that mater too it will be truly unapt of you to make me 
blameworthy, as I spoke them in anguish and ignorance. [4-18-46, 47a]_END

B_4_C_23_13
BEGIN_
रेणु शोणित संवीतम् गात्रम् तव समंततः || ३-२३-१४परिरब्धुम् न शक्नोमि भुजाभ्याम् प्लवगर्षभ |_END
BEGIN_
"I have no strength to closely embrace you with both my arms, oh, best fly-jumper, when the blood and 
dust covering your body comes in between. [3-23-14b, 15a]_END

B_4_C_24_4
BEGIN_
अस्याम् महिष्याम् तु भृशम् रुदत्याम् पुरे अति विक्रोशति दुःख तप्ते |हते नृपे संशयिते अंगदे च न राम 
राज्ये रमते मनो मे || ४-२४-५_END
BEGIN_
"When the king is killed, this empress is wailing bitterly, much wailing is there in city scorched in 
sadness, and Angada too is in a doubtful state of sustaining his lives in the fond of his father, as 
such oh, Rama, my heart is not taking delight in kingdom. [4-24-5]_END

B_4_C_22_19
BEGIN_
देश कालौ भजस्व अद्य क्षममाणः प्रिय अप्रिये |
सुख दुःख सहः काले सुग्रीव वशगो भव || ४-२२-२०_END
BEGIN_
"From now on, observing time and place you have to tolerate pain or pleasure, endure
mirth or misery on your going under the control of Sugreeva. [4-22-20]_END

B_4_C_18_44
BEGIN_
त्वम् हि दृष्टार्थ तत्त्वज्ञः प्रजानाम् च हिते रतः |कार्य कारण सिद्धौ च प्रसन्ना बुद्धिः अव्यया 
|| ४-१८-४७_END
BEGIN_
"You alone are the knower of recourses and their real nature, namely probity, prosperity, pleasure seeking, 
and emancipation; dharma, artha, kaama, moksha ; and you take delight 
in the welfare of subjects, and your faultless intellect is clear in accomplishing ends by judging the 
causes and effects. [4-18-47b, c]_END

B_4_C_24_5
BEGIN_
क्रोधाद् अमर्षाद् अतिविप्रधर्षाद् भ्रातुर् वधो मे अनुमतः पुरस्तात् |हते तु इदानीम् हरि यूधपे अस्मिन् 
सुतीक्ष्णम् इक्ष्वाकु वर प्रतप्स्ये || ४-२४-६_END
BEGIN_
"In the first instance I have agreed for the elimination of my brother owing to my anger, intolerance 
and as I was subjected to too much ignominy, but now, oh, best one from Ikshvaku-s, when the chief of 
monkeys Vali is put to death, I am painfully remorseful. [4-24-6]_END

B_4_C_23_14
BEGIN_
कृत कृत्यो अद्य सुग्रीवो वैरे अस्मिन् अतिदारुणे || ३-२३-१५यस्य राम विमुक्तेन हृतम् एक इषुणा भयम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Single arrow released by Rama has doubly benefited Sugreeva in this highly deplorable enmity between 
you and Sugreeva, as his ambition to become the king is fulfilled and his fear from your persecution, 
too, is evanished. [3-23-15b, 16a]_END

B_4_C_22_20
BEGIN_
यथा हि त्वम् महाबाहो लालितः सततम् मया |
न तथा वर्तमानम् त्वाम् सुग्रीवो बहु मन्यते || ४-२२-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Oh dextrous Angada, as to how I have entertained you in whichever way you conducted
yourself with me, Sugreeva may not approve of such a puerile behaviour of yours, if you resort to
it. [4-22-21]_END

B_4_C_18_45
BEGIN_
माम् अपि अवगतम् धर्मात् व्यतिक्रान्त पुरस्कृतम् |धर्म संहितया वाचा धर्मज्ञ परिपालय || ४-१८-४८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, the knower of probity, I am the one who digressed from the rightness and a forerunner among 
such transgressors, such as I am, give absolution even to me with words abounded with rightness." Vali 
is thus saying to Rama. [4-18-48]_END

B_4_C_24_6
BEGIN_
श्रेयो अद्य मन्ये मम शैल मुख्ये तस्मिन् हि वासः चिरम् ऋष्यमूके |यथा तथा वर्तयतः स्व वृत्या न इमम् 
निहत्य त्रिदिवसय लाभः || ४-२४-७_END
BEGIN_
"I think it would be better for me to live on that best mountain Rishyamuka for ever in an as is where 
is condition, somehow spending life befitting to a monkey, and achieving even heaven on killing my brother 
is of no good. [4-24-7]_END

B_4_C_23_15
BEGIN_
शरेण हृदि लग्नेन गात्र संस्पर्शने तव || ३-२३-१६वार्यामि त्वाम् निरीक्षन्ती त्वयि पंचत्वम् आगते |_END
BEGIN_
"In vain, I have been watching you without a wink, on whom fatality has descended, as this arrow stuck 
in your chest is hindering me to embrace you..." Thus wailed Tara. [3-23-16b, 17a]_END

B_4_C_25_0
BEGIN_
स सुग्रीवम् च ताराम् च स अंगदाम् सह लक्ष्मणः |समान शोकः काकुत्स्थः सांत्वयन् इदम् अब्रवीत् || ४-२५-१_END
BEGIN_
While a similar disquiet of Sugreeva is prevailing over Rama and Lakshmana, Rama palliatively said this 
to Sugreeva, and even to Tara together with Angada. [4-25-1]_END

B_4_C_22_21
BEGIN_
ना अस्य अमित्रैः गतम् गच्छेः मा शत्रुभिः अरिंदम |
भर्तुः अर्थ परो दान्तः सुग्रीव वशगो भव || ४-२२-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Do not reach at his unfriendly ones, nor come near his enemies, oh, enemy-destroyer
Angada, you shall be in the control of Sugreeva attending to the purposes of your lord with
self-control. [4-22-22]_END

B_4_C_18_46
BEGIN_
बाष्प संरुद्ध कण्ठः तु वाली स आर्त रवः शनैः |उवाच रामम् संप्रेक्ष्य पंकलग्न इव द्विपः || ४-१८-४९_END
BEGIN_
Vali who like an elephant plumped in slough continued to say slowly, with tears fully impeding his throat 
and with an agonised moan, on keenly observing Rama. [4-18-49]_END

B_4_C_24_7
BEGIN_
न त्वा जिघांसामि चर इति यत् माम् अयम् महात्मा मतिमान् उवाच |तस्य एवे तत् राम वचो अनुरूपम् इदम् वचः 
कर्म च मे अनुरूपम् || ४-२४-८_END
BEGIN_
"The words which he used to speak to me saying, 'I do not wish to kill you, begone...' are befitting 
to that great-souled and rational vanara, and my words in asking you to him to kill him, and my deeds 
in getting him killed are befitting to me, as an irrational vanara. [4-24-8]_END

B_4_C_23_16
BEGIN_
उद्बबर्ह शरम् नीलः तस्य गात्र गतम् तदा || ३-२३-१७गिरि गह्वर संलीनम् दीप्तम् आशी विषम् यथा |_END
BEGIN_
"Then the monkey chief Nila extricated that arrow which is stuck in the chest of Vali, as with the extraction 
of a firmly wedged sparkling snake from the cavity of a mound. [3-23-17b, 18a]_END

B_4_C_25_1
BEGIN_
न शोक परितापेन श्रेयसा युज्यते मृतः |यद् अत्र अनंतरम् कार्यम् तत् समाधातुम् अर्हथ || ४-२५-२_END
BEGIN_
"Deceased will not derive bliss by sorrowful mourning, hence it will be appropriate to arrange for that 
work which is subsequent in this matter. [4-25-2]_END

B_4_C_22_22
BEGIN_
न च अतिप्रणयः कार्यः कर्तव्यो अप्रणयः च ते |
उभयम् हि महादोषम् तस्मात् अंतर दृक् भव || ४-२२-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Do not conduct yourself with excessive friendliness or unfriendliness, as this pair
of opposites itself has a flaw, therefore you cultivate an intermediary outlook." Vali thus spoke
to Angada. [4-22-23]_END

B_4_C_18_47
BEGIN_
न च आत्मानम् अहम् शोचे न ताराम् न अपि बान्धवान् |यथा पुत्रम् गुणश्रेष्ठम् अंगदम् कनकांगदम् || ४-१८-५०_END
BEGIN_
"Also, I neither worry for myself, nor for Tara, nor even for any relatives of mine, as I do for my 
son Angada, the best-virtuous one with golden bicep-lets. [4-18-50]_END

B_4_C_24_8
BEGIN_
भ्राता कथम् नाम महा गुणस्य भ्रातुर् वधम् राम विरोचयेत |राजस्य दुःखस्य च वीर सारम् विचिन्तयन् काम 
पुरस्कृतो अपि || ४-२४-९_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed, oh, brave Rama, whether killing one's own brother will be self-torturous? Or, taking pleasure 
in kingdom on killing that brother will be more? Or, the distress ensuing that killing will be the most? 
Without truly discriminating these cruces, even if one has one's own own avarice in prospect, who is 
he that is going to take pleasure in killing his own highly honoured brother? Excepting me! [4-24-9]_END

B_4_C_23_17
BEGIN_
तस्य निष्कृष्यमाणस्य बाणस्य च बभौ द्युतिः || ३-२३-१८अस्त मस्तक संरुद्धो रश्मिः दिनकरात् इव |_END
BEGIN_
The sparkle of Rama's arrow while it is being extracted from Vali's chest is much the same as the sparkles 
of more brilliant sunrays that are extracted by the end of daytime, when the sun is sinking beyond the 
summit of dusky western mountain, and as contrasted with the hue of dusk. [3-23-18b, 19a]_END

B_4_C_25_2
BEGIN_
लोक वृत्तम् अनुष्ठेयम् कृतम् वो बाष्प मोक्षणम् |न कालाद् उत्तरम् किंचित् कर्म शक्यम् उपासितुम् || 
४-२५-३_END
BEGIN_
"Worldly observances are to be observed, thus your activity of tear-shedding this far is justifiable, 
but after the lapse of time of any individual, it is impossible to activate that individual by any other 
remote activity like weeping._END

B_4_C_18_48
BEGIN_
स मम अदर्शनात् दीनो बाल्यात् प्रभृति लालितः |तटाक इव पीतांबुः उपशोषम् गमिष्यति || ४-१८-५१_END
BEGIN_
"Right from his childhood I fondly looked after Angada, and he will be dejected when he sees me no more, 
and he withers away like a lake with its water drained for a drink. [4-18-51]_END

B_4_C_22_23
BEGIN_
इति उक्त्वा अथ विवृत्त अक्षः शर संपीडितो भृशम् |
विवृतैः दशनैः भीमैः बभूव उत्क्रान्त जीवितः || ४-२२-२४_END
BEGIN_
He who is highly tortured by the arrow of Rama spoke to Angada in that way, and
afterwards his eyeballs rolled-up, mouth hung open baring his horrid teeth, and his life too took
to flight from his body. [4-22-24]_END

B_4_C_24_9
BEGIN_
वधो हि मे मतो न असीत् स्व महात्म्या अव्यतिक्रमात् |मम आसीत् बुद्धिः दुरात्म्यात् प्राण हारी व्यतिक्रमः 
|| ४-२४-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Killing me is not in the intent of Vali violating his probity, but my intent has become evilly life 
taking, violating my own probity. [4-24-10]_END

B_4_C_23_18
BEGIN_
पेतुः क्षतज धाराः तु व्रणेभ्यः तस्य सर्वशः || ३-२३-१९ताम्र गैरिक संपृक्ता धारा इव धरा धरात् |_END
BEGIN_
The blood streams flown out of the gashes of Vali fell everywhere like the streams of water flowing 
from a mountain saturated with coppery mineral-ores. [3-23-19b, 20a]_END

B_4_C_25_3
BEGIN_
नियतिः कारणम् लोके नियतिः कर्म साधनम् |नियतिः सर्व भूतानाम् नियोगेषु इह कारणम् || ४-२५-४_END
BEGIN_
"Fate is the cause of all the worlds, Fate is the instrument for action, Fate is the deciding factor 
for motivation of all beings in these worlds. [4-25-4]_END

B_4_C_18_49
BEGIN_
बालः च अकृतबुद्धिः च एक पुत्रः च मे प्रियः |तारेयो राम भवता रक्षणीयो महाबलः || ४-१८-५२_END
BEGIN_
"He is boyish, juvenile, and the only dear son of mine, oh, Rama, as such that great-mighty son of Tara 
needs your protection. [4-18-52]_END

B_4_C_22_24
BEGIN_
ततो विचुक्रुशुर् तत्र वानरा हत यूथपाः |
परिदेवयमानाः ते सर्वे प्लवग सत्तमाः || ४-२२-२५_END
BEGIN_
Then, all those best monkeys avaialble there have started to weep when their monkey
chief is dead, and for that matter they have loudly squawked at his death in this way.
[4-22-25]_END

B_4_C_24_10
BEGIN_
द्रुम शाका अवभग्नो अहम् मुहुर्तम् परिनिष्टनन् |स्वान्तयित्वा अनेन उक्तः न पुनः कर्तुम् अर्हसि || 
४-२४-११_END
BEGIN_
"I was whining for a time when Vali thrashed me with a tree branch, as if with a schoolmaster's cane, 
but later on comforting me he said this to me, 'do not do this again, this daring me to fight you back.' 
[4-24-11]_END

B_4_C_23_19
BEGIN_
अवकीर्णम् विमार्जन्ती भर्तारम् रण रेणुना || ३-२३-२०अस्रैः नयनजैः शूरम् सिषेच अस्त्र समाहतम् |_END
BEGIN_
On wiping off war dust with which her husband is muffled up, with tears gushing from her eyes she drenched 
that valiant one who is summarily hit by the missile of Rama. [3-23-20b, 21a]_END

B_4_C_25_4
BEGIN_
न कर्ता कस्यचित् कश्चित् नियोगे च अपि न ईश्वरः |स्वभावे वर्तते लोकः तस्य कालः परायणम् || ४-२५-५_END
BEGIN_
"None is an instrument in motivating someone else to do something or otherwise, none is also a controlling 
entity of others, and even the world functions in its own nature, and that Time is cardinal for that 
world. [4-25-5]_END

B_4_C_18_50
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवे च अंगदे चैव विधत्स्व मतिम् उत्तमाम् |त्वम् हि गोप्ता च शास्ता च कार्याकार्य विधौ स्थितः 
|| ४-१८-५३_END
BEGIN_
"You have firm convictions about practicable and impracticable procedures, and you alone are the protector 
of the good and punisher of the bad, hence treat both Sugreeva and Angada with equal compassion. [4-18-53]_END

B_4_C_22_25
BEGIN_
किष्किन्धा हि अथ शून्या च स्वर् गते वानरेश्वरे |
उद्यानानि च शून्यानि पर्वताः कानानि च || ४-२२-२६
हते प्लवग शार्दूले निष् प्रभा वानराः कृताः |_END
BEGIN_
"When the lord of monkeys departed to heaven Kishkindha is indeed rendered derelict,
dreary are the gardens, deserted are the mountains and forests as well, and when the tiger among
fly-jumpers is dead all the vanara-s are rendered up into a lacklustre life. [4-22-26, 27a]_END

B_4_C_24_11
BEGIN_
भ्रातृत्वम् आर्य भावः च धर्मः च अनेन रक्षितः |मया क्रोधः च कामः च कपित्वम् च प्रदर्शितम् || ४-२४-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Fraternity, dignity and also probity are conserved by him, while I exhibited furiousness, enviousness 
and also naughtiness of a monkey. [4-24-12]_END

B_4_C_23_20
BEGIN_
रुधिरोक्षित सर्वान्गम् दृष्ट्वा विनिहतम् पतिम् || ३-२३-२१उवाच तारा पिंगाक्षम् पुत्रम् अंगदम् अंगना 
|_END
BEGIN_
On giving attention to all of the blood wet limbs of her slain husband that lady Tara spoke to her son 
Angada whose eyes are coppery-red. [3-23-21b, 22a]_END

B_4_C_25_5
BEGIN_
न कालः कालम् अत्येति न कालः परिहीयते |स्वभावम् च समासाद्य न कश्चित् अतिवर्तते || ४-२५-६_END
BEGIN_
"Time will not transcend Time, neither Time transgresses itself, and on attaining the nature endowed 
by Time nothing can overstep its own Fate. [4-25-6]_END

B_4_C_18_51
BEGIN_
या ते नरपते वृत्तिः भरते लक्ष्मणे च या |सुग्रीवे च अंगदे राजन् ताम् चिंतयितुम् अर्हसि || ४-१८-५४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, lord of men, it will be apt of you to show the same kind of outlook towards Sugreeva, oh, king, 
even towards Angada, which you have for Bharata and Lakshmana. [4-18-54]_END

B_4_C_22_26
BEGIN_
यस्य वेगेन महता काननानि वनानि च || ४-२२-२७
पुष्प ओघेण अनुबद्धन्ते करिष्यति तत् अद्य कहः |_END
BEGIN_
"And by the impetus of whose great rapidity flowers available in forests and
woodlands used to shower on him in torrents and enwreathe him from behind, that Vali is no more,
and now who has got such an impetus? [4-22-27b, 28a]_END

B_4_C_24_12
BEGIN_
अचिंतनीयम् परिवर्जनीयम्अनीप्सनीयम् न अन्वेक्षणीयम् |प्राप्तो अस्मि पाप्मानम् वयस्यभ्रातुः 
वध त्वाष्ट्र वधात् इव इन्द्रः || ४-२४-१३_END
BEGIN_
"As Indra acquired sin on killing Vishvarupa, the son of Tvastha, I too derived a sin by killing my 
brother, which sin is absolutely unimaginable for quantification, totally undesirable at any given time, 
wholly discardable by sagacious souls, and a disgustingly horrible spectre of brotherly hate. [4-24-13]_END

B_4_C_26_0
BEGIN_
ततः शोक अभिसंतप्तम् सुग्रीवम् क्लिन्न वासनम् |शाखा मृग महामात्राः परिवार्य उपतस्थिरे || ४-२६-१_END
BEGIN_
The eminent ministers of tree-branch animals then surrounded Sugreeva, who is very much seared in grief and who 
is still wearing damp cloths, as he just a while ago offered watery oblations to his deceased brother, stood accessible 
to him. [4-26-1]_END

B_4_C_23_21
BEGIN_
अवस्थाम् पश्चिमाम् पश्य पितुः पुत्र सुदारुणाम् || ३-२३-२२संप्रसक्तस्य वैरस्य गतो अन्तः पाप कर्मणा 
|_END
BEGIN_
"See the highly harrowing end time plight of your father, oh, son, he reached his end owing to the enmity 
harnessed by sinful deeds. [3-23-22b, 23a]_END

B_4_C_25_6
BEGIN_
न कालस्य अस्ति बंधुत्वम् न हेतुर् न पराक्रमः |न मित्र ज्ञाति संबन्धः कारणम् न आत्मनो वशः || ४-२५-७_END
BEGIN_
"Time has no kinship, thus it has no partiality, there is nothing instrumental to override Time, hence 
nothing can override it, and there are no causative factors to Time that connect through friends or 
relatives, hence all are equal in its viewpoint. [4-25-7]_END

B_4_C_22_27
BEGIN_
येन दत्तम् महत् युद्धम् गन्धर्वस्य महात्मनः || ४-२२-२८
गोलभस्य महाबाहुः दश वर्षाणि पंच च |
न एव रात्रौ न दिवसे तत् युद्धम् उपशाम्यति || ४-२२-२९_END
BEGIN_
"By which great-souled Vali a ferocious duel was given to the celestial, namely the
great armed Golabha, which did not cease either in the daytime or night till Vali felled Golabha,
that Vali is no more. [4-22-28b, 29]_END

B_4_C_18_52
BEGIN_
मत् दोष कृत दोषाम् ताम् यथा ताराम् तपस्विनीम् |सुग्रीवो न अवमन्येत तथा अवस्थातुम् अर्हसि || ४-१८-५५_END
BEGIN_
"The fault occurring from my fault of maltreating Sugreeva may not light upon that self-reproachful 
Tara, and it will be apt of you to see that Sugreeva will not look down on her treating her as the wife 
his rival. [4-18-55]_END

B_4_C_24_13
BEGIN_
पाप्मानम् इन्द्रस्य मही जलम् च वृक्षाः च कामम् जगृहुः स्त्रियः च |को नाम पाप्मानम् इमम् सहेत शाखा 
मृगस्य प्रतिपत्तुम् इच्छेत् || ४-२४-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Earth, waters, trees and women took the burden of Indra's sins, but who in name will bear the burden 
of this sin of mine, that too the sin of a monkey, who wishes to share? [4-24-14]_END

B_4_C_26_1
BEGIN_
अभिगम्य महाबाहुम् रामम् अक्लिष्ट कारिणम् |स्थिताः प्रांजलयः सर्वे पितामहम् इव ऋषयः || ४-२६-२_END
BEGIN_
On going towards the dexterous Rama, whose exploits are effortless, all of those monkeys tarried with their palms 
adjoined as with the sages tarrying in the presence of Brahma, the Forefather. [4-26-2]_END

B_4_C_23_22
BEGIN_
बाल सूर्योज्ज्वल तनुम् प्रयातम् यम सादनम् || ३-२३-२३अभिवादय राजानम् पितरम् पुत्र मानदम् |_END
BEGIN_
"To him, whose physical splendour vied with the dazzle of rising sun, to that father, king, and the 
accorder of honour you pay you last obeisance as he journeyed to the abode of Time-god." Thus Tara said 
to Angada. [3-23-23b, 24a]_END

B_4_C_25_7
BEGIN_
किम् तु काल परीणामो द्रष्टव्यः साधु पश्यता |धर्मः च अर्थः च कामः च कालक्रम समाहिताः || ४-२५-८_END
BEGIN_
"But even the mutations brought forth by Time are observable by a perceiver with a clear vision, and 
the virtue, wealth, pleasures are to be perceived as cumulated during the course of Time. [4-25-8]_END

B_4_C_22_28
BEGIN_
ततः षोडशमे वर्षे गोलभो विनिपातितः |
तम् हत्वा दुर्विनीतिम् तु वाली दंष्ट्र करालवान् |
सर्वा अभयम् करः अस्माकम् कथम् एष निपातितः || ४-२२-३०_END
BEGIN_
"Thereafter, in the sixteenth year Vali unquestionably felled Golabha, and on
killing that evil-minded Golabha with his zigzag teeth Vali accorded fearlessness to all of us, how
such a Vali is felled now?" Thus the monkeys raised hue and cry. [4-22-30]_END

B_4_C_18_53
BEGIN_
त्वया हि अनुगृहीतेन शक्यम् राज्यम् उपासितुम् |त्वत् वशे वर्तमानेन तव चित्त अनुवर्तिना || ४-१८-५६
शक्यम् दिवम् च आर्जयितुम् वसुधाम् च अपि शासितुम् |_END
BEGIN_
"When you indeed approve someone, he is capable enough to govern the kingdom, abiding himself under 
your control and following your heart, why a kingdom, he can rule the earth, why earth, he can even 
achieve the heaven itself. [4-18-56, 57a]_END

B_4_C_24_14
BEGIN_
ना अर्हामि सन्मानम् इमम् प्रजानाम् न यौव राज्यम् कुत एव राज्यम् |अधर्म युक्तम् कुल नाश युक्तम् एवम् 
विधम् राघव कर्म कृत्वा || ४-२४-१५_END
BEGIN_
"On undertaking this sort of deed that includes unjust and involves ruination of one's own race, I am 
unsuited for this sort of accolade from the subjects of this kingdom, and when I am ineligible to be 
the price regent of this kingdom, wherefore to become its regent? [4-24-15]_END

B_4_C_26_2
BEGIN_
ततः कांचन शैल आभः तरुण अर्क निभ आननः |अब्रवीत् प्रांजलिर् वाक्यम् हनुमान् मारुत आत्मजः || ४-२६-३_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma, the son of Air-god, whose sheen is like that of the golden mountain Meru, and whose visage is like that 
of the tender sun in its glint, then spoke this sentence reverently adjoining his palms. [4-26-3]_END

B_4_C_23_23
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः समुत्थाय जग्राह चरणौ पितुः || ३-२३-२४भुजाभ्याम् पीन वृताभ्याम् अंगदो अहम् इति ब्रुवन् 
|_END
BEGIN_
When he is said so, Angada swiftly rose and touched the feet of his father with both of his rotund-shouldered 
sinewy arms saying, "father, I am Angada..." [3-23-24b, 25a]_END

B_4_C_25_8
BEGIN_
इतः स्वाम् प्रकृतिम् वाली गतः प्राप्तः क्रिया फलम् |साम दान अर्थ संयोगैः पवित्रम् प्लवग ईश्वर || 
४-२५-९_END
BEGIN_
"That king of fly-jumpers Vali departed from here on attaining his own nature of subtle-soul, and he 
obtained pious fruits connected with his one time actions befitting to a king like, friendliness, courteousness, 
and forgivingness required of a king. [4-25-9]_END

B_4_C_18_54
BEGIN_
त्वतः अहम् वधम् आकांक्षयन् वार्यमाणो अपि तारया || ४-१८-५७सुग्रीवेण सह भ्राता द्वन्द्व युद्धम् उपागतम् 
|इति उक्त्वा वानरो रामम् विरराम हरीश्वरः || ४-१८-५८_END
BEGIN_
"Though Tara dissuaded me I met with my brother Sugreeva in a duel as though aspiring elimination at 
your hand.." On saying thus to Rama that vanara, Vali the lord of monkeys' paused for a while. [4-18-57b, 
58]_END

B_4_C_22_29
BEGIN_
हते तु वीरे प्लवगाधिपे तदा
प्लवंगमाः तत्र न शर्म लेभिरे |
वने चराः सिंह युते महावने
यथा हि गावो निहते गवाम् पतौ || ४-२२-३१_END
BEGIN_
But when that fly-jumper's brave lord Vali is killed, those fly-jumpers have gone
into a freneticness in that matter of Vali's killing, as with the cows becoming frenetic when their
husbanding bull is killed while moving in a great forest that is riddled with a lion. [4-22-31]_END

B_4_C_24_15
BEGIN_
पापस्य कर्ता अस्मि विगर्हितस्यक्षुद्रस्य लोक अपकृतस्य लोके |शोको महान् मम अभिवर्तते अयम्
वृष्टेः यथा निम्नम् इव अम्बु वेगः || ४-२४-१६_END
BEGIN_
"In this world, I am a committer of a felony which is debased, highly damnable and pernicious to the 
world itself, whereupon this irresistible misery is rushing in on me, as with the rush of speeding rainy-waters 
towards a declivity. [4-24-16]_END

B_4_C_26_3
BEGIN_
भवत् प्रसादात् काकुत्स्थ पितृ पैतामहम् महत् |वानराणाम् सुदंष्ट्राणाम् संपन्न बलशालिनाम् || ४-२६-४महात्मानाम् 
सुदुष्प्रापम् प्राप्तम् राज्यम् इदम् प्रभो |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, lord Rama, this magnificent kingdom of deferential monkeys who are armed with the teeth, and whose might 
is a privileged one - since our might is not dependent on any weapons or other tactical warfare, except our own 
bodily strength - and oh, Kakutstha, that which belongs to his father and forefathers, and that which is otherwise 
impossible for him to regain, Sugreeva regained such a kingdom with your grace. [4-26-4, 5a]_END

B_4_C_23_24
BEGIN_
अभिवादयमानम् त्वाम् अंगदम् त्वम् यथा पुरा || ३-२३-२५दीर्घ आयुर् भव पुत्र इति किम् अर्थम् न अभिभाषसे 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Why do not you bless Angada saying, 'long live, son...' when he is paying resects to you, as earlier?" 
Thus Tara is addressing Vali in her anguish. [3-23-25b, 26a]_END

B_4_C_25_9
BEGIN_
स्व धर्मस्य च संयोगात् जितः तेन महात्मना |स्वर्गः परिगृहीतः च प्राणान् अपरिरक्षता || ४-२५-१०_END
BEGIN_
"That great-souled Vali did not care to safeguard his own lives in combat, and by virtue of his own 
rightness of a true combatant unworried of his life, he acquired heaven. [4-25-10]_END

B_4_C_18_55
BEGIN_
स तम् आश्वासयत् रामो वालिनम् व्यक्त दर्शनम् |साधु सम्मतया वाचा धर्म तत्त्वार्त्ध युक्तया || ४-१८-५९_END
BEGIN_
Rama consoled Vali with words that are agreeable to savants and that contain the essence and meaning 
of rightness, while Vali is with an evincible perspective of righteousness by now. And Rama spoke to 
Vali this way. [4-18-59]_END

B_4_C_22_30
BEGIN_
ततः तु तारा व्यसन अर्णव प्लुता
मृतस्या भर्तुर् वदनम् समीक्ष्य सा |
जगाम भूमिम् परिरभ्य वालिनम्
महा द्रुमम् छिन्नम् इव आश्रिता लता || ४-२२-३२_END
BEGIN_
But then Tara, whelmed under a ocean called affliction closely observed her dead
husband's face, embraced him and collapsed onto ground as with any creeper plant when the giant
tree on which it is hinging is hacked down. [4-22-32]_END

B_4_C_26_4
BEGIN_
भवता समनुज्ञातः प्रविश्य नगरम् शुभम् || ४-२६-५संविधास्यति कार्याणि सर्वाणि ससुहृत् गणः|स्नातो अयम् विविधैर् 
गन्धैर् औषधैः च यथा विधि || ४-२६-६_END
BEGIN_
"And if you empower, this Sugreeva will enter the propitious city Kishkindha along with a group good-hearted friends, 
and he will get anointed procedurally with various essences and herbal-extracts as its king, and thus he can revamp 
all the administration. [4-26-5b, 6]_END

B_4_C_24_16
BEGIN_
सोदर्य अघाता अपर गात्र वालः संताप हस्त अक्षि शिरो विषाणः |एनोमयो माम् अभिहन्ति हस्ती दृप्तो नदी 
कूलम् इव प्रवृद्धः || ४-२४- १७_END
BEGIN_
"The sin of mine in killing my brother assumed a form of an elephant, where my sinister motives of killing 
my own brother have assumed that elephant's hind and tail, and my causing agony to my own brother has 
become that elephant's head, eyes, trunk, and tusks, with them that berserk and monstrous elephant called 
sin, is goring me as it would gore a riverbed. [4-24- 17]_END

B_4_C_23_25
BEGIN_
अहम् पुत्र सहाया त्वाम् उपासे गत चेतनम् |सिंहेन पातितम् सद्यो गौः स वत्सा इव गो वृषम् || ३-२३-२६_END
BEGIN_
"I am living through seeing the lifeless state of yours with the help of my son, no more than a helpless 
cow that sits near her bull with its calf, when that bull is slain by a lion, just now. [3-23-26b, c]_END

B_4_C_25_10
BEGIN_
एषा वै नियतिः श्रेष्ठा याम् गतो हरि यूथपः |तत् अलम् परितापेन प्राप्त कालम् उपास्यताम् || ४-२५-११_END
BEGIN_
"Which course the commander of monkeys undertook is the choicest course of fatality, and hence, enough 
is this sorrowing, and let works incumbent on the present time be undertaken reverently..." So said 
Rama to Sugreeva. [4-25-11]_END

B_4_C_18_56
BEGIN_
न संतापः त्वया कार्यम् एतत् अर्थम् प्लवंगम |न वयम् भवता चिंत्या न अपि आत्मा हरिसत्तम |वयम् भवत् 
विशेषेण धर्मतः कृत निश्चयाः || ४-१८-६०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, fly-jumper, you need not be remorseful about your wife, son and others you leave behind, because 
we take care of them... nor you should bother about us thinking that we have arbitrarily eliminated 
you, nor necessarily bother about yourself for committing sins, as we took this decision according to 
rightness and considerateness in your respect. [4-18-60]_END

B_4_C_24_17
BEGIN_
अंहो बतेदम् नृ वर अविषह्य निवर्तते मे हृदि साधु वृत्तम् |अग्नौ विवर्णम् परितप्य मानम् किट्टम् यथा 
राघव जात रूपम् || ४-२४-१८_END
BEGIN_
"How difficult is this insufferable sacrilege of mine, oh, best king, owing to which my good breeding 
is shed from my heart, as with the gold, which if alloyed will be intolerant of that filth, but oh, 
Raghava, even the gold sheds itself from scum when melted, and though I melt in grief this scum of sacrilege 
is unshed. [4-24-18]_END

B_4_C_26_5
BEGIN_
अर्चयिष्यति माल्यैः च रत्नैः च त्वाम् विशेषतः |इमाम् गिरि गुहाम् रम्याम् अभिगन्तुम् त्वम् अर्हसि || ४-२६-७
कुरुष्व स्वामि संबन्धम् वानरान् संप्रहर्षयन् |_END
BEGIN_
"He would like to honour you in a remarkable way with garlands and precious gems, hence it will be apt of you 
to enter this delightful mountain cave, namely Kishkindha, and you may kindly consolidate the congenial affinity 
between the governor and the governed for the very high exhilaration of Vanara-s." Hanuma appealed Rama in this 
way. [4-26-7, 8a]_END

B_4_C_23_26
BEGIN_
इष्ट्वा संग्राम यज्ञेन राम प्रहरण अंभसा |अस्मिन् अवभृथे स्नातः कथम् पत्न्या मया विना || ३-२३-२७_END
BEGIN_
"How can you singly take the ultimate bath of a Vedic ritual after your conducting a ritual like combat, 
in the waters called bloodstreams caused by Rama's arrow, that too, when I, your wife, am available like 
a co-officiator of a Vedic ritual? [3-23-27]_END

B_4_C_25_11
BEGIN_
वचन अन्ते तु रामस्य लक्ष्मणः पर वीर हा |अवदत् प्रश्रितम् वाक्यम् सुग्रीवम् गत चेतसम् || ४-२५-१२_END
BEGIN_
At the close of Rama's sentence Lakshmana, the eliminator of braving foes, spoke this courteous sentence 
to the disconcerted Sugreeva. [4-25-12]_END

B_4_C_18_57
BEGIN_
दण्ड्ये यः पातयेत् दण्डम् दण्ड्यो यः च अपि दण्ड्यते |कार्य कारण सिद्धार्थौ उभौ तौ न अवसीदतः || ४-१८-६१_END
BEGIN_
"He who administers punishment to the punishable, and he who is punishable and gets punished, both of 
them will achieve the results of cause and effect, where punishment is the effect from the cause of 
wrongdoing, and they both thereby will not be condemned. [4-18-61]_END

B_4_C_24_18
BEGIN_
महा बलानाम् हरि यूथपानाम् इदम् कुलम् राघव मन् निमित्तम् |अस्य अंगदस्य अपि च शोक तापात् अर्थ स्थित 
प्राणम् इतीव मन्ये || ४-२४-१९_END
BEGIN_
"I think this body of great-might monkey commanders is withstanding its lives in a halfway, oh, Raghava, 
just because of me and this Angada who is searing in anguish, for it is half-dead with the death of 
Vali. [4-24-19]_END

B_4_C_26_6
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तो हनुमता राघवः पर वीरहा || ४-२६-८प्रत्युवाच हनूमन्तम् बुद्धिमान् वाक्य कोविदः |_END
BEGIN_
When Hanuma said so, Rama the destroyer of valiant foes, an intellectual and an enunciator replied Hanuma in this 
way. [4-26-8b, 9a]_END

B_4_C_23_27
BEGIN_
या दत्ता देव राजेन तव तुष्टेन संयुगे |शात कौम्भीम् प्रियाम् मालाम् ताम् ते पश्यामि न इह किम् || 
३-२३-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Now where is that treasured golden pendant of yours which the king of gods gave to you when he is satisfied 
with your conduct in wars, I don't see it? [3-23-28]_END

B_4_C_25_12
BEGIN_
कुरु त्वम् अस्य सुग्रीव प्रेत कार्यम् अनंतरम् |तारा अंगदाभ्याम् सहितो वालिनो दहनम् प्रति || ४-२५-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Sugreeva, you attend to the funeral rites, to be performed subsequently along with those two, Tara 
and Angada, and arrange for the cremation of Vali. [4-25-13]_END

B_4_C_18_58
BEGIN_
तत् भवान् दण्ड सम्योगात् अस्मात् विगत कल्मषः |गतः स्वाम् प्रकृतिम् धर्म्याम् धर्म दिष्टेन वर्त्मना 
|| ४-१८-६२_END
BEGIN_
"Thereby, by virtue of the punishment you are completely divested of your blemish, and as contained 
in the scriptures on rightness you attained your true nature, that which is agreeable to rightness. 
[4-18-62]_END

B_4_C_24_19
BEGIN_
सुतः सुलभः सुजनः सुवश्यः कुतः तु पुत्रः सदृशः अंगदेन |न च अपि विद्येत स वीर देशो यस्मिन् भवेत् सोदर 
संनिकर्षः || ४-२४-२०_END
BEGIN_
"It is easy to get an easygoing and easy to deal with son, but where to get a son similar to Angada, 
oh, valiant Rama, also where to get even such a place wherein there will be an easy access to the nearness 
to one's own brother?_END

B_4_C_26_7
BEGIN_
चतुर्दश समाः सौम्य ग्रामम् वा यदि वा पुरम् || ४-२६-९न प्रवेक्ष्यामि हनुमन् पितुर् निर्देश पालकः |_END
BEGIN_
"As a conformist to the directives of my father, oh, gentle Hanuma, I am not supposed to enter either a village 
or a city. [4-26-9b, 10a]_END

B_4_C_23_28
BEGIN_
राज्यश्रीः न जहाति त्वाम् गत असुम् अपि मानद |सूर्यस्य आवर्तमानस्य शैल राजम् इव प्रभा || ३-२३-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Majesty is not deserting you even if your lives have departed, oh, accorder of dignity, as with the 
sunshine that departs the sun while he circumnavigates Mt. Meru, which mount is supposed to overshadow 
everything by its vastness. [3-23-29]_END

B_4_C_25_13
BEGIN_
समाज्ञापय काष्ठानि शुष्काणि च बहूनि च |चन्दनानि च दिव्यानि वालि संस्कार कारणात् || ४-२५-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Order at once for substantial dry firewood, likewise for finest sandalwood, for the purpose of the 
exequies of Vali. [4-25-14]_END

B_4_C_18_59
BEGIN_
त्यज शोकम् च मोहम् च भयम् च हृदये स्थितम् |त्वया विधानम् हर्यग्र्य न शक्यम् अतिवर्तितुम् || ४-१८-६३_END
BEGIN_
"Let distress, desire and even dread that abide in your heart be discarded, oh, monkey's supreme, you 
cannot possibly transcend destiny. [4-18-63]_END

B_4_C_24_20
BEGIN_
अद्य अंगदो वीर वरो न जीवेत् जीवेत माता परि पालनार्थम् |विना तु पुत्रम् परिताप दीना सा नैव जीवेत् 
इत् निश्चितम् मे || ४-२४-२१_END
BEGIN_
"This best of brave ones, Angada, will not live reft of his father, but his mother Tara has to live 
to foster her son Angada, but if Angada dies with his heartbroken for his farther, then without her 
son her misery will become miserable, and then she too may not live... this is my resolve. [4-24-21]_END

B_4_C_26_8
BEGIN_
सुसमृद्धाम् गुहाम् दिव्याम् सुग्रीवो वानरर्षभः || ४-२६-१०प्रविष्टो विधिवत् वीरः क्षिप्रम् राज्ये अभिषिच्यताम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"As and when the best one among Vanara-s valorous Sugreeva enters the highly flourishing and statuesquely Kishkindha, 
he shall be enthroned in the kingdom, immediately and procedurally. [4-26-10b, 11a]_END

B_4_C_23_29
BEGIN_
न मे वचः पथ्यम् इदम् त्वया कृतम्न च अस्मि शक्ता हि निवारणे तव |हता सपुत्रा अस्मि हतेन संयुगे
सह त्वया श्रीः विजहाति माम् अपि || ३-२३-३०_END
BEGIN_
"Neither you heeded my word of expediency, nor I was indeed capable to forestall you, and I am doomed 
along with my son when you are exterminated in fight, whereby the Grace that forsook you, is deserting 
me too, in its entirety. [3-23-30]_END

B_4_C_25_14
BEGIN_
समाश्वासय दीनम् त्वम् अंगदम् दीन चेतसम् |मा भूः बालिश बुद्धिः त्वम् त्वत् अधीनम् इदम् पुरम् || ४-२५-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Bolster up that miserable Angada who is heartbroken, you too should not become frivolous in thinking 
as this city Kishkindha is now dependant on you. [4-25-15]_END

B_4_C_18_60
BEGIN_
यथा त्वयि अंगदो नित्यम् वर्तते वानरेश्वरः |तथा वर्तते सुग्रीवो मयि च अपि न संशयः || ४-१८-६४_END
BEGIN_
"As Angada has always been conducting himself with you, thus he will conduct himself with Sugreeva and 
also even with me, without doubt." Thus Rama spoke to Vali. [4-18-64]_END

B_4_C_24_21
BEGIN_
सो अहम् प्रवेक्ष्यामि अति दीप्तम् अग्निम्भ्रत्रा च पुत्रेण च सख्यम् इच्छन् |इमे विचेष्यन्ति 
हरि प्रवीराःसीताम् निदेशे परिवर्तमानाः || ४-२४-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Such as I am, I wish to enter a highly blazing fire seeking amity with my departed brother and as well 
with son Angada, and these best valiant monkeys will search for Seetha duly conducting themselves under 
your control. [4-24-22]_END

B_4_C_26_9
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा हनूमन्तम् रामः सुग्रीवम् अब्रवीत् || ४-२६-११वृत्तज्ञो वृत्त संपन्नम् उदार बल विक्रमम् |_END
BEGIN_
Replying Hanuma thus, that knower of the etiquette Rama, also spoke to Sugreeva, who is rich in politesse and 
an imposing one by his might and valour. [4-26-11b, 12a]_END

B_4_C_25_15
BEGIN_
अंगदः तु आनयेत् माल्यम् वस्त्राणि विविधानि च |घृतम् तैलम् अथो गन्धान् यत् च अत्र समनंतरम् || ४-२५-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Let Angada bring wreaths, different cloths, ghee, oils, as well perfumes and other items that are consequently 
useful in funeral. [4-25-16]_END

B_4_C_18_61
BEGIN_
स तस्य वाक्यम् मधुरम् महात्मनःसमाहितम् धर्म पथानुवर्तिनः |निशम्य रामस्य रणावमर्दिनोवचः सुयुक्तम् 
निजगाद वानरः || ४-१८-६५_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the agreeable and assertive words of that great-souled Rama, who is the treader on the path 
of rightness and an absolute crusher of enemies in war, Vali, the vanara, spoke these well-disposed 
words to Rama. [4-18-65]_END

B_4_C_24_22
BEGIN_
कृत्स्नम् तु ते सेत्स्यति कार्यम् एतत् मयि अपि अतीते मनुजेन्द्र पुत्र |कुलस्य हन्तारम् अजीवन अर्हम् 
राम अनुजानीहि कृत अगसम् माम् || ४-२४-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, prince, even if I am dead your mission will be achieved in its entirety, and oh, Rama, having perpetrated 
infraction I have become an eliminator of the propriety of our race, hence I have become an unworthy 
one to live, and hence permit me to commit myself to fire..." Thus Sugreeva said to Rama. [4-24-23]_END

B_4_C_26_10
BEGIN_
इमम् अपि अंगदम् वीरम् यौवराज्ये अभिषेचय || ४-२६-१२ज्येष्ठस्य हि सुतो ज्येष्ठः सदृशो विक्रमेण च |अंगदो 
अयम् अदीनात्मा यौवराज्यस्य भाजनम् || ४-२६-१३_END
BEGIN_
"You may even crown this brave Angada as crown prince, he is the eldest son of your elder brother, his bravery 
is kindred to that of his father, and thus this enthusiastic Angada will be a well-chosen designee for the crown-princeship. 
[4-26-12b, 13]_END

B_4_C_25_16
BEGIN_
त्वम् तार शिबिकाम् शीघ्रम् आदाय आगच्छ संभ्रमात् |त्वरा गुणवती युक्ता हि अस्मिन् काले विशेषतः || 
४-२५-१७_END
BEGIN_
"And Lt. Tara, you go quickly and come readily fetching a palanquin of the dead, for despatch is a merit, 
which is truly worthwhile, especially at these times. [4-25-17]_END

B_4_C_24_23
BEGIN_
इति एवम् आर्तस्य रघु प्रवीरः श्रुत्वा वचो वालि जघन्य जस्य |संजात बाष्प पर वीर हन्ता रामो मुहूर्तम् 
विमना बभूव || ४-२४-२४_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the anguished words of the younger brother of Vali, namely Sugreeva, the eyes of Rama, the 
best valiant one from Raghu's dynasty and the eliminator of valiant enemies, are moistened and he became 
perturbed for a moment. [4-24-24]_END

B_4_C_18_62
BEGIN_
शराभितप्तेन विचेतसा मयाप्रदूषितः त्वम् यद् अजानता विभो |इदम् महेन्द्रोपम भीम विक्रमप्रसादितः 
त्वम् क्षम मे नरेश्वर || ४-१८-६६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, lord, oh, tremendously braving one, oh, Rama, the lord of people, I blamed you when your arrow 
sweltered and rendered me imbecile, thus I blamed you unthinkingly for which I may please be pardoned, 
I appease you for the same. [4-18-66]_END

B_4_C_26_11
BEGIN_
पूर्वो अयम् वार्षिको मासः श्रावणः सलिल आगमः |प्रवृत्ताः सौम्य चत्वारो मासा वार्षिक संज्ञिताः || ४-२६-१४_END
BEGIN_
"The four month period specified for rainy season has commenced, oh gentle Sugreeva, and this is shravaNa, the 
first month of rainy season that brings many showers. [4-26-14]_END

B_4_C_25_17
BEGIN_
सज्जी भवन्तु प्लवगाः शिबिक वाहन उचिताः |समर्था बलिनः चैव निर्हरिष्यन्ति वालिनम् || ४-२५-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Let suitable, proficient and sturdy Vaanara-s be at the ready as the bearers of the litter of the dead 
to carry away Vali." Thus said Lakshmana to Sugreeva. [4-25-18]_END

B_4_C_24_24
BEGIN_
तस्मिन् क्षणे अभीक्ष्णम् अवेक्षमाणः क्षिति क्षमावान् भुवनस्य गोप्ता |रामो रुदन्तीम् व्यसने निमग्नाम् 
समुत्सुकः सः अथ ददर्श ताराम् || ४-२४-२५_END
BEGIN_
At that moment, Rama whose perseverance is like that of the earth and who is the protector of earth 
has seen Tara, who is wailing and repeatedly looking around as she is deluged in desperation, and then 
with all his concernedness Rama paced towards her. [4-24-25]_END

B_4_C_26_12
BEGIN_
न अयम् उद्योग समयः प्रविश त्वम् पुरीम् शुभाम् |अस्मिन् वत्स्यामि अहम् सौम्य पर्वते सह लक्ष्मणः || ४-२६-१५_END
BEGIN_
"This is not a time for any striving, hence you enter the propitious city Kishkindha, oh, gentle Sugreeva, and 
I for my part will stay on this mountain along with Lakshmana. [4-26-15]_END

B_4_C_25_18
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा तु सुग्रीवम् सुमित्र आनन्द वर्धनः |तस्थौ भ्रातृ समीपस्थो लक्ष्मणः पर वीरहा || ४-२५-१९_END
BEGIN_
Speaking thus to Sugreeva that enhancer of his mother Sumitra's delight and the eliminator of braving 
foes, Lakshmana stepped off and stayed behind his brother Rama. [4-25-19]_END

B_4_C_24_25
BEGIN_
ताम् चारु नेत्राम् कपि सिंह नाथाम् पतिम् समाश्लिष्य तद शयानाम् |उत्थापयामासुः अदीन सत्त्वाम् मंत्रि 
प्रधानाः कपि राज पत्नीम् || ४-२४-२६_END
BEGIN_
The prominent monkey ministers then started to raise her up, whose eyes are pleasant and intellect unfailing, 
and who had the lion among monkeys as her husband, but now collapsed on ground hugging her departed 
husband. [4-24-26]_END

B_4_C_26_13
BEGIN_
इयम् गिरि गुहा रम्या विशाला युक्त मारुता |प्रभूत सलिला सौम्य प्रभूत कमल उत्पला || ४-२६-१६_END
BEGIN_
"This mountain cave is heart-pleasing by being spacious with worthwhile breeze, oh, gentle one, water is copious 
and red and blue lotuses are aplenty about this place. [4-26-16]_END

B_4_C_25_19
BEGIN_
लक्ष्मणस्य वचः श्रुत्वा तारः संभ्रान्त मानसः |प्रविवेश गुहाम् शीघ्रम् शिबिका आसक्त मानसः || ४-२५-२०_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of Lakshmana Lt. Tara's mood became hectic and he fleetly entered Kishkindha with 
his mood firmed up to get the litter of the dead. [4-25-20]_END

B_4_C_24_26
BEGIN_
सा विस्फुरंती परिरभ्यमाणा भर्तुः समीपात् अपनीयमाना |ददर्श रामम् शर चाप पाणिम् स्व तेजसा सूर्यम् 
इव ज्वलंतम् || ४-२४-२७_END
BEGIN_
She who is hugging her husband wriggled highly when she is disengaged from him, and at a particular 
stage she saw Rama with his bow and arrow in his hands and who is resplendent like sun, by his own resplendence. 
[4-24-27]_END

B_4_C_25_20
BEGIN_
आदाय शिबिकाम् तारः स तु पर्यापयत् पुनः |वानरैः उह्यमानाम् ताम् शूरैः उद्वहन उचितैः || ४-२५-२१_END
BEGIN_
Lt. Tara came back in a trice fetching that litter of the dead, getting it carried by gritty and suitable 
Vanara-s. [4-25-21]_END

B_4_C_26_14
BEGIN_
कार्तिके समनुप्राप्ते त्वम् रावण वधे यत |एष नः समयः सौम्य प्रविश त्वम् स्वम् आलयम् || ४-२६-१७अभिषिंचस्व 
राज्ये च सुहृदः संप्रहर्षय |_END
BEGIN_
"On the advent of kaartika month, October, say post-rainy season, you shall do your best in the cause of Ravana's 
elimination, and this is our covenant, and hence oh, gentle Sugreeva, for now enter your mansion, be enthroned 
in kingdom as well, and exhilarate your friends." [4-26-17, 18a]_END

B_4_C_24_27
BEGIN_
सु संवृत्तम् पार्थिव लक्षणैः च तम् चारु नेत्रम् मृगशाव नेत्रा |अदृष्ट पूर्वम् पुरुष प्रधानम् अयम् 
स काकुत्स्थ इति प्रजज्ञे || ४-२४-२८_END
BEGIN_
On seeing at him whose eyes are graceful, one endowed with all kingly attributes, who looked best among 
men, and who is unseen so far, that fawn-eyed Tara realized him alone as that Rama. [4-24-28]_END

B_4_C_26_15
BEGIN_
इति राम अभ्यनुज्ञातः सुग्रीवो वानरर्षभः || ४-२६-१८प्रविवेश पुरीम् रम्याम् किष्किंधाम् वालि पालिताम् |_END
BEGIN_
Thus when Rama countenanced that best vanara Sugreeva entered the charming city Kishkindha which is so far ruled 
by Vali. [4-26-18b, 19a]_END

B_4_C_25_21
BEGIN_
दिव्याम् भद्र आसन युताम् शिबिकाम् स्यंदन उपमम् |पक्षि कर्मभिः आचित्राम् द्रुम कर्म विभूषिताम् || 
४-२५-२२अचिताम् चित्र पत्तीभिः सुनिविष्टाम् समंततः |विमानम् इव सिद्धानाम् जाल वात आयान आयुताम् 
|| ४-२५-२३सुनियुक्तानाम् विशालाम् च सुकृताम् शिल्पिभिः कृतात् |दारु पर्वतकोपेताम् चारु कर्म 
परिष्कृताम् || ४-२५-२४वर आभरण हारैः च चित्र माल्य उपशोभिताम् |गुहागहन संच्छन्नाम् रक्त चन्दन 
भूषिताम् || ४-२५-२५पुष्प ओघैः समभिच्छन्नाम् पद्म मालाभिः एव च |तरुण आदित्य वर्णाभिः भ्राजमानभिः 
आवृताम् || ४-२५-२६_END
BEGIN_
That palanquin is having a majestic throne and in similarity it is like a divine chariot which is adorned 
and beautified with figurines of birds and trees in high relief. From all over it is well set in with 
strikingly carved figures of foot soldiers, and it is like an aircraft of the gifted souls, namely siddha-s, 
with grills and ventilators. Well seamed-in are its parts and also spacious it is, and well crafted 
by the crafty craftsmen it has wooden play-hills carved in its walls, and finishing touches with a fine 
artistry of polishing are given to that palanquin. It is elaborated with best ornaments and strings 
of pearls, gems, beads and the like, and even with amazing flowery-tassels. Its cabin's roof is covered 
with an ornamental woodcraft of red-sandalwood. It is well covered over with lots of flowers, and in 
its shade it is like a tender sun, while garlands of red-lotuses are further brightening it. And Lt. 
Tara brought such a litter of the dead. [4-25-22, 23, 24, 25, 26]_END

B_4_C_24_28
BEGIN_
तस्य इन्द्र कल्पस्य दुरासदस्य महानुभावस्य समीपम् आर्या |आर्त अति तूर्णम् व्यसनम् प्रपन्ना जगाम तारा 
परिविह्वलन्ती || ४-२४-२९_END
BEGIN_
She on whom misfortune has chanced and who is anguished, that noble lady Tara went very quickly with 
highly squirming movements to the near of the highly exalted soul Rama, who matches Indra in his valour 
and an unreachable one for his enemies. [4-24-29]_END

B_4_C_26_16
BEGIN_
तम् वानर सहस्राणि प्रविष्टम् वानर ईश्वरम् || ४-२६-१९अभिवार्य प्रहृष्टानि सर्वतः प्लवगेश्वरम् |_END
BEGIN_
When the sovereign of vanara-s Sugreeva has entered the city, very gladly thousands of vanara-s have also entered 
and fenced off that lord of fly-jumpers from all over. [4-26-19b, 20a]_END

B_4_C_25_22
BEGIN_
ईदृशी शिबिकाम् दृष्ट्वा रमो लक्ष्मणम् अब्रवीत् |क्षिप्रम् विनीयताम् वली प्रेत कार्यम् विधीयताम् 
|| ४-२५-२७_END
BEGIN_
On seeing such a sort of palanquin Rama said to Lakshmana, "Let Vali be taken away quickly and funeral 
ceremony be undertaken." [4-25-27]_END

B_4_C_24_29
BEGIN_
तम् सा समासाद्य विशुद्ध सत्त्वम् शोकेन संभ्रांत शरीर भावा |मनस्विनी वाक्यम् उवाच तारा रामम् रण उत्कर्षण 
लब्ध लक्ष्यम् || ४-२४-३०_END
BEGIN_
The body language of Tara which is so far disconcerted by the grief felt for Rama's perfect hitting, 
felling and achieving his object in war, namely Vali, is now disoriented to anger on seeing the very 
same Rama, as she is a self-respectful lady. But on arriving at the near of that very pure being Rama, 
that ireful body language of hers again reoriented itself to a sort of serenity, and then she spoke 
this to him. [4-24-30]_END

B_4_C_25_23
BEGIN_
ततो वालिनम् उद्यम्य सुग्रीवः शिबिकाम् तदा |आरोपयत विक्रोशन् अंगदेन सह एव तु || ४-२५-२८_END
BEGIN_
Thereafter Sugreeva along with Angada and others lifted up and then lodged Vali in the litter of the 
dead squalling woefully. [4-25-28]_END

B_4_C_26_17
BEGIN_
ततः प्रकृतयः सर्वा दृष्ट्वा हरि गण ईश्वरम् || ४-२६-२०प्रणम्य मूर्ध्ना पतिता वसुधायाम् समाहिताः |_END
BEGIN_
All the inmates and ministers in Kishkindha then revered the lord of monkey throngs Sugreeva with their head-bent, 
and they have also prostrated before him with an assiduously polite attitude. [4-26-20b, 21a]_END

B_4_C_24_30
BEGIN_
त्वम् अप्रमेयः च दुरासदः च जितेन्द्रियः च उत्तम धर्मकः च |अक्षीण कीर्तिः च विचक्षणः च क्षिति क्षमवान् 
क्षतजोपमा अक्षः || ४-२४-३१_END
BEGIN_
"You are an indeterminable one, an inaccessible one, one with his self conquered, the supreme among 
righteous souls, your glory is unmitigated, and you are the one with clear discrimination, and in endurance 
earth-like, and your eyes are blood streaked like those of an emperor. [4-24-31]_END

B_4_C_26_18
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवः प्रकृतीः सर्वाः संभाष्य उत्थाप्य वीर्यवान् || ४-२६-२१भ्रातुर् अंतः पुरम् सौम्यम् प्रविवेश महाबलः 
|_END
BEGIN_
Raising the rank-and-file members from their prostration, and on exchanging a word or two with them, that valiant 
and highly mighty Sugreeva entered the beautiful palace-chambers of his brother. [4-26-21b, 22a]_END

B_4_C_25_24
BEGIN_
आरोप्य शिबिकाम् चैव वालिनम् गत जीवितम् |अलंकारैः च विविधैः माल्यैः वस्त्रैः च भूषितम् || ४-२५-२९
आज्ञापयत् तदा राजा सुग्रीवः प्लवग ईश्वरः |और्ध्व देहिकम् आर्यस्य क्रियताम् अनुरूपतः || ४-२५-३०_END
BEGIN_
Thus setting that deceased Vali who is diversely decorated and adorned with garlands and cloths onto 
the palanquin, then Sugreeva, the king of best fly-jumpers, has ordered, "let the funeral ceremony of 
this noble brother of mine be undertaken, befitting to his magnificence... [4-25-29, 30]_END

B_4_C_24_31
BEGIN_
त्वम् आत्त बाणासन बाण पाणिः महाबलः संहनन उपपन्नः |मनुष्य देहाभुदयम् 
विहाय दिव्येन देहाभ्युदयेन युक्तः || ४-२४-३२_END
BEGIN_
"You with your proportionate physic are a mighty one handling 
bows and arrows, but your bodily magnificence is more than that of magnificent humanly body. [4-24-32
_END

B_4_C_26_19
BEGIN_
प्रविष्टम् भीम विक्रांतम् सुग्रीवम् वानरर्षभम् || ४-२६-२२अभ्यषिंचंत सुहृदः सहस्राक्षम् इव अमराः |_END
BEGIN_
When that prodigiously venturesome arch-vanara Sugreeva has entered the palace his cohorts anointed him as gods 
would anoint the Thousand-eyed Indra. [4-26-22b, 23a]_END

B_4_C_25_25
BEGIN_
विश्राणयन्तो रत्नानि विविधानि बहूनि च |अग्रतः प्लवगा यान्तु शिबिका तद् अनंतरम् || ४-२५-३१_END
BEGIN_
"Let the vanara-s proceed in van strewing various gems plentifully, and the palanquin afterward... [4-25-31]_END

B_4_C_24_32
BEGIN_
एन एव बाणेन हतः प्रियो मे तेन एव बाणेन हि माम् जहि हि |हता गमिष्यामि समीपम् अस्य न माम् विना वीर 
रमेत वाली || ४-२४-३३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, brave one, kill me too with the same arrow with which you have killed my dear husband, and on getting 
killed at your hand I wish to reach his near, as Vali takes no delight without me. [4-24-33]_END

B_4_C_26_20
BEGIN_
तस्य पाण्डुरम् आजह्रुः छत्रम् हेम परिष्कृतम् || ४-२६-२३शुक्ले च वाल व्यजने हेम दण्डे यशस्करे |तथा सर्वाणि 
रत्नानि सर्व बीज औषधानि च || ४-२६-२४स क्षीराणाम् च वृक्षाणाम् प्ररोहान् कुसुमानि च |शुक्लानि चैव वस्त्राणि 
श्वेतम् चैव अनुलेपनम् || ४-२६-२५सुगंधीनि च माल्यानि स्थलजानि अंबुजानि च |चन्दनानि च दिव्यानि गन्धाम् च 
विविधान् बहून् || ४-२६-२६अक्षतम् जात रूपम् च प्रियंगु मधु सर्पिषी |दधि चर्म च वैयाघ्रम् परार्ध्ये च अपि 
उपानहौ || ४-२६-२७समालंभनम् आदाय गोरोचनम् मनः शिलाम् |आजग्मुः तत्र मुदिता वराः कन्याः च षोडश || ४-२६-२८_END
BEGIN_
A white parasol highly ornate in gold, long-furred royal-fans with golden handles that are the enhancers of celebrity 
are brought for Sugreeva's anointment. Likewise, on taking all kinds of jewels, seeds, herbs, sprouts of trees 
that are still exuding milky latex, also flowers, and white royal-robes and white body-cream, lotuses bloomed 
on dry-land, best sandal paste, also various and numerous perfumes, Holy-yellow-rice, gold, seeds that are small 
and fragrant called priyangu, honey, ghee, curds, skin of tiger, tassels of fragrant flowers, and invaluable sandal 
shoes, unguents before oil bath, orpiment preparations one in yellow called gorochana, and the other in red called 
Manshila, there arrived sixteen best and cheerful damsels. [4-26-23b, 24, 25, 26, 27, 28]_END

B_4_C_25_26
BEGIN_
राज्ञाम् ऋद्धि विशेषा हि दृश्यन्ते भुवि यादृशाः |तादृशैः इह कुर्वन्तु वानरा भ्रतृउ सत् क्रियाम् 
|| ४-२५-३२_END
BEGIN_
"In which way the grandiose of monarchical opulence will be conspicuous on earth when kings decease, 
in a similar way the Vanara-s have to immortalise lord Vali now," Sugreeva ordered monkeys in that way. 
[4-25-32]_END

B_4_C_26_21
BEGIN_
ततः ते वानर श्रेष्ठम् अभिषेक्तुम् यथा विधि |रत्नैर् वस्त्रैः च भक्ष्यैः च तोषयित्वा द्विजर्षभान् || ४-२६-२९_END
BEGIN_
They the Vanara-s have then started to anoint that best Vanara Sugreeva according to the tradition, having appeased 
the eminent Brahmans with jewels, garments and delicacies. [4-26-29]_END

B_4_C_24_33
BEGIN_
स्वर्गे अपि पद्म अमल पत्र नेत्र समेत्य संप्रेक्ष्य च माम् अपश्यन् |न हि एष उच्चावच ताम्र चूडा विचित्र 
वेषाः अप्सरो अभजिष्यत् || ४-२४-३४_END
BEGIN_
"Though Vali with eyes like unblemished lotus petals reaches heaven he looks around for me, and not 
finding me there, he does not have a romance with celestial apsara-s though they will be in amazing 
costumes and wear red-coloured towering tiaras. [4-24-34]_END

B_4_C_25_27
BEGIN_
तादृशम् वालिनः क्षिप्रम् प्राकुर्वन् और्ध्वदैहिकम् |अंगदम् परिरभ्य आशु तार प्रभृतयः तथा || ४-२५-३३
क्रोशन्तः प्रययुः सर्वे वानरा हत बान्धवाः |_END
BEGIN_
On performing services to the dead in the same way as ordered by Sugreeva, then all of those vanara-s 
like Lt. Tara and others, have promptly started out hemming round Angada, keening over their dead relative 
Vali. [4-25-33, 34a]_END

B_4_C_26_22
BEGIN_
ततः कुश परिस्तीर्णम् समिद्धम् जात वेदसम् |मंत्र पूतेन हविषा हुत्वा मंत्रविदो जनाः || ४-२६-३०_END
BEGIN_
Authoritative scholars in Vedic-hymns then spreading the ritual grass around the Fire-altar which is with enkindled 
Ritual-fire oblated fire oblations into it duly sanctifying them with hymns. [4-26-30]_END

B_4_C_24_34
BEGIN_
स्वर्गे अपि शोकम् विवर्णताम् च मया विना प्राप्स्यति वीर वाली |रम्ये नगेन्द्रस्य तटा अवकाशे विदेह 
कन्या अरहितो यथा त्वम् || ४-२४-३५_END
BEGIN_
"Even though Vali is in heaven he will derive despair and despondency without me, like you, who are 
despondent and despaired on the pleasant stretches of mountainsides of that best mountain Rishyamuka, 
as you are without Seetha. [4-24-35]_END

B_4_C_25_28
BEGIN_
ततः प्रणिहिताः सर्वा वानर्यो अस्य वशानुगाः || ४-२५-३४चुक्रुशुः वीर वीर इति भूयः क्रोशन्ती ताः प्रियम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
Then all the female adherents of Vali came together and wept saying, 'oh, brave one, oh, brave one...' 
and they repeatedly wept thus for their departed dear. [4-25-34b, 35a]_END

B_4_C_26_23
BEGIN_
ततो हेम प्रतिष्ठाने वर आस्तरण संवृते |प्रासाद शिखरे रम्ये चित्र माल्य उपशोभिते || ४-२६-३१प्राङ्मुखम् विधिवत् 
मंत्रैः स्थापयित्वा वर आसने |नदी नदेभ्यः संहृत्य तीर्थेभ्यः च समंततः || ४-२६-३२आहृत्य च समुद्रेभ्यः सर्वेभ्यो 
वानरर्षभाः |अपः कनक कुंभेषु निधाय विमलम् जलम् || ४-२६-३३शुभैः वृषभ शृन्गैः च कलशैः च एव कांचनैः |शास्त्र 
दृष्टेन विधिना महर्षि विहितेन च || ४-२६-३४गजो गवाक्षो गवयः शरभो गंधमादनः |मैन्दः च द्विविदः चैव हनूमान् 
जांबवान् तथा || ४-२६-३५अभ्यषिंचंत सुग्रीवम् प्रसन्नेन सुगंधिना |सलिलेन सहस्राक्षम् वसवो वासवम् यथा || 
४-२६-३६_END
BEGIN_
On a splendid, choicest and finely upholstered throne with golden legs that is kept atop a rostrum that is shining 
forth with various flower tassels, Sugreeva is procedurally inducted to sit facing east to the chanting of Vedic 
hymns. Then, Vanara-s like Gaja, Gavaaksha, Gavaya, Sharabha, Gandhamaadana, Mainda, Dvividha, also thus Hanuma, 
Jambavanta have started pouring pure water on Sugreeva, which the best vanara-s have collected from the rivers 
flowing to east, as well as to west, from each of the sacred-declivity of rivers, from every ocean, and stored 
in golden flasks. Thus those have anointed Sugreeva with those pellucid and well-perfumed waters poured from golden 
vessels through the auspicious horns of bulls as revealed in scriptures and as great sages have defined, which 
anointment is like eight of Vasu-gods anointing the Thousand-eyed Indra. [4-26-31, 32, 33, 34, 35, 36]_END

B_4_C_24_35
BEGIN_
त्वम् वेत्थ तावत् वनिता विहीनःप्राप्नोति दुःखम् पुरुषः कुमारः |तत् त्वम् प्रजानन् जहि माम् न 
वालीदुःखम् मम अदर्शनजम् भजेत || ४-२४-३६_END
BEGIN_
"How a virile person derives discomfort without his woman, that much you know, isn't it! Because you 
are aware of it, you kill me; let not Vali get any discomfort when he does not find me. [4-24-36]_END

B_4_C_25_29
BEGIN_
तारा प्रभृतयः सर्वा वानर्यो हत बान्धव || ४-२५-३५अनुजग्मुः च भर्तारम् क्रोशंत्यः करुण स्वनाः |_END
BEGIN_
Lady Tara and all other female Vanara-s, whose husband is dead, followed the funeral procession wailing 
in a pathetic tone. [4-25-35b, 36a]_END

B_4_C_26_24
BEGIN_
अभिषिक्ते तु सुग्रीवे सर्वे वानर पुंगवाः |प्रचुक्रुशुर् महात्मानो हृष्टाः शत सहस्रशः || ४-२६-३७_END
BEGIN_
Hundreds and thousands of the great-souled and prominent vanara-s that are there, all of them have cheerily raised 
high hullabaloos while Sugreeva is anointed. [4-26-37]_END

B_4_C_24_36
BEGIN_
यत् च अपि मन्येत भवान् महात्मास्त्री घात दोषः तु भवेन् न मह्यम् |आत्मा इयम् अस्य इति हि माम् 
जहि त्वम्न स्त्री वधः स्यात् मनुजेन्द्र पुत्र || ४-२४-३७_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, prince, as a high souled one even if you think that, "sin of killing a female will not befall on 
me?" But deem me as his soul, as scriptures say that the wife is the soul of husband, and hence kill 
me, then there will not be any blemish of woman killing. [4-24-37]_END

B_4_C_25_30
BEGIN_
तासाम् रुदित शब्देन वानरीणाम् वन अंतरे || ४-२५-३६वनानि गिरयः चैव विक्रोशंति इव सर्वतः |_END
BEGIN_
With the din of wailing of those Vanara females in the interiors of the forest, that forest along with 
its hillocks appeared to be wailing noisily. [4-25-36b, 37a]_END

B_4_C_26_25
BEGIN_
रामस्य तु वचः कुर्वन् सुग्रीवो हरि पुंगवः |अंगदम् संपरिष्वज्य यौवराज्ये अभिषेचयत् || ४-२६-३८_END
BEGIN_
The best one among monkeys Sugreeva graciously embraced Angada and anointed his as crown prince in order to effectuate 
Rama's word. [4-26-38]_END

B_4_C_24_37
BEGIN_
शास्त्र प्रयोगात् विविधाः च वेदात् अनन्य रूपाः पुरुषस्य दाराः |दार प्रदानात् न हि दानम् अन्यत् प्रदृश्यते 
ज्ञानवताम् हि लोके || ४-२४-३८_END
BEGIN_
"In the course of implementing scriptural rituals, and even as contained in various Vedic sayings, wife 
is not a separate entity than her husband, and no better endowment than endowing a wife to an eligible 
bridegroom by bride's father is countenanced by the wise men in the world, isn't it. [4-24-38]_END

B_4_C_25_31
BEGIN_
पुलिने गिरि नद्याः तु विविक्ते जल संवृते || ४-२५-३७चिताम् चक्रुः सुबहवो वानरा वन चारिणः |_END
BEGIN_
Many Vanara-s have arranged a funeral pile on an unpopulated sandy isle, around which brooks from the 
cascades of hills are encircling. [4-25-37b, 38a]_END

B_4_C_26_26
BEGIN_
अंगदे च अभिषिक्ते तु सानुक्रोशाः प्लवंगमाः |साधु साधु इति सुग्रीवम् महात्मानो हि अपूजयन् || ४-२६-३९_END
BEGIN_
On the anointment of Angada those fly-jumpers that have sympathy for him have acclaimed Sugreeva saying, 'well 
done, well done.' [4-26-39]_END

B_4_C_24_38
BEGIN_
त्वम् च अपि माम् तस्य मम प्रियस्य प्रदास्यसे धर्मम् अवेक्ष्य वीर |अनेन दानेन न लप्स्यसे त्वम् अधर्म 
योगम् मम वीर घातात् || ४-२४-३९_END
BEGIN_
"Even you, oh, valiant one, on examining good and bad bestow me to my dear husband, and by that way, 
oh, brave one, by such an endowment of a wife to her husband, by way of killing and sending her to her 
husband, you too will not get any touch of sin. [4-24-39]_END

B_4_C_25_32
BEGIN_
अवरोप्य ततः स्कंधात् शिबिकाम् वानरोत्तमाः || ४-२५-३८तस्थुः एकांतम् आश्रित्य सर्वे शोक परायणाः |_END
BEGIN_
All of those best vanara-s then lifted down that palanquin from their shoulders and stood aside weltered 
in melancholy. [4-25-38b, 39a]_END

B_4_C_24_39
BEGIN_
आर्ताम् अनाथाम् अपनीयमानाम् एवम् गताम् न अर्हसि माम् अहन्तुम् |अहम् हि मातंग विलास गामिना प्लवंगमानाम् 
ऋषभेण धीमता |विना वरार्होत्तम हेम मालिना चिरम् न शक्ष्यामि नरेन्द्र जीवितुम् || ४-२४-४०_END
BEGIN_
"Anguished and unprotected, such as I am, oh, king, I am being distracted from my departed husband by 
these Vanara misters, and it is unapt of you to not to kill me, as I am incapable to live without him, 
whose sprightly gait is like that of an elephant, a best one among fly-jumping Vanara-s, a courageous 
one, and who wears a precious and exquisite golden pendant..." Thus Tara pleaded with Rama for a mercy-death. 
[4-24-40]_END

B_4_C_26_27
BEGIN_
रामम् च एव महात्मानम् लक्ष्मणम् च पुनः पुनः |प्रीताः च तुष्टुवुः सर्वे तादृशे तत्र वर्तिनि || ४-२६-४०_END
BEGIN_
While that kind of pompous anointment is taking place all are gladdened and that way they repeatedly extolled 
the great-souled Rama, and even Lakshmana too. [4-26-40]_END

B_4_C_25_33
BEGIN_
ततः तारा पतिम् दृष्ट्वा शिबिका तल शायिनम् || ४-२५-३९आरोप्य अंके शिरः तस्य विललाप सुदुःखिता |_END
BEGIN_
Lady Tara on seeing at her husband Vali recumbent on the bier of the litter of the dead, she then brought 
his head onto her lap, and wailed painfully. [4-25-39b, 40a]_END

B_4_C_26_28
BEGIN_
हृष्ट पुष्ट जन आकीर्णा पताका ध्वज शोभिता |बभूव नगरी रम्या क्षिकिंधा गिरि गह्वरे || ४-२६-४१_END
BEGIN_
That magnificent city Kishkindha situated in the cave of mountain which is already splendorous with flags of triumph 
and banners is further splendorous with blithe and burly monkeys overspreading it. [4-26-41]_END

B_4_C_24_40
BEGIN_
इति एवम् उक्तः तु विभुः महात्मा ताराम् समाश्वास्य हितम् बभाषे |मा वीर भार्ये विमतिम् कुरुष्व लोको 
हि सर्वो विहितो विधात्रा || ४-२४-४१_END
BEGIN_
Thus that way when Tara spoke to that lord and great-souled Rama, Rama consoling Tara well, spoke this 
word of expediency, "oh, wife of valiant one, let not your mind go raving, the Creator decreed all the 
world to be in this way, isn't so! [4-24-41]_END

B_4_C_25_34
BEGIN_
हा वानर महाराज हा नाथ माम् वत्सल || ४-२५-४०हा महार्हः महाबाहो हा मम प्रिय पश्य माम् |जनम् न 
पश्यसि इमम् त्वम् कस्मात् शोक अभिपीडितम् || ४-२५-४१_END
BEGIN_
"O, great king of monkeys... o, my consort... my dear... o, meritorious one, o, mighty one, o, my dear... 
see me... why do not you see this grief-stricken creature, that is me... [4-25-40b, 41]_END

B_4_C_24_41
BEGIN_
तम् चैव सर्वम् सुख दुःख योगम् लोको अब्रवीत् तेन कृतम् विधात्रा |त्रयो अपि लोका विहितम् विधानम् न 
अति क्रमन्ते वशगा हि तस्य || ४-२४-४२_END
BEGIN_
"And the same Creator has ordained mirth and misery , and even their association, so say sagely people. 
And even the triad of worlds is indeed under his control, and that triad too, cannot transgress the 
foreordained predestination. [4-24-42]_END

B_4_C_26_29
BEGIN_
निवेद्य रामाय तदा महात्मनेमहा अभिषेकम् कपि वाहनी पतिः |रुमाम् च भार्याम् उपलभ्य वीर्यवान्अवाप राज्यम् 
त्रिदश अधिपो यथा || ४-२६-४२_END
BEGIN_
The valiant Sugreeva who is by now the king of monkeys army, then apprised the great-souled Rama about his grand 
anointment, and thus he not only regained his wife Ruma but also secured the kingdom, like the chief of divinities 
Indra. [4-26-42]_END

B_4_C_25_35
BEGIN_
प्रहृष्टम् इह ते वक्त्रम् गत असोः अपि मानद |अस्त अर्क सम वर्णम् च दृश्यते जीवतो यथा || ४-२५-४२_END
BEGIN_
"Though your lives have gone your face is appearing to be highly enchanting as if it has a similar dazzle 
of the sun on dusking mountain, as it had when you were alive. [4-25-42]_END

B_4_C_27_0
BEGIN_
अभिषिक्ते तु सुग्रीवे प्रविष्टे वानरे गुहाम् |
आजगाम सह भ्रात्रा रामः प्रस्रवणम् गिरिम् || ४-२७-१_END
BEGIN_
Rama along with his brother Lakshmana reached Mt. Prasavana while the enthroned
Sugreeva entered the cave-city Kishkindha. [4-27-1]_END

B_4_C_24_42
BEGIN_
प्रीतिम् पराम् प्राप्स्यसि ताम् तथा एव पुत्रः च ते प्रप्स्यति यौव राज्यम् |धात्र विधानम् विहितम् 
तथा एव न शूर पत्न्यः परिदेवयन्ति || ४-२४-४३_END
BEGIN_
"You will get paramount appeasement as before, and your son will become the crown prince, God has ordained 
destiny only in that way. Wives of the valiant ones will not mourn emotionally." Thus Rama consoled 
Tara. [4-24-43]_END

B_4_C_25_36
BEGIN_
एष त्वाम् राम रूपेण कालः कर्षति वानर |येन स्म विधवाः सर्वाः कृता एक इषुणा रणे || ४-२५-४३_END
BEGIN_
"Time-god in the mien of this Rama is hauling you away, oh, vanara, on rendering all of us as widows 
by flinging a single arrow in the fight. [4-25-43]_END

B_4_C_27_1
BEGIN_
शार्दूल मृग संघुष्टम् सिंहैः भीम रवैः वृतम् |
नाना गुल्म लता गूढम् बहु पादप संकुलम् || ४-२७-२
ऋक्ष वानर गोपुच्छैः मार्जारैः च निषेवितम् |
मेघ राशि निभम् शैलम् नित्यम् शुचिकरम् शिवम् || ४-२७-३_END
BEGIN_
Mt. Prasavana is pervaded with noisily growling tigers and beasts, mightily roaring
lions, compacted with diverse shrubs and creeper-plants, overspread with many a kind of tree, thus
it is adored by bears, monkeys, baboons, and even by wildcats, and that mountain which is always
sanctifying and tranquil is like a heap of clouds in its shine. [4-27-2, 3]_END

B_4_C_24_43
BEGIN_
आश्वासिता तेन महत्मना तु प्रभाव युक्तेन परंतपेन |सा वीर पत्नी ध्वनता मुखेन सुवेष रूपा विरराम् तारा 
|| ४-२४-४४_END
BEGIN_
Thus consoled by that persuasive, noble-souled and enemy-burner Rama, that brave one's wife whose aspect 
is fair and whose attire is proper, she paused her plaint, but with a puling expression. [4-24-44]_END

B_4_C_25_37
BEGIN_
इमाः ताः तव राजेन्द्र वानर्यो अप्लवगाः तव|पादैः विकृष्टम् अध्वानम् आगताः किम् न बुध्यसे || ४-२५-४४
तव इष्टा ननु चैव इमा भार्याः चन्द्र निभ आननाः |_END
BEGIN_
"These are those female vanara-s of yours, oh, best king, unable to come by leaping and jumping as they 
are wont to, they have come treading a much lengthy way of yours, why do not you mind them? They with 
their faces like moonshine are your cherished wives, isn't it! [4-25-44]_END

B_4_C_27_2
BEGIN_
तस्य शैलस्य शिखरे महतीम् आयताम् गुहाम् |
प्रत्यगृह्णीत वासार्थम् रामः सौमित्रिणा सह || ४-२७-४_END
BEGIN_
Rama along with Lakshmana has taken up an ample spaced cave as residence on the
cliff of that mountain. [4-27-4]_END

B_4_C_25_38
BEGIN_
इदानीम् न ईक्षसे कस्मात् सुग्रीवम् प्लवग ईश्वरम् || ४-२५-४५एते हि सचिवा राजन् तार प्रभृतयः तव |
पुर वासि जनः च अयम् परिवार्य विषीदति || ४-२५-४६_END
BEGIN_
"What for you are not seeing the lord of fly-jumpers Sugreeva, and these Lt. Tara and others are all 
your ministers, oh, king, and even the people dwelling in Kishkindha city have gathered around you and 
sinking down, why do not you mind them? [4-25-45b, 46]_END

B_4_C_27_3
BEGIN_
कृत्वा च समयम् रामः सुग्रीवेण सह अनघ |
काल युक्तम् महद् वाक्यम् उवाच रघुनन्दन || ४-२७-५
विनीतम् भ्रातरम् भ्राता लक्ष्मणम् लक्ष्मि वर्धनम् |_END
BEGIN_
Rama, the faultless one and the elder brother of Lakshmana, who is the delight of
Raghu's dynasty, and who made an accord with Sugreeva regarding cessation of activity during rainy
season, spoke these significant and timely words to his humble brother Lakshmana who is the
enhancer of prosperity. [4-27-5, 6a]_END

B_4_C_25_39
BEGIN_
विसर्जय एनान् सचिवान् यथा उचितम् अरिन्दम |ततः क्रीडामहे सर्वा वनेषु मदनोत्कटाः || ४-२५-४७_END
BEGIN_
"Bid adieu to these ministers as usual, oh, enemy subjugator, then we all can sportfully wander in the 
woods in voluptuousness." Thus Tara mourned for Vali. [4-25-47]_END

B_4_C_27_4
BEGIN_
इयम् गिरि गुहा रम्या विशाला युक्त मारुता || ४-२७-६
अस्याम् वस्त्याम सौमित्रे वर्ष रात्रम् अरिंदम |_END
BEGIN_
"This delightful mountain cave is spacious and breezy, hence, oh, enemy destroyer
Soumitri, let us stay in this during rainy nights. [4-27-6]_END

B_4_C_25_40
BEGIN_
एवम् विलपतीम् ताराम् पति शोक परीवृताम् |उत्थापयन्ति स्म तदा वानर्यः शोक कर्शिताः || ४-२५-४८_END
BEGIN_
While Tara is enwrapped in the grief for her husband and wailing that way, then other female Vanara-s, 
who are equally haggard by grief have lifted her up and took her away from the body of Vali. [4-25-48]_END

B_4_C_27_5
BEGIN_
गिरि शृंगम् इदम् रम्यम् उत्तमम् पार्थिवात्मज || ४-२७-७
श्वेताभिः कृष्ण ताम्राभिः शिलाभिः उपशोभितम् |
नाना धातु समाकीर्णम् नदी दर्दुर संयुतम् || ४-२७-८
विविधैः वृक्ष षण्डैः च चारु चित्र लता युतम् |
नाना विहग संघुष्टम् मयूर वर नादितम् || ४-२७-९
मालती कुंद गुल्मैः च सिंदुवारैः शिरीषकैः |
कदंब अर्जुन सर्जैः च पुष्पितैः उपशोभितम् || ४-२७-१०_END
BEGIN_
"This admirable peak of mountain is embellished with white, black and coppery rock
faces, oh, prince, thus this is fully overspread with diverse ores. Bristling with rivers and
frogs, and brimmed with clumps of various trees along with beautiful and amazing creeper-plants it
is elaborated. It is highly reverberated with diverse birds and filled with the screeches of best
peacocks. And bloomed Maalati and Jasmine bushes, also trees like Sindhuvara, Shirrishika, further
the trees like Kadamba, Arjuna, and Sarja in bloom, are brightening it and it is delightful.
[4-27-7b, 8, 9, 10]_END

B_4_C_25_41
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवेण ततः सार्धम् अंगदः पितरम् रुदन् |चिताम् आरोपयामास शोकेन अभिप्लुत इन्द्रियः || ४-२५-४९_END
BEGIN_
Angada wailing along with Sugreeva, started to mount his father's body onto pyre in an involuntary way, 
as his senses are deluged under grief. [4-25-49]_END

B_4_C_27_6
BEGIN_
इयम् च नलिनि रम्या फुल्ल पंकज मण्डितैः |
न अति दूरे गुहाया नौ भविष्यति नृपात्मज || ४-२७-११_END
BEGIN_
"This pleasant lake of lotuses enwreathed with its blossomy lotuses, oh, prince, is
available not far away from our cave. [4-27-11]_END

B_4_C_25_42
BEGIN_
ततो अग्निम् विधिवत् दत्त्वा सो अपसव्यम् चकार ह |पितरम् दीर्घम् अध्वानम् प्रस्थितम् व्याकुल इन्द्रियः 
|| ४-२५-५०_END
BEGIN_
On giving fire to the pyre procedurally, then Angada with dismayed senses performed circumambulations 
in an anticlockwise direction to his father, who is voyaging on a remote avenue. [4-25-50]_END

B_4_C_27_7
BEGIN_
प्राग् उदक् प्रवणे देशे गुहा साधु भविष्यति |
पश्चात् च एव उन्नता सौम्य निवाते अयम् भविष्यति || ४-२७-१२_END
BEGIN_
"This cave with its north-easterly slope will be homely for us since the inrush of
rainwater will be less, oh, gentle one, also thus with its upraised westerly portion this cave will
be less of gusts that come from east. [4-27-12]_END

B_4_C_25_43
BEGIN_
संस्कृत्य वालिनम् तम् तु विधिवत् प्लवगर्षभाः |आजग्मुः उदकम् कर्तुम् नदीम् शुभ जलाम् शिवाम् || ४-२५-५१_END
BEGIN_
On cremating Vali procedurally those best fly-jumpers arrived at the propitious river with auspicious 
waters to offer water oblations to the departed soul. [4-25-51]_END

B_4_C_27_8
BEGIN_
गुहा द्वारे च सौमित्रे शिला सम तला शिवा |
कृष्णा च एव आयता चैव भिन्न अंजन चय उपममा || ४-२७-१३_END
BEGIN_
"The black stone available at the doorway of the cave that looks like a spattered
mound of mascara is broad, even-surfaced, and will be pleasant for a repose. [4-27-13]_END

B_4_C_25_44
BEGIN_
ततः ते सहिताः तत्र हि सः अंगदम् स्थाप्य च अग्रतः |सुग्रीव तारा सहिताः सिषिचुः वानरा जलम् || ४-२५-५२_END
BEGIN_
Those vanara-s on coming together along with Sugreeva and Lady Tara, and then locating Angada in their 
front, they have offered water oblations to the soul of Vali. [4-25-52]_END

B_4_C_28_0
BEGIN_
स तदा वालिनम् हत्वा सुग्रीवम् अभिषिच्य च |वसन् माल्यवतः पृष्टे रामो लक्ष्मणम् अब्रवीत् || ३-२८-१_END
BEGIN_
Rama spoke to Lakshmana while residing on the mountainside of Mt. Malayavata, also known as Mt. Prasavana, ensuing 
the elimination of Vali and enthronement of Sugreeva. [3-28-1]_END

B_4_C_27_9
BEGIN_
गिरि शृंगम् इदम् तात पश्य च उत्तरतः सुभम् |
भिन्न अंजन चय आकारम् अंभोधरम् इव उदितम् || ४-२७-१४_END
BEGIN_
"See this mountain peak that looks like a scattered mound of mascara, dear boy,
which rose up like a black-cloud on the sky, and it is an auspicious one for it is in northern
side. [4-27-14]_END

B_4_C_25_45
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवेण एव दीनेन दीनो भूत्वा महाबलः |समान शोकः काकुत्स्थः प्रेत कार्याणि अकारयत् || ४-२५-५३_END
BEGIN_
He whose sadness evened up with that of Sugreeva, and who became one with Sugreeva in haplessness, that 
great mighty Rama effectuated the funeral rites of Vali. [4-25-53]_END

B_4_C_28_1
BEGIN_
अयम् स कालः संप्राप्तः समयो अद्य जल आगमः |संपश्य त्वम् नभो मेघैः संवृतम् गिरि संनिभैः || ३-२८-२_END
BEGIN_
"This is that time of which we thought and it has come to pass. Now it is rainy season. You see the sky fully 
covered with mountainous clouds. [3-28-2]_END

B_4_C_27_10
BEGIN_
दक्षिणस्याम् अपि दिश स्थितम् श्वेतम् इव अंबरम् |
कैलास शिखर प्रख्यम् नाना धातु विराजितम् || ४-२७-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Even see this mountain available in the southerly direction as if a white cloth is
spread on sky, which is vying with Mt. Kailash and abounding with many an ore. [4-27-15]_END

B_4_C_25_46
BEGIN_
ततो अथ तम् वालिनम् अग्र्य पौरुषम्प्रकाशम् इक्ष्वाकु वर इषुणा हतम् |प्रदीप्य दीप्त अग्नि सम ओजसम् 
तदास लक्ष्मणम् रामम् उपेयवान् हरिः || ४-२५-५४_END
BEGIN_
On cremating Vali of lofty aplomb and manifest-renown and whom the arrow of that Rama, the best of Ikshvaku 
dynasty has eliminated, Sugreeva then approached that Rama, who is with Lakshmana at his side, and whose 
flair equals a flaming fire. [4-25-54]_END

B_4_C_28_2
BEGIN_
नव मास धृतम् गर्भम् भास्कारस्य गभस्तिभिः |पीत्वा रसम् समुद्राणाम् द्यौः प्रसूते रसायनम् || ३-२८-३_END
BEGIN_
"Sustaining a nine-month pregnancy, impregnated through the Sun with his sunrays guzzling the essence of oceans, 
the heaven is giving birth to the elixir of life. [3-28-3]_END

B_4_C_27_11
BEGIN_
प्राचीन वाहिनीम् चैव नदीम् भृशम् अकर्दमम् |
गुहायाः परतः पश्य त्रिकूटे जह्नवीम् इव || ४-२७-१६
चन्दनैः तिलकैः सालैः तमालैः अतिमुक्तकैः |
पद्मकैः सरलैः चैव अशोकैः चैव शोभितम् || ४-२७-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Also see this river unusually sludge-less, flowing from the wide of the cave and
streaming eastward, spruced up with trees like Sandalwood, Tilaka, Saala, Tamaala, Atimukta,
Padmaka, Sarala, and even with Ashoka trees, and it looks as if River Ganga is flowing in Trikuta.
[4-27-16, 17]_END

B_4_C_28_3
BEGIN_
शक्यम् अंबरम् आरुह्य मेघ सोपान पंक्तिभिः |कुटज अर्जुन मालाभिः अलंकर्तुम् दिवाकरम् || ३-२८-४_END
BEGIN_
"It is very likely to climb up the flight of stairs of clouds to bedeck the sun with the garlands of white wild-jasmines, 
and red Arjuna flowers, in these days. [3-28-4]_END

B_4_C_27_12
BEGIN_
वानीरैः तिमिदैः चैव वकुलैः केतकैः अपि |
हिन्तालैः तिनिशैः नीपैः वेतसैः कृतमालकैः || ४-२७-१८
तीरजैः शोभिता भाति नाना रूपैः ततः ततः |
वसन आभरण उपेत प्रमद एव अभ्यलंकृता || ४-२७-१९_END
BEGIN_
"With the trees born on the riverbank and available here and there in various
shapes, like Vaaniira, Timida, Vakula, Ketaka, and with Hintaala, Tinisha, Niipa, Vetasa,
Kritamaala trees, that river is brightened up, and thus that river appears as a dame finely
bedecked with raiment and ornaments. [4-27-18, 19]_END

B_4_C_28_4
BEGIN_
संध्या राग उत्थितैः ताम्रैः अंतेषु अधिक पाण्डुरैः |स्निग्धैः अभ्र पट च्छेदैः बद्ध व्रणम् इव अंबरम् || ३-२८-५_END
BEGIN_
"Those clouds with pure white edges, and with reddish hue of sunset extending on them, look like soft pieces of 
cloth bandaged on the gashes of sky. [3-28-5]_END

B_4_C_27_13
BEGIN_
शतशः पक्षि सन्घैः च नाना नाद विनादिता |
एकैकम् अनुरक्तैः च चक्रवाकैः अलंकृता || ४-२७-२०
पुलिनैः अति रम्यैः च हंस सारस सेविता |
प्रहसंती इव भाति एषा नारी रत्न विभूषिता || ४-२७-२१_END
BEGIN_
"This river is fairly resonated with the calls of diverse birds in hundreds of
flights, beautified with ruddy gees that are doting one upon the other, and admired by the swans
and cranes upon her highly appealing sand-isles, thus she appears to be a damsel decorated with
jewels with a toothy grin. [4-27-20, 21]_END

B_4_C_28_5
BEGIN_
मन्द मारुत निःश्वासम् संध्या चंदन रंजितम् |आपाण्डु जलदम् भाति काम आतुरम् इव अंबरम् || ३-२८-६_END
BEGIN_
"Slothful breezes as her sighs, sunset tingeing her as sandal paste, the sky with blanched clouds on her face 
appears like the one sighing for love. [3-28-6]_END

B_4_C_27_14
BEGIN_
क्वचित् नीलोत्पलैः च्छन्न भाति रक्तोत्पलैः क्वचित् |
क्वचित् भाति शुक्लैः च दिव्यैः कुमुद कुड्मलैः || ४-२७-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Somewhere overspread with blue water-lilies, elsewhere with red water-lilies she is
shining forth, and she is also shimmering with the beautiful buds of white water-lilies, somewhere
else. [4-27-22]_END

B_4_C_28_6
BEGIN_
एषा घर्म परिक्लिष्टा नव वारि परिप्लुता |सीता इव शोक संतप्ता मही बाष्पम् विमुंचति || ३-२८-७_END
BEGIN_
"Overly agonised with the searing-summer, but thoroughly wetted with new waters, this earth looks like Seetha, 
both implacably outpouring tears. [3-28-7]_END

B_4_C_27_15
BEGIN_
पारिप्लव शतैः जुष्टा बर्हि क्रौन्च विनादिता |
रमणिया नदी सौम्य मुनि संघ निषेविता || ४-२७-२३_END
BEGIN_
"With hundreds of waterfowls cherishing it, screeches of peacocks and cackles of
curlews reverberating around, assemblages of sages bustling about, this gracious river is
heart-pleasing. [4-27-23]_END

B_4_C_28_7
BEGIN_
मेघ उदर विनिर्मुक्ताः कर्पूर दल शीतलाः |शक्यम् अंजलिभिः पातुम् वाताः केतकि गन्धिनः || ३-२८-८_END
BEGIN_
"Freed from the wombs of clouds, cool as the leaves of minty-camphor, perfumed with the fragrance of Mogra plants, 
such as these breezes are it is possible to have a draught of them with the bowl of palms. [3-28-8]_END

B_4_C_27_16
BEGIN_
पश्य चंदन वृक्षाणाम् पंक्ती सुरुचिरा इव |
ककुभानम् च दृश्यन्ते मनसा इव उदिताः समम् || ४-२७-२४_END
BEGIN_
"As if seeded by the wish of some divine creativity the rows of sandalwood trees
that are virtually captivating have sprang forth uniformly, so also, the rows of Arjuna trees too
appear in a similar pattern. [4-27-24]_END

B_4_C_28_8
BEGIN_
एष फुल्ल अर्जुनः शैलः केतकैः अधिवासितः |सुग्रीव इव शान्त अरिः धाराभिः अभिषिच्यते || ३-२८-९_END
BEGIN_
"This mountain with fully bloomed Arjuna flowers, further fragranced by Ketaka flowers is being anointed with 
downpours on a par with Sugreeva, who is anointed when his enemy is silenced. [3-28-9]_END

B_4_C_27_17
BEGIN_
अहो सुरमणीयो अयम् देशः शत्रु निषूदन |
दृढम् रंस्याव सौमित्रे साधु अत्र निवसावहे || ४-२७-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Aha! Soumitri, very exhilarating is this locale and we can happily reside here, oh,
enemy-eliminator, we can certainly take delight in this environ. [4-27-25]_END

B_4_C_28_9
BEGIN_
मेघ कृष्ण अजिन धरा धारा यज्ञ उपवीतिनः |मारुत आपूरित गुहाः प्राधीता इव पर्वताः || ३-२८-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Donning clouds as black deer skins, torrents as sacred-threads, and caves replete with breezes as vocals, the 
mountains look like young-scholars reciting Veda-s. [3-28-10]_END

B_4_C_27_18
BEGIN_
इतः च न अति दूरे सा किष्किंधा चित्र कानना |
सुग्रीवस्य पुरी रम्या भविष्यति नृपात्मज || ४-२७-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Further, oh, prince, hedged in charming groves that exquisite Kishkindha, the city
of Sugreeva, will not be very far off from here. [4-27-26]_END

B_4_C_28_10
BEGIN_
कशाभिः इव हैमीभिः विद्युद्भिः इव ताडितम् |अन्तः स्तनित निर्घोषम् सवेदनम् इव अंबरम् || ३-२८-११_END
BEGIN_
"While the flashes of lightning are whipping the sky as if they are the golden whips, it is letting out rattle 
of thunders holding out against its inly throes. [3-28-11]_END

B_4_C_27_19
BEGIN_
गीत वादित्र निर्घोषः श्रूयते जयताम् वर |
नदताम् वानराणाम् च मृदंग आडंबरैः सह || ४-२७-२७_END
BEGIN_
"The melodies of singing and the tunes of musical instruments played and sung in
Kishkindha are heard from here, oh, the best-triumphant Lakshmana, and even the blares of vanara-s
together with their snobbish drumming is heard, hence it is not far away. [4-27-27]_END

B_4_C_28_11
BEGIN_
नील मेघ आश्रिता विद्युत् स्फुरंती प्रतिभाति मे |स्फुरंती रावणस्य अंके वैदेही इव तपस्विनी || ३-२८-१२_END
BEGIN_
"That lightning hingeing on the blue cloud is squirmy, to me it appears like woeful Vaidehi squirming in the grasp 
of Ravana. [3-28-12]_END

B_4_C_27_20
BEGIN_
लब्ध्वा भार्याम् कपिवरः प्राप्य राज्यम् सुहृत् वृतः |
ध्रुवम् नंदति सुग्रीवः संप्राप्य महतीम् श्रियम् || ४-२७-२८_END
BEGIN_
"It is definite that the best monkey Sugreeva must be surrounded by his friends,
thus he must be exuberant, as he won an utmost prosperity in winning back his wife and winning the
kingdom." Rama thus spoke to Lakshmana. [4-27-28]_END

B_4_C_28_12
BEGIN_
इमाः ता मन्मथवताम् हिताः प्रतिहता दिशः |अनुलिप्ता इव घनैः नष्ट ग्रह निशा कराः || ३-२८-१३_END
BEGIN_
"For those who are with their beloveds these precincts are advantageous, as their directions, as to which east 
and which is west, are unclear; and to loverless ones like me they are disadvantageous, because the same precincts 
have their planets and even their moon lost, and they look as though begrimed with dark-clouds. [3-28-13]_END

B_4_C_27_21
BEGIN_
इति उक्त्वा न्यवसत् तत्र राघवः सह लक्ष्मणः |
बहु दृश्य दरी कुंजे तस्मिन् प्रस्रवणे गिरौ || ४-२७-२९_END
BEGIN_
Raghava having said thus resided on that Mt. Prasavana along with Lakshmana, whereat
many sightly caves and arbours are there. [4-27-29]_END

B_4_C_28_13
BEGIN_
क्वचित् बाष्प अभिसंरुद्धान् वर्ष आगम समुत्सुकान् |कुटजान् पश्य सौमित्रे पुष्टितान् गिरि सानुषु |मम शोक 
अभिभूतस्य काम संदीपनान् स्थितान् || ३-२८-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Feeling happy with the arrival of rain wild jasmine plants standing somewhere on the terraces of mountain are 
flowered, and they are thickly covered with droplets of vapour, as if they are the tears of happiness hovering 
round the flower like faces of ladyloves at the arrival of their lovers, and such plants are becoming inciters
