of passion in me, who am let down by my sorrow for my ladylove. [3-28-14]_END

B_4_C_27_22
BEGIN_
सुसुखे हि बहु द्रव्ये तस्मिन् हि धरणी धरे |
वसतः तस्य रामस्य रतिः अल्पा अपि न अभवत् || ४-२७-३०_END
BEGIN_
Though that mountain is indeed very comfortable, though it possess many objects of
nature like flowers, fruits and waters, indeed, there is no slightest bliss to Rama while he
resided there. [4-27-30]_END

B_4_C_28_14
BEGIN_
रजः प्रशांतम् स हिमो अद्य वायुःनिदाघ दोष प्रसराः प्रशांताः |स्थिता हि यात्रा वसुधा अधिपानाम्प्रवासिनो 
यांति नराः स्व देशान् || ३-२८-१५_END
BEGIN_
"In these days the dust is quietened, breeze is chilly, vile pervasions of summer are also quietened, conquests 
of kings indeed came to a halt, and the people in outstation are returning to their own countries. [3-28-15]_END

B_4_C_27_23
BEGIN_
हृताम् हि भार्याम् स्मरतः प्राणेभ्यो अपि गरीयसीम् |
उदय अभ्युदितम् दृष्ट्वा शशांकम् च विशेषतः || ४-२७-३१_END
BEGIN_
He felt despondent in reminiscing about his wife who is loftier that his lives, but
who is kidnapped, especially on seeing the moon just risen on the eastern mountain. [4-27-31]_END

B_4_C_28_15
BEGIN_
संप्रस्थिता मानस वास लुब्धाःप्रिय अन्विताः संप्रति चक्रवाकः |अभीक्ष्ण वर्ष उदक विक्षतेषुयानानि मार्गेषु 
न संपतन्ति || ३-२८-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Presently swans have started journey to Lake Manasa eager to live there, but the Cakravaka birds, ruddy gees, 
that are together with their beloveds are not departing, and vehicles are not taking to road as the rainwater 
has battered the roadways oftentimes. [3-28-16]_END

B_4_C_27_24
BEGIN_
आविवेश न तम् निद्रा निशासु शयनम् गतम् |
तत् समुत्थेन शोकेन बाष्प उपहत चेतसम् || ४-२७-३२_END
BEGIN_
That anguish which is surging high in him has rendered him with a bosom marred with
tears, thereby sleep has no effect on him even if he has gone to bed in nights. [4-27-32]_END

B_4_C_27_25
BEGIN_
तम् शोचमानम् काकुत्स्थम् नित्यम् शोक परायणम् |
तुल्य दुःखो अब्रवीद् भ्राता लक्ष्मणो अनुनयम् वचः || ४-२७-३३_END
BEGIN_
While pacifying Rama who is pensive and who is always subjected to grief, his
brother Lakshmana who is similarly sad for his brother's sadness spoke these words. [4-27-33]_END

B_4_C_28_16
BEGIN_
क्वचित् प्रकाशम् क्वचिद् अप्रकाशम्नभः प्रकीर्णा अंबु धरम् विभाति |क्वचित् क्वचित् पर्वत संनिरुद्धम्
रूपम् यथा शान्त महार्णवस्य || ३-२८-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Widely bestrewn with clouds the sky is bright somewhere, and not so bright somewhere else, thus it is gleaming 
well with an aspect of vast but tideless ocean that is by far dammed up with cloudlike mountains. [3-28-17]_END

B_4_C_27_26
BEGIN_
अलम् वीर व्यथाम् गत्वा न त्वम् शोचितुम् अर्हसि |
शोचतो हि अवसीदन्ति सर्व अर्था विदितम् हि ते || ४-२७-३४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, brave one, enough is this anguishing of yours, and it will be inapt of you to
dishearten. All objectives will backslide for them who will be ceaselessly anguishing. That you
know clearly. [4-27-34]_END

B_4_C_28_17
BEGIN_
व्यामिश्रितम् सर्ज कदंब पुष्पैःनवम् जलम् पर्वत धातु ताम्रम् |मयूर केकाभिः अनुप्रयातम्शैल अपगाः शीघ्रतरम् 
वहन्ति || ३-२८-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Coalesced with Sarja and Wild-jasmine flowers, and also with the coppery ores of the mountain, the new waters 
are swiftly transiting towards ocean, while screams of peacocks haunting them. [3-28-18]_END

B_4_C_27_27
BEGIN_
भवान् क्रिया परो लोके भवान् देव परायणः |
आस्तिको धर्म शीलः च व्यवसायी च राघव || ४-२७-३५_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Raghava, in the world you are a result-oriented person, and a devotee of gods
for achieving those desired results, you are the theist, moralist, and also the mobilizer._END

B_4_C_28_18
BEGIN_
रस आकुलम् षट्पद संनिकाशम्प्रभुज्यते जंबु फलम् प्रकामम् |अनेक वर्णम् पवन अवधूतम्भूमौ पतति आम्र फलम् 
विपक्वम् || ३-२८-१९_END
BEGIN_
"The fruits of rose-apple that resemble honeybees are delightedly devoured as they are highly luscious, but the 
mango fruits that are discoloured and putrefied are falling to ground heaved down by wind. [3-28-19]_END

B_4_C_27_28
BEGIN_
न हि अव्यवसितः शत्रुम् राक्षसम् तम् विशेषतः |
समर्थः त्वम् रणे हन्तुम् विक्रमैः जिह्म कारिणम् || ४-२७-३६_END
BEGIN_
"If you are much too lackadaisical, indeed, you will not be capable to eliminate the
enemy in war, specially a demon, especially a trickster, let alone all of your daring enterprises.
[4-27-36]_END

B_4_C_28_19
BEGIN_
विद्युत् पताकाः स बलाक मालाःशैलेन्द्र कूट आकृति संनिकाशाः |गर्जन्ति मेघाः समुदीर्ण नादामत्त गजेन्द्रा 
इव संयुगस्थाः || ३-२८-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Electric-charges as their fluttering flags of war, flights of cranes as their garlands of gallantry, those clouds 
very similar in their build to the pinnacles of lordly mountains are thundering with very high pitched voices 
like invigorated lordly elephants standing up to a fight. [3-28-20]_END

B_4_C_27_29
BEGIN_
समुन्मूलय शोकम् त्वम् व्यवसायम् स्थिरी कुरु |
ततः सपरिवारम् तम् राक्षसम् हन्तुम् अर्हसि || ४-२७-३७_END
BEGIN_
"On completely rooting out that agony then you stabilise your endeavour, and then
you will be able to eliminate that demon Ravana along with his followers. [4-27-37]_END

B_4_C_28_20
BEGIN_
वर्ष उदक आअप्यायित शाद्वलानिप्रवृत्त नृत्त उत्सव बर्हिणानि |वनानि निर्वृष्ट बलाहकानिपश्य अपराह्णेषु 
अधिकम् विभान्ति || ३-२८-२१_END
BEGIN_
"When clouds have completely rained on the greenery pasturelands are satiated with rainwater and peacocks are 
stimulated to dancing carnivals, thus it is extremely splendorous in afternoons, behold it. [3-28-21]_END

B_4_C_27_30
BEGIN_
पृथिवीम् अपि काकुत्स्थ ससागर वन अचलाम् |
परिवर्तयितुम् शक्तः किम् पुनः तम् हि रावणम् || ४-२७-३८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Kakutstha, you are capable to inverse the order of earth along with all of its
oceans, forests, and mountains, then what to speak of that Ravana, all the more. [4-27-38]_END

B_4_C_28_21
BEGIN_
सम् उद् वहन्तः सलिल अति भारम्बलाकिनो वारि धरा नदन्तः |महत्सु शृंगेषु मही धराणाम्विश्रम्य विश्रम्य 
पुनः प्रयान्ति || ३-२८-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Clouds adorned with cranes around them are rumbling to transport them, and the weighty water contained inside 
their wombs, and reposing on the loftiest mountain peaks they are moving, moving and again reposing, like pregnant 
women. [3-28-22]_END

B_4_C_27_31
BEGIN_
शरत् कालम् प्रतीक्षस्व प्रावृट् कालो अयम् आगतः |
ततः स राष्ट्रम् स गणाम् रावणम् तम् वधिष्यसि || ४-२७-३९_END
BEGIN_
"Look forward to the autumnal season, as this season that has come is of heavy
rains, and thereafter, you will eradicate that Ravana along with his city-state and his followers.
[4-27-39]_END

B_4_C_28_22
BEGIN_
मेघ अभिकामा परिसंपतन्तीसम्मोदिता भाति बलाक पंक्तिः |वात अवधूता वर पौण्डरीकीलंब इव माला रुचिर अंबरस्य 
|| ३-२८-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Highly delighted cranes are flying all over in rows highly desirous of the clouds, and they are shining forth 
like the best and lovely festoons of white lotus flowers as if wind has upheaved and dangled them on the sky. 
[3-28-23]_END

B_4_C_28_23
BEGIN_
बाल इन्द्रगोप्ता अंतर चित्रितेनविभाति भूमिः नव शाद्वलेन |गात्र अनुपृक्तेन शुक प्रभेणनारी इव लाक्ष 
उक्षित कंबलेन || ३-२८-२४_END
BEGIN_
"The meadowland is with its new meadows which are medially dappled with young and small red-beetles, and it is 
shining forth as if she is a woman wearing a parrot-green wraparound on which lac-red spots are embroidered. [3-28-24]_END

B_4_C_27_32
BEGIN_
अहम् तु खलु ते वीर्यम् प्रसुप्तम् प्रतिबोधये |
दीप्तैः आहुतिभिः काले भस्म चन्नम् इव अनलम् || ४-२७-४०_END
BEGIN_
"I am just awakening the fast sleeping vitality of yours, no more than rekindling
fire concealed under embers with the timely offerings of flammable fire-oblations." Thus said
Lakshmana to Rama. [4-27-40]_END

B_4_C_28_24
BEGIN_
निद्रा शनैः केशवम् अभ्युपैतिद्रुतम् नदी सागरम् अभ्युपैति |हृष्टा बलाका घनम् अभ्युपैतिकान्ता स कामा 
प्रियम् अभ्युपैति || ३-२८-२५_END
BEGIN_
"These days sleep is slowly getting closer to Vishnu, rivers are rapidly getting closer to oceans, cranes are 
gleefully getting closer to clouds, and women are passionately getting closer to their beloveds. [3-28-25]_END

B_4_C_27_33
BEGIN_
लक्ष्मणस्य हि तद् वाक्यम् प्रतिपूज्य हितम् शुभम् |
राघवः सुहृदम् स्निग्धम् इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् || ४-२७-४१_END
BEGIN_
Honouring that expedient and propitious advise of Lakshmana, Raghava spoke this
sentence to that good-hearted and good-natured Lakshmana. [4-27-41]_END

B_4_C_28_25
BEGIN_
जाता वनान्ताः शिखि सुप्रनृत्ताजाताः कदंबाः स कदंब शाखाः |जाता वृषा गोषु समान कामाजाता मही सस्य वन 
अभिरामा || ३-२८-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Interiors of forests have become adaptive for the peacocks to dance very well, Kadamba trees have become adaptive 
to their branches and bouquets, bulls with matching sensualities became adaptive to cows, and adaptive is this 
earth with its enrapturing crops and orchards, and all are adaptive to the season's gaiety. [3-28-26]_END

B_4_C_27_34
BEGIN_
वाच्यम् यद् अनुरक्तेन स्निग्धेन च हितेन च |
सत्य विक्रम युक्तेन तद् उक्तम् लक्ष्मण त्वया || ४-२७-४२_END
BEGIN_
"What is to be said by an affectionate, amiable and cordial person, also whose
courage is truth itself, that you have said it, Lakshmana. [4-27-42]_END

B_4_C_27_35
BEGIN_
एष शोकः परित्यक्तः सर्व कार्य अवसादकः |
विक्रमेषु अप्रतिहतम् तेजः प्रोत्साहयामि अहम् || ४-२७-४३_END
BEGIN_
"Yes! Distress is retrogressive to all the functions. I am casting-off this distress
completely. As an undefeatable one in my triumphs I am invigorating my ebullience. [4-27-43]_END

B_4_C_28_26
BEGIN_
वहन्ति वर्षन्ति नदन्ति भान्तिध्यायन्ति नृत्यन्ति समाश्वसन्ति |नद्यो घना मत्त गजा वन अन्ताःप्रिया विहीनाः 
शिखिनः प्लवंगाः || ३-२८-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Rivers are surging, clouds are showering, rutty elephants are shrilling, forest interiors are shining, loverless 
are speculating, and peacocks are rocking, monkeys are resolving to stay at one place, for this is the rainy season. 
[3-28-27]_END

B_4_C_27_36
BEGIN_
शरत् कालम् प्रतीक्षिष्ये स्थितो अस्मि वचने तव |
सुग्रीवस्य नदीनाम् च प्रसादम् अनुपालयन् || ४-२७-४४_END
BEGIN_
"Awaiting for the kind-heartedness of Sugreeva, and for the kindness of the rivers
in their abatement, I look forward for the autumn remaining true to your words. [4-27-44]_END

B_4_C_28_27
BEGIN_
प्रहर्षिताः केतक पुष्प गन्धम्आघ्राय मत्ता वन निर्झरेषु |प्रपात शब्द आकुलिता गजेन्द्राःसार्धम् मयूरैः 
स मदा नदन्ति || ३-२८-२८_END
BEGIN_
"On whiffing the fragrance of new Ketaka flowers the lordly elephants are highly joyous and became excited, but 
they are baffled at the sounds made by the fall of water in the streamlets of forest, and those best ruttish elephants 
are blaring along with screaming peacocks. [3-28-28]_END

B_4_C_27_37
BEGIN_
उपकारेण विरः तु प्रतिकारेण युज्यते |
अकृतज्ञो अप्रतिकृतो हन्ति सत्ववताम् मनः || ४-२७-४५_END
BEGIN_
"A valiant one who is succoured will be indebted with some requital on his part, but
besides being unfaithful, if one who does not make requital for all the favours done in his
interest, he will be wounding the hearts of soft-hearted people." Rama said so to Lakshmana,
keeping Sugreeva in view. [4-27-45]_END

B_4_C_28_28
BEGIN_
धारा निपातैः अभिहन्यमानाःकदंब शाखासु विलंबमानाः |क्षण अर्जितम् पुष्प रस अवगाढम्शनैर् मदम् षट् चरणाः 
त्यजन्ति || ३-२८-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Honeybees languishing on the branches of Kadamba trees are knocked down by the downpour of rain, thereby they 
are slowly forfeiting the intemperance which they acquired in a trice by plunging themselves into the nectar of 
flowers. [3-28-29]_END

B_4_C_27_38
BEGIN_
तत् एव युक्तम् प्रणिधाय लक्ष्मणः
कृत अंजलि तत् प्रतिपूजय भाषितम् |
उवाच रामम् स्वभिराम दर्शनम्
प्रदर्शयन् दर्शनम् आत्मनः शुभम् || ४-२७-४६_END
BEGIN_
Visualising what Rama said about their waiting for pre-winter season to be candid,
and praisefully making palm-fold at that determination of Rama, and even to clarify his own
opportune viewpoint, Lakshmana spoke to Rama who by his own aspect is a delightful one for a ken.
[4-27-46]_END

B_4_C_28_29
BEGIN_
अंगार चूर्ण उत्कर संनिकाशैःफलैः सुपर्याप्त रसैः समृद्धैः |जंबू द्रुमाणाम् प्रविभान्ति शाखानिपीयमाना 
इव षट्पद ओघैः || ३-२८-३०_END
BEGIN_
"Rose-apple trees contain abundant fruits with profuse juice which look like the globated coal powder, with them 
the branches of those trees shine forth as though swilled by hives of honeybees. [3-28-30]_END

B_4_C_27_39
BEGIN_
यथोक्तम् एतत् तव सर्वम् ईप्सितम्
नरेन्द्र कर्ता न चिरात् तु वानर |
शरत् प्रतीक्षः क्षमताम् इमम् भवान्
जल प्रपातम् रिपु निग्रहे धृतः || ४-२७-४७_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, lord of people, Sugreeva will be effectuating everything you have desired and
said, not later but soon, hence awaiting autumn you may please bear up these heavy rainfalls,
besides bearing with the idea of disciplining the enemy. [4-27-47]_END

B_4_C_28_30
BEGIN_
तडित् पताकाभिः अलंकृतानाम्उदीर्ण गंभीर महा रवाणाम् |विभान्ति रूपाणि बलाहकानाम्रण उत्सुकानाम् इव वारणानाम् 
|| ३-२८-३१_END
BEGIN_
"Ornamented with the flags of lightning, and that have whooping, profound and blaring booms, those clouds by their 
appearances are verily shining forth like the elephants enthusiastic for a war. [3-28-31]_END

B_4_C_27_40
BEGIN_
नियम्य कोपम् प्रतिपाल्यताम् शरत्
क्षमस्व मासाम् चतुरो मया सह |
वस अचले अस्मिन् मृग राज सेविते
संवर्तयन् शत्रु वधे समर्थः || ४-२७-४८_END
BEGIN_
"Let autumn be awaited while containing your anger, and along with me you may stay
on this mountain which is adored by lions, and spend these four rainy months here like a monsoon
lion, although you are capable to eliminate the enemy at any moment like a lion. [4-27-48]_END

B_4_C_28_31
BEGIN_
मार्ग अनुगः शैल वन अनुसारीसंप्रस्थितो मेघ रवम् निशम्य |युद्ध अभिकामः प्रतिनाद शन्कीमत्तो गजेन्द्रः 
प्रतिसंनिवृत्तः || ३-२८-३२_END
BEGIN_
"That energetic and lordly elephant which readily started going towards the forest minding the track of that mountain, 
heard the thundering of the cloud, and doubting it a the war-whoop of another elephant took a right about turn 
wishing for a head-on collision with it. [3-28-32]_END

B_4_C_28_32
BEGIN_
क्वचित् प्रगीता इव षट्पद ओघैःक्वचित् प्रवृत्ता इव नील कण्ठैः |क्वचित् प्रमत्ता इव वारण इन्द्रैःविभाति 
अनेक आश्रयिणो वनान्ता || ३-२८-३३_END
BEGIN_
"Somewhere the interiors of forests are finely singing, in affect, as they have swarms of singing honeybees; elsewhere, 
they are richly dancing, practically, as the purple-necked peacocks are bestirring; somewhere else, they are highly 
excited, virtually, as lordly elephants are highly excited, thus the interiors of forests are beaming forth as 
retreats to many bees, birds and animals. [3-28-33]_END

B_4_C_28_33
BEGIN_
कदंब सर्जा अर्जुन कंदल आढ्यावनान्त भूमि मधु वारि पूर्णा |मयूर मत्ता अभिरुत प्रवृत्तैःअपान भूमि प्रतिमा 
विभाति || ३-२८-३४_END
BEGIN_
"Plentiful in Kadamba, Sarja, Arjuna, Kandala trees and with the heaps of their reddish flowers fallen on ground, 
and well-excited peacocks screaming and dancing like the tipplers of that liquor like nectar, thus the interiors 
of forest are aplenty with nectar of those fallen flowers flowing like water, thus they are impressively similar 
to the lands of liquor, say watering-holes. [3-28-34]_END

B_4_C_28_34
BEGIN_
मुक्ता समाभम् सलिलम् पतत् वैसुनिर्मलम् पत्र पुटेषु लग्नम् |हृष्टा विवर्ण च्छदना विहंगाःसुरेन्द्र दत्तम् 
तृषिताः पिबन्ति || ३-२८-३५_END
BEGIN_
"Extremely clear, pure, pearl-similar rainwater given as a gift by Indra is falling down and clinching the hallows 
of leaves, such as it is, it is heartily guzzled down by the thirsty birds whose wings are discoloured by the 
same water. [3-28-35]_END

B_4_C_28_35
BEGIN_
षत्पद तंत्री मधुर अभिधानम्प्लवंगम् उदीरित कण्ठ तालम् |आविष्कृतम् मेघ मृदंग नादैःवनेषु संगीतम् इव प्रवृत्तम् 
|| ३-२८-३६_END
BEGIN_
"Melodious string bass of honeybees as stringendo, frogs crocking as vocal rhythm, fortissimos of clouds as drumbeats, 
music has commenced in the forest as though programmed. [3-28-36]_END

B_4_C_28_36
BEGIN_
क्वचित् प्रनृत्तैः क्वचित् उन् नदद्भिःक्वचित् च वृक्ष अग्र निषण्ण कायैः |व्यालंब बर्ह आभरणैः मयूरैः
वनेषु संगितम् इव प्रवृत्तम् || ३-२८-३७_END
BEGIN_
"Somewhere dancing well, elsewhere voicing in high pitch, and somewhere else seated high on the trees are the 
peacocks with plumaged tails as their dangling decorations, and it appears as the music and dance have commenced 
in the forests as programmed. [3-28-37]_END

B_4_C_28_37
BEGIN_
स्वनैः घनानाम् प्लवगाः प्रबुद्धाविहाय निद्राम् चिर संनिरुद्धाम् |अनेक रूपा आकृति वर्ण नादानव अंबु 
धारा अभिहता नदन्ति || ३-२८-३८_END
BEGIN_
"Thunders of clouds called up the frogs, and casting off their long-time captivity in sleep, frogs of various 
casts, carves, colours and crocks are crocking scourged heavily by the streams of new waters. [3-28-38]_END

B_4_C_28_38
BEGIN_
नद्यः समुद्वाहित चक्रवाकातटानि शीर्णानि अपवाहयित्वा |दृप्ता नव प्राभृत पूर्ण भोगाद्रुतम् स्व भर्तारम् 
उपोप यान्ति || ३-२८-३९_END
BEGIN_
"Prideful rivers are swiftly surging near and near of their lover-like ocean overflowing their own battered riverbanks, 
and in doing so they are swinging and seesawing flights of ruddy gees flying on their bosom, where the curvatures 
of bird-flight look like the new, full-fledged, seducible, nubile breasts of the river, and in doing so the river 
is also lugging other items of romance, namely flowers and fruits, steeped in their new waters. [3-28-39]_END

B_4_C_28_39
BEGIN_
नीलेषु नीला नव वारि पूर्णामेघेषु मेघाः प्रविभान्ति सक्ताः |दवाग्नि दग्धेषु दवाग्नि दग्धाःशैलेषु शैला 
इव बद्ध मूलाः || ३-२८-४०_END
BEGIN_
"When the swarthy clouds full with new waters are docking among swarthily clouds, they are shining forth like 
mountains burnt by wildfire docking among other mountains that are already burnt by wildfire, both moored at mountain-bases. 
[3-28-40]_END

B_4_C_28_40
BEGIN_
प्रमत्त संनाददित बर्हिणानिस शक्रगोप अकुल शाद्वलानि |चरन्ति नीप अर्जुन वासितानिगजाः सुरम्याणि वन अन्तराणि 
|| ३-२८-४१_END
BEGIN_
"Elephants are moving about the very pleasant interiors of forests where peahens are voluptuously screaming, pasturelands 
are overspread with red-beetles, and where they are fragranced with the flowers of Niipa and Arjuna trees. [3-28-41]_END

B_4_C_29_0
BEGIN_
समीक्ष्य विमलम् व्योम गत विद्युत् बलाहकम् |सारसा आकुल संघुष्टम् रम्य ज्योत्स्ना अनुलेपनम् || ४-२९-१समृद्ध 
अर्थम् च सुग्रीवम् मन्द धर्मार्थ संग्रहम् |अत्यर्थम् च असताम् मार्गम् एकांत गत मानसम् || ४-२९-२निवृत्त 
कार्यम् सिद्धार्थम् प्रमद अभिरतम् सदा |प्राप्तवन्तम् अभिप्रेतान् सर्वान् एव मनोरथान् || ४-२९-३स्वाम् च 
पात्नीम् अभिप्रेताम् ताराम् च अपि समीप्सिताम् |विहरंतम् अहो रात्रम् कृतार्थम् विगत ज्वरम् || ४-२९-४क्रीडन्तम् 
इव देवेशम् गन्धर्व अप्सरसाम् गणैः |मंत्रिषु न्यस्त कार्यम् च मंत्रिणाम् अनवेक्षकम् || ४-२९-५उच्छिन्न राज्य 
संदेहम् काम वृत्तम् इव स्थितम् |निश्चित अर्थो अर्थ तत्त्वज्ञः काल धर्म विशेष वित् || ४-२९-६प्रसाद्य वाक्यैः 
मधुरैः हेतुमद्भिः मनो रमैः |वाक्यवित् वाक्य तत्त्वज्ञम् हरीशम् मारुतात्मजः || ४-२९-७हितम् तथ्यम् च पथ्यम् 
च साम धर्म अर्थ नीतिमत् |प्रणय प्रीति संयुक्तम् विश्वास कृत निश्चयम् || ४-२९-८हरीश्वरम् उपागम्य हनुमान् 
वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_
On observing clear sky on which back-clouds and electric charges have disappeared, on which Saarasa birds are 
vibrantly bustling and delightful moonshine is coated, and even on observing him whose riches are abundant, who 
has slowed down in accumulating probity and prosperity from the viewpoint of rectitude, highly engrossed in the 
course of unvirtuous profligates, whose heart is given to undisturbed privacy, and the one who on achieving his 
goals and dearest longings has turned away from other pursuits, who regained his choicest wife, and gained highly 
covetable Lady Tara, thus, who is always indulged in females, merrymaking day in and day out on a par with Indra, 
which Indra will be sporting with the cohorts of gandharva and apsara females, thereby he who is making much of 
his fortune on getting rid of other problems, besides, he who reposed the activity of kingdom in his ministers, 
yet, who does not make eyes at those ministers as he is doubtless of the kingdom which was once disrupted from 
his control, because, that kingdom is looked after well by the very same ministers, as such he is wallowing in 
promiscuity, such as he is, seeking the presence of such a Sugreeva, king of monkeys and an explicator, and even 
on winning his grace, he who is forthright regarding norms of ethics, an exceptional knower of subtleties of transactions 
and the rubrics of duty and time, that golden-tongued Hanuma, the son of Air-god, spoke sweet words that are reasonable, 
heart-pleasing, beneficial, pragmatic, profitable, impressive, immaculate, imperative, and impartial, and which 
words are also inclusive of care and concern of Hanuma, on making a determination with a belief that Sugreeva 
will pay heed to his words. [4-29-1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7, 8, 9a]_END

B_4_C_28_41
BEGIN_
नव अंबु धार आहत केसराणिद्रुतम् परित्यज्य सरोरुहाणि |कदंब पुष्पाणि स केसराणिनवानि हृष्टा भ्रमराः पिबन्ति 
|| ३-२८-४२_END
BEGIN_
"Lashed are the fibrils of lotuses with the downpour of new waters, hence quickly leaving them off the joyful 
honeybees are quaffing the Kadamba flowers with new fibrils. [3-28-42]_END

B_4_C_29_1
BEGIN_
राज्यम् प्राप्तम् यशः चैव कौली श्रीः अभिवर्थिता || ४-२९-९मित्राणाम् संग्रहः शेषः तत् भवान् कर्तुम् अर्हति 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Acquired is the kingdom and glory as well, thus enriched is your dynastic prosperity, but foregathering friends 
is still remaining, and it will be apt of you to negotiate it. [4-29-9b, 10a]_END

B_4_C_28_42
BEGIN_
मत्ता गजेन्द्रा मुदिता गवेन्द्रावनेषु विक्रांततरा मृगेन्द्राः |रम्या नगेन्द्रा निभृता नरेन्द्राःप्रक्रीडितो 
वारि धरैः सुरेन्द्रः || ३-२८-४३_END
BEGIN_
"In forests lordly elephants are ruttish, ideal bulls that are delighted, peerless lions are triumphant to a better 
degree, lofty mountains are heart-pleasant, lords of people are withdrawing from their campaigns, and the lord 
of gods, Indra, is playing well with water giving clouds. [3-28-43]_END

B_4_C_29_2
BEGIN_
यो हि मित्रेषु कालज्ञः सततम् साधु वर्तते || ४-२९-१०तस्य राज्यम् च कीर्तिः च प्रतापः च अपि वर्धते |_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed, he who really conducts himself punctually and amicably with friends, his kingdom, glory and valour will 
flourish. [4-29-10b, 11a]_END

B_4_C_28_43
BEGIN_
मेघाः समुद् भूत समुद्र नादामहाजल ओघैः गगन अवलंबाः |नदीः तटाकानि सरांसि वापिःमहीम् च कृत्स्नाम् अपवाहयन्ति 
|| ३-२८-४४_END
BEGIN_
"The clouds having torrential water are soaring the sky, and spurning the booms of oceans with their rumbles they 
are inundating rivers, lakes, pools, tanks and even the earth. [3-28-44]_END

B_4_C_29_3
BEGIN_
यस्य कोशः च दण्डः च मित्राणि आत्मा च भूमिप |समानि एतानि सर्वाणि स राज्यम् महत् अश्नुते || ४-२९-११_END
BEGIN_
"Matchless kingdom is his who can keep his treasury, army, friends and his own sovereignty - all these four, in 
equiponderance. [4-29-11b, c]_END

B_4_C_28_44
BEGIN_
वर्ष प्रवेगा विपुला पतन्तिप्रवान्ति वाताः समुदीर्ण वेगाः |प्रनष्ट कूलाः प्रवहन्ति शीघ्रम्नद्यो जलम् 
विप्रतिपन्न मार्गाः || ३-२८-४५_END
BEGIN_
"Rains are falling substantially and speedily, gales are blowing intensified in their speediness, while rivers 
are conducting water speedily over their eroded riverbanks and far afield of their course. [3-28-45]_END

B_4_C_29_4
BEGIN_
तत् भवान् वृत्त संपन्नः स्थितः पथि निरत्यये |मित्रार्थम् अभिनीतार्थम् यथावत् कर्तुम् अर्हति || ४-२९-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Therefore, as the one with straightforward actions firstly you resort to an unimperilled course of action, lest 
any peril is imminent, and it will be apt of you to dutifully achieve the purpose of your friend Rama, for which 
alone Rama along with Lakshmana came to you, thus let your power preponderate. [4-29-12]_END

B_4_C_28_45
BEGIN_
नरैः नरेन्द्रा इव पर्वतेन्द्राःसुरेन्द्र नीतैः पवन उपनीतैः |घन अंबु कुम्भैः अभिषिच्यमानारूपम् श्रियम् 
स्वाम् इव दर्शयन्ति || ३-२८-४६_END
BEGIN_
"Lords of people will be anointed by people with water carried in pots on their shoulders, and then those kings 
show their propitious aspect of a humanly king with applied divinity, whereas the lords of mountains are being 
anointed with the water sent directly by Indra and hitherto wafted straight by Air-god in the pots called black-clouds, 
thus these lordly mountains are standing alone as if showing their grandeur and divinity on earth. [3-28-46]_END

B_4_C_29_5
BEGIN_
संत्यज्य सर्व कर्माणि मित्रार्थम् यो न वर्तते |संभ्रमात् हि कृत उत्साहः सः अनर्थेन अवरुध्यते || ४-२९-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Adversity thwarts him who comports himself with overenthusiasm only in self-indulgences, and who does not expeditiously 
strive for the sake of his friend leaving off all other activities of self-indulgence. [4-29-13]_END

B_4_C_28_46
BEGIN_
घन उपगूढम् गगनम् न तारान भास्करो दर्शनम् अभ्युपैति |नवैः जल ओघैः धरणी वितृप्तातमो विलिप्ता न दिशः 
प्रकाशाः || ३-२८-४७_END
BEGIN_
"Sky is closely enshrouded with clouds, neither sun nor stars are getting around for a glimpse, earth is fully 
satiated with the torrents of new water, enswathed in obscurity the precincts are unilluminated... [3-28-47]_END

B_4_C_29_6
BEGIN_
यो हि काल व्यतीतेषु मित्र कार्येषु वर्तते |स कृत्वा महतो अपि अर्थान् न मित्रार्थेन युज्यते || ४-२९-१४_END
BEGIN_
"One who belatedly functions for the present mission of his friend, he will indeed be unassociated with that mission, 
despite of the fact that he has once performed great deeds in respect of the same friend. [4-29-14]_END

B_4_C_29_7
BEGIN_
तत् इदम् मित्रकार्यम् नः काल अतीतम् अरिंदम |क्रियताम् राघवस्य एतत् वैदेह्याः परिमार्गणम् || ४-२९-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Hence, the task of our friend is delayed, oh, enemy-destroyer, searching for Vaidehi is Raghava's mission and 
let it be done. [4-29-15]_END

B_4_C_28_47
BEGIN_
महान्ति कूटानि मही धराणाम्धारा विधौतानि अधिकम् विभान्ति |महा प्रमाणैः विपुलैः प्रपातैःमुक्त कलापैः 
इव लंबमानैः || ३-२८-४८_END
BEGIN_
"The paramount pinnacles of the mountains are thoroughly washed by the torrential rains and are shining forth 
surpassingly, and the voluminous and widespread torrents that are pitching down are like the pearly necklaces 
pendulous on the chests of mountains. [3-28-48]_END

B_4_C_30_0
BEGIN_
गुहाम् प्रविष्टे सुग्रीवे विमुक्ते गगने घनैः |
वर्ष रात्रे स्थितो रामः काम शोक अभिपीडितः || ४-३०-१
पाण्डुरम् गगनम् दृष्ट्वा विमलम् चन्द्र मण्डलम् |
शारदीम् रजनीम् चैव दृष्ट्वा ज्योत्स्न अनुलेपनाम् || ४-३०-२
काम वृत्तम् च सुग्रीवम् नष्टाम् च जनक आत्मजाम् |
दृष्ट्वा कालम् अतीतम् च मुमोह परम आतुरः || ४-३०-३_END
BEGIN_
On Sugreeva's entering the cave-like Kishkindha, Rama who spent rainy nights on that
mountain with much distress owing to the misery of yearning for Seetha, has seen the immaculate
sphere of moon on silvern sky freed by ceasing rains, and even autumnal nights that are enamelled
with moonshine, and thus he observed that Seetha is lost hopelessly, engrossed in lust Sugreeva is
lost to world intractably, and furthermore time too is being lost irretrievably, and thus he became
highly impatient and even swooned. [4-30-1, 2, 3]_END

B_4_C_29_8
BEGIN_
न च कालम् अतीतम् ते निवेदयति कालवित् |त्वरमाणो अपि स प्राज्ञः तव राजन् वशानुगः || ४-२९-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Though the time is lagging, oh, king, that insightful and punctual Rama is not indicating about it to you, though 
he is hurrying to complete his mission within a time-frame, because he is following you alone abiding under the 
control abiding by your promise. [4-29-16]_END

B_4_C_28_48
BEGIN_
शैलोपल प्रस्खलमान वेगाःशैलोत्तमानाम् विपुलाः प्रपाताः |गुहासु संनादित बर्हिणासुहारा विकीर्यन्त इव 
अवभान्ति || ३-२८-४९_END
BEGIN_
"Washing the mountain stones speedily the torrents on the lofty mountains are widespread and entering the caves, 
in which peacocks are highly screaming, and thus they are in the gleam of lavalieres strewn around. [3-28-49]_END

B_4_C_30_1
BEGIN_
स तु संज्ञाम् उपागम्य मुहूर्तात् मतिमान् नृपः |
मनः स्थाम् अपि वैदेहीम् चिंतयामास राघवः || ४-३०-४_END
BEGIN_
But on getting consciousness in a moment, that thoughtful king Raghava started to
think of Vaidehi who is abiding in his heart, though not at his side. [4-30-4]_END

B_4_C_29_9
BEGIN_
कुलस्य हेतुः स्फीतस्य दीर्घ बन्धुः च राघवः |अप्रमेय प्रभावः च स्वयम् च अप्रतिमो गुणैः || ४-२९-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Raghava is the cause for augmentation of multitudes, a long-lasting covenentor, and even an undefinable one in 
his proficiency, and an unparalleled one by his grace. [4-29-17]_END

B_4_C_28_49
BEGIN_
शीघ्र प्रवेगा विपुलाः प्रपातानिर्धौत शृंग उपतला गिरीणाम् |मुक्ता कलाप प्रतिमाः पतन्तोमहा गुह उस्त्संग 
तलैः ध्रियन्ते || ३-२८-५०_END
BEGIN_
"On neatly washing the crests of wide mountains and their nearby planes, the high-speeded waterfalls are falling 
like pearl-necklaces and the mountains are wearing them at the planes of their cavernous caves. [3-28-50]_END

B_4_C_30_2
BEGIN_
दृष्ट्वा च विमलम् व्योम गत विद्युत् बलाहकम् |
सारस आरव संघुष्टम् विललाप आर्तया गिरा || ४-३०-५_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the sky to be spic and span when set free of black-clouds and lightning,
and even vibrant with the shrieks of Saarasa birds, Rama bemoaned in woeful words. [4-30-5]_END

B_4_C_29_10
BEGIN_
तस्य त्वम् कुरु वै कार्यम् पूर्वम् तेन कृतम् तव |हरीश्वर हरि श्रेष्ठान् आज्ञापयितुम् अर्हसि || ४-२९-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Certainly you have to carry through his mission as he has carried out your mission previously, and oh, lord of 
monkeys, it will be apt of you to summon worthy monkeys for searching Seetha. [4-29-18]_END

B_4_C_28_50
BEGIN_
सुरताम् अर्द विच्छिन्नाः स्वर्ग स्त्री हार मौक्तिकाः |पतन्ति च अतुलाः दिक्षु तोय धाराः समन्ततः || ३-२८-५१_END
BEGIN_
"Like the strings of pearls of heavenly females plopping down when broken in the friction of lovemaking, excellent 
streams of water are falling all over and in all directions. [3-28-51]_END

B_4_C_30_3
BEGIN_
आसीनः पर्वतस्य अग्रे हेम धातु विभूषिते |
शारदम् गगनम् दृष्ट्वा जगाम मनसा प्रियाम् || ४-३०-६_END
BEGIN_
Rama's concepts are on the rove towards his ladylove when he beheld the skyscape of
autumn while sitting on the summit of a mountain that is embellished with gold and other ores, and
he soliloquised his thoughts in this way. [4-30-6]_END

B_4_C_29_11
BEGIN_
न हि तावत् भवेत् कालो व्यतीतः चोदनात् ऋते |चोदितस्य हि कार्यस्य भवेत् काल व्यतिक्रमः || ४-२९-१९_END
BEGIN_
"As long as Rama is not going to prod us for action deem that there is no time lapse, but the minute he does deem 
it as lapsed. [4-29-19]_END

B_4_C_28_51
BEGIN_
विलीयमानैः विहगैः निमीलद्भिः च पंकजैः |विकसन्त्या च मालत्या गतो अस्तम् ज्ञायते रविः || ३-२८-५२_END
BEGIN_
"With the return of birds to nests, doubling up of lotuses, and blooming up jasmines, the sun is know to have 
gone into dusk. [3-28-52]_END

B_4_C_30_4
BEGIN_
सारस आरव संनादैः सारस आरव नादिनी |
या आश्रमे रमते बाला सा अद्य मे रमते कथम् || ४-३०-७_END
BEGIN_
"Young Seetha with a voice that is a soundalike to the callings of Saarasa birds
used to take delight in these resonant calls of Saarasa birds when we were together in hermitage,
but how she might be taking delight in these chirrups now without me. [4-30-7]_END

B_4_C_29_12
BEGIN_
अकर्तुर् अपि कार्यस्य भवान् कर्ता हरीश्वर |किम् पुनः प्रतिकर्तुः ते राज्येन च वधेन च || ४-२९-२०_END
BEGIN_
"You are a helpful one even to those that are unhelpful to you, oh, king of monkeys, then why repeat about him 
who helped you in getting your kingdom, and even in killing your enemy, Vali._END

B_4_C_30_5
BEGIN_
पुष्पिताम् च आसनान् दृष्ट्वा कांचनान् इव निर्मलान् |
कथम् सा रमते बाला पश्यंती माम् अपश्यती || ४-३०-८_END
BEGIN_
"On seeing the flawless Asana trees flowered as if with golden flowers, she checks
up for my availability thereabout, but now finding me nowhere near her, how can she be happy.
[4-30-8]_END

B_4_C_28_52
BEGIN_
वृत्ता यात्रा नरेन्द्राणाम् सेना पथि एव वर्तते |वैराणि चैव मार्गाः च सलिलेन समीकृताः || ३-२८-५३_END
BEGIN_
"Reversed are the campaigns of kings as the armies are marooned and thus rainwater has neutralised conflicts and 
roadways. [3-28-53]_END

B_4_C_29_13
BEGIN_
शक्तिमान् अतिविक्रान्तो वानर ऋष्क गण ईश्वर |कर्तुम् दाशरथेः प्रीतिम् आज्ञायाम् किम् नु सज्जसे || ४-२९-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Highly adventurous and powerful vanara as you are, oh, lord of multitudes of monkeys and bears, why do you really 
temporise in issuing orders to fulfil the cherish of Rama. [4-29-21]_END

B_4_C_30_6
BEGIN_
या पुरा कलहंसानाम् स्वरेण कल भाषिणी |
बुध्यते चारु सर्वांगी सा अद्य मे रमते कथम् || ४-३०-९_END
BEGIN_
"She who is enchanting to me by her well-proportioned limbs that clucky-voiced
Seetha earlier used to wake me up in tune with the melodious callings of clucking-swans, but how
that ladylove of mine might be amusing herself now. [4-30-9]_END

B_4_C_28_53
BEGIN_
मासि प्रौष्ठपदे ब्रह्म ब्राह्मणानाम् विवक्षताम् |अयम् अध्याय समयः सामगानाम् उपस्थितः || ३-२८-५४_END
BEGIN_
"The month of Bhaadrapada, August-September, is the time for learning the singing of Sama Veda, and this is the 
time that has come for those Brahmans who concern themselves for learning the singing of Sama Veda. [3-28-54]_END

B_4_C_31_0
BEGIN_
स कामिनम् दीनम् अदीन सत्त्वः
शोक अभिपन्नम् समुदीर्ण कोपम् |
नरेन्द्र सूनुर् नरदेव पुत्रम्
रामानुजः पूर्वजम् इति उवाच || ४-३१-१_END
BEGIN_
When Rama of undeterred stamina has become pitiable while yearning for Seetha,
overcome with grief while the search for Seetha is becoming futile, overwrought with anger while
Sugreeva is reneging on his promise, to such an elder prince-brother from a godlike king, his
younger prince-brother Lakshmana spoke in this way. [4-31-1]_END

B_4_C_29_14
BEGIN_
कामम् खलु शरैः शक्तः सुर असुर महा उरगान् |वशे दाशरथिः कर्तुम् त्वत् प्रतिज्ञाम् अवेक्षते || ४-२९-२२_END
BEGIN_
"If need be Rama of Dasharatha is really capable of keeping gods, demons and great-vipers under his control with 
his arrows, but he is anticipating fulfilment of your promise. [4-29-22]_END

B_4_C_30_7
BEGIN_
निःस्वनम् चक्रवाकानाम् निशम्य सहचारिणाम् |
पुण्डरीकविशालाक्षी कथम् एषा भविष्यति || ४-३०-१०_END
BEGIN_
"On hearing the sharp notes of Cakravaka birds that always move together in couples,
what will become of this white-lotus-like broad-eyed Seetha, since she is not together with me.
[4-30-10]_END

B_4_C_28_54
BEGIN_
निवृत्त कर्म आयतनो नूनम् संचित संचयः |आषाढीम् अभ्युपगतो भरतः कोसल अधिपः || ३-२८-५५_END
BEGIN_
"On carrying out all the domestic affairs and completely garnering the goods for rainy season, Bharata, the king 
of Kosala, might have definitely undertaken the 'four-month-vow' on the full moon day of aSaaDha month. [3-28-55]_END

B_4_C_31_1
BEGIN_
न वानरः स्थास्यति साधु वृत्ते
न मन्यते कर्म फल अनुषंगान् |
न भोक्ष्यते वानर राज्य लक्ष्मीम्
तथा हि न अभिक्रमते अस्य बुद्धिः || ४-३१-२_END
BEGIN_
"As a forester Sugreeva will not abide by the conduct of gentlefolk, he is not
appreciative of the fruits of incidental events like gaining kingdom and regaining wife occurring
out of your deed of eliminating Vali, thus he will not enjoy the prosperity of the kingdom anymore.
Obviously his prudence is behindhand, isn't it! [4-31-2]_END

B_4_C_29_15
BEGIN_
प्राण त्याग अविशंकेन कृतम् तेन महत् प्रियम् |तस्य मार्गाम वैदेहीम् पृथिव्याम् अपि च अंबरे || ४-२९-२३_END
BEGIN_
"He fulfilled an exceptional cherish of yours without much doubting for the forfeiture of his own life, hence 
we search for his wife Vaidehi anywhere on earth or even on skies. [4-29-23]_END

B_4_C_30_8
BEGIN_
सरांसि सरितो वापीः काननानि वनानि च |
ताम् विना मृगशावाक्षीम् चरन् न अद्य सुखम् लभे || ४-३०-११_END
BEGIN_
"I am not able to enjoy myself without that deer-eyed lady though wandering around
enjoyable lakes, rivers, tanks, forests and woodlands, whose thirst is drenched by rainwater and my
thirsting for her is not. [4-30-11]_END

B_4_C_28_55
BEGIN_
नूनम् आपूर्यमाणायाः सरय्वा वधते रयः |माम् समीक्ष्य समायान्तम् अयोध्याया इव स्वनः || ३-२८-५६_END
BEGIN_
"Definitely the River Sarayu must be overfilling and its swashing must be mounting as with the commotion of Ayodhya 
on beholding my returning to city. [3-28-56]_END

B_4_C_31_2
BEGIN_
मति क्षयात् ग्राम्य सुखेषु सक्तः
तव प्रसाद अप्रतिकार बुद्धिः |
हतो अग्रजम् पश्यतु वालिनम्
न राज्यम् एवम् विगुणस्य देयम् || ४-३१-३_END
BEGIN_
"Without any notion of requiting the beneficence you have accorded he is insanely
involved in primitive pleasures, such as he is, let him see his elder brother Vali when slain.
Hence, kingdoms are unaffordable to dishonest. [4-31-3]_END

B_4_C_29_16
BEGIN_
न देवा न च गंधर्वा न असुरा न मरुत् गणाः |न च यक्षा भयम् तस्य कुर्युः किम् इव राक्षसाः || ४-२९-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Gods cannot cause dismay to him, then gandharva-s - no; multitudes of wind-gods - no; asura-s - no; yaksha-s 
- no; and then wherefore the raakshasa-s can? [4-29-24]_END

B_4_C_30_9
BEGIN_
अपि ताम् मत् वियोगात् च सौकुमार्यात् च भामिनीम् |
सुदूरम् पीडयेत् कामः शरत् गुण निरंतरः || ४-३०-१२_END
BEGIN_
"The Love-god with a plethora of provocative autumnal features will be prolongedly
agonising her, because she is separated from me, and because her ladyship is a frailty - won't he?"
Thus Rama worried for Seetha. [4-30-12]_END

B_4_C_28_56
BEGIN_
इमाः स्फीत गुणा वर्षाः सुग्रीवः सुखम् अश्नुते |विजित अरिः स दारः च राज्ये महति च स्थितः || ३-२८-५७_END
BEGIN_
"This rainy season as such has manifold inbuilt facilities for self-contained entertainment, so Sugreeva must 
be luxuriating in them, besides, revelling for conquering his enemy, regaining his wife, and instituting himself 
as a king of an admirable kingdom. [3-28-57]_END

B_4_C_31_3
BEGIN_
न धारये कोपम् उदीर्ण वेगम्
निहन्मि सुग्रीवम् असत्यम् अद्य |
हरि प्रवीरैः सह वालि पुत्रो
नरेन्द्र पुत्र्या विचयम् करोतु || ४-३१-४_END
BEGIN_
"Unbearable is this anger that is tiding quickly, now I shall kill that unfaithful
Sugreeva and the best braving monkeys shall search for that princess Seetha, remaining under the
command of Vali's son, Angada." Thus said Lakshmana to Rama. [4-31-4]_END

B_4_C_29_17
BEGIN_
तत् एवम् शक्ति युक्तस्य पूर्वम् प्रिय कृतः तथा |रामस्य अर्हसि पिंगेश कर्तुम् सर्व आत्मना प्रियम् || ४-२९-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Therefore, oh, lord of monkeys, that Rama is energetic to exert himself, but he fulfilled your aspiration earlier, 
and it will be apt of you requite him with his aspiration at all events. [4-29-25]_END

B_4_C_30_10
BEGIN_
एवम् आदि नरश्रेष्ठो विललाप नृपात्मजः |
विहंग इव सारंगः सलिलम् त्रिदशेश्वरात् || ४-३०-१३_END
BEGIN_
So on and so forth that best one among men and the son of a king keened over, like a
Rain-cuckoo which will be keen on Indra, the king of divinities, for rainy-water. [4-30-13]_END

B_4_C_28_57
BEGIN_
अहम् तु हृत दारः च राज्यात् च महतः च्युतः |नदी कूलम् इव क्लिन्नम् अवसीदामि लक्ष्मण || ३-२८-५८_END
BEGIN_
"As for me, Lakshmana, I am the one who is toppled from a great kingdom, whose wife is stolen, such as I am, I 
am toppling down like a riverbank that is toppled over. [3-28-58]_END

B_4_C_31_4
BEGIN_
तम् आत्त बाण आसनम् उत्पतंतम्
निवेदित अर्थम् रण चण्ड कोपम् |
उवच रामः पर वीर हन्ता
स्व वेक्षितम् स अनुनयम् च वाक्यम् || ४-३१-५_END
BEGIN_
Rama, the slayer of braving enemies, spoke this well thought sentence that includes
persuasiveness to Lakshmana who is with an irrepressible wartime anger, who has apprised his
intention to slay Sugreeva, and who on taking his bow is now leaping at Kishkindha. [4-31-5]_END

B_4_C_29_18
BEGIN_
न अधस्तात् अवनौ न अप्सु गतिः न उपरि च अम्बरे |कस्यचित् सज्जते अस्माकम् कपीश्वर तव आज्ञया || ४-२९-२६_END
BEGIN_
"In case you were ordering us, oh, king of monkeys, among us whosoever he may be his impetus will be unhampered 
either in netherworlds, or in water, or up above on the sky. [4-29-26]_END

B_4_C_30_11
BEGIN_
ततः चंचूर्य रम्येषु फलार्थी गिरि सानुषु |
ददर्श पर्युपावृत्तो लक्ष्मीवान् लक्ष्मणो अग्रजम् || ४-३०-१४_END
BEGIN_
Meandering on the pleasant mountain-terraces in search of fruits brilliant Lakshmana
returned and has seen his elder brother Rama. [4-30-14]_END

B_4_C_28_58
BEGIN_
शोकः च मम विस्तीर्णो वर्षाः च भृश दुर्गमाः |रावणः च महान् शत्रुः अपारम् प्रतिभाति मे || ३-२८-५९_END
BEGIN_
"Also my anguish is boundless, the rains have definitely made the pathways impassable, my enemy Ravana is a formidable 
one, thus these three appear to me as insurmountable obstacles. [3-28-59]_END

B_4_C_32_0
BEGIN_
अंगदस्य वचः श्रुत्वा सुग्रीवः सचिवैः सह |लक्ष्मणम् कुपितम् श्रुत्वा मुमोच आसनम् आत्मवान् || ४-३२-१_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of Angada along with those of his ministers, namely Hanuma, Plaksha, and Prabhava et al, 
also on knowing that Lakshmana is angered, that sensible Sugreeva stirred from seat. [4-32-1]_END

B_4_C_31_5
BEGIN_
न हि वै त्वत् विधो लोके पापम् एवम् समाचरेत् |
कोपम् आर्येण यो हन्ति स वीरः पुरुषोत्तमः || ४-३१-६_END
BEGIN_
"Certainly none of your kind shall commit this sort of sin in this world, and if
such a situation occurs, he who by his noble gesture kills his own anger is a valorous one, and he
really becomes the best one among men." Thus Rama is saying to Lakshmana. [4-31-6]_END

B_4_C_29_19
BEGIN_
तत् आज्ञापय कः किम् ते कुतो वा अपि व्यवस्यतु |हरयो हि अप्रधृष्याः ते सन्ति कोटि अग्रतो अनघ || ४-२९-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Therefore command us, oh, merited one, as you have more than ten million unchallengeable monkeys under your command, 
as to who should start from where and for which purpose, and as to how one should exert himself." Thus Hanuma 
appealed to Sugreeva. [4-29-27]_END

B_4_C_30_12
BEGIN_
स चिन्तया दुस्सहया परीतम्
विसंज्ञम् एकम् विजने मनस्वी |
भ्रातुर् विषादात् त्वरितो अति दीनः
समीक्ष्य सौमित्रिः उवाच रामम् || ४-३०-१५_END
BEGIN_
Noble-hearted Saumitri, on observing lone Rama in a lonely place, who is beset with
unbearable sadness and whose posture is vacuous, became very miserable for the sad condition of his
brother, and spoke to Rama fretfully. [4-30-15]_END

B_4_C_28_59
BEGIN_
अयात्राम् चैव दृष्ट्वा इमाम् मार्गाम् च भृश दुर्गमान् |प्रणते चैव सुग्रीवे न मया किंचित् ईरितम् || ३-२८-६०_END
BEGIN_
"Though Sugreeva is very humble to embark on a campaign, visualising the rainy season as an impossible one for 
any campaign, and even the pathways are rendered highly impassable I have not said anything to him in the affirmative. 
[3-28-60]_END

B_4_C_32_1
BEGIN_
स च तान् अब्रवीत् वाक्यम् निश्चित्य गुरु लाघवम् |मंत्रज्ञान् मंत्र कुशलो मंत्रेषु परिनिष्ठितः || ४-३२-२_END
BEGIN_
On discriminating the pros and cons Sugreeva spoke this sentence to the strategist-ministers, for he himself is 
an expert in strategies and a diligent one in carrying out those strategies. [4-32-2]_END

B_4_C_29_20
BEGIN_
तस्य तद् वचनम् श्रुत्वा काले साधु निरूपितम् |सुग्रीवः सत्त्व संपन्नः चकार मतिम् उत्तमाम् || ४-२९-२८_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of Hanuma that are validly demonstrated on time, Sugreeva whose soldiery is substantial, 
took a noble decision. [4-29-28]_END

B_4_C_31_6
BEGIN_
न इदम् अत्र त्वया ग्राह्यम् साधु वृत्तेन लक्ष्मण |
ताम् प्रीतिम् अनुवर्तस्व पूर्व वृत्तम् च संगतम् || ४-३१-७_END
BEGIN_
"Lakshmana, as person with righteous conduct you are not supposed to understand this
matter in this way, or undertake in this way, but you are supposed to adhere to those aspects of
friendliness with Sugreeva and the affinity earlier existed in dealing with him. [4-31-7]_END

B_4_C_30_13
BEGIN_
किम् आर्य कामस्य वशम् गतेन
किम् आत्म पौरुष्य पराभवेन |
अयम् ह्रिया संह्रियते समाधिः
किम् अत्र योगेन निवर्तितेन || ४-३०-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, noble one, what is the use in getting into fetters of passion, what for soul's
bold-temper is being trounced, this remorseful sadness is arrogating self-assurance, and what
purpose can be achieved now in retracing steps from the goal. [4-30-16]_END

B_4_C_28_60
BEGIN_
अपि च अति परिक्लिष्टम् चिरात् दारैः समागतम् |आत्म कार्य गरीयस्त्वात् वक्तुम् न इच्छामि वानरम् || ३-२८-६१_END
BEGIN_
"Even Sugreeva has undergone many difficulties in their entirety, after a long while he is united with his wife, 
and even owing to the magnitude involved in our task of tracking down Ravana I did not desire to insist on that 
monkey. [3-28-61]_END

B_4_C_32_2
BEGIN_
न मे दुर् व्याहृतम् किंचित् न अपि मे दुर् अनुष्ठितम् |लक्ष्मणो राघव भ्राता क्रुद्धः किम् इति चिंतये || ४-३२-३_END
BEGIN_
"I have not in the least spoken any ill of them, nor committed any misdeed in their respect, thus I am thinking 
why should Raghava's brother Lakshmana take offence at me? [4-32-3]_END

B_4_C_31_7
BEGIN_
साम उपहितया वाचा रूक्षाणि परिवर्जयन् |
वक्तुम् अर्हसि सुग्रीवम् व्यतीतम् काल पर्यये || ४-३१-८_END
BEGIN_
"It will be apt of you to speak to that reneger Sugreeva with placating words rather
than with caustic remarks, as his sin is no more than flouting the timeframe." Thus Rama said to
Lakshmana. [4-31-8]_END

B_4_C_29_21
BEGIN_
संदिदेश अति मति मान् नीलम् नित्य कृत उद्यमम् |दिक्षु सर्वासु सर्वेषाम् सैन्यानाम् उपसंग्रहे || ४-२९-२९_END
BEGIN_
And the noble minded Sugreeva directed Nila, one of the commanders of vanara army, and who always strives to foregather 
vanara army, to foregather all of the monkey-forces available in all the directions. [4-29-29]_END

B_4_C_28_61
BEGIN_
स्वयम् एव हि विश्रम्य ज्ञात्वा कालम् उपागतम् |उपकारम् च सुग्रीवो वेत्स्यते न अत्र संशयः || ३-२८-६२_END
BEGIN_
"After a respite Sugreeva will realise on his own that the time has come, and he will also realise the he has 
something to requite, isn't it! So, there needn't be any doubt in that matter. [3-28-62]_END

B_4_C_30_14
BEGIN_
क्रियाभियोगम् मनसः प्रसादम्
समाधि योग अनुगतम् च कालम् |
सहाय सामर्थ्यम् अदीन सत्त्वः
स्व कर्म हेतुम् च कुरुष्व तात ४-३०-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, dear sir, engage yourself in your mission with an undeterred spirit and with a
good disposition of mind, and bring time under control with steadfastness and ideation, and the
capabilities of your helpmates, say Sugreeva and others be gathered, and the basis for your
achievements, say daily rituals towards gods, be performed by you as your means. [4-30-17]_END

B_4_C_32_3
BEGIN_
असुहृद्भिः मम अमित्रैः नित्यम् अन्तर दर्शिभिः |मम दोषान् असंभूतान् श्रावितो राघवानुजः || ४-३२-४_END
BEGIN_
"Unsympathetic rivals of mine, who will always be snoopy for scope, might have ear-filled Raghava's brother about 
the fabricated faults of mine. [4-32-4]_END

B_4_C_31_8
BEGIN_
सो अग्रजेन अनुशिष्ट अर्थो यथावत् पुरुषर्षभः |
प्रविवेश पुरीम् वीरो लक्ष्मणः पर वीर हा || ४-३१-९_END
BEGIN_
That brave one and the slayer of braving enemies Lakshmana thus schooled expediently
by his elder brother about the means of gainfulness, that best one among men proceeded to enter the
city of Kishkindha. [4-31-9]_END

B_4_C_29_22
BEGIN_
यथा सेना समग्रा मे यूथपालाः च सर्वशः |समागच्छन्ति असंगेन सेनाग्राणि तथा कुरु || ४-२९-३०_END
BEGIN_
"You have to have organise that way as to how my army in its entirety and from all over, together with corps commanders, 
is to be marshalled to stay in the cutting edge of army. [4-29-30]_END

B_4_C_30_15
BEGIN_
न जानकी मानव वंश नाथ
त्वया सनाथा सुलभा परेण |
न च अग्नि चूडाम् ज्वलिताम् उपेत्य
न दह्यते वीर वरार्ह कश्चित् || ४-३०-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, the lord of human kindred, with you as her husband Janaki is not an easily
attainable one for others, oh, highly honourable one, if it is said that none will be burnt if he
nears the tongues of flaming fire, oh, brave one, it is not so, for Janaki is a flaming fire, and
anyone nearing her in ill-will will be burnt to ashes like a grass-hopper." Thus Lakshmana said to
Rama. [4-30-18]_END

B_4_C_28_62
BEGIN_
तस्मात् काल प्रतीक्षो अहम् स्थितो अस्मि शुभ लक्षण |सुग्रीवस्य नदीनाम् च प्रसादम् अभिकांक्षयन् || ३-२८-६३_END
BEGIN_
"I therefore stay abidingly looking forward for the time, oh, Lakshmana with felicitous aspects, expectant of 
the generosity of Sugreeva and of these rivers. [3-28-63]_END

B_4_C_32_4
BEGIN_
अत्र तावत् यथा बुद्धि सर्वैः एव यथा विधि |भावस्य निश्चयः तावत् विज्ञेयो निपुणम् शनैः || ४-३२-५_END
BEGIN_
"In this situation, all of you on your part and according to your perspectives have to find out firstly and meticulously 
about the attitude of Lakshmana, along with a steady but diligent determination thereof. [4-32-5]_END

B_4_C_31_9
BEGIN_
ततः शुभ मतिः प्राज्ञो भ्रातुः प्रियहितेरतः |
लक्ष्मणः प्रतिसंरब्धो जगाम भवनम् कपेः || ४-३१-१०
शक्र बाणासन प्रख्यम् धनुः कालांतक उपमः |
प्रगृह्य गिरि शृंगाभम् मन्दरः सानुमान् इव || ४-३१-११_END
BEGIN_
That right-minded and well-informed Lakshmana who is bent on doing only that which
is agreeable and beneficial to his elder brother, then swallowing his exasperation and wielding a
bow which is shining forth like the bow of Indra, and which is standing out like a peaking mountain
proceeded towards the palace of the monkey, namely Sugreeva, and with such a bow he appeared to be
the peaking Mt. Mandhara and like the Era-Ender. [4-31-10, 11]_END

B_4_C_29_23
BEGIN_
ये तु अंतपालाः प्लवगाः शीघ्रगा व्यवसायिनः |समानयंतु ते शीघ्रम् त्वरिताः शासनात् मम |स्वयम् च अनंतरम् सैन्यम् 
भवान् एव अनुपश्यतु || ४-२९-३१_END
BEGIN_
"Those that are the quickstepped, venturesome fly-jumpers who are the defenders on the perimeter of army, they 
shall be fetched quickly an speedily at my order, and oh, Niila, you on your own have to personally and closely 
monitor the military establishment without any heterogeneity. [4-29-31]_END

B_4_C_28_63
BEGIN_
उपकारेण वीरो हि प्रतिकारेण युज्यते |अकृतज्ञो अप्रतिकृतो हन्ति सत्त्ववताम् मनः || ३-२८-६४_END
BEGIN_
"A valiant one who is succoured will be indebted with some requital on his part, but besides being unfaithful, 
if one who does not make requital for all the favours done in his interest, he will be wounding the hearts of 
soft-hearted people." Rama said so to Lakshmana, keeping Sugreeva in view. [3-28-64]_END

B_4_C_30_16
BEGIN_
सलक्षणम् लक्ष्मणम् अप्रधृष्यम्
स्वभावजम् वाक्यम् उवाच रामः |
हितम् च पथ्यम् च नय प्रसक्तम्
ससाम धर्मार्थ समाहितम् च || ४-३०-१९_END


B_4_C_32_5
BEGIN_
न खलु अस्ति मम त्रासो लक्ष्मणान् न अपि राघवात् |मित्रम् तु अस्थान कुपितम् जनयति एव संभ्रमम् || ४-३२-६_END
BEGIN_
"Definitely there is no fear for me from Lakshmana, not even from Raghava, but an unfounded ire of a friend alone 
is giving rise to disquiet. [4-32-6]_END

B_4_C_31_10
BEGIN_
यथा उक्त कारी वचनम् उत्तरम् चैव स उत्तरम् |
बृहस्पति समो बुद्ध्या मत्त्वा रामानुजः तदा || ४-३१-१२
काम क्रोध समुत्थेन भ्रातुः कोपाग्निना वृतः |
प्रभंजन इव अप्रीतः प्रययौ लक्ष्मणः तदा || ४-३१-१३_END
BEGIN_
Lakshmana the non-defying adherer of Rama, a coequal of Brihaspati-Jupiter, in
intelligence, then mulled over the exact words of Rama to be spoken to Sugreeva, possible reply of
Sugreeva on them, and his own sensible counter-reply to them, enwrapped as he is in a furious fire
fired up by the desire of Rama for Seetha, proceeded to Sugreeva's palace like an embittered
whirlwind aided and abetted by a furious fire. [4-31-12, 13]_END

B_4_C_29_24
BEGIN_
त्रि पंच रात्रात् ऊर्ध्वम् यः प्राप्नुयात् इह वानरः |तस्य प्राण अन्तिको दण्डो न अत्र कार्या विचारणा || ४-२९-३२_END
BEGIN_
"And, the monkey who arrives here after fifteen nights, to him termination of life is the punishment, there is 
no business for further adjudication. [4-29-32]_END

B_4_C_28_64
BEGIN_
अथ एवम् उक्तः प्रणिधाय लक्ष्मणःकृत अंजलिः तत् प्रतिपूज्य भाषितम् |उवाच रामम् स्वभिराम दर्शनम्प्रदर्शयन् 
दर्शनम् आत्मनः शुभम् || ३-२८-६५_END
BEGIN_
Visualising what Rama said about their waiting for pre-winter season to be candid, and praisefully making palm-fold 
at that determination of Rama, and even to clarify his own opportune viewpoint, Lakshmana spoke to Rama who by 
his own aspect is a delightful one for a ken. [3-28-65]_END

B_4_C_30_17

BEGIN_
Lakshmana with his seemliness spoke those undeniable and expedient words that
emerged from his very nature, which are tasteful, morally abiding, and further abounding with
friendliness, righteousness, and meaningfulness, and on listening such words Rama spoke to
Lakshmana._END

B_4_C_32_6
BEGIN_
सर्वथा सुकरम् मित्रम् दुष्करम् प्रतिपालनम् |अनित्यत्वात् तु चित्तानाम् प्रीतिः अल्पे अपि भिद्यते || ४-३२-७_END
BEGIN_
"It is always practicable to befriend any, but in turn it is impracticable to manage that friendship, even a trifle 
splits off that friendliness for sentiments are transient. [4-32-7]_END

B_4_C_31_11
BEGIN_
साल ताल अश्व कर्णाम् च तरसा पातयन् बलात् |
पर्यस्यन् गिरि कूटानि द्रुमान् अन्याम् च वेगितः || ४-३१-१४
शिलाः च शकली कुर्वन् पद्भ्याम् गज इव आशु गः |
दूरम् एक पदम् त्यक्त्वा ययौ कार्यवशात् द्रुतम् || ४-३१-१५_END
BEGIN_
While knocking down Saala, Palm, Ashvakarna trees with his might, razing
mountain-crests and even other trees with his strength, splintering boulders underfoot, Lakshmana
made haste through an enmeshed path leaving off one-foot-pathway as with an elephant striding
fleetly, and proceeded swiftly impelled by the mission. [4-31-15]_END

B_4_C_29_25
BEGIN_
हरीन् च वृद्धान् उपयातु स अंगदोभवान् मम आज्ञाम् अधिकृत्य निश्चितम् |इति व्यवस्थाम् हरि पुंगव ईश्वरो
विधाय वेश्म प्रविवेश वीर्यवान् || ४-२९-३३_END
BEGIN_
"Associated with Angada you shall approach elderly monkeys like Jambavanta and others, according to my decision 
and authorised by my order." Thus, Sugreeva, the king of best monkeys on assigning the set-up, and ordering Niila, 
the Commander of Vanara Forces, that glorious Sugreeva re-entered his palace-chambers. [4-29-33]_END

B_4_C_28_65
BEGIN_
यत् उक्तम् एतत् तव सर्वम् ईप्सितम्नर इन्द्र कर्ता नचिरा हरि ईश्वरः |शरत् प्रतीक्षः क्षमताम् इमम् भवान्
जल प्रपातम् रिपु निग्रहे धृतः || ३-२८-६६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, lord of people, Sugreeva will be effectuating everything you have desired and said, not later but soon, hence 
awaiting autumn you may please bear up these heavy rainfalls, besides bearing with the idea of disciplining the 
enemy." So said Lakshmana to Rama. [3-28-66]_END

B_4_C_30_18
BEGIN_
निस्संशयम् कार्यम् अवेक्षितव्यम्
क्रिया विशेषो अपि अनुवर्तितव्यः |
न तु प्रवृद्धस्य दुरासदस्य
कुमार वीर्यस्य फलम् च चिन्त्यम् || ४-३०-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Doubtless accomplishment of the task is to be held in view, even oh, boy, the
factors that contribute to its accomplishment, like enthusiasm, helpmates etc., are to be followed
through, and not only these aspects but we also have to observe the fruition of task when that task
is becoming unwieldy, unattainable and formidable, along with the lapse of time and lapsing of
help." Thus Rama said to Lakshmana. [4-30-20]_END

B_4_C_32_7
BEGIN_
अतो निमित्तम् त्रस्तो अहम् रामेण तु महात्मना |यन् मम उपकृतम् शक्यम् प्रतिकर्तुम् न तन् मया || ४-३२-८_END
BEGIN_
"On that score I am flustering because of the noble-souled Rama, and I cannot possibly requite the favour that 
has been done to me." So said Sugreeva to his ministers. [4-32-8]_END

B_4_C_33_0
BEGIN_
अथ प्रतिसंआदिष्टो लक्ष्मणः परवीरहा |प्रविवेश गुहाम् रम्याम् किष्किंधाम् राम शासनात् || ४-३३-१_END
BEGIN_
Then on invitation to inside, Lakshmana, the slayer of braving enemies, entered that delightful cavelike Kishkindha 
at Rama's orders. [4-33-1]_END

B_4_C_31_12
BEGIN_
ताम् अपश्यत् बल आकीर्णाम् हरिराज महापुरीम् |
दुर्गाम् इक्ष्वाकु शार्दूलः किष्किंधाम् गिरि संकटे || ४-३१-१६_END
BEGIN_
Entrenched among mountains, impregnated with vanara-army is the magnificent citadel
of the king of monkeys, and the tigerly-Ikshvaku, Lakshmana, has seen such an impassable city,
namely Kishkindha. [4-31-16]_END

B_4_C_30_19
BEGIN_
अथ पद्म पलाश अक्षीम् मैथिलीम् अनुचिन्तयन् |
उवाच लक्ष्मणम् रामो मुखेन परिशुष्यता || ४-३०-२१_END
BEGIN_
On thinking about the fruit of his mammoth task, namely that lotus-petal-eyed
Maithili, thereafter Rama spoke to Lakshmana with a dried-up face. [4-30-21]_END

B_4_C_32_8
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवेण एवम् उक्ते तु हनुमान् हरि पुंगवः |उवाच स्वेन तर्केण मध्ये वानर मंत्रिणाम् || ४-३२-९_END
BEGIN_
While Sugreeva is saying that way, the eminent-monkey Hanuma spoke with a dint of his own expediency, from among 
the Vanara ministers. [4-32-9]_END

B_4_C_33_1
BEGIN_
द्वारस्था हरयः तत्र महाकाया महाबलाः |बभूवुः लक्ष्मणम् दृष्ट्वा सर्वे प्रांजलयः स्थिताः || ४-३३-२_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Lakshmana the huge bodied and highly mighty monkeys available at the gateway stood back with their palms 
adjoined in supplication. [4-33-2]_END

B_4_C_31_13
BEGIN_
रोषात् प्रस्फुरमाण ओष्ठः सुग्रीवम् प्रति लक्ष्मणः |
ददर्श वानरान् भीमान् किष्किंधाया बहिः चरान् || ४-३१-१७_END
BEGIN_
While his lips are quivering owing to rancour towards Sugreeva, Lakshmana saw
formidable Vaanara-s at the outposts of Kishkindha. [4-31-17]_END

B_4_C_30_20
BEGIN_
तर्पयित्वा सहस्राक्षः सलिलेन वसुंधराम् |
निर्वर्तयित्वा सस्यानि कृत कर्मा व्यवस्थितः || ४-३०-२२_END
BEGIN_
"On satisfying mother earth with rainwater and on effectuating the crops on earth,
the Thousand-eyed Indra is complacent as his task is effectuated, whereas my task is yet to take
off. [4-30-22]_END

B_4_C_33_2
BEGIN_
निःश्वसन्तम् तु तम् दृष्ट्वा क्रुद्धम् दशरथ आत्मजम् |बभूवुः हरयः त्रस्ता न च एनम् पर्यवारयन् || ४-३३-३_END
BEGIN_
But on seeing at the fumingly infuriated son of Dasharatha, all the monkeys have become scared and they did not 
even gather around him. [4-33-3]_END

B_4_C_32_9
BEGIN_
सर्वथा न एतद् आश्चर्यम् यत् त्वम् हरिगणेश्वर |न विस्मरसि सुस्निग्धम् उपकारम् कृतम् शुभम् || ४-३२-१०_END
BEGIN_
"In any case, it is not astonishing to say, oh, king of monkey troops, that you with a deep regard have not forgotten 
the advantageous help rendered to you, since it is natural for you. [4-32-10]_END

B_4_C_31_14
BEGIN_
तम् दृष्ट्वा वानराः सर्वे लक्ष्मणम् पुरुषर्षभम्
शैल शृंगाणि शतशः प्रवृद्धाम् च महीरुहान् |
जगृहुः कुंजर प्रख्या वानराः पर्वत अंतरे || ४-३१-१८_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the most notable one among men, Lakshmana all of the elephantine vanara-s
available in the gorges of mountain have grabbed hundreds of mountain-crests and gigantic trees,
and they are at the ready. [4-31-18]_END

B_4_C_32_10
BEGIN_
राघवेण तु वीरेण भयम् उत्सृज्य दूरतः |त्वत् प्रिय अर्थम् हतो वाली शक्र तुल्य पराक्रमः || ४-३२-११_END
BEGIN_
"On his part Raghava tossed off his fear distantly and eliminated Vali, whose valour equals that of Indra, only 
to fulfil your cherish. [4-32-11]_END

B_4_C_33_3
BEGIN_
स तम् रत्नमयीम् दिव्याम् श्रीमान् पुष्पित काननाम् |रम्याम् रत्न समाकीर्णाम् ददर्श महतीम् गुहाम् || ४-३३-४_END
BEGIN_
Glorious Lakshmana has seen the splendid Kishkindha which is a colossal cave crafted with jewels, replete with 
flowered orchards and richly rife with gemlike-objects d'art. [4-33-4]_END

B_4_C_30_21
BEGIN_
दीर्घ गंभीर निर्घोषाः शैल द्रुम पुरोगमाः |
विसृज्य सलिलम् मेघाः परिश्रांता नृप आत्मज || ४-३०-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Clouds roving on the tops of mountains and trees with their protracted and profound
peals have let the water loose and they are now retired, oh, prince, but tireless are rumbles and
grumbles in my heart, thus I cannot retire. [4-30-23]_END

B_4_C_31_15
BEGIN_
तान् गृहीत प्रहरणान् सर्वान् दृष्ट्वा तु लक्ष्मणः |
बभूव द्विगुणम् क्रुद्धो बहु इंधन इव अनलः || ४-३१-१९_END
BEGIN_
But on seeing all of them handling assaultive peaks and trees, Lakshmana's fury has
become twofold as with a fire to which much fuel is added. [4-31-19]_END

B_4_C_33_4
BEGIN_
हर्म्य प्रासाद संबाधाम् नाना रत्नोपशोभिताम् |सर्व काम फलैः वृक्षैः पुष्पितैः उपशोभिताम् || ४-३३-५_END
BEGIN_
Kishkindha is compacted with mansions and multi-storied buildings that are embellished with various precious stones, 
and it is enlivened with blossomed trees that bear fruit of every relish and of every season, and Lakshmana has 
seen such a Kishkindha. [4-33-5]_END

B_4_C_30_22
BEGIN_
नील उत्पल दल श्यामः श्यामी कृत्वा दिशो दश |
विमदा इव मातंगाः शान्त वेगाः पयो धराः || ४-३०-२४_END
BEGIN_
"On blackening ten quarters of earth blue-black clouds that looked like petals of
blue-lotuses are now quietened in their nimbleness like rut-less elephants. [4-30-24]_END

B_4_C_32_11
BEGIN_
सर्वथा प्रणयात् क्रुद्धो राघवो न अत्र संशयः |भ्रातरम् संप्रहितवान् लक्ष्मणम् लक्ष्मि वर्धनम् || ४-३२-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Anywise, by virtue of his friendliness with you Raghava must be annoyed, hence he must have expedited his brother 
Lakshmana, whose disposition in effect to is enhance prosperity. [4-32-12]_END

B_4_C_31_16
BEGIN_
तम् ते भयपरीत अंगाः ख्सुब्धम् दृष्ट्वा प्लवंगमाः |
काल मृत्यु युगांताअभम् शतशो विद्रुता दिशः || ४-३१-२०_END
BEGIN_
On seeing overexcited Lakshmana who is like the Time-god and the Epoch-Ender, troops
and troops of those fly-jumpers quickly fled away in all directions with scare coiling their
bodies. [4-31-20]_END

B_4_C_33_5
BEGIN_
देव गंधर्व पुत्रैः च वानरैः काम रूपिभिः |दिव्य माल्य अम्बर धारैः शोभिताम् प्रिय दर्शनैः || ४-३३-६_END
BEGIN_
That city is brightened with vanara-s who with their prepossessing appearances are attired in marvellous garlands 
and garments, and who can change their guise just by their wish, as they are the children of gods and gandharva-s, 
and Lakshmana has seen such a city. [4-33-6]_END

B_4_C_30_23
BEGIN_
जल गर्भा महा वेगाः कुटज अर्जुन गंधिनः |
चरित्वा विरताः सौम्य वृष्टि वाताः समुद्यताः || ४-३०-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Now pausing are the high-speeded rainy-winds, which once speedily swooped with
water in their wombs, and wafted the fragrance of Kutaja and Arjuna flowers. [4-30-25]_END

B_4_C_32_12
BEGIN_
त्वम् प्रमत्तो न जानीषे कालम् कलविदाम् वर |फुल्ल सप्त च्छद श्यामा प्रवृत्ता तु शरत् शिवा || ४-३२-१३_END
BEGIN_
"You have become ecstatic, oh, the best of the best timekeepers, hence you are unaware of the slippage of time, 
but the sedate and dark-green autumn on its part is underway unfolding dark-green leaves canopying seven-leaved 
banana plants. [4-32-13]_END

B_4_C_34_0
BEGIN_
तम् अप्रतिहतम् क्रुद्धम् प्रविष्टम् पुरुषर्षभम् |
सुग्रीवो लक्ष्मणम् दृष्ट्वा बभूव व्यथित इन्द्रियः || ४-३४-१_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the illustrious Lakshmana who entered unimpededly and infuriately,
Sugreeva became one with agitated senses. [4-34-1]_END

B_4_C_31_17
BEGIN_
ततः सुग्रीव भवनम् प्रविश्य हरिपुंगवाः |
क्रोधम् आगमनम् चैव लक्ष्मणस्य न्यवेदयन् || ४-३१-२१_END
BEGIN_
Then on entering the palace of Sugreeva, some best ones among monkeys have appraised
about the arrival of Lakshmana, and even about his fury. [4-31-21]_END

B_4_C_30_24
BEGIN_
घनानाम् वारणानाम् च मयूराणाम् च लक्ष्मण |
नादः प्रस्रवणानाम् च प्रशान्तः सहसा अनघ || ४-३०-२६_END
BEGIN_
"The rales of clouds, elephants, peacocks, and oh, merited Lakshmana, of the
freshets too, are suddenly quietened. [4-30-26]_END

B_4_C_33_6
BEGIN_
चन्दन अगरु पद्मानाम् गन्धैः सुरभि गन्धिताम् |मैरेयाणाम् मधूनाम् च सम्मोदित महा पथाम् || ४-३३-७_END
BEGIN_
She is perfumed with the fragrances that are pleasing the sense of smell like sandal-scent, true-aloe-scent, and 
the scents of lotuses, and her wide avenues are highly exhilarated with the bouquet of flower-liquors and grape-wines, 
and Lakshmana has seen such a sweet-scanted city Kishkindha. [4-33-7]_END

B_4_C_32_13
BEGIN_
निर्मल ग्रह नक्षत्रा द्यौः प्रनष्ट बलाहका |प्रसन्नाः च दिशः सर्वाः सरितः च सरांसि च || ४-३२-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Clear is the sky with its planets and stars as clouds have vanished on it, even all the ten directions are clear, 
and the rivers and lakes too are equable. [4-32-14]_END

B_4_C_34_1
BEGIN_
क्रुद्धम् निःश्वसमानम् तम् प्रदीप्तम् इव तेजसा |
भ्रातुर् व्यसन संतप्तम् दृष्ट्वा दशरथ आत्मजम् || ४-३४-२
उत्पपात हरिश्रेष्ठो हित्वा सौवर्णम् आसनम् |
महान् महेन्द्रस्य यथा स्वलंकृत इव ध्वजः || ४-३४-३_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Lakshmana, the son of Dasharatha, who is exasperated and exhaling heavily,
and who searing in the anguish of his brother is flaring up like a firestorm, Sugreeva hopped up
from his golden seat and tottered like the highly decorated flagstaff of Indra, which will be
wobbly before it is thrown to ground after the ritual. [4-34-2, 3]_END

B_4_C_31_18
BEGIN_
तारया सहितः कामी सक्तः कपिवृषः तदा |
न तेषाम् कपि वीराणाम् शुश्राव वचनम् तदा || ४-३१-२२_END
BEGIN_
At that time, he who is in a lustful mood, who is in the company of Lady Tara and
who is enmired in privacy, that foremost monkey Sugreeva is unheedful of the words of those bold
monkeys who brought the message. [4-31-22]_END

B_4_C_30_25
BEGIN_
अभिवृष्टा महा मेघैः निर्मलाः चित्र सानवः |
अनुलिप्ता इव आभान्ति गिरयः चन्द्र रश्मिभिः || ४-३०-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Scoured well by rains from colossal clouds those amusing mountain terraces are
grime-less and they shine forth as though enamelled with the moonbeams. [4-30-27]_END

B_4_C_33_7
BEGIN_
विंध्य मेरु गिरि प्रख्यैः प्रासादैः न एक भूमिभिः |ददर्श गिरि नद्यः च विमलाः तत्र राघवः || ४-३३-८_END
BEGIN_
In that city Lakshmana of Raghava dynasty has seen buildings that are not single-storied but multi-storied, semblable 
with Mt. Vindhya and Mt. Meru, and he even saw mountain-rapids with pure water. [4-33-8]_END

B_4_C_32_14
BEGIN_
प्राप्तम् उद्योग कालम् तु न अवैषि हरिपुंगव |त्वम् प्रमत्त इति व्यक्तम् लक्ष्मणो अयम् इह आगतः || ४-३२-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Because the time for campaigns has chanced, oh, the ablest monkey, and because you were very slumberous you have 
not got the drift of it, as such Lakshmana must have come here, and it is obvious. [4-32-15]_END

B_4_C_34_2
BEGIN_
उत्पतंतम् अनूत्पेतू रुमा प्रभृतयः स्त्रियः |
सुग्रीवम् गगने पूर्णम् चंद्रम् तारा गणा इव || ४-३४-४_END
BEGIN_
While Sugreeva is jumping up stumblingly, stumbled with him are Ruma and the other
females in tow, who are so far clinging to him, like the clusters of stars that spring up on the
emergence of full moon in sky. [4-34-4]_END

B_4_C_31_19
BEGIN_
ततः सचिव संदिष्टा हरयो रोमहर्षणाः |
गिरि कुंजर मेघ आभा नगर्या निर्ययुः तदा || ४-३१-२३_END
BEGIN_
Then, as directed by ministers of Kishkindha in order to figure out the mood of
Lakshmana, some of the elephantine monkeys who are frightening just by their appearance, who in
sheen are similar to mountains and dark-clouds have gone out of the city. [4-31-23]_END

B_4_C_30_26
BEGIN_
शाखासु सप्त च्छद पादपानाम्
प्रभासु तार अर्क निशा कराणाम् |
लीलासु चैव उत्तम वारणानाम्
श्रियम् विभज्य अद्य शरत् प्रवृत्ता || ४-३०-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Presently autumn has shown itself dividing its charm on the branches of
seven-leaved banana plants, on the stars, sun and moon, and also on those best elephants that are
rollicking. [4-30-28]_END

B_4_C_33_8
BEGIN_
अंगदस्य गृहम् रम्यम् मैन्दस्य द्विविदस्य च |गवयस्य गवाक्षस्य गजस्य शरभस्य च || ४-३३-९विद्युन्मालेः च संपातेः 
सूर्याक्षस्य हनूमतः |वीरबाहोः सुबाहोः च नलस्य च महात्मनः || ४-३३-१०कुमुदस्य सुषेणस्य तार जाम्बवतोः तथा 
|दधिवक्त्रस्य नीलस्य सुपाटल सुनेत्रयोः || ४-३३-११एतेषाम् कपि मुख्यानाम् राज मार्गे महात्मनाम् |ददर्श 
गृह मुख्यानि महासाराणि लक्ष्मणः || ४-३३-१२_END
BEGIN_
On the kings-way Lakshmana has seen the exquisite mansion of Angada, likewise the lavish mansions of distinction 
pertaining to the other vanara chiefs, namely Dvivida, Gavaya, Gavaaksha, Gaja, and Sharabha, Vidyunmaali, Sampaati, 
Suuryaaksha, Hanuma, and that of the noble-souled Nala, and even those of Virabaahu, Subaahu, Kumuda, Sushena, 
Lt. Taara, Jambavanta, Dadhivaktra, Niila, Supaatala, and that of Sunetra. [4-33-9, 10, 11, 12]_END

B_4_C_32_15
BEGIN_
आर्तस्य हृत दारस्य परुषम् पुरुष अन्तरात् |वचनम् मर्षणीयम् ते राघवस्य महात्मनः || ४-३२-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Raghava's bitter words are endurable by you as he is primarily an anguished person, further he is the one whose 
is wife is abducted, and furthermore he is magnanimous in giving kingdom to you, besides, he is reproachful through 
another person, namely Lakshmana. [4-32-16]_END

B_4_C_34_3
BEGIN_
संरक्त नयनः श्रीमान् संचचार कृतांजलिः |
बभूव अवस्थितः तत्र कल्प वृक्षो महान् इव || ४-३४-५_END
BEGIN_
That fortunate Sugreeva whose eyes are bloodshot with drinking flurried towards
Lakshmana adjoining palms in supplication, and became standstill at his nearby, like a lofty
kalpa vriksha wish-fulfilling tree. [4-34-5]_END

B_4_C_31_20
BEGIN_
नख दंष्ट्र आयुधा सर्वे वीराः विकृत दर्शनाः |
सर्वे शार्दूल दर्पाः च सर्वे च विकृत आननाः || ४-३१-२४_END
BEGIN_
All of those brave vanara-s are armed with their own teeth and nails, all are with
tigerish pride, all are hideous in look and horrendous by their faces. [4-31-24]_END

B_4_C_30_27
BEGIN_
संप्रति अनेक आश्रय चित्र शोभा
लक्ष्मीः शरत् काल गुण उपपन्ना |
सूर्य अग्र हस्त प्रतिबोधितेषु
पद्माकरेषु अभ्यधिकम् विभाति || ४-३०-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Fascinatingly glistening grandeur of autumn that is derived from the merits of the
season and that resorts to many objects of the season, is now splendidly shining in the lotus lakes
that are flourished by the rays of dawning sun. [4-30-29]_END

B_4_C_33_9
BEGIN_
पाण्डुर अभ्र प्रकाशानि गन्ध माल्य युतानि च |प्रभूत धन धान्यानि स्त्री रत्नैः शोभितानि च || ४-३३-१३_END
BEGIN_
Those mansions that glitter like silver-clouds, fragrant with scents and festooned with flower-tassels, replete 
with wealth and food grains, are beaming with gemlike female-vanara-s, and Lakshmana saw them on his way. [4-33-13]_END

B_4_C_32_16
BEGIN_
कृत अपराधस्य हि ते न अन्यत् पश्यामि अहम् क्षमम् |अंतरेण अंजलिम् बद्ध्वा लक्ष्मणस्य प्रसादनात् || ४-३२-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed, I do not foresee any other appropriate means for you, as a blunder is committed by you, other than seeking 
Lakshmana's pardon duly adjoining your palms. [4-32-17]_END

B_4_C_34_4
BEGIN_
रुमा द्वितीयम् सुग्रीवम् नारी मध्य गतम् स्थितम् |
अब्रवीत् लक्ष्मणः क्रुद्धः स तारम् शशिनम् यथा || ४-३४-६_END
BEGIN_
Infuriate Lakshmana spoke to Sugreeva who like the star clustered moon is standing
with his wife Ruma at his side amid other vanara females. [4-34-6]_END

B_4_C_31_21
BEGIN_
दश नाग बलाः केचित् केचित् दश गुणोत्तराः |
केचित् नाग सहस्रस्य बभूवुः तुल्य वर्चसः || ४-३१-२५_END
BEGIN_
Some of those vanara-s are with the might of ten elephants, some ten times more, and
some with vigour matching that of a thousand elephants. [4-31-25]_END

B_4_C_30_28
BEGIN_
सप्त च्छदानाम् कुसुमोप गंधी
षट् पाद वृन्दैः अनुगीयमानः |
मत्त द्विपानाम् पवन अनुसारी
दर्पम् विनेष्यन् अधिकम् विभाति || ४-३०-३०_END
BEGIN_
"The breeze is wafting the fragrance of flowers of seven-leaved banana plants, and
the swarms of honeybees that are singing in accompaniment to the rustle of breeze are tagging along
that breeze for its fragrance, and because that breeze is breezing unceasingly, that alone is
fetching the pride of rut for the already rutted elephants, and thus this autumnal season is highly
glistening. [4-30-30]_END

B_4_C_33_10
BEGIN_
पाण्डुरेण तु शैलेन परिक्षिप्तम् दुरासदम् |वानरेन्द्र गृहम् रम्यम् महेन्द्र सदन उपमम् || ४-३३-१४शुल्कैः 
प्रासाद शिखरैः कैलास शिखर उपमैः |सर्व काम फलैः वृक्षैः पुष्पितैः उपशोभितम् || ४-३३-१५महेन्द्र दत्तैः श्रीमद्भिः 
नील जीमूत संनिभैः |दिव्य पुष्प फलैः वृक्षैः शीत च्छायैः मनोरमैः || ४-३३-१६हरिभिः संवृत द्वारम् बलिभिः 
शस्त्र पाणिभिः |दिव्य माल्य आवृतम् शुभ्रम् तप्त कांचन तोरणम् || ४-३३-१७सुग्रीवस्य गृहम् रम्यम् प्रविवेश 
महाबलः |अवार्यमाणः सौमित्रिः महाअभ्रम् इव भास्करः || ४-३३-१८_END
BEGIN_
The grand palace of the king of monkeys, Sugreeva, which vies with the palace of Indra is inaccessibly immured 
in a whitely mountain. The spires of that palace are similar to the peaks of Mt. Kailash and it is shining forth 
with fully blossomed trees yielding fruits that can fulfil every relish of everyone. Some more providential and 
heart-pleasing trees available there are the endowment of Indra, which in shine are equal to blackish rainy-clouds, 
yielding divine flowers and fruits, and casting cool shades. Excellent garlands are strung round the palace and 
robust monkeys wielding weapons are screening its gateways, while its main archway cast in refined golden is splendorous. 
And the very bold Lakshmana unimpededly entered such a fascinating palace of Sugreeva, as with the sun entering 
a colossal cloud. [4-33-14, 15, 16, 17, 18]_END

B_4_C_34_5
BEGIN_
सत्त्व अभिजन संपन्नः स अनुक्रोशो जितेन्द्रियः |
कृतज्ञः सत्य वादी च राजा लोके महीयते || ४-३४-७_END
BEGIN_
"One who is dynamic, abounding with best troopers, sympathetic, senses conquered, a
faithful one and an advocate of truth, he alone thrives as a king in the world. [4-34-7]_END

B_4_C_32_17
BEGIN_
नियुक्तैः मंत्रिभिः वाच्यो अवश्यम् पार्थिवो हितम् |इत एव भयम् त्यक्त्वा ब्रवीमि अवधृतम् वचः || ४-३२-१८_END
BEGIN_
"A king is to be advised beneficially and unhesitatingly by the minister designates, that is why I am speaking 
what I hold fast discarding fear. [4-32-18]_END

B_4_C_31_22
BEGIN_
ततः तैः कपिभिर् व्याप्ताम् द्रुम हस्तैर् महाबलैः |
अपश्यत् लक्ष्मणः क्रुद्धः किष्किंधाम् ताम् दुरासदम् || ४-३१-२६_END
BEGIN_
Infuriated Lakshmana has then seen Kishkindha, an unassailable city, as those
great-mighty monkeys flaunting trees are spreading throughout it. [4-31-26]_END

B_4_C_30_29
BEGIN_
अभ्यागतैः चारु विशाल पक्षैः
सरः प्रियैः पद्म रजो अवकीर्णैः |
महा नदीनाम् पुलिन उपयातैः
क्रीडन्ति हंसाः सह चक्रवाकैः || ४-३०-३१_END
BEGIN_
"Broad and cute winged Cakravaka birds that are fond of lakes and that have pollen
of lotuses overspread on them have come to the sand-dunes of vast rivers, and with them that have
come nigh the swans are larking. [4-30-31]_END

B_4_C_33_11
BEGIN_
स सप्त कक्ष्या धर्मात्मा यान आसन समावृताः |प्रविश्य सुमहत् गुप्तम् ददर्श अंतःपुरम् महत् || ४-३३-१९हैम 
राजत पर्यन्कैः बहुभिः च वर आसनैः |महा अर्ह आस्तरण उपेतैः तत्र तत्र समावृतम् || ४-३३-२०_END
BEGIN_
Passing through a set of seven courtyards in which carriers like palanquins, sedans, and even settees are spread 
over, that duty-bound Lakshmana has seen the highly protected and prodigious palace-chambers of Sugreeva, which 
is stuffed here and there with numerous golden and silver love-beds and divans on which highly valuable upholstery 
is provided. [4-33-19, 20]_END

B_4_C_34_6
BEGIN_
यस्तु राजा स्थितो अधर्मे मित्राणाम् उपकारिणाम् |
मिथ्या प्रतिज्ञाम् कुरुते को नृशंस तरः ततः || ४-३४-८_END
BEGIN_
"He who is enthroned as a king but anchored himself to dishonesty and makes fake
assurances to helpful friends, who can be more ruthless than him? [4-34-8]_END

B_4_C_32_18
BEGIN_
अभिक्रुद्धः समर्थो हि चापम् उद्यम्य राघवः |स देव असुर गंधर्वम् वशे स्थापयितुम् जगत् || ४-३२-१९_END
BEGIN_
"If Raghava is highly infuriated he is capable to keep the world under his control along with gods, demons, gandharva-s 
just on hitching up his bow, isn't it! [4-32-19]_END

B_4_C_31_23
BEGIN_
ततः ते हरयः सर्वे प्राकार परिख अंतरात् |
निष्क्रम्य उदग्र सत्त्वाः तु तस्थुर् आविष्कृतम् तदा || ४-३१-२७_END
BEGIN_
All of those monkeys then exiting from the inside of the compound-wall of the castle
and coming underneath of the iron-latches of the castle's gateway, they became visible and stood up
to Lakshmana with their ebullient might. [4-31-27]_END

B_4_C_33_12
BEGIN_
प्रविशन् एव सततम् शुश्राव मधुर स्वनम् |तंत्री गीत समाकीर्णम् सम ताल पदाक्षरम् || ४-३३-२१_END
BEGIN_
On his very entry Lakshmana heard the ongoing melodious tunes commixed with lyrics and strains of string-instruments, 
and all are unvarying in cadence, wording and lettering._END

B_4_C_30_30
BEGIN_
मद प्रगल्भेषु च वारिणेषु
गवाम् समूहेषु च दर्पितेषु |
प्रसन्न तोयासु च निम्न गासु
विभाति लक्ष्मीः बहुधा विभक्ता || ४-३०-३२_END
BEGIN_
"Divided variously the autumnal glory is shining forth among the overbearingly
ruttish elephants that are trumpeting, among the herds of haughty bulls bellowing, and among the
limpid waters that are murmuringly slopping down. [4-30-32]_END

B_4_C_34_7
BEGIN_
शतम् अश्व अनृते हन्ति सहस्रम् तु गव अनृते |
आत्मानम् स्व जनम् हन्ति पुरुषः पुरुष अनृते || ४-३४-९_END
BEGIN_
"A person gets attached to the sin of killing of a hundred of his manes, deified
souls of his own ancestors, if he promises to gift one horse but fails to do so, and in promising
to gift one cow but failing in it he gets the sin of killing a thousand manes, and if he promises
to a person to do the needful help and fails in rendering that help, then he gets the sin of
suicide along with the sin of killing his own kith and kin. [4-34-9]_END

B_4_C_32_19
BEGIN_
न स क्षमः कोपयितुम् यः प्रसाद्य पुनर् भवेत् |पूर्व उपकारम् स्मरता कृतज्ञेन विशेषतः || ४-३२-२०_END
BEGIN_
"It becomes unseemly to infuriate him who is to be placated time and again, especially when remembering his earlier 
beneficence to you and when you are beholden to him. [4-32-20]_END

B_4_C_31_24
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवस्य प्रमादम् च पूर्वजस्य अर्थम् आत्मवान् |
दृष्ट्वा कोप वशम् वीरः पुनर् एव जगाम सः || ४-३१-२८_END
BEGIN_
On envisaging Sugreeva's blunder and of his elder-brother's expediency, that
sensible one and fury restrained Lakshmana, again went into the restraint of fury on seeing the
monkeys. [4-31-28]_END

B_4_C_30_31
BEGIN_
नभः समीक्ष्या अंबु धरैः विमुक्तम्
विमुक्त बर्ह आभरणा वनेषु |
प्रियासु अरक्ता विनिवृत्त शोभा
गत उत्सवा ध्यान परा मयूराः || ४-३०-३३_END
BEGIN_
"Exploring the sky well which is now set free by the clouds, the peacocks are
setting their ornamental plumaged-tails free, and they are even divested of their dear peahens as
they are uninterested in them, and thus divested of their festivity those peacocks are abiding in
their muse. [4-30-33]_END

B_4_C_33_13
BEGIN_
बह्वीः च विविध आकारा रूप यौवन गर्विताः |स्त्रियः सुग्रीव भवने ददर्श स महाबलः || ४-३३-२२_END
BEGIN_
And the great-mighty Lakshmana has seen many females in Sugreeva's palace with diverse features and prideful of 
their beauty and youth. [4-33-22]_END

B_4_C_34_8
BEGIN_
पूर्वम् कृतार्थो मित्राणाम् न तत् प्रति करोति यः |
कृतघ्नः सर्व भूतानाम् स वध्यः प्लवगेश्वर || ४-३४-१०_END
BEGIN_
"He who gets his means fulfilled earlier through his friends but does not requite
them, oh, king of monkeys, such a treacherous one is eliminable for all beings. [4-34-10]_END

B_4_C_32_20
BEGIN_
तस्य मूर्ध्ना प्रणम्य त्वम् स पुत्रः स सुहृत् जनः |राजन् तिष्ठ स्व समये भर्तुः भार्या इव तत् वशे || ४-३२-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Prostrate yourself before him along with your son, friends and relatives to pay deference, oh, king, and abide 
by your own accord you made with him remaining under his auspices, like a wife abiding in the care of her husband. 
[4-32-21]_END

B_4_C_31_25
BEGIN_
स दीर्घ उष्ण महा उच्छ्वासः कोप संरक्त लोचनः |
बभूव नर शार्दूल स धूम इव पावकः || ४-३१-२९_END
BEGIN_
With his long, fiery, and endless exhales and eyes bloodshot in fury, that
tigerly-man Lakshmana is like a fuming fire. [4-31-29]_END

B_4_C_35_0
BEGIN_
तथा ब्रुवाणम् सौमित्रिम् प्रदीप्तम् इव तेजसा |अब्रवीत् लक्ष्मणम् तारा तारा अधिप निभ आनना || ४-३५-१_END
BEGIN_
Tara with her visage that shines like the Lord of Stars, namely the Moon, then spoke to the son of queen Sumitra, 
namely Lakshmana, who while he is speaking is as though blazing with his own resplendence. [4-35-1]_END

B_4_C_30_32
BEGIN_
मनोज्ञ गन्धैः प्रियकैः अनल्पैः
पुष्प अति भार अवनत अग्र शाखैः |
सुवर्ण गौरैः नयन अभिरामैः
उद्योतितान् इव वन अन्तराणि || ४-३०-३४_END
BEGIN_
"Umpteen are those Priyaka trees with their pleasingly fragrant flowers, the apices
of the boughs of those trees are sagging down by their much weighty flowers-bunches, and
eye-delighting is the golden-yellow hue of those flowers, and with them the interiors of these
forests look as though illuminated, lit with golden lamps. [4-30-34]_END

B_4_C_33_14
BEGIN_
दृष्ट्वा अभिजन संपन्नाः तत्र माल्य कृत स्रजः |वर माल्य कृत व्यग्रा भूषण उत्तम भूषिताः || ४-३३-२३न अतृप्तान् 
न अति च व्यग्रान् न अनुदात्त परिच्छदान् |सुग्रीव अनुचरान् च अपि लक्षयामास लक्ष्मणः || ४-३३-२४_END
BEGIN_
On observing the females of a worthy bloodline in the palace of Sugreeva, who are wearing garlands of worthily 
flowers, engrossed in making worthwhile flower-tassels and even adorned with worthiest jewellery, he also made 
a mark of the chambermaids. None of them is overawed, overstrained, and everyone is over-embellished in dressiness. 
[4-33-23, 24]_END

B_4_C_32_21
BEGIN_
न राम रामानुज शासनम् त्वयाकपीन्द्र युक्तम् मनसा अपि अपोहितुम् |मनो हि ते ज्ञास्यति मानुषम् बलम्स राघवस्य 
अस्य सुरेन्द्र वर्चसः || ४-३२-२२_END
BEGIN_
"It will be unseemly to fend off the ruling of Rama, or of his brother Lakshmana even in your imagination, oh, 
king of monkeys, as your heart is aware of the humanly tenacity of that Rama, whose resplendence vies with that 
of Indra, and who is associated with selfsame Lakshmana, isn't it." Thus Hanuma spoke to Sugreeva. [4-32-22]_END

B_4_C_34_9
BEGIN_
गीतो अयम् ब्रह्मणा श्लोकः सर्व लोक नमस्कृतः |
दृष्ट्वा कृतघ्नम् क्रुद्धेन तम् निबोध प्लवम्गम || ४-३४-११_END
BEGIN_
"On seeing such perfidious soul, oh, fly-jumper, Brahma irefully declared this verse
which is reverenced by all the worlds, you too may know it. [4-34-11]_END

B_4_C_31_26
BEGIN_
बाण शल्य स्फुरत् जिह्वः सायक आसन भोगवान् |
स्व तेजो विष संघातः पंच आस्य इव पन्नगः || ४-३१-३०_END
BEGIN_
Lakshmana has become identical to a five-faced serpent as his curvi-bow looked like
the curvi-hood of a serpent, arrowheads looked like the poking tongues of the serpent, and as his
own fervency is proliferating as that serpent's venom. [4-31-30]_END

B_4_C_35_1
BEGIN_
न एवम् लक्ष्मण वक्तव्यो न अयम् परुषम् अर्हति |हरीणाम् ईश्वरः श्रोतुम् तव वक्त्रात् विशेषतः || ४-३५-२_END
BEGIN_
