"Let not this king of monkeys be addressed in this way, oh, Lakshmana, and he is not warranted to listen such 
tongue-lashing, especially from your tongue. [4-35-2]_END

B_4_C_30_33
BEGIN_
प्रिय अन्वितानाम् नलिनी प्रियाणाम्
वन प्रियाणाम् कुसुम उद्धतानाम् |
मद उत्कटानाम् मद लालसानाम्
गज उत्तमानम् गतयो अद्य मन्दाः || ४-३०-३५_END
BEGIN_
"On scenting the fragrance of the seven-leaved banana plants, the ruttish lather of
those best elephants that have a fond for forests and lotus-lakes has started to flow on their
temples, thus they are indulgent in rut and their strides are slackening while they are moving
along with their beloved female elephants. [4-30-35]_END

B_4_C_33_15
BEGIN_
कूजितम् नूपुराणाम् च कंचनीम् निःस्वनम् तथा |स निशम्य ततः श्रीमान् सौमित्रिः लज्जितो अभवत् || ४-३३-२५_END
BEGIN_
Thereafter on hearing the chimes of silver-anklets and tintinnabulations of golden cinctures of female vanara-s 
that refulgent Saumitri is embarrassed to proceed further. [4-33-25]_END

B_4_C_34_10
BEGIN_
गो घ्ने च एव सुरापे च चौरे भग्न व्रते तथा |
निष्कृतिर् विहिता सद्भिः कृतघ्ने न अस्ति निष्कृतिः || ४-३४-१२_END
BEGIN_
" 'The savants have ordained atonement for slayers of cows, for drinkers of liquors,
thus for thieves and infringers of solemnity, but no atonement is available to a treacherous
person. [4-34-12]_END

B_4_C_31_27
BEGIN_
तम् दीप्तम् इव कालाग्निम् नागेन्द्रम् इव कोपितम् |
समासाद्य अंगदः त्रासात् विषादम् अगमत् परम् || ४-३१-३१_END
BEGIN_
Angada succumbing to high despair caused by the scare neared Lakshmana who is aglow
like the Fire of Perdition and like aadi seSa, the Thousand-hooded
King of Serpents, who is perforce infuriated. [4-31-31]_END

B_4_C_35_2
BEGIN_
न एव अकृतज्ञः सुग्रीवो न शठो न अपि दारुणः |न एव अनृत कथो वीर न जिह्मः च कपीश्वरः || ४-३५-३_END
BEGIN_
"Sugreeva is not an unthankful one, oh, brave Lakshmana, a treacherous one - no; a flagitious one - no; an utterer 
of untruth - no; a duplicitous one, no, this king of monkeys is not even that. [4-35-3]_END

B_4_C_30_34
BEGIN_
व्यक्तम् नभः शस्त्र विधौत वर्णम्
कृश प्रवाहानि नदी जलानि |
कह्लार शिताः पवनाः प्रवान्ति
तमो विमुक्ताः च दिशः प्रकाशाः || ४-३०-३६_END
BEGIN_
"The sky is clear as with the tinge of just whetted weapon, lessened are the flows
of river-waters, breeze is chilly while wafting the chillness of red-lotuses, and all the
directions released from the darkness are looking bright. [4-30-36]_END

B_4_C_33_16
BEGIN_
रोष वेग प्रकुपितः श्रुत्वा च आभरण स्वनम् |चकार ज्या स्वनम् वीरो दिशः शब्देन पूरयन् || ४-३३-२६_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the tinkles of the jewellery of female vanara-s valiant Lakshmana is highly provoked with an instantaneous 
bitterness, and he twitched bowstring as though to fill all the points of compass with twanging. [4-33-26]_END

B_4_C_34_11
BEGIN_
अनार्य त्वम् कृतघ्नः च मिथ्या वादी च वानर |
पूर्वम् कृतार्थो रामस्य न तत् प्रतिकरोषि यत् || ४-३४-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Vanara, firstly you have got your purpose fulfilled and by that reason you are
not reciprocating help to Rama, thereby you are an uncultured and unfriendly one, and illusive is
your word of honour. [4-34-13]_END

B_4_C_31_28
BEGIN_
सो अंगदम् रोष ताम्राक्षः संदिदेश महायशाः |
सुग्रीवः कथ्यताम् वत्स मम आगमनम् इति उत || ४-३१-३२_END
BEGIN_
With his eyes reddened in rancour that highly adorable Lakshmana sent a word through
Angada, saying "oh, boy, let Sugreeva be informed about my arrival," and said this way.
[4-31-32]_END

B_4_C_35_3
BEGIN_
उपकारम् कृतम् वीरो न अपि अयम् विस्मृतः कपिः |रामेण वीर सुग्रीवो यत् अन्यैः दुष्करम् रणे || ४-३५-४_END
BEGIN_
"Although he is a monkey this Sugreeva has not dismissed from his mind even the favour Rama has done in his respect, 
oh, valiant Lakshmana, which in combat is impractical for others. [4-35-4]_END

B_4_C_33_17
BEGIN_
चारित्रेण महाबाहुः अपकृष्टः स लक्ष्मनः |तस्थौ एकांतम् आश्रित्य राम शोक समन्वितः || ४-३३-२७_END
BEGIN_
His decent conduct hauling him down dextrous Lakshmana stood aside contingent on isolation, and alongside his 
heartfelt anguish of Rama. [4-33-27]_END

B_4_C_30_35
BEGIN_
सूर्य आतप क्रामण नष्ट पंका
भूमिः चिर उद्घाटित सांद्र रेणुः |
अन्योन्य वैरेण समायुतानाम्
उद्योग कालो अद्य नर अधिपानाम् || ४-३०-३७_END
BEGIN_
"Overcome by the sun's heat dried out is the sludge, at last the earth is dense with
the up-heaved dust, and for the lords of people who have mutual animosity this is the time to
foregather their forces to strive against one another. [4-30-37]_END

B_4_C_34_12
BEGIN_
ननु नाम कृतार्थेन त्वया रामस्य वानर |
सीताया मार्गणे यत्नः कर्तव्यः कृतम् इच्छता || ४-३४-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Vanara, you achieved your means through Rama, and Rama is wishing for his
endeavour through you, and I wonder whether the search for Seetha is not your duty? [4-34-14]_END

B_4_C_31_29
BEGIN_
एष रामानुजः प्राप्तः त्वत् सकाशम् अरिन्दमः |
भ्रातुर् व्यसन संतप्तो द्वारि तिष्ठति लक्ष्मणः || ४-३१-३३
तस्य वाक्यम् यदि रुचिः क्रियताम् साधु वानरः |
इति उक्त्वा शीघ्रम् आगच्छ वत्स वाक्यम् अरिन्दम || ४-३१-३४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, enemy-destroyer Angada, oh, boy, you may say these words to Sugreeva, 'oh,
enemy-destroyer Sugreeva, distressed by the distress of his brother this Lakshmana has arrived in
your presence and waiting at the door, oh, Sugreeva, the vanara, if you are interested it will be
apt of you to listen to his advise, either by coming here or inviting him inside...' saying so oh,
boy Angada, you comeback quickly." Thus Lakshmana spoke to Angada. [4-31-33, 34]_END

B_4_C_35_4
BEGIN_
राम प्रसादात् कीर्तिम् च कपि राज्यम् च शाश्वतम् |प्राप्तवान् इह सुग्रीवो रुमाम् माम् च परंतप || ४-३५-५_END
BEGIN_
"By the beneficence of Rama, oh, the enemy-scorcher Lakshmana, now Sugreeva is privileged with reputation, everlasting 
kingship of monkeys, more so with Ruma and me as well. [4-35-5]_END

B_4_C_30_36
BEGIN_
शरत् गुण आप्यायित रूप शोभाः
प्रहर्षित पांशु समुक्षित अंगाः |
मद उत्कटाः संप्रति युद्ध लुब्धा
वृषा गवाम् मध्य गता नदन्ति || ४-३०-३८_END
BEGIN_
"The nature of autumn has enhanced the features of bulls' bullishness and with their
bodies covered with dust and their vigour pepping them up they are ecstatic, and staying in the
midst of cowherd they are bellowing hankering for bullfights. [4-30-38]_END

B_4_C_33_18
BEGIN_
तेन चाप स्वनेन अथ सुग्रीवः प्लवगाधिपः |विज्ञाय आगमनम् त्रस्तः स चचाल वर आसनात् || ४-३३-२८_END
BEGIN_
With that twang of the bowstring the king of fly-jumpers Sugreeva is startled and jerked up from his exquisite 
seat as he ensured that Lakshmana has arrived. [4-33-28]_END

B_4_C_34_13
BEGIN_
स त्वम् ग्राम्येषु भोगेषु सक्तो मिथ्या प्रतिश्रवः |
न त्वाम् रामो विजानीते सर्पम् मण्डूक राविणम् || ४-३४-१५_END
BEGIN_
"An illusive promisor basking in churlish pleasures, such as you are, Rama has not
realised that you are a serpent with the croaking of a frog. [4-34-15]_END

B_4_C_31_30
BEGIN_
लक्ष्मणस्य वचः श्रुत्वा शोकाविष्टो अंगदो अब्रवीत् |
पितुः समीपम् आगम्य सौमित्रिः अयम् आगतः || ४-३१-३५_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of Lakshmana Angada is muffled up in grief, and on arriving in
the presence of his father Sugreeva he informed "Soumitri has come." [4-31-35]_END

B_4_C_35_5
BEGIN_
सुदुःख शयितः पूर्वम् प्राप्य इदम् सुखम् उत्तमम् |प्राप्त कालम् न जानीते विश्वामित्रो यथा मुनिः || ४-३५-६_END
BEGIN_
"Hitherto he has tolerated high anguish and on the attainment of this high comfort of kingship he has not oriented 
himself to the time-oriented actions as with saint Vishvamitra. [4-35-6]_END

B_4_C_30_37
BEGIN_
स मन्मध तीव्रतर अनुरागा
कुलान्विता मन्द गतिः करेणुः |
मदान्वितम् संपरिवार्य यान्तम्
वनेषु भर्तारम् अनुप्रयाति || ४-३०-३९_END
BEGIN_
"While a ruttish male elephant is going in the forest the slow paced she-elephant is
tagging along her male along with other elephants of her breed, and with an intensified attachment
and passion she is bumping and rubbing her husband. [4-30-39]_END

B_4_C_33_19
BEGIN_
अंगदेन यथा मह्यम् पुरस्तात् प्रतिवेदितम् |सुव्यक्तम् एष संप्रप्तः सौमित्रिः भ्रातृ वत्सलः || ४-३३-२९_END
BEGIN_
"As Angada indicated to me earlier, Saumitri, the votary of his brother, has come down on... it is very clear..." 
Thus Sugreeva exclaimed. [4-33-29]_END

B_4_C_34_14
BEGIN_
महाभागेन रामेण पापः करुण वेदिना |
हरीणाम् प्रापितो राज्यम् त्वम् दुरात्मा महात्मना || ४-३४-१६_END
BEGIN_
"By the highly prudent and compassionate Rama, you the sinner got the kingdom of
monkeys, and it is a gain of an evil-soul from a noble-soul. [4-34-16]_END

B_4_C_31_31
BEGIN_
अथ अंगदः तस्य सुतीव्र वाचा
संभ्रांत भावः परिदीन वक्त्रः |
निर्गत्य पूर्वम् नृपतेः तरस्वी
ततो रुमायाः चरणौ ववन्दे || ४-३१-३६_END
BEGIN_
Bewildered in his perception at the very sharp words of Lakshmana, mighty Angada
then has gone to the palace assuming a very sad face, and there he firstly saluted the feet of his
father Sugreeva and then at the feet of Ruma, wife of Sugreeva. [4-31-36]_END

B_4_C_36_0
BEGIN_
इति उक्तः तारया वाक्यम् प्रश्रितम् धर्म संहितम् |
मृदु स्वभावः सौमित्रिः प्रतिजग्राह तत् वचः || ४-३६-१_END
BEGIN_
In that way when Tara has submissively argued with words containing probity,
Saumitri gave assent to her perspective as he is soft by his nature. [4-36-1]_END

B_4_C_35_6
BEGIN_
घृताच्याम् किल संसक्तो दश वर्षाणि लक्ष्मण |अहो अमन्यत धर्मात्मा विश्वामित्रो महामुनिः || ४-३५-७_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Lakshmana, that great-sage Vishvamitra clinging together with Ghritaachi, an angelic apsara, for a period 
of ten years, forsooth that virtue-souled sage regarded that period as one day. [4-35-7]_END

B_4_C_30_38
BEGIN_
त्यक्त्वा वराणि आत्म विभूषणानि
बर्हाणि तीर उपगता नदीनाम् |
निर्भर्त्स्यमाना इव सार ओघैः
प्रयान्ति दीना विमना मयूराः || ४-३०-४०_END
BEGIN_
"The excellent plumaged-tails that form their individual ornaments of peacocks are
now cast out, and the plumeless peacocks on nearing the banks of rivers they look as if intimidated
by the Saarasa birds, thus they had to turn back despondently and dispiritedly. [4-30-40]_END

B_4_C_33_20
BEGIN_
अंगदेन समाख्यतो ज्या स्वनेन च वानरः |बुबुधे लक्ष्मणम् प्राप्तम् मुखम् च अस्य व्यशुष्यत || ४-३३-३०_END
BEGIN_
As has been apprised by Angada earlier, and even now by the twang of bowstring, that vanara Sugreeva made up his 
mind about Lakshmana's arrival, and he has become whey-faced. [4-33-30]_END

B_4_C_34_15
BEGIN_
कृतम् चेत् न अभिजानीषे राघवस्य महात्मनः |
सद्यः त्वम् निशितैर् बाणैर् हतो द्रक्ष्यसि वालिनम् || ४-३४-१७_END
BEGIN_
"If you do not recognise what the noble-souled Raghava has done to you, you will be
instantly killed with incisive arrows enabling you to see Vali. [4-34-17]_END

B_4_C_31_32
BEGIN_
संगृह्य पादौ पितुः उग्रतेजा
जग्राह मातुः पुनर् एव पादौ |
पादौ रुमायाः च निपीडयित्वा
निवेदयामास ततः तत् अर्थम् || ४-३१-३७_END
BEGIN_
Angada whose vitality is intense clinched himself to the feet of his father
Sugreeva, and later clung to the feet of his mother Tara, and he even clasped the feet of his
paternal-aunt Ruma, and latching on to the feet of his parents then he stated to appeal to them
about the message of Lakshmana. [4-31-37]_END

B_4_C_36_1
BEGIN_
तस्मिन् प्रतिगृहीते तु वाक्ये हरि गण ईश्वरः |
लक्ष्मणात् सुमहत् त्रासम् वस्त्रम् क्लिन्नम् इव अत्यजत् || ४-३६-२_END
BEGIN_
And when Lakshmana conceded to that argument of Tara, Sugreeva, the king of
monkey-troops, got rid of his highly intense scare of Lakshmana, like the riddance of a dampened
cloth. [4-36-2]_END

B_4_C_35_7
BEGIN_
स हि प्राप्तम् न जानीते कालम् कालविदाम् वरः |विश्वामित्रो महातेजाः किम् पुनर् यः पृथग् जनः || ४-३५-८_END
BEGIN_
"When he who is a best one among the time-knowers, that great-resplendent Sage Vishvamitra himself is not privy 
to the occasioned time for a good many years, why talking about a commoner again. [4-35-8]_END

B_4_C_30_39
BEGIN_
वित्रास्य कारण्डव चक्रवाकान् |
महा रवैः भिन्न कटा गजेन्द्राः |
सरस्सु बद्ध अंबुज भूषणेषु
विक्षोभ्य विक्षोभ्य जलम् पिबन्ति || ४-३०-४१_END
BEGIN_
"With their blaring trumpeting lordly elephants with slit temples are alarming
Karandava and Cakravaka birds abiding in lakes that are embellished with blooming lotuses, and
those elephants are drinking water after swishing and swashing the tranquillity of those lakes.
[4-30-41]_END

B_4_C_33_21
BEGIN_
ततः ताराम् हरि श्रेष्ठः सुग्रीवः प्रिय दर्शनाम् |उवाच हितम् अव्यग्र त्रास संभ्रांत मानसः || ४-३३-३१_END
BEGIN_
The chief of monkeys Sugreeva then staidly spoke this advantageous word to the exquisite lady Tara while his heart 
is bewildered with dismay. [4-33-31]_END

B_4_C_34_16
BEGIN_
न च संकुचितः पन्था येन वाली हतो गतः |
समये तिष्ठ सुग्रीव मा वालि पथम् अन्वगाः || ४-३४-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Sugreeva, abide by your commitment. The path by which slain Vali has gone that
path is not tapered off, as such do not tread Vali's path. [4-34-18]_END

B_4_C_31_33
BEGIN_
स निद्रा मद संवीतो वानरो न विबुद्धवान् |
बभूव मद मत्तः च मदनेन च मोहितः || ४-३१-३८_END
BEGIN_
Sugreeva, the vanara, who is bound up in drowsiness and dizziness could not
comprehend clearly what Angada is talking about, as he is benumbed with intoxication, and even
numbed down with the torpor of lustfulness. [4-31-38]_END

B_4_C_36_2
BEGIN_
ततः कण्ठ गतम् माल्यम् चित्रम् बहु गुणम् महत् |
चिच्छेद विमदः च आसीत् सुग्रीवो वानर ईश्वरः || ४-३६-३_END
BEGIN_
Sugreeva, the king of vanara-s, then ripped apart the superb garland which is so far
enwreathing his neck, and which has several strands according several gratifications, and he also
became sober as though the insobriety is ripped from his mind. [4-36-3]_END

B_4_C_35_8
BEGIN_
देह धर्म गतस्य अस्य परिश्रान्तस्य लक्ष्मण |अवितृप्तस्य कामेषु रामः क्षन्तुम् इह अर्हति || ४-३५-९_END
BEGIN_
"He who is overwrought and now undergoing natural bodily appetites, oh, Lakshmana, and who is overtired as he 
is absolutely discontent in the concupiscence, such as Sugreeva is, it will be apt of Rama to bear with him for 
a while. [4-35-9]_END

B_4_C_30_40
BEGIN_
व्यपेत पंकजासु स वालुकासु
प्रसन्न तोयासु स गो कुलासु |
स सारसा राव विनादितासु
नदिषु हंसा निपतन्ति हृष्टाः || ४-३०-४२_END
BEGIN_
"De-silted is the silt of rivers and they are with sand-dunes and serene waters, and
cow-stock is gathering there, besides, they are resonant with clucking of Saarasa birds, in such
rivers swans are delightedly taking deep dives. [4-30-42]_END

B_4_C_33_22
BEGIN_
किम् नु रुट् कारणम् सुभ्रु प्रकृत्या मृदु मानसः |स रोष इव संप्राप्तो येन अयम् राघवानुजः || ४-३३-३२_END
BEGIN_
"This brother of Raghava is mellow-hearted by his nature, oh, suavely eye-browed Tara, but he turned up as if 
with some disdain, really what must be the reason for a grudge! [4-33-32]_END

B_4_C_34_17
BEGIN_
न नूनम् इक्ष्वाकु वरस्य कार्मुकात्
शरान् च तान् पश्यसि वज्र संनिभान् |
ततः सुखम् नाम विषेवसे सुखी
न राम कार्यम् मनसा अपि अवेक्षसे || ४-३४-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Definitely you are not envisaging the Thunderbolt similar arrows from the bow of
the best one from Ikshvaku dynasty, Rama, thereby you are enjoying luxuries joyously without giving
a thought to Rama's mission even at your heart. [4-34-19]_END

B_4_C_31_34
BEGIN_
ततः किल किलाम् चक्रुः लक्ष्मणम् प्रेक्ष्य वानराः |
प्रसादयन्तः तम् क्रुद्धम् भय मोहित चेतसः || ४-३१-३९_END
BEGIN_
The hearts of mobbing monkeys are flustered with fear when they pored over
infuriated Lakshmana, thus they jibber-jabbered so as to appease him. [4-31-39]_END

B_4_C_36_3
BEGIN_
स लक्ष्मणम् भीम बलम् सर्व वानर सत्तमः |
अब्रवीत् प्रश्रितम् वाक्यम् सुग्रीवः संप्रहर्षयन् || ४-३६-४_END
BEGIN_
Sugreeva who is the most powerful one among all vanara-s, then placatingly spoke
this humble sentence to Lakshmana, whose prowess is most formidable. [4-36-4]_END

B_4_C_35_9
BEGIN_
न च रोष वशम् तात गंतुम् अर्हसि लक्ष्मण |निश्चयार्थम् अविज्ञाय सहसा प्राकृतो यथा || ४-३५-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Without knowing realities, oh, young man Lakshmana, it will be extraneous of you to hastily enter into the control 
of your rancour like a commoner. [4-35-10]_END

B_4_C_30_41
BEGIN_
नदी घन प्रस्रवण उदकानाम्
अति प्रवृद्ध अनिल बर्हिणानाम् |
प्लवंगमानाम् च गत उत्सवानाम्
ध्रुवम् रवाः संप्रति संप्रणष्टाः || ४-३०-४३_END
BEGIN_
"The ruffles of rivers, rumbles of clouds, rattles of rapids, such rackets of waters
are quietened, and much amplified gusts of wind, and screams of peacocks along with crocks of
frogs, are now completely undone as their festivity is definitely lost with the rains.
[4-30-43]_END

B_4_C_33_23
BEGIN_
किम् पश्यसि कुमारस्य रोष स्थानम् अनिन्दिते |न खलु अकारणे कोपम् आहरेत् नरपुंगवः || ४-३३-३३_END
BEGIN_
"What do you see as the basis of this young man's spite, oh impeccable Tara, this best one among men will not 
invoke despite, indeed, to a fault. [4-33-33]_END

B_4_C_31_35
BEGIN_
ते महा ओघ निभम् दृष्ट्वा वज्र अशनि सम स्वनम् |
सिंह नादम् समम् चक्रुर् लक्ष्मणस्य समीपतः || ४-३१-४०_END
BEGIN_
And those monkeys on observing Lakshmana instantly raised a hubbub at his nearby
that is similar to a storm of a torrent, thunder of a thunderbolt, and the roar of a lion.
[4-31-40]_END

B_4_C_36_4
BEGIN_
प्रनष्टा श्रीः च कीर्तिः च कपि राज्यम् च शाश्वतम् |
राम प्रसादात् सौमित्रे पुनः च आप्तम् इदम् मया || ४-३६-५_END
BEGIN_
"My prosperity, prominence and this perpetual kingdom of monkeys are once mislaid,
but oh, Soumitri, I regained all this just by the beneficence of Rama. [4-36-5]_END

B_4_C_35_10
BEGIN_
सत्त्व युक्ता हि पुरुषाः त्वत् विधाः पुरुषर्षभ |अविमृश्य न रोषस्य सहसा यान्ति वश्यताम् || ४-३५-११_END
BEGIN_
"Men of your kind having conscientiousness, oh, best one among men, do not hurriedly rush in and get clutched 
by their own rancour, unconscionably. [4-35-11]_END

B_4_C_33_24
BEGIN_
यदि अस्य कृतम् अस्माभिः बुध्यसे किंचित् अप्रियम् |तत् बुध्या संप्रधार्य आशु क्षिप्रम् एव अभिधीयताम् || ४-३३-३४_END
BEGIN_
"If you consider that we have done something objectionable to him, in the least, let that be quickly determined 
by your nimble-wittedness and let that be made known immediately. [4-33-34]_END

B_4_C_30_42
BEGIN_
अनेक वर्णाः सुविनष्ट कायाः
नव उदितेषु अंबुधरेषु नष्टाः |
क्षुध अर्दिता घोर विषा बिलेभ्यः
चिर उषिता विप्रसरन्ति सर्पाः || ४-३०-४४_END
BEGIN_
"Variously coloured and dangerously venomous snakes have contracted into their snake
pits with the advent of new rain clouds, and containing in there for a long time they are highly
emaciated for they are hunger-stricken, but now they are snaking out of those pits. [4-30-44]_END

B_4_C_31_36
BEGIN_
तेन शब्देन महता प्रत्यबुध्यत वानरः |
मद विह्वल ताम्राक्षो व्याकुल स्रग्वि भूषणः || ४-३१-४१_END
BEGIN_
With that uproarious noise of monkeys Sugreeva came to his senses, but because of
stupor his coppery eyes are helter-skelter and his garlands and ornaments are topsy-turvy.
[4-31-41]_END

B_4_C_36_5
BEGIN_
कः शक्तः तस्य देवस्य ख्यातस्य स्वेन कर्मणा |
तादृशम् प्रतिकुर्वीत अंशेन अपि नृपात्मज || ४-३६-६_END
BEGIN_
"Who is capable of requiting Rama, oh, prince Lakshmana, even by a fraction of that
kind of inestimable help taken from him, as that lord is renowned by actions particular to himself,
like daring and eliminating Vali._END

B_4_C_35_11
BEGIN_
प्रसादये त्वाम् धर्मज्ञ सुग्रीवार्थे समाहिता |महान् रोष समुत्पन्नः संरंभः त्यज्यताम् अयम् || ४-३५-१२_END
BEGIN_
"I beg for your grace, oh, virtue-knower, in the interest of Sugreeva with all my equability, and you may dispel 
this clangour upshot in high dudgeon of yours. [4-35-12]_END

B_4_C_33_25
BEGIN_
अथवा स्वयम् एव एनम् द्रष्टुम् अर्हसि भामिनी |वचनैः स्वांत्व युक्तैः च प्रसादयितुम् अर्हसि || ४-३३-३५_END
BEGIN_
"Otherwise, oh, lady, you alone are apt to see him in person, and it will be apt of you to appease him with words 
blent with mitigation. [4-33-35]_END

B_4_C_30_43
BEGIN_
चंचत् चन्द्र कर स्पर्श हर्ष उन्मीलित तारका |
अहो रागवती संध्या जहाति स्वयम् अंबरम् || ४-३०-४५_END


B_4_C_31_37
BEGIN_
अथ अंगद वचः श्रुत्वा तेन एव च समागतौ |
मंत्रिणो वानरेन्द्रस्य सम्मत उदार दर्शिनौ || ४-३१-४२
प्लक्षः च एव प्रभावः च मंत्रिणौ अर्थ धर्मयोः |
वक्तुम् उच्चावचम् प्राप्तम् लक्ष्मणम् तौ शशंसतुः || ४-३१-४३_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of Angada two ministers who are agreeable in their advice and
appreciable in their aspect have come along with him, and those two ministers of the king of
vanara-s, namely Plaksha and Prabhava, have appraised Sugreeva that Lakshmana has arrived to
discuss variously about the prosperity and probity. [4-31-42, 43]_END

B_4_C_36_6
BEGIN_
सीताम् प्राप्स्यति धर्मात्मा वधिष्यति च रावणम् |
सहाय मात्रेण मया राघवः स्वेन तेजसा || ४-३६-७_END
BEGIN_
"Virtue-souled Raghava reacquires Seetha, and even exterminates Ravana by himself
with his own resplendence, while I and my assistance remain only in name. [4-36-7]_END

B_4_C_35_12
BEGIN_
रुमाम् माम् च अंगदम् राज्यम् धन धान्य पशूनि च |राम प्रियार्थम् सुग्रीवः त्यजेत् इति मतिर् मम || ४-३५-१३_END
BEGIN_
"In the honour of Rama, Sugreeva will disown his wife Ruma, even me, even Angada, why us, he will disown whole 
kingdom with its riches, food grains, livestock and whatnot, as I can infer. [4-35-13]_END

B_4_C_30_44

BEGIN_
"Aha! By the touch of the moonbeam of the shining moon, the damsel called twilight
is delightedly unfolding the stars releasing her ochry hue off the sky on her own, in all her love
for the moon._END

B_4_C_33_26
BEGIN_
त्वत् दर्शने विशुद्ध आत्मा न स कोपम् करिष्यति |न हि स्त्रीषु महात्मानः क्वचित् कुर्वन्ति दारुणम् || ४-३३-३६_END
BEGIN_
"Just on seeing you he that highly pure-souled Lakshmana will stop venting his spleen, by the way, great-souls 
will not be rampageous with women, isn't it! [4-33-36]_END

B_4_C_31_38
BEGIN_
प्रसादयित्वा सुग्रीवम् वचनैः स अर्थ निश्चितैः |
आसीनम् पर्युपासीनौ यथा शक्रम् मरुत्पतिम् || ४-३१-४४_END
BEGIN_
Those two ministers sitting around and nearby Sugreeva, who is seated like the king
of wind-gods, namely Indra, on appeasing him with meaningful and expressive words they spoke to him
in this way. [4-31-44]_END

B_4_C_36_7
BEGIN_
सहाय कृत्यम् किम् तस्य येन सप्त महाद्रुमाः |
शैलः च वसुधा चैव बाणेन एकेन दारिताः || ४-३६-८_END
BEGIN_
"Basically, why some measures of succour need be extended to him who has ripped
seven gigantic-trees, a mountain, and even the earth, all just with one arrow! [4-36-8]_END

B_4_C_35_13
BEGIN_
समानेष्यति सुग्रीवः सीतया सह राघवम् |शशांकम् इव रोहिण्या हत्वा तम् राक्षस अधमम् || ४-३५-१४_END
BEGIN_
"On eliminating that worst demon Ravana, Sugreeva can bring Seetha together with Raghava, as with the coalescing 
of star Rohini with the Moon. [4-35-14]_END

B_4_C_37_0
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु सुग्रीवो लक्ष्मणेन महात्मना |
हनूमन्तम् स्थितम् पार्श्वे वचनम् च इदम् अब्रवीत् || ४-३७-१_END
BEGIN_
When the great-souled Lakshmana spoke to Sugreeva in this way, Sugreeva spoke this
word to Hanuma who is available at his side. [4-37-1]_END

B_4_C_30_45
BEGIN_
रात्रिः शशांक उदित सौम्य वक्त्रा
तारा गण उन्मीलित चारु नेत्रा |
ज्योत्स्ना अंशुक प्रावरणा विभाति
नारी इव शुक्ल अंशुक संवृत अंगी || ४-३०-४६_END
BEGIN_
"Damsel-night is with the risen-moon as her genteel-face, myriad-stars as her
twinkling-eyes, moonlight as her veiling-cloth, and she is glistening like the one who
fully-enfolded her limbs within a whitish-cloth-like moonshine. [4-30-46]_END

B_4_C_33_27
BEGIN_
त्वया स्वांत्वैः उपक्रांतम् प्रसन्न इन्द्रिय मानसम् |ततः कमलपत्राक्षम् द्रक्ष्याअमि अहम् अरिंदमम् || ४-३३-३७_END
BEGIN_
"If you seek his presence with propitiatory words his heart and senses will be pacified, and then I will be able 
to see that lotus-petal-eyed Lakshmana, the destroyer of his enemies." Sugreeva thus spoke to Tara. [4-33-37]_END

B_4_C_31_39
BEGIN_
सत्य संधौ महाभागौ भ्रातरौ राम लक्ष्मणौ |
वयस्य भावम् संप्राप्तौ राज्य अर्हौ राज्य दायिनौ || ४-३१-४५_END
BEGIN_
"Rama and Lakshmana are the brothers who abide by truth, highly-providential, and
though they are worthy enough to rule kingdom for themselves they have bestowed the kingdom to you,
such as they are, they have become your true friends." Thus started the ministers to say to
Sugreeva. [4-31-45]_END

B_4_C_36_8
BEGIN_
धनुर् विस्फारमाणस्य यस्य शब्देन लक्ष्मण |
स शैला कम्पिता भूमिः सहायैः किम् नु तस्य वै || ४-३६-९_END
BEGIN_
"He who outstretches his bow with a clangour by which the earth with its mountains
quakes, oh, Lakshmana, to him these aides are really of what aid, indeed! [4-36-9]_END

B_4_C_35_14
BEGIN_
शत कोटि सहस्राणि लंकायाम् किल रक्षसाम् |अयुतानि च षट् त्रिंशत् सहस्राणि शतानि च || ४-३५-१५_END
BEGIN_
"It is said that the demons in Lanka are a trillion, plus thirty-six thousands of units of military, where one 
unit consists of a ten-thousand warriors, and hundreds and thousands of other demons are there, thus they say. 
[4-35-15]_END

B_4_C_37_1
BEGIN_
महेन्द्र हिमवत् विंध्य कैलास शिखरेषु च |
मन्दरे पाण्डु शिखरे पंच शैलेषु ये स्थिताः || ४-३७-२
तरुण आदित्य वर्णेषु भ्राजमानेषु नित्यशः |
पर्वतेषु समुद्र अंते पश्चिमस्याम् तु ये दिशि || ४-३७-३
आदित्य भवने चैव गिरौ संध्या अभ्र संनिभे |
पद्म ताल वनम् भीमाः संश्रिता हरि पुंगवाः || ४-३७-४
अंजन अंबुद संकाशाः कुंजर प्रतिम ओजसः |
अंजने पर्वते चैव ये वसन्ति प्लवंगमाः || ४-३७-५
महाशैल गुहा आवासा वानराः कनक प्रभाः |
मेरु पार्श्व गताः चैव ये च धूम्र गिरिम् श्रिताः || ४-३७-६
तरुण आदित्य वर्णाः च पर्वते ये महाअरुणे |
पिबंतो मधु मैरेयम् भीम वेगाः प्लवंगमाः || ४-३७-७
वनेषु च सुरम्येषु सुगन्धिषु महत्सु च |
तापस आश्रम रम्येषु वन अन्तेषु समंततः || ४-३७-८
तान् तान् त्वम् आनय क्षिप्रम् पृथिव्याम् सर्व वानरान् |
साम दान आदिभिः कल्पैः वानरैः वेगवत्तरैः || ४-३७-९_END
BEGIN_
"Convoke the Vaanara-s available on the summits of these five mountains, namely Mt.
Mahendra, Mt. Himalaya, Mt. Vindhya, and Mt. Kailash and those that are on the whitish peak of Mt.
Mandara. As well as those that are on the mountains at seashore, udaya
adri, namely 'sunrise-mountain,' which mountains will always be dazzling with the tinge of
youthful sun. And them that are on the mountains which shine in the ochry hue of evening clouds,
asta adri, namely 'sunset-mountain' and which mountains are situated
at the Palace of Sun. And the catastrophic monkey chiefs that are abiding in the palm groves of Mt.
Padma. Also thus, the fly-jumpers who are similar to black-mascara and black-clouds in their shine,
and who match elephants in their vigour, and who live on Mt. Anjana, they too are to be convened.
Those fly-jumpers whose complexion will be golden and dwell in the caves of Great-Mountain, besides
those who are on the mountainsides of Mt. Meru, and those biding on the Black-Red mountain, along
with those topmost speeded fly-jumpers living on Mt. Great-Ochre swilling palm-toddy, these are to
be summoned. Further, the vanara-s who will be in the tinge of rising sun and who dwell in the
highly delightful, richly fragrant and lofty woodlands that are surrounded with the delightful
hermitages of sages are to be summoned. Along with them, the vanara-s who are in the interiors of
forests, they are also to be called for. Why citing a few? Those and those monkeys that are on the
earth, all of them are to be assembled. Oh, Hanuma, you quickly summon all of the topmost speeded
vanara-s by employing concessions, conciliations and the like procedures. [4-37-2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7,
8, 9]_END

B_4_C_33_28
BEGIN_
सा प्रस्खलंती मद विह्वल अक्षीप्रलंब कांची गुण हेम सूत्रा |सलक्षणा लक्ष्मण संनिधानम्जगाम तारा नमित 
अंग यष्टिः || ४-३३-३८_END
BEGIN_
Exquisitely featured Tara went to the proximity of Lakshmana with a waddling gait, tipsily flustering eyes, rrivière-strings 
of golden cincture dangling, and with a sticklike gracile body humbly bent. [4-33-38]_END

B_4_C_30_46
BEGIN_
विपक्व शालि प्रसवानि भुक्त्वा
प्रहर्षिता सारस चारु पंक्ति |
नभः समाक्रामति शीघ्र वेगा
वात अवधूता ग्रथित इव माला || ४-३०-४७_END
BEGIN_
"On eating richly ripened yield of rice delighted are the Saarasa birds, and in a
delightful bird-line with swift speed they are overrunning the sky like a stringed flowery-tassel
up-heaved by wind. [4-30-47]_END

B_4_C_31_40
BEGIN_
तयोः एको धनुष्पाणिर् द्वारि तिष्ठति लक्ष्मणः |
यस्य भीताः प्रवेपन्ते नादान् मुंचन्ति वानराः || ४-३१-४६_END
BEGIN_
"One among those two, Lakshmana, is biding at the door wielding his bow, by whom the
monkeys are panicked and venting out alarms shuddering utterly. [4-31-46]_END

B_4_C_36_9
BEGIN_
अनुयात्राम् नर इन्द्रस्य करिष्ये अहम् नरषभ |
गच्छतो रावणम् हन्तुम् वैरिणम् स पुरःसरम् || ४-३६-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Lakshmana, I just can tread behind that king of people, Rama, on his charging to
eliminate enemy Ravana along with all of his vanguards, that's all. [4-36-10]_END

B_4_C_35_15
BEGIN_
अहत्वा ताम् च दुर्धर्षान् राक्षसान् काम रूपिणः |न शक्यो रावणो हंतुम् येन सा मैथिली हृता || ४-३५-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Without eliminating those unassailable and guise changing demons, it is impracticable to eliminate him who has 
abducted Maithili, namely Ravana. [4-35-16]_END

B_4_C_37_2
BEGIN_
प्रेषिताः प्रथमम् ये च मया आज्ञाताः महाजवाः |
त्वरण अर्थम् तु भूयः त्वम् संप्रेषय हरीश्वरान् || ४-३७-१०_END
BEGIN_
"In the first instance highly speedy vanara-s are hastened at my commanded, however,
you hasten some more monkey chiefs for the purpose of hastening them. [4-37-10]_END

B_4_C_33_29
BEGIN_
स ताम् समीक्ष्य एव हरि ईश पत्नीम्तस्थौ उदासीनतया महात्मा |अवाङ्मुखो आभूत् मनुजेन्द्र पुत्रःस्त्री 
सन्निकर्षात् विनिवृत्त कोपम् || ४-३३-३९_END
BEGIN_
On observing the wife of the king of monkeys, the great-souled son of the king of humans stood aside unemotionally, 
and because of the presence of females he backed down on his anger with his face cast down. [4-33-39]_END

B_4_C_30_47
BEGIN_
सुप्त एक हंसम् कुमुदैः उपेतम्
महा ह्रदस्थम् सलिलम् विभाति |
घनैः विमुक्तम् निशि पूर्ण चन्द्रम्
तारा गण कीर्णम् इव अंतरिक्षम् || ४-३०-४८_END
BEGIN_
"One swan is sleeping in the water of a vast lake thick with white-lotuses, and that
lake is glistening like the star-studded nightly skyscape that is disengaged from clouds, and that
has the full-moon. [4-30-48]_END

B_4_C_31_41
BEGIN_
स एष राघव भ्राता लक्ष्मणो वाक्य सारथिः |
व्यवसाय रथः प्राप्तः तस्य रामस्य शासनात् || ४-३१-४७_END
BEGIN_
"This Lakshmana, the brother of Raghava, has arrived here at the decree of Rama on
the chariot called his 'endeavour', charioted by the charioteer called 'the word of Rama.'
[4-31-47]_END

B_4_C_36_10
BEGIN_
यदि किंचित् अतिक्रान्तम् विश्वासात् प्रणयेन वा |
प्रेष्यस्य क्षमितव्यम् मे न कश्चिन् न अपराध्यति || ४-३६-११_END
BEGIN_
"If I have overstepped either in faith or friendliness, in the least, that may be
pardoned for I am an attendant of yours. By the way, none is unoffending. [4-36-11]_END

B_4_C_35_16
BEGIN_
ते न शक्या रणे हंतुम् असहायेन लक्ष्मण |रावणः क्रूर कर्मा च सुग्रीवेण विशेषतः || ४-३५-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Lakshmana, it is impossible to kill those demons, or that Ravana, the evil-doer and abductor of Seetha, without 
any assistance, more so to Sugreeva... [4-35-17]_END

B_4_C_37_3
BEGIN_
ये प्रसक्ताः च कामेषु दीर्घ सूत्राः च वानराः |
इह आनयस्व तान् शीघ्रम् सर्वान् एव कपीश्वरान् || ४-३७-११_END
BEGIN_
"Those that are entangled with creature comforts, and those that are stringy
dawdlers, you quickly lead all of those monkey chiefs in here. [4-37-11]_END

B_4_C_33_30
BEGIN_
सा पान योगात् च निवृत्त लज्जादृष्टि प्रसादात् च नरेन्द्र सूनोः |उवाच तारा प्रणय प्रगल्भम्वाक्यम् महार्थम् 
परिसांत्व रूपम् || ४-३३-४०_END
BEGIN_
She who is unblushing by virtue of her inebriety ad even by the gracious look of the prince Lakshmana, such a 
Tara spoke a highly noteworthy sentence that is dauntless in friendliness and entirely mitigatory in its vein. 
[4-33-40]_END

B_4_C_30_48
BEGIN_
प्रकीर्ण हंसा अकुल मेखलानाम्
प्रबुद्ध पद्म उत्पल मालिनीनाम् |
वापीः उत्तमानाम् अधिक अद्य लक्ष्मीः
वर अंगनाम् इव भूषितानाम् || ४-३०-४९_END
BEGIN_
"With swans spreading and swaying around as her swaying girdle-ornaments, and with
well-bloomed red and blue lotuses as her swinging flowery-tassels, the resplendence of those best
tanks is now heightening as with a dame embellished with girdle-ornaments and flowery-tassels.
[4-30-49]_END

B_4_C_31_42
BEGIN_
अयम् च तनयो राजन् ताराया दयितो अंगदः |
लक्ष्मणेन सकाशम् ते प्रेषितः त्वरया अनघ || ४-३१-४८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, merited one, even Lakshmana has ushered this Angada hastily, oh, king, the
precious son of Tara, to your presence. [4-31-48]_END

B_4_C_36_11
BEGIN_
इति तस्य ब्रुवाणस्य सुग्रीवस्य महात्मनः |
अभवत् लक्ष्मणः प्रीतः प्रेम्णा च इदम् उवाच ह || ४-३६-१२_END
BEGIN_
Lakshmana is pleased with that great-souled Sugreeva who is speaking thus, and said
this he said to him, indeed, in friendliness. [4-36-12]_END

B_4_C_37_4
BEGIN_
अहोभिः दशभिः ये च न आगच्छन्ति मम आज्ञया |
हन्तव्याः ते दुरात्मानो राज शासन दूषकाः || ४-३७-१२_END
BEGIN_
"And such of those vanara-s that do not arrive within ten days by my command, those
miscreants are eliminable as the abusers of king's decree. [4-37-12]_END

B_4_C_35_17
BEGIN_
एवम् आख्यातवान् वाली स हि अभिज्ञो हरीश्वरः |आगमः तु न मे व्यक्तः श्रवात् तस्य ब्रवीमि अहम् || ४-३५-१८_END
BEGIN_
"This way Vali was saying and that king of monkeys is well-informed in these aspects, isn't it! But how Ravana 
mustered up these many troops is unclear to me, and I am saying what I heard from Vali. [4-35-18]_END

B_4_C_33_31
BEGIN_
किम् कोप मूलम् मनुजेन्द्र पुत्रकः ते न सन्तिष्ठति वाक् निदेशे |कः शुष्क वृक्षम् वनम् आपतन्तम्दवाग्निम् 
आसीदति निर्विशंकः || ४-३३-४१_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, prince, what is the cause of your anger? Who is not abiding by your oral order? And who is he that draweth 
nigh of a wildfire that is befalling on a forest of dried-up trees, without a shadow of doubt?" Tara enquired 
thus with Lakshmana. [4-33-41]_END

B_4_C_30_49
BEGIN_
वेणु स्वर व्यंजित तूर्य मिश्रः
प्रत्यूष काले अनिल संप्रवृत्तः |
संमूर्च्छितो गह्वर गो वृषाणाम्
अन्योन्यम् आपूरयति इव शब्दः || ४-३०-५०_END
BEGIN_
"In tune with the tunes of flute the dawn-time breeze is tuned-up, and it is
spreading to broadcast the tuneful tunes from the caves, cows and bulls, and the sounds are as
though surpassing one another. [4-30-50]_END

B_4_C_31_43
BEGIN_
सः अयम् रोष परीताक्षो द्वारि तिष्ठति वीर्यवान् |
वानरान् वानरपते चक्षुसा निर्दहन इव || ४-३१-४९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, king of monkeys, such as he is, that brave Lakshmana is sticking fast at the
door with an awning of rancour on his eyes and as if to burn down the monkeys just with his eyes.
[4-31-49]_END

B_4_C_36_12
BEGIN_
सर्वथा हि मम भ्राता स नाथो वानरेश्वर |
त्वया नाथेन सुग्रीव प्रश्रितेन विशेषतः || ४-३६-१३_END
BEGIN_
"In anyway, my brother indeed has a defender with him, oh, king of vanara-s
Sugreeva, especially you, who are a defender of your own word and a deferential one towards Rama.
[4-36-13]_END

B_4_C_37_5
BEGIN_
शतानि अथ सहस्राणि कोट्यः च मम शासनात् |
प्रयान्तु कपि सिंहानाम् निदिशे मम ये स्थिताः || ४-३७-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Let all the lionly monkeys available on earth that abide by my control start coming
to this place in hundreds, thousands, even in millions, by my command. [4-37-13]_END

B_4_C_35_18
BEGIN_
त्वत् सहाय निमित्तम् हि प्रेषिता हरिपुंगवाः |आनेतुम् वानरान् युद्धे सुबहून् हरिपुंगवान् || ४-३५-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Intending that assistance to you in war, best monkeys are hastened in all directions, to muster up very many 
best of the best monkeys. [4-35-19]_END

B_4_C_33_32
BEGIN_
स तस्य वचनम् श्रुत्वा सांत्व पूर्वम् अशंकितः |भूयः प्रणय दृष्टार्थम् लक्ष्मणो वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् || ४-३३-४२_END
BEGIN_
On hearing her words which are with a prelude of propitiation, and which by far evince friendship for all practical 
purposes, Lakshmana trustfully spoke these words. [4-33-42]_END

B_4_C_30_50
BEGIN_
नवैः नदीनाम् कुसुम प्रहासैः
व्या धूयमानैः मृदु मारुतेन |
धौत अमल क्षौम पट प्रकाशैः
कूलानि काशैः उपशोभितानि || ४-३०-५१_END
BEGIN_
"The riverbanks are with smiley white flowers of new reeds that are softly swayed by
the gentle breeze, and the silken reed-bed on them is shining forth like a well-washed white
silk-cloth that is shiny. [4-30-51]_END

B_4_C_31_44
BEGIN_
तस्य मूर्ध्ना प्रणम्य त्वम् स पुत्र सह बान्धवः |
गच्छ शीघ्रम् महाराज रोषो हि अद्य उपशम्यताम् || ४-३१-५०_END
BEGIN_
"You may approach him quickly along with your son and relatives, oh, great-king,
prostrate yourself before him holding him in reverence, and thus let his bitterness be indeed
pacified now. [4-31-50]_END

B_4_C_36_13
BEGIN_
यः ते प्रभावः सुग्रीव यत् च ते शौचम् ईदृशम् |
अर्हः तम् कपि राज्यस्य श्रियम् भोक्तुम् अनुत्तमाम् || ४-३६-१४_END
BEGIN_
"With this kind of preponderance and plainness you possess, Sugreeva, you are the
only merited one to enjoy this unexcelled kingdom of monkeys. [4-36-14]_END

B_4_C_37_6
BEGIN_
मेघ पर्वत संकाशाः छादयन्त इव अंबरम् |
घोर रूपाः कपि श्रेष्ठा यान्तु मत् शासनात् इतः || ४-३७-१४_END
BEGIN_
"The champions of monkeys with ghastly aspects and similar in shine with the
mountains and clouds shall start coming here by my command, fly-jumping as though to overcast the
sky. [4-37-4]_END

B_4_C_35_19
BEGIN_
ताम् च प्रतीक्षमाणो अयम् विक्रांतान् सुमहा बलान् |राघवस्य अर्थ सिद्धि अर्थम् न निर्याति हरि ईश्वरः || ४-३५-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Determined to achieve the objective of Raghava this king of monkeys Sugreeva has not bestirred himself while 
awaiting the return of those venturesome and very great mighty monkey-warriors who are sent out. [4-35-20]_END

B_4_C_33_33
BEGIN_
किम् अयम् काम वृत्तः ते लुप्त धर्मार्थ संग्रहः |भर्ता भर्तृ हिते युक्ते न च एवम् अवबुध्यसे || ४-३३-४३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Tara, the associate of husband's prosperity! Why your husband is bound up in profligacy alone, remiss in 
garnering rectitude and riches, and his dereliction is unbeknownst to you, is it! [4-33-43]_END

B_4_C_30_51
BEGIN_
वन प्रचण्डा मधु पान शौण्डाः
प्रिय अन्विताः षट् चरणाः प्रहृष्टाः |
वनेसु मत्ताः पवन अनु यात्राम्
कुर्वन्ति पद्म आसन रेणु गौराः || ४-३०-५२_END
BEGIN_
"Honeybees that are on the loose in forests and roguish in drinking honey are
yellowed with the pollen of lotuses and asana flowers when they had bouts of nectar, and they are
saucily but delightedly making their journey along with their lady-loves in tow with the forest
breeze. [4-30-52]_END

B_4_C_31_45
BEGIN_
यथा आह रामो धर्मात्मा तत् कुरुष्व समाहितः |
राजन् तिष्ठ स्व समये भव सत्य प्रतिश्रवः || ४-३१-५१_END
BEGIN_
"Whatever that virtue-souled Rama says that you have to implement wholeheartedly,
oh, king, you abide by the forthrightness of your promise, stick up for the pact you made." Thus
the ministers advised Sugreeva. [4-31-51]_END

B_4_C_36_14
BEGIN_
सहायेन च सुग्रीव त्वया रामः प्रतापवान् |
वधिष्यति रणे शत्रून् अचिरात् न अत्र संशयः || ४-३६-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Before long, Sugreeva, dauntless Rama will be eliminating enemies in a war with you
as his supporter, there is no doubt about it. [4-36-15]_END

B_4_C_37_7
BEGIN_
ते गतिज्ञा गतिम् गत्वा पृथिव्याम् सर्व वानराः |
आनयंतु हरीन् सर्वान् त्वरिताः शासनान् मम || ४-३७-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Let those vanara-s who know the routes to the dwelling places of other monkeys
expeditiously proceed on quick-routes, and gather all of the monkeys available on earth at my
command." Sugreeva ordered Hanuma that way. [4-37-15]_END

B_4_C_35_20
BEGIN_
कृता सुसंस्था सौमित्रे सुग्रीवेण यथा पुरा |अद्य तैः वानरैः सर्वैः आगंतव्यम् महाबलैः || ४-३५-२१_END
BEGIN_
"According to the well-organised groundwork earlier made by Sugreeva, oh, Saumitri, all of those great-mighty 
monkeys have to arrive here today itself. [4-35-21]_END

B_4_C_33_34
BEGIN_
न चिंतयति राज्यार्थम् सः अस्मान् शोक परायणान् |स अमात्य परिषत् तारे कामम् एव उपसेवते || ४-३३-४४_END
BEGIN_
"Without thinking either about the interests of the kingdom or about us that are cringing to anguish, oh, Tara, 
your husband along with his council of ministers is indulged in lechery. [4-33-44]_END

B_4_C_30_52
BEGIN_
जलम् प्रसन्नम् कुसुम प्रहासम्
क्रौन्च स्वनम् शालि वनम् विपक्वम् |
मृदुः च वायुः विमलः च चन्द्रः
शंसन्ति वर्ष व्यपनीत कालम् || ४-३०-५३_END
BEGIN_
"Waters are standing tranquilly, flowers are smiley, crane-birds are noisily,
rice-crops are ripely, breeze is softly, and moon is brightly, thus they denote the time of rains
has phased out. [4-30-53]_END

B_4_C_36_15
BEGIN_
धर्मज्ञस्य कृतज्ञस्य संग्रामेषु अनिवर्तिनः |
उपपन्नम् च युक्तम् च सुग्रीव तव भाषितम् || ४-३६-१६_END
BEGIN_
"You are the knower of virtuousness and gratefulness and you do not retreat from
battlegrounds, or, on your own word, thus what you have said is conclusive as well as coherent.
[4-36-16]_END

B_4_C_37_8
BEGIN_
तस्य वानर राजस्य श्रुत्वा वायु सुतो वचः |
दिक्षु सर्वासु विक्रान्तान् प्रेषयामास वानरान् || ४-३७-१६_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the order of Sugreeva, the king of vanara-s, Hanuma, the son of Air-god
has started to dispatch valorous monkeys in all directions. [4-37-16]_END

B_4_C_35_21
BEGIN_
ऋक्ष कोटि सहस्राणि गोलांगूल शतानि च |अद्य त्वाम् उपयास्यन्ति जहि कोपम् अरिन्दमकोट्यो अनेकाः तु काकुत्स्थ 
कपीनाम् दीप्त तेजसाम् || ४-३५-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Only today millions and millions of bears and hundredfold millions of baboons, and innumerable monkeys who by 
their own flare are like firebrands will arrive in your fore, oh, Lakshmana, thereby, oh, the enemy-repressor, 
therefore rebut your rage. [4-35-22]_END

B_4_C_38_0
BEGIN_
प्रतिगृह्य च तत् सर्वम् उपानयम् उपाहृतम् |वानरान् सान्त्वयित्वा च सर्वान् एव व्यसर्जयत् || ४-३८-१_END
BEGIN_
On receiving all those gifts brought in by the Vanara-s from Himalayas, Sugreeva dispersed them all with approbation. 
[4-38-1]_END

B_4_C_33_35
BEGIN_
स मासान् चतुर कृत्वा प्रमाणम् प्लवगेश्वरः |व्यतीतान् तान् मद उदग्रो विहरन् न अवबुध्यते || ४-३३-४५_END
BEGIN_
"On stipulating a four month criterion for an embargo the king of fly-jumpers is not able to realise the completion 
of that period as he is frantically insensible. [4-33-45]_END

B_4_C_30_53
BEGIN_
मीन उप संदर्शित मेखलानाम्
नदी वधूनाम् गतयो अद्य मंदाः |
कान्त उपभुक्त अलस गामिनीनाम्
प्रभात कालेषु इव कामिनीनाम् || ४-३०-५४_END
BEGIN_
"In the dame-like rivers fish are very closely seen as if they are girdle ornaments
of that dame, and nowadays these dames are strutting slothfully like ladyloves who strut tiresomely
in the early morning of next day, after a nightlong romancing with their lovers. [4-30-54]_END

B_4_C_36_16
BEGIN_
दोषज्ञः सति सामर्थ्ये को अन्यो भाषितुम् अर्हति |
वर्जयित्वा मम ज्येष्ठम् त्वाम् च वानर सत्तम || ४-३६-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Even though one has capability to know his own lapse and speak it up, oh, ablest
among Vanara-s, who is he that behoves outspokenly, excepting my elder brother and you.
[4-36-17]_END

B_4_C_37_9
BEGIN_
ते पदम् विष्णु विक्रान्तम् पतत्रि ज्योतिः अध्वगाः |
प्रयाताः प्रहिता राज्ञा हरयः तु क्षणेन वै || ४-३७-१७_END
BEGIN_
In a split-second, the vanara-s that are sent by the king of vanara-s have
skyrocketed to the airways of birds and stars on their way, and indeed reached the vault of heaven,
which was once trodden by Vishnu. [4-37-17]_END

B_4_C_35_22
BEGIN_
तव हि मुखम् इदम् निरीक्ष्य कोपात्क्षतज समे नयने निरीक्षमाणाः |हरि वर वनिता न यान्ति शान्तिम्प्रथम 
भयस्य हि शन्किताः स्म सर्वाः || ४-३५-२३_END
BEGIN_
"On staring at this angry face of yours, and on gazing at the angrily bloodshot eyes of yours, unsecured is the 
peace to the females of monkeys chief, and with the fear caused at first by Vali's elimination we are all indeed 
premonished about such a happening in respect of Sugreeva too. [4-35-23]_END

B_4_C_38_1
BEGIN_
विसर्जयित्वा स हरीन् सहस्रान् तान् कृत कर्मणः |मेने कृतार्थम् आत्मानम् राघवम् च महाबलम् || ४-३८-२_END
BEGIN_
On dispersing thousands of monkeys who have effectuated their errand of summoning all monkeys on the earth, Sugreeva 
deemed that his own aspirations and as well as those of that great-mighty Rama are achieved. [4-38-2]_END

B_4_C_33_36
BEGIN_
न हि धर्मार्थ सिद्ध्यर्थम् पानम् एवम् प्रशस्यते |पानात् अर्थस्य कामः च धर्मः च परिहीयते || ४-३३-४६_END
BEGIN_
"For the purpose of achieving rightly rectitude and rightful riches this way of bacchanalia is inappreciable, 
isn't it! Just going on drinking will bring prosperity, aspirations and even probity to ruin. [4-33-46]_END

B_4_C_30_54
BEGIN_
स चक्रवाकानि स शैवलानि
काशैः दुकूलैः इव संवृतानि |
स पत्र रेखाणि स रोचनानि
वधू मुखानि इव नदी मुखानि || ४-३०-५५_END
BEGIN_
"With Cakravaka birds, with riverweeds, and with reeds that lookalike a veiling
silk-cloth, half-veiled are the river-shores and they look painted with foliage-lines in vermilion,
like the faces of maidens. [4-30-55]_END

B_4_C_36_17
BEGIN_
सदृशः च असि रामस्य विक्रमेण बलेन च |
सहायो दैवतैः दत्तः चिराय हरि पुंगव || ४-३६-१८_END
BEGIN_
"You are a coequal to Rama by your valour and vigour and oh, best one among monkeys,
gods have given you after a long time. [4-36-18]_END

B_4_C_37_10
BEGIN_
ते समुद्रेषु गिरिषु वनेषु च सरःसु च |
वानरा वानरान् सर्वान् राम हेतोः अचोदयन् || ४-३७-१८_END
BEGIN_
After skyrocketing those monkeys have reached the monkeys that are living at
seashores and islands, in the caves and crags of mountains, and at lakeshores and their surrounds,
and motivated all of the monkeys available there towards the cause of Rama. [4-37-18]_END

B_4_C_38_2
BEGIN_
स लक्ष्मणो भीम बलम् सर्व वानर सत्तमम् |अब्रवीत् प्रश्रितम् वाक्यम् सुग्रीवम् संप्रहर्षयन् || ४-३८-३किष्किंधाया 
विनिष्क्राम यदि ते सौम्य रोचते |_END
BEGIN_
Gladdening Sugreeva who is indomitably mighty and the indomitable one among all vanara-s, Lakshmana spoke these 
courteous words to him, "oh, gentle one, if it please you, make an exit from Kishkindha." [4-38-3, 4a]_END

B_4_C_30_55
BEGIN_
प्रफुल्ल बाण आसन चित्रितेषु
प्रहृष्ट षट्पदानि कूजितेषु |
गृहीत चापः उद्यत दण्ड चण्डः
प्रचण्ड चारो अद्य वनेषु कामः || ४-३०-५६_END
BEGIN_
"In the forest that is portrayed with the flourishing Baana and Asana trees, where
the honeybees are humming elatedly, there alone the Love-god, Manmatha, is moving about unimpededly
taking his bow to punish the lovesick. [4-30-56]_END

B_4_C_33_37
BEGIN_
धर्म लोपो महान् तावत् कृते हि अप्रति कुर्वतः |अर्थ लोपः च मित्रस्य नाशे गुणवतो महान् || ४-३३-४७_END
BEGIN_
"If one is not going to requite the favour done in his respect an awful detriment occurs in his own rectitude, 
isn't it. Thereby, that reneger will loose a highly noble friend and thereby a great shortcoming occurs to him 
in achieving his purposes. Thus a threefold ill befalls on that reneger. [4-33-47]_END

B_4_C_36_18
BEGIN_
किम् तु शीघ्रम् इतो वीर निष्क्राम त्वम् मया सह |
सान्त्वयस्व वयस्यम् च भार्या हरण दुःखितम् || ४-३६-१९_END
BEGIN_
"However, you quickly start from here along with me, oh, brave one, and embolden
your friend who is anguishing in the despoilment of his wife. [4-36-19]_END

B_4_C_37_11
BEGIN_
मृत्यु काल उपमस्य आज्ञाम् राज राजस्य वानराः |
सुग्रीवस्य आययुः श्रुत्वा सुग्रीव भय शन्किताः || ४-३७-१९_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that command of the king of kings of Vanara-s, Sugreeva, who is semblable
with the Death-god and Time-god, all of the monkeys have arrived with the terror of Sugreeva
haunting them. [4-37-19]_END

B_4_C_38_3
BEGIN_
तस्य तत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा लक्ष्मणस्य सुभाषितम् || ४-३८-४सुग्रीवः परम प्रीतो वाक्यम् एतत् उवाच ह |एवम् भवतु 
गच्छामः स्थेयम् त्वत् शासने मया || ४-३८-५_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the courteous words of Lakshmana Sugreeva is extremely pleased and he indeed spoke this sentence to 
him, "So be it. Let us go. I remain biddable in your command." [4-38-4b, 5]_END

B_4_C_30_56
BEGIN_
लोकम् सुवृष्ट्या परितोषयित्व
नदीः तटाकानि च पूरयित्वा |
निष्पन्न सस्याम् वसुधाम् च कृत्वा
त्यक्त्वा नभः तोय धराः प्रणष्टाः || ४-३०-५७_END
BEGIN_
"On appeasing the world with good rains, on filling the rivers and tanks, and on
making the earth to derive good harvests also, clouds have dissipated forsaking the sky.
[4-30-57]_END

B_4_C_33_38
BEGIN_
मित्रम् हि अर्थ गुण श्रेष्ठम् सत्य धर्म परायणम् |तत् द्वयम् तु परित्यक्तम् न तु धर्मे व्यवस्थितम् || ४-३३-४८_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed a friend avowed to truthfulness and virtuousness is greater than one's own means and aspirations, but 
you husband forsaking that pair of his means and aspirations that have been fulfilled by such a righteous friend, 
he is not even standing by the probity. [4-33-48]_END

B_4_C_37_12
BEGIN_
ततः ते अंजन संकाशा गिरेः तस्मात् महाजवाः |
तिस्रः कोट्यः प्लवंगानाम् निर्ययुर् यत्र राघवः || ४-३७-२०_END
BEGIN_
Then thirty million fly-jumpers whose swiftness is inconceivable, and whose shine is
like that of black-mascara have sallied forth from mountain Anjana to there where Raghava is
camping, i.e., Mt. Prasravana. [4-37-20]_END

B_4_C_36_19
BEGIN_
यत् च शोक अभिभूतस्य श्रुत्वा रामस्य भाषितम् |
मया त्वम् परुषाणि उक्तः तत् क्षमस्व सखे मम || ४-३६-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, friend, on hearing that which querulously spoken by Rama, who is downhearted in
his anguish, I too reflexively spoke bitter-words to you, and thus whatever I spoke that may be
pardoned. [4-36-20]_END

B_4_C_38_4
BEGIN_
तम् एवम् उक्त्वा सुग्रीवो लक्ष्मणम् शुभ लक्षणम् |विसर्जयामास तदा तारा अद्याः च एव योषितः || ४-३८-६_END
BEGIN_
Sugreeva speaking thus to Lakshmana, whose person itself is auspicious, then bade adieu to Lady Tara and the other 
female vanara-s. [4-38-6]_END

B_4_C_30_57
BEGIN_
दर्शयन्ति शरन् नद्यः पुलिनानि शनैः शनैः |
नव संगम सव्रीडा जघनानि इव योषितः || ४-३०-५८_END
BEGIN_
"The autumnal rivers are showing their dunes slowly and slowly, as with shying
brides showing hips in their new trysts, slowly and slowly. [4-30-58]_END

B_4_C_33_39
BEGIN_
तत् एवम् प्रस्तुते कार्ये कार्यम् अस्माभिः उत्तरम् |यत् कार्यम् कार्य तत्त्वज्ञे त्वम् उदाहर्तुम् अर्हसि || 
४-३३-४९_END
BEGIN_
"Therefore, when our present task is standstill in this way due to the bouts of your husband, oh, the knower of 
the brunt of tasks, what is it we can undertake hereafter...you yourself may aptly give an example..." Thus, Lakshmana 
spoke curtly to Tara. [4-33-49]_END

B_4_C_37_13
BEGIN_
अस्तम् गच्छति यत्र अर्कः तस्मिन् गिरिवरे रताः |
संतप्त हेम वर्ण आभा तस्मात् कोट्यो दश च्युताः || ४-३७-२१_END
BEGIN_
Hundred million monkeys who take delight on the best mountain where the sun goes
into dusk, namely the westerly mountains, asta adri, and whose hue is
similar to the refined gold, for dusk has a golden hue, have jumped in. [4-37-21]_END

B_4_C_38_5
BEGIN_
एहि इति उच्छैः हरि वरान् सुग्रीवः समुदाहरत् |तस्य तद् वचनम् श्रुत्वा हरयः शीघ्रम् आययुः || ४-३८-७बद्ध 
अंजलि पुटाः सर्वे ये स्युः स्त्री दर्शन क्षमाः |_END
BEGIN_
Sugreeva shouted sharply saying, "come here," at the best monkey-adjutants and on hearing his call all of those 
monkeys that are spared to see the ladies of palace chambers have come there swiftly with their palms adjoined 
in supplication. [4-38-7]_END

B_4_C_30_58
BEGIN_
प्रसन्न सलिलाः सौम्य कुरराभिः विनादिताः |
चक्रवाक गण आकीर्णा विभांति सलिल आशयाः || ४-३०-५९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, gentle Lakshmana, with clear waters, well sounding fish-hawks, teeming teams of
Cakravaka birds the lakes are glistening well. [4-30-59]_END

B_4_C_33_40
BEGIN_
सा तस्य धर्मार्थ समाधि युक्तम्निशम्य वाक्यम् मधुर स्वभावम् |तारा गतार्थे मनुजेन्द्र कार्येविश्वास 
युक्तम् तम् उवाच भूयः || ४-३३-५०_END
BEGIN_
On hearing his words containing means, merit and reconciliation, and of mellowly tendency of Lakshmana, Tara realized 
that the purpose of Rama is lapsed, but having confidence in ultimate success she again said to him._END

B_4_C_38_6
BEGIN_
तान् उवाच ततः प्राप्तान् राजा अर्क सदृश प्रभः || ४-३८-८उपस्थापयत क्षिप्रम् शिबिकाम् मम वानराः |_END
BEGIN_
Then the king Sugreeva whose refulgence is kindred to that of sun has said to those vanara-s that have arrived 
there, "oh, vanara-s, immediately position my palanquin before me." [4-38-8b, 9a]_END

B_4_C_37_14
BEGIN_
कैलास शिखरेभ्यः च सिंह केसर वर्चसाम् |
ततः कोटि सहस्राणि वानराणाम् समागमन् || ४-३७-२२_END
BEGIN_
Vanara-s who are in the hue of lion's mane have turned up in thousand crores, say
hundred billion, from the pinnacles of Mt. Kailash. [4-37-22]_END

B_4_C_30_59
BEGIN_
अन्योन्य बद्ध वैराणाम् जिगीषूणाम् नृपात्मज |
उद्योग समयः सौम्य पार्थिवानाम् उपस्थितः || ४-३०-६०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, prince, those that are reciprocally bound by hostilities and desirous of
victory, oh, gentle Lakshmana, for those kings their striving time has come up. [4-30-60]_END

B_4_C_33_41
BEGIN_
न कोप कालः क्षितिपाल पुत्रन च अपि कोपः स्व जने विधेयः |त्वत् अर्थ कामस्य जनस्य तस्यप्रमादम् अपि अर्हसि 
वीर सोढुम् || ४-३३-५१_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, prince, this not the time for angering, also your own people shall not be subjected to anger, and it will 
be apt of you to tolerate Sugreeva's fault because he is desirous of achieving results for you. [4-33-51]_END

B_4_C_37_15
BEGIN_
फल मूलेन जीवन्तो हिमवन्तम् उपाश्रिताः |
तेषाम् कोटि सहस्राणाम् सहस्रम् समवर्तत || ४-३७-२३_END
BEGIN_
Those that are sheltered on Himalayas subsisting on fruits and tubers have arrived
in a thousand of thousand crores, say a trillion. [4-37-23]_END

B_4_C_38_7
BEGIN_
श्रुत्वा तु वचनम् तस्य हरयः शीघ्र विक्रमाः || ४-३८-९समुपस्थापयामासुः शिबिकाम् प्रिय दर्शनाम् |_END
BEGIN_
On hearing his words those monkeys who are the adept ones in their agility right away brought an exquisite palanquin 
and readily started to position it at his nearby. [4-38-9b, 10a]_END

B_4_C_30_60
BEGIN_
इयम् सा प्रथमा यात्रा पार्थिवानाम् नृपात्मज |
न च पश्यामि सुग्रीवम् उद्योगम् वा तथा विधम् || ४-३०-६१_END
BEGIN_
"This is the starting time for invasions of the kings, but I do not even perceive
Sugreeva, or his striving for any invasion as such. [4-30-61]_END

B_4_C_33_42
BEGIN_
कोपम् कथम् नाम गुण प्रकृष्टःकुमार कुर्यात् अपकृष्ट सत्त्वे |कः त्वत् विधः कोप वशम् हि गच्छेसत्त्व 
अवरुद्धः तपसः प्रसूतिः || ४-३३-५२_END
BEGIN_
How in name can a meritoriously high-minded being will show his anger on a relatively mightless inferior being, 
say Sugreeva, whose mightiest brother's mightiness and essence, say that of Vali, are deducted by none other but 
by your brother associated with you, and oh, lad, who goes into the control of fury, say of your kind, while he 
is restrained by his perfection, and a source of abstemiousness. [4-33-52]_END

B_4_C_38_8
BEGIN_
ताम् उपस्थापिताम् दृष्ट्वा शिबिकाम् वानराधिपः || ४-३८-१०लक्ष्मण आरुह्यताम् शीघ्रम् इति सौमित्रिम् अब्रवीत् 
|_END
BEGIN_
And on seeing palanquin positioned at his nearby the king of monkeys Sugreeva said to Saumitri, "you mount it, 
Lakshmana, be quick." [4-38-10b, 11a]_END

B_4_C_37_16
BEGIN_
अंगारक समानानाम् भीमानाम् भीम कर्मणाम् |
विंध्यात् वानर कोटीनाम् सहस्राणि अपतन् द्रुतम् || ४-३७-२४_END
BEGIN_
Millions and millions of Vanara-s whose looks and deeds are gruesome, and who equal
the planet Mars in their crimson-flush, as they dwell on the hotbeds of Mt. Vindhya, have swiftly
alighted from Mt. Vindhya. [4-37-24]_END

B_4_C_30_61
BEGIN_
असनाः सप्त पर्णाः च कोविदाराः च पुष्पिताः |
दृश्यन्ते बन्धुजीवाः च श्यामाः च गिरि सानुषु || ४-३०-६२_END
BEGIN_
"On mountain terraces there appear flowered Asana trees, seven-leaved banana plants,
Kovidaara, Bandhujiiva trees, and the Shyaama creepers. [4-30-62]_END

B_4_C_33_43
BEGIN_
जानामि कोपम् हरि वीर बन्धोःजानामि कार्यस्य च काल संगम् |जानामि कार्यम् त्वयि यत् कृतम् नःतत् च अपि 
जानामि यत् अत्र कार्यम् || ४-३३-५३_END
BEGIN_
"I am aware of the fury of Rama, the friend of champion of the monkeys, namely Sugreeva, I am also aware of the 
time lapse in the task, I am even aware of the folly we have committed, and what need be done in this matter, 
I am well aware. [4-33-53]_END

B_4_C_38_9
BEGIN_
इति उक्त्वा कांचनम् यानम् सुग्रीवः सूर्य सन्निभम् || ४-३८-११बहुभिः हरिभिः युक्तम् आरुरोह स लक्ष्मणः |_END
BEGIN_
Saying so Sugreeva got into that golden carriage which in shine is like the sun and which has many monkey-carriers 
along with Lakshmana. [4-38-11b, 12a]_END

B_4_C_39_0
BEGIN_
इति ब्रुवाणम् सुग्रीवम् रामो धर्मभृताम् वरः |बाहुभ्याम् संपरिष्वज्य प्रत्युवाच कृतांजलिम् || ३-३९-१_END
BEGIN_
Rama, the best proponent of probity, happily embraced Sugreeva with both of his arms and replied him who is speaking 
in this way suppliantly adjoining palms at Rama. [3-39-1]_END

B_4_C_37_17
BEGIN_
क्षीर उद वेला निलयाः तमाल वन वासिनः |
नारि केल अशनाः चैव तेषाम् संख्या न विद्यते || ४-३७-२५_END
BEGIN_
The count of those vanara-s who are basically domiciled at the coasts of milky
ocean, the residents of Tamala woodlands, and those who feed on coconuts dwelling in coconut
groves, and who have presently come from those places is uncountable. [4-37-25]_END

B_4_C_30_62
BEGIN_
हंस सारस चक्राह्वैः कुररैः च समंततः |
पुलिनानि अवकीर्णानि नदीनाम् पश्य लक्ष्मण || ४-३०-६३_END
BEGIN_
"On the sand-dunes of rivers Swans, Saarasa-s, Cakravaka-s, also Kraunca birds are
fully overspreading from all over, see Lakshmana. [4-30-63]_END

B_4_C_33_44
BEGIN_
तत् च अपि जानामि यथा अविषह्यम्बलम् नरश्रेष्ठ शरीरजस्य |जानामि यस्मिन् च जने अवबद्धम्कामेन सुग्रीवम् 
अस्तकम् अद्य || ४-३३-५४_END
BEGIN_
"As to how the intensity of bodily pleasure-seeking will be highly intolerable, I am aware even of that, and I 
am equally aware of those female vanara-s with whom Sugreeva is now incessantly bound up with lust. [4-33-54]_END

B_4_C_38_10
BEGIN_
पाण्डुरेण आतपत्रेण ध्रियमाणेन मूर्धनि || ४-३८-१२शुक्लैः च वाल व्यजनैः धूयमानैः समंततः |शंख भेरी निनादैः 
च वन्दिभिः च अभिवन्दितः || ४-३८-१३निर्ययौ प्राप्य सुग्रीवो राज्य श्रियम् अनुत्तमाम् |_END
BEGIN_
Sugreeva who achieved the kingdom of unexcelled magnificence has started out that magnificently to the high extolment 
of panegyrists, while a white royal-parasol spread overhead the palanquin, white fur-fans fanning him from all 
over, and while conch-shells are blowing loud and drums are drumming high. [4-38-12b, 13, 14a]_END

B_4_C_39_1
BEGIN_
यत् इन्द्रो वर्षते वर्षम् न तत् चित्रम् भविष्यति |आदित्यो असौ सहस्रांशुः कुर्यात् वितिमिरम् नभः || ३-३९-२
चन्द्रमा रजनीम् कुर्यात् प्रभया सौम्य निर्मलाम् |त्वत् विधो वा अपि मित्राणाम् प्रीतिम् कुर्यात् परंतप || ३-३९-३_END
BEGIN_
"There is no wonder, oh, enemy-flamer, if Indra gives rain, or if that thousand-rayed sun makes the sky undark, 
or if the moon makes night shiny with his moonshine, so also oh, gentle one, if a true-friend of your kind gladdens 
his indigent-friend, there is no wonder. [3-39-2, 3]_END

B_4_C_37_18
BEGIN_
वनेभ्यो गह्वरेभ्यः च सरित्भ्यः च महाबलाः |
आगच्छत् वानरी सेना पिबन्ति इव दिवा करम् || ४-३७-२६_END
BEGIN_
That highly forceful military force of vanara-s has arrived from forests, caverns
and riversides with their leaping and bounding on the sky blocking up the sun as if they have
gulped him down. [4-37-26]_END

B_4_C_30_63
BEGIN_
चत्वारो वार्षिका मासा गता वर्ष शत उपमाः |
मम शोक अभितप्तस्य तथा सीताम् अपश्यतः || ४-३०-६४_END
BEGIN_
"Four rainy months have rolled by and to me they are like a hundred years, for I
have not seen Seetha, likewise I am seethed in grief. [4-30-64]_END

B_4_C_33_45
BEGIN_
न काम तंत्रे तव बुद्धिः अस्तित्वम् वै यथा मन्यु वशम् प्रपन्नः |न देश कालौ हि न च अर्थ धर्मौअवेक्षते 
काम रतिः मनुष्यः || ४-३३-५५_END
BEGIN_
"Gauging by your mindset which is presently bridled by fury, you appear to be disinclined towards spells of sensualities, 
thus these aspects are past your comprehension. All right! If a man were to be voluptuary he will be inadvertent 
of place and time, isn't it! Then, how about ethicalities, or rights and wrongs? [4-33-55]_END

B_4_C_38_11
BEGIN_
स वानर शतैः तीष्क्णैः बहुभिः शस्त्र पाणिभिः || ४-३८-१४परिकीर्णो ययौ तत्र यत्र रामो व्यवस्थितः |_END
BEGIN_
Sugreeva travelled thus surrounded with many hundreds of vanara-s, who look confrontational and who wielded weapons, 
to the place where Rama is staying. [4-38-14b, 15a]_END

B_4_C_39_2
BEGIN_
एवम् त्वयि तत् न चित्रम् भवेत् यत् सौम्य शोभनम् |जानामि अहम् त्वाम् सुग्रीव सततम् प्रिय वादिनम् || ३-३९-४_END
BEGIN_
"In this way, oh, nice Sugreeva, that helpful nature which is decorously prevailing in you, ushering you for organising 
the worthwhile, will not be a wonder but natural. I am aware that you have always been the exponent of affability. 
[3-39-4]_END

B_4_C_37_19
BEGIN_
ये तु त्वरयितुम् याता वानराः सर्व वानरान् |
ते वीरा हिमवत् शैले ददृशुः तम् महाद्रुमम् || ४-३७-२७_END
BEGIN_
The Vanara-s who went from Kishkindha to hasten up all the other monkeys of all
quarters, those champions have reached Himalayan Mountains and saw exceptional trees on them.
[4-37-27]_END

B_4_C_30_64
BEGIN_
चक्रवाकी इव भर्तारम् पृष्टतो अनुगता वनम् |
विषमम् दण्डकारण्यम् उद्यान वनम् इव च अंगना || ४-३०-६५_END
BEGIN_
"Like a female Cakravaka bird that follows rearward of her husband, that lady Seetha
followed her husband, that is what I am, to the precarious forest of Dandaka, as if she is going to
pleasure-gardens. [4-30-65]_END

B_4_C_33_46
BEGIN_
तम् काम वृत्तम् मम सन्निकृष्टम्काम अभियोगात् च विमुक्त लज्जम् |क्षमस्व तावत् पर वीर हन्तःतव भ्रातर्म 
वानर वंश नाथम् || ४-३३-५६_END
BEGIN_
"He who shunned decency because of the vehemence of randiness, oh, the eradicator of braving enemies, and he who 
is delighting in lust is consorted with me, ergo condone your brother-like Sugreeva, the protector of Vaanara 
dynasty. [4-33-56]_END

B_4_C_38_12
BEGIN_
स तम् देशम् अनुप्राप्य श्रेष्ठम् राम निषेवितम् || ४-३८-१५अवातरत् महातेजाः शिबिकायाः स लक्ष्मणः |_END
BEGIN_
On reaching the province where Rama is staying in all his adoration to that place, the great-resplendent Sugreeva 
descended the palanquin along with Lakshmana. [4-38-15b, 16a]_END

B_4_C_39_3
BEGIN_
त्वत् स नाथः सखे संख्ये जेता अस्मि सकलान् अरीन् |त्वम् एव मे सुहृत् मित्रम् साहाय्यम् कर्तुम् अर्हसि || ३-३९-५_END
BEGIN_
"With you as the helmsman, oh, friend, I will be triumphing over all the enemies, and you alone are worthy to 
proffer a helping hand to me as a good-hearted friend of mine. [3-39-5]_END

B_4_C_37_20
BEGIN_
तस्मिन् गिरि वरे पुण्ये यज्ञो माहेश्वरः पुरा |
सर्व देव मनः तोषो बभूव सु मनोरमः || ४-३७-२८_END
BEGIN_
On that best and auspicious mountain, once a glorious Vedic-ritual intending God
Shiva took place, which pleased the hearts of all gods. [4-37-28]_END

B_4_C_30_65
BEGIN_
प्रिया विहीने दुःख आर्ते हृत राज्ये विवासिते |
कृपाम् न कुरुते राजा सुग्रीवो मयि लक्ष्मण || ४-३०-६६_END
BEGIN_
"Dear departed, kingdom plundered, rendered homeless, and one in desperate straits,
such as I am Lakshmana, king Sugreeva is not benevolent to me. [4-30-66]_END

B_4_C_33_47
BEGIN_
महर्षयो धर्म तपोभिरामाःकामा अनुकामाः प्रति बद्ध मोहाः |अयम् प्रकृत्या चपलः कपिः तुकथम् न सज्जेत सुखेषु 
राजा || ४-३३-५७_END
BEGIN_
"Esteemed sages who take delight in their holy merit and pious asceticism, they themselves will be closely following 
the course of their desire fulfilment when entangled in lust, then how about this one, namely Sugreeva, being 
an impulsive monkey, besides being a king, how he cannot wallow in enjoyments. [4-33-57]_END

B_4_C_38_13
BEGIN_
आसाद्य च ततो रामम् कृत अंजलि पुटो अभवत् || ४-३८-१६कृत अंजलौ स्थिते तस्मिन् वानराः च अभवन् तथा |_END
BEGIN_
When Sugreeva reached Rama he stood still with adjoined-palms, and when he remained still with palm-fold all the 
other monkeys stood still with palm-fold. [4-38-16b, 17a]_END

B_4_C_39_4
BEGIN_
जहार आत्म विनाशाय वैदेहीम् राक्षस अधमः |वंचयित्वा तु पौलोमीम् अनुह्लादो यथा शचीम् || ३-३९-६_END
BEGIN_
"That knavish demon Ravana deceitfully carried off Vaidehi for his own extinction, as demon Anuhlaada carried 
off Sachi Devi, the daughter of Puloma. [3-39-6]_END

B_4_C_30_66
BEGIN_
अनाथो हृत राज्यो अयम् रावणेन च धर्षितः ||
दीनो दूर गृहः कामी माम् चैव शरणम् गतः || ४-३०-६७_END
BEGIN_
" 'He is insecure, kingdom forfeited, persecuted by Ravana, a dismal, came from a
distant home, lovelorn and sought shelter in me alone...' thus Sugreeva may be thinking of me._END

B_4_C_37_21
BEGIN_
अन्न निस्यंद जातानि मूलानि च फलानि च |
अमृत स्वादु कल्पानि ददृशुः तत्र वानराः || ४-३७-२९_END
BEGIN_
There the vanara-s have seen luscious tubers and fruits similar to nectar, which
have originated from the oblational food material spattered in the Vedic-ritual for Shiva.
[4-37-29]_END

B_4_C_33_48
BEGIN_
इति एवम् उक्त्वा वचनम् महार्थम्सा वानरी लक्ष्मणम् अप्रमेयम् |पुनः स खेदम् मद विह्वलाक्षीभर्तुर् हितम् 
वाक्यम् इदम् बभाषे || ४-३३-५८_END
BEGIN_
She that vanara female Tara whose eyes are fluttery under the influence having said this way, she again picked 
up where she left off and sentimentally spoke this sentence to Lakshmana whose brunt is inestimable, in the interest 
of her husband's wellbeing. [4-33-58]_END

B_4_C_38_14
BEGIN_
तटाकम् इव तम् दृष्ट्वा रामः कुड्मल पंकजम् || ४-३८-१७वानराणाम् महत् सैन्यम् सुग्रीवे प्रीतिमान् अभूत् |_END
BEGIN_
Rama became exultant of Sugreeva on seeing the massive army of Vanara-s which is just like a vast lake plethoric 
with buds of lotuses. [4-38-17b, 18a]_END

B_4_C_39_5
BEGIN_
न चिरात् तम् हनिष्यामि रावणम् निशितैः शरैः |पौलोम्याः पितरम् दृप्तम् शत क्रतुः इव अरिहा || ३-३९-७_END
BEGIN_
"As soon as possible I wish to eliminate that Ravana with sharp arrows, as has been done by the enemy slyer Indra 
when he eliminated the insolent father of Sachi Devi, namely Puloma." Thus Rama is about to tell other things 
to Sugreeva, but... [3-39-7]_END

B_4_C_30_67
BEGIN_
इति एतैः कारणैः सौम्य सुग्रीवस्य दुरात्मनः |
अहम् वानर राजस्य परिभूतः परंतप || ४-३०-६८_END
BEGIN_
"By these reasons, oh gentle Lakshmana, I am perhaps scoffed off by the spiteful
king of Vanara-s Sugreeva oh, the enemy-blazer, Lakshmana. [4-30-68]_END

B_4_C_37_22
BEGIN_
तत् अन्न संभवम् दिव्यम् फलम् मूलम् मनोहरम् |
यः कश्चित् सकृत् अश्नाति मासम् भवति तर्पितः || ४-३७-३०_END
BEGIN_
If one eats for one time, a little of those divine and heart-pleasing fruits and
tubers that have taken their origin from that oblational food material, he remains satiated for a
month. [4-37-30]_END

B_4_C_33_49
BEGIN_
उद्योगः तु चिर आज्ञप्तः सुग्रीवेण नरोत्तम |कांस्य अपि विधेयेन तव अर्थ प्रति साधने || ४-३३-५९_END
BEGIN_
"On the part of his endeavour in your task, oh, best one among men, he has ordered long before for its operation 
aiming to achieve your objective, despite of the fact that he is servile to overindulgence. [4-33-59]_END

B_4_C_38_15
BEGIN_
पादयोः पतितम् मूर्ध्ना तम् उत्थाप्य हरीश्वरम् || ४-३८-१८प्रेम्णा च बहुमानात् च राघवः परिषस्वजे |_END
BEGIN_
Raghava raised and tightly hugged the king of monkeys Sugreeva, who has prostrated himself with his head touching 
the feet of Rama, with care and credit. [4-38-18b, 19a]_END

B_4_C_39_6
BEGIN_
एतस्मिन् अन्तरे च एव रजः समभिवर्तत |उष्णाम् तीव्राम् सहस्रांशोः छादयत् गगने प्रभाम् || ३-३९-८_END
BEGIN_
In the meanwhile dust started to overcast the sky covering the intensely scorching radiation of the sun. [3-39-8]_END

B_4_C_30_68
BEGIN_
स कालम् परिसंख्याय सीतायाः परिमार्गणे |
कृतार्थः समयम् कृत्वा दुर्मतिः न अवबुध्यते || ४-३०-६९_END
BEGIN_
"He computed the time for search of Seetha well, and entered into a treaty with me
as well, but on achieving his means that base-minded one is unmindful of it. [4-30-69]_END

B_4_C_37_23
BEGIN_
तानि मूलानि दिव्यानि फलानि च फल अशनाः |
औषधानि च दिव्यानि जगृहुर् हरि पुंगवाः || ४-३७-३१_END
BEGIN_
The best monkeys that are fruit-eaters have collected those divine fruits, tubers,
and even the divine medicinal herbs. [4-37-31]_END

B_4_C_33_50
BEGIN_
आगता हि महा वीर्या हरयः काम रूपिणः |कोटि शत सहस्राणि नाना नग निवासिनः || ४-३३-६०_END
BEGIN_
"By all means, marvellously intrepid Vanara-s that are the residents of various mountains and that can change 
gusie just by their wish have come in hundreds, in thousands, in millions. [4-33-60]_END

B_4_C_38_16
BEGIN_
परिष्वज्य च धर्मात्मा निषीद इति ततो अब्रवीत् || ४-३८-१९निषण्णम् तम् ततो दृष्ट्वा क्षितौ रामो अब्रवीत् ततः 
|_END
BEGIN_
After hugging Sugreeva that virtue-souled Rama then said to him, "be seated." Then on seeing Sugreeva who took 
seat on ground Rama spoke to him. [4-38-19b, 20a]_END

B_4_C_39_7
BEGIN_
दिशः पर्याकुलाः च आसन् तमसा तेन दूषिताः |चचाल च मही सर्वा स शैल वन कानना || ३-३९-९_END
BEGIN_
Stained with that darkness the directions are confounded, and the entire earth together with its mountains, woods, 
and forests has wobbled. [3-39-9]_END

B_4_C_37_24
BEGIN_
तस्मात् च यज्ञ आयतनात् पुष्पाणि सुरभीणि च |
आनिन्युर् वानरा गत्वा सुग्रीव प्रिय कारणात् || ४-३७-३२_END
BEGIN_
On going to the cardinal ground of Vedic-ritual which was performed once, those
vanara-s fetched highly fragrant flowers in order to please Sugreeva. [4-37-32]_END

B_4_C_30_69
BEGIN_
स किष्किंधाम् प्रविश्य त्वम् ब्रूहि वानर पुंगवम् |
मूर्खम् ग्राम्य सुखे सक्तम् सुग्रीवम् वचनात् मम || ४-३०-७०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, enemy blazer Lakshmana, such as you are, you enter Kishkindha and upon my word
speak to that arch-vanara Sugreeva, which stupid is tangled up in uncouth pleasures. [4-30-70]_END

B_4_C_33_51
BEGIN_
तत् आगच्छ महाबाहो चारित्रम् रक्षितम् त्वया |अच्छलम् मित्र भावेन सताम् दरा अवलोकनम् || ४-३३-६१_END
BEGIN_
"Hence oh, dextrous one, get inside the palace-chambers for you have been standing here at the door coyly unwilling 
to behold womenfolk inside, and enough is this upholding of tradition by you. Oh, come on, peering at the wives 
of friends with a friendly intent is not at all impolite for good-willers." Thus Tara affectionately invited Lakshmana 
inside the palace-chambers. [4-33-61]_END

B_4_C_40_0
BEGIN_
अथ राजा समृद्ध अर्थः सुग्रीवः प्लवगेश्वरः |उवाच नरशार्दूलम् रामम् परबलार्दनम् || ४-४०-१_END
BEGIN_
The lord of fly-jumpers, king Sugreeva, who by now is replete with every means, then spoke to the tigerly-man 
and the vanquisher of enemy's might, Rama. [4-40-1]_END

B_4_C_38_17
BEGIN_
धर्मम् अर्थम् च कामम् च काले यः तु निषेवते || ४-३८-२०विभज्य सततम् वीर स राजा हरिसत्तम |_END
BEGIN_
"He alone is the king, oh, valiant Sugreeva, who always divides time for devoting himself to probity, prosperity 
and pleasure-seeking. [4-38-20b, 21a]_END

B_4_C_39_8
BEGIN_
ततो नगेन्द्र संकाशैः तीक्ष्ण दन्ष्ट्रैः महाबलैः |कृत्स्ना संछादिता भूमिः असंख्येयैः प्लवंगमैः || ३-३९-१०
निमेष अंतर मात्रेण ततः तैः हरि यूथपैः |कोटी शत परीवारैः कामरूपिभिः आवृता || ३-३९-११नादेयैः पार्वतेयैः 
च सामुद्रैः च महाबलैः |हरिभिः मेघ निर्ह्रादैः अन्यैः च वन वासिभिः || ३-३९-१२तरुण आदित्य वर्णैः च शशि गौरैः 
च वानरैः |पद्म केसर वर्णैः च श्वेतैः मेरु कृत आलयैः || ३-३९-१३_END
BEGIN_
In a split-second the entire ground is then enshrouded with incalculable fly-jumpers whose size is mountainous, 
fangs excruciating, and might abnormal, and each monkey commander is surrounded with hundreds of millions of legions 
of monkeys, who by their wish can change of their guise, and these monkeys of amazing strength have come crashing 
war-whoops as clouds letting out thunders while they are on their way from their habitation like riversides, seashores, 
mountains, and some other monkeys have come from forests as they are forest dwellers, and in the vast of masses 
their complexion alone remained as an identity to their habitation, like the stripe of tender-sun of some monkeys 
is marking them from the place of rising sun, moon-white body colour of some more telling that they are from the 
place of nightly moon, and the colour of skin looking like lotus-fibrils of many more indicates that they are 
from fertile watery lands, and the snow-white complexion of yet some more indicates that the dwelling place of 
those monkeys is Mt. Meru. [3-39-10, 11, 12, 13]_END

B_4_C_37_25
BEGIN_
ते तु सर्वे हरिवराः पृथिव्याम् सर्व वानरान् |
संचोदयित्वा त्वरितम् यूथानाम् जग्मुर् अग्रतः || ४-३७-३३_END
BEGIN_
On motivating all of the monkeys on earth, all those best monkeys who proceeded to
forgather other monkeys, quickly returned to Kishkindha ahead of the forgathered troops of monkeys.
[4-37-33]_END

B_4_C_30_70
BEGIN_
अर्थिनाम् उपपन्नानाम् पूर्वम् च अपि उपकारिणाम् |
आशाम् संश्रुत्य यो हन्ति स लोके पुरुषाधमः || ४-३०-७१_END
BEGIN_
" 'He who promises the requesters that have come under his shelter, and especially
those that have cooperated earlier, but breaks that promise, and even shatters their hope, he is
the worst fellow in the world. [4-30-71]_END

B_4_C_33_52
BEGIN_
ताराया च अभ्यनुज्ञात त्वरया चा अपि चोदितः |प्रविवेश महाबाहुः अभ्यंतरम् अरिन्दमः || ४-३३-६२_END
BEGIN_
Welcomed by Tara and hastened by haste of his duty, that dextrous enemy-destroyer Lakshmana entered the select-chambers. 
[4-33-62]_END

B_4_C_40_1
BEGIN_
आगता विनिविष्टाः च बलिनः कामरूपिणः |वानरेन्द्रा महेन्द्र आभा ये मत् विषय वासिनः || ४-४०-२_END
BEGIN_
"The mighty vanara chiefs who are guise-changers by their wish and who in sheen are like Mahendra, and who dwell 
in my province have arrived and they are properly encamped too. [4-40-2]_END

B_4_C_38_18
BEGIN_
हित्वा धर्मम् तथा अर्थम् च कामम् यः तु निषेवते || ४-३८-२१स वृक्ष अग्रे यथा सुप्तः पतितः प्रतिबुध्यते |_END
BEGIN_
"If one devotes himself to pleasure-seeking alone, casting off the probity and like that the prosperity also, 
he is like the one who slept on a treetop who awakens only after falling down. [4-38-21b, 22a]_END

B_4_C_39_9
BEGIN_
कोटी सहस्रैः दशभिः श्रीमान् परिवृतः तदा |वीरः शतबलिः नाम वानरः प्रत्यदृश्यत || ३-३९-१४_END
BEGIN_
In the meantime the arrival of a distinguished and valorous vanara named Shatabali, hemmed in with ten thousand 
crores of vanara-s, came into the view of Rama and others. [3-39-14]_END

B_4_C_30_71
BEGIN_
शुभम् वा यदि वा पापम् यो हि वाक्यम् उदीरितम् |
सत्येन परिगृह्णाति स वीरः पुरुषोत्तमः || ४-३०-७२_END
BEGIN_
" 'Whether it is good or bad, he who promises a word, and truthfully takes action
for its accomplishment, indeed he is the champion and a best one among men. [4-30-72]_END

B_4_C_37_26
BEGIN_
ते तु तेन मुहूर्तेन कपयः शीघ्र चारिणः |
किष्किंधाम् त्वरया प्राप्ताः सुग्रीवो यत्र वानरः || ४-३७-३४_END
BEGIN_
Those quick paced monkeys quickly reached Kishkindha just at that moment when
Lakshmana is still with Sugreeva, and those monkeys arrived at that place where Sugreeva is
available along with Lakshmana. [4-37-34]_END

B_4_C_33_53
BEGIN_
ततः सुग्रीवम् आसीनम् कांचने परम आसने |महाअर्ह आस्तरणोपेते ददर्श आदित्य संनिभम् || ४-३३-६३दिव्य आभरण चित्रांगम् 
दिव्य रूपम् यशस्विनम् |दिव्य माल्यांबर धरम् महेन्द्रम् इव दुर्जयम् || ४-३३-६४दिव्य आभरण माल्याभिः प्रमदाभिः 
समावृतम् |संरब्धतर रक्ताक्षो बभूव अंतक संनिभः || ४-३३-६५_END
BEGIN_
Lakshmana has then seen him who is seated like the Sun in firmament on a choicest golden seat which is elaborated 
with worthiest upholstery, whose body is remarkable besides being spruced up with excellent ornaments, who is 
wearing exquisite garlands and robes, who is glorious with a marvellous appearance and even appeared as an unconquerable 
as with Indra, and who is presently enwreathed with vanara-females who are also bedecked with precious ornamentation 
and garlands, and on seeing him Lakshmana with franticly bloodshot eyes appeared as the Terminator. [4-33-63, 
64, 65]_END

B_4_C_40_2
BEGIN_
त इमे बहु विक्रान्तैः बलिभिः भीम विक्रमैः |आगता वानरा घोरा दैत्य दानव संनिभाः || ४-४०-३_END
BEGIN_
"Those ghastly vanara-chiefs who are a match to the monsters and ogres have arrived with these diversely triumphant, 
terribly victorious and mighty vanara-soldiers. [4-40-3]_END

B_4_C_38_19
BEGIN_
अमित्राणाम् वधे युक्तो मित्राणाम् संग्रहे रतः || ४-३८-२२त्रिवर्ग फल भोक्ता च राजा धर्मेण युज्यते |_END
BEGIN_
"And the king who is bound up in eliminating unfriendly ones and bound up with forgathering friends, he will be 
enjoined with righteousness, and he even becomes the real enjoyer of the fruit of threefold virtues, namely
dharma, artha, kaama - probity, prosperity and pleasures. [4-38-22b, 23a]_END

B_4_C_39_10
BEGIN_
ततः कांचन शैल आभः ताराया वीर्यवान् पिता |अनेकैः बहु साहस्रैः कोटिभिः प्रत्यदृश्यत || ३-३९-१५_END
BEGIN_
Sushena, the father of Lady Tara, a valorous one with the sheen of golden mountain then appeared with very many 
thousands of crores of vanara-s. [3-39-15]_END

B_4_C_30_72
BEGIN_
कृतार्था हि अकृतार्थानाम् मित्राणाम् न भवन्ति ये |
तान् मृतान् अपि क्रव्यादाः कृतघ्नान् न उपभुंजते || ४-३०-७३_END
BEGIN_
" 'Indeed, those that have achieved their means through their friends, but do not
come to the rescue of the same friends whose means are still unachieved, the carrion-devourers will
not devour even the flesh of those ingrates after their death. [4-30-73]_END

B_4_C_37_27
BEGIN_
ते गृहीत्वा ओषधीः सर्वाः फल मूलम् च वानराः |
तम् प्रतिग्राहयामासुर् वचनम् च इदम् अब्रुवन् || ४-३७-३५_END
BEGIN_
Taking the medicinal herbs, fruits, and tubers along with them, all of those
Vaanaras obliged Sugreeva to accept fruits, tubers and herbs as royal gifts, and they also spoke
this word to Sugreeva. [4-37-35]_END

B_4_C_33_54
BEGIN_
रुमाम् तु वीरः परिरभ्य गाढम्वर आसनस्थो वर हेम वर्णः |ददर्श सौमित्रिम् अदीन सत्त्वम्विशाल नेत्रः स 
विशाल नेत्रम् || ४-३३-६६_END
BEGIN_
Sugreeva whose complexion is like that of rich gold is seated on an exquisite seat tightly hugging his wife Ruma, 
and that brave one has seen Lakshmana whose quintessence is never-flinching, thus, that suspiciously wide-eyed 
Sugreeva made sheep eyes at the furiously broad-eyed Lakshmana. [4-33-66]_END

B_4_C_40_3
BEGIN_
ख्यात कर्म अपदानाः च बलवन्तो जित क्लमाः |पराक्रमेषु विख्याता व्यवसायेषु च उत्तमाः || ४-४०-४पृथिवि अंबु 
चरा राम नाना नग निवासिनः |कोटि ओघाः च इमे प्राप्ता वानराः तव किंकराः || ४-४०-५_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, these vanara-s are acclaimed for undertaking impossible deeds, and they will accomplish whatever task 
they have undertaken. They are powerful ones who have overcome weariness. They are renowned for their confrontation 
and noteworthy in their manoeuvres. These who are the dwellers on diverse mountains can travel either on earth 
or on water. Such as they are these vanara-s have come in millionfold as your servants. [4-40-4, 5]_END

B_4_C_38_20
BEGIN_
उद्योग समयः तु एष प्राप्तः शत्रु निषूदन || ४-३८-२३संचिंत्यताम् हि पिंगेश हरिभिः सह मंत्रिभिः |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, enemy-eliminator, time for endeavour has come, oh, king of monkeys, let this be discussed along with your 
monkey-ministers." Thus Rama spoke to Sugreeva. [4-38-23b, 24a]_END

B_4_C_39_11
BEGIN_
तथा अपरेण कोटीनाम् साहस्रेण समन्वितः |पिता रुमयाः संप्राप्तः सुग्रीव श्वशुरो विभुः || ३-३९-१६_END
BEGIN_
Like that the most efficient vanara-chief Taara, the father of Ruma and Sugreeva's father-in-law, turned up with 
another thousand crores of vanara-s following him. [3-39-16]_END

B_4_C_37_28
BEGIN_
सर्वे परिसृताः शैलाः सरितः च वनानि च |
पृथिव्याम् वानराः सर्वे शासनात् उपयान्ति ते || ४-३७-३६_END
BEGIN_
"We have rounded up all the mountains, rivers, and forests even, and all of the
Vanara-s available on earth are fetched to your fore according to your command." Thus the monkeys
said to Sugreeva. [4-37-36]_END

B_4_C_30_73
BEGIN_
नूनम् कांचन पृष्ठस्य विकृष्टस्य मया रणे |
द्रष्टुम् इच्छसि चापस्य रूपम् विद्युत् गण उपमम् || ४-३०-७४_END
BEGIN_
" 'You definitely aspire to see that facet of the gold-spined bow of mine which in
simile will be like a cluster of electric-discharges when I fully stretch it in war. [4-30-74]_END

B_4_C_40_4
BEGIN_
निदेश वर्तिनः सर्वे सर्वे गुरु हिते स्थिताः |अभिप्रेतम् अनुष्ठातुम् तव शक्ष्यन्ति अरिंदम || ४-४०-६_END
BEGIN_
"All of them will conduct themselves in orderliness and all abide by the welfare of their king, and oh, Rama, 
the enemy-repressor, they will be able to discharge whatever task entrusted to them at your discretion. [4-40-6]_END

B_4_C_38_21
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु सुग्रीवो रामम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् || ४-३८-२४प्रनष्टा श्रीः च कीर्तिः च कपि राज्यम् च शाश्वतम् |
त्वत् प्रसादात् महाबाहो पुनः प्राप्तम् इदम् मया || ४-३८-२५_END
BEGIN_
When Rama addressed him in this way, Sugreeva said these words to Rama, "oh, dextrous Rama, by your beneficence 
I have repossessed prosperity, popularity and this everlasting kingdom of monkeys which are actually mislaid. 
[4-38-24b, 25]_END

B_4_C_39_12
BEGIN_
पद्म केसर संकाशः तरुण अर्क निभ आननः |बुद्धिमान् वानर श्रेष्ठः सर्व वानर सत्तमः || ३-३९-१७अनीकैः बहु साहस्रैः 
वानराणाम् समन्वितः |पिता हनुमतः श्रीमान् केसरी प्रत्यदृश्यत || ३-३९-१८_END
BEGIN_
Honourable Kesari, the father of Hanuma, with his bodily gleam like that of the fibrils of lotuses and visage 
glittering in the gleam of nascent sun, and who is an intellectual, graceful and prominent vanara among all the 
vanara-s, then came into view associated with thousands and thousands of armies of vanara-s. [3-39-17]_END

B_4_C_37_29
BEGIN_
एवम् श्रुत्वा ततो हृष्टः सुग्रीवः प्लवग अधिपः |
प्रतिजग्राह च प्रीतः तेषाम् सर्वम् उपायनम् || ४-३७-३७_END
BEGIN_
On listening these words then the king of fly-jumpers Sugreeva is gladdened and
accepted the gifts brought from Himalayas from all of them. [4-37-37]_END

B_4_C_30_74
BEGIN_
घोरम् ज्या तल निर्घोषम् क्रुद्धस्य मम संयुगे |
निर्घोषम् इव वज्रस्य पुनः संश्रोतुम् इच्छसि || ४-३०-७५_END
BEGIN_
" 'Once more you desire to clearly hear that calamitous crashing boom from my
bowstring, which is a soundalike with the crash of thunderbolt, when I angrily clang the unbent
bowstring in a given war. [4-30-75]_END

B_4_C_38_22
BEGIN_
तव देव प्रसदात् च भ्रातुः च जयताम् वर |कृतम् न प्रतिकुर्यात् यः पुरुषाणाम् स दूषकः || ४-३८-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, god, by your and your brother's benevolence alone I regained what I lost, oh, victorious one among victors,
