When the chiefs of monkey-troops are on their way Rama spoke to Sugreeva, "Indeed, how do you know very-well about 
the globe of earth in its entirety?" [4-46-1]_END

B_4_C_45_7
BEGIN_
एवम् संचोदिताः सर्वे राज्ञा वानर यूथपाः |
स्वाम् स्वाम् दिशम् अभिप्रेत्य त्वरिताः संप्रतस्थिरे || ४-४५-९_END
BEGIN_
In this way when despatched by their king Sugreeva all the vanara lieutenants
expeditiously started towards one's own direction. [4-45-9]_END

B_4_C_42_32
BEGIN_
शृंगे तस्य महत् दिव्यम् भवनम् सूर्य संनिभम् |
प्रासाद गण संबाधम् विहितम् विश्वकर्मणा || ४-४२-४४_END
BEGIN_
"On the pinnacle of Mt. Astagiri, or the Mt. Dusk, there is a supreme and heavenly
manor-house compacted with multi-storied buildings, which in shine will be similar to Sun and which
is arranged by Vishvakarma, the Divine Architect. [4-42-44]_END

B_4_C_43_24
BEGIN_
वसन्ति हि महात्मानः तत्र सूर्य सम प्रभाः |
देवैः अभ्यर्थिताः सम्यक् देव रूपा महर्षयः || ४-४३-२६_END
BEGIN_
"In that tunnel great-souled sages reside at the request of gods, and those
great-sages are similar to Sun in their resplendence and godly in their mien. Even then, you search
for Ravana therein that tunnel. [4-43-26]_END

B_4_C_44_14
BEGIN_
स तत् गृह्य हरिश्रेष्ठः स्थाप्य मूर्ध्नि कृतांजलिः |वन्दित्वा चरणौ चैव प्रस्थितः प्लवगर्षभः || ४-४४-१५_END
BEGIN_
On taking the ring that foremost monkey Hanuma kept it on his own head, and making palm-fold he reverenced the 
feet of Rama, and then that noteworthy monkey started off. [4-44-15]_END

B_4_C_46_1
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवः च ततो रामम् उवाच प्रणत आत्मवान् |श्रूयताम् सर्वम् आख्यास्ये विस्तरेण वचो मम || ४-४६-२_END
BEGIN_
Then Sugreeva bowing down before Rama said, "I will narrate all vividly, and let my words be heard." [4-46-2]_END

B_4_C_45_8
BEGIN_
नदन्तः च उन्नदन्तः च गर्जन्तः च प्लवंगमाः |
क्ष्वेलन्तो धावमानाः च विनदन्तो महाबलाः || ४-४५-१०_END
BEGIN_
When those great mighty fly-jumpers have started to dash off some are bawling, some
highly blaring, some more thundering, and some more oddly bellowing, while some more are roaring
like lions. [4-45-10]_END

B_4_C_42_33
BEGIN_
शोभितम् तरुभिः चित्रैः नाना पक्षि समाकुलैः |
निकेतम् पाश हस्तस्य वरुणस्य महात्मनः || ४-४२-४५_END
BEGIN_
"That villa is brightened by amazing trees, on which diverse birds will be
twittering musically, belongs to the great-souled Varuna, the Rain-god, who wields a tether.
[4-42-45]_END

B_4_C_44_15
BEGIN_
स तत् प्रकर्षन् हरिणाम् महत् बलम्बभूव वीरः पवनात्मजः कपिः |गत अंबुदे व्योम्नि विशुद्ध मण्डलःशशी इव 
नक्षत्र गणोपशोभितः || ४-४४-१६_END
BEGIN_
That brave monkey-son of Air-god leapt to sky along with that massive force of monkeys as if he is hauling them 
up, and he who is brightened by monkeys around him on the skyscape appeared like the moon in a very clear lunar 
sphere on a cloudless sky brightened by clusters of stars around. [4-44-16]_END

B_4_C_43_25
BEGIN_
क्रौन्चस्य तु गुहाः च अन्याः सानूनि शिखराणि च |
निर्दराः च नितंबाः च विचेतव्याः ततः ततः || ४-४३-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Besides the main peak of Mt. Kraunca, its other peaks, terraces, crevices and
midriffs shall be searched, far and wide. [4-43-27]_END

B_4_C_46_2
BEGIN_
यदा तु दुंदुभिम् नाम दानवम् महिष आकृतिम् |परिकालयते वाली मलयम् प्रति पर्वतम् || ४-४६-३तदा विवेश महिषो 
मलयस्य गुहाम् प्रति |विवेश वाली तत्र अपि मलयम् तत् जिघांसया || ४-४६-४_END
BEGIN_
"When Vali repulsed the buffalo-shaped demon Dundubhi towards Malaya mountain, then that buffalo entered the cave 
of Mt. Malaya, and even Vali entered therein wishing to kill that buffalo. [4-46-3, 4]_END

B_4_C_45_9
BEGIN_
एवम् संचोदिताः सर्वे राज्ञा वानर यूथपाः |
आनयिष्यामहे सीताम् हनिष्यामः च रावणम् || ४-४५-११_END
BEGIN_
Well-motivated this way by the king Sugreeva those vanara lieutenants put their
fortitude into boastful words and said, "we lead forth Seetha, we wish to kill Ravana."
[4-45-11]_END

B_4_C_42_34
BEGIN_
अन्तरा मेरुम् अस्तम् च तालो दश शिरा महान् |
जातरूपमयः श्रीमान् भ्राजते चित्र वेदिकः || ४-४२-४६_END
BEGIN_
"In between Mt. Meru and Mt. Astaadri there is a gigantic ten-leaved Date-palm-tree,
which is completely golden and shines forth with a marvellous podium. [4-42-46]_END

B_4_C_44_16
BEGIN_
अतिबल बलम् आश्रितः तव अहम्हरि वर विक्रम विक्रमैः अनल्पैः |पवन सुत यथा अधिगम्यते साजनक सुता हनुमन् 
तथा कुरुष्व || ४-४४-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, highly powerful Hanuma, I rely upon your vivacity, being the best venturesome monkey, oh, son of Air-god, 
showing your adventures that are not inconsequential you make happen as to how access can be gained to Janaka's 
daughter, Seetha." Thus, Rama shouted at Hanuma flying in the sky. [4-44-17]_END

B_4_C_43_26
BEGIN_
अवृक्षम् काम शैलम् च मानसम् विहग आलयम् |
न गतिः तत्र भूतानाम् देवानाम् न च रक्षसाम् || ४-४३-२८_END
BEGIN_
"The treeless Mt. Kaama and the abode of birds Mt. Maanasa are also to be searched,
and there is no inlet for any being, let alone gods or demons. [4-43-28]_END

B_4_C_46_3
BEGIN_
ततो अहम् तत्र निक्षिप्तो गुहा द्वारि विनीतवत् |न च निष्क्रमते वाली तदा संवत्सरे गते || ४-४६-५_END
BEGIN_
"Vali then kept me at the mouth of the cave as I was an amenable brother, but Vali did not exit from cave even 
after one full year. [4-46-5]_END

B_4_C_45_10
BEGIN_
अहम् एको वधिष्यामि प्राप्तम् रावणम् आहवे |
ततः च उन्मथ्य सहसा हरिष्ये जनक आत्मजाम् || ४-४५-१२_END
BEGIN_
"I will kill Ravana single-handedly if he chances on battlefield, and then on
drubbing the other demons I will quickly bring back Janaka's daughter, Seetha." Another monkey
soldier said so. [4-45-12]_END

B_4_C_42_35
BEGIN_
तेषु सर्वेषु दुर्गेषु सरस्सु च सरित्सु च |
रावणः सह वैदेह्या मार्गितव्यः ततः ततः || ४-४२-४७_END
BEGIN_
"On all those mountains, lakesides and riversides Vaidehi shall be searched together
with Ravana, far and wide. [4-42-47]_END

B_4_C_43_27
BEGIN_
स च सर्वैः विचेतव्यः स सानु प्रस्थ भूधरः |
क्रौन्चम् गिरिम् अतिक्रम्य मैनाको नाम पर्वतः || ४-४३-२९_END
BEGIN_
"You all have to search Mt. Kraunca inclusive of its mountainsides, grades, and its
fringe mountains, and on moving away from that Mt. Kraunca, a mountain named Mainaaka is there.
[4-43-29]_END

B_4_C_46_4
BEGIN_
ततः क्षतज वेगेन आपुपूरे तदा बिलम् |तत् अहम् विस्मितो दृष्ट्वा भ्रातुः शोक विष अर्दितः || ४-४६-६_END
BEGIN_
"I was dumbfounded to see that cave is then fully filled with blood, and then a venom like anguish called the 
loss of my brother agonised me. [4-46-6]_END

B_4_C_45_11
BEGIN_
वेपमानम् श्रमेण अद्य भवद्भिः स्थीयताम् इति |
एक एव आहरिष्यामि पातालात् अपि जानकीम् || ४-४५-१३_END
BEGIN_
"I alone will bring back Janaki even from netherworlds, who might be shivering owing
to enervation, and you my monkey-soldier colleagues, you all may stay behind now." Thus another
monkey-hero said. [4-45-13]_END

B_4_C_42_36
BEGIN_
यत्र तिष्ठति धर्मज्ञः तपसा स्वेन भावितः |
मेरु सावर्णिर् इति एष ख्यातो वै ब्रह्मणा समः || ४-४२-४८_END
BEGIN_
"This is where the virtue-knower, an enlightened one by his own asceticism, a
selfsame personality to Brahma and one renowned as Sage Merusaavarni indeed resides. [4-42-48]_END

B_4_C_43_28
BEGIN_
मयस्य भवनम् तत्र दानवस्य स्वयम् कृतम् |
मैनाकः तु विचेतव्यः स सानु प्रस्थ कंदरः || ४-४३-३०
स्त्रीणाम् अश्व मुखीनाम् च निकेताः तत्र तत्र तु |_END
BEGIN_
"The mansion of the demon Maya is there which is built by himself and that Mt.
Mainaaka is to be searched out, inclusive of its crests, grades and caves. Thereabout the dwellings
of horse-faced females, namely KimpuruSa-s, are there and you have to search them also. [4-43-30,
31a]_END

B_4_C_46_5
BEGIN_
अथ अहम् गत बुद्धिः तु सुव्यक्तम् निहतो गुरुः |शिला पर्वत संकाशा बिल द्वारि मया कृता || ४-४६-७अशक्नुवन् 
निष्क्रमितुम् महिषो विनशिष्यति |_END
BEGIN_
"Then I concluded that 'my brother is unmistakably killed,' and then I fixed a mountain similar boulder in the 
mouth of that cavity with a thinking that it will be impossible for that buffalo to exit and it will get destroyed 
within that cave itself. [4-46-7, 8a]_END

B_4_C_45_12
BEGIN_
विधमिष्यामि अहम् वृक्षान् दारयिष्यामि अहम् गिरीन् |
धरणीम् दारयिष्यामि क्षोभयिष्यामि सागरान् || ४-४५-१४_END
BEGIN_
"I will completely shatter the trees, shred the mountains, split the earth and storm
the oceans." Thus another monkey gave war cry. [4-45-14]_END

B_4_C_42_37
BEGIN_
प्रष्टव्यो मेरुसावर्णिः महर्षिः सूर्य संनिभः |
प्रणम्य शिरसा भूमौ प्रवृत्तिम् मैथिलीम् प्रति || ४-४२-४९_END
BEGIN_
"And that sage Merusaavarni who is Sun-similar in his shine can be asked, only on
your prostration before him in veneration, about the tidings of Maithili, and her whereabouts.
[4-42-49]_END

B_4_C_43_29
BEGIN_
तम् देशम् समतिक्रम्य आश्रमम् सिद्ध सेवितम् || ४-४३-३१
सिद्धा वैखानसाः तत्र वालखिल्याः च तापसाः |_END
BEGIN_
"On crossing over that province there is the hermitage adored by siddha-s, the
resolved-souls. There the sages, namely siddha-s, vaikhaanasa-s, and vaalakhilyaa-s will be there.
[4-43-31b, 32a]_END

B_4_C_46_6
BEGIN_
ततो अहम् आगाम् किष्किंधाम् निराशः तस्य जीविते || ४-४६-८राज्यम् च सुमहत् प्राप्य ताराम् च रुमया सह |मित्रैः 
च सहितः तत्र वसामि विगत ज्वरः || ४-४६-९_END
BEGIN_
"Unhopeful of Vali's aliveness then I arrived in Kishkindha, and on getting the very magnificent kingdom of Kishkindha, 
and also Ruma along with Tara, I was peaceably staying there with friends. [4-46-8, 9]_END

B_4_C_45_13
BEGIN_
अहम् योजन संख्यायाः प्लविता न अत्र संशयः |
शतम् योजन संख्यायाः शतम् समधिकम् हि अहम् || ४-४५-१५_END
BEGIN_
"I can fly-jump a hundred yojana-s, undoubtedly," said one monkey while the other
said, "I can jump even more than a hundred yojana-s, for sure." [4-45-15]_END

B_4_C_42_38
BEGIN_
एतावत् जीव लोकस्य भास्करो रजनी क्षये |
कृत्वा वितिमिरम् सर्वम् अस्तम् गच्छति पर्वतम् || ४-४२-५०_END
BEGIN_
"On effacing the utter darkness of all the mortal world up to here, the illuminator
of mortal world and the decliner of night, namely the Sun, will go to the Mt. Astagiri, say Mt.
Dusk. [4-42-50]_END

B_4_C_43_30
BEGIN_
वन्दितव्याः ततः सिद्धाः तापसा वीत कल्मषाः || ४-४३-३२
प्रष्टव्याः च अपि सीतायाः प्रवृत्तिम् विनय अन्वितैः |_END
BEGIN_
"Then you venerate those sages with accomplished souls, whose asceticism alone has
effaced their blemishes, and you may even humbly ask them after Seetha's whereabouts. [4-43-32b,
33a]_END

B_4_C_47_0
BEGIN_
दर्शनार्थम् तु वैदेह्याः सर्वतः कपि कुंजराः |
व्यादिष्टाः कपि राजेन यथा उक्तम् जग्मुर् अंजसा || ४-४७-१_END
BEGIN_
As commanded by the king of monkeys Sugreeva all of the elephantine monkeys essayed
everywhere with post-hast for a glimpse of Vaidehi. [4-47-1]_END

B_4_C_46_7
BEGIN_
आजगाम ततो वाली हत्वा तम् दानवर्षभः |ततो अहम् अददाम् राज्यम् गौरवात् भय यंत्रितः || ४-४६-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Vali then came back to Kishkindha on killing that great demon, and then I was spellbound in fear of Vali's killing 
me, and I gave back the kingdom to Vali owing to my deference to him. [4-46-10]_END

B_4_C_45_14
BEGIN_
भू तले सागरे वा अपि शैलेषु च वनेषु च |
पातालस्य अपि वा मध्ये न मम आच्छिद्यते गतिः || ४-४५-१६_END
BEGIN_
"My transit cannot be thwarted either on the plane of earth, or in the ocean, or on
mountains or in forests, or in the netherworld, or in its core." This is the slogan of another
monkey-warrior. [4-45-16]_END

B_4_C_42_39
BEGIN_
एतावत् वानरैः शक्यम् गन्तुम् वानर पुंगवाः |
अभास्करम् अमर्यादम् न जानीमः ततः परम् || ४-४२-५१_END
BEGIN_
"It is possible for the vanara-s to go only up to there, oh, best vanara-s, and we
have no knowledge of those sunless and boundless realms available far and beyond. [4-42-51]_END

B_4_C_43_31
BEGIN_
हेम पुष्कर संछन्नम् तत्र वैखानसम् सरः || ४-४३-३३
तरुण आदित्य संकाशैः हंसैः विचरितम् शुभैः |_END
BEGIN_
"There is the lake belonging to Vaikhaanasa sages, overspread with golden lotuses,
and overrun with prosperous swans whose resplendence will be similar to the tender sun. [4-43-33b,
34a]_END

B_4_C_47_1
BEGIN_
ते सरांसि सरित् कक्षान् आकाशम् नगराणि च |
नदी दुर्गान् तथा शैलान् विचिन्वन्ति समन्ततः || ४-४७-२_END
BEGIN_
Those monkeys have thoroughly searched at lakes, in the pens of creepers on
riverbanks, in vacant lands and in crowded cities and at impassable places with rivers and
mountains. [4-47-2]_END

B_4_C_46_8
BEGIN_
स माम् जिघांसुः दुष्टात्मा वाली प्रव्यथित इन्द्रियः |परिकालयते क्रोधात् धावंतम् सचिवैः सह || ४-४६-११_END
BEGIN_
"That evil-minded Vali becoming highly perturbed at his senses furiously repulsed me further and further away, 
even though I was running away from him with my ministers, as he wished to kill me. [4-46-11]_END

B_4_C_45_15
BEGIN_
इति एकैकः तदा तत्र वानरा बल दर्पिताः |
ऊचुः च वचनम् तस्य हरि राजस्य सन्निधौ || ४-४५-१७_END
BEGIN_
Thus each individual vanara gave war-whoops with the proper proud of his might in
the audience of monkeys king Sugreeva and departed. [4-45-17]_END

B_4_C_42_40
BEGIN_
अवगम्य तु वैदेहीम् निलयम् रावणस्य च |
अस्तम् पर्वतम् आसाद्य पूर्णे मासे निवर्तत || ४-४२-५२_END
BEGIN_
"You shall return within a month on knowing about Vaidehi and also about the
residency of Ravana, or on your reaching Mt. Astagiri, say Mt. Dusk. [4-42-52]_END

B_4_C_43_32
BEGIN_
औपवाह्यः कुबेरस्य सर्वभौम इति स्मृतः || ४-४३-३४
गजः पर्येति तम् देशम् सदा सह करेणुभिः |_END
BEGIN_
"The carrier elephant of Kubera known as Saarvabhauma will always be visiting that
place along with she-elephants. [4-43-34b, 35a]_END

B_4_C_47_2
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवेण समाख्याताः सर्वे वानर यूथपाः |
तत्र देशान् प्रविचिन्वन्ति स शैल वन काननान् || ४-४७-३_END
BEGIN_
All the monkey commanders explicitly commanded by Sugreeva, very carefully searched all the provinces inclusive of mountains,
woodlands, and thick forests of those provinces. [4-47-3]_END

B_4_C_46_9
BEGIN_
ततो अहम् वालिना तेन सानुबन्धः प्रधावितः |नदीः च विविधाः पश्यन् वनानि नगराणि च || ४-४६-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Such as I was, who is repulsed by Vali, I was made to run away rapidly, and during that fleeing I went on seeing 
diverse rivers, forests and cities. [4-46-12]_END

B_4_C_42_41
BEGIN_
ऊर्ध्वम् मासान् न वस्तव्यम् वसन् वध्यो भवेन् मम |
सह एव शूरो युष्माभिः श्वशुरो मे गमिष्यति || ४-४२-५३_END
BEGIN_
"And none shall stay behind for more than a month, and if anyone stays, I have to
exercise coup de grace in his respect. By the way, my valorous father-in-law, namely Sushena, is
proceeding along with you. [4-42-53]_END

B_4_C_43_33
BEGIN_
तत् सारः समतिक्रम्य नष्ट चन्द्र दिवाकरम् |
अनक्षत्र गणम् व्योम निष्पयोदम् अनाअदितम् || ४-४३-३५_END
BEGIN_
"Passing that lake there will be just sky which will be devoid of moon, or sun, or
the clusters of stars, and it will be cloudless and noiseless. [4-43-35b, c]_END

B_4_C_47_3
BEGIN_
विचिन्त्य दिवसम् सर्वे सीता अधिगमने धृताः |
समायान्ति स्म मेदिन्याम् निशा कालेषु वानराः || ४-४७-४_END
BEGIN_
All the Vanara-s firmed up in finding Seetha have searched nooks and corners of
earth by day, and at nighttimes they used to come together onto earth at scheduled places.
[4-47-4]_END

B_4_C_46_10
BEGIN_
आदर्श तल संकाशा ततो वै पृथिवी मया |अलात चक्र प्रतिमा दृष्टा गोष्पदवत् तदा - कृता || ४-४६-१३_END
BEGIN_
"I have then really seen the earth as in the reflection on the surface of a mirror, where the mirror shows all 
the objects in exactness, and the earth is like the circle of a fireball, where it is encircled with fire-like 
reddish, brownish, ochreish minerals and ores, and it appeared to me in my high flight like a cow-hoof-print in 
the mirror, called my perception. [4-46-13]_END

B_4_C_42_42
BEGIN_
श्रोतव्यम् सर्वम् एतस्य भवद्भिः दिष्ट कारिभिः |
गुरुः एष महाबाहुः श्वशुरो मे महाबलः || ४-४२-५४_END
BEGIN_
"As achievers of ordered tasks you shall give heed to all of the orders given by
him. He who is highly dextrous and great mighty such a Sushena is my father-in-law, thus he is a
venerable to me, as well as to you. [4-42-54]_END

B_4_C_43_34
BEGIN_
गभस्तिभिः इव अर्कस्य स तु देशः प्रकाशते |
विश्राम्यद्भिः तपः सिद्धैः देव कल्पैः स्वयंप्रभैः || ४-४३-३६_END
BEGIN_
"That place will be luminescent with the self-resplendence of godlike sages who have
accomplished their asceticism and who are taking rest at that place, as if illuminated with
innumerable rays of the sun. [4-43-36]_END

B_4_C_47_4
BEGIN_
सर्व ऋतुकान् च देशेषु वानराः स फलान् द्रुमान् |
आसाद्य रजनीम् शय्याम् चक्रुः सर्वेषु अहस्सु ते || ४-४७-५_END
BEGIN_
In all those days those Vanara-s used to come to trees which have fruits of all
seasons, to make those trees as their beds at bedtime. [4-47-5]_END

B_4_C_46_11
BEGIN_
पूर्वम् दिशाम् ततो गत्वा पश्यामि विविधान् द्रुमान् |पर्वतान् स दरीन् रम्यान् सरांसि विविधानि च || ४-४६-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Then on going to eastern direction I saw various trees, enchanting mountains with caves, and also numerous lakes. 
[4-46-14]_END

B_4_C_42_43
BEGIN_
भवन्तः च अपि विक्रान्ताः प्रमाणम् सर्वे एव हि |
प्रमाणम् एनम् संस्थाप्य पश्यध्वम् पश्चिमाम् दिशम् || ४-४२-५५_END
BEGIN_
"Even all of you are triumphant ones and indeed archetypes by yourselves, but
instituting him as your archetype you shall search the western direction. [4-42-55]_END

B_4_C_43_35
BEGIN_
तम् तु देशम् अतिक्रम्य शैलोदा नाम निम्नगा |
उभयोः तीरयोः तस्याः कीचका नाम वेणवः || ४-४३-३७
ते नयंति परम् तीरम् सिद्धान् प्रत्यानयन्ति च |_END
BEGIN_
"On crossing over that province there is a deep flowing river named Shailoda. On
both of its riverbanks bamboo brakes called as Keecaka-s will be there. Those bamboos will be
enabling the movement of siddha-s, accomplished souls, from one bank to the other. [4-43-37,
38a]_END

B_4_C_47_5
BEGIN_
तत् अहः प्रथमम् कृत्वा मासे प्रस्रवणम् गताः |
कपि राजेन संगम्य निराशाः कपि कुंजराः || ४-४७-६_END
BEGIN_
Counting the day of their starting as day one, those elephantine monkeys returned to
Mt. Prasavana within one month, hopeless of Seetha, and met Sugreeva, the king of monkeys, who is
with Rama awaiting the return of monkeys. [4-47-6]_END

B_4_C_46_12
BEGIN_
उदयम् तत्र पश्यामि पर्वतम् धातु मण्डितम् |क्षीरोदम् सागरम् चैव नित्यम् अप्सर आलयम् || ४-४६-१५_END
BEGIN_
"There I saw the mountain wreathed in with ores, namely Mt. Udaya, the Sun-Rise, and I have also seen the Milk 
Water Oceans which is forever an abode for apsara-s. [4-46-15]_END

B_4_C_42_44
BEGIN_
दृष्टायाम् तु नरेन्द्रस्या पत्न्याम् अमित तेजसः |
कृत कृत्या भविष्यामः कृतस्य प्रतिकर्मणा || ४-४२-५६_END
BEGIN_
"We all fulfil ourselves in reciprocating him who has done good to us, only if we
can locate Seetha, the wife of the king of humans whose vitality is unlimited, namely Rama.
[4-42-56]_END

B_4_C_47_6
BEGIN_
विचित्य तु दिशम् पूर्वाम् यथा उक्ताम् सचिवैः सह |
अदृष्ट्वा विनतः सीताम् आजगाम महाबलः || ४-४७-७_END
BEGIN_
Cmdr. Vinata, the great-mighty vanara, came back after searching eastern quarter as
Sugreeva had advised, but without finding Seetha there. [4-47-7]_END

B_4_C_43_36
BEGIN_
उत्तराः कुरवः तत्र कृत पुण्य प्रतिश्रियाः || ४-४३-३८
ततः कांचन पद्माभिः पद्मिनीभिः कृतोदकाः |
नील वैदूर्य पत्राढ्या नद्यः तत्र सहस्रशः || ४-४३-३९
रक्तोत्पल वनैः च अत्र मण्डिताः च हिरण्मयैः |_END
BEGIN_
"Then there is the North Kuru, the dwelling of those who have achieved divine merit
in their previous births and now born in that country to enjoy the fruits of that divine merit,
thus that country itself is earmarked for meritorious beings. At that place, the lotuses in the
rivers will be golden in hue. The runners and stalks of lotus plants bear lotus-leaves that are
bluish like the bluishness of lapis lazuli. There will be thousands of such rivers filled with such
plants in water, and with waters mingled with the waters of other lakes, and decorated with the
thickets of red Costuses alongshore. [4-43-38b, 39, 40a]_END

B_4_C_46_13
BEGIN_
परिकाल्यमानः तदा वालिना अभिद्रुतः हि अहम् |पुनः आवृत्य सहसा प्रस्थितो अहम् तदा विभो || ४-४६-१६_END
BEGIN_
"I fled speedily when Vali repulsed me, but oh, lord Rama, when I returned he again made me to flee forthwith. 
[4-46-16]_END

B_4_C_42_45
BEGIN_
अतो अन्यत् अपि यत् कार्यम् कार्यस्य अस्य प्रियम् भवेत् |
संप्रधार्य भवद्भिः च देश काल अर्थ संहितम् || ४-४२-५७_END
BEGIN_
"Even if any other task than this is there, that which shall be conducive to this
task, and which shall also be conducive to time, place and purpose, you shall undertake that task
also on deciding about it among yourselves." Sugreeva spoke thus to the monkeys going to western
direction. [4-42-57]_END

B_4_C_43_37
BEGIN_
तरुण आदित्य संकाशा भान्ति तत्र जलाशयाः || ४-४३-४०
महाअर्ह मणि पत्रैः च कांचन प्रभ केसरैः |
नीलोत्पल वनैः चित्रैः स देशः सर्वतो वृतः || ४-४३-४१_END
BEGIN_
"Everywhere that province shines forth with highly valuable leaves which will be in
the hue of sapphires, with fibrils in the hue of gold, and with amazing thickets of blue costuses
around lakes, which lakes will be surrounding that province with a resplendence similar to sun.
[4-43-40b, 41]_END

B_4_C_47_7
BEGIN_
दिशम् अपि उत्तराम् सर्वाम् विविच्य स महाकपिः |
आगतः सह सैन्येन वीरः शतबलिः तदा || ४-४७-८_END
BEGIN_
Even the valiant and matchless monkey Shatabali explored whole of the northern
direction along with his army, but he too came back as Seetha is undiscovered there. [4-47-8]_END

B_4_C_46_14
BEGIN_
दिशः तस्याः ततो भूयः प्रस्थितो दक्षिणम् दिशम् |विन्ध्य पादप संकीर्णाम् चन्दन द्रुम शोभिताम् || ४-४६-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Then from that eastern direction I fled to southern direction, which is thick with Vindhya Range mountains and 
diverse trees, especially with sandalwood trees. [4-46-17]_END

B_4_C_42_46
BEGIN_
ततः सुषेण प्रमुखाः प्लवंगमाः
सुग्रीव वाक्यम् निपुणम् निशम्य |
आमंत्र्य सर्वे प्लवगाधिपम् ते
जग्मुर् दिशम् ताम् वरुण अभिगुप्ताम् || ४-४२-५८_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the sentences of Sugreeva sedulously, then Sushena and the other
important fly-jumpers took leave of the king of fly-jumpers, namely Sugreeva, and proceeded along
with their individual troops to that western direction which is well cloistered by Varuna, the
Rain-god. [4-42-58]_END

B_4_C_47_8
BEGIN_
सुषेणः पश्चिमाम् आशाम् विविच्य सह वानरैः |
समेत्य मासे पूर्णे तु सुग्रीवम् उपचक्रमे || ४-४७-९_END
BEGIN_
Sushena, the father-in-law of Sugreeva, searching whole of western quarter along
with vanara-s, but not finding Seetha there, he came back when one month is completed, and
approached Sugreeva. [4-47-9]_END

B_4_C_46_15
BEGIN_
द्रुम शैल अन्तरे पश्यन् भूयो दक्षिणतो अपराअम् |अपराम् च दिशम् प्राप्तो वालिना समभिद्रुतः || ४-४६-१८_END
BEGIN_
"While I was seeing the interiors of forest and mountains again I was made to run by Vali, who was setting upon 
me from within the interiors of those forests and mountains, and then I reached the western direction. [4-46-18]_END

B_4_C_43_38
BEGIN_
निस्तुलाभिः च मुक्ताभिः मणिभिः च महाधनैः |
उद्भूत पुलिनाः तत्र जातरूपैः च निम्नगाः || ४-४३-४२_END
BEGIN_
"There the sand dunes of deep flowing rivers are lumped together with incomparable
pearls, highly valuable jewels and gold. [4-43-42]_END

B_4_C_46_16
BEGIN_
स पश्यन् विविधान् देशान् अस्तम् च गिरि सत्तमम् |प्राप्य च अस्तम् गिरि श्रेष्ठम् उत्तरम् संप्रधावितः || ४-४६-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Such as I was, on seeing diverse cities and the best mountain Astagiri, Mt. Dusk, I reached that excellent Mt. 
Dusk also, and since Vali is at my heel, I took to my heels, by a long way to north. [4-46-19]_END

B_4_C_47_9
BEGIN_
तम् प्रस्रवण पृष्ठस्थम् समासाद्य अभिवाद्य च |
आसीनम् सह रामेण सुग्रीवम् इदम् अब्रुवन् || ४-४७-१०_END
BEGIN_
All of the expeditionists have reached and venerated Sugreeva who is sitting along
with Rama on the peak of Mt. Prasavana and spoke this to him. [4-47-10]_END

B_4_C_43_39
BEGIN_
सर्व रत्नमयैः चित्रैः अवगाढा नगोत्तमैः |
जातरूपमयैः च अपि हुताशन सम प्रभैः || ४-४३-४३_END
BEGIN_
"That province is with amazing mountains that are replete with every kind of jewel,
golden in hue, splendorous like Ritual-fire, and they are intercalated into the deep flowing
rivers. [4-43-43]_END

B_4_C_47_10
BEGIN_
विचिताः पर्वताः सर्वे वनानि गहनानि च |
निम्नगाः सागर अन्ताः च सर्वे जनपदाः तथा || ४-४७-११_END
BEGIN_
"All of the mountains, all of the serried forests, all of the riversides up to the
edge of oceans, likewise, all of the inhabitations have been searched. [4-47-11]_END

B_4_C_46_17
BEGIN_
हिमवंतम् च मेरुम् च समुद्रम् च तथा उत्तरम् |यदा न विन्दे शरणम् वालिना समभिद्रुतः || ४-४६-२०ततो माम् बुद्धि 
संपन्नो हनुमान् वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_
"Even at Himalayas, Mt. Meru, like that at the Northern Ocean, Vali drove me back, and when the clemency from 
Vali, or a shelter, or even a foothold on earth was indeterminable, then Hanuma, whose prosperity is his wisdom, 
said a word to me. [4-46-20, 21a]_END

B_4_C_43_40
BEGIN_
नित्य पुष्प फलाः तत्र नगाः पत्ररथ आकुलाः |
दिव्य गन्ध रस स्पर्शाः सर्व कामान् स्रवन्ति च || ४-४३-४४
नाना आकाराणि वासांसि फलन्ति अन्ये नगोत्तमाः |_END
BEGIN_
"There the trees will be eternally flowering and fruiting on which birds will be
endlessly squawking. Their yield will be spilling forth meeting every delicacy with a divine smell,
taste and touch. Some other best trees will yield clothing in numerous shapes. [4-43-44, 45a]_END

B_4_C_47_11
BEGIN_
गुहाः च विचिताः सर्वा याः च ते परिकीर्तिताः |
विचिताः च महागुल्मा लता वितत संतताः || ४-४७-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Those caves that were explicitly extolled by you, they are all thoroughly searched,
and immense shrubby hutches that are thickly entwined with climber plants have also been rummaged.
[4-47-12]_END

B_4_C_46_18
BEGIN_
इदानीम् मे स्मृतम् राजन् यथा वाली हरीश्वरः || ४-४६-२१मतंगेन तदा शप्तो हि अस्मिन् आश्रम मण्डले |प्रविशेत् 
यदि वै वाली मूर्धा अस्य शतधा भवेत् || ४-४६-२२तत्र वासः सुखो अस्माकम् निर्उद्विग्नो भविष्यति |_END
BEGIN_
" 'Oh, king Sugreeva, now I remember how Sage Matanga cursed the king of monkeys Vali at that time. If Vali really 
enters the fringes of the hermitage of Sage Matanga, Vali's head gets splintered in hundred ways. Hence dwelling 
in sage Matanga's hermitage will be peaceful and imperturbable for us.' Thus Hanuma spoke to me. [4-46-21b, 22, 
23a]_END

B_4_C_43_41
BEGIN_
मुक्ता वैदूर्य चित्राणि भूषणानि तथैव च |
स्त्रीणाम् यानि अनुरूपाणि पुरुषाणाम् तथैव च || ४-४३-४५
सर्व ऋतु सुख सेव्यानि फलन्ति अन्ये नगोत्तमाः |
महा अर्हाणि मणि चित्राणि फलन्ति अन्ये नगोत्तमाः || ४-४३-४६_END
BEGIN_
"Some of the best trees will be yielding such of those adornments which will be
vying with ornament made with pearls or with lapis gemstones, and suitable both for women and men.
Like that, they can be worn happily in all seasons. Some other best trees will be yielding gemlike
marvellous decorations applicable to noblesse. [4-43-45, 46]_END

B_4_C_48_0
BEGIN_
सह तार अंगदाभ्याम् तु सहसा हनुमान् कपिः |
सुग्रीवेण यथा उद्दिष्टम् तम् देशम् उपचक्रमे || ४-४८-१_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma, the monkey, quickly started along with Angada, Lt. Tara, and others to that
province which Sugreeva has indicated, namely the south. [4-48-1]_END

B_4_C_46_19
BEGIN_
ततः पर्वतम् आसाद्य ऋश्यमूकम् नृपात्मज || ४-४६-२३न विवेश तदा वाली मतंगस्य भयात् तदा |एवम् मया तदा राजन् 
प्रत्यक्षम् उपलक्षितम् |पृथिवी मण्डलम् सर्वम् गुहाम् अस्मि आगतः ततः || ४-४६-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, prince Rama, then Vali though reached Mt. Rishyamuka, he did not enter into its precincts at that time fearing 
Sage Matanga and his curse, oh, king Rama, thus this globe of earth is apparently and closely sighted by me in 
its entirety, and then I came into the cave of Rishyamuka and did not stir out." So said Sugreeva to Rama. [4-46-23b, 
24]_END

B_4_C_47_12
BEGIN_
गहनेषु च देशेषु दुर्गेषु विषमेषु च |
सत्त्वानि अतिप्रमाणानि विचितानि हतानि च |
ये चैव गहना देशा विचिताः ते पुनः पुनः || ४-४७-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Search is conducted in the compacted, lopsided, and impenetrable provinces, and
colossal beings are hunted out and killed presuming that Ravana might have assumed those odd
shapes, and the impassable provinces are searched high and low, time and again. [4-47-13]_END

B_4_C_43_42
BEGIN_
शयनानि प्रसूयन्ते चित्र आस्तारणवन्ति च |
मनः कान्तानि माल्यानि फलन्ति अत्र अपरे द्रुमाः || ४-४३-४७
पानानि च महा अर्हाणि भक्ष्याणि विविधानि च |_END
BEGIN_
"There are other trees that produce wooden-beds with astonishing upholsteries, and
even garlands that will be attractively heartening, while some other trees will be yielding juices
and foodstuffs that are relevant to highly choicest consumers. [4-43-47]_END

B_4_C_48_1
BEGIN_
स तु दूरम् उपागम्य सर्वैः तैः कपि सत्तमैः |
ततो विचित्य विन्ध्यस्य गुहाः च गहनानि च || ४-४८-२
पर्वताग्र नदी दुर्गान् सरांसि विपुल द्रुमान् |
वृक्ष खण्डान् च विविधान् पर्वतान् वन पादपान् || ४-४८-३_END
BEGIN_
Arriving at a remote place with all of those powerful monkeys, then Hanuma searched
the caves and forests of Vindhya Mountains, and on their mountaintops, at impassable places, at
rivers and lakes, and in stands of trees with beamy trees, also on diverse mountains, forests and
trees. [4-48-2, 3]_END

B_4_C_47_13
BEGIN_
उदार सत्त्व अभिजनो हनूमान्
स मैथिलीम् ज्ञास्यसि वानरेन्द्र |
दिशम् तु याम् एव गता तु सीता
ताम् आस्थितो वायु सुतो हनूमान् || ४-४७-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Hanuma is high-born and exceptionally mighty, oh, Sugreeva, the king of vanara-s,
he will ascertain about Maithili, because the son of Air-god, Hanuma, resorted to the direction in
which Seetha is taken away." Thus, monkey chiefs reported to their king Sugreeva. [4-47-14]_END

B_4_C_43_43
BEGIN_
स्त्रियः च गुण संपन्ना रूप यौवन लक्षिताः || ४-४३-४८
गन्धर्वाः किंनरा सिद्धा नागा विद्याधराः तथा |
रमन्ते सहिताः तत्र नारीभिः भास्वर प्रभाः || ४-४३-४९_END
BEGIN_
"The females of Uttara Kuru province will be handsome and youthful and they are rich
by their attributes. There the radiantly bright celestials like gandharva-s, kinnaraa-s, siddha-s,
vidyaadharaa-s will be delighting along with their own females. [4-43-48b, 49]_END

B_4_C_48_2
BEGIN_
अन्वेषमाणाः ते सर्वे वानराः सर्वतो दिशम् |
न सीताम् ददृशुर् वीरा मैथिलीम् जनक आत्मजाम् || ४-४८-४_END
BEGIN_
Though all of those brave vanara-s have searched in all directions they have not
noticed the princess of Mithila and the daughter of Janaka, namely Seetha. [4-48-4]_END

B_4_C_43_44
BEGIN_
सर्वे सुकृत कर्माणः सर्वे रति परायणाः |
सर्वे काम अर्थ सहिता वसंति सह योषितः || ४-४३-५०_END
BEGIN_
"All the inhabitants of North Kuru have carried out good deeds in earlier births,
hence they are accorded with paradisiacal pleasures now. All are engaged in passion, all of them
live in pleasure and prosperity along with their youthful females. [4-43-50]_END

B_4_C_48_3
BEGIN_
ते भक्षयन्तो मूलानि फलानि विविधानि अपि |
अन्वेषमाणा दुर्धर्षा न्यवसन् तत्र तत्र ह || ४-४८-५_END
BEGIN_
Feeding upon unalike fruits and tubers, sojourning here and there, those
invulnerable vanara-s conducted their search. [4-48-5]_END

B_4_C_48_4
BEGIN_
स तु देशो दुर्अन्वेषो गुहा गहनवान् महान् |
निर्जलम् निर्जनम् शून्यम् गहनम् घोर दर्शनम् || ४-४८-६_END
BEGIN_
But that province is an inscrutable one, deeply caved, deeply forested, much less of
water and still less of people, a void and an impenetrable one with a ghastly look. [4-48-6]_END

B_4_C_43_45
BEGIN_
गीत वादित्र निर्घोषः स उत्कृष्ट हसित स्वनः |
श्रूयते सततम् तत्र सर्व भूत मनोरमः || ४-४३-५१_END
BEGIN_
"The notes of vocal and instrumental music will be flowing out mixed with the peals
of vivacious laughter, which will always come to ears in a heart-stealing manner for all beings.
[4-43-51]_END

B_4_C_43_46
BEGIN_
तत्र न अमुदितः कश्चिन् न अत्र कश्चित् असत् प्रियः |
अहनि अहनि वर्धन्ते गुणाः तत्र मनोरमाः || ४-४३-५२_END
BEGIN_
"There is none who is infelicitous and there is none who is friendly to untruthful
ones, and in that province these heart-pleasing attributes of those blessed souls like rejoicing,
festivity etc. will be enriching day by day. [4-43-52]_END

B_4_C_48_5
BEGIN_
ता दृशानि अन्या अपि अरण्यानि विचित्य भृइश पीडिताः |
स देशः च दुर्अन्वेष्यो गुहा गहनवान् महान् || ४-४८-७_END
BEGIN_
They are highly tormented when they vainly searched there, and even in another
province that is also of the same kind, waterless and people-less, and an unreachable one,
abstrusely caved and forested. [4-48-7]_END

B_4_C_43_47
BEGIN_
तम् अतिक्रम्य शैलेन्द्रम् उत्तरः पय्साम् निधिः |
तत्र सोम गिरिर् नाम मध्ये हेममयो महान् || ४-४३-५३_END
BEGIN_
"On passing beyond that mountain in Uttara Kuru, there is a treasure trove of
waters, namely vast of Northern Ocean, in the mid of which there is gigantic golden mountain named
Mt. Soma. [4-43-53]_END

B_4_C_48_6
BEGIN_
त्यक्त्वा तु तम् ततः देशम् सर्वे वै हरि यूथपाः |
देशम् अन्यम् दुराधर्षम् विविशुः च अकुतो भयाः || ४-४८-८_END
BEGIN_
Then all of those monkey commanders gave up that province and entered another
impermeable province as they are fearless from any quarter. [4-48-8]_END

B_4_C_43_48
BEGIN_
इन्द्र लोक गता ये च ब्रह्म लोक गताः च ये |
देवाः तम् समवेक्षन्ते गिरि राजम् दिवम् गताः || ४-४३-५४_END
BEGIN_
"Those who have gone to the sphere of Indra, and those who have gone to the sphere
of Brahma can clearly see that lordly Mt. Soma, situated in the vast of ocean from the vast of
heavens. [4-43-54]_END

B_4_C_48_7
BEGIN_
यत्र वन्ध्य फला वृक्षा विपुष्पाः पर्ण वर्जिताः |
निस्तोयाः सरितो यत्र मूलम् यत्र सुदुर्लभम् || ४-४८-९_END
BEGIN_
Whereat the trees are infertile for fruiting, destitute of leaves and flowers, and
whereat the brooks are deprived of waters, and whereat it is highly impossible to get even tubers,
there they entered. [4-48-9]_END

B_4_C_43_49
BEGIN_
स तु देशो विसूर्यो अपि तस्य भासा प्रकाशते |
सूर्य लक्ष्म्या अभिविज्ञेयः तपता इव विवस्वता || ४-४३-५५_END
BEGIN_
"Even though that place is sunless it is comprehensible as if with sunshine, since
it is illuminated with the resplendence of Mt. Soma itself, which will be irradiating that place as
if with the resplendence of the Sun. [4-43-55]_END

B_4_C_48_8
BEGIN_
न सन्ति महिषा यत्र न मृगा न च हस्तिनः |
शार्दूलाः पक्षिणो वा अपि ये च अन्ये वन गोचराः || ४-४८-१०_END
BEGIN_
Where there are no buffalos, no elephants, no animals, nor even birds or tigers, or
no other forest moving beings are there, for they do not have their feed there, they entered such a
province. [4-48-10]_END

B_4_C_43_50
BEGIN_
भगवान् तत्र विश्वात्मा शम्भुः एकादश आत्मकः |
ब्रह्मा वसति देवेशो ब्रह्म ऋषि परिवारितः || ४-४३-५६_END
BEGIN_
"The God and Cosmic-Souled Vishnu and Shambhu or Shiva, an embodiment of eleven
selfsame Souls, called ekaadasha rudra-s , and the god of gods Brahma
who is surrounded by Brahma-Sages, will be sojourning on that Mt. Soma. [4-43-56]_END

B_4_C_48_9
BEGIN_
न च अत्र वृक्षा न ओषध्यो न वल्ल्यो न अपि वीरुधः |
स्निग्ध पत्राः स्थले यत्र पद्मिन्यः फुल्ल पंकजाः || ४-४८-११
प्रेक्षणीयाः सुगन्धाः च भ्रमरैः च वर्जिताः |_END
BEGIN_
Where there are no useful trees, nor herbal plants, nor climbing plants on trees,
nor creeping plants on earth, and lotus-lakes which will be normally pleasing for sight have no
soft leaves, nor bloomed lotuses on their creepers, and even honeybees are discarding them as they
are not richly fragranced, in such a province those vanara-s have entered. [4-48-11,12a]_END

B_4_C_43_51
BEGIN_
न कथंचन गंतव्यम् कुरूणाम् उत्तरेण वः |
अन्येषाम् अपि भूतानाम् न अनुक्रामति वै गतिः || ४-४३-५७_END
BEGIN_
"Under any circumstances you shall not go to the north of Kuru province as there is
no other way out to follow, even for other beings like daitya, daanava,
yaksha, gandharva-s, though they possess some extraordinary capabilities. [4-43-57]_END

B_4_C_48_10
BEGIN_
कण्डुर् नाम महाभागः सत्य वादी तपो धनः || ४-४८-१२
महर्षिः परम अमर्षी नियमैः दुष्प्रधर्षणः |_END
BEGIN_
A highly fortunate, veracious, ascetically wealthy sage known as Kandu is there in
that province, and that great sage is a highly short-tempered, and an impossible one to subjugate
by virtue of his own self-discipline. [4-48-12b, 13a]_END

B_4_C_43_52
BEGIN_
सा हि सोम गिरिः नाम देवानाम् अपि दुर्गमः |
तम् आलोक्य ततः क्षिप्रम् उपावर्तितुम् अर्हथ || ४-४३-५८_END
BEGIN_
"That mountain named Soma is an impassable one even for gods, and it will be apt of
you to quickly return from there on seeing that mountain. [4-43-58]_END

B_4_C_48_11
BEGIN_
तस्य तस्मिन् वने पुत्रो बालको दश वार्षिकः || ४-४८-१३
प्रणष्टो जीवित अन्ताय क्रुद्धः तेन महामुनिः |_END
BEGIN_
In that forest that sage lost his son, a ten-year-old boy, as that boy's life ended
there by which that great sage is infuriated. [4-48-13b, 14a]_END

B_4_C_43_53
BEGIN_
एतावत् वानरैः शक्यम् गंतुम् वानर पुंगवाः |
अभास्करम् अमर्यादम् न जानीमः ततः परम् || ४-४३-५९_END
BEGIN_
" It is possible for the vanara-s to go only up to there, oh, best vanara-s, and we
have no knowledge of those sunless and boundless realms available far and beyond. [4-43-59]_END

B_4_C_43_54
BEGIN_
सर्वम् एतत् विचेतव्यम् यन् मया परिकीर्तितम् |
यत् अन्यत् अपि न उक्तम् च तत्र अपि क्रियताम् मतिः || ४-४३-६०_END
BEGIN_
"You shall thoroughly search in all those provinces that are explained by me, and
you have to make up your mind for searching in other places that are not referred by me.
[4-43-60]_END

B_4_C_48_12
BEGIN_
तेन धर्माअत्मना शप्तम् कृत्स्नम् तत्र महद् वनम् || ४-४८-१४
अशरण्यम् दुराधर्षम् मृग पक्षि विवर्जितम् |_END
BEGIN_
Thereby that virtue-souled sage cursed that great forest in it entirety to become an
uninhabitable and impermeable forest abandoned by birds and animals. [4-48-14b, 15a]_END

B_4_C_48_13
BEGIN_
तस्य ते कानन अन्तान् तु गिरीणाम् कन्दराणि च || ४-४८-१५
प्रभवाणि नदीनाम् च विचिन्वन्ति समाहिताः |_END
BEGIN_
But those monkeys conscientiously searched such a forest up to its fringes,
including its mountains, caves, fountains, and rivers. [4-48-15b, 16a]_END

B_4_C_43_55
BEGIN_
ततः कृतम् दाशरथेः महत् प्रियम्
महत्तरम् च अपि ततो मम प्रियम् |
कृतम् भविष्यति अनिलोअनलौपमा
विदेहजा दर्शनजेन कर्मणा || ४-४३-६१_END
BEGIN_
"Thereby, oh, Air-godlike and Wind-godlike vanara-s, on your seeing the princess
born in Videha kingdom, namely Vaidehi, an extremely desirable task for the sake of Dasharatha's
son Rama is considered as done. Thereby it becomes a still privileged accomplishment even for me
achieved through your efforts. [4-43-61]_END

B_4_C_43_56
BEGIN_
ततः कृतार्थाः सहिताः सबान्धवा
मया अर्चिताः सर्व गुणैः मनो रमैः |
चरिष्यथ उर्वीम् प्रतिशान्त शत्रवाअः
सह प्रिया भूत धराः प्लवंगमाः || ४-४३-६२_END
BEGIN_
"Thereafter, oh, fly-jumpers, when you with accomplished purpose and adored by me
with heart-pleasing concessions, and when your enemies are silenced, you will rove over the earth
with your friends and relatives and with your beloveds, also fostering your progeny." Thus Sugreeva
said to the monkeys going to North. [4-43-62]_END

B_4_C_48_14
BEGIN_
तत्र च अपि महात्मानो न अपश्यन् जनक आत्मजाम् || ४-४८-१६
हर्तारम् रावणम् वा अपि सुग्रीव प्रिय कारिणः |_END
BEGIN_
But not finding the daughter of Janaka or even her kidnapper Ravana there, those
monkeys who are the perfecters of that which is acceptable to Sugreeva, have entered another
fearsome forest. [4-48-16b, 17a]_END

B_4_C_48_15
BEGIN_
ते प्रविश्य तु तम् भीमम् लता गुल्म समावृतम् || ४-४८-१७
ददृशुः भीम कर्माणम् असुरम् सुर निर्भयम् |_END
BEGIN_
On entering another fearsome forest which is overly encompassed with climbers and
shrubberies they saw a demon of fiendish deeds who is fearless of gods. [4-48-17b, 18a]_END

B_4_C_48_16
BEGIN_
तम् दृष्ट्वा वनरा घोरम् स्थितम् शैलम् इव असुरम् || ४-४८-१८
गाढम् परिहिताः सर्वे दृष्ट्वा तम् पर्वत उपमम् |_END
BEGIN_
All of those vanara-s are amazed to see that fiendish demon standing similar to a
mountainous boulder, and apprehending an imminent danger on observing that mountain similar demon,
those vanara-s have tightly girthed their wrestler's girdle-cloth. [4-48-18b, 19a]_END

B_4_C_48_17
BEGIN_
सो अपि तान् वानरान् सर्वान् नष्टाः स्थ इति अब्रवीत् बली || ४-४८-१९
अभ्यधावत सम्क्रुद्धो मुष्टिम् उद्यम्य संगतम् |_END
BEGIN_
Even that mighty demon shouting at all vanara-s, 'you are all dead... stay,' rushed
towards them shoving up his clenched fist. [4-48-19b, 20a]_END

B_4_C_48_18
BEGIN_
तम् आपतन्तम् सहसा वालि पुत्रो अंगदः तदा || ४-४८-२०
रावणो अयम् इति ज्ञात्वा तलेन अभिजघान ह |_END
BEGIN_
Angada, the son of Vali, then presumed him who is onrushing as Ravana and saying,
'he is Ravana...' he quickly thwacked that demon indeed with his palm. [4-48-20b, 21a]_END

B_4_C_48_19
BEGIN_
स वालि पुत्र अभिहतो वक्त्रात् शोणितम् उद्वमन् || ४-४८-२१
असुरो न्यपतत् भूमौ पर्यस्त इव पर्वतः |_END
BEGIN_
When Vali's son whacked him that demon spewed forth blood from his throat and fell
onto ground alike an inverted mountain. [4-48-21b, 22a]_END

B_4_C_48_20
BEGIN_
ते तु तस्मिन् निर् उच्छ्वासे वानरा जित काशिनः || ४-४८-२२
व्यचिन्वन् प्रायशः तत्र सर्वम् तत् गिरि गह्वरम् |_END
BEGIN_
When that demon breathed his last all of those monkeys with triumphal shimmer have
wellnigh searched everywhere, and even in that cave of that mountain where that demon appeared,
presuming that cave belonged to Ravana. [4-48-22b, 23a]_END

B_4_C_48_21
BEGIN_
विचितम् तु ततः सर्वम् सर्वे ते कानन ओकसः || ४-४८-२३
अन्यत् एव अपरम् घोरम् विविशुर् गिरि गह्वरम् |_END
BEGIN_
Then all those forest dwelling monkeys searched everywhere else, and like that they
entered another horrible cave which is nearby. [4-48-23b, 24a]_END

B_4_C_48_22
BEGIN_
ते विचित्य पुनः खिन्ना विनिष्पत्य समागताः |
एकांते वृक्ष मूले तु निषेदुर् दीन मानसाः || ४-४८-२४_END
BEGIN_
On searching that cave they came out saddened as their search is futile, and coming
together they sat down at the base of a lonely tree downheartedly as their efforts are unsuccessful
in searching Seetha. [4-48-24]_END

B_4_C_49_0
BEGIN_
अथ अंगदः तदा सर्वान् वानरान् इदम् अब्रवीत् |
परिश्रान्तो महा प्राज्ञः समाश्वास्य शनैर् वचः || ४-४९-१_END
BEGIN_
Then on comforting all of those vanara-s the highly diligent one but overly tired
Angada slowly spoke this word to them. [4-49-1]_END

B_4_C_49_1
BEGIN_
वनानि गिरयो नद्यो दुर्गाणि गहनानि च |
दरी गिरि गुहाः चैव विचिता नः समंततः || ४-४९-२
तत्र तत्र सह अस्माभिः जानकी न च दृश्यते |
तथा रक्षः अपहर्ता च सीतायाः चैव दुष्कृती || ४-४९-३_END
BEGIN_
"We in oneness have searched there and thereabouts in the impassable forests,
mountains, and rivers, and unfathomable cavities and in mountain caves up to their end, but we have
not seen Janaki, so also that ill-natured demon, the abductor of Seetha, is not seen. [4-49-2,
3]_END

B_4_C_49_2
BEGIN_
कालः च नः महान् यातः सुग्रीवः च उग्र शासनः |
तस्मात् भवन्तः सहिता विचिन्वन्तु समंततः || ४-४९-४_END
BEGIN_
"We started a long time back and a great deal of time is lapsed, and Sugreeva is a
severe disciplinarian, therefore let the search continued everywhere collectively. [4-49-4]_END

B_4_C_49_3
BEGIN_
विहाय तन्द्रीम् शोकम् च निद्राम् चैव समुत्थिताम् |
विचिनुध्वम् तथा सीताम् पश्यामो जनक आत्मजाम् || ४-४९-५_END
BEGIN_
"Surrender not to sluggishness, submit not to sorrowfulness, slouch not to sleep, as
these lethargies are presently have come up against you. Let all of you search in such a way how
best we can find the daughter of Janaka, Seetha. [4-49-5]_END

B_4_C_49_4
BEGIN_
अनिर्वेदम् च दाक्ष्यम् च मनसः च अपराजयम् |
कार्य सिद्धि कराणि आहुः तस्मात् एतत् ब्रवीमि अहम् || ४-४९-६_END
BEGIN_
"Insistency, ingenuity and indomitability of heart are said to be the causes for
achieving results, therefore I am speaking all this. [4-49-6]_END

B_4_C_49_5
BEGIN_
अद्य अपि इदम् वनम् दुर्गम् विचिन्वन्तु वन ओकसः |
खेदम् त्यक्त्वा पुनः सर्वम् वनम् एतत् विचिन्वताम् || ४-४९-७_END
BEGIN_
"Even now the forest dwellers can search this impenetrable forest, thus get rid of
your rue and let all of this forest be searched in its entirety. [4-49-7]_END

B_4_C_50_0
BEGIN_
सह तारा अंगदाभ्याम् तु संगम्य हनुमान् कपिः |
विचिनोति च विन्ध्यस्य गुहाः च गहनानि च || ४-५०-१_END
BEGIN_
Associated with Angada, Lt. Tara and others, the monkey Hanuma searched the caves
and thick forests of Vindhya Range. [4-50-1]_END

B_4_C_49_6
BEGIN_
अवश्यम् कुर्वताम् दृश्यते कर्मणः फलम् |
परम् निर्वेदम् आगम्य न हि नः मीलनम् क्षमम् || ४-४९-८_END
BEGIN_
"Fruit of pursuit will definitely be evident for those who undertake an endeavour
earnestly, on the other hand, it will be unforgivable to shut our eyes deriving a high dejection.
[4-49-8]_END

B_4_C_50_1
BEGIN_
सिंह शार्दूल जुष्टाः च गुहाः च परितः तथा |
विषमेषु नग इन्द्रस्य महा प्रस्रवणेषु च || ४-५०-२_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma has searched in the caves of that kingly Mt. Vindhya, which are jammed in
with lions and tigers, and even at the towering rapids. [4-50-2, 3a]_END

B_4_C_49_7
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवः क्रोधनो राजा तीक्ष्ण दण्डः च वानराः |
भेतव्यम् तस्य सततम् रामस्य च महात्मनः || ४-४९-९_END
BEGIN_
"King Sugreeva is irascible and he is a ruthful persecutor too, oh, vanara-s, we
shall always be frightened of him, and of self-reliant Rama as well. [4-49-9]_END

B_4_C_50_2
BEGIN_
आसेदुः तस्य शैलस्य कोटिम् दक्षिण पस्चिमाम् |
तेषाम् तत्र एव वसताम् स कालो व्यत्यवर्तत || ४-५-३_END
BEGIN_
They reached the southwest peak of that mountain during their search and the time
set by Sugreeva swiftly lapsed while they are overstaying thereat that Mt. Vindhya alone._END

B_4_C_49_8
BEGIN_
हितार्थम् एतत् उक्तम् वः क्रियताम् यदि रोचते |
उच्यताम् हि क्षमम् यत् तत् सर्वेषाम् एव वानराः || ४-४९-१०_END
BEGIN_
"All this is being said in the interest of your well-being, and if it is obliging to
you it may be done in this way as I have said, if not, any other way out is there which will be
conducive for all of us, oh, vanara-s, it may be said." Thus Angada spoke to the troops of monkeys.
[4-49-10]_END

B_4_C_50_3
BEGIN_
स हि देशो दुरन्वेष्यो गुहा गहनवान् महान् |
तत्र वायु सुतः सर्वम् विचिनोति स्म पर्वतम् || ४-५०-४_END
BEGIN_
Though that extensive province is indeed an unsearchable one with its impenetrable
caves and forests, yet Hanuma, the son of Air-god, searched everywhere on that mountain. [4-50-3b,
4]_END

B_4_C_49_9
BEGIN_
अंगदस्य वचः श्रुत्वा वचनम् गंधमादनः |
उवाच व्यक्तया वाचा पिपासा श्रम खिन्नया || ४-४९-११_END
BEGIN_
On hearing Angada's words, Gandhamaadana who is enervated with thirst and fatigue
spoke this sentence with inexplicit words. [4-49-11]_END

B_4_C_50_4
BEGIN_
परस्परेण रहिता अन्योन्यस्य अविदूरतः |
गजो गवाक्षो गवयः शरभो गन्धमादनः || ४-५०-५
मैन्दः च द्विविदः चैव हनुमान् जांबवान् अपि |
अंगदो युव राजः च तारः च वनगोचरः || ४-५०-६
गिरि जाल आवृतान् देशान् मार्गित्वा दक्षिणाम् दिशम् |
विचिन्वन्तः ततः तत्र ददृशुः विवृतम् बिलम् || ४-५०-७
दुर्गम् ऋक्ष बिलम् नाम दानवेन अभिरक्षितम् |_END
BEGIN_
Without pressing one another closely, yet not distancing from one another largely,
Gaja, Gavaaksha, Gavaya, Sharabha, Gandhamaadana, also thus Mainda, Dvivida, and Hanuma, and even
Jaambavanta, crown prince Angada, also the forest-mover Lt. Tara have searched that province in
southern direction that is encompassed with interlocked mountains, and during their search there
they have observed a wide-opened and impassable cavity known as Riksha cavity which is well guarded
by a demon called Maya. [4-50-5, 6, 7, 8a]_END

B_4_C_49_10
BEGIN_
सदृशम् खलु वः वाक्यम् अंगदो यत् उवाच ह |
हितम् च एव अनुकूलम् च क्रियताम् अस्य भाषितम् || ४-४९-१२_END
BEGIN_
"What Angada has said that is indeed appropriate, isn't it! It is advantageous and
pragmatic also. Let us carry out as said by him. [4-49-12]_END

B_4_C_50_5
BEGIN_
क्षुत् पिपासा परीताः तु श्रान्ताः तु सलिल अर्थिनः || ४-५०-८
अवकीर्णम् लता वृक्षैः ददृशुः ते महा बिलम् |_END
BEGIN_
Thirst and hunger invading them they are fatigued and craving for water, and such as
they are they beheld that capacious cavity which is enwrapped in climbers and trees. [4-50-8,
9a]_END

B_4_C_49_11
BEGIN_
पुनः मार्गामहे शैलान् कन्दराम् च शिलान् तथा |
काननानि च शून्यानि गिरि प्रस्रवणानि च || ४-४९-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Again let us search out mountains, caves, crags, also like that the uninhabited
forests and mountain rapids, too. [4-49-13]_END

B_4_C_50_6
BEGIN_
तत्र क्रौन्चाः च हंसाः च सारसाः च अपि निष्क्रमन् || ४-५०-९
जल आर्द्राः चक्रवाकाः च रक्त अंगाः पद्म रेणुभिः |_END
BEGIN_
There they have seen the swans and the waterfowls like Kraunca, Saarasa, and even
Cakravaka waterfowls exiting from the cavity with their bodies drenched in water and reddened with
the dapples of lotuses' pollen. [4-50-9b, 10a]_END

B_4_C_49_12
BEGIN_
यथा उद्दिष्ठानि सर्वाणि सुग्रीवेण महात्मना |
विचिन्वन्तु वनम् सर्वे गिरि दुर्गाणि संगताः || ४-४९-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Let us all collectively search all of the places with forests, mountains and gorges
as indicated by that self-assertive Sugreeva." Thus Gandhamaadana spoke to all monkeys.
[4-49-14]_END

B_4_C_50_7
BEGIN_
ततः तत् बिलम् आसाद्य सुगन्धि दुरतिक्रमम् || ४-५०-१०
विस्मय व्यग्र मनसो बभूवुः वानरर्षभाः |_END
BEGIN_
When those best vanara-s have neared that fragrant and impermeable cavity they are
disheartened with amazement. [4-50-10b, 11a]_END

B_4_C_49_13
BEGIN_
ततः समुत्थाय पुनः वानराः ते महाबलाः |
विन्ध्य कानन संकीर्णाम् विचेरुर् दक्षिणाम् दिशम् || ४-४९-१५_END
BEGIN_
Those great-mighty vanara-s again perking themselves up searched the southern
compass that is overspread with Vindhya forests. [4-49-15]_END

B_4_C_50_8
BEGIN_
संजात परिशंकाः ते तत् बिलम् प्लवग उत्तमाः || ४-५०-११
अभ्यपद्यन्त संहृष्टाः तेजोवन्तो महाबलाः |_END
BEGIN_
Though a suspicion in general is evoked in them, as they presumed that cavity to be
Naraka, The Hell of Yama, or Paataala, the Netherworld of Emperor Bali, those highly resplendent
and great mighty fly-jumpers have neared it, rejoicing for the availability of water in there.
[4-50-11b, 12a]_END

B_4_C_49_14
BEGIN_
ते शारद अभ्र प्रतिमम् श्रीमत् रजत पर्वतम् |
शृंगवन्तम् दरीवंतम् अधिरुह्य च वानराः || ४-४९-१६
तत्र लोध्र वनम् रम्यम् सप्त पर्ण वनानि च |
विचिन्वन्तो हरि वराः सीता दर्शन कान्क्षिणः || ४-४९-१७_END
BEGIN_
Those vanara-s who are the best among monkeys who are desirous of getting a glance
of Seetha have clambered up a magnificent Silver Mountain which in statuesque is like an autumnal
silvery cloud, and which has many zeniths and caverns, and searched there in the delightful woods
of Lodhra trees, and even in the groves of seven-leaved banana plants. [4-49-16, 17]_END

B_4_C_50_9
BEGIN_
नाना सत्त्व समाकीर्णाम् दैत्य इन्द्र निलय उपमम् || ४-५०-१२
दुर्दर्शम् इव घोरम् च दुर्विगाह्यम् च सर्वशः |_END
BEGIN_
That hideous cavity is dispersed with diverse beings, similar to the residence of
the emperor of demons, namely Emperor Bali, in Paataala, the Netherworld, and it is unsightly and
impermeable from anywhere. [4-50-12b, 13a]_END

B_4_C_49_15
BEGIN_
तस्य अग्रम् अधिरूढाः ते श्रान्ता विपुल विक्रमाः |
न पश्यन्ति स्म वैदेहीम् रामस्य महिषीम् प्रियाम् || ४-४९-१८_END
BEGIN_
Though they searched everywhere on ascending the mountaintop they have not found
Seetha, the dear queen of Rama, and though they are immensely venturesome they are fatigued.
[4-49-18]_END

B_4_C_50_10
BEGIN_
ततः पर्वत कूट आभो हनुमान् मारुत आत्मजः || ४-५०-१३
अब्रवीत् वानरान् घोरान् कान्तार वन कोविदः |_END
BEGIN_
The son of Air-god Hanuma whose glossiness is like that of a mountaintop and who is
a mastermind in scrutinising every inscrutable forest, then spoke to all of the formidable
Vanara-s. [4-50-13b, 14a]_END

B_4_C_51_0
BEGIN_
इति उक्त्वा हनुमान् तत्र पुनः कृष्ण अजिन अंबराम् |
अब्रवीत् ताम् महाभागाम् तापसीम् धर्म चारिणीम् || ४-५१-१_END
BEGIN_
Thus, Hanuma on saying therein [that subject,] again spoke to that most reverential
and sainted lady who is dressed in black deerskin and conducting herself in probity. [4-51-1]_END

B_4_C_49_16
BEGIN_
ते तु दृष्टि गतम् दृष्ट्वा तम् शैलम् बहु कंदरम् |
अध्यारोहन्त हरयो वीक्षमाणाः समंततः || ४-४९-१९_END
BEGIN_
On searching what all they could see all over on that many caved mountain those
monkeys descended yet keeping an eye on all over that mountain. [4-49-19]_END

B_4_C_50_11
BEGIN_
गिरि जाल आवृतान् देशान् मार्गित्वा दक्षिणाम् दिशम् || ४-५०-१४
वयम् सर्वे परिश्रांता न च पश्याम मैथिलीम् |_END
BEGIN_
"We all have searched the southern quarter including those places that are enmeshed
with meshes of mountains, and we are overly fatigued, but Maithili is unnoticed. [4-50-14b,
15a]_END

B_4_C_51_1
BEGIN_
इदम् प्रविष्टाः सहसा बिलम् तिमिर संवृतम् |
क्षुत् पिपासा परिश्रांताः परिखिन्नाः च सर्वशः || ४-५१-२_END
BEGIN_
"Overtired with hunger and thirst we are overawed anywise, and we suddenly entered
this cavity, which is overspread with darkness..." [Thus Hanuma is speaking to her.] [4-51-2]_END

B_4_C_49_17
BEGIN_
अवरुह्य ततो भूमिम् श्रान्ता विगत चेतसः |
स्थित्वा मुहूर्तम् तत्र अथ वृक्ष मूलम् उपाश्रिताः || ४-४९-२०_END
BEGIN_
Then on climbing down the mountain they reached ground and became tired and inane,
and staying there for moment they took shelter at the base of a tree. [4-49-20]_END

B_4_C_50_12
BEGIN_
अस्मात् च अपि बिलात् हंसाः क्रौन्चाः च सह सारसैः || ४-५०-१५
जल आर्द्राः चक्रवाकाः च निष्पतन्ति स्म सर्वशः |
नूनम् सलिलवान् अत्र कूपो वा यदि वा ह्रदः || ४-५०-१६
तथा च इमे बिल द्वारे स्निग्धाः तिष्ठन्ति पादपाः |_END
BEGIN_
"Swans along with waterfowls like Saarasa, Kruanca, and water drenched Cakravaka
birds are coming out of this cavity from all over, and even the trees available at its doorway are
verdant. Certainly there must be a wellspring, or otherwise a pond with water." Thus Hanuma spoke
to all monkeys. [4-50-15b, 16, 17a]_END

B_4_C_51_2
BEGIN_
महत् धरण्या विवरम् प्रविष्टाः स्म पिपासिताः |
इमाम् तु एवम् विधान् भावान् विविधान् अद्भुत उपमान् || ४-५१-३
दृष्ट्वा वयम् प्रव्यथिताः संभ्रांता नष्ट चेतसः |
कस्य एते कांचना वृक्षाः तरुण आदित्य सन्निभाः || ४-५१-४_END
BEGIN_
"We entered this extensive hollow of earth thirstily, but on seeing this kind of
these diverse and marvellous mansions we are verily amazed [presuming that this is a dominion of
some demon,] and we are agitated [in not knowing dos and don'ts,] and agonised [at our
incarceration...] whose trees are all these golden ones, splendent like young sun... [4-51-3,
4]_END

B_4_C_49_18
BEGIN_
ते मुहूर्तम् समाश्वस्ताः किंचित् भग्न परिश्रमाः |
पुनर् एव उद्यताः कृत्स्नाम् मार्गितुम् दक्षिणाम् दिशम् || ४-४९-२१_END
BEGIN_
They took respite for a moment and when their laboriousness intermitted a little,
again they ventured to search the southern direction in its entirety. [4-49-21]_END

B_4_C_50_13
BEGIN_
इति उक्ताः तत् बिलम् सर्वे विविशुः तिमिर आवृतम् || ४-५०-१७
अचन्द्र सूर्यम् हरयो ददृशू रोम हर्षणम् |_END
BEGIN_
When Hanuma spoke to them thus as a kind of assurance, all those monkeys entered the
cavity and found it as a sunless or moonless cavity, enfolded in hair-raising darkness. [4-50-17b,
18a]_END

B_4_C_51_3
BEGIN_
शुचीनि अभ्यवहार्याणि मूलानि च फलानि च |
कांचनानि विमानानि राजतानि गृहाणि च || ४-५१-५
तपनीय गव अक्षाणि मणि जाल आवृतानि च |_END
BEGIN_
"The edibles, tubers, and fruits are all depurated... golden are the aircrafts...
mansions silvern... ventilators golden and encased in jewelly laces... [4-51-5, 6a]_END

B_4_C_49_19
BEGIN_
हनुमत् प्रमुखाः ते तु प्रस्थिताः प्लवग ऋषभाः |
विंध्यम् एव आदितः कृत्वा विचेरुः ते समंततः || ४-४९-२२_END
BEGIN_
Again making Mt. Vindhya as the starting point of search, those best fly-jumpers,
namely Hanuma and the other chieftains of vanara-s, have searched all over the southern direction
for Seetha. [4-49-22]_END

B_4_C_51_4
BEGIN_
पुष्पिताः फालवन्तः च पुण्याः सुरभि गन्धयः || ४-५१-६
इमे जांबूनदमयाः पादपाः कस्य तेजसा |_END
BEGIN_
"Flowered and fruited and also aromatically scented are these auspicious and
completely golden trees... by whose splendour [they are rendered thus?] [4-51-6b, 7a]_END

B_4_C_50_14
BEGIN_
निशम्य तस्मात् सिंहाः च तान् तान् च मृग पक्षिणः || ४-५०-१८
प्रविष्टा हरि शार्दूला बिलम् तिमिर आवृतम् |_END
BEGIN_
Those tigerly monkeys have also seen lions and various other animals and birds
exiting therefrom, and entered that cavity which is enshrouded in obscurity. [4-50-18b, 19a]_END

B_4_C_51_5
BEGIN_
कांचनानि च पद्मानि जातानि विमले जले || ४-५१-७
कथम् मत्स्याः च सौवर्णा दृश्यन्ते सह कच्छपैः |_END
BEGIN_
"Also how the lotuses born in limpid water are golden, and how the fishes along with
tortoises are ostensibly golden? [4-51-7b, 8a]_END

B_4_C_50_15
BEGIN_
न तेषाम् सज्जते दृष्टिः न तेजः न पराक्रमः || ४-५०-१९
वायोः इव गतिः तेषाम् दृष्टिः तम् अपि वर्तते |_END
BEGIN_
Their eyesight, or their vigour, or their valorousness is rendered ineffectual, and
their permeation is just like the directionless air as their eyesight is thwarted in
gloominess._END

B_4_C_51_6
BEGIN_
आत्मानः अनुभावात् वा कस्य वै एतत् तपो बलम् || ४-५१-८
अजानताम् नः सर्वेषाम् सर्वम् आख्यातुम् अर्हसि |_END
BEGIN_
"Or, is all this owing to the innate prodigy of yours or to whose ascesis' prowess
all this is owed... as all of us are oblivious of it, so it will be apt of you to narrate all of
it..." [Thus Hanuma requested that sainted lady.] [4-51-8b, 9a]_END

B_4_C_50_16
BEGIN_
ते प्रविष्टाः तु वेगेन तत् बिलम् कपि कुंजराः || ४-५०-२०
प्रकाशम् च अभिरामम् च ददृशुः देशम् उत्तमम् |_END
BEGIN_
But on their going further into that cavity speedily, those elephantine monkeys
beheld a best place that is luminous, as well as lovely. [4-50-20b, 21a]_END

B_4_C_51_7
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्ता हनुमता तापसी धर्म चारिणी || ४-५१-९
प्रति उवाच हनूमंतम् सर्व भूत हिते रता |_END
BEGIN_
Thus when Hanuma addressed her, that sainted lady, and a blissful one in the well
being of all the beings, she replied Hanuma. [4-51-9b, 10a]_END

B_4_C_50_17
BEGIN_
ततः तस्मिन् बिले भीमे नाना पादप संकुले || ४-५०-२१
अन्योन्यम् संपरिष्वज्य जग्मुर् योजनम् अंतरम् |_END
BEGIN_
In that awful cave that is compacted with various trees, then they advanced further
an interstice of yojana distance, hand in hand lest one may miss the other. [4-50-21b, 22a]_END

B_4_C_50_18
BEGIN_
ते नष्ट संज्ञाः तृषिताः संभ्रांताः सलिल अर्थिनः || ४-५०-२२
परिपेतुर् बिले तस्मिन् कंचित् कालम् अतन्द्रिताः |_END
BEGIN_
Though they are craving for water, highly perplexed, and lost track of their
destination or any waterway, and yet hopeful of their mission they unwearyingly hopped in that
cavity for a good while. [4-50-22b, 23a]_END

B_4_C_51_8
BEGIN_
मयो नाम महातेजा मायावी दानवर्षभः || ४-५१-१०
तेन इदम् निर्मितम् सर्वम् मायया कांचनम् वनम् |_END
BEGIN_
"A marvellous fantasist by name Maya was there, a bullish demon of wizardry and by
him with his phenomenal expertise all this golden woodland is constructed..." [Thus, that sainted
lady started her narration.] [4-51-10b]_END

B_4_C_50_19
BEGIN_
ते कृशा दीन वदनाः परिश्रान्ताः प्लवंगमाः || ४-५०-२३
आलोकम् ददृशुः वीरा निराशा जीविते यदा |_END
BEGIN_
Those fly-jumpers are presently enervated and overly tired, and sad faced, and when
those brave ones are despaired of their life, just then they perceived a luminescence. [4-50-23b,
24a]_END

B_4_C_51_9
BEGIN_
पुरा दानव मुख्यानाम् विश्वकर्मा बभूव ह || ४-५१-११
येन इदम् कांचनम् दिव्यम् निर्मितम् भवन उत्तमम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Once he was the Universal Craftsman to the lords of demons by whom this divinely
golden and superb mansion was constructed... [4-51-11]_END

B_4_C_50_20
BEGIN_
ततः तम् देशम् आगम्य सौम्याः वितिमिरम् वनम् || ४-५०-२४
ददृशुः कान्चनान् वृक्षान् दीप्त वैश्वानर प्रभान् |
सालान् तालान् तमालान् च पुन्नागान् वंजुलान् धवान् || ४-५०-२५
चंपकान् नाग वृक्षान् च कर्णिकारान् च पुष्पितान् |
स्तबकैः कांचनैः चित्रैः रक्तैः किसलयैः तथा || ४-५०-२६
आपीडैः च लताभिः च हेम आभरण भूषितैः |
तरुण आदित्य संकाशान् वैदूर्यमय वेदिकान् || ४-५०-२७
विभ्राजमानान् वपुषा पादपान् च हिरण्मयान् |
नील वैदूर्य वर्णाः च पद्मिनीः पतगैः आवृताः || ४-५०-२८
महद्भिः कांचनैः वृक्षैः वृता बाल अर्क संनिभैः |_END
BEGIN_
Those amenable monkeys on arriving at that province then beheld a shadowless
woodland with golden trees which in irradiance is like the irradiated Ritual-fire. They beheld
Saala, Taala [Palmyra,] Tamaala trees and some flowered trees like Punnaaga, Vanjula, Dhava,
Campaka, Naaga, also Karnikaara trees. The bunches of their flowers are golden and amazing,
leaflets are reddish, and like that the climbers enwreathing at their tops are like their towering
diadems and since those trees have golden fruits, they look as though decorated with golden
jewellery. Those golden-bodied tress are shining forth like tender sun and their pedestals are
completely studded with lapis gems. The birds encircling those trees are in the hue of lapis lazuli
gems. The lotus lakes are encompassed with golden lotuses with broad petals, which in shine are
similar to tender sun. [4-50-24b, 25, 26, 27, 28, 29a]_END

B_4_C_51_10
BEGIN_
स तु वर्ष सहस्राणि तपः तप्त्वा महत् वने || ४-५१-१२
पितामहात् वरम् लेभे सर्वम् औशसनम् धनम् |_END
BEGIN_
"But he on practising ascesis for thousands of years in this horrendous forest,
obtained a boon from Brahma, the Forefather, [which entails acquirement of] entire wealth of Sage
Shukra..._END

B_4_C_50_21
BEGIN_
जातरूपमयैः मत्स्यैः महद्भिः च अथ पन्कजैः || ४-५०-२९
नलिनीः तत्र ददृशुः प्रसन्न सलिल आयुताः |_END
BEGIN_
Then they beheld there the lotus-lakes containing serene waters and stocky lotuses
and burly fishes that are golden. [4-50-29b, 30a]_END

B_4_C_51_11
BEGIN_
विधाय सर्वम् बलवान् सर्व काम ईश्वरः तदा || ४-५१-१३
उवास सुखितः कालम् कंचित् अस्मिन् महावने |_END
BEGIN_
"That dynamic one methodised everything and then resided comfortably in this great
forest for some time, privileged with all his wishes... [4-51-13b, 14a]_END

B_4_C_51_12
BEGIN_
तम् अप्सरसि हेमायाम् सक्तम् दानव पुंगवम् || ४-५१-१४
विक्रम्य एव अशनिम् गृह्य जघान ईशः पुरंदरः |_END
BEGIN_
"Indra, the Administrator of Worlds and destroyer of enemy citadels, on taking His
Thunderbolt eliminated Maya, when that eminent demon was engaged with an apsara, a paradisiacal
nymph, called Hema... [4-51-14b, 15a]_END

B_4_C_50_22
BEGIN_
कांचनानि विमानानि राजतानि तथा एव च || ४-५०-३०
तपनीय गवाक्षाणि मुक्ता जाल आवृतानि च |
हैम राजत भौमानि वैदूर्य मणिमन्ति च || ४-५०-३१
ददृशुः तत्र हरयो गृह मुख्यानि सर्वशः |_END
BEGIN_
There the monkeys beheld choicest mansions everywhere made out of gold and silver,
some with golden and some with silver domes, while some with golden and some with silver
multi-stories, but all are studded with lapis gems with golden windows covered with laceworks of
pearls. [4-50-30b-32a]_END

B_4_C_51_13
BEGIN_
इदम् च ब्रह्मणा दत्तम् हेमायै वनम् उत्तमम् || ४-५१-१५
शाश्वतः काम भोगः च गृहम् च इदम् हिरण्मयम् |_END
BEGIN_
"This marvellous woodland, these everlasting wish-fulfillers, and this golden
mansion, are beneficed by Brahma for Hema... [4-51-15]_END

B_4_C_50_23
BEGIN_
पुष्पितान् फलिनो वृक्षान् प्रवाल मणि संनिभान् || ४-५०-३२
कांचन भ्रमरान् चैव मधूनि च समन्ततः |_END
BEGIN_
They have also seen everywhere flowered and fruited trees that are similar in shine
to red corals and rubies, and golden honeybees, as well as honeys. [4-50-32b, 33a]_END

B_4_C_52_0
BEGIN_
अथ तान् अब्रवीत् सर्वान् विश्रांतान् हरि यूथपान् |इदम् वचनम् एकाग्रा तापसी धर्म चारिणी || ४-५२-१_END
BEGIN_
When those monkey commanders are relaxed after refreshments, then that sainted lady, who concentrates single-mindedly 
and who is a pursuer of probity, spoke this word to all of them. [4-52-1]_END

B_4_C_51_14
BEGIN_
दुहिता मेरुसावर्णेः अहम् तस्याः स्वयंप्रभा || ४-५१-१६
इदम् रक्षामि भवनम् हेमाया वानरोत्तम |_END
BEGIN_
"I am the daughter of Merusaavarni, oh, best monkey, named Swayamprabha and I am
safeguarding this mansion of her, [that apsara] Hema... [4-51-16b, 17a]_END

B_4_C_50_24
BEGIN_
मणि कांचन चित्राणि शयनानि आसनानि च || ४-५०-३३
विविधानि विशालानि ददृशुः ते समन्ततः |
हेम रजत कांस्यानाम् भाजनानाम् च राशयः || ४-५०-३४_END
BEGIN_
They beheld everywhere diverse and capacious beds and seats that are amazingly
crafted with gemstones and gold, and also stacks of utensils made of gold, silver and bell metal.
[4-50-33b, 34]_END

B_4_C_52_1
BEGIN_
वानरा यदि वः खेदः प्रनष्टः फल भक्षणात् |यदि च एतत् मया श्राव्यम् श्रोतुम् इच्छामि कथताम् || ४-५२-२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, vanara-s, if your enervation is eased off by devouring fruits, and if I may listen to that episode of yours, 
I wish to listen to it." Thus Swayamprabha addressed the monkeys. [4-52-2]_END

B_4_C_51_15
BEGIN_
मम प्रिय सखी हेमा नृत्त गीत विशारदा || ४-५१-१७
तया दत्त वरा च अस्मि रक्षामि भवनम् महान् |_END
BEGIN_
"Hema is a virtuoso in dance and music and my dearest nymphean-friend, and she
bestowed a boon upon me [by which none can dishonour me, and thus] I am safeguarding this superb
mansion... [4-51-17b, 18a]_END

B_4_C_50_25
BEGIN_
अगुरूणाम् च दिव्यानाम् चंदनानाम् च संचयम् |
शुचीनि अभ्यवहाराणि मूलानि च फलानि च || ४-५०-३५_END
BEGIN_
They saw the stockpiles of heavenly aloe vera substances and sandalwood sticks and
depurated eatables, tubers and fruits. [4-50-35]_END

B_4_C_52_2
BEGIN_
तस्याः तत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा हनुमान् मारुत आत्मजः |आर्जवेन यथा तत्त्वम् आख्यातुम् उपचक्रमे || ४-५२-३_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma, the son of Air-god, sincerely started to narrate their episode in its pithiness on hearing her words. 
[4-52-3]_END

B_4_C_51_16
BEGIN_
किम् कार्यम् कस्य वा हेतोः कांताराणि प्रपद्यथ || ४-५१-१८
कथम् च इदम् वनम् दुर्गम् युष्माभिः उपलक्षितम् |_END
BEGIN_
"What is your effort or for what reason you came to pass this impervious forest, and
how you all have discovered this impassable forest... [4-51-18b, 19a]_END

B_4_C_50_26
BEGIN_
महा अर्हाणि च पानानि मधूनि रसवन्ति च |
दिव्यानाम् अम्बराणाम् च महा अर्हाणाम् च संचयान् || ४-५०-३६
कंबलानाम् च चित्राणाम् अजिनानाम् च संचयान् |_END
BEGIN_
They have also seen top-grade soft drinks, luscious honeys, heaps of finest quality
clothing, exotic blankets and sheaves of deerskins. [4-50-36, 37a]_END

B_4_C_52_3
BEGIN_
राजा सर्वस्य लोकस्य महेन्द्र वरुण उपमः |रामो दाशरथिः श्रीमान् प्रविष्टो दण्डका वनम् || ४-५२-४लक्ष्मणेन 
सह भ्रात्रा वैदेह्या च अपि भार्यया |तस्य भार्या जनस्थानात् रावणेन हृता बलात् || ४-५२-५_END
BEGIN_
"The king of all the world and one similar to Mahendra and Rain-god, such an illustrious Rama of Dasharatha entered 
Dandaka forest with his bother Lakshmana, even along with his wife Vaidehi, but Ravana coercively abducted his 
wife from Janasthaana. [4-52-4, 5]_END

B_4_C_51_17
BEGIN_
शुचीनि अभ्यवहार्याणि मूलानि च फलानि च |
भुक्त्वा पीत्वा च पानीयम् सर्वम् मे वक्तुम् अर्हथ || ४-५१-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Dine on these wholesome edibles, fruits and tubers, also on drinking soft drinks,
it is apt of you to inform me all about [your mission..." Thus Swayamprabha gave hospitality to the
monkeys.] [4-51-19b, 19c]_END

B_4_C_50_27
BEGIN_
तत्र तत्र विन्यस्तान् दीप्तान् वैश्वानर प्रभान् || ४-५०-३७
ददृशुः वानराः शुभ्रान् जातरूपस्य संचयान् |_END
BEGIN_
Vanara-s have also observed mounds of undefiled gold stockpiled here and there
glowing with the glow of ritual fire. [4-50-37b, 38a]_END

B_4_C_52_4
BEGIN_
वीरः तस्य सखा राज्ञः सुग्रीवो नाम वानरः |राजा वानर मुख्यानाम् येन प्रस्थापिता वयम् || ४-५२-६_END
BEGIN_
"A valiant one and the king of important vanara-s known as Sugreeva is a vanara and the friend of that kingly 
Rama, and that vanara king expedited us. [4-52-6]_END

B_4_C_50_28
BEGIN_
तत्र तत्र विचिन्वन्तो बिले तत्र महा प्रभाः || ४-५०-३८
ददृशुः वानराः शूराः स्त्रियम् कांचित् अदूरतः |_END
BEGIN_
When searching here and there in that cavity those valiant vanara-s of high
resplendence have perceived some lady rather not far from them. [4-50-38b, 39a]_END

B_4_C_52_5
BEGIN_
अगस्त्य चरिताम् आशाम् दक्षिणाम् यम रक्षिताम् |सहैभिर्वानरैमुख्यैरङ्गदप्रमुखैर्वयम् - यद्वा -सह एभिः वानरैः 
मुख्यैः अंगद प्रमुखैः वयम् || ४-५२-७रावणम् सहिताः सर्वे राक्षसम् काम रूपिणम् |सीतया सह वैदेह्या मार्गध्वम् 
इति चोदिताः || ४-५२-८_END
BEGIN_
"He mobilised us along with these important vanara-s and Angada as helmsman to this southerly prospect, which 
is the walkabout of Sage Agastya and watched over by Yama, the Death-god, saying, 'you all shall collectively 
search for Seetha of Videha kingdom together with the demon Ravana, a guise-changer by his wish.' [4-52-7, 8]_END

B_4_C_50_29
BEGIN_
ताम् च ते ददृशुः तत्र चीर कृष्ण अजिन अम्बराम् || ४-५०-३९
तापसीम् नियत आहाराम् ज्वलंतीम् इव तेजसा |_END
BEGIN_
They saw a sainted lady there who is attired in jute-cloths and who is on a
controlled diet and who is like a luminiferous entity by her own luminescence of asceticism.
[4-50-38b, 39a]_END

B_4_C_53_0
BEGIN_
ततः ते ददृशुः घोरम् सागरम् वरुण आलयम् |अपारम् अभिगर्जन्तम् घोरैः ऊर्मिभिः आकुलम् || ४-५३-१_END
BEGIN_
Then they saw an inexorable ocean, the realm of Rain-god, tumultuous with out-roaring and implacable waves, and 
shoreless otherwhere. [4-53-1]_END

B_4_C_52_6
BEGIN_
विचित्य तु वयम् सर्वे समग्रम् - समुद्रम् - दक्षिणाम् दिशम् |वयम् बुभुक्षिताः सर्वे वृक्ष मूलम् उपाश्रिताः 
|| ४-५२-९_END
BEGIN_
"On searching out the southerly direction in its entirety we are all hungered and we all gathered around at a 
tree-stem. [4-52-9]_END

B_4_C_50_30
BEGIN_
विस्मिता हरयः तत्र व्यवतिष्टन्त सर्वशः |
प्रपच्छ हनुमान् तत्र का असि त्वम् कस्य वा बिलम् || ४-५०-४०_END
BEGIN_
In wonderment the monkeys stood still all over, and in the matter of her identity
Hanuma asked her, "Who are you? Whose cavity is this, either? [4-50-40b, 40c]_END

B_4_C_53_1
BEGIN_
मयस्य माया विहितम् गिरि दुर्गम् विचिन्वताम् |तेषाम् मासो व्यतिक्रान्तो यो राज्ञा समयः कृतः || ४-५३-२_END
BEGIN_
Which month is set as timeframe for the monkeys by king Sugreeva that month passed off while the monkeys are searching 
mountains, impassable areas and within the cavity concocted by the wizardry of demon Maya. [4-53-2]_END

B_4_C_52_7
BEGIN_
विवर्ण वदनाः सर्वे सर्वे ध्यान परायणाः |न अधिगच्छामहे पारम् मग्नाः चिन्ता महाअर्णवे || ४-५२-१०_END
BEGIN_
"All of us were whey-faced, all of us were preoccupied with propositions, thus deluged in the depthless deep of 
our despair we could not overreach the other shore of our oceanic despair. [4-52-10]_END

B_4_C_53_2
BEGIN_
विन्ध्यस्य तु गिरेः पादे संप्रपुष्पित पादपे |उपविश्य महात्मानः चिन्ताम् आपेदिरे तदा || ४-५३-३_END
BEGIN_
Sitting on a foothill of Mt. Vindhya which is with fully flowered trees those virtue-souled monkeys are then driven 
in desperation. [4-53-3]_END

B_4_C_50_31
BEGIN_
ततो हनूमान् गिरि सन्निकाशः
कृत अंजलिः ताम् अभिवाद्य वृद्धाम् |
पप्रच्छ का त्वम् भवनम् बिलम् च
रत्नानि च इमानि वदस्व कस्य || ४-५०-४१_END
BEGIN_
Then Hanuma whose shine is similar to that of a mountain making palm-fold and
reverencing that aged lady asked, "Who are you? Whose is this cavity, or the mansion or these
jewels? Please speak." [4-50-41]_END

B_4_C_52_8
BEGIN_
चारयन्तः ततः चक्षुः दृष्टवन्तो महद् बिलम् |लता पादप संछन्नम् तिमिरेण समावृतम् || ४-५२-११_END
BEGIN_
"Then straggling our eyes we perceived this wide cavity wrapped up with vines and woods and enwrapped in darkling. 
[4-52-11]_END

B_4_C_53_3
BEGIN_
ततः पुष्पातिभाराग्राँल्ल्ताशतसमावृतान् -यद्वा -ततः पुष्प अतिभार अग्रान् लता शत समावृतान् |द्रुमान् वासन्तिकान् 
दृष्ट्वा बभूवुः भय शन्किताः || ४-५३-४_END
BEGIN_
Then on seeing the treetops of spring season, weighty with flowers and enshrouded with hundreds of vines, they 
became incredulous with the fright of failing Sugreeva's timeframe. [4-53-4]_END

B_4_C_52_9
BEGIN_
अस्मात् हंसा जल क्लिन्नाः पक्षैः सलिल रेणुभिः |कुरराः सारसाः चैव निष्पतन्ति पतत्रिणः || ४-५२-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Swans, water-hawks, saarasa-waterfowls were coming out of this cavity drenched in water and sprinkling drops 
of water with the flaps of their wings. [4-52-12]_END

B_4_C_53_4
BEGIN_
ते वसंतम् अनुप्राप्तम् प्रतिवेद्य परस्परम् |नष्ट संदेश काल अर्था निपेतुर् धरणी तले || ४-५३-५_END
BEGIN_
On discussing among themselves they found that spring season has arrived, and they also found the purpose of timely 
messaging about Seetha to Sugreeva is lost, thus they plumped down onto the surface of earth. [4-53-5]_END

B_4_C_52_10
BEGIN_
साधु अत्र प्रविशाम इति मया तु उक्ताः प्लवंगमाः |तेषाम् अपि हि सर्वेषाम् अनुमानम् उपागतम् || ४-५२-१३_END
BEGIN_
"I said to all of them, 'Good! Let us enter it,' while they too had some inference about the availability of water 
in here. [4-52-13]_END

B_4_C_54_0
BEGIN_
तथा ब्रुवति तारे तु तारा अधिपति वर्चसि |अथ मेने हृतम् राज्यम् हनुमान् अंगदेन तत् || ४५४१_END
BEGIN_
When Lt Tara whose resplendence is similar to moonshine has spoken that way, then Hanuma deemed that Angada is 
laying siege to that kingdom of Vanaras. [4541]_END

B_4_C_53_5
BEGIN_
ततः तान् कपि वृद्धान् च शिष्टान् चैव वनौकसः |वाचा मधुरया अभाष्य यथावत् अनुमान्य च || ४-५३-६स तु सिंह ऋषभ 
स्कंधः पीन आयत भुजः कपिः |युवराजो महाप्राज्ञ अंगदो वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् || ४-५३-७_END
BEGIN_
The crown prince and a great foreseer Angada, the monkey, whose nape of neck is leonine and bullish, arms lengthy 
and sturdy, then as usual paying respects to elderly monkeys greeted all of the forest dwellers and spoke this 
sentence in a modest voice. [4-53-6, 7]_END

B_4_C_52_11
BEGIN_
अस्मिन् निपतिताः सर्वे अपि अथ कार्य त्वरान्विताः |ततो गाढम् निपतिता गृह्य हस्तौ परस्परम् || ४-५२-१४_END
BEGIN_
"As our task was hastening us then we all readied ourselves to fall in the cavity by tightly clasping each other's 
hand, and then we fell in this cavity. [4-52-14]_END

B_4_C_54_1
BEGIN_
बुद्ध्या हि अष्ट अंगया युक्तम् चतुर् बल समन्वितम् |चतुर् दश गुणम् मेने हनुमान् वालिनः सुतम् || ४५४२_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma considered Vali's son Angada indeed as having eightfold intelligence, fourfold tactics, fourteen traits. 
[4542]_END

B_4_C_53_6
BEGIN_
शासनात् कपि राजस्य वयम् सर्वे विनिर्गताः |मासः पूर्णो बिलस्थानाम् हरयः किम् न बुध्यते || ४-५३-८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, monkeys, we all have started at the command of the king of monkeys, and the month fixed by him is zeroed 
out while we were in Black Cavity. Are you aware of it?" Thus Angada started to speak his mind. [4-53-8]_END

B_4_C_52_12
BEGIN_
इदम् प्रविष्टाः सहसा बिलम् तिमिर संवृतम् |एतत् नः कार्यम् एतेन कृत्येन वयम् आगताः || ४-५२-१५त्वाम् च एव 
उपगताः सर्वे परिद्यूना बुभुक्षिताः |_END
BEGIN_
"Thus we readily entered this Black Cavity, and this much is our activity in here as we all have come here by 
our escapade for water, and we neared you when we were ravenous and retrogressing. [4-52-15, 16a]_END

B_4_C_54_2
BEGIN_
आपूर्यमाणम् शश्वत् च तेजो बल पराक्रमैः |शशिनम् शुक्ल पक्ष आदौ वर्धमानम् इव श्रिया || ४५४३बृहस्पति समम् 
बुद्ध्या विक्रमे सदृशम् पितुः |शुश्रूषमाणम् तारस्य शुक्रस्य इव पुरंदरम् || ४५४४भर्तुः अर्थे परिश्रान्तम् 
सर्व शास्त्र विशारदः |अभिसंधातुम् आरेभे हनुमान् अंगदम् ततः || ४५४५_END
BEGIN_
Angada who is steadily brimming over with his spiritedness, mightiness, valorousness, and waxing like the moon 
starting from day one of White Fortnight of a month, who is comparable to Brihaspati, the Jupiter, in sagacity, 
who mirrors up his father Vali in intrepidity, but who is now assiduously attentive to the rebellious teachings 
of Lt. Tara, like Indra who once listened to the unlistenable teachings of demon's mentor, namely Shukraacaarya, 
as that Angada is overly enervated to fulfil the concerns of the king Sugreeva. Then Hanuma who is the scholar 
in all scriptures started to confederate the confidence of Angada with the present regime of Sugreeva. [4543, 
4, 5]_END

B_4_C_53_7
BEGIN_
वयम् आश्वयुजे मासि काल संख्या व्यवस्थिताः |प्रस्थिताः सो अपि च अतीतः किम् अतः कार्यम् उत्तरम् || ४-५३-९_END
BEGIN_
"We were sent out scheduling time calculating from the month of aashviiyuja nearly 
October. Even that time fixed for us has also lapsed. Thereby, what is to be done next? [4-53-9]_END

B_4_C_52_13
BEGIN_
आतिथ्य धर्म दत्तानि मूलानि च फलानि च || ४-५२-१६अस्माभिः उपभुक्तानि बुभुक्षा परिपीडितैः |_END
BEGIN_
"And we who are overly harassed by hunger have devoured the fruits and tubers you have offered with the grace 
of your hospitality. [4-52-16]_END

B_4_C_54_3
BEGIN_
स चतुर्णाम् उपायानाम् तृतीयम् उपवर्णयन् |भेदयामास तान् सर्वान् वानरान् वाक्य संपदा || ४५४६_END
BEGIN_
Hanuma then rhetorically started to the schismatic secession of all those vanaras, who are desirous of avoiding 
Sugreeva and desiring a hideout, exemplifying the third ideation, namely the partition, among the four political 
ideations, viz., placation, presentation, partition, persecution. [4546]_END

B_4_C_53_8
BEGIN_
भवन्त प्रत्ययम् प्राप्ता नीति मार्ग विशारदाः |हितेषु अभिरता भर्त्तुः निसृष्टाः सर्व कर्मसु || ४-५३-१०_END
BEGIN_
"You all the pioneers in the pathway of principles, you have notched up the credibility of your king, you are 
all well-disposed in the well-being of your king, and you are the contrivers of any exploit. [4-53-10]_END

B_4_C_52_14
BEGIN_
यत् त्वया रक्षिताः सर्वे म्रियमाणा बुभुक्षया || ४-५२-१७ब्रूहि प्रत्युपकार अर्थम् किम् ते कुर्वन्तु वानराः 
|_END
BEGIN_
"You have rescued all of us who were on the verge of hunger-deaths, and what is to be done by vanara-s for you 
in requital that you may please tell." Thus Hanuma spoke to that sainted lady. [4-52-17b, 18a]_END

B_4_C_54_4
BEGIN_
तेषु सर्वेषु भिन्नेषु ततो अभीषय अंगदम् |भीषणैः विविधैः वाक्यैः कोप उपाय समन्वितैः || ४५४७_END
BEGIN_
When Hanuma made all of the vanaras to defect from Angada's idea of defecting Sugreeva, then Hanuma further overawed 
Angada with diverse and awesome orations containing the fourth ideation, namely the persecutory measures, employable 
by Sugreeva on defectors. [4547]_END

B_4_C_53_9
BEGIN_
कर्मसु अप्रतिमाः सर्वे दिक्षु विश्रुत पौरुषाः |माम् पुरस्कृत्य निर्याताः पिन्गाक्ष प्रतिचोदिताः || ४-५३-११_END
BEGIN_
"All of you are unparalleled in all tasks, all your asperity is renowned in all directions, and all of you have 
come impelled by that ochreish eyed Sugreeva keeping me as your helmsman. [4-53-11]_END

B_4_C_52_15
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्ता तु सर्वज्ञा वानरैः तैः स्वयंप्रभा || ४-५२-१८प्रत्युवाच ततः सर्वान् इदम् वानर यूथपान् |_END
BEGIN_
When she is spoken thus by those vanara-s then that omniscient Swayamprabha replied this to all of the vanara 
commanders. [4-52-18b, 19a]_END

B_4_C_53_10
BEGIN_
इदानीम् अकृत अर्थानाम् मर्तव्यम् न अत्र संशयः |हरि राजस्य संदेशम् अकृत्वा कः सुखी भवेत् || ४-५३-१२_END
BEGIN_
"As of now our mission is incomplete hence we are scheduled to die, and there is no doubt about it. Who can be 
complacent by keeping the directive of monkey's king incomplete? [4-53-12]_END

B_4_C_54_5
BEGIN_
त्वम् समर्थ तरः पित्रा युद्धे तारेय वै ध्रुवम् |दृढम् धारयितुम् शक्तः कपि राज्यम् यथा पिता || ४५४८_END
BEGIN_
"As with your father you are undeniably abler in warfare, oh, the son of Lady Tara, and as with your father you 
are unquestionably capable enough to sustain the monkey kingdom." Thus Hanuma started to address Angada. [4548]_END

B_4_C_52_16
BEGIN_
सर्वेषाम् परितुष्टा अस्मि वानराणाम् तरस्विनाम् || ४-५२-१९चरंत्या मम धर्मेण न कार्यम् इह केनचित् |_END
BEGIN_
"I am very happy with all of the mighty vanara-s and what I have done to you is a part of my conduct in equity, 
hence nothing need be done now in my favour, in the least. [4-52-9b, 20a]_END

B_4_C_53_11
BEGIN_
आस्मिन् अतीते काले तु सुग्रीवेण कृते स्वयम् |प्रायोपवेशनम् युक्तम् सर्वेषाम् च वन ओकसाम् || ४-५३-१३_END
BEGIN_
"But in this matter of course, as the time set by Sugreeva is lapsed, it is appropriate for all of us forest dwelling 
monkeys to voluntarily undertake fasting unto death. [4-53-13]_END

B_4_C_54_6
BEGIN_
नित्यम् अस्थिर चित्ता हि कपयो हरि पुंगव |न आज्ञाप्यम् विषहिष्यन्ति पुत्र दारान् विना त्वया || ४५४९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, best monkey, Angada, monkeys will be inconsistent at their will, isn't it! Separated from their sons and 
wives they cannot tolerate to remain under your control for a long. [4549]_END

B_4_C_52_17
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः शुभम् वाक्यम् तापस्या धर्म संहितम् || ४-५२-२०उवाच हनुमान् वाक्यम् ताम् अनिन्दित लोचनाम् |_END
BEGIN_
When Hanuma is said that blessed word by that sainted lady in that way, that which is agreeable to propriety, 
then Hanuma said this sentence to her who is with an unreprovable discernment. [4-52-20b, 21a]_END

B_4_C_53_12
BEGIN_
तीक्ष्णः प्रकृत्या सुग्रीवः स्वामि भावे व्यवस्थितः |न क्षमिष्यति नः सर्वान् अपराध कृतो गतान् || ४-५३-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Instinctively Sugreeva is a tormentor and now he is institutionalised in lordship, thus he will not condone any 
of us as we will be as good as transgressors if we were to return. [4-53-14]_END

B_4_C_54_7
BEGIN_
त्वाम् न एते हि अनुयुंजेयुः प्रत्यक्षम् प्रवदामि ते |यथा अयम् जांबवान् नीलः सुहोत्रः च महाकपिः || ४५४१०
न हि अहम् ते इमे सर्वे साम दान आदिभिः गुणैः |दण्डेन न त्वया शक्याः सुग्रीवात् अपकर्षितुम् || ४५४११_END
BEGIN_
"I plainly tell you what is obvious. This Jambavanta, these monkeys like Niila, and great monkey Suhotra and others 
do not definitely tagalong you, isn't it. Likewise I too do not definitely tagalong you. Such as we are, it will 
be impossible for you to sidetrack us from Sugreeva using tactics like placation, presentation or even persecution, 
isn't so! [45410, 11]_END

B_4_C_52_18
BEGIN_
शरणम् त्वाम् प्रपन्नाः स्मः सर्वे वै धर्मचारिणिम् || ४-५२-२१यः कृतः समयो अस्माकम् सुग्रीवेण महात्मना |
स तु कालो व्यतिक्रान्तो बिले च परिवर्तताम् || ४-५२-२२_END
BEGIN_
"We are now under the auspices of your ladyship comporting yourself in scrupulosity. We lapsed the time stipulated 
for us by the noble-souled Sugreeva by our roving around in this cavity. [4-52-21b, 22]_END

B_4_C_53_13
BEGIN_
अप्रवृत्तौ च सीतायाः पापम् एव करिष्यति |तस्मात् क्षमम् इह अद्य एव गंतुम् प्रायोपविशनम् || ४-५३-१५त्यक्त्वा 
पुत्रन् च दारान् च धनानि च गृहाणि च |_END
BEGIN_
