"Sugreeva commits sin alone in our respect by killing all of us as we failed in the facts about Seetha, therefore 
it is pertinent to enter upon fasting unto, leaving off our sons, wives, riches and houses and homes, too. [4-53-15, 
16a]_END

B_4_C_54_8
BEGIN_
विगृह्य आसनम् अपि आहुः दुर्बलेन बलीयसा |आत्म रक्षा करः तस्मात् न विगृह्णीत दुर्बलः || ४५४१२_END
BEGIN_
"Even if a mightless is at odds with the mighty he can linger on, so to speak, therefore guard yourself, for no 
mediocrity will be at odds... [45412]_END

B_4_C_52_19
BEGIN_
सा त्वम् अस्मात् बिलात् अस्मान् उत्तारयितुम् अर्हसि |तस्मात् सुग्रीव वचनात् अतिक्रान्तान् गत आयुषः || ४-५२-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Such as you are, a righteous lady, it will be apt of you to cross us over this cavity, as we have overextended 
the timeframe fixed by Sugreeva, whereby our longevity itself is threatened. [4-52-23]_END

B_4_C_53_14
BEGIN_
ध्रुवम् नः हिंसते राजा सर्वान् प्रतिगतान् इतः || ४-५३-१६वधेन अप्रतिरूपेण श्रेयान् मृत्युः इह एव नः |_END
BEGIN_
"That king Sugreeva definitely and freakishly tortures all of us on our going back futilely, hence suicide at 
this place is justifiable for all us. [4-53-16b, c]_END

B_4_C_54_9
BEGIN_
याम् च इमाम् मन्यसे धात्रीम् एतत् बिलम् इति श्रुतम् |एतत् लक्ष्मण बाणानाम् ईषत् कार्यम् विदारणे || ४५४१३_END
BEGIN_
"This matter of going underground into that Black Hole which you suppose as a hideout from Sugreeva, as you heard 
from Lt. Tara and others, but it is a deed of trifle to Lakshmana's arrows, not necessarily for Rama's arrows, 
in splitting apart whole of that Black Hole in a trice. [45413]_END

B_4_C_52_20
BEGIN_
त्रातुम् अर्हसि नः सर्वान् सुग्रीव भय शन्कितान् |महत् च कार्यम् अस्माभिः कर्तव्यम् धर्मचारिणि || ४-५२-२४
तत् च अपि न कृतम् कार्यम् अस्माभिः इह वासिभिः |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, prudent lady, sail all of us through. We are rendered as hesitaters with the fear from Sugreeva. We still 
have to achieve an admirable achievement and that deed is also left undone as we are held-up in here." Thus Hanuma 
spoke to her. [4-52-24, 25a]_END

B_4_C_53_15
BEGIN_
न च अहम् यौवराज्येन सुग्रीवेण अभिषेचितः || ४-५३-१७नरेन्द्रेण अभिषिक्तो अस्मि रामेण अक्लिष्ट कर्मणा |_END
BEGIN_
"I am not anointed to crown-princedom by Sugreeva, but I am anointed by the unbigoted Rama, the king of people. 
[4-53-17b, 18a]_END

B_4_C_54_10
BEGIN_
स्वल्पम् हि कृतम् इन्द्रेण क्षिपता हि अशनिम् पुरा |लक्ष्मणो निशितैः बाणैः भिन्द्यात् पत्र पुटम् यथा || ४५४१४_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed, once Indra thudded his Thunderbolt on this very underground illusory place, but that act was indeed a 
trivial deed for that Thunderbolt made a single demonsized aperture to eliminate a single demon, Maya, which we 
now call Riksha bila, Black Hole, nevertheless Lakshmana will splinter whole of this 
Black Hole with his acute arrows, as if it is leafy bowl. [45414]_END

B_4_C_55_0
BEGIN_
श्रुत्वा हनुमतो वाक्यम् प्रश्रितम् धर्म संहितम् |स्वामि सत्कार संयुक्तम् अंगदो वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् || ४-५५-१_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the polite and righteous words of Hanuma, which are just yeomanly towards Hanuma's lord, namely Sugreeva, 
Angada said these sentences. [4-55-1]_END

B_4_C_52_21
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्ता हनुमता तापसी वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् || ४-५२-२५जीवता दुष्करम् मन्ये प्रविष्टेन निवर्तितुम् |_END
BEGIN_
When Hanuma said thus that sainted lady said sentence, "I believe outgoing is impracticable for the incomers in 
aliveness from this cavity. [4-52-25b, 26a]_END

B_4_C_53_16
BEGIN_
स पूर्वम् बद्ध वैरो माम् राजा दृष्ट्वा व्यतिक्रमम् || ४-५३-१८घातयिष्यति दण्डेन तीक्ष्णेन कृत निश्चयः |_END
BEGIN_
"That king Sugreeva who is already bound up in animosity with my father, and thus with me too, now on observing 
me transgressing his directive will decisively wish to liquidate me by a tyrannous victimisation. [4-53-18a, 19a]_END

B_4_C_54_11
BEGIN_
लक्ष्मणस्य च नाराचा बहवः सन्ति तत् विधाः |वज्र अशनि सम स्पर्शा गिरीणाम् अपि दारकाः || ४५४१५_END
BEGIN_
"There are numerous ironarrows with Lakshmana that are kindred to Thunderbolt of Indra, whose punch will be equalling 
that of Thunderbolt and Lightning Flashes, and which are the splitters of mountains. [45415]_END

B_4_C_55_1
BEGIN_
स्थैर्यमात्ममनःशौचमानृशंस्यमथाअर्जवम् - यद्व -स्थैर्यम् आत्म मनः शौचम् आनृशंस्यम् अथ आर्जवम् |विक्रमः 
चैव धैर्यम् च सुग्रीवे न उपपद्यते || ४-५५-२_END
BEGIN_
"Un-deducible in Sugreeva are his steadiness, or harmlessness, or frankness, also thus salience, or even valiance, 
further more cleanliness of heart or soul. [4-55-2]_END

B_4_C_52_22
BEGIN_
तपसः सुप्रभावेन नियम उपार्जितेन च || ४-५२-२६सर्वान् एव बिलात् अस्मात् तारयिष्यामि वानरान् |_END
BEGIN_
"By the sublime efficacy of ascesis acquired through my practices of numerous self-restraints I wish to sail all 
of the vanara-s through the incarceration, called this cavity. [4-52-26b, 27a]_END

B_4_C_53_17
BEGIN_
किम् मे सुहृद्भिः व्यसनम् पश्यद्भिः जीवितांतरे |इह एव प्रायम् आसिष्ये पुण्ये सागर रोधसि ||| ४-५३-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Of what use is the witnessing of my kith and kin at me when I am tortured in the prime of my life, hence here 
on this sacred seashore alone I will outwait my death fasting unto it." Thus Angada said to all the monkeys. [4-53-19b, 
c]_END

B_4_C_54_12
BEGIN_
अवस्थाने यदा एव त्वम् आसिष्यसि परंतप |तदा एव हरयः सर्वे त्यक्ष्यन्ति कृत निश्चयाः || ४५४१६_END
BEGIN_
"As and when you settle down in that underground, more so, an unbefitting place for a crown prince, oh, enemyburner 
Angada, then and there all the monkeys will desert you resolvedly. [45416]_END

B_4_C_55_2
BEGIN_
भ्रातुः ज्येष्ठस्य यो भार्याम् जीवितो महिषीम् प्रियाम् |धर्मेण मातरम् यः तु स्वीकरोति जुगुप्सितः || ४-५५-३
कथम् स धर्मम् जानीते येन भ्रात्रा दुरात्मना |युद्धाय अभिनियुक्तेन बिलस्य पिहितम् मुखम् || ४-५५-४_END
BEGIN_
"Which Sugreeva has arrogated his elder brother's wife when that elder brother is still alive and well, where 
she is morally his motherlike, an empress and a lady love of that elder brother, thus he is despicable, and which 
Sugreeva closed the mouth of the cavity when his brother in all his belief assigned and stationed him alone at 
the mouth of the cavity to fightback the demon Dundubhi if he tries to escape, all the more when his own brother 
is still inside the cavity, thus he is nefarious, how then he can be said as one conversant with moral rectitude? 
[4-55-3, 4]_END

B_4_C_52_23
BEGIN_
निमीलयत चक्षून्षि सर्वे वानर पुंगवाः || ४-५२-२७न हि निष्क्रमितुम् शक्यम् अनिमीलित लोचनैः |_END
BEGIN_
"All of you best vanara-s shall close up your eyelids, for it is indeed impossible to attempt an exit with unclose 
eyes." Thus that sainted lady said to monkeys. [4-52-27b, 28a]_END

B_4_C_53_18
BEGIN_
एतत् श्रुत्वा कुमारेण युव राजेन भाषितम् |सर्वे ते वानर श्रेष्ठाः करुणम् वाक्यम् अब्रुवन् || ४-५३-२०_END
BEGIN_
On hearing all that uttered by that youngish Angada, the crown prince, all of those prominent Vanara-s sympathetically 
spoke these words. [4-53-20]_END

B_4_C_54_13
BEGIN_
स्मरंतः पुत्र दाराणाम् नित्य उद्विग्ना बुभुक्षिताः |खेदिता दुःख शय्याभिः त्वाम् करिष्यन्ति पृष्ठतः || ४५४१७_END
BEGIN_
"Always sulking and reminiscing on their sons and wives, and hungered for the proximity of their kinfolk and hungered 
for diverse palatability as any monkey would cherish, even so, lamenting on the beds of lament they push you backwards. 
[45417]_END

B_4_C_55_3
BEGIN_
सत्यात् पाणि गृहीतः च कृत कर्मा महायशाः |विस्मृतो राघवो येन स कस्य सुकृतम् स्मरेत् || ४-५५-५_END
BEGIN_
"Which Sugreeva has overlooked no less than the great glorious Raghava, whom he truthfully befriended and from 
whom his own task of arrogating my kingdom by eliminating my father is facilitated, how then can he remember the 
good services of others like us? [4-55-5]_END

B_4_C_52_24
BEGIN_
ततो निमीलिताः सर्वे सुकुमार अंगुलैः करैः || ४-५२-२८सहसा पिदधुः दृष्टिम् हृष्टा गमन कान्क्षिणः |_END
BEGIN_
Then all of those desirers of departure are gladdened and immediately shut their eyelids, and further they lidded 
them with their delicately fingered hands. [4-52-28b, 29a]_END

B_4_C_53_19
BEGIN_
तीक्ष्णः प्रकृत्या सुग्रीवः प्रिया रक्तः च राघवः |समीक्ष्य अकृत कार्यान् तु तस्मिन् च समये गते || ४-५३-२१
अदृष्टायाम् च वैदेह्याम् दृष्ट्वा चैव समागतान् |राघव प्रिय कामाय घातयिष्यति असंशयम् || ४-५३-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Instinctively Sugreeva is a hot-tempered vanara and Raghava is interested in his beloved wife. The timeframe 
is lapsed and Vaidehi is unspotted. If we go back to Kishkindha now, on seeing us returning without completing 
our assignment, and with a thinking to satisfy Rama Sugreeva wishes to liquidate us without any doubt. [4-53-21, 
22]_END

B_4_C_54_14
BEGIN_
स त्वम् हीनः सुहृद्भिः च हित कामैः च बंधुभिः |तृणात् अपि भृश उद्विग्नः स्पंदमानात् भविष्यसि || ४५४१८_END
BEGIN_
"Devoid of goodhearted friends and wellwishing relatives, you will become highly sullen in solitariness. Such 
as you are you will end up as a highly frightened monkey, even from the shaking of a piece of straw._END

B_4_C_55_4
BEGIN_
लक्ष्मणस्य भयेन इह न अधर्म भय भीरुणा |आदिष्टा मार्गितुम् सीताम् धर्मः तस्मिन् कथम् भवेत् || ४-५५-६_END
BEGIN_
"He has ordered and sent us for searching Seetha owing to the fear from Lakshmana, but not as a coward fearing 
his own unscrupulousness, how then can scrupulosity be manifest in him? [4-55-6]_END

B_4_C_52_25
BEGIN_
वानराः तु महात्मानो हस्त रुद्ध मुखाः तदा || ४-५२-२९निमेष अन्तर मात्रेण बिलात् उत्तारिताः तथा |_END
BEGIN_
She then sailed those noble souled vanara-s who covered their faces with their hands through that cavity barely 
within a minute. [4-52-29b. 30a]_END

B_4_C_54_15
BEGIN_
अति उग्र वेगा निशिता घोरा लक्ष्मण सायकाः |अपवृत्तम् जिघांसन्तो महावेगा दुरासदाः || ४५४१९_END
BEGIN_
"By far, those fiercely frantic arrows of Lakshmana if targeted to kill you, in case you become a sidestepper 
from loyalties, will be terrifyingly twingeing. Further, those fierily frenetic arrows are irreversible. [45419]_END

B_4_C_53_20
BEGIN_
न क्षमम् च अपराद्धानाम् गमनम् स्वामि पार्श्वतः |प्रधानबूताः च वयम् सुग्रीवस्य समागताः || ४-५३-२३_END
BEGIN_
"It will be inexcusable for the culprits to pass at the sideways of lords, then where is the question of their 
coming into king's audience, and we should be barefaced to return because we are all the chieftains of Sugreeva 
who are coordinated and sent here. [4-53-23]_END

B_4_C_55_5
BEGIN_
तस्मिन् पापे कृतघ्ने तु स्मृति भिन्ने चल आत्मनि |आर्यः को विश्वसेत् जातु तत् कुलीनो विशेषतः || ४-५५-७_END
BEGIN_
"Who is that respectable one who can put belief in Sugreeva, while that Sugreeva is shameful by his shameless 
act of eliminating my father, and unmindful of tradition in usurping my mother and throne, and unthankful in requiting 
Rama by himself, instead of using us as pawns, and changeful in ignoring his promise to Rama, but in fearing for 
Lakshmana? Will it be possible especially for one like me belonging to his family? [4-55-7]_END

B_4_C_52_26
BEGIN_
उवाच सर्वान् तान् तत्र तापसी धर्म चारिणी || ४-५२-३०निःसृतान् विषमात् तस्मात् समाश्वास्य इदम् अब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_
That virtuous and sainted lady on comforting all of the monkeys, who are taken out of that precarious cavity, 
spoke this to them at the exterior of cavity. [4-52-30b, 31a]_END

B_4_C_54_16
BEGIN_
अस्माभिः तु गतम् सार्धम् विनीतवत् उपस्थितम् |आनुपूर्व्यात् तु सुग्रीवो राज्ये त्वाम् स्थापयिष्यति || ४५४२०_END
BEGIN_
"But, if you return to Kishkindha along with us, and if you obediently become Sugreeva's flanker, he establishes 
you only in kingdom as before. [45420]_END

B_4_C_53_21
BEGIN_
इह एव सीताम् अन्वीक्ष्य प्रवृत्तिम् उपलभ्य वा |नः चेत् गच्छाम तम् वीरम् गमिष्यामो यम क्षयम् || ४-५३-२४_END
BEGIN_
"If we do not return to that champion Sugreeva on searching somewhere here for Seetha, or on our educing some 
information about her, we will rather enter the realm of Yama, the Terminator." Thus the other monkeys discussed 
among themselves. [4-53-24]_END

B_4_C_56_0
BEGIN_
उपविष्टाः तु ते सर्वे यस्मिन् प्रायम् गिरि स्थले |
हरयो गृध्र राजः च तम् देशम् उपचक्रमे || ४-५६-१
सांपातिः नाम नाम्ना तु चिर जीवी विहंगमः |
भ्राता जटायुषः श्रीमान् प्रख्यात बल पौरुषः || ४-५६-२_END
BEGIN_
At which mountain's tableland those monkeys sat down for self-immolation, to that
area the elder brother of Jataayu, a kingly eagle known as Sampaati by name, one renowned one for
his forcefulness and aggressiveness, and a celebrated and sempiternal sky-flying eagle has arrived.
[4-56-1, 2]_END

B_4_C_55_6
BEGIN_
राज्ये पुत्रः प्रतिष्ठाप्यः स गुणो निर्गुणो अपि वा |कथम् शत्रु कुलीनम् माम् सुग्रीवो जीवयिष्यति || ४-५५-८_END
BEGIN_
"Whether a son is honest or dishonest he alone is investable in the kingdom. How then can Sugreeva let me, the 
one from the family of his enemy, live on? [4-55-8]_END

B_4_C_52_27
BEGIN_
एष विन्ध्यो गिरिः श्रीमान् नाना द्रुम लता आयुतः || ४-५२-३१एष प्रसवणः शैलः सागरो अयम् महा उदधिः |स्वस्ति 
वो अस्तु गमिष्यामि भवनम् वानरर्षभाः |इति उक्त्वा तत् बिलम् श्रीमत् प्रविवेश स्वयम्प्रभा || ४-५२-३२_END
BEGIN_
"This one which is surrounded by diverse trees and vines is the magnificent Vindhya Mountain, this mountain is 
Prasravana, and this vast expanse of water is the southerly ocean. Now I wish to return to my mansion... oh, best 
vanara-s, let safety betide you." saying thus Swayamprabha the Sainted Lady, re-entered the ostentatious cavity, 
called Riksha Bila. [4-52-31b, 32]_END

B_4_C_54_17
BEGIN_
धर्म राजः पितृव्यः ते प्रीति कामो दृढ व्रतः |शुचिः सत्य प्रतिज्ञः च स त्वाम् जातु न नाशयेत् || ४५४२१_END
BEGIN_
"Your paternaluncle Sugreeva's gleam is his honesty as he is free of dishonesty, his desire is affection as he 
is free of aversion, his dedication is staunch as he is free of prevarication, and he himself is exoneration as 
he is free from exploitation, thus in no way he liquidates you. [45421]_END

B_4_C_53_22
BEGIN_
प्लवंगमानाम् तु भय अर्दितानाम्श्रुत्वा वचः तार इदम् बभाषे |अलम् विषादेन बिलम् प्रविश्यवसाम सर्वे यदि 
रोचते वः || ४-५३-२५_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of fly-jumpers, who are tormented by fear of Sugreeva, Lt. Tara spoke this to them, "enough 
is your desperation, if you all are interested let us enter that cave again where we can live. [4-53-25]_END

B_4_C_56_1
BEGIN_
कंदरात् अभिनिष्क्रम्य स विन्ध्यस्य महागिरेः |
उपविष्टान् हरीन् दृष्ट्वा हृष्टात्मा गिरम् अब्रवीत् || ४-५६-३_END
BEGIN_
On coming out of the cave of the great-mountain Vindhya, Sampaati is gladden at
heart to see the monkeys sitting down there, and he spoke these words. [4-56-3]_END

B_4_C_55_7
BEGIN_
भिन्न मन्त्रो अपराद्धः च हीन शक्तिः कथम् हि अहम् |किष्किन्धाम् प्राप्य जीवेयम् अनाथ इव दुर्बलः || ४-५५-९_END
BEGIN_
"My slyness in planning to live in Black Hole has backfired, I am now culpable in not finding Seetha being the 
troop leader, and I am a powerless as you all are Sugreeva's side, how then can I live on indeed after reaching 
Kishkindha, like caitiff turned into a wretch. [4-55-9]_END

B_4_C_53_23
BEGIN_
इदम् हि माया विहितम् सुदुर्गमम्प्रभूत वृक्ष उदक भोज्य पेयम् |इह अस्ति नः न एव भयम् पुरंदरात्न राघवात् 
वानर राजतो अपि वा || ४-५३-२६_END
BEGIN_
"That highly impassable cavity is contrived by the demon Maya and it is abundant with trees, water, eatables and 
potables, and there is no fear even from Indra in that cavity, nor from Raghava, nor from Sugreeva, the king of 
monkeys." So said Lt. Tara to all. [4-53-26]_END

B_4_C_54_18
BEGIN_
प्रिय कामः च ते मातुः तत् अर्थम् च अस्य जीवितम् |तस्य अपत्यम् च न अस्ति अन्यत् तस्मात् अंगद गम्यताम् || ४५४२२_END
BEGIN_
"He is your mother's wellwisher, the strife of Sugreeva's life is for her only, more so, there is no other posterity 
to him than you. Oh, Angada, therefore go back to Kishkindha, rather than deflecting, deviating and deserting 
your own kingdom. [45422]_END

B_4_C_56_2
BEGIN_
विधिः किल नरम् लोके विधानेन अनुवर्तते |
यथा अयम् विहितो भक्ष्यः चिरात् मह्यम् उपागतः || ४-५६-४_END
BEGIN_
"Whether it is good or bad, fate indeed follows humans in this world procedurally,
why because, this fated and long-waited food has now come nigh of me... [4-56-4]_END

B_4_C_55_8
BEGIN_
उपांशु दण्डेन हि माम् बंधनेन उपपादयेत् |शठः क्रूरो नृशंसः च सुग्रीवो राज्य कारणात् || ४-५५-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed he surceases me by some mysterious trammelling punishment, for that Sugreeva becomes disingenuous, ferocious, 
also barbarous just for the reason of his kingship. [4-55-10]_END

B_4_C_53_24
BEGIN_
श्रुत्वा अंगदस्य अपि वचो अनुकूलम्ऊचुः च सर्वे हरयः प्रतीताः |यथा न हन्येम तथा विधानम्असक्तम् अद्य 
एव विधीयताम् नः || ४-५३-२७_END
BEGIN_
On hearing Angada's words, as well as the words of Lt. Tara that are trended to Angada's words, all the monkeys 
compliantly spoke with believability, "in which way we all will not be killed that way may be waymarked, and promptly 
make it happen now only." So said all the monkeys to Angada. [4-53-27]_END

B_4_C_56_3
BEGIN_
परंपराणाम् भक्षिष्ये वानराणाम् मृतम् मृतम् |
उवाच एतत् वचः पक्षी तान् निरीक्ष्य प्लवंगमान् || ४-५६-५_END
BEGIN_
"I wish to eat them frugally, killing one by one and eating one by one, preying on
one on one day, and then preying upon the other on the other day..." thus that bird spoke those
words on seeing the massy fly-jumpers. [4-56-5]_END

B_4_C_55_9
BEGIN_
बंधनात् च अवसादात् मे श्रेयः प्रायोपवेशनम् |अनुजानंतु माम् सर्वे गृहम् गच्छंतु वानराः || ४-५५-११_END
BEGIN_
"Fast unto death behoves me than trammels and tramples, thus you all be acquiescent to my proposal and you may 
go back to your dwellings. [4-55-11]_END

B_4_C_56_4
BEGIN_
तस्य तत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा भक्ष लुब्धस्य पक्षिणः |
अंगदः परम् आयस्तो हनूमंतम् अथ अब्रवीत् || ४-५६-६_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of that gormandising bird, Angada became highly breathless and
then spoke to Hanuma. [4-56-6]_END

B_4_C_55_10
BEGIN_
अहम् वः प्रतिजानामि न गमिष्यामि अहम् पुरीम् |इह एव प्रायम् आसिष्ये श्रेयो मरणम् एव मे || ४-५५-१२_END
BEGIN_
"I am reiterating to you all that I do not wish to go to the city of Kishkindha, and here only I sit fasting unto 
death, as death alone is expedient to me. [4-55-12]_END

B_4_C_56_5
BEGIN_
पश्य सीता - गृध्रा - अपदेशेन साक्षात् वैवस्वतो यमः |
इमम् देशम् अनुप्राप्तो वानराणाम् विपत्तये || ४-५६-७_END
BEGIN_
"Look! In the name of an eagle, the son of the Sun, Yama, the Terminator, has
manifestly arrived at this area for the fatality of monkeys... thus ill luck is still haunting
us... [4-56-7]_END

B_4_C_55_11
BEGIN_
अभिवादन पूर्वम् तु राजा कुशलम् एव च |अभिवादन पूर्वम् तु राघवौ बलशालिनौ || ४-५५-१३वाच्यः तातः यवीयान् मे 
सुग्रीवो वानर ईश्वरः |_END
BEGIN_
"On my behalf Raghava-s wellbeing may be enquired firstly paying deference to them, so also the wellbeing of my 
paternal uncle and king may be enquired, only after paying deference to that lord of vanara-s. [4-55-13, 14a]_END

B_4_C_56_6
BEGIN_
रामस्य न कृतम् कार्यम् न कृतम् राज शाशनम् |
हरीणाम् इयम् अज्ञाता विपत्तिः सहसा आगता || ४-५६-८_END
BEGIN_
"We fulfilled neither Rama's task, nor the decree of our king, but this unknown
catastrophe has abruptly bechanced for the monkeys... [4-56-8]_END

B_4_C_55_12
BEGIN_
आरोग्य पूर्वम् कुशलम् वाच्या माता रुमा च मे || ४-५५-१४मातरम् चैव मे ताराम् आश्वासयितुम् अर्हथ |प्रकृत्या 
प्रिय पुत्रा सा सानुक्रोशा तपस्विनी || ४-५५-१५विनष्टम् माम् इह श्रुत्वा व्यक्तम् हास्यति जीवितम् |_END
BEGIN_
"My step-mother Ruma may be asked after regarding her healthiness. And it will be apt of you to solace my mother 
Lady Tara, who by her nature is a warm-hearted and austerely lady who cherishes her son more, and such as she 
is she will obviously leave off her life on hearing that I breathed my last." So said Angada to all monkeys. [4-55-14b, 
16a]_END

B_4_C_56_7
BEGIN_
वैदेह्याः प्रिय कामेन कृतम् कर्म जटायुषा |
गृध्र राजेन यत् तत्र श्रुतम् वः तत् अशेषतः || ४-५६-९_END
BEGIN_
"You all have heard in its entirety what deed the kingly Jataayu has done wishing to
do good to Vaidehi... [4-56-9]_END

B_4_C_55_13
BEGIN_
एतावत् उक्त्वा वचनम् वृद्धान् तान् अभिवाद्य च || ४-५५-१६विवेश अंगदो भूमौ रुदन् दर्भेषु दुर्मनाः |_END
BEGIN_
On speaking to that point and after paying deference to older vanara-s available there, Angada puling glum facedly 
reclined on the sacred grass spread on ground. [4-55-16b, 17a]_END

B_4_C_56_8
BEGIN_
तथा सर्वाणि भूतानि तिर्यक् योनि गतानि अपि |
प्रियम् कुर्वन्ति रामस्य त्यक्त्वा प्राणान् यथा वयम् || ४-५६-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Like that all beings, even those birthed in animality, are doing what that is
agreeable to Rama even on forgoing their own lives, as with us... [4-56-10]_END

B_4_C_57_0
BEGIN_
शोकात् भ्रष्ट स्वरम् अपि श्रुत्वा ते हरि यूथपाः |
श्रद्दधुः न एव तत् वाक्यम् कर्मणा तस्य शन्किताः || ४-५७-१_END
BEGIN_
Though Sampaati's voice is turned husky by his sadness for the demise of his brother
Jataayu, the monkey commanders doubtingly disbelieved neither him nor even his words by the fact of
his being an eagle intending to kill and eat up all the monkeys. [4-57-1]_END

B_4_C_55_14
BEGIN_
तस्य संविशतः तत्र रुदन्तो वानर ऋषभाः || ४-५५-१७नयनेभ्यः प्रमुमुचुः उष्णम् वै वारि दुःखिताः |_END
BEGIN_
Apropos to Angada's recumbency on ground, the other outstanding Vanara-s snivellingly sluiced down seethingly 
effusive teardrops emotionally. [4-55-17b, 18a]_END

B_4_C_56_9
BEGIN_
अन्योन्यम् उपकुर्वन्ति स्नेह कारुण्य यन्त्रिताः |
ततः तस्य उपकार अर्थम् त्यजत आत्मानम् आत्मना || ४-५६-११_END
BEGIN_
"Even animals will be mutually succouring by their instinct of concern and
camaraderie, therefore, let each of us leave off our souls, soulfully... [4-56-11]_END

B_4_C_57_1
BEGIN_
ते प्रायम् उपविष्टाः तु दृष्ट्वा गृध्रम् प्लवंगमाः |
चक्रुः बुद्धिम् तदा रौद्राम् सर्वान् नः भक्षयिष्यति || ४-५७-२_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the eagle those fly-jumpers who sat for fast-unto-death have become
furious at the eagle thinking that, "that eagle wishes to eat up all of us..." Thus, the monkeys
deliberated the eagle's words. [4-57-2]_END

B_4_C_55_15
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवम् चैव निन्दन्तः प्रशंसन्तः च वालिनम् || ४-५५-१८परिवार्य अंगदम् सर्वे व्यवस्यन् प्रायम् आसितुम् |_END
BEGIN_
While disesteeming Sugreeva but esteeming Vali, all of the vanara-s have gathered around Angada deciding to sit 
down for fasting unto death in step with Angada. [4-55-18b, 19a]_END

B_4_C_56_10
BEGIN_
प्रियम् कृत्वा हि रामस्य धर्मज्ञेन जटायुषा |
राघव अर्थे परिश्रान्ता वयम् संत्यक्त जीविताः || ४-५६-१२
कांताराणि प्रपन्नाः स्म न च पश्याम मैथिलीम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Conscientious Jataayu has done a deed much liked by Rama, and we too have been
trekking the forests without caring even for our lives in the cause of Rama, but we have not seen
Maithili... [4-56-12, 13a]_END

B_4_C_57_2
BEGIN_
सर्वथा प्रायम् आसीनान् यदि नः भक्षयिष्यति |
कृत कृत्या भविष्यामः क्षिप्रम् सिद्धिम् इतो गताः || ४-५७-३_END
BEGIN_
"We are sitting for fast-unto-death and if that eagle wishes eat us let it be so...
then our deliverance will be achieved in anyway and we will go to heaven from here..." Thus, some
other monkeys gave thought to lower that eagle down. [4-57-3]_END

B_4_C_55_16
BEGIN_
तत् वाक्यम् वालि पुत्रस्य विज्ञाय प्लवग ऋषभाः || ४-५५-१९उपस्पृश्य उदकम् सर्वे प्राक् मुखाः समुपाविशन् |
दक्षिण अग्रेषु दर्भेषु उदक् तीरम् समाश्रिताः || ४-५५-२०मुमूर्षवओ हरिश्रेष्टा एतत् क्षमम् इति स्म ह |_END
BEGIN_
Those best ones among fly-jumpers on discerning the words of Angada, the son of Vali, and agreeing to what all 
said by Angada as appropriate, they positioned themselves on the sacred grass after touching waters sacramentally. 
The sacred-grass is spread as sacred beds to cast off their lives. The edges of grass blades are positioned southward. 
As they are on that northern shore of southern ocean, all those best monkeys who are bent on to self-immolation, 
they became recumbent facing eastward. [4-55-19b, 21a]_END

B_4_C_57_3
BEGIN_
एताम् बुद्धिम् ततः चक्रुः सर्वे ते हरि यूथपाः |
अवतार्य गिरेः शृंगात् गृध्रम् आह अंगदः तदा || ४-५७-४_END
BEGIN_
When all of the monkey chiefs made up their mind in this way, then some of them on
going to the mountaintop brought that eagle down, and then Angada spoke to the eagle. [4-57-4]_END

B_4_C_56_11
BEGIN_
स सुखी गृध्र राजः तु रावणेन हतो रणे |
मुक्तः च सुग्रीव भयात् गतः च परमाम् गतिम् || ४-५६-१३_END
BEGIN_
"He that kingly eagle Jataayu who is killed by Ravana is a happy soul, and he is
even relieved from the fear of Sugreeva as he departed on the Avenue of Sublimity... [4-56-13b,
c]_END

B_4_C_55_17
BEGIN_
रामस्य वन वासम् च क्षयम् दशरथस्य च || ४-५५-२१जनस्थान वधम् चैव वधम् चैव जटायुषः |हरणम् चैव वैदेह्या वालिनः 
च वधम् तथा |राम कोपम् च वदताम् हरीणाम् भयम् आगतः || ४-५५-२२_END
BEGIN_
An unknown apprehensive dread came upon those monkeys when they discussed Rama's living in forests, Dasharatha's 
demise, calamity caused to Janasthaana, casualty to Jataayu, like that the stealing of Vaidehi and slaying of 
Vali. [4-55-21, 22]_END

B_4_C_56_12
BEGIN_
जटायुषो विनाशेन राज्ञो दशरथस्य च |
हरणेन च वैदेह्याः संशयम् हरयो गताः || ४-५६-१४_END
BEGIN_
"By the ending of Jataayu and by the end of Dasharatha, also by the purloin of
Vaidehi, all of the monkeys are piled into a predicament... [4-56-14]_END

B_4_C_57_4
BEGIN_
बभूवुः ऋक्षरजो नाम वानरेन्द्रः प्रतापवान् |
मम आर्यः पार्थिवः पक्षिन् धार्मिकौ तस्य च आत्मजौ || ४-५७-५
सुग्रीवः चैव वली च पुत्रौ घन बलौ उभौ |
लोके विश्रुत कर्मा अभूत् राजा वाली पिता मम || ४-५७-६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, bird, my noble grandfather is known as Rikshaja who was a valorous and an
outstanding monkey among all monkeys, was the king of monkeys. He has two generous and great mighty
sons namely Vali and Sugreeva. My father Vali was highly renowned in the world for his bold acts,
and he became the king later to my grandfather... [4-57-5, 6]_END

B_4_C_55_18
BEGIN_
स संविशद्भिः बहुभिः महीधरोमहाअद्रि कूट प्रमितैः प्लवंगमैः |बभूव सन्नादित निर्दर अन्तरोभृशम् नदद्भिः 
जलदैः इव अंबरम् || ४-५५-२३_END
BEGIN_
While those many fly-jumpers who mirror up great mountaintops by their physique are recumbent discussing stridently, 
the entrails of caves of mountain are rendered strident, and that mountain itself appeared like skyscape filled 
with strident clouds about to burst a good fortune. [4-55-23]_END

B_4_C_56_13
BEGIN_
राम लक्ष्मणयोः वासाम् अरण्ये सह सीतया |
राघवस्य च बाणेन वालिनः च तथा वधः || ४-५६-१५
राम कोपात् अशेषाणाम् राक्षसाम् च तथा वधम् |
कैकेय्या वर दानेन इदम् च विकृतम् कृतम् || ४-५६-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Just by giving boons to Kaikeyi, the quandaries like Rama's dwelling in forests
along with Seetha and Lakshmana, as a result Rama's fury eliminating complete demons of
Janasthaana, and as a result Raghava's arrow exterminating Val, have come to pass." Thus Angada is
lamenting. [4-56-15,16]_END

B_4_C_57_5
BEGIN_
राजा कृत्स्नस्य जगतः इक्ष्वाकूणाम् महारथः |
रामो दाशरथिः श्रीमान् प्रविष्टो दण्डका वनम् || ४-५७-७
लक्ष्मणेन सह भ्रात्रा वैदेह्या च अपि भार्यया |
पितुः निदेश निरतो धर्मम् पन्थानम् आश्रितः || ४-५७-८_END
BEGIN_
"Among Ikshvaku-s there is a great-charioteer, a king for the entire world, a
peerless person, and he is the son of Dasharatha, namely Rama, and abiding by his father's
directives and opting for righteous course of conduct, he moved into Dandaka forests along with his
brother Lakshmana and even with his wife Vaidehi... [4-57-7, 8]_END

B_4_C_56_14
BEGIN_
तत् असुखम् अनुकीर्तितम् वचो
भुवि पतितान् च निरीक्ष्य वानरान् |
भृश चकित मतिः महामतिः
कृपणम् उदाहृतवान् स गृध्रराजः || ४-५६-१७_END
BEGIN_
On observing the monkeys who lay recumbent on ground and on hearing them eulogising
the death of Jataayu he that king of eagles Sampaati is highly perturbed at that uncomfortable
information about Jatayu, and that high minded Sampaati sorrowfully spelled out this word.
[4-56-17]_END

B_4_C_57_6
BEGIN_
तस्य भार्या जनस्थानात् रावणेन हृता बलात् |
रामस्य च पितुः मित्रम् जटायुः नाम गृध्र राट् || ४-५७-९
ददर्श सीताम् वैदेहीम् ह्रियमाणाम् विहायसा |_END
BEGIN_
"Ravana forcibly abducted his wife from Janasthaana, namely Seetha, the princess
from Videha kingdom, and a kingly eagle named Jataayu, who is a friend of Rama's father Dasharatha,
has seen her while she was being abducted by skyway. [4-57-9, 10a]_END

B_4_C_56_15
BEGIN_
तत् तु श्रुत्वा तदा वाक्यम् अंगदस्य मुख उद्गतम् |
अब्रवीत् वचनम् गृध्रः तीक्ष्ण तुण्डो महास्वनः || ४-५६-१८_END
BEGIN_
That shredder-billed eagle Sampaati said this sentence voicing thunderously on
hearing words voiced by Angada. [4-56-18]_END

B_4_C_57_7
BEGIN_
रावणम् विरथम् कृत्वा स्थापयित्वा च मैथिलीम् |
परिश्रान्तः च वृद्धः च रावणेन हतो रणे || ४-५७-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Jatayu is overly tired when he made Ravana's chariot defective and withheld
Maithili from abduction as he is senescent, then Ravana killed him in that conflict... [4-57-10b,
c]_END

B_4_C_56_16
BEGIN_
को अयम् गिरा घोषयति प्राणैः प्रियतरस्य मे |
जटायुषो वधम् भ्रातुः कंपयन् इव मे मनः || ४-५६-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Who speaks to announce as though to quake my heart that Jatayu, the more precious
brother of mine than my own lives, is slain? [4-56-19]_END

B_4_C_57_8
BEGIN_
एवम् गृध्रो हतः तेन रावणेन बलीयसा |
संस्कृतः च अपि रामेण गतः च गतिम् उत्तमाम् || ४-५७-११_END
BEGIN_
"Thus that eagle was killed by that mighty Ravana, but solemnised by the obsequies
performed by Rama, he departed on a sublime avenue to heavens... [4-57-11]_END

B_4_C_56_17
BEGIN_
कथम् आसीत् जनस्थाने युद्धम् राक्षस गृध्रयोः |
नामधेयम् इदम् भ्रातुः चिरस्य अद्य मया श्रुतम् || ४-५६-२०_END
BEGIN_
"How a combat occasioned between that eagle and a demon in Janasthaana, and how am I
hearing this name of my brother after a long time... [4-56-20]_END

B_4_C_57_9
BEGIN_
ततो मम पितृव्येण सुग्रीवेण महात्मना |
चकार राघवः सख्यम् सः अवधीत् पितरम् मम || ४-५७-१२
मम पित्रा विरुद्धो हि सुग्रीवः सचिवैः सह |
निहत्य वालिनम् रामः ततः तम् अभिषेचयत् || ४-५७-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Then Raghava made friendship with my paternal uncle Sugreeva, an intellectual
autocrat, and Sugreeva got my father killed. Since Sugreeva antagonised my father, my father
interdicted him along with his ministers, and Rama killed my father Vali and anointed Sugreeva...
[4-57-12, 13]_END

B_4_C_56_18
BEGIN_
इच्छेयम् गिरि दुर्गात् च भवद्भिः अवतारितुम् |
यवीयसो गुणज्ञस्य श्लाघनीयस्य विक्रमैः || ४-५६-२१
अति दीर्घस्य कालस्य परितुष्टो अस्मि कीर्तितनात् |_END
BEGIN_
"I wish you to get me down from these mountain soars. After a long time I have heard
about my younger brother who is straightforward, praiseworthy for his valour, and I am glad that
too spoke of him praisefully... [4-56-21, 22a]_END

B_4_C_57_10
BEGIN_
स राज्ये स्थापितः तेन सुग्रीवो वानरेश्वरः |
राजा वानर मुख्यानाम् तेन प्रस्थापिता वयम् || ४-५७-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Rama enthroned Sugreeva as the ruler of all vanara-s and that king of all vanara
chiefs expedited all of us... [4-57-14]_END

B_4_C_56_19
BEGIN_
तत् इच्छेयम् अहम् श्रोतुम् विनाशम् वानर ऋषभाः || ४-५६-२२
भ्रातुः जटायुषः तस्य जनस्थान निवासिनः |_END
BEGIN_
"Thereby, oh, best vanara-s, I wish to listen about the death of my brother Jataayu
when he was in Janasthaana... [4-56-22b, 23a]_END

B_4_C_57_11
BEGIN_
एवम् राम प्रयुक्ताः तु मार्गमाणाः ततः ततः |
वैदेहीम् न अधिगच्छामो रात्रौ सूर्य प्रभाम् इव || ४-५७-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Though we are spearheaded by Rama and though we searched thereabouts for Vaidehi at
the behest of Sugreeva, as with a nightly sunshine Vaidehi is unattainable for us... [4-57-15]_END

B_4_C_56_20
BEGIN_
तस्य एव च मम भ्रातुः सखा दशरथः कथम् || ४-५६-२३
यस्य रामः प्रियः पुत्रो ज्येष्ठो गुरु जन प्रियः |_END
BEGIN_
"Whose eldest and dear son is Rama, the creditable one for doyens, that Dasharatha
is the friend of my brother Jatayu/ But how did Dasharatha pass away? [4-56-23b, 24a]_END

B_4_C_57_12
BEGIN_
ते वयम् दण्दकारण्यम् विचित्य सुसमाहिताः |
अज्ञानात् तु प्रविष्टाः स्म धरण्या विवृतम् बिलम् || ४-५७-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Such as we were we searched Dandaka forest very meticulously, but we unwittingly
entered into a wide-opened Black Hole of the earth... [4-57-16]_END

B_4_C_56_21
BEGIN_
सूर्य अंशु दग्ध पक्षत्वात् न शक्नोमि विसर्पितुम् |
इच्छेयम् पर्वतात् अस्मात् अवतर्तुम् अरिन्दमाः || ४-५६-२४_END
BEGIN_
"I am incapable to spread my wings widely as they are burnt by Sun's rays, hence oh,
enemy-chasteners, I wish you to lower me down from this mountain..." Thus Sampaati sought for the
help of monkeys. [4-56-24b, c]_END

B_4_C_57_13
BEGIN_
मयस्य माया विहितम् तत् बिलम् च विचिन्वताम् |
व्यतीतः तत्र नः मासः यः राज्ञा समयः कृतः || ४-५७-१७_END
BEGIN_
"During our search in that Black Hole, which was crafted by the wizardry of demon
Maya, the month fixed by our king for our return has been elapsed... [4-57-17]_END

B_4_C_57_14
BEGIN_
ते वयम् कपि राजस्य सर्वे वचन कारिणः |
कृताम् संस्थाम् अतिक्रान्ता भयात् प्रायम् उपासिताः || ४-५७-१८_END
BEGIN_
"We who are all supposed to execute the order of our king, we have exceeded the
established norm of timeframe, and for fear of fury from our king Sugreeva we sat down for
fast-unto-death... [4-57-18]_END

B_4_C_57_15
BEGIN_
क्रुद्धे तस्मिन् तु काकुत्स्थे सुग्रीवे च स लक्ष्मणे |
गतानाम् अपि सर्वेषाम् तत्र नः न अस्ति जीवितम् || ४-५७-१९_END
BEGIN_
"When Rama along with Lakshmana, and even Sugreeva will be infuriated by our
infringement of time, and even on our going to Kishkindha, as infringers there will be no survival
for all of us..." Thus Angada narrated their plight to Sampaati. [4-57-19]_END

B_4_C_58_0
BEGIN_
इति उक्तः करुणम् वाक्यम् वानरैः त्यक्त जीवितैः |
स बाष्पो वानरान् गृध्रः प्रत्युवाच महास्वनः || ४-५८-१_END
BEGIN_
When those monkeys whose lives are almost purged spoke to Sampaati with such dreary
words, that thunder-voiced eagle tearfully spoke to those vanara-s. [4-58-1]_END

B_4_C_58_1
BEGIN_
यवीयान् मम स भ्राता जटायुः नाम वानराः |
यम् आख्यात हतम् युद्धे रावणेन बलीयसा || ४-५८-२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, vanara-s, of whom it is enounced that mighty Ravana felled him in a combat,
that one is my younger brother named Jatayu... [4-58-2]_END

B_4_C_58_2
BEGIN_
वृद्ध भावात् अपक्षत्वात् शृण्वन् तत् अपि मर्षये |
न हि मे शक्तिः अद्य अस्ति भ्रातुः वैर विमोक्षणे || ४-५८-३_END
BEGIN_
"Even though I hear that my brother is slain I have to resign myself from any
activity owing to my oldness and my winglessness, and presently I am indeed incapacitated to
retaliate my brother's enemy... [4-58-3]_END

B_4_C_58_3
BEGIN_
पुरा वृत्र वधे वृत्ते स च अहम् च जय एषिणौ |
आदित्यम् उपयातौ स्वो ज्वलंतम् रश्मि मालिनम् || ४-५८-४_END
BEGIN_
"Once, when the elimination of demon Vritta was taking place at the hand of Indra,
we two eagle-brothers sportively desiring to surpass each other flew sunward, and we have gone very
near to the scorch-rayed sun... [4-58-4]_END

B_4_C_58_4
BEGIN_
आवृत्य आकाश मार्गेण जवेन स्वर् गतौ भृशम् |
मध्यम् प्राप्ते च सूर्ये च जटायुः अवसीदति || ४-५८-५_END
BEGIN_
"Covering the skyway we have gone to firmament much speedily, then bechanced is
noontide and thus bechanced is the scorching of the noontime sun, and then Jataayu started to
founder... [4-58-5]_END

B_4_C_58_5
BEGIN_
तम् अहम् भ्रातरम् दृष्ट्वा सूर्य रश्मिभिः अर्दितम् |
पक्षाभ्यम् छादयामास स्नेहात् परम विह्वलम् || ४-५८-६_END
BEGIN_
"On seeing him who is being thwarted by scorching sunrays, then I started to cover
my highly fretful brother with both of my wings in all my brotherliness... [4-58-6]_END

B_4_C_59_0
BEGIN_
ततः तत् अमृत आस्वादम् गृध्र राजेन भाषितम् |
निशम्य मुदितो हृष्टाः ते वचः प्लवगर्षभाः || ४-५९-१_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of that kingly eagle Sampaati that are relishable like
ambrosia, then those best fly-jumpers are gladdened and rejoiced. [4-59-1]_END

B_4_C_58_6
BEGIN_
निर्दग्ध पत्रः पतितो विन्ध्ये अहम् वानरर्षभाः |
अहम् अस्मिन् वसन् भ्रातुः प्रवृत्तिम् न उपलक्षये || ४-५८-७_END
BEGIN_
"And oh, vanara-chiefs, when sunrays have utterly burned my wings I fell down on
this Mt. Vindhya, and while living hereabouts constrainedly, I could pay no attention to my
brother's experiences or, at least his existence, or otherwise..." So lamented old Sampaati.
[4-58-7]_END

B_4_C_59_1
BEGIN_
जांबवान् वानर श्रेष्ठः सह सर्वैः प्लवंगमैः |
भू तलात् सहसा उत्थाय गृध्र राजानम् अब्रवीत् || ४-५९-२_END
BEGIN_
Then the best fly-jumper Jambavanta got up along with all of the fly-jumpers from
the surface of earth on which they sat for self-immolation, and spoke to kingly eagle Sampaati.
[4-59-2]_END

B_4_C_58_7
BEGIN_
जटायुषः तु एवम् उक्तो भ्रात्रा सम्पातिना तदा |
युव राजो महाप्राज्ञः प्रत्युवाच अंगदः तदा || ४-५८-८_END
BEGIN_
When Sampaati the brother of Jataayu spoke in that way, then the highly discerning
crown prince Angada replied him. [4-58-8]_END

B_4_C_59_2
BEGIN_
क्व सीता केन वा दृष्टा को वा हरति मैथिलीम् |
तत् आख्यातु भवान् सर्वम् गतिः भव वन ओकसाम् || ४-५९-३_END
BEGIN_
"You please tell vividly as to where is Seetha, who has actually seen her, who has
abducted Maithili, and thus you help all these forest-dwellers. [4-59-3]_END

B_4_C_58_8
BEGIN_
जटायुषो यदि भ्राता श्रुतम् ते गदितम् मया |
आख्याहि यदि जानासि निलयम् तस्य रक्षसः || ४-५८-९_END
BEGIN_
"If you are the brother of Jataayu, if you have heard whatever I have said in praise
of Jataayu, and if you are aware of the whereabouts of Ravana... please tell it... [4-58-9]_END

B_4_C_59_3
BEGIN_
को दाशरथि बाणानाम् वज्र वेग निपातिनाम् |
स्वयम् लक्ष्मणम् मुक्तानाम् न चिंतयति विक्रमम् || ४-५९-४_END
BEGIN_
"Who is inadvertent of the onslaught of Rama's arrows, or of those that are
personally bolted by Lakshmana, which arrows will be falling with the speed of thunderbolts?" Thus,
Jambavanta and others asked Sampaati. [4-59-4]_END

B_4_C_58_9
BEGIN_
अदीर्घ दर्शिनम् तम् वा रावणम् राक्षसाधिपम् |
अन्तिके यदि वा दूरे यदि जानासि शंस नः || ४-५८-१०_END
BEGIN_
"If you are aware of the location of that bigoted and knavish demon Ravana, please
inform us. Doesn't matter whether that location is nearby or far off as we can search far and
wide..." Thus Angada asked Sampaati. [4-58-10]_END

B_4_C_59_4
BEGIN_
स हरीन् प्रति संयुक्तान् सीता श्रुति समाहितान् |
पुनः आश्वासयन् प्रीत इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् || ४-५९-५_END
BEGIN_
Sampaati is gladdened at the monkeys who refrained from self-immolation, and he
gladly said this sentence to them so as to cheer them up who are now contemplating to listen about
Seetha. [4-59-5]_END

B_4_C_58_10
BEGIN_
ततो अब्रवीत् महातेजा भ्राता ज्येष्ठो जटायुषः |
आत्म अनुरूपम् वचनम् वानरान् संप्रहर्षयन् || ४-५८-११_END
BEGIN_
Then Sampaati, the high-spirited elder brother of Jataayu, spoke these words that
are self-befitting and that would highly gladden the monkeys. [4-58-11]_END

B_4_C_59_5
BEGIN_
श्रूयताम् इह वैदेह्या यथा मे हरणम् श्रुतम् |
येन च अपि मम आख्यातम् यत्र च आयत लोचना || ४-५९-६_END
BEGIN_

whom it is said to me, and where that wide-eyed Seetha is... [4-59-6]_END

B_4_C_58_11
BEGIN_
निर्दग्ध पक्षो गृध्रो अहम् गत वीर्यः प्लवम् गमाः |
वाङ् मात्रेण तु रामस्य करिष्ये साह्यम् उत्तमम् || ४-५८-१२_END
BEGIN_
"I am an eagle with utterly burnt wings and vanished valiance, even then, I wish to
render a best service in the task of Rama, at least verbally... [4-58-12]_END

B_4_C_59_6
BEGIN_
अहम् अस्मिन् गिरौ दुर्गे बहु योजनम् आयते |
चिरात् निपतितो वृद्धः क्षीण प्राण पराक्रमः || ४-५९-७_END
BEGIN_
"At one time I fell down on this impassable mountain which is breadth-wise in many
yojana-s, whereupon my age has advanced and my liveliness and forcefulness have slackened...
[4-59-7]_END

B_4_C_58_12
BEGIN_
जानामि वारुणान् लोकान् विष्णोः त्रैविक्रमान् अपि |
देव असुर विमर्दाम् च हि अमृतस्य च मंथनम् || ४-५८-१३_END
BEGIN_
"I have seen the netherworlds of Rain-god viz., earth and its substrata like
atala. vitala, sutala, paataala terrains... and I have even seen those
empyrean worlds that were triply trodden by Vishnu, and the intermediary regions of upper and lower
worlds where gods and demons combated ghastlily, and because I am that aged I have also seen the
unseeable Milky Ocean when it was churned for ambrosia... [4-58-13]_END

B_4_C_60_0
BEGIN_
ततः कृत उदकम् स्नातम् तम् गृध्रम् हरि यूथपाः |
उपविष्टा गिरौ रम्ये परिवार्य समन्ततः || ४-६०-१_END
BEGIN_
Then the monkey commanders sat on that beautiful mountain surrounding the eagle from
all over, after that eagle has offered water-oblations for his deceased Jataayu and bathed for
purification. [4-60-1]_END

B_4_C_59_7
BEGIN_
तम् माम् एवम् गतम् पुत्रः सुपार्श्वो नाम नामतः |
आहारेण यथा कालम् बिभर्ति पतताम् वरः || ४-५९-८_END
BEGIN_
"My son who is the best one among all birds, and who is named as Supaarshva by his
name is sustaining me who am deteriorated to dire straits, with timely sustenance... [4-59-8]_END

B_4_C_58_13
BEGIN_
रामस्य यत् इदम् कार्यम् कर्तव्यम् प्रथमम् मया |
जरया च हतम् तेजः प्राणाः च शिथिला मम || ४-५८-१४_END
BEGIN_
"It is I who am to render service in this task of Rama firstly, than you vanara-s,
as the common enemy of Rama and Jataayu is my first enemy, but I am decrepit as oldness has marred

B_4_C_60_1
BEGIN_
तम् अंगदम् उपासीनम् तैः सर्वैः हरिभिः वृतम् |
जनित प्रत्ययो हर्षात् संपातिः पुनः अब्रवीत् || ४-६०-२_END
BEGIN_
Sampaati who earned trustworthiness of monkeys, and who is sitting surrounded by all
monkeys, again gladly spoke to Angada who sat at his close by. [4-60-2]_END

B_4_C_58_14
BEGIN_
तरुणी रूप संपन्ना सर्व आभरण भूषिता |
ह्रियमाणा मया दृष्टा रावणेन दुरात्मना || ४-५८-१५
क्रोशन्ती राम राम इति लक्ष्मण इति च भामिनी |
भूषणानि अपविध्यन्ती गात्राणि च विधुन्वती || ४-५८-१६_END
BEGIN_
"I have seen a youngish lady while she is being stolen away by the black-hearted
demon Ravana. She richly in her mien, embellished with every befitting jewellery for a princess,
and that lady in fury was bewailing calling, 'Rama... Rama...' even calling 'Lakshmana...' and she
was throwing her ornaments down and her limbs were highly wriggly to set herself free from that
demon... [4-58-15, 16]_END

B_4_C_59_8
BEGIN_
तीक्ष्ण कामाः तु गंधर्वाः तीक्ष्ण कोपा भुजंगमाः |
मृगाणाम् तु भयम् तीक्ष्णम् ततः तीक्ष्ण क्षुधा वयम् || ४-५९-९_END
BEGIN_
"Passion is exigent to the celestial-artists gandharva-s, aggression is exigent to

B_4_C_60_2
BEGIN_
कृत्वा निःशब्दम् एक अग्राः शृण्वन्तु हरयो मम |
तथ्यम् संकीर्तयिष्यामि यथा जानामि मैथिलीम् || ४-६०-३_END

B_4_C_58_15

सूर्य प्रभा इव शैल अग्रे तस्याः कौशेयम् उत्तमम् |
असिते राक्षसे भाति यथा वा तडित् अंबुदे || ४-५८-१७_END

"In the flank of that blackish demon her best ochry silk-sari was dazzling like

B_4_C_59_9
BEGIN_
स कदाचित् क्षुधा आर्तस्य मम आहार कान्क्षिणः |

B_4_C_60_3

सूर्य ताप परीत अंगो निर्दग्धः सूर्य रश्मिभिः || ४-६०-४_END

"Oh, impeccable Angada, once I have fallen on the peak of this Mt. Vindhya when

B_4_C_58_16

श्रूयताम् मे कथयतो निलयम् तस्य रक्षसः || ४-५८-१८_END

B_4_C_59_10

अनुमान्य यथा तत्त्वम् इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् || ४-५९-११_END

"I reproved him as I was deprived of food, and my son who is an enhancer of my

B_4_C_60_4

लब्ध संज्ञः तु षड् रात्रात् विवशो विह्वलन् इव |

"On getting sensitivity after six days, and on looking in all directions I could not

B_4_C_58_17

अध्यास्ते नगरीम् लंकाम् रावणो नाम राक्षसः || ४-५८-१९_END

"Literally, he is the son of Vishravasa and brother of Kubera, and he presides over

B_4_C_59_11

महेन्द्रस्य गिरेः द्वारम् आवृत्य च सुसमाश्रितः || ४-५९-१२_END
BEGIN_

B_4_C_60_5
BEGIN_
ततः तु सागरान् शैलान् नदीः सर्वाः सरांसि च |

B_4_C_58_18
BEGIN_
इतो द्वीपे समुद्रस्य संपूर्णे शत योजने |

BEGIN_
"There is a lavish city in the oceanic island afar a hundred yojana-s all in all
from here, which Vishvakarma, the Divine-Architect, has built, and it is called Lanka.

B_4_C_59_12
BEGIN_
तत्र सत्त्व सहस्राणाम् सागर अन्तर चारिणाम् |
पंथानम् एको अध्यवसम् संनिरोद्धुम् अवाङ् मुखः || ४-५९-१३_END

" 'I have been hovering there looking downward to completely impede the pathway of

B_4_C_61_0
BEGIN_

BEGIN_

impracticable deed done indiscreetly by me and Jataayu and our following the Sun in red heat, as

B_4_C_60_6
BEGIN_
हृष्ट पक्षि गण आकीर्णः कन्दर उदर कूटवान् |

BEGIN_
"Since this mountain is teeming with teams of birds, caves in its midriffs, and it
is with peaks of its own kind, thus I resolved this to be Mt. Vindhya at the coast of southern

B_4_C_58_19
BEGIN_
जांबूनदमयैः द्वारैः चित्रैः कांचन वेदिकैः |
प्रासादैः हेम वर्णैः च महद्भिः सुसमाकृता || ४-५८-२१
प्राकारेण अर्क वर्णेन महता च समन्विता |_END
BEGIN_
"Its multi-storied buildings are built very symmetrically and they will be in golden

B_4_C_59_13
BEGIN_

स्त्रियम् आदाय गच्छन् वै भिन्न अंजन चय उपमः || ४-५९-१४_END
BEGIN_
" 'There I have seen someone who in simile is like a shoved heap of mascara and he
is going away captivating a lady who equals the aurora in her shine. [4-59-14]_END

B_4_C_61_1
BEGIN_
भगवन् व्रण युक्तत्वात् लज्जया च अकुल इन्द्रियः |
परिश्रान्तो न शक्नोमि वचनम् परिभाषितुम् || ४-६१-२_END
BEGIN_

B_4_C_60_7
BEGIN_

ऋषिः निशाकरो नाम यस्मिन् उग्र तपा अभवत् || ४-६०-८_END
BEGIN_
"There was a sacred hermitage belonging to a sage of intense ascesis known as Sage

B_4_C_58_20

तस्याम् वसति वैदेही दीना कौशेय वासिनी || ४-५८-२२

जनकस्य आत्मजाम् राज्ञः तस्याम् द्रक्ष्यथ मैथिलीम् || ४-५८-२३_END
BEGIN_

B_4_C_59_14
BEGIN_
सो अहम् अभ्यवहार अर्थम् तौ दृष्ट्वा कृत निश्चयः |
तेन साम्ना विनीतेन पन्थानम् अनुयाचितः || ४-५९-१५_END
BEGIN_
" 'On seeing two of them I resolved to use them up for the purpose of food, but he

B_4_C_61_2
BEGIN_
अहम् चैव जटायुः च संघर्षात् दर्प मोहितौ |
आकाशम् पतितौ दूरात् जिज्ञासन्तौ पराक्रमम् || ४-६१-३_END
BEGIN_
"Fascinated by our arrogance and inquisitive of our relative triumphs, myself and

B_4_C_60_8
BEGIN_

B_4_C_58_21
BEGIN_

संप्राप्य सागरस्य अंतम् संपूर्णम् शत योजनम् || ४-५८-२४
आसाद्य दक्षिणम् तीरम् ततो द्रक्ष्यथ रावणम् |
तत्र एव त्वरिताः क्षिप्रम् विक्रमध्वम् प्लवंगमाः || ४-५८-२५_END
BEGIN_

B_4_C_59_15

someone among basely people, isn't it! Then what else is to be said of my kind, aha! [4-59-16]_END

B_4_C_61_3
BEGIN_

B_4_C_60_9

तीक्ष्ण दर्भाम् वसुमतीम् दुःखेन पुनर् आगतः || ४-६०-१०_END

B_4_C_58_22
BEGIN_
ज्ञानेन खलु पश्यामि दृष्ट्वा प्रत्यागमिष्यथ |
आद्यः पंथाः कुलिंगानाम् ये च अन्ये धान्य जीविनः || ४-५८-२६
द्वितीयो बलि भोजानाम् ये च वृक्ष फल अशिनः |
भासाः तृतीयम् गच्छन्ति क्रौन्चाः च कुररैः सह || ४-५८-२७
श्येनाः चतुर्थम् गच्छन्ति गृध्रा गच्छन्ति पंचमम् |_END
BEGIN_
"I foresee by my prognosis that your sighting Seetha is definite at that place, and
definite is your return from there. The first flight level of birds is that of the small Kulinga
birds, house sparrows, songbirds and the like subsisting on food-grains. The second flight level is
that of the birds that are the eaters of leftovers like crows and doves, or the eaters of
tree-fruits like parrots. The third flight level is that of the wading birds like Bhaasa, Kraunca,
Kurara birds and cranes, herons and the like. The fourth flight level is that of hawks and the
fifth is that of the vultures. [4-58-26, 27, 28a]_END

राक्षसेन्द्रो जनस्थानात् अवध्यः सुर दानवैः || ४-६२-६_END
BEGIN_
" 'A demon named Ravana, the chief of demons, and an unkillable one even for gods or
demons abducts Rama's wife from Janasthaana... [4-62-6]_END

B_4_C_58_30
BEGIN_
ततो नीत्वा तु तम् देशम् तीरे नद नदी पतेः |
निर्दग्ध पक्षम् संपातिम् वानराः सुमहौओजसः || ४-५८-३६
तम् पुनः प्रत्यानयित्वा वै तम् देशम् पतग ईश्वरम् |
बभूवुः वानरा हृष्टाः प्रवृत्तिम् उपलभ्य ते || ४-५८-३७_END
BEGIN_
Then those vanara-s of utmost dynamism on taking wing-burnt-bird Sampaati to the
husband rivulets and rivers, namely the ocean, placed him on the shoreline. Again, the vanara-s
sincerely brought back that king of birds, Sampaati, after his offering oblations to Jataayu, and
lodged him as a returnee at his own place. On deriving indication form Sampaati regarding Seetha,
Ravana and Lanka, those returnless vanara-s returned to their search while their gladness returning
to them. [4-58-36, 37]_END

B_4_C_63_1
BEGIN_
कंदरात् तु विसर्पित्वा पर्वतस्य शनैः शनैः |
अहम् विंध्यम् समारुह्य भवतः प्रतिपालये || ४-६३-२_END
BEGIN_
"But on creeping slowly and slowly from the cave of that mountain I clambered up the
Mt. Vindhya and I am looking forward for your arrival... [4-63-2]_END

B_4_C_61_12
BEGIN_
जटायुः माम् अनापृच्छ्य निपपात महीम् ततः |
तम् दृष्ट्वा तूर्णम् आकाशात् आत्मानम् मुक्तवान् अहम् || ४-६१-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Without informing me Jataayu started to trip over the earth, and then on seeing him
I too let myself loose from the sky... [4-61-14]_END

B_4_C_60_18
BEGIN_
गृध्रौ द्वौ दृष्ट पूर्वौ मे मातरिश्व समौ जवे |
गृध्राणाम् चैव राजानौ भ्रातरौ काम रूपिणौ || ४-६०-१९_END
BEGIN_
" 'I have earlier seen you two eagle brothers, kingly eagles among eagles, similar
in your speed to Wind-god and form-changers by your wish... [4-60-19]_END

B_4_C_59_25
BEGIN_
कामम् खलु दशग्रीवः तेजो बल समन्वितः |
भवताम् तु समर्थानाम् न किंचित् अपि दुष्करम् || ४-५९-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Perchance that Decahedral demon is definitely a powerful and prideful demon. But,
as capable vanara-s there is nothing impossible to you, even in the least. [4-59-27]_END

B_4_C_62_6
BEGIN_
सा च कामैः प्रलोभ्यन्ती भक्ष्यैः भोज्यैः च मैथिली |
न भोक्ष्यति महाभागा दुःख मग्ना यशस्विनी || ४-६२-७_END
BEGIN_
" 'She that Maithili, a highly privileged and prestigious lady does not touch any
food, though she is highly lured by banquets and feasts by that Ravana, for she will be sunken in
sorrow... [4-62-7]_END

B_4_C_63_2
BEGIN_
अद्य तु एतस्य कालस्य साग्रम् वर्ष शतम् गतम् |
देश काल प्रतीक्षो अस्मि हृदि कृत्वा मुनेः वचः || ४-६३-३_END
BEGIN_
"As of now, a little more than a hundred years have slipped by, and I am awaiting
events and times minding sage's words in my heart... [4-63-3]_END

B_4_C_61_13
BEGIN_
पक्षभ्याम् च मया गुप्तो जटायुः न प्रदह्यत |
प्रमादात् तत्र निर्दग्धः पतन् वायु पथात् अहम् || ४-६१-१५_END
BEGIN_
"I have hidden Jataayu in sky with both my wings from the scorching Sun... hence, he
is not burn that much... but I am completely burnt when falling from the sky... [4-61-15]_END

B_4_C_60_19
BEGIN_
ज्येष्ठो अवित स्त्वम् तु संपाते जटायुः अनुजः तव |
मानुषम् रूपम् आस्थाय गृह्णीताम् चरणौ मम || ४-६०-२०_END
BEGIN_
" 'You are the elder, isn't it! And Jataayu is your younger brother. You used to
touch my feet taking up human forms... [4-60-20]_END

B_4_C_62_7
BEGIN_
परमान्नम् च वैदेह्या ज्ञात्वा दास्यति वासवः |
यत् अन्नम् अमृत प्रख्यम् सुराणाम् अपि दुर्लभम् || ४-६२-८_END
BEGIN_
" 'On knowing Seetha's plight Indra gives a nectarean food for Vaidehi, which food
is renowned to be Nectarous and unattainable even by gods... [4-62-8]_END

B_4_C_59_26
BEGIN_
तत् अलम् काल संगेन क्रियताम् बुद्धि निश्चयः |
न हि कर्मसु सज्जन्ते बुद्धिमन्तो भवत् विधाः || ४-५९-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Thereby, enough is the time-lapse and make a mental determination. Adventurers and
prudent souls of your kind with not backslide in tasks, isn't it! [4-59-28]_END

B_4_C_63_3
BEGIN_
महाप्रस्थानम् आसाद्य स्वर् गते तु निशाकरे |
माम् निर्दहति संतापो वितर्कैः बहुभिः वृतम् || ४-६३-४_END
BEGIN_
"But many illogical thoughts crowded round me when Sage Nishaakara has gone on great
voyage to heaven, thus my anguish burned me down... [4-63-4]_END

B_4_C_61_14
BEGIN_
आशन्के तम् निपतितम् जनस्थाने जटायुषम् |
अहम् तु पतितो विन्ध्ये दग्ध पक्षो जडी कृतः || ४-६१-१६_END
BEGIN_
"I supposed that Jataayu as has fallen in Janasthaana, but I have fallen on Mt.
Vindhya, as a wing-burnt and insensate eagle... [4-61-16]_END

B_4_C_60_20
BEGIN_
किम् ते व्याधि समुत्थानम् पक्षयोः पतनम् कथम् |
दण्डो वा अयम् धृतः केन सर्वम् आख्याहि पृच्छतः || ४-६०-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Is this falling of wings a result of any illness, if so what is it... or is this
any scourge imposed on you, if so, who is he... tell me all who am inquiring into those details...
[4-60-21]_END

B_4_C_62_8
BEGIN_
तत् अन्नम् मैथिली प्राप्य विज्ञाय इन्द्रात् इदम् तु इति |
अग्रम् उद्धृत्य रामाय भू तले निर्वपिष्यति || ४-६२-९_END
BEGIN_
" 'But on getting that food, and on knowing that it is from Indra, Maithili takes up
the first morsel and dispenses it on the surface of earth for Rama, saying... [4-62-9]_END

B_4_C_63_4
BEGIN_
उदिताम् मरणे बुद्धिम् मुनि वाक्यैः निवर्तये |
बुद्धिः या तेन मे दत्ता प्राणानाम् रक्षणे मम || ४-६३-५
सा मे अपनयते दुःखम् दीप्ता इव अग्नि शिखा तमः |_END
BEGIN_
"I have been reversing the thought cropped up for my suicide by virtue of the
afflatus endowed to me by that sage, and I have been safeguarding my lives as that afflatus is
taking away my anguish, as a tongue of flaring fire takes away darkness... [4-63-5, 6a]_END

B_4_C_61_15
BEGIN_
राज्यात् हीनो भ्रात्रा च पक्षाभ्याम् विक्रमेण च |
सर्वथा मर्तुम् एव इच्छन् पतिष्ये शिखरात् गिरेः || ४-६१-१७_END
BEGIN_
"As one who is divested of his kingdom, his brother, both of his wings, and his own
valance too, such as I was I wished to fall from the mountaintop to die, in any way...
[4-61-17]_END

B_4_C_62_9
BEGIN_
यदि जीवति मे भर्ता लक्ष्मणो वा अपि देवरः |
देवत्वम् गतयोः वा अपि तयोः अन्नम् इदम् तु इति || ४-६२-१०_END
BEGIN_
" 'If my husband is living, or even my younger brother-in-law Lakshmana is living,
or even if they have attained godhood, this food belongs to both of them...' Saying so Seetha
offers oblation to them... [4-62-10_END

B_4_C_63_5
BEGIN_
बुध्यता च मया वीर्यम् रावणस्य दुरात्मनः || ४-६३-६
पुत्रः संतर्जितो वाग्भिः न त्राता मैथिली कथम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Though I am aware of the valour of that dirty-minded Ravana, I was rebuking my son
saying, 'how you have not saved Maithili?' [4-63-6b, 7a]_END

B_4_C_62_10
BEGIN_
एष्यन्ति प्रेषिताः तत्र राम दूताः प्लवंगमाः |
आख्येया राम महिषी त्वया तेभ्यो विहंगम || ४-६२-११_END
BEGIN_
" 'Ushered by Rama, oh, sky-flyer Sampaati, fly-jumpers will be going over to the
place where Seetha is captivated as harbingers of Rama, and you ought to tell those monkeys about
the queen of Rama... [4-62-11]_END

B_4_C_63_6
BEGIN_
तस्या विलपितम् श्रुत्वा तौ च सीता वियोजितौ || ४-६३-७
न मे दशरथ स्नेहात् पुत्रेण उत्पादितम् प्रियम् |_END
BEGIN_
"My son has not effectuated my cherish even on hearing the bewail of Seetha, or at
least on hearing that Rama and Lakshmana are separated from Seetha, or at least on knowing my
friendship with Dasharatha..." Thus Sampaati spoke to monkeys. [4-63-7b, 8a]_END

B_4_C_63_7
BEGIN_
तस्य तु एवम् ब्रुवाणस्य संहतैः वानरैः सह || ४-६३-८
उत्पेततुः तदा पक्षौ समक्षम् वन चारिणाम् |_END
BEGIN_
Both the wings of Sampaati have then cropped up just before the eyes of those
monkeys who are clustering around him, while Sampaati is speaking in this way to those monkeys...
[4-63-8b, 9a]_END

B_4_C_62_11
BEGIN_
सर्वथा तु न गंतव्यम् ईदृशः क्व गमिष्यसि |
देश कालौ प्रतीक्षस्व पक्षौ त्वम् प्रतिपत्स्यसे || ४-६२-१२_END
BEGIN_
" 'In any case you ought not to go-as-you-please... a wingless eagle of your kind
where you wish to go... await the times and scenes, you will regain both of your wings...
[4-62-12]_END

B_4_C_62_12
BEGIN_
उत्सहेयम् अहम् कर्तुम् अद्य एव त्वाम् स पक्षकम् |
इह स्थः त्वम् तु लोकानाम् हितम् कार्यम् करिष्यसि || ४-६२-१३_END
BEGIN_
" 'I am capable of making you a winged eagle now itself, but how can you stay here
and do an agreeable deed to the worlds! So you have to wait. [4-62-13]_END

B_4_C_63_8
BEGIN_
स दृष्ट्वा स्वाम् तनुम् पक्षैः उद्गतैः अरुण च्छदैः || ४-६३-९
प्रहर्षम् अतुलम् लेभे वानरान् च इदम् अब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_
On looking at his own body which is now covered with newborn reddish-feathered wings
Sampaati obtained an incomparable rejoice, and he also said this to vanara-s. [4-63-9b, 10a]_END

B_4_C_64_0
BEGIN_
आख्याता गृध्र राजेन समुत्प्लुत्य प्लवंगमाः |संगताः प्रीति संयुक्ता विनेदुः सिंह विक्रमाः || ४-६४-१_END
BEGIN_
Those lion-hearted fly-jumpers who are informed thus by the kingly eagle Sampaati have gladly jumped and loped 
and screamed in league [4-64-1]_END

B_4_C_62_13
BEGIN_
त्वया अपि खलु तत् कार्यम् तयोः च नृप पुत्रयोः |
ब्राह्मणानाम् गुरूणाम् च मुनीनाम् वासवस्य च || ४-६२-१४_END
BEGIN_
" 'That deed aimed at the wellbeing of both those princes, Rama and Lakshmana, and
of Brahmans, teaches, sages and also of Indra is to be done by you alone, isn't it! [4-62-14]_END

B_4_C_63_9
BEGIN_
निशाकरस्य राजर्षेः प्रभावात् अमित ओजसः || ४-६३-१०
आदित्य रश्मि निर्दग्धौ पक्षौ पुनः उपस्थितौ |_END
BEGIN_
By the efficacy of that kingly sage of illimitable magnificence both the wings of
Sampaati that were burnt down by sunrays have resurfaced again. [4-63-10b, 11a]_END

B_4_C_64_1
BEGIN_
संपातेः वचनम् श्रुत्वा हरयो रावण क्षयम् |हृष्टाः सागरम् आजग्मुः सीता दर्शन कान्क्षिणः || ४-६४-२_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of Sampaati, the monkeys have delightedly come to the ocean to go to the residence of Ravana, 
longing for a glimpse of Seetha. [4-64-2]_END

B_4_C_62_14
BEGIN_
इच्छामि अहम् अपि द्रष्टुम् भ्रातरौ राम लक्ष्मणौ |
न इच्छे चिरम् धारयितुम् प्राणान् त्यक्ष्ये कलेवरम् |
महर्षि तु तत् अब्रवीत् इदम् दृष्ट तत्त्व अर्थ दर्शिनः || ४-६२-१५_END
BEGIN_
" 'Even I wish to see those brothers, Rama and Lakshmana, but I do not wish to bear
lives prolongedly, hence I castaway my mortal body...' and thus that is what the great sage
Nishakara said to me. Saying so that sage, who is a discerner who discerned the sum and substance
of Supreme Person castaway his mortal body in his ascent to heaven." Sampaati continued his
narration in this way. [4-62-15]_END

B_4_C_63_10
BEGIN_
यौवने वर्तमानस्य मम आसीत् यः पराक्रमः || ४-६३-११
तम् एव अद्य अवगच्छामि बलम् पौरुषम् एव च |_END
BEGIN_
"Which valour, vigour, and valiance were prevailing in my youth, now I am
experiencing them alone... [4-63-11b, 12a]_END

B_4_C_64_2
BEGIN_
अभिक्रम्य तु तम् देशम् ददृशुर् भीम विक्रमाः |कृत्स्नम् लोकस्य महतः प्रतिबिंबम् इव स्थितम् || ४-६४-३_END
BEGIN_
Passing across that province those superbly venturesome monkeys have seen the ocean available there, appearing 
like a great mirror image of the world in it entirety. [4-64-3]_END

B_4_C_63_11
BEGIN_
सर्वथा क्रियताम् यत्नः सीताम् अधिगमिष्यथ || ४-६३-१२
पक्ष लाभो मम अयम् वः सिद्धि प्रत्यय कारकः |_END
BEGIN_
"Let an endeavour be made by all of you. For sure, you will come by Seetha. This
event of my regaining wings shall be the causer of credibility in you all... [4-63-12b, 13a]_END

B_4_C_64_3
BEGIN_
दक्षिणस्य समुद्रस्य समासाद्य उत्तराम् दिशम् |संनिवेशम् ततः चक्रुः सहिता वानर उत्तमाः || ४-६४-४_END
BEGIN_
On reaching the northern side of southern ocean those best monkeys have collectively made a camp there. [4-64-4]_END

B_4_C_63_12
BEGIN_
इति उक्त्वा तान् हरीन् सर्वान् संपातिः पतगोत्तम || ४-६३-१३
उत्पपात गिरेः शृंगात् जिज्ञासुः ख गमो गतिम् |_END
BEGIN_
On saying thus to all of those monkeys that best bird Sampaati took wing from that
mountaintop to ascertain the plight of a sky-going bird when anew on the wing. [4-63-13b, 14a]_END

B_4_C_64_4

BEGIN_
That ocean is uproarious with its tides, and with its gigantic and misshapen beings that are sporting in water 
with their wide-opened mouths._END

B_4_C_63_13
BEGIN_
तस्य तत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा प्रतिसंहृष्ट मानसाः |
बभूवुः हरि शार्दूला विक्रम अभ्युदय उन्मुखाः || ४-६३-१४_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that word of Sampaati those tigerly monkeys are heartily gladdened and
while their valour inspiriting them they have became proactive towards their task. [4-63-14]_END

B_4_C_64_5
BEGIN_
प्रसुप्तम् इव च अन्यत्र क्रीडन्तम् इव च अन्यतः |क्वचित् पर्वत मात्रैः च जल राशिभिः आवृतम् || ४-६४-५संकुलम् 
दानव इन्द्रैः च पाताल तल वासिभिः |रोम हर्ष करम् दृष्ट्वा विषेदुः कपिकुंजराः || ४-६४-६_END
BEGIN_
Somewhere that ocean is as though sleeping well, and somewhere else it is as though sporting, elsewhere it is 
overspread with tidewaters as high as mountains, somewhere else it is tumultuous with the best demonic beings 
who are the residents on the plane of netherworld, and the elephantine monkeys despaired on seeing such a hair-raising 
ocean.. [4-64-5, 6]_END

B_4_C_63_14
BEGIN_
अथ पवन समान विक्रमाः
प्लवग वराः प्रतिलब्ध पौरुषाः |
अभिजित् अभिमुखाम् दिशम् ययुः
जनक सुता परिमार्गण उन्मुखाः || ४-६३-१५_END
BEGIN_
Those best fly-jumpers having redeemed their certitude, then with a gustily gusto
waited for an opportune time called abhijit lagna and then journeyed
on to the southern direction, as they are the pioneers in searching Seetha, the daughter of Janaka.
[4-63-15]_END

B_4_C_64_6
BEGIN_
आकाशम् इव दुष्पारम् सागरम् प्रेक्ष्य वानराः |विषेदुः सहिता सर्वे कथम् कार्यम् इति ब्रुवन् || ४-६४-७_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the shoreless ocean that is like an endless sky, hence unnavigable, the vanara-s are despaired and said 
each to each, "how to vault this ocean?" [4-64-7]_END

B_4_C_65_0
BEGIN_
अथ अंगद वचः श्रुत्वा सर्वे ते वानर उत्तमाः |
स्वम् स्वम् गतौ समुत्साहम् ऊचुः तत्र यथा क्रमम् || ४-६५-१
गजो गवाक्षो गवयः शरभो गंधमादनः |
मैन्दः च द्विविदः चैव सुषेणो जांबवान् तथा || ४-६५-२_END
BEGIN_
Then on hearing the words of Angada those best vanara-s, anamely Gaja, Gavaaksha,
Gavaya, Sharabha, Gandhamaadana, Mainda and Dvivida, and Susheshana, and like that Jambavanta have
individually said about their abilities in the matter of leaping the ocean according to their turn.
[4-65-1]_END

B_4_C_64_7
BEGIN_
विषण्णाम् वाहिनीम् दृष्ट्वा सागरस्य निरीक्षणात् |आश्वासयामास हरीन् भय आर्तान् हरि सत्तमः || ४-६४-८_END
BEGIN_
Then the best one among monkeys, Angada, started to inspirit the army of monkeys who are anguished by fear on 
their gazing at the ocean. [4-64-8]_END

B_4_C_65_1
BEGIN_
आबभाषे गजः तत्र प्लवेयम् दश योजनम् |
गवाक्षो योजनानि आह गमिष्यामि इति विंशतिम् || ४-६५-३_END
BEGIN_
In that matter Gaja said, "I can fly ten yojana-s..." and Gavaaksha said, "I can go
over twenty yojana-s..." [4-65-3]_END

B_4_C_64_8
BEGIN_
न विषादे मनः कार्यम् विषादो दोषवत्तरः |विषादो हन्ति पुरुषम् बालम् क्रुद्ध इव उरगः || ४-६४-९_END
BEGIN_
"Loosing heart to dismay is an unworkability, because dismaying itself is detrimental, and dismay alone ruins 
a person, as a vicious viper unworkably ruins an innocent child... [4-64-9]_END

B_4_C_65_2
BEGIN_
शरभो वानरः तत्र वानरान् तान् उवाच ह |
त्रिंशत् गमिष्यामि योजनानाम् प्लवंगमाः || ४-६५-४
ऋषरभो वानरः तत्र वानरान् तान् उवाच ह |
चत्वारिंशत् गमिष्यामि योजनानाम् न संशयः || ४-६५-५
वानरान् तु महातेजा अब्रवीत् गंधमादनः |
योजनानाम् गमिष्यामि पंचाशत् तु न संशयः || ४-६५-६
मैन्दः तु वानरः तत्र वानरान् तान् उवाच ह |
योजनानाम् परम् षष्टिम् अहम् प्लवितुम् उत्सहे || ४-६५-७
ततः तत्र महातेजा द्विविदः प्रत्यभाषत |
गमिष्यामि न संदेहः सप्ततिम् योजनानि अहम् || ४-६५-८
सुषेणः तु महातेजाः सत्त्ववान् कपि सत्तमः |
अशीतिम् प्रतिजाने अहम् योजनानाम् पराक्रमे || ४-६५-९_END
BEGIN_
In that matter the vanara Sharabha said to the monkeys, "oh, fly-jumpers, I can
indeed go up to thirty yojana-s..." The vanara Sharabha said, "I can go up to forty yojana-s,
undoubtedly..." The great-resplendent Gandhamaadana said, "I can go up to fifty yojana-s, no
doubt..." The vanara Mainda said the monkeys in that matter, "I venture to jump just sixty
yojana-s..." Then the great-resplendent Dvivida informed, "I can go up to seventy yojana-s, no
doubt..." But mighty Shushena, the best and the great resplendent monkey said, "I promise to jump
eighty yojana-s..." [4-65-4]_END

B_4_C_64_9
BEGIN_
यो विषादो प्रसहते विक्रमे समुपस्थिते |तेजसा तस्य हीनस्य पुरुष अर्थो न सिद्ध्यति || ४-६४-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Individual achievement will be unachievable to him who readily braces himself with despair when the time for 
venturesomeness verges on, because of the lacking of his own vitality..." So said Angada and then the nightfall 
has occurred. [4-64-10]_END

B_4_C_65_3
BEGIN_
तेषाम् कथयताम् तत्र सर्वान् तान् अनुमान्य च |
ततो वृद्धतमः तेषाम् जांबवान् प्रत्यभाषत || ४-६५-१०_END
BEGIN_
Jambavanta, the oldest one among all of them, appreciating them who are telling
about their jumping capacities, has informed them in this way. [4-65-10]_END

B_4_C_64_10
BEGIN_
तस्याम् रात्र्याम् व्यतीतायाम् अंगदो वानरैः सह |हरि वृद्धैः समागम्य पुनर् मंत्रम् अमंत्रयत् || ४-६४-११_END
BEGIN_
While that night is elapsing into the wee hours of next day, Angada met all the golden-ager monkeys, and again 
deliberated with them. [4-64-11]_END

B_4_C_65_4
BEGIN_
पूर्वम् अस्माकम् अपि आसीत् कश्चित् गति पराक्रमः |
ते वयम् वयसः पारम् अनुप्राप्ताः स्म सांप्रतम् || ४-६५-११_END
BEGIN_
"Previously there was some traversal daredevilry even for us, such as we were, we
are presently on the other shore of our age... [4-65-11]_END

B_4_C_64_11
BEGIN_
सा वानराणाम् ध्वजिनी परिवार्य अंगदम् बभौ |वासवम् परिवार्य इव मरुताम् वाहिनी स्थिता || ४-६४-१२_END
BEGIN_
When those troops of monkey army stood encircling Angada, it beamed forth like the army of gods encircling Indra. 
[4-64-12]_END

B_4_C_65_5
BEGIN_
किम् तु न एवम् गते शक्यम् इदम् कार्यम् उपेक्षितुम् |
यद् अर्थम् कपि राजः च रामः च कृत निश्चयौ || ४-६५-१२_END
BEGIN_
"That being so, for which purpose the king of monkeys Sugreeva and even Rama are
decisively decided on this task, it is impossible for us to marginalize this task... [4-65-12]_END

B_4_C_64_12
BEGIN_
को अन्यः ताम् वानरीम् सेनाम् शक्तः स्तंभयितुम् भवेत् |अन्यत्र वालि तनयात् अन्यत्र च हनूमतः || ४-६४-१३_END
BEGIN_
Who can capably consolidate that army of monkeys, other than Vali's son Angada, or, other than Hanuma? None. Because 
that army itself is an army of fickly, tickly monkeys. [4-64-13]_END

B_4_C_65_6
BEGIN_
सांप्रतम् कालम् अस्माकम् या गतिः ताम् निबोधत |
नवतिम् योजनानाम् तु गमिष्यामि न संशयः || ४-६५-१३_END
BEGIN_
"While we say you may hear what cruise we have at this age... we can go up to ninety
yojana-s, undoubtedly... [4-65-13]_END

B_4_C_64_13
BEGIN_
ततः तान् हरि वृद्धान् च तत् च सैन्यम् अरिन्दमः |अनुमान्य अंगदः श्रीमान् वाक्यम् अर्थवत् अब्रवीत् || ४-६४-१४_END
BEGIN_
Then that enemy-subjugator and illustrious Angada, on revering the old-ager monkeys and paying due respects to 
the army of monkeys, spoke this meaningful sentence. [4-64-14]_END

B_4_C_65_7
BEGIN_
तान् च सर्वान् हरि श्रेष्ठान् जांबवान् इदम् अब्रवीत् |
न खलु एतावत् एव आसीत् गमने मे पराक्रमः || ४-६५-१४_END
BEGIN_
Jambavanta further said this to all of those best monkeys, "my capability in the
stint of going was not definitely limited only thereunto... [4-65-14]_END

B_4_C_64_14
BEGIN_
क इदानीम् महातेजा लंघयिष्यति सागरम् |कः करिष्यति सुग्रीवम् सत्य सन्धम् अरिन्दमम् || ४-६४-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Now, who is that great-resplendent one who can vault over the ocean and who is he who can facilitate the enemy-repressor 
Sugreeva to become truthful to his word... [4-64-15]_END

B_4_C_65_8
BEGIN_
मया वैरोचने यज्ञे प्रभविष्णुः सनातनः |
प्रदक्षिणी कृतः पूर्वम् क्रममाणः त्रिविक्रमः || ४-६५-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Once I have performed circumambulation around the Omnipresent and Eternal Vishnu in
His incarnation as Trivikrama, when He grandiosely increased His physique from that of a
Divine-Dwarfish Brahman boy to that of an Omnidirectional Being, thus filling whole of the Universe
to tread all the three worlds, during the time of Vedic-ritual of Emperor Bali, the legatee of
Vairocana... [4-65-15]_END

B_4_C_64_15
BEGIN_
को वीरो योजन शतम् लंघयेत प्लवंगमाः |इमान् च यूथपान् सर्वान् मोचयेत् को महाभयात् || ४-६४-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Who is that brave hurdler who can hurdle over a hundred yojana distance, oh, fly-jumpers, who is he who can even 
emancipate all these monkey commanders from the great fear of Sugreeva... [4-64-16]_END

B_4_C_65_9
BEGIN_
स इदानीम् अहम् वृद्धः प्लवने मन्दविक्रमः |
यौवने च तदा आसीत् मे बलम् अप्रतिमम् परम् || ४-६५-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Such as I was, I am presently old and decrepit and I have become slow jumping
soldier of misfortune, though my energy in youth was unmatchable and unsurpassable. [4-65-16]_END

B_4_C_64_16
BEGIN_
कस्य प्रसादात् दारान् च पुत्रान् चैव गृहाणि च |इतो निवृत्ताः पश्येम सिद्ध अर्थाः सुखिनो वयम् || ४-६४-१७_END
BEGIN_
"By whose benignancy we can rejoicingly see our wives, sons, houses and homes on going back from here after achieving 
the purpose of our task... [4-64-17]_END

B_4_C_65_10
BEGIN_
संप्रति एतावत् एव अद्य शक्यम् मे गमने स्वतः |
न एतावता च संसिद्धिः कार्यस्य अस्य भविष्यति || ४-६५-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Now, at this age it is possible for me to go on my own only thereunto... and by
that much endeavour that task will be unaccomplished..." So said Jambavanta to monkeys.
[4-65-17]_END

B_4_C_64_17
BEGIN_
कस्य प्रसादात् रामम् च लक्ष्मणम् च महाबलम् |अभिगच्छेम संहृष्टाः सुग्रीवम् च महाबलम् || ४-६४-१८_END
BEGIN_
"By whose benevolence we can unworriedly approach Rama, or even that irascible Lakshmana, or ruthless Sugreeva, 
as well... [4-64-18]_END

B_4_C_65_11
BEGIN_
अथ उत्तरम् उदार अर्थम् अब्रवीत् अंगदः तदा |
अनुमान्य महाप्राज्ञो जांबवंतम् महाकपिम् || ४-६५-१८_END
BEGIN_
Then on reverencing the great monkey Jambavanta, the highly intelligent Angada
thereafter said these salutary words. [4-65-18]_END

B_4_C_64_18
BEGIN_
यदि कश्चित् समर्थो वः सागर प्लवने हरिः |स ददातु इह नः शीघ्रम् पुण्याम् अभय दक्षिणाम् || ४-६४-१९_END
BEGIN_
"If someone among you is competent enough to jump over the ocean, that monkey may now quickly give us all, a munificence, 
called a solemn impunity from Sugreeva..." Angada addressed monkeys in this way. [4-64-19]_END

B_4_C_65_12
BEGIN_
अहम् एतत् गमिष्यामि योजनानाम् शतम् महत् |
निवर्तने तु मे शक्तिः स्यात् न वा इति न निश्चितम् || ४-६५-१९_END
BEGIN_
"I can vault over this ocean which is broadwise in a hundred yojana-breadth, but
whether I am capable of coming back or not, it is indefinite... [4-65-19]_END

B_4_C_64_19
BEGIN_
अंगदस्य वचः श्रुत्वा न कश्चित् किंचित् अब्रवीत् |स्तिमिता इव अभवत् सर्वा सा तत्र हरि वाहिनी || ४-६४-२०_END
BEGIN_
On hearing Angada's words there is none someone to say something in that matter, as the entire monkey troop is 
as though dumbfounded. [4-64-20]_END

B_4_C_65_13
BEGIN_
तम् उवाच हरि श्रेष्ठो जांबवान् वाक्य कोविदः |
ज्ञायते गमने शक्तिः तव हरि ऋक्ष सत्तम || ४-६५-२०_END
BEGIN_
That expert in sentence making, Jambavanta said to the best one among monkeys namely
Angada, "oh, Angada, the best one among monkeys and bears, I know about your capability in
traversal... [4-65-20]_END

B_4_C_64_20
BEGIN_
पुनर् एव अंगदः प्राह तान् हरीन् हरि सत्तमः |सर्वे बलवताम् श्रेष्ठा भवन्तो दृढ विक्रमाः |व्यपदेश्य कुले 
जाताः पूजिताः च अपि अभीक्ष्णशः || ४-६४-२१_END
BEGIN_
Again that best one among monkeys Angada clearly said to those monkeys thus, "all of you are the best ones among 
powerful monkeys, you all are determinedly venturesome, born in flawless families and even adored again and again 
for your adventures... [4-64-21]_END

B_4_C_65_14
BEGIN_
कामम् शत सहस्रम् वा न हि एष विधिः उच्यते |
योजनानाम् भवान् शक्तो गन्तुम् प्रतिनिवर्तितुम् || ४-६५-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Why a hundred, if need be you are capable to go up to a hundred thousand yojana-s
and come back... but this method of our sending you is uncanonical... [4-65-21]_END

B_4_C_64_21
BEGIN_
न हि वो गमने संगः कदाचित् अपि कस्यचित् भवेत् |ब्रुवध्वम् यस्य या शक्तिः प्लवने प्लवगर्षभाः || ४-६४-२२_END
BEGIN_
"There will be no barrier to whomsoever, whensoever he wanted essay wheresoever, isn't it! Hence, oh, best fly-jumpers, 
each one you may give an account as to which one has got which capability in jump-leaping the ocean. [4-64-22]_END

B_4_C_65_15
BEGIN_
न हि प्रेषयिता तात स्वामी प्रेष्यः कथंचन |
भवता अयम् जनः सर्वः प्रेष्यः प्लवग सत्तम || ४-६५-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, dear Angada, in anyway lord assigner cannot be an assignee, hence oh, best
fly-jumper, all of these people are assignable by you... [4-65-22]_END

B_4_C_65_16
BEGIN_
भवान् कलत्रम् अस्माकम् स्वामि भावे व्यवस्थितः |
स्वामी कलत्रम् सैन्यस्य गतिः एषा परंतप || ४-६५-२३_END
BEGIN_
"You are notionally established as our lord and we have to become your
protectionists and, oh, enemy-inflamer Angada, lord becomes the protectionist of army... this alone
is the method... [4-65-23]_END

B_4_C_65_17
BEGIN_
अपि वै एतस्य कार्यस्य भवान् मूलम् अरिम् दम |
तस्मात् कलत्रवत् तात प्रतिपाल्यः सदा भवान् || ४-६५-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, enemy-subjugator, really you are the linchpin to this mission, thereby oh, dear
Angada, you are always to be protected like anything that needs safeguarding... [4-65-24]_END

B_4_C_66_0
BEGIN_
अनेक शत साहस्रीम् विषण्णाम् हरि वाहिनीम् |
जांबवान् समुदीक्ष्य एवम् हनुमंतम् अथ अब्रवीत् || ४-६६-१_END
BEGIN_
On overseeing the crestfallen monkey-soldiery, which is with many hundreds and
thousands of soldiers, then Jambavanta sad this way to Hanuma. [4-66-1]_END

B_4_C_65_18
BEGIN_
मूलम् अर्थस्य संरक्ष्यम् एष कार्यविदाम् नयः |
मूले हि सति सिध्यन्ति गुणाः पुष्प फल उदयः || ४-६५-२५_END
BEGIN_
" 'The prime mover of a task is to be safeguarded...' is the byword of the
taskmasters, and indeed if only the prime mover is there, all the endowments are achievable that
yield fruits... [4-65-25]_END

B_4_C_66_1
BEGIN_
वीर वानर लोकस्य सर्व शास्त्र विदाम् वर |
तूष्णीम् एकांतम् आश्रित्य हनुमन् किम् न जल्पसि || ४-६६-२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, valiant one in the world of vanara-s, being an erudite scholar among all the
scriptural scholars, Hanuma, why do not you mumble something, why do you resort to a calmly
loneliness... [4-66-2]_END

B_4_C_65_19
BEGIN_
तद् भवान् अस्य कार्यस्य साधनम् सत्य विक्रमः |
बुद्धि विक्रम संपन्नो हेतुः अत्र परंतपः || ४-६५-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Thereby, oh, truth-valiant Angada, you are instrumental to this task and as you are
privileged with sagacity and audacity, oh, enemy-inflamer, you are the keystone for this task of
searching Seetha... [4-65-26]_END

B_4_C_66_2
BEGIN_
हनुमन् हरि राजस्य सुग्रीवस्य समो हि असि |
राम लक्ष्मणयोः च अपि तेजसा च बलेन च || ४-६६-३_END
BEGIN_
"By your brilliance and brawn, oh, Hanuma, you match up to king of monkeys Sugreeva,
or even to Rama and Lakshmana, as well... [4-66-3]_END

B_4_C_65_20
BEGIN_
गुरुः च गुरु पुत्रः च त्वम् हि नः कपि सत्तम |
भवन्तम् आश्रित्य वयम् समर्था हि अर्थ साधने || ४-६५-२७_END
BEGIN_
"For us you are indeed a respectable one by yourself, and as the son of respected
Vali too, and oh, best monkey, sheltered by you we are indeed capable of achieving the objective of
our task..." So said Jambavanta to Angada. [4-65-27]_END

B_4_C_66_3
BEGIN_
अरिष्टनेमिनः पुत्रो वैनतेयो महाबलः |
गरुत्मान् इव विख्यात उत्तमः सर्व पक्षिणाम् || ४-६६-४_END
BEGIN_
"The son of Kashyapa Prajapati and Lady Vinata is the best bird among all the birds
who is superbly mighty and who is universally renowned as Garuda... [4-66-4]_END

B_4_C_65_21
BEGIN_
उक्त वाक्यम् महाप्राज्ञम् जांबवंतम् महाकपिः |
प्रत्युवाच उत्तरम् वाक्यम् वालि सूनुः अथ अंगदः || ४-६५-२८_END
BEGIN_
When that highly scholarly Jambavanta has said thus, the great monkey and the son of
Vali Angada said this sentence in reply as an answer. [4-65-28]_END

B_4_C_66_4
BEGIN_
बहुशो हि मया दृष्टः सागरे स महाबलः |
भुजगान् उद्धरन् पक्षी महावेगो महायशाः || ४-६६-५_END
BEGIN_
"Iindeed, I have oftentimes seen that highly glorious, rapidly speedy, great mighty

B_4_C_65_23

B_4_C_65_24

B_4_C_67_0
BEGIN_

विनेदुः तुष्टुवुः च अपि हनूमन्तम् महाबलम् || ४-६७-२_END
BEGIN_
On seeing that best monkey Hanuma, who is burgeoning to cross over the hundred
yojana-ocean and who is also quickly, progressively, and stupendously maximising his body, the
other monkeys instantly shunning off their sadness, raved and rhapsodized over that staggeringly
mighty monkey, Hanuma. [4-67-1, 2]_END

B_4_C_66_8

B_4_C_65_26
BEGIN_

जांबवान् उत्तमम् वाक्यम् प्रोवाच इदम् ततो अंगदम् || ४-६५-३३_END
BEGIN_
When that best and valiant fly-jumper Jambavanta is said that way by Angada, then
Jambavanta advised him in this best sentence to Angada. [4-65-33]_END

B_4_C_67_1
BEGIN_
प्रहृष्टा विस्मिताः च अपि ते वीक्षन्ते समंततः |

BEGIN_
Those monkeys available all over there are altogether buoyed up and utterly
astounded, and as with the people who have enthusiastically seen Narayana when He maximised His
physique to tread the triad of worlds in His Trivikrama incarnation, these monkeys too are looking
at Hanuma who is now maximising his body. [4-67-3]_END

B_4_C_66_9
